%%%% TITLE

\title[Bicombing MCG and Teich via stable cubical intervals]{Bicombing the mapping class group and Teichm\"uller space via stable cubical intervals}



 
 
 \author{Matthew Gentry Durham}
 \address{Department of Mathematics and Statistics, CUNY Hunter College, New York, NY }
 \email{matthew.durham@hunter.edu}
 

\newwrite\markfile
\immediate\openout\markfile=boxpositions_teichmuller.txt

\newcommand{\markbox}[2]{%
  \setbox0=\hbox{#2}%
  \immediate\write\markfile{#1:pwhd:\the\value{page}:\the\wd0:\the\ht0:\the\dp0}%
  \pdfsavepos
  \write\markfile{#1:spxy:\the\value{page}:\the\pdflastxpos:\the\pdflastypos:}%
  #2% 
  \pdfsavepos
  \write\markfile{#1:epxy:\the\value{page}:\the\pdflastxpos:\the\pdflastypos:}%
}

\begin{document}
\begin{abstract}
  In this mostly expository article, we provide a new account of our proof with Minsky and Sisto that mapping class groups and Teichm\"uller spaces admit bicombings.  More generally, we explain how the hierarchical hull of a pair of points in any colorable hierarchically hyperbolic space is quasi-isometric to a finite CAT(0) cube complex of bounded dimension, with the added property that perturbing the pair of points results in a uniformly bounded change to the cubical structure.  Our approach is simplified and new in many aspects.
  
\end{abstract}


\maketitle


\section{Introduction} \label{sec:intro}

The \markbox{0}{recent} \markbox{1}{infusion} \markbox{2}{of} \markbox{3}{techniques} \markbox{4}{from} \markbox{5}{cube} \markbox{6}{complexes} \markbox{7}{into} \markbox{8}{the} \markbox{9}{study} \markbox{10}{of} \markbox{11}{mapping} \markbox{12}{class} \markbox{13}{groups} \markbox{14}{of} \markbox{15}{finite-type} \markbox{16}{surfaces} \markbox{17}{has} \markbox{18}{had} \markbox{19}{dramatic} \markbox{20}{consequences,} \markbox{21}{including} \markbox{22}{toward} \markbox{23}{our} \markbox{24}{ability} \markbox{25}{to} \markbox{26}{control} \markbox{27}{top-dimensional} \markbox{28}{quasi-isometrically} \markbox{29}{embedded} \markbox{30}{flats} \cite{HHS_quasi}, \markbox{31}{build} \markbox{32}{bicombings} \cite{DMS_bary, HHP}, \markbox{33}{and} \markbox{34}{understand} \markbox{35}{their} \markbox{36}{geometry} \markbox{37}{at} \markbox{38}{infinity} \cite{DZ22, Ham_boundary, Dur_infcube}, \markbox{39}{among} \markbox{40}{others} \cite{ABD, Petyt_quasicube, DZ22, zalloum2025effective}.

The \markbox{41}{central} \markbox{42}{result} \markbox{43}{facilitating} \markbox{44}{most} \markbox{45}{of} \markbox{46}{the} \markbox{47}{above} \markbox{48}{work} \markbox{49}{was} \markbox{50}{the} \emph{cubical model theorem} \markbox{51}{of} \markbox{52}{Behrstock--Hagen--Sisto} \cite{HHS_quasi}.  \markbox{53}{It} \markbox{54}{says,} \markbox{55}{roughly,} \markbox{56}{that} \markbox{57}{the} \markbox{58}{coarse} \markbox{59}{convex} \markbox{60}{hull} \markbox{61}{of} \markbox{62}{a} \markbox{63}{finite} \markbox{64}{set} \markbox{65}{of} \markbox{66}{points} \markbox{67}{in} \markbox{68}{the} \markbox{69}{mapping} \markbox{70}{class} \markbox{71}{group} \markbox{72}{is} \markbox{73}{quasi-isometrically} \markbox{74}{approximated} \markbox{75}{by} \markbox{76}{a} \markbox{77}{CAT(0)} \markbox{78}{cube} \markbox{79}{complex,} \markbox{80}{which} \markbox{81}{is} \markbox{82}{a} \markbox{83}{higher} \markbox{84}{dimensional} \markbox{85}{analogue} \markbox{86}{of} Gromov's \markbox{87}{tree} \markbox{88}{approximation} \markbox{89}{theorem} \markbox{90}{for} \markbox{91}{hyperbolic} \markbox{92}{spaces.}  \markbox{93}{The} \markbox{94}{cubical} \markbox{95}{model} \markbox{96}{theorem} \markbox{97}{was} \markbox{98}{later} \markbox{99}{generalized} \markbox{100}{by} \markbox{101}{Bowditch} \cite{Bowditch_hulls} \markbox{102}{(to} \markbox{103}{certain} \markbox{104}{coarse} \markbox{105}{median} \markbox{106}{spaces)} \markbox{107}{and} \markbox{108}{the} \markbox{109}{author} \cite{Dur_infcube} \markbox{110}{(to} \markbox{111}{allow} \markbox{112}{for} \markbox{113}{points} \markbox{114}{at} \markbox{115}{infinity).}  \markbox{116}{All} \markbox{117}{versions} \markbox{118}{hold} \markbox{119}{in} \markbox{120}{the} \markbox{121}{broader} \markbox{122}{context} \markbox{123}{of} \markbox{124}{hierarchically} \markbox{125}{hyperbolic} \markbox{126}{spaces} \cite{HHS_I}, \markbox{127}{a} \markbox{128}{framework} \markbox{129}{for} \markbox{130}{studying} \markbox{131}{a} \markbox{132}{wide} \markbox{133}{variety} \markbox{134}{of} \markbox{135}{spaces} \markbox{136}{with} \markbox{137}{blended} \markbox{138}{negative} \markbox{139}{and} \markbox{140}{positive} \markbox{141}{curvature,} \markbox{142}{e.g.} Teichm\"uller \markbox{143}{spaces} \cite{Brock, Rafi:hypteich, Dur:augmented}, \markbox{144}{that} \markbox{145}{built} \markbox{146}{off} \markbox{147}{the} \markbox{148}{seminal} \markbox{149}{work} \markbox{150}{of} \markbox{151}{Masur--Minsky} \cite{MM99,MM00} \markbox{152}{on} \markbox{153}{the} \markbox{154}{mapping} \markbox{155}{class} \markbox{156}{group;} \markbox{157}{see} \markbox{158}{Section} \ref{sec:HHS}. 

The \markbox{159}{cubical} \markbox{160}{approximation} \markbox{161}{theorem} \markbox{162}{allows} \markbox{163}{one} \markbox{164}{to} \markbox{165}{build} \markbox{166}{any} \markbox{167}{number} \markbox{168}{of} \markbox{169}{cubically-defined} \markbox{170}{(and} \markbox{171}{hierarchically} \markbox{172}{well-behaved)} \markbox{173}{paths} \markbox{174}{between} \markbox{175}{a} \markbox{176}{pair} \markbox{177}{of} \markbox{178}{points} \markbox{179}{by} \markbox{180}{importing} \markbox{181}{them} \markbox{182}{from} \markbox{183}{the} \markbox{184}{cubical} \markbox{185}{model} \markbox{186}{of} \markbox{187}{their} \markbox{188}{hull.}  \markbox{189}{This} \markbox{190}{observation} \markbox{191}{was} \markbox{192}{at} \markbox{193}{the} \markbox{194}{core} \markbox{195}{of} \markbox{196}{two} \markbox{197}{recent} \markbox{198}{proofs} \markbox{199}{that} \markbox{200}{the} \markbox{201}{mapping} \markbox{202}{class} \markbox{203}{group} \markbox{204}{is} \emph{bicombable}\footnote{Roughly, a bicombing on a metric space is a transitive family of quasi-geodesic paths that are stable under small perturbations of the endpoints; see Definition \ref{defn:bicombing}.}.  \markbox{205}{The} \markbox{206}{two} \markbox{207}{proofs,} \markbox{208}{due} \markbox{209}{to} \markbox{210}{Haettel--Hoda--Petyt} \cite{HHP} \markbox{211}{and} \markbox{212}{Minsky,} \markbox{213}{Sisto,} \markbox{214}{and} \markbox{215}{the} \markbox{216}{author} \cite{DMS_bary}, \markbox{217}{are} \markbox{218}{very} \markbox{219}{different} \markbox{220}{but} \markbox{221}{both} \markbox{222}{depend} \markbox{223}{crucially} \markbox{224}{on} \markbox{225}{this} \markbox{226}{cubical} \markbox{227}{model} \markbox{228}{machinery.}  \markbox{229}{See} \markbox{230}{also} \markbox{231}{a} \markbox{232}{recent} \markbox{233}{elegant} \markbox{234}{proof} \markbox{235}{of} \markbox{236}{bicombability} \markbox{237}{using} \markbox{238}{wallspace} \markbox{239}{techniques} \markbox{240}{due} \markbox{241}{to} \markbox{242}{Petyt--Zalloum} \cite{PZ_walls}.

The \markbox{243}{purpose} \markbox{244}{of} \markbox{245}{this} \markbox{246}{paper} \markbox{247}{is} \markbox{248}{to} \markbox{249}{explain} \markbox{250}{a} \markbox{251}{new} \markbox{252}{proof} \markbox{253}{of} \markbox{254}{the} \markbox{255}{two-point} \markbox{256}{version} \markbox{257}{of} \markbox{258}{the} \markbox{259}{main} \markbox{260}{technical} \markbox{261}{result} \markbox{262}{of} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{263}{via} \markbox{264}{the} \markbox{265}{machinery} \markbox{266}{in} \cite{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{267}{which} \markbox{268}{we} \markbox{269}{state} \markbox{270}{here} \markbox{271}{informally} \markbox{272}{(see} \markbox{273}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}):

\begin{thmi}\label{thmi:main}
The \markbox{274}{hierarchical} \markbox{275}{hull} \markbox{276}{of} \markbox{277}{a} \markbox{278}{pair} \markbox{279}{of} \markbox{280}{points} \markbox{281}{in} \markbox{282}{a} \markbox{283}{colorable} \markbox{284}{HHS} \markbox{285}{can} \markbox{286}{be} \markbox{287}{stably} \markbox{288}{approximated} \markbox{289}{by} \markbox{290}{a} \markbox{291}{CAT(0)} \markbox{292}{cube} complex.
\end{thmi}

With \markbox{293}{this} \markbox{294}{tool} \markbox{295}{in} \markbox{296}{hand,} \markbox{297}{bicombability} \markbox{298}{is} \markbox{299}{a} \markbox{300}{straight-forward} \markbox{301}{application} \markbox{302}{of} \markbox{303}{cubical} \markbox{304}{techniques} \markbox{305}{essentially} \markbox{306}{via} \markbox{307}{the} \markbox{308}{arguments} \markbox{309}{in}  \cite[Sections \markbox{310}{5} \markbox{311}{and} 6]{DMS_bary}:

\begin{cori}\label{cori:semihyp}
Let \markbox{m312}{$S$} \markbox{313}{be} \markbox{314}{a} \markbox{315}{finite} \markbox{316}{type} \markbox{317}{surface.}  \markbox{318}{Then} \markbox{319}{its} \markbox{320}{mapping} \markbox{321}{class} \markbox{322}{group} \markbox{323}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{324}{space} \markbox{325}{with} \markbox{326}{the} Teichm\"uller \markbox{327}{metric} \markbox{328}{admit} \markbox{329}{bicombings} \markbox{330}{by} \markbox{331}{hierarchy} paths.
\end{cori}


\begin{remark}
One \markbox{332}{can} \markbox{333}{upgrade} \markbox{334}{both} \markbox{335}{of} \markbox{336}{these} \markbox{337}{statements} \markbox{338}{to} \markbox{339}{ensure} \markbox{340}{coarse} \markbox{341}{equivariance} \markbox{342}{in} \markbox{343}{the} \markbox{344}{presence} \markbox{345}{of} \markbox{346}{an} \markbox{347}{appropriate} \markbox{348}{group} \markbox{349}{action.}  \markbox{350}{In} \markbox{351}{particular,} \markbox{352}{in} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{353}{we} \markbox{354}{showed} \markbox{355}{that} \markbox{356}{the} \markbox{357}{bicombings} \markbox{358}{in} \markbox{359}{Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp} \markbox{360}{are} \markbox{361}{coarsely} \markbox{362}{equivariant} \markbox{363}{with} \markbox{364}{respect} \markbox{365}{to} \markbox{366}{the} \markbox{367}{mapping} \markbox{368}{class} \markbox{369}{group} \markbox{370}{action,} \markbox{371}{and} \markbox{372}{that} \markbox{373}{the} \markbox{374}{mapping} \markbox{375}{class} \markbox{376}{group} \markbox{377}{is} \emph{semi-hyperbolic} \markbox{378}{in} \markbox{379}{the} \markbox{380}{sense} \markbox{381}{of} \cite{AB95}.  \markbox{382}{This} \markbox{383}{equivariance} \markbox{384}{upgrade} \markbox{385}{is} \markbox{386}{relatively} \markbox{387}{straight-forward} \markbox{388}{once} \markbox{389}{one} \markbox{390}{has} \markbox{391}{the} \markbox{392}{bicombing,} \markbox{393}{but} \markbox{394}{we} \markbox{395}{have} \markbox{396}{omitted} \markbox{397}{it} \markbox{398}{since} \markbox{399}{it} \markbox{400}{adds} \markbox{401}{yet} \markbox{402}{another} \markbox{403}{layer} \markbox{404}{complexity} \markbox{405}{to} \markbox{406}{the} \markbox{407}{statements} \markbox{408}{and} \markbox{409}{proofs} \markbox{410}{in} \markbox{411}{an} \markbox{412}{already} \markbox{413}{technical} \markbox{414}{construction.}  \markbox{415}{We} \markbox{416}{point} \markbox{417}{the} \markbox{418}{reader} \markbox{419}{to} \cite[Remark 2]{DMS_bary} \markbox{420}{for} \markbox{421}{a} \markbox{422}{discussion} \markbox{423}{of} \markbox{424}{how} \markbox{425}{equivariance} \markbox{426}{works} \markbox{427}{for} \markbox{428}{this} \markbox{429}{construction.} 
\end{remark}

% More generally, these results hold in the context of \emph{hierarchically hyperbolic spaces} (HHSes), a framework for studying a wide variety of spaces with blended negative and positive curvature that built off the seminal work of Masur--Minsky \cite{MM99,MM00} on the mapping class group; see Section \ref{sec:HHS}.  In the HHS setting, the guiding philosophy is to study objects by projecting to a family of hyperbolic spaces and then use techniques from hyperbolic geometry.  The cubical model theorem is utilized similarly---one exports problems from the mapping class group to a family cube complexes and employs cubical techniques.


We \markbox{430}{have} \markbox{431}{several} \markbox{432}{motivations} \markbox{433}{for} \markbox{434}{writing} \markbox{435}{this} \markbox{436}{paper.}  \markbox{437}{First,} \markbox{438}{we} \markbox{439}{wanted} \markbox{440}{to} \markbox{441}{give} \markbox{442}{a} \markbox{443}{simplified} \markbox{444}{account} \markbox{445}{of} \markbox{446}{the} \markbox{447}{cubical} \markbox{448}{model} \markbox{449}{results} \markbox{450}{in} \cite{DMS_bary, DMS_FJ} \markbox{451}{in} \markbox{452}{less} \markbox{453}{generality.}  \markbox{454}{Roughly} \markbox{455}{speaking,} \markbox{456}{the} \markbox{457}{cubical} \markbox{458}{model} \markbox{459}{for} \markbox{460}{a} \markbox{461}{finite} \markbox{462}{subset} \markbox{m463}{$F$} \markbox{464}{of} \markbox{465}{an} \markbox{466}{HHS} \markbox{467}{from} \cite{HHS_quasi} \markbox{468}{is} \markbox{469}{produced} \markbox{470}{from} \markbox{471}{a} \markbox{472}{wallspace} \markbox{473}{on} \markbox{474}{a} \markbox{475}{family} \markbox{476}{of} \markbox{477}{trees} \markbox{478}{obtained} \markbox{479}{by} \markbox{480}{projecting} \markbox{m481}{$F$} \markbox{482}{to} \markbox{483}{each} \markbox{484}{of} \markbox{485}{the} \markbox{486}{hyperbolic} \markbox{487}{spaces} \markbox{488}{in} \markbox{489}{the} \markbox{490}{hierarchy.}  \markbox{491}{The} \markbox{492}{proof} \markbox{493}{of} \markbox{494}{bicombability} \markbox{495}{in} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{496}{proceeds} \markbox{497}{by} \markbox{498}{using} \markbox{499}{hyperbolic} \markbox{500}{geometry} \markbox{501}{techniques---culminating} \markbox{502}{in} \markbox{503}{the} \markbox{504}{Stable} \markbox{505}{Tree} \markbox{506}{Theorem} \cite[Theorem 3.2]{DMS_bary}---to \markbox{507}{produce} \markbox{508}{a} \markbox{509}{family} \markbox{510}{of} \markbox{511}{trees} \markbox{512}{which} \markbox{513}{is} \markbox{514}{coarsely} \markbox{515}{stable} \markbox{516}{under} \markbox{517}{bounded} \markbox{518}{perturbations} \markbox{519}{of} \markbox{m520}{$F$}.  \markbox{521}{In} \markbox{522}{this} \markbox{523}{paper,} \markbox{524}{we} \markbox{525}{simplify} \markbox{526}{a} \markbox{527}{number} \markbox{528}{of} \markbox{529}{aspects} \markbox{530}{of} \markbox{531}{this} \markbox{532}{initial} \markbox{533}{portion} \markbox{534}{of} \markbox{535}{the} \markbox{536}{argument} \markbox{537}{by} \markbox{538}{limiting} \markbox{539}{ourselves} \markbox{540}{to} \markbox{541}{modeling} \markbox{542}{only} \markbox{543}{a} \markbox{544}{pair} \markbox{545}{of} \markbox{546}{points} \markbox{547}{instead} \markbox{548}{of} \markbox{549}{arbitrary} \markbox{550}{collections} \markbox{551}{of} \markbox{552}{points} \markbox{553}{and} rays.

The \markbox{554}{second} \markbox{555}{motivation} \markbox{556}{is} \markbox{557}{to} \markbox{558}{explain} \markbox{559}{how} \markbox{560}{to} \markbox{561}{combine} \markbox{562}{the} \markbox{563}{stability} \markbox{564}{techniques} \markbox{565}{from} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{566}{with} \markbox{567}{the} \markbox{568}{new} \markbox{569}{cubical} \markbox{570}{model} \markbox{571}{construction} \markbox{572}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}\footnote{This construction has many extra benefits as compared to the construction from \cite{HHS_quasi}.  We point interested readers to the in-depth discussion in the introduction of \cite{Dur_infcube}.}.  \markbox{573}{This} \markbox{574}{involves} \markbox{575}{a} \markbox{576}{new,} \markbox{577}{more} \markbox{578}{elementary} \markbox{579}{proof} \markbox{580}{of} \markbox{581}{the} \markbox{582}{key} \markbox{583}{Stable} \markbox{584}{Trees} \markbox{585}{Theorem} \markbox{586}{for} \markbox{587}{intervals;} \markbox{588}{see} \markbox{589}{Section} \ref{sec:stable intervals} \markbox{590}{below.}  \markbox{591}{Notably,} \markbox{592}{with} \markbox{593}{Minsky} \markbox{594}{and} \markbox{595}{Sisto,} \markbox{596}{we} \markbox{597}{recently} \cite{DMS_FJ} \markbox{598}{implemented} \markbox{599}{a} \markbox{600}{significant} \markbox{601}{expansion} \markbox{602}{of} \markbox{603}{the} \markbox{604}{techniques} \markbox{605}{from} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{606}{utilizing} \markbox{607}{the} \markbox{608}{framework} \markbox{609}{of} \cite{Dur_infcube}\footnote{The first version of this expository article appeared before \cite{DMS_FJ}, but we have subsequently adapted it to account for that paper.}.  \markbox{610}{This} \markbox{611}{allowed} \markbox{612}{us} \markbox{613}{to} \markbox{614}{build} \markbox{615}{an} \markbox{616}{asymptotically} \markbox{617}{CAT(0)} \markbox{618}{metric} \cite{Kar_asymp} \markbox{619}{on} \markbox{620}{any} \markbox{621}{colorable} \markbox{622}{HHS,} \markbox{623}{construct} \markbox{624}{a} \markbox{m625}{$\calZ$}-boundary \markbox{626}{(in} \markbox{627}{the} \markbox{628}{sense} \markbox{629}{of} \cite{bestvina1996local, Dra:BM_formula}) \markbox{630}{for} \markbox{631}{any} \markbox{632}{colorable} \markbox{633}{HHG} \markbox{634}{(see} \markbox{635}{also} \cite{hamenstadt2025z} \markbox{636}{for} \markbox{637}{mapping} \markbox{638}{class} \markbox{639}{groups),} \markbox{640}{and} \markbox{641}{establish} \markbox{642}{the} \markbox{643}{Farrell--Jones} \markbox{644}{Conjecture} \cite{farrell1993isomorphism} \markbox{645}{for} \markbox{646}{many} \markbox{647}{HHGs,} \markbox{648}{including} \markbox{649}{extra-large} \markbox{650}{type} \markbox{651}{Artin} \markbox{652}{groups.}  \markbox{653}{This} \markbox{654}{paper} \markbox{655}{can} \markbox{656}{be} \markbox{657}{seen} \markbox{658}{as} \markbox{659}{explaining} \markbox{660}{the} \markbox{661}{simplest} \markbox{662}{possible} \markbox{663}{case} \markbox{664}{of} \markbox{665}{the} \markbox{666}{main} \markbox{667}{technical} \markbox{668}{construction} \markbox{669}{in} \cite{DMS_FJ}.

Unsurprisingly, \markbox{670}{combining} \markbox{671}{the} \markbox{672}{work} \markbox{673}{in} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{674}{and} \cite{Dur_infcube} \markbox{675}{involves} \markbox{676}{an} \markbox{677}{exposition} \markbox{678}{of} \markbox{679}{both,} \markbox{680}{though} \markbox{681}{we} \markbox{682}{have} \markbox{683}{mostly} \markbox{684}{focused} \markbox{685}{on} \markbox{686}{where} \markbox{687}{they} \markbox{688}{meet.}  \markbox{689}{We} \markbox{690}{summarize} \markbox{691}{the} \markbox{692}{main} \markbox{693}{features} \markbox{694}{of} \markbox{695}{this} \markbox{696}{(mostly)} \markbox{697}{expository} \markbox{698}{paper} \markbox{699}{as} follows:

\begin{itemize}
\item We \markbox{700}{give} \markbox{701}{an} \markbox{702}{exposition} \markbox{703}{of} \markbox{704}{the} \markbox{705}{basic} \markbox{706}{cubical} \markbox{707}{model} \markbox{708}{construction} \markbox{709}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{710}{which} \markbox{711}{is} \markbox{712}{significantly} \markbox{713}{simplified} \markbox{714}{from} \markbox{715}{the} \markbox{716}{much} \markbox{717}{more} \markbox{718}{general} \markbox{719}{setting} \markbox{720}{considered} \markbox{721}{therein,} \markbox{722}{(i.e.,} \markbox{723}{which} \markbox{724}{allows} \markbox{725}{for} \markbox{726}{modeling} \markbox{727}{points} \markbox{728}{at} infinity).

\item We \markbox{729}{explain} \markbox{730}{how} \markbox{731}{to} \markbox{732}{combine} \markbox{733}{the} \markbox{734}{stability} \markbox{735}{techniques} \markbox{736}{from} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{737}{with} \markbox{738}{the} \markbox{739}{cubical} \markbox{740}{model} \markbox{741}{construction} \markbox{742}{of} \cite{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{743}{In} \markbox{744}{particular,} \markbox{745}{this} \markbox{746}{involves} \markbox{747}{defining} \markbox{748}{a} \markbox{749}{refined} \markbox{750}{notion} \markbox{751}{of} \markbox{752}{a} \emph{stable decomposition} \markbox{753}{(Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}), \markbox{754}{and} \markbox{755}{giving} \markbox{756}{a} \markbox{757}{new} \markbox{758}{proof} \markbox{759}{of} \markbox{760}{the} \markbox{761}{Stable} \markbox{762}{Trees} \markbox{763}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{764}{for} \markbox{765}{intervals.}  \markbox{766}{We} \markbox{767}{note} \markbox{768}{that} \markbox{769}{these} \markbox{770}{stable} \markbox{771}{decompositions} \markbox{772}{also} \markbox{773}{appear} \markbox{774}{in} \cite{DMS_FJ}.

\item Using \markbox{775}{the} \markbox{776}{above,} \markbox{777}{we} \markbox{778}{prove} \markbox{779}{bicombability} \markbox{780}{of} \markbox{781}{mapping} \markbox{782}{class} \markbox{783}{groups} \markbox{784}{(and} \markbox{785}{HHSes)} \markbox{786}{via} \markbox{787}{the} \markbox{788}{stable} \markbox{789}{cubulation} \markbox{790}{techniques} \markbox{791}{from} \cite{DMS_bary}, \markbox{792}{while} \markbox{793}{restricting} \markbox{794}{ourselves} \markbox{795}{to} \markbox{796}{the} \markbox{797}{simplified} \markbox{798}{setting} \markbox{799}{of} \markbox{800}{cubical} \markbox{801}{models} \markbox{802}{for} \markbox{803}{pairs} \markbox{804}{of} \markbox{805}{points.}  \markbox{806}{Notably,} \markbox{807}{the} \markbox{808}{bicombing} \markbox{809}{construction} \markbox{810}{from} \cite{HHP} \markbox{811}{also} \markbox{812}{depends} \markbox{813}{on} \markbox{814}{the} \markbox{815}{cubical} \markbox{816}{models} \markbox{817}{(from} \cite{HHS_quasi}), \markbox{818}{so} \markbox{819}{one} \markbox{820}{can} \markbox{821}{also} \markbox{822}{see} \markbox{823}{this} \markbox{824}{paper} \markbox{825}{as} \markbox{826}{supplying} \markbox{827}{an} \markbox{828}{exposition} \markbox{829}{for} \markbox{830}{some} \markbox{831}{of} \markbox{832}{the} \markbox{833}{underlying} \markbox{834}{technology} \markbox{835}{of} \markbox{836}{their} construction.

\item By \markbox{837}{focusing} \markbox{838}{on} \markbox{839}{the} \markbox{840}{bicombing} \markbox{841}{result} \markbox{842}{(Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp}), \markbox{843}{we} \markbox{844}{are} \markbox{845}{able} \markbox{846}{significantly} \markbox{847}{simplifly} \markbox{848}{the} \markbox{849}{endgame} \markbox{850}{of} \markbox{851}{the} \markbox{852}{path} \markbox{853}{construction.}  \markbox{854}{In} \markbox{855}{particular,} \markbox{856}{we} \markbox{857}{utilize} \markbox{858}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{859}{paths} \cite{NibloReeves} \markbox{860}{in} \markbox{861}{the} \markbox{862}{cubical} \markbox{863}{model} \markbox{864}{instead} \markbox{865}{of} \markbox{866}{the} \markbox{867}{more} \markbox{868}{elaborate} \markbox{869}{version} \markbox{870}{of} \markbox{871}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{872}{contractions} \markbox{873}{from} \markbox{874}{our} \markbox{875}{work} \markbox{876}{with} \markbox{877}{Minsky} \markbox{878}{and} \markbox{879}{Sisto} \cite[Section 5]{DMS_bary}.
\end{itemize}

\subsection{Background reading}

Our \markbox{880}{main} \markbox{881}{focus} \markbox{882}{in} \markbox{883}{this} \markbox{884}{article} \markbox{885}{is} \markbox{886}{explaining} \markbox{887}{how} \markbox{888}{to} \markbox{889}{adapt} \markbox{890}{the} \markbox{891}{stable} \markbox{892}{cubulation} \markbox{893}{techniques} \markbox{894}{from} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{895}{to} \markbox{896}{the}  \markbox{897}{cubical} \markbox{898}{model} \markbox{899}{setup} \markbox{900}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{901}{which} \markbox{902}{we} \markbox{903}{note} \markbox{904}{is} \markbox{905}{done} \markbox{906}{in} \markbox{907}{much} \markbox{908}{more} \markbox{909}{general} \markbox{910}{setting} \markbox{911}{in} \cite{DMS_FJ}.  \markbox{912}{As} \markbox{913}{such,} \markbox{914}{the} \markbox{915}{reader} \markbox{916}{will} \markbox{917}{benefit} \markbox{918}{from} \markbox{919}{a} \markbox{920}{variety} \markbox{921}{of} \markbox{922}{contextual} \markbox{923}{information} \markbox{924}{and} \markbox{925}{motivation} \markbox{926}{in} \markbox{927}{and} \markbox{928}{around} \markbox{929}{cube} \markbox{930}{complexes} \markbox{931}{and} \markbox{932}{HHSes.}  \markbox{933}{We} \markbox{934}{provide} \markbox{935}{some} \markbox{936}{suggested} \markbox{937}{reading} \markbox{938}{in} \markbox{939}{the} \markbox{940}{list} below:
\begin{itemize}
	\item  See Sisto's \markbox{941}{notes} \cite{Sisto_HHS} \markbox{942}{and} \markbox{943}{the} \markbox{944}{background} \markbox{945}{in} \markbox{946}{Casals-Ruiz--Hagen--Kazachkov} \cite{CRHK} \markbox{947}{for} \markbox{948}{an} \markbox{949}{introduction} \markbox{950}{to} \markbox{951}{HHSes.}  \markbox{952}{While} \markbox{953}{we} \markbox{954}{do} \markbox{955}{give} \markbox{956}{a} \markbox{957}{proof} \markbox{958}{of} \markbox{959}{the} \markbox{960}{harder} \markbox{961}{bound} \markbox{962}{of} \markbox{963}{the} \markbox{964}{Distance} \markbox{965}{Formula} \markbox{966}{in} \markbox{967}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF lower bound}, \markbox{968}{we} \markbox{969}{expect} \markbox{970}{the} \markbox{971}{reader} \markbox{972}{to} \markbox{973}{be} \markbox{974}{familiar} \markbox{975}{with} \markbox{976}{the} \markbox{977}{general} framework.
	\item  See \markbox{978}{Farb--Margalit} \cite{FM_primer} \markbox{979}{for} \markbox{980}{an} \markbox{981}{introduction} \markbox{982}{to} \markbox{983}{mapping} \markbox{984}{class} \markbox{985}{groups,} \markbox{986}{and} \cite[Section 11]{HHS_II} \markbox{987}{and} \markbox{988}{there} \markbox{989}{references} \markbox{990}{therein} \markbox{991}{(particular,} Masur--Minsky's \markbox{992}{work} \cite{MM99, MM00}) \markbox{993}{for} \markbox{994}{its} \markbox{995}{hierarchically} \markbox{996}{hyperbolic} \markbox{997}{structure.}  \markbox{998}{Similarly,} \markbox{999}{see} \markbox{1000}{Rafi} \cite{Rafi:combo, Rafi:hypteich} \markbox{1001}{and} \markbox{1002}{the} \markbox{1003}{author} \cite{Dur:augmented} \markbox{1004}{for} \markbox{1005}{the} \markbox{1006}{hierarchical} \markbox{1007}{structure} \markbox{1008}{on} Teichm\"uller \markbox{1009}{space} \markbox{1010}{with} \markbox{1011}{the} Teichm\"uller metric.
	\item For \markbox{1012}{an} \markbox{1013}{introduction} \markbox{1014}{to} \markbox{1015}{bicombings} \markbox{1016}{and} \markbox{1017}{semihyperbolicity,} \markbox{1018}{see} \markbox{1019}{Alonso--Bridson} \cite{AB95}.
	\item For \markbox{1020}{background} \markbox{1021}{on} \markbox{1022}{cube} \markbox{1023}{complexes,} \markbox{1024}{see} Sageev's \markbox{1025}{notes} \cite{Sageev:pcmi} \markbox{1026}{and} Schwer's \markbox{1027}{book} \cite{schwer2324cat}.
	\item  For \markbox{1028}{a} \markbox{1029}{discussion} \markbox{1030}{of} \markbox{1031}{cubical} \markbox{1032}{techniques} \markbox{1033}{in} \markbox{1034}{HHSes} \markbox{1035}{and} \markbox{1036}{related} \markbox{1037}{objects,} \markbox{1038}{see} Zalloum's \markbox{1039}{expository} article\cite{Zalloum_expo}.  
\end{itemize}

\subsection{Structure of the paper}

The \markbox{1040}{paper} \markbox{1041}{begins} \markbox{1042}{with} \markbox{1043}{a} \markbox{1044}{high-level} \markbox{1045}{discussion} \markbox{1046}{of} \markbox{1047}{the} \markbox{1048}{endgame} \markbox{1049}{for} \markbox{1050}{the} \markbox{1051}{bicombing} \markbox{1052}{construction} \markbox{1053}{using} \markbox{1054}{cubical} \markbox{1055}{approximation} \markbox{1056}{techniques.}  \markbox{1057}{In} \markbox{1058}{particular,} \markbox{1059}{in} \markbox{1060}{Section} \ref{sec:endgame}, \markbox{1061}{we} \markbox{1062}{will} \markbox{1063}{extract} \markbox{1064}{the} \markbox{1065}{key} \markbox{1066}{facts} \markbox{1067}{that} \markbox{1068}{we} \markbox{1069}{prove} \markbox{1070}{about} \markbox{1071}{colorable} \markbox{1072}{hierarchically} \markbox{1073}{hyperbolic} \markbox{1074}{spaces,} \markbox{1075}{namely} \markbox{1076}{the} \markbox{1077}{Stable} \markbox{1078}{Cubes} \markbox{1079}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes} \markbox{1080}{and} \markbox{1081}{Stable} \markbox{1082}{Moves} \markbox{1083}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}, \markbox{1084}{to} \markbox{1085}{build} \markbox{1086}{a} \markbox{1087}{bicombing} \markbox{1088}{on} \markbox{1089}{any} \markbox{1090}{metric} \markbox{1091}{space} \markbox{1092}{possessing} \markbox{1093}{the} \markbox{1094}{properties} \markbox{1095}{described} \markbox{1096}{in} \markbox{1097}{the} \markbox{1098}{former.}  \markbox{1099}{This} \markbox{1100}{includes} \markbox{1101}{the} \markbox{1102}{much} \markbox{1103}{simplified} \markbox{1104}{construction} \markbox{1105}{of} \markbox{1106}{the} \markbox{1107}{bicombing} \markbox{1108}{paths} \markbox{1109}{themselves} \markbox{1110}{via} \markbox{1111}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{1112}{paths} \markbox{1113}{in} \markbox{1114}{Subsection} \ref{sec:NR stability}.

With \markbox{1115}{this} \markbox{1116}{setup} \markbox{1117}{as} \markbox{1118}{motivation,} \markbox{1119}{we} \markbox{1120}{then} \markbox{1121}{proceed} \markbox{1122}{to} \markbox{1123}{describe} \markbox{1124}{the} \markbox{1125}{cubical} \markbox{1126}{model} \markbox{1127}{construction} \markbox{1128}{for} \markbox{1129}{HHSes.}  \markbox{1130}{Sections} \ref{sec:interval systems} \markbox{1131}{through} \ref{sec:cubulation} \markbox{1132}{explain} \markbox{1133}{the} \markbox{1134}{interval} \markbox{1135}{version} \markbox{1136}{of} \markbox{1137}{the} \markbox{1138}{cubical} \markbox{1139}{model} \markbox{1140}{theorem} \markbox{1141}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{1142}{The} \markbox{1143}{heart} \markbox{1144}{of} \markbox{1145}{the} \markbox{1146}{paper} \markbox{1147}{is} \markbox{1148}{in} \markbox{1149}{Sections} \ref{sec:controlling domains} \markbox{1150}{and} \ref{sec:stable intervals}, \markbox{1151}{where} \markbox{1152}{we} \markbox{1153}{explain} \markbox{1154}{how} \markbox{1155}{to} \markbox{1156}{build} \markbox{1157}{the} \markbox{1158}{stabilized} \markbox{1159}{family} \markbox{1160}{of} \markbox{1161}{intervals} \markbox{1162}{which} \markbox{1163}{serve} \markbox{1164}{as} \markbox{1165}{input,} \markbox{1166}{as} \markbox{1167}{well} \markbox{1168}{as} \markbox{1169}{in} \markbox{1170}{Section} \ref{sec:stable cubes}, \markbox{1171}{where} \markbox{1172}{we} \markbox{1173}{see} \markbox{1174}{how} \markbox{1175}{to} \markbox{1176}{plug} \markbox{1177}{this} \markbox{1178}{stabilized} \markbox{1179}{input} \markbox{1180}{into} \markbox{1181}{the} \markbox{1182}{cubulation} machine.

\markbox{1248}{Harry} \markbox{1249}{Petyt} \markbox{1250}{for} \markbox{1251}{giving} \markbox{1252}{many} \markbox{1253}{detailed} \markbox{1254}{comments} \markbox{1255}{which} \markbox{1256}{greatly} \markbox{1257}{improved} \markbox{1258}{the} \markbox{1259}{paper.}  \markbox{1260}{This} \markbox{1261}{paper} \markbox{1262}{was} \markbox{1263}{written} \markbox{1264}{for} \markbox{1265}{the} \markbox{1266}{conference} \markbox{1267}{proceedings} \markbox{1268}{and} \markbox{1269}{I} \markbox{1270}{appreciated} Thomas' \markbox{1271}{patience} \markbox{1272}{and} \markbox{1273}{encouragement} \markbox{1274}{while} \markbox{1275}{completing} \markbox{1276}{it.}  \markbox{1277}{Thanks} \markbox{1278}{also} \markbox{1279}{to} \markbox{1280}{the} \markbox{1281}{other} \markbox{1282}{speakers---Anne} \markbox{1283}{Lonjou,} \markbox{1284}{Marissa} \markbox{1285}{Kawehi} \markbox{1286}{Loving,} \markbox{1287}{and} \markbox{1288}{Jean-Pierre} \markbox{1289}{Mutanguha---for} \markbox{1290}{their} \markbox{1291}{outstanding} \markbox{1292}{minicourses.}  \markbox{1293}{Finally,} \markbox{1294}{thanks} \markbox{1295}{to} \markbox{1296}{the} \markbox{1297}{attendees} \markbox{1298}{of} \markbox{1299}{RivGGT23} \markbox{1300}{where} \markbox{1301}{my} \markbox{1302}{minicourse} \markbox{1303}{covered} \markbox{1304}{some} \markbox{1305}{of} \markbox{1306}{the} \markbox{1307}{material} \markbox{1308}{in} \markbox{1309}{this} \markbox{1310}{paper,} \markbox{1311}{and} \markbox{1312}{the} \markbox{1313}{UCR} \markbox{1314}{graduate} \markbox{1315}{students} \markbox{1316}{who} \markbox{1317}{attended} \markbox{1318}{my} \markbox{1319}{topics} \markbox{1320}{course} \markbox{1321}{on} \markbox{1322}{the} \markbox{1323}{construction} \markbox{1324}{in} \cite{Dur_infcube}.




\section{Beginning at the end} \label{sec:endgame}

The \markbox{1325}{purpose} \markbox{1326}{of} \markbox{1327}{this} \markbox{1328}{section} \markbox{1329}{is} \markbox{1330}{to} \markbox{1331}{prove} \markbox{1332}{the} \markbox{1333}{main} \markbox{1334}{consequence} \markbox{1335}{of} \markbox{1336}{the} \markbox{1337}{technical} \markbox{1338}{results} \markbox{1339}{we} \markbox{1340}{will} \markbox{1341}{spend} \markbox{1342}{the} \markbox{1343}{rest} \markbox{1344}{of} \markbox{1345}{the} \markbox{1346}{paper} \markbox{1347}{establishing.}  \markbox{1348}{That} \markbox{1349}{is,} \markbox{1350}{we} \markbox{1351}{will} \markbox{1352}{begin} \markbox{1353}{by} \markbox{1354}{explaining} \markbox{1355}{how} \markbox{1356}{the} \markbox{1357}{Stable} \markbox{1358}{Cubical} \markbox{1359}{Intervals} \markbox{1360}{Theorem} \ref{thmi:main}  \markbox{1361}{(Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}) \markbox{1362}{is} \markbox{1363}{enough} \markbox{1364}{to} \markbox{1365}{prove} \markbox{1366}{bicombability} \markbox{1367}{of} \markbox{1368}{the} \markbox{1369}{mapping} \markbox{1370}{class} \markbox{1371}{groups} \markbox{1372}{and} \markbox{1373}{colorably} \markbox{1374}{hierarchically} \markbox{1375}{hyperbolic} \markbox{1376}{spaces,} \markbox{1377}{more} generally.

We \markbox{1378}{begin} \markbox{1379}{with} \markbox{1380}{a} \markbox{1381}{brief} \markbox{1382}{primer} \markbox{1383}{on} \markbox{1384}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1385}{cube} \markbox{1386}{complexes} \markbox{1387}{and} \markbox{1388}{a} \markbox{1389}{discussion} \markbox{1390}{of} \markbox{1391}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{1392}{paths} \markbox{1393}{and} \markbox{1394}{their} \markbox{1395}{stability} \markbox{1396}{under} \markbox{1397}{hyperplane} \markbox{1398}{deletions.}  \markbox{1399}{In} \markbox{1400}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:stable cubes, early}, \markbox{1401}{we} \markbox{1402}{give} \markbox{1403}{a} \markbox{1404}{precise} \markbox{1405}{version} \markbox{1406}{of} \markbox{1407}{our} \markbox{1408}{stable} \markbox{1409}{cubulations} \markbox{1410}{result} \markbox{1411}{along} \markbox{1412}{with} \markbox{1413}{its} \markbox{1414}{associated} \markbox{1415}{path-building} \markbox{1416}{construction.}  \markbox{1417}{In} \markbox{1418}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:semihyp}, \markbox{1419}{we} \markbox{1420}{then} \markbox{1421}{define} \markbox{1422}{and} \markbox{1423}{discuss} \markbox{1424}{bicombings.}  \markbox{1425}{In} \markbox{1426}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:building bicombing}, \markbox{1427}{we} \markbox{1428}{explain} \markbox{1429}{how} \markbox{1430}{to} \markbox{1431}{put} \markbox{1432}{these} \markbox{1433}{parts} \markbox{1434}{together} \markbox{1435}{to} \markbox{1436}{give} \markbox{1437}{a} \markbox{1438}{bicombing} \markbox{1439}{for} \markbox{1440}{any} \markbox{1441}{metric} \markbox{1442}{space} \markbox{1443}{satisfying} \markbox{1444}{some} \markbox{1445}{version} \markbox{1446}{of} \markbox{1447}{our} \markbox{1448}{stable} \markbox{1449}{cubulations} setup.

\subsection{Wall spaces, cube complexes, and hyperplane deletions}\label{subsec:CCC background}


%@@@@Adapt to median setup

This \markbox{1450}{subsection} \markbox{1451}{includes} \markbox{1452}{a} \markbox{1453}{quick} \markbox{1454}{set} \markbox{1455}{of} \markbox{1456}{definitions} \markbox{1457}{and} \markbox{1458}{references} \markbox{1459}{for} \markbox{1460}{readers} \markbox{1461}{unfamiliar} \markbox{1462}{with} \markbox{1463}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1464}{cube} complexes.

Our \markbox{1465}{approach} \markbox{1466}{here} \markbox{1467}{follows} \markbox{1468}{most} \markbox{1469}{closely} Roller's \markbox{1470}{approach} \cite{Roller} \markbox{1471}{to} Sageev's \markbox{1472}{cubulation} \markbox{1473}{machine} \cite{Sageev:cubulation}, \markbox{1474}{which} \markbox{1475}{uses} \markbox{1476}{the} \markbox{1477}{notion} \markbox{1478}{of} \markbox{1479}{wall-space} \markbox{1480}{as} \markbox{1481}{introduced} \markbox{1482}{by} \markbox{1483}{Haglund-Paulin} \cite{HP_wallspace}.  \markbox{1484}{See} Sageev's \markbox{1485}{notes} \cite{Sageev:pcmi}, \markbox{1486}{as} \markbox{1487}{well} \markbox{1488}{as} \markbox{1489}{Hruska-Wise} \cite{HW_CCC}, \markbox{1490}{for} \markbox{1491}{excellent} \markbox{1492}{expositions} \markbox{1493}{on} \markbox{1494}{this} \markbox{1495}{subject.}  \markbox{1496}{We} \markbox{1497}{note} \markbox{1498}{that} \markbox{1499}{we} \markbox{1500}{will} \markbox{1501}{later} \markbox{1502}{take} \markbox{1503}{an} \markbox{1504}{approach} \markbox{1505}{using} \markbox{1506}{medians} \markbox{1507}{in} \markbox{1508}{Section} \ref{sec:cubulation}.  

A \emph{cube complex} \markbox{1509}{is} \markbox{1510}{a} \markbox{1511}{CW} \markbox{1512}{complex} \markbox{1513}{obtained} \markbox{1514}{by} \markbox{1515}{gluing} \markbox{1516}{a} \markbox{1517}{collection} \markbox{1518}{of} \markbox{1519}{unit} \markbox{1520}{Euclidean} \markbox{1521}{cubes} \markbox{1522}{of} \markbox{1523}{various} \markbox{1524}{dimensions} \markbox{1525}{along} \markbox{1526}{their} \markbox{1527}{faces} \markbox{1528}{by} \markbox{1529}{a} \markbox{1530}{collection} \markbox{1531}{of} \markbox{1532}{(Euclidean)} \markbox{1533}{isometries.}  \markbox{1534}{A} \markbox{1535}{cube} \markbox{1536}{complex} \markbox{m1537}{$\Sigma$} \markbox{1538}{is} \emph{non-positively curved} \markbox{1539}{when} \markbox{1540}{it} \markbox{1541}{satisfies} Gromov's \markbox{1542}{link} \markbox{1543}{condition,} \markbox{1544}{and} \markbox{1545}{every} \markbox{1546}{non-positively} \markbox{1547}{curved} \markbox{1548}{simply} \markbox{1549}{connected} \markbox{1550}{cube} \markbox{1551}{complex} \markbox{1552}{admits} \markbox{1553}{a} \markbox{1554}{unique} \markbox{1555}{CAT(0)} metric.

A \emph{hyperplane} \markbox{1556}{in} \markbox{1557}{a} \markbox{1558}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1559}{cube} \markbox{1560}{complex} \markbox{m1561}{$\Sigma$} \markbox{1562}{is} \markbox{1563}{a} \markbox{1564}{connected} \markbox{1565}{subspace} \markbox{1566}{whose} \markbox{1567}{intersection} \markbox{1568}{with} \markbox{1569}{each} \markbox{1570}{cube} \markbox{m1571}{$\sigma = [0,1]^{n}$} \markbox{1572}{is} \markbox{1573}{either} \markbox{m1574}{$\emptyset$} \markbox{1575}{or} \markbox{1576}{the} \markbox{1577}{subspace} \markbox{1578}{obtained} \markbox{1579}{by} \markbox{1580}{restricting} \markbox{1581}{exactly} \markbox{1582}{one} \markbox{1583}{coordinate} \markbox{1584}{to} \markbox{m1585}{$\frac{1}{2}$}.  \markbox{1586}{In} \markbox{1587}{particular,} \markbox{1588}{every} \markbox{1589}{hyperplane} \markbox{1590}{partitions} \markbox{m1591}{$\Sigma$}.  \markbox{1592}{This} \markbox{1593}{motivates} \markbox{1594}{the} \markbox{1595}{definition} \markbox{1596}{of} \markbox{1597}{a} \markbox{1598}{half-spaces} \markbox{1599}{and} \markbox{1600}{pocsets,} \markbox{1601}{following} \markbox{1602}{Roller} \cite{Roller}.

\begin{definition}[Pocset]\label{defn:pocset}
Let \markbox{m1603}{$(\Sigma,<)$} \markbox{1604}{be} \markbox{1605}{a} \markbox{1606}{partially-ordered} \markbox{1607}{set.}  \markbox{1608}{A} \emph{pocset} \markbox{1609}{structure} \markbox{1610}{on} \markbox{m1611}{$\Sigma$} \markbox{1612}{has} \markbox{1613}{the} \markbox{1614}{additional} \markbox{1615}{structure} \markbox{1616}{of} \markbox{1617}{an} \markbox{1618}{order-reversing} \markbox{1619}{involution} \markbox{m1620}{$A \mapsto A^*$} satisfying
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m1621}{$A \neq A^*$} \markbox{1622}{and} \markbox{m1623}{$A, A^*$} \markbox{1624}{are} \markbox{m1625}{$<$}-incomparable;
\item \markbox{m1626}{$A < B \implies B^* < A^*$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item Given \markbox{m1627}{$A<B$}, \markbox{1628}{the} \emph{interval} \markbox{1629}{between} \markbox{m1630}{$A$} \markbox{1631}{and} \markbox{m1632}{$B$} \markbox{1633}{is} \markbox{m1634}{$[A,B] = \{C|A<C<B\}$}.
\item The \markbox{1635}{pocset} \markbox{m1636}{$(\Sigma,<)$} \markbox{1637}{is} \emph{locally finite} \markbox{1638}{if} \markbox{1639}{every} \markbox{1640}{interval} \markbox{1641}{is} finite.
\item Given \markbox{m1642}{$A,B \in \Sigma$}, \markbox{1643}{we} \markbox{1644}{say} \markbox{m1645}{$A$} \markbox{1646}{is} \emph{transverse} \markbox{1647}{to} \markbox{m1648}{$B$} \markbox{1649}{if} \markbox{1650}{none} \markbox{1651}{of} \markbox{m1652}{$A<B, A<B^*, A^*<B, A^*<B^*$} \markbox{1653}{holds.}  \markbox{1654}{The} \markbox{1655}{pocset} \markbox{m1656}{$(\Sigma,<)$} \markbox{1657}{has} \emph{finite width} \markbox{1658}{if} \markbox{1659}{the} \markbox{1660}{maximal} \markbox{1661}{size} \markbox{1662}{of} \markbox{1663}{a} \markbox{1664}{pairwise} \markbox{1665}{transverse} \markbox{1666}{subset} \markbox{1667}{is} finite.

\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

In \markbox{1668}{a} \markbox{1669}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1670}{cube} \markbox{1671}{complex,} \markbox{1672}{every} \markbox{1673}{vertex} \markbox{1674}{is} \markbox{1675}{contained} \markbox{1676}{in} \markbox{1677}{exactly} \markbox{1678}{one} \markbox{1679}{half-space} \markbox{1680}{associated} \markbox{1681}{to} \markbox{1682}{each} \markbox{1683}{hyperplane.}  \markbox{1684}{The} \markbox{1685}{following} \markbox{1686}{notion} \markbox{1687}{abstracts} \markbox{1688}{the} \markbox{1689}{combinatorial} \markbox{1690}{structure} \markbox{1691}{of} \markbox{1692}{such} \markbox{1693}{a} \markbox{1694}{family} \markbox{1695}{of} half-spaces:

\begin{definition}[Ultrafilters \markbox{1696}{and} \markbox{1697}{the} DCC]\label{defn:ultrafilter}
Given \markbox{1698}{a} \markbox{1699}{locally} \markbox{1700}{finite} \markbox{1701}{pocset} \markbox{m1702}{$(\Sigma, <)$}, \markbox{1703}{an} \emph{ultrafilter} \markbox{m1704}{$\alpha$} \markbox{1705}{on} \markbox{m1706}{$\Sigma$} \markbox{1707}{is} \markbox{1708}{a} \markbox{1709}{subset} \markbox{1710}{of} \markbox{m1711}{$\Sigma$} satisfying
\begin{enumerate}
\item (Choice) \markbox{1712}{Exactly} \markbox{1713}{one} \markbox{1714}{element} \markbox{1715}{of} \markbox{1716}{each} \markbox{1717}{pair} \markbox{m1718}{$\{A,A^*\}$} \markbox{1719}{is} \markbox{1720}{an} \markbox{1721}{element} \markbox{1722}{of} \markbox{m1723}{$\alpha$};
\item (Consistency) \markbox{m1724}{$A \in \alpha$} \markbox{1725}{and} \markbox{m1726}{$A< B \implies B \in \alpha$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item An \markbox{1727}{ultrafilter} \markbox{m1728}{$\alpha$} \markbox{1729}{satisfies} \markbox{1730}{the} \emph{descending chain condition} \markbox{1731}{(DCC)} \markbox{1732}{if} \markbox{1733}{every} \markbox{1734}{descending} \markbox{1735}{chain} \markbox{1736}{of} \markbox{1737}{elements} terminates.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

We \markbox{1738}{can} \markbox{1739}{now} \markbox{1740}{define} \markbox{1741}{the} \markbox{1742}{dual} \markbox{1743}{cube} \markbox{1744}{complex} \markbox{1745}{to} \markbox{1746}{a} \markbox{1747}{locally} \markbox{1748}{finite,} \markbox{1749}{discrete,} \markbox{1750}{finite-width} pocset:

\begin{definition}[Dual \markbox{1751}{cube} complex]\label{defn:dual CCC}
Given \markbox{1752}{a} \markbox{1753}{locally} \markbox{1754}{finite,} \markbox{1755}{discrete,} \markbox{1756}{finite-width} \markbox{1757}{pocset} \markbox{m1758}{$(\Sigma,<)$}, \markbox{1759}{we} \markbox{1760}{define} \markbox{1761}{a} \markbox{1762}{CW} \markbox{1763}{complex} \markbox{m1764}{$X(\Sigma)$} \markbox{1765}{as} follows:
\begin{enumerate}
\item The \markbox{m1766}{$0$}-cells \markbox{m1767}{$X^{(0)}$} \markbox{1768}{of} \markbox{m1769}{$X$} \markbox{1770}{are} \markbox{1771}{the} \markbox{1772}{DCC} \markbox{1773}{ultrafilters} \markbox{1774}{on} \markbox{m1775}{$(\Sigma, <)$}.
\item Two \markbox{m1776}{$0$}-cells \markbox{m1777}{$\alpha, \beta$} \markbox{1778}{are} \markbox{1779}{connected} \markbox{1780}{by} \markbox{1781}{an} \markbox{1782}{edge} \markbox{1783}{in} \markbox{m1784}{$X^{(1)}$} \markbox{1785}{if} \markbox{1786}{and} \markbox{1787}{only} \markbox{1788}{if} \markbox{m1789}{$|\alpha \triangle \beta| = 2$}, \markbox{1790}{i.e.} \markbox{m1791}{$\alpha = (\beta - \{A\}) \cup \{A^*\}$} \markbox{1792}{for} \markbox{1793}{some} \markbox{m1794}{$A \in \Sigma$}.
\item Define \markbox{m1795}{$X^{(n)}$} \markbox{1796}{inductively} \markbox{1797}{by} \markbox{1798}{adding} \markbox{1799}{an} \markbox{m1800}{$n$}-cube \markbox{1801}{whenever} \markbox{1802}{the} \markbox{1803}{boundary} \markbox{1804}{of} \markbox{1805}{one} \markbox{1806}{appears} \markbox{1807}{in} \markbox{1808}{the} \markbox{m1809}{$X^{(n-1)}$}-skeleton.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}


The \markbox{1810}{following} \markbox{1811}{is} \markbox{1812}{a} \markbox{1813}{theorem} \markbox{1814}{of} \markbox{1815}{Roller} \cite{Roller}, \markbox{1816}{building} \markbox{1817}{on} \markbox{1818}{Sageev} \cite{Sageev:cubulation}:

\begin{theorem}[Sageev's machine]\label{thm:Sageev}
Given \markbox{1819}{a} \markbox{1820}{locally} \markbox{1821}{finite,} \markbox{1822}{finite-width} \markbox{1823}{pocset} \markbox{m1824}{$(\Sigma,<)$}, \markbox{1825}{the} \markbox{1826}{CW} \markbox{1827}{complex} \markbox{m1828}{$X(\Sigma)$} \markbox{1829}{is} \markbox{1830}{a} \markbox{1831}{finite} \markbox{1832}{dimensional} \markbox{1833}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1834}{cube} \markbox{1835}{complex,} \markbox{1836}{where} \markbox{1837}{the} \markbox{1838}{dimension} \markbox{1839}{is} \markbox{1840}{equal} \markbox{1841}{to} \markbox{1842}{the} \markbox{1843}{width} \markbox{1844}{of} \markbox{m1845}{$(\Sigma, <)$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item We \markbox{1846}{call} \markbox{m1847}{$X(\Sigma)$} \markbox{1848}{the} \emph{dual cube complex} \markbox{1849}{to} \markbox{m1850}{$(\Sigma, <)$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{theorem}

We \markbox{1851}{note} \markbox{1852}{that} \markbox{1853}{the} \markbox{1854}{dual} \markbox{1855}{cube} \markbox{1856}{complex} \markbox{1857}{to} \markbox{1858}{the} \markbox{1859}{pocset} \markbox{1860}{coming} \markbox{1861}{from} \markbox{1862}{the} \markbox{1863}{hyperplanes} \markbox{1864}{of} \markbox{1865}{a} \markbox{1866}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1867}{cube} \markbox{1868}{complex} \markbox{1869}{is} \markbox{1870}{(isomorphic} \markbox{1871}{to)} \markbox{1872}{that} \markbox{1873}{cube} complex.

The \markbox{1874}{following} \markbox{1875}{lemma} \markbox{1876}{is} \markbox{1877}{useful} \markbox{1878}{for} \markbox{1879}{obtaining} \markbox{1880}{isomorphisms} \markbox{1881}{between} \markbox{1882}{cube} \markbox{1883}{complexes} \markbox{1884}{whose} \markbox{1885}{wall-spaces} \markbox{1886}{we} \markbox{1887}{can} \markbox{1888}{directly} \markbox{1889}{compare.}  \markbox{1890}{Its} \markbox{1891}{proof} \markbox{1892}{is} \markbox{1893}{an} \markbox{1894}{exercise} \markbox{1895}{in} \markbox{1896}{the} \markbox{1897}{basics} \markbox{1898}{of} \markbox{1899}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1900}{cube} \markbox{1901}{complexes} \markbox{1902}{which} \markbox{1903}{we} \markbox{1904}{leave} \markbox{1905}{to} \markbox{1906}{the} reader.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:halfspaces_bijection}
 \markbox{1907}{Let} \markbox{m1908}{$\calW$}, \markbox{m1909}{$\calW'$} \markbox{1910}{be} \markbox{1911}{wallspaces,} \markbox{1912}{and} \markbox{1913}{let} \markbox{m1914}{$\iota:\calH_{\calW} \to \calH_{\calW'}$} \markbox{1915}{be} \markbox{1916}{a} \markbox{1917}{bijection} \markbox{1918}{of} \markbox{1919}{their} \markbox{1920}{half-spaces,} \markbox{1921}{which} preserves
 \markbox{1922}{complements} \markbox{1923}{and} \markbox{1924}{disjointness.}  \markbox{1925}{Then} \markbox{m1926}{$\iota$} \markbox{1927}{induces} \markbox{1928}{a} \markbox{1929}{cubical} isomorphism
\markbox{m1930}{$h:\calD(\calW)\to \calD(\calW')$}
between \markbox{1931}{the} \markbox{1932}{corresponding} \markbox{1933}{dual} \markbox{1934}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1935}{cube} complexes.
\end{lemma}

Finally, \markbox{1936}{in} \markbox{1937}{our} \markbox{1938}{stable} \markbox{1939}{cubulations} \markbox{1940}{theorem,} \markbox{1941}{we} \markbox{1942}{will} \markbox{1943}{want} \markbox{1944}{to} \markbox{1945}{realize} \markbox{1946}{maps} \markbox{1947}{between} \markbox{1948}{certain} \markbox{1949}{cube} \markbox{1950}{complexes} \markbox{1951}{as} \markbox{1952}{a} \markbox{1953}{sort} \markbox{1954}{of} \markbox{1955}{collapsing} \markbox{1956}{of} \markbox{1957}{a} \markbox{1958}{controlled} \markbox{1959}{piece} \markbox{1960}{of} \markbox{1961}{their} \markbox{1962}{combinatorial} \markbox{1963}{data.}  \markbox{1964}{The} \markbox{1965}{right} \markbox{1966}{notion} \markbox{1967}{here} \markbox{1968}{is} \markbox{1969}{of} \markbox{1970}{a} \emph{hyperplane deletion}.  \markbox{1971}{The} \markbox{1972}{motivating} \markbox{1973}{example} \markbox{1974}{is} \markbox{1975}{where} \markbox{1976}{one} \markbox{1977}{has} \markbox{1978}{a} \markbox{1979}{wall-space} \markbox{m1980}{$\calW(\calH)$} \markbox{1981}{on} \markbox{1982}{some} \markbox{1983}{set} \markbox{1984}{of} \markbox{1985}{walls} \markbox{m1986}{$\calH$}, \markbox{1987}{and} \markbox{1988}{one} \markbox{1989}{removes} \markbox{1990}{some} \markbox{1991}{collection} \markbox{1992}{of} \markbox{1993}{the} \markbox{1994}{walls} \markbox{m1995}{$\calH - \calG$}, \markbox{1996}{to} \markbox{1997}{obtain} \markbox{1998}{a} \emph{restriction map} \markbox{m1999}{$\calD(\calW(\calH)) \to \calD(\calW(\calH- \calG))$} \markbox{2000}{between} \markbox{2001}{their} \markbox{2002}{dual} \markbox{2003}{cube} \markbox{2004}{complexes} \markbox{2005}{in} \markbox{2006}{the} \markbox{2007}{sense} \markbox{2008}{of} \cite{CapraceSageev}.  \markbox{2009}{This} \markbox{2010}{map} \markbox{2011}{collapses} \markbox{2012}{the} \markbox{2013}{carriers} \markbox{2014}{of} \markbox{2015}{the} \markbox{2016}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2017}{in} \markbox{m2018}{$\calG$} \markbox{2019}{(recall} \markbox{2020}{that} \markbox{2021}{a} \markbox{2022}{carrier} \markbox{2023}{of} \markbox{2024}{a} \markbox{2025}{hyperplane} \markbox{m2026}{$\hh$} \markbox{2027}{is} \markbox{2028}{naturally} \markbox{2029}{isomorphic} \markbox{2030}{to} \markbox{m2031}{$\hh \times [0,1]$}).










\subsection{Stable cubes and stable moves}\label{subsec:stable cubes, early}

We \markbox{2032}{will} \markbox{2033}{prove} \markbox{2034}{Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp} \markbox{2035}{in} \markbox{2036}{an} \markbox{2037}{ostensibly} \markbox{2038}{more} \markbox{2039}{general} \markbox{2040}{framework} \markbox{2041}{than} \markbox{2042}{that} \markbox{2043}{of} \markbox{2044}{(colorable)} HHSes\footnote{We actually suspect that coarse median spaces satisfying some version of the property in Definition \ref{defn:stable cubes} will be HHSes, though it is unclear to us what exactly the right property is, e.g. perhaps a factor system in the sense of \cite{HHS_I}.}.  \markbox{2045}{That} \markbox{2046}{is,} \markbox{2047}{we} \markbox{2048}{only} \markbox{2049}{need} \markbox{2050}{a} \markbox{2051}{metric} \markbox{2052}{space} \markbox{2053}{which} \markbox{2054}{satisfies} \markbox{2055}{the} \markbox{2056}{following} \markbox{2057}{definitions.}  \markbox{2058}{The} \markbox{2059}{first} \markbox{2060}{is} \markbox{2061}{effectively} \markbox{2062}{a} \markbox{2063}{weak} \markbox{2064}{two-point} \markbox{2065}{version} \markbox{2066}{of} \markbox{2067}{the} \markbox{2068}{cubical} \markbox{2069}{model} \markbox{2070}{property} \markbox{2071}{for} \markbox{2072}{HHSes} \markbox{2073}{from} \cite{HHS_quasi}, \markbox{2074}{proven} \markbox{2075}{in} \markbox{2076}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC} \markbox{2077}{in} \markbox{2078}{this} paper.

\begin{definition}[Weak \markbox{2079}{local} quasi-cubicality]\label{defn:lqc pair}

Let \markbox{m2080}{$X$} \markbox{2081}{be} \markbox{2082}{a} \markbox{2083}{metric} \markbox{2084}{space.}  \markbox{2085}{A} \markbox{m2086}{$B_0$}-\emph{cubical model} \markbox{2087}{for} \markbox{2088}{a} \markbox{2089}{pair} \markbox{m2090}{$a,b \in X$} \markbox{2091}{is} \markbox{2092}{a} \markbox{2093}{CAT(0)} \markbox{2094}{cube} \markbox{2095}{complex} \markbox{m2096}{$\calQ$} \markbox{2097}{of} \markbox{2098}{dimension} \markbox{2099}{at} \markbox{2100}{most} \markbox{m2101}{$B_0$} \markbox{2102}{satisfying} \markbox{2103}{the} following:
\begin{enumerate}
\item There \markbox{2104}{is} \markbox{2105}{a} \markbox{m2106}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{2107}{embedding} \markbox{m2108}{$\hO:\calQ \to X$} \markbox{2109}{(the} \emph{cubical model map}),
\item There \markbox{2110}{are} \markbox{2111}{two} \emph{distinguished vertices} \markbox{m2112}{$\ha,\hb \in \calQ$} \markbox{2113}{so} \markbox{2114}{that} \markbox{2115}{any} \markbox{m2116}{$\ell^{\infty}$}-geodesic \markbox{m2117}{$\gamma \subset \calQ$} \markbox{2118}{between} \markbox{m2119}{$\ha,\hb$} \markbox{2120}{is} \markbox{2121}{sent} \markbox{2122}{to} \markbox{2123}{a} \markbox{m2124}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-geodesic \markbox{m2125}{$\hO(\gamma) \subset X$} \markbox{2126}{between} \markbox{m2127}{$a,b$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item We \markbox{2128}{say} \markbox{m2129}{$X$} \markbox{2130}{is} \markbox{m2131}{$B_0$}-\emph{weakly locally quasi-cubical} \markbox{2132}{(wLQC)} \markbox{2133}{if} \markbox{2134}{there} \markbox{2135}{exists} \markbox{m2136}{$B_0>0$} \markbox{2137}{so} \markbox{2138}{that} \markbox{2139}{any} \markbox{2140}{pair} \markbox{m2141}{$a,b\in X$} \markbox{2142}{admits} \markbox{2143}{a} \markbox{m2144}{$B_0$}-cubical model.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

 \markbox{2145}{While} \markbox{2146}{CAT(0)} \markbox{2147}{cube} \markbox{2148}{complexes} \markbox{2149}{have} \markbox{2150}{many} \markbox{2151}{standard} \markbox{2152}{metrics} \markbox{2153}{(all} \markbox{2154}{of} \markbox{2155}{which} \markbox{2156}{are} \markbox{2157}{quasi-isometric),} \markbox{2158}{the} \markbox{2159}{convenient} \markbox{2160}{one} \markbox{2161}{for} \markbox{2162}{us} \markbox{2163}{is} \markbox{2164}{the} \markbox{m2165}{$\ell^{\infty}$}-metric, \markbox{2166}{which,} \markbox{2167}{for} \markbox{2168}{vertices} \markbox{2169}{in} \markbox{2170}{a} \markbox{2171}{single} \markbox{2172}{unit} \markbox{2173}{cube,} \markbox{2174}{is} \markbox{2175}{just} \markbox{2176}{the} \markbox{m2177}{$\sup$}-metric. 

The \markbox{2178}{next} \markbox{2179}{definition} \markbox{2180}{is} \markbox{2181}{extracted} \markbox{2182}{from} \markbox{2183}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes} \markbox{2184}{below.}  \markbox{2185}{This} \markbox{2186}{property} \markbox{2187}{holds} \markbox{2188}{for} \markbox{2189}{colorable} \markbox{2190}{hierarchically} \markbox{2191}{hyperbolic} \markbox{2192}{spaces,} \markbox{2193}{e.g.,} \markbox{2194}{the} \markbox{2195}{mapping} \markbox{2196}{class} \markbox{2197}{group} \markbox{2198}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{2199}{space;} \markbox{2200}{see} \cite[Theorem 4.1]{DMS_bary} \markbox{2201}{for} \markbox{2202}{the} \markbox{2203}{original,} \markbox{2204}{more} \markbox{2205}{general} \markbox{2206}{version,} \markbox{2207}{and} \cite[Theorem 9.1]{DMS_FJ} \markbox{2208}{for} \markbox{2209}{the} \markbox{2210}{state-of-the-art.}  \markbox{2211}{Part} \markbox{2212}{of} \markbox{2213}{our} \markbox{2214}{purpose} \markbox{2215}{here} \markbox{2216}{for} \markbox{2217}{extracting} \markbox{2218}{it} \markbox{2219}{from} \markbox{2220}{the} \markbox{2221}{HHS} \markbox{2222}{setting} \markbox{2223}{is} \markbox{2224}{to} \markbox{2225}{highlight} \markbox{2226}{the} \markbox{2227}{structure} \markbox{2228}{of} \markbox{2229}{the} endgame.


\begin{definition}[Stable \markbox{2230}{weak} \markbox{2231}{local} quasicubicality]\label{defn:stable cubes}
We \markbox{2232}{say} \markbox{2233}{that} \markbox{2234}{a} \markbox{2235}{metric} \markbox{2236}{space} \markbox{m2237}{$X$} \markbox{2238}{is} \emph{$B_0$-stably wLQC} \markbox{2239}{if} \markbox{2240}{there} \markbox{2241}{is} \markbox{2242}{a} \markbox{m2243}{$B_0$} \markbox{2244}{so} \markbox{2245}{that} \markbox{2246}{the} \markbox{2247}{following} \markbox{2248}{holds:}  

\begin{itemize}
\item For \markbox{2249}{any} \markbox{m2250}{$a,b, a',b' \in X$} \markbox{2251}{with} \markbox{m2252}{$d_X(a,a') \leq 1$} \markbox{2253}{and} \markbox{m2254}{$d_X(b,b')\leq 1$}, \markbox{2255}{there} \markbox{2256}{exist} \markbox{m2257}{$B_0$}-cubical \markbox{2258}{models} \markbox{m2259}{$\calQ, \calQ_0$} \markbox{2260}{and} \markbox{m2261}{$\calQ',\calQ'_0$} \markbox{2262}{for} \markbox{m2263}{$a,b$} \markbox{2264}{and} \markbox{m2265}{$a',b'$} \markbox{2266}{so} \markbox{2267}{that} \markbox{2268}{the} \markbox{2269}{following} \markbox{2270}{diagram} \markbox{2271}{commutes} \markbox{2272}{up} \markbox{2273}{to} \markbox{2274}{additive} \markbox{2275}{error} \markbox{m2276}{$B_0$}:
\begin{equation}\label{Phi diagram, early}
  \begin{tikzcd}
   \calQ \arrow[ddrr,"\hO", bend left=40] \arrow[dr,"\Delta_0 \hspace{.075in}" left] &  \\
    &\calQ_{0} \arrow[dr,"\hO_0 \hspace{.2in}" below]\arrow[dd, "I_0"] \\
    & & X\\
    & \calQ'_{0} \arrow[ur,"\hO'_0"] \\
    \calQ'\arrow[uurr,"\hspace{.2in} \vspace{.1in} \hO'" below, bend right=40] \arrow[ur,"\Delta'_0"] & \\
  \end{tikzcd}
  \end{equation}
 \item In \markbox{2277}{the} above,
  \begin{enumerate}
  \item  \markbox{m2278}{$\hO, \hO_0, \hO', \hO'_0$} \markbox{2279}{are} \markbox{2280}{cubical} \markbox{2281}{model} \markbox{2282}{maps} \markbox{2283}{and} \markbox{2284}{hence} \markbox{m2285}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-isometric embeddings,
  \item the \markbox{2286}{map} \markbox{m2287}{$I_0$} \markbox{2288}{is} \markbox{2289}{a} \markbox{2290}{cubical} isomorphism,
  \item the \markbox{2291}{maps} \markbox{m2292}{$\Delta_0, \Delta'_0$} \markbox{2293}{are} \markbox{2294}{induced} \markbox{2295}{by} \markbox{2296}{deleting} \markbox{2297}{at} \markbox{2298}{most} \markbox{m2299}{$B_0$}-many \markbox{2300}{hyperplanes,} and
  \item \markbox{m2301}{$\Delta_0, \Delta'_0$} \markbox{2302}{take} \markbox{2303}{the} \markbox{2304}{distinguished} \markbox{2305}{vertices} \markbox{2306}{associated} \markbox{2307}{to} \markbox{m2308}{$a,b$} \markbox{2309}{and} \markbox{m2310}{$a',b'$} \markbox{2311}{in} \markbox{m2312}{$\calQ,\calQ'$} \markbox{2313}{to} \markbox{2314}{those} \markbox{2315}{in} \markbox{m2316}{$\calQ_0,\calQ'_0$}, respectively.
  \end{enumerate}
  \end{itemize}
\end{definition}

Requirement \markbox{2317}{(4)} \markbox{2318}{says} \markbox{2319}{that} \markbox{2320}{the} \markbox{2321}{way} \markbox{2322}{that} \markbox{2323}{the} \markbox{2324}{cube} \markbox{2325}{complexes} \markbox{m2326}{$\calQ,\calQ_0$} \markbox{2327}{model} \markbox{m2328}{$a,b$} \markbox{2329}{align,} \markbox{2330}{and} \markbox{2331}{similarly} \markbox{2332}{for} \markbox{m2333}{$\calQ', \calQ'_0$} \markbox{2334}{and} \markbox{m2335}{$a',b'$}.  \markbox{2336}{Note} \markbox{2337}{that} \markbox{2338}{if} \markbox{m2339}{$X$} \markbox{2340}{satisfies} \markbox{2341}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes} \markbox{2342}{then} \markbox{2343}{it} \markbox{2344}{satisfies} \markbox{2345}{Definition} \ref{defn:lqc pair}.  

\begin{remark}
Theorems \ref{thm:Q CCC} \markbox{2346}{and} \ref{thm:stable cubes} \markbox{2347}{actually} \markbox{2348}{provide} \markbox{2349}{a} \markbox{2350}{lot} \markbox{2351}{more} \markbox{2352}{information} \markbox{2353}{about} \markbox{2354}{these} \markbox{2355}{cubical} \markbox{2356}{models.}  \markbox{2357}{In} \markbox{2358}{particular,} \markbox{2359}{if} \markbox{m2360}{$\calX$} \markbox{2361}{is} \markbox{2362}{an} \markbox{2363}{HHS} \markbox{2364}{and} \markbox{m2365}{$a,b \in \calX$}, \markbox{2366}{then} \markbox{2367}{the} \markbox{2368}{cube} \markbox{2369}{complexes} \markbox{m2370}{$\calQ$} \markbox{2371}{and} \markbox{m2372}{$\calQ_0$} \markbox{2373}{above} \markbox{2374}{model} \markbox{2375}{the} \emph{hierarchical hull} \markbox{2376}{of} \markbox{m2377}{$a,b$} \markbox{2378}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hier hull}), \markbox{2379}{which} \markbox{2380}{is} \markbox{2381}{a} \markbox{2382}{coarsely} \markbox{2383}{convex} \markbox{2384}{subspace} \markbox{2385}{which} \markbox{2386}{encodes} \markbox{2387}{the} \markbox{2388}{hierarchical} \markbox{2389}{geometry} \markbox{2390}{between} \markbox{m2391}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{2392}{Moreover,} \markbox{2393}{the} \markbox{2394}{combinatorial} \markbox{2395}{geometry} \markbox{2396}{of} \markbox{2397}{the} \markbox{2398}{cube} \markbox{2399}{complex} \markbox{2400}{encodes} \markbox{2401}{essentially} \markbox{2402}{all} \markbox{2403}{of} \markbox{2404}{this} \markbox{2405}{hierarchical} \markbox{2406}{data.}  \markbox{2407}{See} \markbox{2408}{the} \markbox{2409}{introduction} \markbox{2410}{of} \cite{Dur_infcube} \markbox{2411}{for} \markbox{2412}{a} \markbox{2413}{detailed} discussion.
\end{remark}

\subsection{Stable moves}\label{sec:NR stability}

In \markbox{2414}{this} \markbox{2415}{subsection,} \markbox{2416}{we} \markbox{2417}{establish} \markbox{2418}{the} \markbox{2419}{key} \markbox{2420}{path-building} \markbox{2421}{portion} \markbox{2422}{of} \markbox{2423}{our} \markbox{2424}{bicombing} \markbox{2425}{construction,} \markbox{2426}{namely} \markbox{2427}{the} \markbox{2428}{Stable} \markbox{2429}{Moves} \markbox{2430}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}.  \markbox{2431}{This} \markbox{2432}{involves} \markbox{2433}{proving} \markbox{2434}{that} \markbox{2435}{a} \markbox{2436}{well-studied} \markbox{2437}{family} \markbox{2438}{of} \markbox{2439}{paths} \markbox{2440}{in} \markbox{2441}{a} \markbox{2442}{cube} \markbox{2443}{complex} \markbox{2444}{due} \markbox{2445}{to} \markbox{2446}{Niblo--Reeves} \cite{NibloReeves} \markbox{2447}{behaves} \markbox{2448}{well} \markbox{2449}{under} \markbox{2450}{hyperplane} \markbox{2451}{deletion.}  \markbox{2452}{These} \markbox{2453}{paths} \markbox{2454}{were} \markbox{2455}{at} \markbox{2456}{the} \markbox{2457}{center} \markbox{2458}{of} \markbox{2459}{their} \markbox{2460}{construction} \markbox{2461}{of} \markbox{2462}{a} \markbox{2463}{biautomatic} \markbox{2464}{structure} \markbox{2465}{on} \markbox{2466}{an} \markbox{2467}{CAT(0)} \markbox{2468}{cubical} \markbox{2469}{group,} \markbox{2470}{and} \markbox{2471}{so} \markbox{2472}{it} \markbox{2473}{is} \markbox{2474}{quite} \markbox{2475}{agreeable} \markbox{2476}{that} \markbox{2477}{they} \markbox{2478}{play} \markbox{2479}{a} \markbox{2480}{central} \markbox{2481}{role} \markbox{2482}{in} \markbox{2483}{our} \markbox{2484}{construction} \markbox{2485}{of} \markbox{2486}{a} \markbox{2487}{bicombing} \markbox{2488}{for} \markbox{2489}{our} \markbox{2490}{sort} \markbox{2491}{of} \markbox{2492}{quasi-cubical} \markbox{2493}{spaces.}  \markbox{2494}{While} \markbox{2495}{we} \markbox{2496}{have} \markbox{2497}{maintained} \markbox{2498}{some} \markbox{2499}{of} \markbox{2500}{the} \markbox{2501}{structure} \markbox{2502}{and} \markbox{2503}{terminology} \markbox{2504}{from} \markbox{2505}{our} \markbox{2506}{work} \markbox{2507}{with} \markbox{2508}{Minsky} \markbox{2509}{and} \markbox{2510}{Sisto} \markbox{2511}{in} \cite[Section 5]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{2512}{our} \markbox{2513}{limited} \markbox{2514}{setting} \markbox{2515}{allows} \markbox{2516}{for} \markbox{2517}{a} \markbox{2518}{much} \markbox{2519}{simpler} \markbox{2520}{path} construction.

Let \markbox{m2521}{$X$} \markbox{2522}{be} \markbox{2523}{a} \markbox{2524}{finite} \markbox{2525}{CAT(0)} \markbox{2526}{cube} \markbox{2527}{complex} \markbox{2528}{with} \markbox{m2529}{$X = \hull_X(a,b)$} \markbox{2530}{the} \markbox{2531}{cubical} hull\footnote{The  assumption that $X = \hull_X(a,b)$ is not necessary, but is convenient for our purposes.} \markbox{2532}{of} \markbox{m2533}{$a,b \in X^0$}.  \markbox{2534}{Set} \markbox{m2535}{$\calH = \calH(a,b)$} \markbox{2536}{to} \markbox{2537}{be} \markbox{2538}{the} \markbox{2539}{set} \markbox{2540}{of} \markbox{2541}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2542}{in} \markbox{m2543}{$X$} \markbox{2544}{separating} \markbox{m2545}{$a,b$}, \markbox{2546}{so} \markbox{2547}{that} \markbox{m2548}{$X = \calX(\calH)$} \markbox{2549}{is} \markbox{2550}{the} \markbox{2551}{dual} \markbox{2552}{cube} \markbox{2553}{complex} \markbox{2554}{to} \markbox{m2555}{$\calH$}.  \markbox{2556}{Recall} \markbox{2557}{that} \markbox{2558}{we} \markbox{2559}{can} \markbox{2560}{think} \markbox{2561}{of} \markbox{2562}{vertices} \markbox{2563}{of} \markbox{m2564}{$X$} \markbox{2565}{as} \markbox{2566}{coherent} \markbox{2567}{orientations} \markbox{2568}{on} \markbox{2569}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2570}{in} \markbox{m2571}{$\calH$}.

\begin{definition}
Let \markbox{m2572}{$p \in X^0$}.  \markbox{2573}{A} \markbox{2574}{hyperplane} \markbox{m2575}{$\hh \in \calH$} \markbox{2576}{is} \emph{transitional}, \markbox{2577}{denoted} \markbox{m2578}{$\hh \in T(p,\calH)$}, if
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m2579}{$\hh$} \markbox{2580}{separates} \markbox{m2581}{$p$} \markbox{2582}{from} \markbox{m2583}{$b$}, and
\item \markbox{m2584}{$p$} \markbox{2585}{is} \emph{adjacent} \markbox{2586}{to} \markbox{m2587}{$\hh$}, \markbox{2588}{i.e.} \markbox{m2589}{$\hh$} \markbox{2590}{crosses} \markbox{2591}{some} \markbox{2592}{cube} \markbox{2593}{of} \markbox{2594}{which} \markbox{m2595}{$p$} \markbox{2596}{is} \markbox{2597}{a} vertex.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

We \markbox{2598}{note} \markbox{2599}{that} \markbox{2600}{there} \markbox{2601}{is} \markbox{2602}{a} \markbox{2603}{natural} \markbox{2604}{partial} \markbox{2605}{order} \markbox{m2606}{$\prec$} \markbox{2607}{on} \markbox{m2608}{$\calH$}, \markbox{2609}{where} \markbox{m2610}{$\hh \prec \hh'$} \markbox{2611}{when} \markbox{m2612}{$\hh$} \markbox{2613}{separates} \markbox{m2614}{$\hh'$} \markbox{2615}{from} \markbox{m2616}{$a$}, \markbox{2617}{or} \markbox{2618}{equivalently} \markbox{m2619}{$\hh'$} \markbox{2620}{separates} \markbox{m2621}{$\hh$} \markbox{2622}{from} \markbox{m2623}{$b$}.  \markbox{2624}{In} \markbox{2625}{our} \markbox{2626}{special} \markbox{2627}{setting} \markbox{2628}{with} \markbox{m2629}{$X = \hull_X(a,b)$}, \markbox{2630}{every} \markbox{2631}{vertex} \markbox{m2632}{$p \in X^0$} \markbox{2633}{occurs} \markbox{2634}{on} \markbox{2635}{some} \markbox{m2636}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic \markbox{2637}{from} \markbox{m2638}{$a$} \markbox{2639}{to} \markbox{m2640}{$b$}.  \markbox{2641}{The} \markbox{2642}{property} \markbox{2643}{of} \markbox{2644}{transitionality} \markbox{2645}{for} \markbox{m2646}{$\hh \in T(p,\calH)$} \markbox{2647}{is} \markbox{2648}{encoding} \markbox{2649}{that} \markbox{m2650}{$\hh$} \markbox{2651}{is} \markbox{2652}{minimal} \markbox{2653}{in} \markbox{2654}{the} \markbox{2655}{partial} \markbox{2656}{order} \markbox{2657}{on} \markbox{m2658}{$\calH(p,b) \subset \calH$}.

The \markbox{2659}{following} \markbox{2660}{lemma} \markbox{2661}{says} \markbox{2662}{that} \markbox{2663}{minimal} \markbox{2664}{elements} \markbox{2665}{in} \markbox{2666}{the} \markbox{2667}{partial} \markbox{2668}{order} \markbox{2669}{must} cross:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:trans cross}
If \markbox{m2670}{$\hh_1,\hh_2 \in T(p,\calH)$}, \markbox{2671}{then} \markbox{m2672}{$\hh_1$} \markbox{2673}{crosses} \markbox{m2674}{$\hh_2$}.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}
If \markbox{m2675}{$\hh_1$} \markbox{2676}{and} \markbox{m2677}{$\hh_2$} \markbox{2678}{do} \markbox{2679}{not} \markbox{2680}{cross,} \markbox{2681}{then,} \markbox{2682}{without} \markbox{2683}{loss} \markbox{2684}{of} \markbox{2685}{generality,} \markbox{2686}{there} \markbox{2687}{is} \markbox{2688}{a} \markbox{2689}{half-space} \markbox{2690}{of} \markbox{m2691}{$\hh_2$} \markbox{2692}{containing} \markbox{m2693}{$a, \hh_1$}.  \markbox{2694}{On} \markbox{2695}{the} \markbox{2696}{other} \markbox{2697}{hand,} \markbox{m2698}{$p$} \markbox{2699}{is} \markbox{2700}{adjacent} \markbox{2701}{to} \markbox{m2702}{$\hh_2$}.  \markbox{2703}{This} \markbox{2704}{implies} \markbox{2705}{that} \markbox{m2706}{$p,a$} \markbox{2707}{are} \markbox{2708}{in} \markbox{2709}{different} \markbox{2710}{half-spaces} \markbox{2711}{of} \markbox{m2712}{$\hh_1$}, \markbox{2713}{which} \markbox{2714}{is} \markbox{2715}{a} contradiction.
\end{proof}

With \markbox{2716}{this} \markbox{2717}{lemma,} \markbox{2718}{we} \markbox{2719}{can} \markbox{2720}{define} \markbox{2721}{our} \emph{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{2722}{paths} \markbox{m2723}{$p_0=a, p_1, \dots, p_n = b$} \markbox{2724}{as} \markbox{2725}{follows} \cite{NibloReeves}:

\begin{itemize}
\item Let \markbox{m2726}{$p_0 = a$}.
\item By \markbox{2727}{Lemma} \ref{lem:trans cross}, \markbox{m2728}{$p_0$} \markbox{2729}{is} \markbox{2730}{the} \markbox{2731}{corner} \markbox{2732}{of} \markbox{2733}{a} \markbox{2734}{unique} \markbox{2735}{cube} \markbox{m2736}{$C_0$} \markbox{2737}{for} \markbox{2738}{which} \markbox{2739}{the} \markbox{2740}{set} \markbox{2741}{of} \markbox{2742}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2743}{that} \markbox{2744}{cross} \markbox{m2745}{$C_0$} \markbox{2746}{is} \markbox{2747}{precisely} \markbox{m2748}{$T(p,\calH)$}.  \markbox{2749}{Set} \markbox{m2750}{$p_1$} \markbox{2751}{to} \markbox{2752}{be} \markbox{2753}{the} \markbox{2754}{diagonally} \markbox{2755}{opposite} \markbox{2756}{corner} \markbox{2757}{of} \markbox{m2758}{$C_0$}.  \markbox{2759}{Equivalently,} \markbox{m2760}{$p_1$} \markbox{2761}{is} \markbox{2762}{obtained} \markbox{2763}{from} \markbox{m2764}{$p_0$} \markbox{2765}{by} \markbox{2766}{flipping} \markbox{2767}{orientations} \markbox{2768}{on} \markbox{2769}{the} \markbox{2770}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2771}{in} \markbox{m2772}{$T(p,\calH)$}.
\item Define \markbox{m2773}{$p_i$} \markbox{2774}{for} \markbox{m2775}{$i \geq 1$} \markbox{2776}{recursively} \markbox{2777}{with} \markbox{m2778}{$p_i$} \markbox{2779}{in} \markbox{2780}{place} \markbox{2781}{of} \markbox{m2782}{$p_0$}.
\end{itemize}



Thus, \markbox{2783}{at} \markbox{2784}{each} \markbox{2785}{step} \markbox{m2786}{$p_i \mapsto p_{i+1}$}, \markbox{2787}{the} \markbox{2788}{path} \markbox{2789}{crosses} \markbox{2790}{the} \markbox{2791}{set} \markbox{2792}{of} \markbox{m2793}{$\prec$}-minimal \markbox{2794}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2795}{in} \markbox{m2796}{$\calH(p_i,b)$}.  \markbox{2797}{The} \markbox{2798}{following} \markbox{2799}{proposition} \markbox{2800}{states} \markbox{2801}{the} \markbox{2802}{basic} \markbox{2803}{properties} \markbox{2804}{of} \markbox{2805}{the} \markbox{2806}{Niblo--Reeves} paths:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:NR basics}
Continuing \markbox{2807}{with} \markbox{2808}{the} \markbox{2809}{above} \markbox{2810}{notation,} \markbox{2811}{the} \markbox{2812}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item There \markbox{2813}{exists} \markbox{2814}{some} \markbox{m2815}{$n$} \markbox{2816}{so} \markbox{2817}{that} \markbox{m2818}{$p_n=b$}.
\item For \markbox{2819}{all} \markbox{m2820}{$0 \leq i \leq n$}, \markbox{2821}{we} \markbox{2822}{have} \markbox{m2823}{$d^{\infty}_X(p_{i}, p_{i+1}) =1$}.
\item Any \markbox{2824}{path} \markbox{2825}{obtained} \markbox{2826}{by} \markbox{2827}{concatenating} \markbox{m2828}{$\ell^1$}-geodesics \markbox{2829}{between} \markbox{m2830}{$p_i, p_{i+1}$} \markbox{2831}{for} \markbox{m2832}{$0 \leq i < n$} \markbox{2833}{is} \markbox{2834}{an} \markbox{m2835}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
For \markbox{2836}{(1),} \markbox{2837}{observe} \markbox{2838}{that} \markbox{2839}{the} \markbox{2840}{sequence} \markbox{m2841}{$p_i$} \markbox{2842}{only} \markbox{2843}{crosses} \markbox{2844}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2845}{separating} \markbox{m2846}{$a$} \markbox{2847}{from} \markbox{m2848}{$b$}.  \markbox{2849}{Each} \markbox{2850}{step} \markbox{m2851}{$p_i \mapsto p_{i+1}$} \markbox{2852}{of} \markbox{2853}{the} \markbox{2854}{sequence} \markbox{2855}{crosses} \markbox{2856}{the} \markbox{2857}{collection} \markbox{2858}{of} \markbox{m2859}{$\prec$}-minimal \markbox{2860}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2861}{in} \markbox{m2862}{$\calH(p_i, b)\subset \calH$}.  \markbox{2863}{Now} \markbox{2864}{(1)} \markbox{2865}{is} \markbox{2866}{equivalent} \markbox{2867}{to} \markbox{2868}{the} \markbox{2869}{claim} \markbox{2870}{that} \markbox{m2871}{$\calH = \bigcup_i \calH(p_i,b)$}, \markbox{2872}{which} \markbox{2873}{is} \markbox{2874}{to} \markbox{2875}{say} \markbox{2876}{that} \markbox{2877}{this} \markbox{2878}{process} \markbox{2879}{exhausts} \markbox{2880}{the} \markbox{2881}{set} \markbox{2882}{of} \markbox{2883}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2884}{separating} \markbox{m2885}{$a$} \markbox{2886}{and} \markbox{m2887}{$b$}, \markbox{2888}{which} \markbox{2889}{is} \markbox{2890}{clear} \markbox{2891}{because} \markbox{m2892}{$\calH$} \markbox{2893}{is} finite.

Item \markbox{2894}{(2)} \markbox{2895}{is} \markbox{2896}{by} \markbox{2897}{construction,} \markbox{2898}{since} \markbox{m2899}{$p_i$} \markbox{2900}{and} \markbox{m2901}{$p_{i+1}$} \markbox{2902}{are} \markbox{2903}{opposite} \markbox{2904}{corners} \markbox{2905}{of} \markbox{2906}{a} cube.

Finally, \markbox{2907}{item} \markbox{2908}{(3)} \markbox{2909}{follows} \markbox{2910}{from} \markbox{2911}{the} \markbox{2912}{fact} \markbox{2913}{that} \markbox{m2914}{$\calH(p_i, b) \subset \calH(p_{i+1},b)$} \markbox{2915}{with} \markbox{m2916}{$\calH(p_{i+1},b) - \calH(p_i, b) = \calH(p_i,p_{i+1})$}.  \markbox{2917}{Hence} \markbox{2918}{if} \markbox{m2919}{$\hh \in T(p_i,b)$}, \markbox{2920}{then} \markbox{m2921}{$\hh$} \markbox{2922}{does} \markbox{2923}{not} \markbox{2924}{separate} \markbox{m2925}{$p_i$} \markbox{2926}{from} \markbox{m2927}{$p_j$} \markbox{2928}{for} \markbox{m2929}{$j<i$}.  \markbox{2930}{This} \markbox{2931}{says} \markbox{2932}{that} \markbox{2933}{the} \markbox{2934}{sequence} \markbox{m2935}{$\{p_i\}$} \markbox{2936}{does} \markbox{2937}{not} \markbox{2938}{cross} \markbox{2939}{any} \markbox{2940}{hyperplane} \markbox{2941}{twice,} \markbox{2942}{and} \markbox{2943}{it} \markbox{2944}{follows} \markbox{2945}{that} \markbox{2946}{the} \markbox{2947}{concatenation} \markbox{2948}{of} \markbox{2949}{the} \markbox{m2950}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic \markbox{2951}{segments} \markbox{2952}{will} \markbox{2953}{not} \markbox{2954}{either,} \markbox{2955}{making} \markbox{2956}{it} \markbox{2957}{an} \markbox{m2958}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic.
\end{proof}

The \markbox{2959}{following} \markbox{2960}{is} \markbox{2961}{a} \markbox{2962}{useful} \markbox{2963}{observation} \markbox{2964}{about} \markbox{2965}{this} construction:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:NR iso}
Let \markbox{m2966}{$\Phi:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{2967}{be} \markbox{2968}{an} \markbox{2969}{isomorphism} \markbox{2970}{of} \markbox{2971}{cube} \markbox{2972}{complexes.}  \markbox{2973}{If} \markbox{m2974}{$\gamma$} \markbox{2975}{is} \markbox{2976}{the} \markbox{2977}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{2978}{path} \markbox{2979}{between} \markbox{m2980}{$a,b \in \calQ^0$}, \markbox{2981}{then} \markbox{m2982}{$\Phi(\gamma)$} \markbox{2983}{is} \markbox{2984}{the} \markbox{2985}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{2986}{path} \markbox{2987}{between} \markbox{m2988}{$\Phi(a), \Phi(b) \in \left(\calQ'\right)^{0}$}.
\end{proposition}

We \markbox{2989}{can} \markbox{2990}{now} \markbox{2991}{state} \markbox{2992}{the} \markbox{2993}{main} \markbox{2994}{result} \markbox{2995}{of} \markbox{2996}{this} subsection.

\begin{theorem}[Stable moves]\label{thm:stable moves}
Suppose \markbox{2997}{that} \markbox{m2998}{$\hh \in \calH$} \markbox{2999}{is} \markbox{3000}{hyperplane,} \markbox{3001}{and} \markbox{3002}{let} \markbox{m3003}{$\Delta_{\hh}:\calD(\calH) \to \calD(\calH - \{\hh\})$} \markbox{3004}{denote} \markbox{3005}{the} \markbox{3006}{hyperplane} \markbox{3007}{collapse} \markbox{3008}{map.}  \markbox{3009}{Set} \markbox{m3010}{$\Delta_{\hh}(a) = a'$} \markbox{3011}{and} \markbox{m3012}{$\Delta_{\hh}(b) =b'$}.  \markbox{3013}{Let} \markbox{m3014}{$p_0,\dots,p_n$} \markbox{3015}{denote} \markbox{3016}{the} \markbox{3017}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3018}{path} \markbox{3019}{in} \markbox{m3020}{$X = \calD(\calH)$}  \markbox{3021}{between} \markbox{m3022}{$a,b$} \markbox{3023}{and} \markbox{m3024}{$p'_0, \dots, p'_m$} \markbox{3025}{the} \markbox{3026}{path} \markbox{3027}{between} \markbox{m3028}{$a',b'$} \markbox{3029}{in} \markbox{m3030}{$\calD(\calH- \{\hh\})$}.  \markbox{3031}{Then} \markbox{3032}{the} \markbox{3033}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item We \markbox{3034}{have} \markbox{m3035}{$n \leq m+1$}.
\item For \markbox{3036}{all} \markbox{m3037}{$1 \leq i \leq n$}, \markbox{3038}{we} \markbox{3039}{have} \markbox{m3040}{$d^{\infty}_{\calD(\calH - \{\hh\})}(\Delta_{\hh}(p_i), p'_i) \leq 1$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

In \markbox{3041}{other} \markbox{3042}{words,} \markbox{3043}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3044}{paths} \markbox{3045}{are} \markbox{3046}{stable} \markbox{3047}{under} \markbox{3048}{hyperplane} \markbox{3049}{deletion} maps.

The \markbox{3050}{following} \markbox{3051}{notation} \markbox{3052}{will} \markbox{3053}{be} \markbox{3054}{useful} \markbox{3055}{for} us:

\begin{definition}
Let \markbox{m3056}{$\hh' \in \calH$}.  \markbox{3057}{We} \markbox{3058}{set} \markbox{m3059}{$t_{\hh'}(a, \calH)$}, \markbox{3060}{called} \markbox{3061}{the} \emph{transition index} \markbox{3062}{of} \markbox{m3063}{$\hh'$}, \markbox{3064}{to} \markbox{3065}{be} \markbox{3066}{the} \markbox{3067}{index} \markbox{m3068}{$i$} \markbox{3069}{at} \markbox{3070}{which} \markbox{m3071}{$\hh' \in \calH(p_i, p_{i+1})$}.  \markbox{3072}{Similarly,} \markbox{3073}{if} \markbox{m3074}{$\hh' \in \calH - \{\hh\}$}, \markbox{3075}{we} \markbox{3076}{define} \markbox{m3077}{$t_{\hh'}(a', \calH - \{\hh\})$} \markbox{3078}{to} \markbox{3079}{be} \markbox{3080}{the} \markbox{3081}{index} \markbox{m3082}{$i$} \markbox{3083}{so} \markbox{3084}{that} \markbox{m3085}{$\hh' \in \calH(p'_i, p'_{i+1})$}.
\end{definition} 

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:move control}
If \markbox{m3086}{$\hh' \in \calH - \{\hh\}$}, \markbox{3087}{then} \markbox{m3088}{$t_{\hh'}(a,\calH) = t_{\hh'}(a', \calH - \{\hh\}) + \delta$} \markbox{3089}{for} \markbox{m3090}{$\delta \in \{0,1\}$}.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}
This \markbox{3091}{is} \markbox{3092}{essentially} \cite[Lemma 5.12]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{3093}{though} \markbox{3094}{the} \markbox{3095}{proof} \markbox{3096}{is} \markbox{3097}{basically} \markbox{3098}{immediate} \markbox{3099}{in} \markbox{3100}{our} \markbox{3101}{setting.}  \markbox{3102}{Note} \markbox{3103}{that} \markbox{3104}{the} \markbox{3105}{transition} \markbox{3106}{index} \markbox{m3107}{$t_{\hh} = d_{\infty}(a, \hh) + \frac{1}{2}$}.  \markbox{3108}{Since} \markbox{3109}{the} \markbox{m3110}{$\ell^{\infty}$} \markbox{3111}{distance} \markbox{3112}{between} \markbox{m3113}{$a'$} \markbox{3114}{and} \markbox{m3115}{$\hh'$} \markbox{3116}{measures} \markbox{3117}{the} \markbox{3118}{maximal} \markbox{3119}{length} \markbox{3120}{of} \markbox{3121}{a} \markbox{3122}{chain} \markbox{3123}{of} \markbox{3124}{hyperplanes} \markbox{3125}{separating} \markbox{3126}{them} \markbox{3127}{(plus} \markbox{m3128}{$\frac{1}{2}$}), \markbox{3129}{that} \markbox{3130}{distance} \markbox{3131}{can} \markbox{3132}{be} \markbox{3133}{at} \markbox{3134}{most} \markbox{m3135}{$1$} \markbox{3136}{more} \markbox{3137}{than} \markbox{m3138}{$d_{\infty}(a,\hh)$}.  \markbox{3139}{This} \markbox{3140}{completes} \markbox{3141}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{3142}{of} \markbox{3143}{the} \markbox{3144}{Stable} \markbox{3145}{Moves} \markbox{3146}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}]
Suppose \markbox{m3147}{$\hh_1, \hh_2$} \markbox{3148}{separate} \markbox{m3149}{$\Delta_{\hh}(p_i)$} \markbox{3150}{and} \markbox{m3151}{$p'_i$} \markbox{3152}{in} \markbox{m3153}{$X' = \calD(\calH - \{\hh\})$} \markbox{3154}{but} \markbox{3155}{do} \markbox{3156}{not} \markbox{3157}{cross,} \markbox{3158}{since} \markbox{3159}{we} \markbox{3160}{are} \markbox{3161}{done} \markbox{3162}{if} \markbox{3163}{all} \markbox{3164}{such} \markbox{3165}{hyperplanes} cross.
