Without \markbox{3166}{loss} \markbox{3167}{of} \markbox{3168}{generality,} \markbox{3169}{we} \markbox{3170}{may} \markbox{3171}{assume} \markbox{3172}{that} \markbox{m3173}{$\hh_1$} \markbox{3174}{separates} \markbox{m3175}{$\Delta_{\hh}(p_i)$} \markbox{3176}{from} \markbox{m3177}{$\hh_2$}.  \markbox{3178}{Let} \markbox{m3179}{$j = t_{\hh_1}(a',\calH - \{\hh\})$}.  \markbox{3180}{Then} \markbox{m3181}{$j < t_{\hh_2}(a',\calH - \{\hh\}) < i$}, \markbox{3182}{with} \markbox{3183}{the} \markbox{3184}{latter} \markbox{3185}{inequality} \markbox{3186}{following} \markbox{3187}{because} \markbox{m3188}{$p'_{i+1}$} \markbox{3189}{has} \markbox{3190}{already} \markbox{3191}{crossed} \markbox{m3192}{$\hh_2$} \markbox{3193}{(and} \markbox{m3194}{$\hh_1$}).  \markbox{3195}{Thus} \markbox{m3196}{$j + 1 < i$}.

But \markbox{3197}{then} \markbox{m3198}{$t_{\hh_1}(a, \calH) \leq t_{\hh_1}(a', \calH - \{\hh\}) + 1 = j+1 < i$}, \markbox{3199}{which} \markbox{3200}{says} \markbox{3201}{that} \markbox{m3202}{$\hh_1$} \markbox{3203}{separates} \markbox{m3204}{$p_i$} \markbox{3205}{from} \markbox{m3206}{$a$}, \markbox{3207}{which} \markbox{3208}{is} \markbox{3209}{a} contradiction.
\end{proof}


\subsection{Bicombings}\label{subsec:semihyp}

Our \markbox{3210}{ultimate} \markbox{3211}{goal} \markbox{3212}{is} \markbox{3213}{to} \markbox{3214}{prove} \markbox{3215}{that} \markbox{3216}{mapping} \markbox{3217}{class} \markbox{3218}{groups} \markbox{3219}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{3220}{spaces} \markbox{3221}{admits} \markbox{3222}{bicombings} \markbox{3223}{(Theorem} \ref{thmi:main}).  \markbox{3224}{Roughly,} \markbox{3225}{a} \markbox{3226}{bicombing} \markbox{3227}{on} \markbox{3228}{a} \markbox{3229}{space} \markbox{m3230}{$X$} \markbox{3231}{is} \markbox{3232}{a} \markbox{3233}{family} \markbox{3234}{of} \markbox{3235}{uniform} \markbox{3236}{quasi-geodesic} \markbox{3237}{paths} \markbox{3238}{that} \markbox{3239}{is} \markbox{3240}{transitive} \markbox{3241}{(i.e.,} \markbox{3242}{connects} \markbox{3243}{any} \markbox{3244}{pair} \markbox{3245}{of} \markbox{3246}{points} \markbox{3247}{of} \markbox{m3248}{$X$}), \markbox{3249}{and} \markbox{3250}{for} \markbox{3251}{which} \markbox{3252}{paths} \markbox{3253}{in} \markbox{3254}{the} \markbox{3255}{family} \markbox{3256}{between} \markbox{3257}{pairs} \markbox{3258}{of} \markbox{3259}{endpoints} \markbox{3260}{that} \markbox{3261}{are} \markbox{3262}{close} \markbox{3263}{to} \markbox{3264}{each} \markbox{3265}{other} \markbox{3266}{uniformly} \markbox{3267}{fellow-travel} \markbox{3268}{in} \markbox{3269}{a} \markbox{3270}{parameterized} \markbox{3271}{fashion.}   \markbox{3272}{The} \markbox{3273}{notion} \markbox{3274}{of} \markbox{3275}{bicombing} \markbox{3276}{was} \markbox{3277}{first} \markbox{3278}{introduced} \markbox{3279}{by} \markbox{3280}{Thurston} \markbox{3281}{in} \markbox{3282}{the} \markbox{3283}{context} \markbox{3284}{of} \markbox{3285}{algorithmic} \markbox{3286}{problems} \markbox{3287}{in} \markbox{3288}{groups.}  \markbox{3289}{It} \markbox{3290}{is} \markbox{3291}{a} \markbox{3292}{straightforward} \markbox{3293}{but} \markbox{3294}{informative} \markbox{3295}{exercise} \markbox{3296}{to} \markbox{3297}{prove} \markbox{3298}{that} \markbox{3299}{geodesics} \markbox{3300}{in} \markbox{3301}{hyperbolic} \markbox{3302}{and} \markbox{3303}{CAT(0)} \markbox{3304}{spaces} \markbox{3305}{satisfy} \markbox{3306}{this} \markbox{3307}{property,} \markbox{3308}{and} \markbox{3309}{this} \markbox{3310}{is} \markbox{3311}{precisely} \markbox{3312}{what} \markbox{3313}{the} \markbox{3314}{definition} \markbox{3315}{is} \markbox{3316}{intended} \markbox{3317}{to} generalize.

\smallskip
The \markbox{3318}{following} \markbox{3319}{definition} \markbox{3320}{is} \markbox{3321}{essentially} \markbox{3322}{from} \cite{AB95}, \markbox{3323}{as} \markbox{3324}{restated} \markbox{3325}{in} \cite[Definition 6.4]{DMS_bary}:  

\begin{definition}[Bicombings]\label{defn:bicombing}
A \emph{discrete, bounded, quasi-geodesic bicombing} \markbox{3326}{of} \markbox{3327}{a} \markbox{3328}{metric} \markbox{3329}{space} \markbox{m3330}{$X$} \markbox{3331}{consists} \markbox{3332}{of} \markbox{3333}{a} \markbox{3334}{family} \markbox{3335}{of} \markbox{3336}{discrete} \markbox{3337}{paths} \markbox{m3338}{$\{\Gamma_{x,y}\}_{x,y \in X}$} \markbox{3339}{and} \markbox{3340}{a} \markbox{3341}{constant} \markbox{m3342}{$\zeta>0$} \markbox{3343}{satisfying} \markbox{3344}{the} following:
\begin{enumerate}
\item \emph{Quasi-geodesic}: \markbox{3345}{For} \markbox{3346}{any} \markbox{m3347}{$x,y \in X$} \markbox{3348}{with} \markbox{m3349}{$d = d_{X}(x,y)$}, \markbox{3350}{there} \markbox{3351}{exists} \markbox{m3352}{$n_{x,y} \leq d\zeta + \zeta$} \markbox{3353}{so} \markbox{3354}{that} \markbox{3355}{the} \markbox{3356}{path} \markbox{m3357}{$\Gamma_{x,y}:\{0, \dots, n_{x,y}\} \rightarrow X$} \markbox{3358}{is} \markbox{3359}{a} \markbox{m3360}{$(\zeta,\zeta)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{3361}{embedding} \markbox{3362}{with} \markbox{m3363}{$\Gamma_{x,y}(0)=x$} \markbox{3364}{and} \markbox{m3365}{$\Gamma_{x,y}(n_{x,y}) = y$}; and
\item \emph{Fellow-traveling}: \markbox{3366}{If} \markbox{m3367}{$x',y' \in X$} \markbox{3368}{and} \markbox{m3369}{$d_X(x,x'), d_X(y,y') \leq 1$}, \markbox{3370}{then} \markbox{3371}{for} \markbox{3372}{all} \markbox{m3373}{$t \in \{0, \dots, \max\{n_{x,y}, n_{x',y'}\}\}$}, \markbox{3374}{we} have
$$d_X(\Gamma_{x,y}(t), \Gamma_{x',y'}(t)) \leq \zeta.$$
\end{enumerate}


For \markbox{3375}{our} \markbox{3376}{purposes,} \markbox{3377}{the} \markbox{3378}{fellow-traveling} \markbox{3379}{condition} \markbox{3380}{in} \markbox{3381}{item} \markbox{3382}{(2)} \markbox{3383}{is} \markbox{3384}{the} \markbox{3385}{key} \markbox{3386}{challenge.}  \markbox{3387}{At} \markbox{3388}{this} \markbox{3389}{point,} \markbox{3390}{there} \markbox{3391}{are} \markbox{3392}{many} \markbox{3393}{constructions} \markbox{3394}{of} \markbox{3395}{uniform} \markbox{3396}{quasigeodesics} \markbox{3397}{in} \markbox{3398}{mapping} \markbox{3399}{class} groups.


\end{definition}

\subsection{Building the bicombing}\label{subsec:building bicombing}

We \markbox{3400}{are} \markbox{3401}{now} \markbox{3402}{ready} \markbox{3403}{to} \markbox{3404}{define} \markbox{3405}{the} \markbox{3406}{bicombing.}  \markbox{3407}{Let} \markbox{m3408}{$X$} \markbox{3409}{be} \markbox{m3410}{$B_0$}-stably \markbox{3411}{wLQC} \markbox{3412}{(Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes}).  \markbox{3413}{For} \markbox{3414}{any} \markbox{m3415}{$a,b \in X$}, \markbox{3416}{let} \markbox{m3417}{$\calQ$} \markbox{3418}{be} \markbox{3419}{a} \markbox{3420}{CAT(0)} \markbox{3421}{cube} \markbox{3422}{complex} \markbox{3423}{provided} \markbox{3424}{by} \markbox{3425}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes} \markbox{3426}{and} \markbox{m3427}{$\ha,\hb\in \calQ$} \markbox{3428}{the} \markbox{3429}{distinguished} \markbox{3430}{vertices} \markbox{3431}{associated} \markbox{3432}{to} \markbox{m3433}{$a,b$}.

We \markbox{3434}{can} \markbox{3435}{define} \markbox{3436}{a} \markbox{3437}{family} \markbox{3438}{of} \markbox{3439}{paths} \markbox{m3440}{$\{\Gamma_{a,b}\}_{a,b \in X}$} \markbox{3441}{by} \markbox{3442}{taking} \markbox{m3443}{$\Gamma_{a,b}$} \markbox{3444}{to} \markbox{3445}{be} \markbox{3446}{the} \markbox{3447}{image} \markbox{3448}{under} \markbox{3449}{the} \markbox{3450}{quasi-isometry} \markbox{m3451}{$\hO:\calQ \to X$} \markbox{3452}{of} \markbox{3453}{the} \markbox{3454}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3455}{path} \markbox{3456}{between} \markbox{m3457}{$\ha,\hb$}.  \markbox{3458}{By} \markbox{3459}{Definition} \ref{defn:lqc pair}, \markbox{3460}{this} \markbox{3461}{is} \markbox{3462}{a} \markbox{3463}{uniform} \markbox{m3464}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-geodesic \markbox{3465}{between} \markbox{m3466}{$a,b$}.

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:bicombing}
The \markbox{3467}{family} \markbox{3468}{of} \markbox{3469}{paths} \markbox{m3470}{$\{\Gamma_{a,b}\}_{a,b \in X}$} \markbox{3471}{forms} \markbox{3472}{a} \markbox{3473}{discrete} \markbox{3474}{bounded} \markbox{3475}{quasi-geodesic} \markbox{3476}{bicombing} \markbox{3477}{on} \markbox{m3478}{$X$}.
\end{theorem}

\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.8\textwidth]{figures/bicombing_example.pdf}
    \caption{Stable Moves: A simple example of how Niblo--Reeves paths behave under hyperplane collapses.  In each cube complex, the red vertices correspond to $a,b$.  The orange hyperplanes are collapsed when passing to $\calQ_0 = \calQ'_0$.  The Niblo--Reeves path in $\calQ_0$ between $a,b$ travels in a straight line between the red vertices.  The Niblo--Reeves paths in $\calQ$ (blue) and $\calQ'$ (purple) descend to paths which are close to it the Niblo--Reeves path in $\calQ_0$, and hence close to each other.  This example is a modified version of \cite[Figure 25]{DMS_bary}.}
    \label{fig:bicoming_example}
\end{figure}


\begin{proof}
We \markbox{3479}{need} \markbox{3480}{to} \markbox{3481}{confirm} \markbox{3482}{the} \markbox{3483}{properties} \markbox{3484}{in} \markbox{3485}{Definition} \ref{defn:bicombing}.  \markbox{3486}{The} \markbox{3487}{paths} \markbox{3488}{are} \markbox{3489}{clearly} \markbox{3490}{discrete} \markbox{3491}{and} \markbox{3492}{are} \markbox{m3493}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-geodesics \markbox{3494}{by} \markbox{3495}{assumption.}  \markbox{3496}{So} \markbox{3497}{we} \markbox{3498}{need} \markbox{3499}{to} \markbox{3500}{show} \markbox{3501}{that} \markbox{3502}{they} \markbox{3503}{satisfy} \markbox{3504}{the} \markbox{3505}{fellow-traveling} \markbox{3506}{property} \markbox{3507}{in} \markbox{3508}{item} \markbox{3509}{(2)} \markbox{3510}{of} \markbox{3511}{that} \markbox{3512}{definition.}  \markbox{3513}{This} \markbox{3514}{is} \markbox{3515}{a} \markbox{3516}{direct} \markbox{3517}{application} \markbox{3518}{of} \markbox{3519}{the} \markbox{3520}{properties} \markbox{3521}{in} \markbox{3522}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes} \markbox{3523}{and} \markbox{3524}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}.

Let \markbox{m3525}{$\ha,\hb \in \calQ$} \markbox{3526}{and} \markbox{m3527}{$\ha_0,\hb_0 \in \calQ_0$} \markbox{3528}{be} \markbox{3529}{the} \markbox{3530}{distinguished} \markbox{3531}{vertices} \markbox{3532}{associated} \markbox{3533}{to} \markbox{m3534}{$a,b$}, \markbox{3535}{and} \markbox{3536}{the} \markbox{3537}{same} \markbox{3538}{for} \markbox{m3539}{$\ha',\hb' \in \calQ'$} \markbox{3540}{and} \markbox{m3541}{$\ha'_0,\hb'_0 \in \calQ'_0$} \markbox{3542}{with} \markbox{m3543}{$a',b'$}, \markbox{3544}{respectively.}  \markbox{3545}{Note} \markbox{3546}{that} \markbox{m3547}{$\Delta_0(\ha) = \ha_0$}, \markbox{3548}{etc,} \markbox{3549}{by} \markbox{3550}{item} \markbox{3551}{(4)} \markbox{3552}{of} \markbox{3553}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes}.  \markbox{3554}{Let} \markbox{m3555}{$\Lambda, \Lambda_0, \Lambda',\Lambda'_0$} \markbox{3556}{be} \markbox{3557}{the} \markbox{3558}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3559}{paths} \markbox{3560}{in} \markbox{m3561}{$\calQ,\calQ_0,\calQ',\calQ'_0$} \markbox{3562}{connecting} \markbox{3563}{the} \markbox{3564}{respective} \markbox{3565}{pairs} \markbox{m3566}{$(\ha,\hb), (\ha_0,\hb_0), (\ha',\hb'), (\ha'_0,\hb'_0)$} \markbox{3567}{in} \markbox{3568}{their} \markbox{3569}{respective} \markbox{3570}{cube} \markbox{3571}{complexes} \markbox{m3572}{$\calQ,\calQ_0,\calQ',\calQ'_0$}.  \markbox{3573}{So} \markbox{3574}{in} \markbox{3575}{our} \markbox{3576}{notation,} \markbox{m3577}{$\Gamma_{a,b} = \hO(\Lambda)$} \markbox{3578}{and} \markbox{m3579}{$\Gamma_{a',b'} = \hO'(\Lambda')$}.  \markbox{3580}{We} \markbox{3581}{have} \markbox{3582}{the} \markbox{3583}{following} estimate
\begin{eqnarray}
d_X(\Gamma_{a,b}(i), \Gamma_{a',b'}(i)) &=& d_X(\hO(\Lambda(i)), \hO'(\Lambda'(i)))\\
&\leq& d_X(\hO_0 \circ \Delta_0(\Lambda(i)), \hO'_0 \circ \Delta'_0 (\Lambda'(i))) + 2B_0\\
&\leq& d_X(\hO_0(\Lambda_0(i)), \hO'_0(\Lambda'_0(i))) + 4B_0\\
&\leq& d_X(\hO'_0 \circ I_0(\Lambda_0(i)), \hO'_0(\Lambda'_0(i))) + 5B_0\\
&=& d_X(\hO'_0(\Lambda'_0(i)), \hO'_0(\Lambda'_0(i)))\\
&=& 5B_0.
\end{eqnarray}
In \markbox{3584}{the} \markbox{3585}{above,} \markbox{3586}{(3)} \markbox{3587}{follows} \markbox{3588}{from} \markbox{3589}{commutativity} \markbox{3590}{of} \markbox{3591}{the} \markbox{3592}{top} \markbox{3593}{and} \markbox{3594}{bottom} \markbox{3595}{triangles} \markbox{3596}{in} \markbox{3597}{diagram} \ref{Phi diagram, early}, \markbox{3598}{(4)} \markbox{3599}{follows} \markbox{3600}{from} \markbox{3601}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}, \markbox{3602}{(5)} \markbox{3603}{follows} \markbox{3604}{from} \markbox{3605}{commutativity} \markbox{3606}{the} \markbox{3607}{middle} \markbox{3608}{triangle} \markbox{3609}{of} \markbox{3610}{diagram} \ref{Phi diagram, early}, \markbox{3611}{and} \markbox{3612}{(6)} \markbox{3613}{follows} \markbox{3614}{from} \markbox{3615}{the} \markbox{3616}{fact} \markbox{3617}{that} \markbox{3618}{the} \markbox{3619}{cubical} \markbox{3620}{isomorphism} \markbox{m3621}{$I_0:\calQ_0 \to \calQ'_0$} \markbox{3622}{identifies} \markbox{3623}{the} \markbox{3624}{paths} \markbox{m3625}{$\Lambda_0$} \markbox{3626}{and} \markbox{m3627}{$\Lambda'_0$}, \markbox{3628}{i.e.} \markbox{m3629}{$\Lambda_0(i) = \Lambda'_0(i)$} \markbox{3630}{for} \markbox{3631}{each} \markbox{m3632}{$i$} \markbox{3633}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:NR iso}).  \markbox{3634}{This} \markbox{3635}{completes} \markbox{3636}{the} proof.


\end{proof}

With \markbox{3637}{this} \markbox{3638}{in} \markbox{3639}{hand,} \markbox{3640}{we} \markbox{3641}{can} \markbox{3642}{prove} \markbox{3643}{our} \markbox{3644}{bicombing} result:

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{3645}{of} \markbox{3646}{Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp}]
Mapping \markbox{3647}{class} \markbox{3648}{groups} \markbox{3649}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{3650}{spaces} \markbox{3651}{of} \markbox{3652}{finite} \markbox{3653}{type} \markbox{3654}{surfaces} \markbox{3655}{are} \markbox{3656}{colorable} \markbox{3657}{HHSes} \markbox{3658}{(see} \markbox{3659}{Section} \ref{sec:HHS} \markbox{3660}{for} \markbox{3661}{references),} \markbox{3662}{so} \markbox{3663}{they} \markbox{3664}{are} \markbox{3665}{stably} \markbox{3666}{weakly} \markbox{3667}{locally} \markbox{3668}{quasi-cubical} \markbox{3669}{by} \markbox{3670}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}.  \markbox{3671}{Hence} \markbox{3672}{Theorem} \ref{thm:bicombing} \markbox{3673}{provides} \markbox{3674}{a} \markbox{3675}{bicombing} \markbox{3676}{by} \markbox{3677}{pushing} \markbox{3678}{forward} \markbox{3679}{the} \markbox{3680}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3681}{path} \markbox{3682}{in} \markbox{3683}{an} \markbox{3684}{appropriate} \markbox{3685}{cubical} \markbox{3686}{model} \markbox{3687}{to} \markbox{3688}{the} \markbox{3689}{respective} \markbox{3690}{space.}  \markbox{3691}{Any} \markbox{3692}{such} \markbox{m3693}{$\ell^{\infty}$}-geodesic \markbox{3694}{can} \markbox{3695}{be} \markbox{3696}{completed} \markbox{3697}{to} \markbox{3698}{an} \markbox{m3699}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic \markbox{3700}{by} \markbox{3701}{connecting} \markbox{3702}{vertices} \markbox{3703}{via} \markbox{m3704}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic \markbox{3705}{segments} \markbox{3706}{as} \markbox{3707}{in} \markbox{3708}{Proposition} \ref{prop:NR basics}.  \markbox{3709}{But} \markbox{3710}{now} \markbox{3711}{Proposition} \ref{prop:cubical hp} \markbox{3712}{says} \markbox{3713}{that} \markbox{3714}{the} \markbox{3715}{images} \markbox{3716}{of} \markbox{3717}{these} \markbox{3718}{paths} \markbox{3719}{are} \markbox{3720}{hierarchy} \markbox{3721}{paths} \markbox{3722}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hp}).  \markbox{3723}{This} \markbox{3724}{completes} \markbox{3725}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}\label{rem:no medians}
A \markbox{3726}{reader} \markbox{3727}{familiar} \markbox{3728}{with} \markbox{3729}{both} \cite{HHS_quasi} \markbox{3730}{and} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{3731}{will} \markbox{3732}{note} \markbox{3733}{that} \markbox{3734}{one} \markbox{3735}{usually} \markbox{3736}{uses} \markbox{3737}{the} \markbox{3738}{fact} \markbox{3739}{that} \markbox{3740}{the} \markbox{3741}{cubical} \markbox{3742}{model} \markbox{3743}{maps} \markbox{3744}{are} \emph{quasi-median} \markbox{3745}{maps} \markbox{3746}{to} \markbox{3747}{get} \markbox{3748}{this} \markbox{3749}{last} \markbox{3750}{hierarchy} \markbox{3751}{path} \markbox{3752}{property.}  \markbox{3753}{However,} \markbox{3754}{we} \markbox{3755}{have} \markbox{3756}{avoided} \markbox{3757}{discussions} \markbox{3758}{of} \markbox{3759}{median} \markbox{3760}{structures} \markbox{3761}{in} \markbox{3762}{this} \markbox{3763}{paper} \markbox{3764}{because} \markbox{3765}{they} \markbox{3766}{are} \markbox{3767}{unnecessary} \markbox{3768}{for} \markbox{3769}{our} \markbox{3770}{purposes.}  \markbox{3771}{See} \cite[Section 15]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{3772}{for} \markbox{3773}{how} \markbox{3774}{our} \markbox{3775}{cubical} \markbox{3776}{model} \markbox{3777}{construction} \markbox{3778}{works} \markbox{3779}{with} medians.
\end{remark}


\section{A brief primer on HHSes}\label{sec:HHS}

Hierarchically \markbox{3780}{hyperbolic} \markbox{3781}{spaces} \markbox{3782}{were} \markbox{3783}{introduced} \markbox{3784}{by} \markbox{3785}{Behrstock--Hagen--Sisto} \markbox{3786}{in} \cite{HHS_I, HHS_II}, \markbox{3787}{building} \markbox{3788}{off} \markbox{3789}{of} \markbox{3790}{work} \markbox{3791}{of} \markbox{3792}{Masur--Minsky} \cite{MM99,MM00} \markbox{3793}{on} \markbox{3794}{the} \markbox{3795}{mapping} \markbox{3796}{class} \markbox{3797}{group,} \markbox{3798}{among} \markbox{3799}{others} \cite{Brock, Rafi:combo, Rafi:hypteich, Dur:augmented, EMR:rank}.

For \markbox{3800}{our} \markbox{3801}{purposes,} \markbox{3802}{we} \markbox{3803}{will} \markbox{3804}{introduce} \markbox{3805}{the} \markbox{3806}{basic} \markbox{3807}{foundational} \markbox{3808}{concepts} \markbox{3809}{that} \markbox{3810}{we} \markbox{3811}{need.}  \markbox{3812}{It} \markbox{3813}{turns} \markbox{3814}{out} \markbox{3815}{that} \markbox{3816}{the} \markbox{3817}{cubical} \markbox{3818}{model} \markbox{3819}{construction} \markbox{3820}{is} \markbox{3821}{a} \markbox{3822}{foundational-level} \markbox{3823}{construction,} \markbox{3824}{as} \markbox{3825}{one} \markbox{3826}{can} \markbox{3827}{use} \markbox{3828}{it} \markbox{3829}{to} \markbox{3830}{prove} \markbox{3831}{key} \markbox{3832}{facts} \markbox{3833}{like} \markbox{3834}{the} \markbox{3835}{Distance} \markbox{3836}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}; \markbox{3837}{see} \markbox{3838}{Bowditch} \cite{Bowditch_hulls} \markbox{3839}{and} \cite{Dur_infcube}.

The \markbox{3840}{following} \markbox{3841}{is} \markbox{3842}{a} \markbox{3843}{complete} \markbox{3844}{list} \markbox{3845}{(at} \markbox{3846}{the} \markbox{3847}{time} \markbox{3848}{of} \markbox{3849}{writing)} \markbox{3850}{of} \markbox{3851}{the} \markbox{3852}{spaces} \markbox{3853}{known} \markbox{3854}{to} \markbox{3855}{be} \markbox{3856}{hierarchically} \markbox{3857}{hyperbolic.}  \markbox{3858}{With} \markbox{3859}{the} \markbox{3860}{exception} \markbox{3861}{of} \markbox{3862}{some} \markbox{3863}{cubical} \markbox{3864}{examples,} \markbox{3865}{all} \markbox{3866}{of} \markbox{3867}{them} \markbox{3868}{are} \markbox{3869}{colorable} \markbox{3870}{(Definition} \ref{defn:colorable}), \markbox{3871}{and} \markbox{3872}{so} \markbox{3873}{our} \markbox{3874}{main} \markbox{3875}{results} \markbox{3876}{Theorem} \ref{thmi:main} \markbox{3877}{and} \markbox{3878}{Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp} apply:

\begin{itemize}
\item Hyperbolic spaces.
\item Mapping \markbox{3879}{class} \markbox{3880}{groups} \cite{MM99, MM00, Aougab_hyp, HHS_I} \markbox{3881}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{3882}{spaces,} \markbox{3883}{with} \markbox{3884}{both} \markbox{3885}{the} Teichm\"uller \cite{Rafi:combo, Dur:augmented} \markbox{3886}{and} \markbox{3887}{Weil-Petersson} \markbox{3888}{metrics} \cite{Brock}.
\item Many \cite{HS:cubical}, \markbox{3889}{but} \markbox{3890}{not} \markbox{3891}{all} \cite{shepherd2025cubulation}, \markbox{3892}{CAT(0)} \markbox{3893}{cubical} \markbox{3894}{groups,}  \markbox{3895}{including} \markbox{3896}{all} \markbox{3897}{right-angled} \markbox{3898}{Artin} \markbox{3899}{and} \markbox{3900}{Coxeter} \markbox{3901}{groups} \cite{HHS_I}.
\item Fundamental \markbox{3902}{groups} \markbox{3903}{of} \markbox{3904}{closed} \markbox{3905}{3-manifolds} \markbox{3906}{without} \markbox{3907}{Nil} \markbox{3908}{or} \markbox{3909}{Sol} \markbox{3910}{summands} \cite{HHS_II, hagen2022equivariant}.
\item Quotients \markbox{3911}{of} \markbox{3912}{mapping} \markbox{3913}{class} \markbox{3914}{groups} \markbox{3915}{by} \markbox{3916}{large} \markbox{3917}{powers} \markbox{3918}{of} \markbox{3919}{Dehn} \markbox{3920}{twists} \cite{behrstock2024combinatorial} \markbox{3921}{and} \markbox{3922}{pseudo-Anosovs} \cite{HHS:asdim}.
\item Surface \markbox{3923}{group} \markbox{3924}{extensions} \markbox{3925}{of} \markbox{3926}{Veech} \markbox{3927}{groups} \cite{DDLS1, DDLS2, bongiovanni2024extensions} \markbox{3928}{and} \markbox{3929}{multicurve} \markbox{3930}{stabilizers} \cite{russell2021extensions} \markbox{3931}{of} \markbox{3932}{mapping} \markbox{3933}{class} groups.
\item  The \markbox{3934}{genus-2} \markbox{3935}{handlebody} \markbox{3936}{group} \cite{chesser2022stable}.
\item Artin \markbox{3937}{groups} \markbox{3938}{of} \markbox{3939}{extra-large} \markbox{3940}{type} \cite{MMS:Artin}.
\item Many \markbox{3941}{free-by-cyclic} \markbox{3942}{groups} \cite{bongiovanni2025characterizing}.
\item Admissible \markbox{3943}{curve} \markbox{3944}{graphs} \cite{calderon2024hierarchical}.
\item The \markbox{3945}{class} \markbox{3946}{of} \markbox{3947}{HHSes} \markbox{3948}{is} \markbox{3949}{closed} \markbox{3950}{under} \markbox{3951}{products} \markbox{3952}{and} \markbox{3953}{appropriate} \markbox{3954}{combinations} \cite{HHS_II}, \markbox{3955}{including} \markbox{3956}{graph} \markbox{3957}{products} \cite{BR:graph_prods} \markbox{3958}{and} \markbox{3959}{graph} \markbox{3960}{braid} \markbox{3961}{groups}  \cite{berlyne2021hierarchical}.
\end{itemize}

We \markbox{3962}{note} \markbox{3963}{that} \markbox{3964}{there} \markbox{3965}{are} \markbox{3966}{non-colorable} \markbox{3967}{cubical} \markbox{3968}{HHSes} \cite{Hagen:non-col} \markbox{3969}{and} \markbox{3970}{non-HHS} \markbox{3971}{cubical} \markbox{3972}{groups} \cite{shepherd2025cubulation}.  \markbox{3973}{CAT(0)} \markbox{3974}{cube} \markbox{3975}{complexes} \markbox{3976}{are} \markbox{3977}{obviously} \markbox{3978}{locally} \markbox{3979}{modeled} \markbox{3980}{by} \markbox{3981}{cube} \markbox{3982}{complexes} \markbox{3983}{and,} \markbox{3984}{moreover,} \markbox{3985}{are} \markbox{3986}{bicombable} \cite{NibloReeves}, \markbox{3987}{so} \markbox{3988}{they} \markbox{3989}{are} \markbox{3990}{not} \markbox{3991}{of} \markbox{3992}{interest} \markbox{3993}{in} \markbox{3994}{this} \markbox{3995}{paper} \markbox{3996}{in} \markbox{3997}{any} event.

\subsection{Basic setup of an HHS}\label{subsec:basic HHS}

Roughly, \markbox{3998}{a} \emph{hierarchically hyperbolic} \markbox{3999}{structure} \markbox{4000}{is} \markbox{4001}{a} \markbox{4002}{pair} \markbox{m4003}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{4004}{where} \markbox{m4005}{$\calX$} \markbox{4006}{is} \markbox{4007}{a} \markbox{4008}{uniformly} \markbox{4009}{quasigeodesic} \markbox{4010}{metric} \markbox{4011}{space} \markbox{4012}{and} \markbox{m4013}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{4014}{is} \markbox{4015}{an} \markbox{4016}{index} \markbox{4017}{set} \markbox{4018}{for} \markbox{4019}{a} \markbox{4020}{family} \markbox{4021}{of} \markbox{4022}{uniformly} \markbox{4023}{hyperbolic} \markbox{4024}{spaces} \markbox{m4025}{$\{\calC(U)\}_{U \in \mathfrak S}$}.  \markbox{4026}{The} \markbox{4027}{ambient} \markbox{4028}{space} \markbox{m4029}{$\calX$} \markbox{4030}{admits} \markbox{4031}{a} \markbox{4032}{family} \markbox{4033}{of} \markbox{4034}{uniformly} \markbox{4035}{coarsely} \markbox{4036}{Lipschitz} \markbox{4037}{projections} \markbox{m4038}{$\pi_U:\calX \to \calC(U)$}, \markbox{4039}{and} \markbox{4040}{those} \markbox{4041}{projections,} \markbox{4042}{along} \markbox{4043}{with} \markbox{4044}{certain} \markbox{4045}{relations} \markbox{4046}{on} \markbox{4047}{the} \markbox{4048}{family} \markbox{m4049}{$\mathfrak S$}, \markbox{4050}{largely} \markbox{4051}{control} \markbox{4052}{the} \markbox{4053}{coarse} \markbox{4054}{geometry} \markbox{4055}{of} \markbox{m4056}{$\calX$}.

The \markbox{4057}{following} \markbox{4058}{extracts} \markbox{4059}{some} \markbox{4060}{of} \markbox{4061}{the} \markbox{4062}{properties} \markbox{4063}{we} \markbox{4064}{need} \markbox{4065}{from} \markbox{4066}{the} \markbox{4067}{axiomatic} \markbox{4068}{setup} \cite{HHS_II}, \markbox{4069}{see} \cite{Sisto_HHS} \markbox{4070}{for} \markbox{4071}{a} discussion.


\begin{enumerate}

\item For \markbox{4072}{each} \markbox{m4073}{$U \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4074}{there} \markbox{4075}{exist} \markbox{4076}{an} \markbox{m4077}{$\ES$}-hyperbolic \markbox{4078}{space} \markbox{m4079}{$\calC(U
)$} \markbox{4080}{and} \markbox{4081}{a} \markbox{m4082}{$\ES$}-coarsely \markbox{4083}{surjective} \markbox{m4084}{$(\ES,\ES)$}-coarsely \markbox{4085}{Lipschitz} \markbox{4086}{map} \markbox{m4087}{$\pi_U: \calX \rightarrow \calC(U),$} \markbox{4088}{with} \markbox{m4089}{$\ES$} \markbox{4090}{independent} \markbox{4091}{of} \markbox{m4092}{$U$}.

    \item The \markbox{4093}{set} \markbox{m4094}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{4095}{has} \markbox{4096}{the} \markbox{4097}{following} relations:
    \begin{itemize}
        \item It \markbox{4098}{is} \markbox{4099}{equipped} \markbox{4100}{with} \markbox{4101}{a} \markbox{4102}{partial} \markbox{4103}{order} \markbox{m4104}{$\nest$} \markbox{4105}{called} \emph{nesting}. \markbox{4106}{If} \markbox{m4107}{$\mathfrak S \neq \emptyset,$} \markbox{4108}{the} \markbox{4109}{set} \markbox{m4110}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{4111}{contains} \markbox{4112}{a} \markbox{4113}{unique} \markbox{m4114}{$\nest$}-maximal \markbox{4115}{element} \markbox{m4116}{$S.$}
        
        \item It \markbox{4117}{has} \markbox{4118}{a} \markbox{4119}{symmetric,} \markbox{4120}{anti-reflexive} \markbox{4121}{relation} \markbox{m4122}{$\perp$} \markbox{4123}{called} \emph{orthogonality}. \markbox{4124}{If} \markbox{m4125}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{4126}{then} \markbox{m4127}{$U,V$} \markbox{4128}{are} \markbox{4129}{not} \markbox{4130}{related} \markbox{4131}{via} \markbox{m4132}{$\perp$}. \markbox{4133}{Furthermore,} \markbox{4134}{domains} \markbox{4135}{have} \emph{orthogonal containers}: \markbox{4136}{if} \markbox{m4137}{$U \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4138}{and} \markbox{4139}{there} \markbox{4140}{is} \markbox{4141}{a} \markbox{4142}{domain} \markbox{4143}{orthogonal} \markbox{4144}{to} \markbox{m4145}{$U$} \markbox{4146}{then} \markbox{4147}{there} \markbox{4148}{is} \markbox{4149}{a} \markbox{4150}{domain} \markbox{m4151}{$W$} \markbox{4152}{such} \markbox{4153}{that} \markbox{m4154}{$V \nest W$} \markbox{4155}{whenever} \markbox{m4156}{$V \perp U.$}
        
        \item For \markbox{4157}{any} \markbox{4158}{distinct} \markbox{m4159}{$ U, V \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4160}{unrelated} \markbox{4161}{via} \markbox{m4162}{$\perp, \nest$}, \markbox{4163}{then} \markbox{4164}{we} \markbox{4165}{say} \markbox{m4166}{$U,V$} \markbox{4167}{are} \emph{transverse} \markbox{4168}{and} \markbox{4169}{write} \markbox{m4170}{$U  \pitchfork V.$} 
     
        \end{itemize}
          
        \item There \markbox{4171}{exists} \markbox{4172}{an} \markbox{4173}{integer} \markbox{4174}{called} \markbox{4175}{the} \emph{complexity} \markbox{4176}{of} \markbox{m4177}{$\calX$} \markbox{4178}{and} \markbox{4179}{denoted} \markbox{m4180}{$\xi(\mathfrak S)$} \markbox{4181}{such} \markbox{4182}{that} \markbox{4183}{whenever} \markbox{m4184}{$U_1,U_2,\cdots U_n$} \markbox{4185}{is} \markbox{4186}{a} \markbox{4187}{collection} \markbox{4188}{of} \markbox{4189}{pairwise} \markbox{4190}{non-transverse} \markbox{4191}{domains,} \markbox{4192}{then} \markbox{m4193}{$n \leq \xi(\mathfrak S).$}
        
        \item If \markbox{m4194}{$U  \sqsubset V$} \markbox{4195}{or} \markbox{m4196}{$U  \pitchfork V,$} \markbox{4197}{then} \markbox{4198}{there} \markbox{4199}{exists} \markbox{4200}{a} \markbox{4201}{set} \markbox{m4202}{$\rho^U_V$} \markbox{4203}{of} \markbox{4204}{diameter} \markbox{4205}{at} \markbox{4206}{most} \markbox{m4207}{$\ES$} \markbox{4208}{in} \markbox{m4209}{$\calC(V)$}.
        
        \item If \markbox{m4210}{$U  \sqsubset V$}, \markbox{4211}{there} \markbox{4212}{is} \markbox{4213}{a} \markbox{4214}{map} \markbox{m4215}{$\rho^V_U:\calC(V) \rightarrow \calC(U)$}, \markbox{4216}{called} \markbox{4217}{the} \emph{relative projection} \markbox{4218}{of} \markbox{m4219}{$U$} \markbox{4220}{to} \markbox{m4221}{$V$} \markbox{4222}{which} \markbox{4223}{satisfies} \markbox{4224}{the} \markbox{4225}{following:} \markbox{4226}{For} \markbox{m4227}{$x \in \calX$} \markbox{4228}{with} \markbox{m4229}{$d_{ V}(\pi_V(x),\rho^U_V)>\ES,$} \markbox{4230}{we} \markbox{4231}{have} \markbox{m4232}{$\pi_U(x) \underset{\ES}{\asymp} \rho^V_U(\pi_V(x)).$}

        
        


\end{enumerate}

For \markbox{4233}{two} \markbox{4234}{points} \markbox{m4235}{$x,y \in \calX,$} \markbox{4236}{it} \markbox{4237}{is} \markbox{4238}{standard} \markbox{4239}{to} \markbox{4240}{use} \markbox{m4241}{$d_U(x,y)$} \markbox{4242}{to} \markbox{4243}{denote} \markbox{m4244}{$d_{\calC(U)}(\pi_U(x), \pi_U(y)),$} \markbox{4245}{and} \markbox{4246}{similarly} \markbox{4247}{for} \markbox{4248}{subsets} \markbox{4249}{of} \markbox{m4250}{$\calX.$} \markbox{4251}{For} \markbox{4252}{a} \markbox{4253}{subset} \markbox{m4254}{$A \subseteq \calX,$} \markbox{4255}{we} \markbox{4256}{will} \markbox{4257}{also} \markbox{4258}{use} \markbox{m4259}{$\diam_U(A)$} \markbox{4260}{to} \markbox{4261}{denote} \markbox{4262}{the} \markbox{4263}{diameter} \markbox{4264}{of} \markbox{4265}{the} \markbox{4266}{set} \markbox{m4267}{$\pi_U(A) \subset \calC(U)$}.

\subsection{Basic HHS facts}

We \markbox{4268}{now} \markbox{4269}{collect} \markbox{4270}{some} \markbox{4271}{useful} \markbox{4272}{facts} \markbox{4273}{about} \markbox{4274}{HHSes} \markbox{4275}{from} \markbox{4276}{various} \markbox{4277}{places.} \medskip

The \markbox{4278}{following} \markbox{4279}{definition} \markbox{4280}{from} \cite{Beh:thesis, BKMM:qirigid, HHS_II}, \markbox{4281}{will} \markbox{4282}{be} \markbox{4283}{important} \markbox{4284}{for} \markbox{4285}{us.}  \markbox{4286}{The} \markbox{4287}{idea} \markbox{4288}{here} \markbox{4289}{is} \markbox{4290}{that} \markbox{4291}{we} \markbox{4292}{want} \markbox{4293}{to} \markbox{4294}{combine} \markbox{4295}{all} \markbox{4296}{of} \markbox{4297}{the} \markbox{4298}{projections} \markbox{m4299}{$\pi_U:\calX \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{4300}{for} \markbox{4301}{each} \markbox{m4302}{$U \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4303}{into} \markbox{4304}{a} \markbox{4305}{global} \markbox{4306}{projection} \markbox{m4307}{$\Pi:\calX \to \prod_U \calC(U)$}.  \markbox{4308}{The} \markbox{4309}{following} \markbox{4310}{definition} \markbox{4311}{uses} \markbox{4312}{the} \markbox{4313}{relations} \markbox{4314}{on} \markbox{m4315}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{4316}{to} \markbox{4317}{constrain} \markbox{4318}{tuples} \markbox{4319}{in} \markbox{m4320}{$\prod_U \calC(U)$}.

\begin{definition}[Consistent tuple]\label{defn:consistency}
Let \markbox{m4321}{$\kappa\geq 0$} \markbox{4322}{and} \markbox{4323}{let} \markbox{m4324}{$(b_U)\in\prod_{U\in\mathfrak S}2^{\calC(U)}$} \markbox{4325}{be} \markbox{4326}{a} \markbox{4327}{tuple} \markbox{4328}{such} \markbox{4329}{that} \markbox{4330}{for} \markbox{4331}{each} \markbox{m4332}{$U\in\mathfrak S$}, 
the \markbox{m4333}{$U$}--coordinate  \markbox{m4334}{$b_U$} \markbox{4335}{has} \markbox{4336}{diameter} \markbox{m4337}{$\leq\kappa$}.  \markbox{4338}{Then} \markbox{m4339}{$(b_U)$} \markbox{4340}{is} \textbf{\em $\kappa$--consistent} \markbox{4341}{if} \markbox{4342}{for} \markbox{4343}{all} 
\markbox{m4344}{$V,W\in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{4345}{we} \markbox{4346}{have} $$\min\{\dist_V(b_V,\rho^W_V),\dist_W(b_W,\rho^V_W)\}\leq\kappa$$ \markbox{4347}{whenever} \markbox{m4348}{$V\pitchfork W$} \markbox{4349}{and} 
$$\min\{\dist_W(x,\rho^V_W),\diam_V(b_V\cup\rho^W_V)\}\leq\kappa$$ \markbox{4350}{whenever} \markbox{m4351}{$V\nest W$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item We \markbox{4352}{refer} \markbox{4353}{to} \markbox{4354}{the} \markbox{4355}{above} \markbox{4356}{inequalities} \markbox{4357}{as} \markbox{4358}{the} \emph{consistency inequalities}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}




\medskip


The \markbox{4359}{following} \markbox{4360}{is} \markbox{4361}{a} \markbox{4362}{key} \markbox{4363}{fact} \markbox{4364}{for} \markbox{4365}{us.}  \markbox{4366}{It} \markbox{4367}{says} \markbox{4368}{that} \markbox{4369}{the} \markbox{4370}{image} \markbox{4371}{of} \markbox{m4372}{$\Pi:\calX \to \prod_U \calC(U)$} \markbox{4373}{consists} \markbox{4374}{of} \markbox{4375}{uniformly} \markbox{4376}{consistent} tuples:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:base consistency}
There \markbox{4377}{exists} \markbox{m4378}{$\theta = \theta(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{4379}{so} \markbox{4380}{that} \markbox{4381}{if} \markbox{m4382}{$x \in \calX$}, \markbox{4383}{then} \markbox{4384}{the} \markbox{4385}{tuple} \markbox{m4386}{$(\pi_U(x)) \in \prod_{U \in \mathfrak S} \calC(U)$} \markbox{4387}{is} \markbox{m4388}{$\theta$}-consistent.
\end{lemma}


On \markbox{4389}{the} \markbox{4390}{other} \markbox{4391}{hand,} \markbox{4392}{we} \markbox{4393}{would} \markbox{4394}{like} \markbox{4395}{to} \markbox{4396}{know} \markbox{4397}{whether} \markbox{4398}{all} \markbox{4399}{consistent} \markbox{4400}{tuples} \markbox{4401}{in} \markbox{m4402}{$\prod_U \calC(U)$} \markbox{4403}{essentially} \markbox{4404}{come} \markbox{4405}{from} \markbox{m4406}{$\calX$}.  \markbox{4407}{That} \markbox{4408}{is} \markbox{4409}{the} \markbox{4410}{content} \markbox{4411}{of} \markbox{4412}{the} \markbox{4413}{following} \markbox{4414}{Realization} \markbox{4415}{Theorem.}  \markbox{4416}{In} \markbox{4417}{particular,} \markbox{4418}{says} \markbox{4419}{that} \markbox{4420}{any} \markbox{4421}{tuple} \markbox{4422}{satisfying} \markbox{4423}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency} \markbox{4424}{can} \markbox{4425}{be} \markbox{4426}{coarsely} \markbox{4427}{realized} \markbox{4428}{via} \markbox{4429}{a} \markbox{4430}{point} \markbox{4431}{in} \markbox{m4432}{$\calX$}.  \markbox{4433}{It} \markbox{4434}{is} \cite[Theorem 4.3]{BKMM:qirigid} \markbox{4435}{for} \markbox{4436}{mapping} \markbox{4437}{class} \markbox{4438}{groups,} \cite[Theorem 3.2]{EMR:rank} \markbox{4439}{for} Teichm\"uller \markbox{4440}{space} \markbox{4441}{with} \markbox{4442}{the} Teichm\"uller \markbox{4443}{metric,} \markbox{4444}{and} \cite[Theorem 3.1]{HHS_II} \markbox{4445}{for} \markbox{4446}{the} \markbox{4447}{general} \markbox{4448}{HHS} case:

\begin{theorem}[Realization]\label{thm:realization}
For \markbox{4449}{each} \markbox{m4450}{$\kappa \geq 1$} \markbox{4451}{there} \markbox{4452}{exists} \markbox{m4453}{$\theta_e, \theta_u \geq 0$} \markbox{4454}{such} \markbox{4455}{that} \markbox{4456}{the} \markbox{4457}{following} \markbox{4458}{holds.}  \markbox{4459}{Let} \markbox{m4460}{$\mathbf{b} = (b_U)_{U \in \mathfrak S} \in \prod_{U \in \mathfrak S} 2^{\calC(U)}$} \markbox{4461}{be} \markbox{m4462}{$\kappa$}-consistent.

Then \markbox{4463}{there} \markbox{4464}{exists} \markbox{m4465}{$x \in X$} \markbox{4466}{so} \markbox{4467}{that} \markbox{m4468}{$d_U(b_U, \pi_W(x)) \leq \theta_e$} \markbox{4469}{for} \markbox{4470}{all} \markbox{m4471}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{4472}{Moreover,} \markbox{m4473}{$x$} \markbox{4474}{is} \emph{coarsely unique} \markbox{4475}{in} \markbox{4476}{the} \markbox{4477}{sense} \markbox{4478}{that} 
$$\diam_{\calX} \{x \in \calX| d_W(b_W, \pi_W(x)) \leq \theta_e \textrm{ for all } U \in \mathfrak S\} < \theta_u.$$
\end{theorem}

\begin{remark}
Notably, \markbox{4479}{the} \markbox{4480}{proof} \markbox{4481}{of} \markbox{4482}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization} \markbox{4483}{in} \cite{HHS_II} \markbox{4484}{does} \markbox{4485}{not} \markbox{4486}{involve} \markbox{4487}{the} \markbox{4488}{hyperbolicity} \markbox{4489}{of} \markbox{4490}{the} \markbox{4491}{associated} \markbox{4492}{spaces} \markbox{m4493}{$\{\calC(U)\}_{U \in \mathfrak S}$}, \markbox{4494}{and} \markbox{4495}{actually} \markbox{4496}{follows} \markbox{4497}{from} \markbox{4498}{a} \markbox{4499}{weak} \markbox{4500}{form} \markbox{4501}{which} \markbox{4502}{is} \markbox{4503}{axiomatized} \markbox{4504}{into} \markbox{4505}{the} \markbox{4506}{HHS} \markbox{4507}{setup.}  \markbox{4508}{In} \markbox{4509}{this} \markbox{4510}{sense,} \markbox{4511}{realization} \markbox{4512}{is} \markbox{4513}{a} \markbox{4514}{purely} \markbox{4515}{hierarchical} \markbox{4516}{fact} \markbox{4517}{which} \markbox{4518}{plays} \markbox{4519}{a} \markbox{4520}{similar} \markbox{4521}{role} \markbox{4522}{to} \markbox{4523}{the} \markbox{4524}{existence} \markbox{4525}{of} \markbox{4526}{a} \markbox{4527}{coarse} \markbox{4528}{median} \markbox{4529}{in} Bowditch's \markbox{4530}{analysis} \cite{Bowditch_hulls}.


\end{remark}

Perhaps \markbox{4531}{the} \markbox{4532}{main} \markbox{4533}{technique} \markbox{4534}{in} \markbox{4535}{HHSes} \markbox{4536}{is} \markbox{4537}{taking} \markbox{4538}{an} \markbox{4539}{object} \markbox{4540}{in} \markbox{4541}{the} \markbox{4542}{ambient} \markbox{4543}{space} \markbox{m4544}{$\calX$} \markbox{4545}{and} \markbox{4546}{projecting} \markbox{4547}{it} \markbox{4548}{to} \markbox{4549}{all} \markbox{4550}{of} \markbox{4551}{the} \markbox{4552}{hyperbolic} \markbox{4553}{spaces,} \markbox{4554}{doing} \markbox{4555}{hyperbolic} \markbox{4556}{geometry,} \markbox{4557}{and} \markbox{4558}{then} \markbox{4559}{reassembling} \markbox{4560}{the} \markbox{4561}{pieces} \markbox{4562}{via} \markbox{4563}{hierarchical} \markbox{4564}{tools} \markbox{4565}{like} \markbox{4566}{the} \markbox{4567}{Realization} \markbox{4568}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization}.  \markbox{4569}{Toward} \markbox{4570}{that} \markbox{4571}{end,} \markbox{4572}{and} \markbox{4573}{recognizing} \markbox{4574}{that} \markbox{4575}{HHSes} \markbox{4576}{are} \markbox{4577}{fundamentally} \markbox{4578}{coarse} \markbox{4579}{spaces,} \markbox{4580}{we} \markbox{4581}{will} \markbox{4582}{usually} \markbox{4583}{want} \markbox{4584}{to} \markbox{4585}{restrict} \markbox{4586}{ourselves} \markbox{4587}{to} \markbox{4588}{the} \emph{relevant} \markbox{4589}{collection} \markbox{4590}{of} \markbox{4591}{hyperbolic} \markbox{4592}{spaces} \markbox{4593}{to} \markbox{4594}{which} \markbox{4595}{an} \markbox{4596}{object} \markbox{4597}{has} \markbox{4598}{a} \markbox{4599}{sufficiently} \markbox{4600}{large} projection.

\begin{definition}[Relevant domains] \label{defn:relevant}
Given \markbox{4601}{a} \markbox{4602}{subset} \markbox{m4603}{$A \subset \calX$} \markbox{4604}{and} \markbox{m4605}{$K > 0$}, \markbox{4606}{we} \markbox{4607}{say} \markbox{4608}{that} \markbox{m4609}{$U \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4610}{is} \markbox{m4611}{$K$}-\emph{relevant} \markbox{4612}{for} \markbox{m4613}{$A$} \markbox{4614}{if} \markbox{m4615}{$\diam_U(A) \geq K$}.  \markbox{4616}{We} \markbox{4617}{denote} \markbox{4618}{the} \markbox{4619}{set} \markbox{4620}{of} \markbox{m4621}{$K$}-relevant \markbox{4622}{domains} \markbox{4623}{for} \markbox{m4624}{$A$} \markbox{4625}{by} \markbox{m4626}{$\Rel_K(A)$}.
\end{definition}


The \markbox{4627}{following} \markbox{4628}{Passing-Up} \markbox{4629}{lemma} \markbox{4630}{is} \markbox{4631}{a} \markbox{4632}{foundational} \markbox{4633}{fact} \markbox{4634}{about} \markbox{4635}{HHSes;} \markbox{4636}{in} \markbox{4637}{fact,} \markbox{4638}{it} \markbox{4639}{can} \markbox{4640}{be} \markbox{4641}{taken} \markbox{4642}{to} \markbox{4643}{be} \markbox{4644}{an} \markbox{4645}{axiom} \cite[Proposition 4.15]{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{4646}{Roughly} \markbox{4647}{speaking,} \markbox{4648}{the} \markbox{4649}{passing-up} \markbox{4650}{lemma} \markbox{4651}{says} \markbox{4652}{that} \markbox{4653}{if} \markbox{m4654}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{4655}{have} \markbox{4656}{a} \markbox{4657}{large} \markbox{4658}{number} \markbox{4659}{of} \markbox{4660}{lower} \markbox{4661}{complexity} \markbox{4662}{relevant} \markbox{4663}{domains,} \markbox{4664}{then} \markbox{4665}{there} \markbox{4666}{must} \markbox{4667}{be} \markbox{4668}{some} \markbox{4669}{higher} \markbox{4670}{complexity} \markbox{4671}{relevant} \markbox{4672}{domain} \markbox{4673}{containing} \markbox{4674}{at} \markbox{4675}{least} \markbox{4676}{one} \markbox{4677}{of} \markbox{4678}{them,} \markbox{4679}{thereby} \markbox{4680}{allowing} \markbox{4681}{us} \markbox{4682}{to} ``pass up'' \markbox{4683}{the} \markbox{m4684}{$\nest$}-lattice.

\begin{lemma}[Passing-up]\label{lem:passing-up}
Let \markbox{m4685}{$\calX$} \markbox{4686}{be} \markbox{4687}{an} \markbox{4688}{HHS} \markbox{4689}{with} \markbox{4690}{constant} \markbox{m4691}{$\ES$}.  \markbox{4692}{For} \markbox{4693}{every} \markbox{m4694}{$D>0$} \markbox{4695}{there} \markbox{4696}{is} \markbox{4697}{an} \markbox{4698}{integer} \markbox{m4699}{$PU=PU(D)>0$} \markbox{4700}{such} \markbox{4701}{that} \markbox{4702}{if} \markbox{m4703}{$V \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4704}{and} \markbox{m4705}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{4706}{satisfy} \markbox{m4707}{$d_{U_i}(x,y)>\ES$} \markbox{4708}{for} \markbox{4709}{a} \markbox{4710}{collection} \markbox{4711}{of} \markbox{4712}{domains} \markbox{m4713}{$\{U_i\}_{i=1}^{PU}$} \markbox{4714}{with} \markbox{4715}{each} \markbox{m4716}{$U_i \in \mathfrak S_V$}, \markbox{4717}{then} \markbox{4718}{there} \markbox{4719}{exists} \markbox{m4720}{$W \in \mathfrak S_V$} \markbox{4721}{and} \markbox{m4722}{$i$} \markbox{4723}{with} \markbox{m4724}{$U_i \sqsubsetneq W$} \markbox{4725}{such} \markbox{4726}{that} \markbox{m4727}{$d_W(x,y)>D.$}
\end{lemma}

As \markbox{4728}{an} \markbox{4729}{example} \markbox{4730}{of} \markbox{4731}{how} \markbox{4732}{this} \markbox{4733}{lemma} \markbox{4734}{is} \markbox{4735}{foundational,} \markbox{4736}{we} \markbox{4737}{observe} \markbox{4738}{the} \markbox{4739}{following} \markbox{4740}{corollary.}  \markbox{4741}{The} \markbox{4742}{original} \markbox{4743}{proof} \markbox{4744}{is} \markbox{4745}{embedded} \markbox{4746}{in} \markbox{4747}{the} \markbox{4748}{proof} \markbox{4749}{of} \markbox{4750}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization} \markbox{4751}{in} \cite[Theorem 3.1]{HHS_II}, \markbox{4752}{but} \markbox{4753}{not} \markbox{4754}{explicitly} \markbox{4755}{stated.}  \markbox{4756}{We} \markbox{4757}{give} \markbox{4758}{a} \markbox{4759}{proof} \markbox{4760}{for} completeness:

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:rel sets are finite}
For \markbox{4761}{any} \markbox{m4762}{$x,y \in \calX$}, \markbox{4763}{the} \markbox{4764}{set} \markbox{m4765}{$\Rel_{\ES}(x,y)$} \markbox{4766}{is} finite.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Let \markbox{m4767}{$C$} \markbox{4768}{be} \markbox{4769}{the} \markbox{4770}{coarse} \markbox{4771}{Lipschitz} \markbox{4772}{constant} \markbox{4773}{for} \markbox{4774}{all} \markbox{4775}{of} \markbox{4776}{the} \markbox{4777}{projections} \markbox{m4778}{$\pi_U$} \markbox{4779}{for} \markbox{m4780}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{4781}{and} \markbox{4782}{set} \markbox{m4783}{$D > C d_{\calX}(x,y) + C$}.  \markbox{4784}{If} \markbox{m4785}{$\# \Rel_{\ES}(x,y) > P(D)$}, \markbox{4786}{then} \markbox{4787}{the} \markbox{4788}{Passing-Up} \markbox{4789}{Lemma} \ref{lem:passing-up} \markbox{4790}{provides} \markbox{4791}{a} \markbox{4792}{domain} \markbox{m4793}{$W \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4794}{with} \markbox{m4795}{$d_W(x,y)>D$}, \markbox{4796}{which} \markbox{4797}{is} impossible.
\end{proof}

Another \markbox{4798}{fundamental} \markbox{4799}{fact} \markbox{4800}{about} \markbox{4801}{HHSes} \markbox{4802}{is} \markbox{4803}{the} \markbox{4804}{following} \markbox{4805}{distance} \markbox{4806}{formula,} \markbox{4807}{which} \markbox{4808}{originated} \markbox{4809}{in} \markbox{4810}{work} \markbox{4811}{of} \markbox{4812}{Masur-Minsky} \cite{MM00}, \markbox{4813}{and} \markbox{4814}{found} \markbox{4815}{various} \markbox{4816}{iterations} \markbox{4817}{elsewhere} \cite{Brock, Rafi:combo, Dur:augmented, kim2014geometry} \markbox{4818}{before} \markbox{4819}{being} \markbox{4820}{generalized} \markbox{4821}{to} \markbox{4822}{all} \markbox{4823}{HHSes} \markbox{4824}{in} \cite{HHS_II}.  \markbox{4825}{See} \cite[Theorem 4.5]{HHS_II} \markbox{4826}{for} \markbox{4827}{a} \markbox{4828}{proof} \markbox{4829}{from} \markbox{4830}{the} \markbox{4831}{now-standard} \markbox{4832}{HHS} \markbox{4833}{setup,} \markbox{4834}{and} \markbox{4835}{also} \cite[Theorem 1.2]{Bowditch_hulls} \markbox{4836}{and} \cite[Corollary C]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{4837}{from} \markbox{4838}{proofs} \markbox{4839}{using} \markbox{4840}{cubical} \markbox{4841}{model} \markbox{4842}{techniques,} \markbox{4843}{which} \markbox{4844}{we} \markbox{4845}{also} \markbox{4846}{recover} \markbox{4847}{here} \markbox{4848}{below} \markbox{4849}{in} \markbox{4850}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF lower bound}.

\begin{theorem}[Distance formula]\label{thm:DF}
There \markbox{4851}{exists} \markbox{m4852}{$K_0 = K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{4853}{so} \markbox{4854}{that} \markbox{4855}{if} \markbox{m4856}{$K>K_0$} \markbox{4857}{and} \markbox{m4858}{$x,y \in \calX$}, then
$$d_{\calX}(x,y) \asymp \sum_{U \in \mathfrak S} [d_U(x,y)]_K$$
where \markbox{4859}{the} \markbox{4860}{coarse} \markbox{4861}{equality} \markbox{m4862}{$\asymp$} \markbox{4863}{depends} \markbox{4864}{only} \markbox{4865}{on} \markbox{m4866}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{4867}{and} \markbox{m4868}{$K$}.
\end{theorem}

Philosophically \markbox{4869}{(for} \markbox{4870}{our} \markbox{4871}{purposes),} \markbox{4872}{the} \markbox{4873}{distance} \markbox{4874}{formula} \markbox{4875}{says} \markbox{4876}{that} \markbox{4877}{if} \markbox{4878}{we} \markbox{4879}{want} \markbox{4880}{to} \markbox{4881}{understand} \markbox{4882}{how} \markbox{4883}{to} \markbox{4884}{move} \markbox{4885}{between} \markbox{4886}{two} \markbox{4887}{points} \markbox{4888}{in} \markbox{4889}{an} \markbox{4890}{HHS,} \markbox{4891}{it} \markbox{4892}{should} \markbox{4893}{be} \markbox{4894}{enough} \markbox{4895}{to} \markbox{4896}{focus} \markbox{4897}{on} \markbox{4898}{the} \markbox{4899}{set} \markbox{4900}{of} \markbox{4901}{relevant} \markbox{4902}{domains} \markbox{4903}{between} \markbox{4904}{them.} 

The \markbox{4905}{next} \markbox{4906}{definition} \markbox{4907}{is} \markbox{4908}{of} \markbox{4909}{a} \markbox{4910}{special} \markbox{4911}{kind} \markbox{4912}{of} \markbox{4913}{path} \markbox{4914}{in} \markbox{4915}{an} \markbox{4916}{HHS.}  \markbox{4917}{The} \markbox{4918}{proof} \markbox{4919}{of} \markbox{4920}{their} \markbox{4921}{existence} \markbox{4922}{is} \markbox{4923}{always} \markbox{4924}{tied} \markbox{4925}{up} \markbox{4926}{in} \markbox{4927}{the} \markbox{4928}{proof} \markbox{4929}{of} \markbox{4930}{the} \markbox{4931}{more} \markbox{4932}{difficult} \markbox{4933}{bound} \markbox{4934}{of} \markbox{4935}{the} \markbox{4936}{distance} \markbox{4937}{formula,} \markbox{4938}{as} \markbox{4939}{is} \markbox{4940}{the} \markbox{4941}{case} \markbox{4942}{in} \markbox{4943}{this} \markbox{4944}{paper} \markbox{4945}{in} \markbox{4946}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:HP and DF}.  \markbox{4947}{Otherwise,} \markbox{4948}{we} \markbox{4949}{will} \markbox{4950}{not} \markbox{4951}{need} \markbox{4952}{this} notion.

\begin{definition}\label{defn:hp}
A \markbox{4953}{path} \markbox{m4954}{$\gamma:I \to \calX$} \markbox{4955}{in} \markbox{4956}{an} \markbox{4957}{HHS} \markbox{m4958}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{4959}{is} \markbox{4960}{a} \markbox{m4961}{$L$}-\emph{hierarchy path} \markbox{4962}{if} \markbox{4963}{its} \markbox{4964}{projection} \markbox{m4965}{$\pi_U(\gamma) \subset \calC(U)$} \markbox{4966}{is} \markbox{4967}{an} \markbox{4968}{unparameterized} \markbox{m4969}{$(L,L)$}-quasi-geodesic \markbox{4970}{for} \markbox{4971}{each} \markbox{m4972}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}.
\end{definition}

We \markbox{4973}{end} \markbox{4974}{this} \markbox{4975}{subsection} \markbox{4976}{with} \markbox{4977}{a} \markbox{4978}{basic} \markbox{4979}{observation,} \markbox{4980}{which} \markbox{4981}{generalizes} \markbox{4982}{the} \markbox{4983}{observation} \markbox{4984}{that} \markbox{4985}{if} \markbox{4986}{two} \markbox{4987}{subsurfaces} \markbox{m4988}{$U,V$} \markbox{4989}{are} \markbox{4990}{not} \markbox{4991}{transverse,} \markbox{4992}{then} \markbox{4993}{their} \markbox{4994}{boundary} \markbox{4995}{curves} \markbox{4996}{must} \markbox{4997}{be} \markbox{4998}{disjoint} \markbox{4999}{up} \markbox{5000}{to} isotopy.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:rho control}
Suppose \markbox{5001}{that} \markbox{m5002}{$U,V,W \in \Rel_{K_0}(a,b)$} \markbox{5003}{for} \markbox{m5004}{$a,b \in \calX$}.
\begin{enumerate}
\item If \markbox{m5005}{$U, V \nest W$} \markbox{5006}{and} \markbox{m5007}{$U,V$} \markbox{5008}{are} \markbox{5009}{not} \markbox{5010}{transverse,} \markbox{5011}{then} \markbox{m5012}{$d_W(\rho^U_W, \rho^V_W) < \ES$}.
\item If \markbox{m5013}{$U \pitchfork V$} \markbox{5014}{and} \markbox{m5015}{$W \nest V$} \markbox{5016}{with} \markbox{m5017}{$W,U$} \markbox{5018}{not} \markbox{5019}{orthogonal,} \markbox{5020}{then} \markbox{m5021}{$d_U(\rho^V_W, \rho^W_U)<\ES$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{lemma}

Finally, \markbox{5022}{we} \markbox{5023}{end} \markbox{5024}{with} \markbox{5025}{a} \markbox{5026}{key} \markbox{5027}{HHS} \markbox{5028}{axiom,} \markbox{5029}{originally} \markbox{5030}{proven} \markbox{5031}{for} \markbox{5032}{mapping} \markbox{5033}{class} \markbox{5034}{groups} \markbox{5035}{in} \cite[Theorem 3.1]{MM_II}:

\begin{axiom}[Bounded \markbox{5036}{geodesic} image]\label{ax:BGIA}  \markbox{5037}{If} \markbox{m5038}{$U  \sqsubset V$} \markbox{5039}{and} \markbox{m5040}{$\gamma \in \calC(V)$} \markbox{5041}{is} \markbox{5042}{a} \markbox{5043}{geodesic} \markbox{5044}{with} \markbox{m5045}{$d_{V}(\rho^U_V,\gamma)>\ES$}, \markbox{5046}{then} diam\markbox{m5047}{$(\rho^V_U(\gamma))\leq \ES.$} \markbox{5048}{Furthermore,} \markbox{5049}{for} \markbox{5050}{any} \markbox{m5051}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{5052}{and} \markbox{5053}{any} \markbox{5054}{geodesic} \markbox{m5055}{$\gamma$} \markbox{5056}{connecting} \markbox{m5057}{$\pi_V(x),\pi_V(y)$}, \markbox{5058}{if} \markbox{m5059}{$d_{V}(\rho^U_V,\gamma)>\ES$}, \markbox{5060}{then} \markbox{m5061}{$d(\pi_U(x), \pi_U(y)) \leq \ES.$}
\end{axiom} 

\subsection{Hierarchical hulls and related basic facts}

In \markbox{5062}{our} \markbox{5063}{HHS} \markbox{5064}{setup,} \markbox{5065}{the} \markbox{5066}{basic} \markbox{5067}{object} \markbox{5068}{we} \markbox{5069}{will} \markbox{5070}{want} \markbox{5071}{to} \markbox{5072}{consider} \markbox{5073}{is} \markbox{5074}{the} \markbox{5075}{following} \markbox{5076}{hierarchical} \markbox{5077}{notion} \markbox{5078}{of} \markbox{5079}{a} \markbox{5080}{coarse} \markbox{5081}{convex} \markbox{5082}{hull.}  \markbox{5083}{These} \emph{hierarchical hulls} \markbox{5084}{are} \markbox{5085}{built} \markbox{5086}{out} \markbox{5087}{of} \markbox{5088}{consistent} \markbox{5089}{tuples} \markbox{5090}{of} \markbox{5091}{points} \markbox{5092}{whose} \markbox{5093}{coordinates} \markbox{5094}{are} \markbox{5095}{contained} \markbox{5096}{in} \markbox{5097}{the} \markbox{5098}{hyperbolic} \markbox{5099}{hulls} \markbox{5100}{in} \markbox{5101}{each} \markbox{5102}{domain.}  \markbox{5103}{More} \markbox{5104}{specifically,} \markbox{5105}{given} \markbox{5106}{a} \markbox{5107}{pair} \markbox{5108}{of} \markbox{5109}{points} \markbox{m5110}{$x,y \in \calX$}, \markbox{5111}{for} \markbox{5112}{each,} \markbox{m5113}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{5114}{we} \markbox{5115}{set} \markbox{m5116}{$H_U = \hull_U(\pi_U(\{x,y\}))$}, \markbox{5117}{where} \markbox{m5118}{$\hull_U$} \markbox{5119}{denotes} \markbox{5120}{the} \markbox{5121}{hyperbolic} \markbox{5122}{hull} \markbox{5123}{in} \markbox{m5124}{$\calC(U)$}.

\begin{definition}[Hierarchical hull]\label{defn:hier hull}
Given \markbox{5125}{a} \markbox{5126}{constant} \markbox{m5127}{$\theta>0$}, \markbox{5128}{we} \markbox{5129}{define} \markbox{5130}{the} \emph{$\theta$-hull} \markbox{5131}{of} \markbox{m5132}{$x,y$} \markbox{5133}{to} \markbox{5134}{be} \markbox{5135}{all} \markbox{m5136}{$z \in \calX$} \markbox{5137}{so} \markbox{5138}{that} \markbox{m5139}{$d_U(z, H_U)<\theta$} \markbox{5140}{for} \markbox{5141}{all} \markbox{m5142}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item We \markbox{5143}{denote} \markbox{5144}{the} \markbox{m5145}{$\theta$}-hull \markbox{5146}{of} \markbox{m5147}{$x,y$} \markbox{5148}{by} \markbox{m5149}{$H_{\theta} = \hull_{\theta}(x,y)$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

One \markbox{5150}{of} \markbox{5151}{the} \markbox{5152}{key} \markbox{5153}{facts} \markbox{5154}{about} \markbox{5155}{hierarchical} \markbox{5156}{hulls} \markbox{5157}{is} \markbox{5158}{that} \markbox{5159}{they} \markbox{5160}{are} \emph{hierarchically quasiconvex} \cite[Lemma 6.2]{HHS_II}, \markbox{5161}{see} \cite{russell2023convexity} \markbox{5162}{for} \markbox{5163}{more} \markbox{5164}{on} \markbox{5165}{convexity} \markbox{5166}{in} \markbox{5167}{HHSes.}  \markbox{5168}{We} \markbox{5169}{do} \markbox{5170}{not} \markbox{5171}{need} \markbox{5172}{this} \markbox{5173}{definition} \markbox{5174}{for} \markbox{5175}{our} \markbox{5176}{purposes,} \markbox{5177}{but} \markbox{5178}{we} \markbox{5179}{do} \markbox{5180}{need} \markbox{5181}{the} \markbox{5182}{following} consequence:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:gate retract}
For \markbox{5183}{any} \markbox{m5184}{$\theta>0$}, \markbox{5185}{there} \markbox{5186}{exists} \markbox{5187}{is} \markbox{5188}{a} \markbox{m5189}{$(J,J)$}-coarse \markbox{5190}{Lipschitz} \markbox{5191}{retract} \markbox{m5192}{$\gate_{H_{\theta}}:\calX \to H_{\theta}$}, \markbox{5193}{where} \markbox{m5194}{$J = J(\theta, \mathfrak S)>0$} .
\end{lemma}

In \markbox{5195}{the} \markbox{5196}{above} \markbox{5197}{lemma,} \markbox{5198}{the} \markbox{5199}{map} \markbox{m5200}{$\gate_{H_{\theta}}: \calX \to H_{\theta}$} \markbox{5201}{is} \markbox{5202}{a} \markbox{5203}{hierarchical} \markbox{5204}{analogue} \markbox{5205}{of} \markbox{5206}{a} \markbox{5207}{cubical} \markbox{5208}{gate} \markbox{5209}{map.}  \markbox{5210}{When} \markbox{m5211}{$z \in \calX$}, \markbox{5212}{the} \markbox{5213}{point} \markbox{m5214}{$\gate_{H_{\theta}}(z) \in H_{\theta}$} \markbox{5215}{is} \markbox{5216}{defined} \markbox{5217}{by} \markbox{5218}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{5219}{closest-point} \markbox{5220}{projection} \markbox{5221}{of} \markbox{m5222}{$\pi_U(z)$} \markbox{5223}{to} \markbox{m5224}{$H_U$} \markbox{5225}{and} \markbox{5226}{then} \markbox{5227}{applying} \markbox{5228}{the} \markbox{5229}{Realization} \markbox{5230}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization}; \markbox{5231}{see} \cite[Proposition 6.3]{HHS_II} \markbox{5232}{and} \markbox{5233}{the} \markbox{5234}{surrounding} \markbox{5235}{text} \markbox{5236}{for} details.







\subsection{Consequences of the Passing-up Lemma \ref{lem:passing-up}}

The \markbox{5237}{following} \markbox{5238}{statements} \markbox{5239}{are} \markbox{5240}{useful} \markbox{5241}{for} \markbox{5242}{the} \markbox{5243}{sort} \markbox{5244}{of} \markbox{5245}{distance} \markbox{5246}{formula} \markbox{5247}{related} \markbox{5248}{hierarchical} \markbox{5249}{accounting} \markbox{5250}{that} \markbox{5251}{we} \markbox{5252}{need} \markbox{5253}{to} \markbox{5254}{do} \markbox{5255}{the} \markbox{5256}{proof} \markbox{5257}{of} \markbox{5258}{the} \markbox{5259}{cubical} \markbox{5260}{model} \markbox{5261}{theorem.}  \markbox{5262}{The} \markbox{5263}{first} \markbox{5264}{says} \markbox{5265}{that} \markbox{5266}{any} \markbox{5267}{given} \markbox{5268}{relevant} \markbox{5269}{domain} \markbox{5270}{for} \markbox{5271}{a} \markbox{5272}{pair} \markbox{m5273}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{5274}{can} \markbox{5275}{only} \markbox{5276}{nest} \markbox{5277}{into} \markbox{5278}{boundedly-many} \markbox{5279}{other} \markbox{5280}{relevant} \markbox{5281}{domains} \markbox{5282}{for} \markbox{m5283}{$x,y$}.  \markbox{5284}{It} \markbox{5285}{first} \markbox{5286}{appeared} \markbox{5287}{in} \cite[Lemma 2.15]{DMS_bary}; \markbox{5288}{see} \cite[Lemma 11.13]{CRHK} \markbox{5289}{for} \markbox{5290}{a} \markbox{5291}{different} \markbox{5292}{proof} \markbox{5293}{and} \cite[Lemma 4.8]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{5294}{for} \markbox{5295}{a} \markbox{5296}{version} \markbox{5297}{that} \markbox{5298}{allows} \markbox{m5299}{$x,y$} \markbox{5300}{to} \markbox{5301}{be} \markbox{5302}{at} infinity.

\begin{lemma}[Covering]\label{lem:covering}
For \markbox{5303}{any} \markbox{5304}{HHS} \markbox{m5305}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$}, \markbox{5306}{there} \markbox{5307}{exists} \markbox{m5308}{$N = N(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{5309}{so} \markbox{5310}{that} \markbox{5311}{the} \markbox{5312}{following} \markbox{5313}{holds.}  \markbox{5314}{For} \markbox{5315}{any} \markbox{m5316}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{5317}{and} \markbox{5318}{all} \markbox{m5319}{$U \in \Rel_{50\ES}(x,y)$}, \markbox{5320}{there} \markbox{5321}{are} \markbox{5322}{at} \markbox{5323}{most} \markbox{m5324}{$N$} \markbox{5325}{domains} \markbox{m5326}{$V \in \Rel_{50\ES}(x,y)$} \markbox{5327}{so} \markbox{5328}{that} \markbox{m5329}{$U \nest V$}.
\end{lemma}

Another \markbox{5330}{consequence} \markbox{5331}{of} \markbox{5332}{Lemma} \ref{lem:passing-up} \markbox{5333}{is} \markbox{5334}{the} \markbox{5335}{following} \markbox{5336}{distance} \markbox{5337}{formula} \markbox{5338}{type} \markbox{5339}{statement,} \markbox{5340}{which} \markbox{5341}{is} \markbox{5342}{a} \markbox{5343}{less} \markbox{5344}{general} \markbox{5345}{version} \markbox{5346}{of} \cite[Proposition 4.14]{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{5347}{Roughly,} \markbox{5348}{it} \markbox{5349}{says} \markbox{5350}{that} \markbox{5351}{the} \markbox{5352}{number} \markbox{5353}{of} \markbox{5354}{medium-sized} \markbox{5355}{relevant} \markbox{5356}{domains} \markbox{5357}{for} \markbox{5358}{a} \markbox{5359}{pair} \markbox{m5360}{$x,y$} \markbox{5361}{can} \markbox{5362}{be} \markbox{5363}{accounted} \markbox{5364}{for} \markbox{5365}{(i.e.,} \markbox{5366}{in} \markbox{5367}{terms} \markbox{5368}{of} \markbox{5369}{the} \markbox{5370}{domain} \markbox{5371}{projections)} \markbox{5372}{by} \markbox{5373}{large-sized} \markbox{5374}{domains} \markbox{5375}{higher} \markbox{5376}{up} \markbox{5377}{the} \markbox{5378}{hierarchy} \markbox{5379}{in} \markbox{5380}{a} \markbox{5381}{precise} \markbox{5382}{fashion.}  

\begin{proposition}[Bounding \markbox{5383}{large} containers] \label{prop:bounding containers}
Let \markbox{m5384}{$K_1 >50\ES$}, \markbox{m5385}{$K_2 \geq K_1+47\ES$}, \markbox{5386}{and} \markbox{m5387}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{5388}{with} \markbox{m5389}{$\calU_1 = \Rel_{K_1}(x,y), \calU_2 = \Rel_{K_2}(x,y),$} \markbox{5390}{and} \markbox{m5391}{$\calV = \calU_1 - \calU_2$}.  \markbox{5392}{Then} \markbox{5393}{the} \markbox{5394}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
    \item For \markbox{5395}{all} \markbox{5396}{but} \markbox{m5397}{$PU(K_2)-1$} \markbox{5398}{domains} \markbox{m5399}{$V \in \calV$}, \markbox{5400}{there} \markbox{5401}{exists} \markbox{m5402}{$W \in \calU_2$} \markbox{5403}{with} \markbox{m5404}{$V \nest W$}.
    \item For \markbox{5405}{any} \markbox{m5406}{$W \in \calU_2$}, \markbox{5407}{if} \markbox{m5408}{$\calW = \{V \in \calV| V \nest W\}$} \markbox{5409}{then} \markbox{5410}{we} \markbox{5411}{have} \markbox{m5412}{$\#\calW \prec d_W(x,y)$} \markbox{5413}{with} \markbox{5414}{constants} \markbox{5415}{depending} \markbox{5416}{only} \markbox{5417}{on} \markbox{m5418}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{5419}{and} \markbox{m5420}{$K_2$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

The \markbox{5421}{above} \markbox{5422}{proposition} \markbox{5423}{is} \markbox{5424}{useful} \markbox{5425}{for} \markbox{5426}{proving} \markbox{5427}{the} \markbox{5428}{following} \markbox{5429}{slight} \markbox{5430}{generalization} \markbox{5431}{of} \markbox{5432}{the} \markbox{5433}{Distance} \markbox{5434}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}.  It's \markbox{5435}{useful} \markbox{5436}{for} \markbox{5437}{circumstances,} \markbox{5438}{such} \markbox{5439}{as} \markbox{5440}{in} \markbox{5441}{Section} \ref{subsec:Q qie}, \markbox{5442}{where} \markbox{5443}{we} \markbox{5444}{want} \markbox{5445}{to} \markbox{5446}{make} \markbox{5447}{distance} \markbox{5448}{formula-type} \markbox{5449}{arguments} \markbox{5450}{where} \markbox{5451}{the} \markbox{5452}{summands} \markbox{5453}{are} \markbox{5454}{only} \markbox{5455}{coarsely} \markbox{5456}{equal} \markbox{5457}{to} \markbox{5458}{the} \markbox{5459}{standard} \markbox{5460}{distance} \markbox{5461}{formula} \markbox{5462}{terms.}  \markbox{5463}{Probably} \markbox{5464}{the} \markbox{5465}{key} \markbox{5466}{example} \markbox{5467}{of} \markbox{5468}{this} \markbox{5469}{is} \markbox{5470}{when} \markbox{5471}{we} \markbox{5472}{want} \markbox{5473}{to} \markbox{5474}{replace} \markbox{m5475}{$d_U(x,y)$} \markbox{5476}{with} \markbox{m5477}{$d_{T_U}(x,y)$}, \markbox{5478}{where} \markbox{5479}{each} \markbox{m5480}{$T_U$} \markbox{5481}{is} \markbox{5482}{a} \markbox{5483}{uniform} \markbox{5484}{quasi-geodesic} \markbox{5485}{in} \markbox{m5486}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{5487}{between} \markbox{m5488}{$\pi_U(x)$} \markbox{5489}{and} \markbox{m5490}{$\pi_U(y)$}.  \markbox{5491}{This} \markbox{5492}{originally} \markbox{5493}{appeared} \markbox{5494}{in} \cite[Lemma 9.6]{Min_ELC} \markbox{5495}{for} \markbox{5496}{mapping} \markbox{5497}{class} \markbox{5498}{groups,} \markbox{5499}{and} \markbox{5500}{see} \cite[Theorem 2.9]{BHMS:kill_twists} \markbox{5501}{(which} \markbox{5502}{depends} \markbox{5503}{on} \markbox{5504}{the} \markbox{5505}{distance} \markbox{5506}{formula)} \markbox{5507}{and} \cite[Corollary 4.17]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{5508}{(which} \markbox{5509}{does} \markbox{5510}{not)} \markbox{5511}{for} \markbox{5512}{proofs} \markbox{5513}{in} \markbox{5514}{the} \markbox{5515}{HHS} setting.

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:DF replace}
Let \markbox{m5516}{$x,y \in \calX$}.  \markbox{5517}{Suppose} \markbox{5518}{that} \markbox{m5519}{$\sigma:\mathbb R_+ \to \mathbb R_+$} \markbox{5520}{is} \markbox{5521}{a} \markbox{5522}{function} \markbox{5523}{satisfying} 
$$\sigma(d_U(x,y)) \asymp d_U(x,y)$$
for \markbox{5524}{each} \markbox{m5525}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{5526}{where} \markbox{5527}{the} \markbox{5528}{constants} \markbox{5529}{in} \markbox{m5530}{$\asymp$} \markbox{5531}{are} \markbox{5532}{independent} \markbox{5533}{of} \markbox{m5534}{$U$}.  \markbox{5535}{Then} \markbox{5536}{for} \markbox{5537}{any} \markbox{m5538}{$K_1>50\ES$}, \markbox{5539}{we} have
$$\sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_1} \asymp \sum_{U \in \calU} [\sigma(d_U(x,y))]_{K_1}$$
where \markbox{5540}{the} \markbox{5541}{constants} \markbox{5542}{in} \markbox{m5543}{$\asymp$} \markbox{5544}{depend} \markbox{5545}{only} \markbox{5546}{on} \markbox{m5547}{$\mathfrak S$}, \markbox{m5548}{$K_1$}, \markbox{5549}{and} \markbox{m5550}{$\sigma$}.
\end{corollary}











\section{From hierarchical hulls to collapsed interval systems} \label{sec:interval systems}

In \markbox{5551}{the} \markbox{5552}{next} \markbox{5553}{three} \markbox{5554}{sections,} \markbox{5555}{we} \markbox{5556}{will} \markbox{5557}{give} \markbox{5558}{an} \markbox{5559}{overview} \markbox{5560}{of} \markbox{5561}{the} \markbox{5562}{cubical} \markbox{5563}{model} \markbox{5564}{construction} \markbox{5565}{for} \markbox{5566}{the} \markbox{5567}{hierarchical} \markbox{5568}{hull} \markbox{5569}{of} \markbox{5570}{a} \markbox{5571}{pair} \markbox{5572}{of} \markbox{5573}{points} \markbox{5574}{in} \markbox{5575}{an} \markbox{5576}{HHS} \markbox{5577}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{5578}{The} \markbox{5579}{original} \markbox{5580}{construction} \markbox{5581}{is} \markbox{5582}{due} \markbox{5583}{to} \markbox{5584}{Behrstock-Hagen-Sisto} \cite{HHS_quasi}, \markbox{5585}{and} \markbox{5586}{see} \markbox{5587}{also} \markbox{5588}{Bowditch} \cite{Bowditch_hulls} \markbox{5589}{for} \markbox{5590}{a} \markbox{5591}{version} \markbox{5592}{in} \markbox{5593}{the} \markbox{5594}{more} \markbox{5595}{general} \markbox{5596}{setting} \markbox{5597}{of} \markbox{5598}{coarse} \markbox{5599}{median} \markbox{5600}{spaces} \markbox{5601}{satisfying} \markbox{5602}{HHS-like} axioms.

The \markbox{5603}{main} \markbox{5604}{goal} \markbox{5605}{of} \markbox{5606}{this} \markbox{5607}{section} \markbox{5608}{is} \markbox{5609}{to} \markbox{5610}{explain} \markbox{5611}{how} \markbox{5612}{to} \markbox{5613}{take} \markbox{5614}{a} \markbox{5615}{pair} \markbox{5616}{of} \markbox{5617}{points} \markbox{m5618}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{5619}{in} \markbox{5620}{an} \markbox{5621}{HHS} \markbox{m5622}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{5623}{and} \markbox{5624}{produce} \markbox{5625}{a} \markbox{5626}{family} \markbox{5627}{of} \markbox{5628}{intervals} \markbox{5629}{which} \markbox{5630}{encode} \markbox{5631}{the} \markbox{5632}{relevant} \markbox{5633}{hierarchical} \markbox{5634}{data} \markbox{5635}{in} \markbox{5636}{a} \markbox{5637}{fairly} \markbox{5638}{efficient} \markbox{5639}{manner.}  \markbox{5640}{Roughly,} \markbox{5641}{the} \markbox{5642}{result} \markbox{5643}{of} \markbox{5644}{this} \markbox{5645}{process} \markbox{5646}{is} \markbox{5647}{a} \markbox{5648}{collection} \markbox{5649}{of} \markbox{5650}{intervals} \markbox{m5651}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{5652}{equipped} \markbox{5653}{with} \markbox{5654}{a} \markbox{5655}{family} \markbox{5656}{of} \markbox{5657}{relative} \markbox{5658}{projections} \markbox{5659}{satisfying} \markbox{5660}{certain} \markbox{5661}{HHS-like} \markbox{5662}{properties,} \markbox{5663}{where} \markbox{5664}{the} \markbox{5665}{index} \markbox{5666}{set} \markbox{m5667}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$} \markbox{5668}{is} \markbox{5669}{the} \markbox{5670}{set} \markbox{5671}{of} \markbox{m5672}{$K$}-relevant \markbox{5673}{domains} \markbox{5674}{for} \markbox{m5675}{$a,b$} \markbox{5676}{(Definition} \ref{defn:relevant}).  \markbox{5677}{For} \markbox{5678}{any} \markbox{5679}{such} \markbox{5680}{collection} \markbox{5681}{of} \markbox{5682}{intervals,} \markbox{5683}{one} \markbox{5684}{can} \markbox{5685}{define} \markbox{5686}{a} \markbox{5687}{notion} \markbox{5688}{of} \markbox{m5689}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{5690}{(an} \markbox{5691}{exact} \markbox{5692}{form} \markbox{5693}{of} \markbox{5694}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency}), \markbox{5695}{which} \markbox{5696}{defines} \markbox{5697}{a} \markbox{5698}{special} \markbox{m5699}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{5700}{subset} \markbox{m5701}{$\calQ$} \markbox{5702}{of} \markbox{5703}{the} \markbox{5704}{product} \markbox{m5705}{$\prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U$}.  \markbox{5706}{In} \markbox{5707}{Section} \ref{sec:hPsi qi} \markbox{5708}{below} \markbox{5709}{we} \markbox{5710}{will} \markbox{5711}{explain} \markbox{5712}{why} \markbox{5713}{this} \markbox{5714}{set} \markbox{m5715}{$\calQ$} \markbox{5716}{is} \markbox{5717}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{5718}{to} \markbox{5719}{the} \markbox{5720}{hierarchical} \markbox{5721}{hull} \markbox{5722}{of} \markbox{m5723}{$a,b$} \markbox{5724}{in} \markbox{m5725}{$\calX$}.  \markbox{5726}{Finally} \markbox{5727}{in} \markbox{5728}{Section} \ref{sec:cubulation}, \markbox{5729}{we} \markbox{5730}{will} \markbox{5731}{axiomatize} \markbox{5732}{the} \markbox{5733}{properties} \markbox{5734}{any} \markbox{5735}{such} \markbox{5736}{family} \markbox{5737}{of} \markbox{5738}{intervals} \markbox{5739}{satisfies,} \markbox{5740}{explain} \markbox{5741}{how} \markbox{5742}{it} \markbox{5743}{admits} \markbox{5744}{a} \markbox{5745}{natural} \markbox{5746}{wallspace} \markbox{5747}{structure,} \markbox{5748}{and} \markbox{5749}{show} \markbox{5750}{that} \markbox{5751}{the} \markbox{5752}{associated} \markbox{m5753}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{5754}{set} \markbox{m5755}{$\calQ$} \markbox{5756}{is} \markbox{5757}{isometric} \markbox{5758}{to} \markbox{5759}{the} \markbox{5760}{cubical} \markbox{5761}{dual} \markbox{5762}{of} \markbox{5763}{this} \markbox{5764}{wallspace.} 


\subsection{Basic setup of the section}

For \markbox{5765}{the} \markbox{5766}{rest} \markbox{5767}{of} \markbox{5768}{this} \markbox{5769}{section,} \markbox{5770}{we} \markbox{5771}{fix} \markbox{5772}{a} \markbox{5773}{constant} \markbox{m5774}{$K\geq K_0$}, \markbox{5775}{where} \markbox{m5776}{$K_0 = K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{5777}{is} \markbox{5778}{the} \markbox{5779}{constant} \markbox{5780}{from} \markbox{5781}{the} \markbox{5782}{Distance} \markbox{5783}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}.  \markbox{5784}{In} \markbox{5785}{this} \markbox{5786}{section,} \markbox{5787}{we} \markbox{5788}{will} \markbox{5789}{be} \markbox{5790}{able} \markbox{5791}{to} \markbox{5792}{allow} \markbox{m5793}{$K$} \markbox{5794}{to} \markbox{5795}{be} \markbox{5796}{as} \markbox{5797}{large} \markbox{5798}{as} necessary.

Fix \markbox{5799}{also} \markbox{m5800}{$a, b\in \calX$}.  \markbox{5801}{Let} \markbox{m5802}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b) = \{U \in \mathfrak S| d_U(a,b)>K\}$} \markbox{5803}{denote} \markbox{5804}{their} \markbox{m5805}{$K$}-relevant \markbox{5806}{set.}  \markbox{5807}{To} \markbox{5808}{each} \markbox{m5809}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{5810}{let} \markbox{m5811}{$\phi_U:T_U\to \calC(U)$} \markbox{5812}{denote} \markbox{5813}{a} \markbox{m5814}{$(C,C)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{5815}{embedding} \markbox{5816}{of} \markbox{5817}{an} \markbox{5818}{interval} \markbox{5819}{between} \markbox{m5820}{$a_U$} \markbox{5821}{and} \markbox{m5822}{$b_U$}, \markbox{5823}{so} \markbox{5824}{that} \markbox{m5825}{$\phi_U(a_U) = \pi_U(a)$} \markbox{5826}{and} \markbox{m5827}{$\phi_U(b_U) = \pi_U(b)$}.  \markbox{5828}{Here} \markbox{5829}{we} \markbox{5830}{can} \markbox{5831}{assume} \markbox{5832}{that} \markbox{m5833}{$C=C(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{5834}{depends} \markbox{5835}{only} \markbox{5836}{on} \markbox{5837}{the} \markbox{5838}{ambient} \markbox{5839}{HHS.}  \markbox{5840}{Note} \markbox{5841}{that} \markbox{5842}{we} \markbox{5843}{are} \markbox{5844}{only} \markbox{5845}{taking} \markbox{5846}{a} \markbox{5847}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{5848}{embedding,} \markbox{5849}{instead} \markbox{5850}{of} \markbox{5851}{a} \markbox{5852}{geodesic,} \markbox{5853}{because} \markbox{5854}{that} \markbox{5855}{is} \markbox{5856}{the} \markbox{5857}{level} \markbox{5858}{of} \markbox{5859}{generality} \markbox{5860}{that} \markbox{5861}{we} \markbox{5862}{will} \markbox{5863}{require} later.

We \markbox{5864}{also} \markbox{5865}{set} \markbox{5866}{some} \markbox{5867}{terminology} \markbox{5868}{for} \markbox{m5869}{$a_U,b_U$}, \markbox{5870}{since} \markbox{5871}{they} \markbox{5872}{will} \markbox{5873}{play} \markbox{5874}{a} \markbox{5875}{distinguished} \markbox{5876}{role} \markbox{5877}{below.} 

\begin{definition}[Marked \markbox{5878}{points} \markbox{5879}{on} intervals] \label{defn:marked}
For \markbox{5880}{each} \markbox{m5881}{$U\in \calU$} \markbox{5882}{the} \markbox{5883}{points} \markbox{m5884}{$a_U, b_U \in T_U$} \markbox{5885}{are} \markbox{5886}{called} \emph{marked points}.
\end{definition}

We \markbox{5887}{note} \markbox{5888}{that} \markbox{5889}{in} \markbox{5890}{the} \markbox{5891}{basic} \markbox{5892}{construction} \markbox{5893}{explained} \markbox{5894}{in} \markbox{5895}{this} \markbox{5896}{section,} \markbox{5897}{marked} \markbox{5898}{points} \markbox{5899}{will} \markbox{5900}{always} \markbox{5901}{been} \markbox{5902}{the} \markbox{5903}{endpoints} \markbox{5904}{of} \markbox{5905}{the} \markbox{5906}{intervals} \markbox{m5907}{$T_U$}.  \markbox{5908}{This} \markbox{5909}{will} \markbox{5910}{also} \markbox{5911}{be} \markbox{5912}{true} \markbox{5913}{of} \markbox{5914}{our} \markbox{5915}{collapsed} \markbox{5916}{stable} \markbox{5917}{trees} \markbox{5918}{defined} \markbox{5919}{in} \markbox{5920}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:collapsed stable intervals}, \markbox{5921}{though} \markbox{5922}{not} \markbox{5923}{necessarily} \markbox{5924}{of} \markbox{5925}{the} \markbox{5926}{stable} \markbox{5927}{intervals} themselves.

The \markbox{5928}{discussion} \markbox{5929}{in} \markbox{5930}{this} \markbox{5931}{section} \markbox{5932}{closely} \markbox{5933}{follows} \cite[Sections \markbox{5934}{6} \markbox{5935}{and} 7]{Dur_infcube}. \markbox{5936}{Given} \markbox{5937}{the} \markbox{5938}{technical} \markbox{5939}{nature} \markbox{5940}{of} \markbox{5941}{this} \markbox{5942}{part,} \markbox{5943}{we} \markbox{5944}{will} \markbox{5945}{mostly} \markbox{5946}{state} \markbox{5947}{definitions} \markbox{5948}{and} \markbox{5949}{important} \markbox{5950}{properties,} \markbox{5951}{providing} \markbox{5952}{sketches} \markbox{5953}{where} \markbox{5954}{convenient} \markbox{5955}{but} \markbox{5956}{leaving} \markbox{5957}{the} \markbox{5958}{details} \markbox{5959}{for} \markbox{5960}{the} \markbox{5961}{reader} \markbox{5962}{to} verify.

\subsection{Reduced interval systems} \label{subsec:reduced interval systems}

Our \markbox{5963}{first} \markbox{5964}{goal} \markbox{5965}{is} \markbox{5966}{to} \markbox{5967}{push} \markbox{5968}{the} \markbox{5969}{hierarchical} \markbox{5970}{data} \markbox{5971}{associated} \markbox{5972}{to} \markbox{m5973}{$a,b$} \markbox{5974}{onto} \markbox{5975}{the} \markbox{5976}{family} \markbox{5977}{of} \markbox{5978}{intervals} \markbox{m5979}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$}.  \markbox{5980}{This} \markbox{5981}{involves} \markbox{5982}{producing} \markbox{5983}{a} \markbox{5984}{notion} \markbox{5985}{of} \markbox{5986}{relative} \markbox{5987}{projection} \markbox{5988}{between} \markbox{5989}{the} \markbox{5990}{intervals} \markbox{5991}{and} \markbox{5992}{verifying} \markbox{5993}{some} \markbox{5994}{HHS-like} \markbox{5995}{properties} \markbox{5996}{for} them.

These \emph{interval projections} \markbox{5997}{are} \markbox{5998}{defined} \markbox{5999}{simply} \markbox{6000}{by} \markbox{6001}{closest-point} \markbox{6002}{projecting} \markbox{6003}{the} \markbox{6004}{relative} \markbox{6005}{projections} \markbox{6006}{of} \markbox{m6007}{$(\calX,\mathfrak S)$} \markbox{6008}{to} \markbox{6009}{the} \markbox{6010}{images} \markbox{6011}{of} \markbox{m6012}{$\phi_U(T_U) \subset \calC(U)$} \markbox{6013}{then} \markbox{6014}{pulling} \markbox{6015}{back} \markbox{6016}{to} \markbox{m6017}{$T_U$} \markbox{6018}{via} \markbox{m6019}{$\phi^{-1}_U$}.  \markbox{6020}{We} \markbox{6021}{write} \markbox{m6022}{$\delta^V_U$}, \markbox{6023}{rather} \markbox{6024}{than} \markbox{m6025}{$\rho^V_U$}, \markbox{6026}{for} \markbox{6027}{the} \markbox{6028}{relative} \markbox{6029}{interval} \markbox{6030}{projections} \markbox{6031}{among} \markbox{6032}{the} \markbox{m6033}{$T_U$}.  \markbox{6034}{These} \markbox{6035}{interval} \markbox{6036}{projections} \markbox{6037}{are} \markbox{6038}{interval} \markbox{6039}{versions} \markbox{6040}{of} \markbox{6041}{the} ``tree projections'' \markbox{6042}{described} \markbox{6043}{in} \cite[Section 6]{Dur_infcube}.

The \markbox{6044}{following} \markbox{6045}{lemma,} \markbox{6046}{which} \markbox{6047}{summarizes} \markbox{6048}{the} \markbox{6049}{basic} \markbox{6050}{properties} \markbox{6051}{that} \markbox{6052}{we} \markbox{6053}{need,} \markbox{6054}{says} \markbox{6055}{that} \markbox{6056}{the} \markbox{m6057}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6058}{behave} \markbox{6059}{in} \markbox{6060}{essentially} \markbox{6061}{the} \markbox{6062}{same} \markbox{6063}{way} \markbox{6064}{as} \markbox{6065}{the} \markbox{m6066}{$\rho^V_U$}.  \markbox{6067}{Its} \markbox{6068}{proof} \markbox{6069}{is} \markbox{6070}{an} \markbox{6071}{exercise} \markbox{6072}{in} \markbox{6073}{the} \markbox{6074}{definitions} \markbox{6075}{and} \markbox{6076}{the} \markbox{6077}{basic} \markbox{6078}{properties} \markbox{6079}{of} \markbox{6080}{an} \markbox{6081}{HHS;} \markbox{6082}{see} \cite[Lemma 6.13]{Dur_infcube}.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:interval control}
For \markbox{6083}{any} \markbox{m6084}{$C>0$} \markbox{6085}{there} \markbox{6086}{exists} \markbox{m6087}{$R_C = R_C(C,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{6088}{so} \markbox{6089}{that} \markbox{6090}{the} \markbox{6091}{following} holds:

\begin{enumerate}
    \item If \markbox{m6092}{$U \pitchfork V \in \calU$}, \markbox{6093}{then} \markbox{6094}{both} \markbox{m6095}{$\delta^V_U \subset T_U$} \markbox{6096}{and} \markbox{m6097}{$\delta^U_V \subset T_V$} \markbox{6098}{are} \markbox{6099}{sets} \markbox{6100}{of} \markbox{6101}{diameter} \markbox{6102}{at} \markbox{6103}{most} \markbox{m6104}{$R_C$} \markbox{6105}{which} \markbox{6106}{are} \markbox{m6107}{$R_C$}-close \markbox{6108}{to} \markbox{6109}{a} \markbox{6110}{marked} \markbox{6111}{point} \markbox{6112}{of} \markbox{m6113}{$T_U,T_V$}, \markbox{6114}{respectively.}  \markbox{6115}{Moreover,} \markbox{m6116}{$d_U(\phi_U(\delta^V_U), \rho^V_U)<R_C$}, \markbox{6117}{and} \markbox{6118}{similarly} \markbox{6119}{for} \markbox{m6120}{$\delta^U_V$}.
    \item If \markbox{m6121}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}, \markbox{6122}{then} \markbox{m6123}{$\delta^U_V \subset T_V$} \markbox{6124}{has} \markbox{6125}{diameter} \markbox{6126}{bounded} \markbox{6127}{by} \markbox{m6128}{$R_C$}.  \markbox{6129}{Moreover,} \markbox{m6130}{$d_V(\phi_V(\delta^U_V), \rho^U_V)<R_C$}.
     \item If \markbox{m6131}{$U, V \nest W \in \calU$} \markbox{6132}{with} \markbox{m6133}{$U,V$} \markbox{6134}{not} \markbox{6135}{transverse,} \markbox{6136}{then} \markbox{m6137}{$\diam_{T_W}(\delta^U_W \cup \delta^V_W) < R_C$}.
    \item If \markbox{m6138}{$U \pitchfork V$} \markbox{6139}{and} \markbox{m6140}{$W \nest V$} \markbox{6141}{and} \markbox{m6142}{$W,U$} \markbox{6143}{not} \markbox{6144}{orthogonal,} \markbox{6145}{then} \markbox{m6146}{$\diam_{T_U}(\delta^V_U \cup \delta^W_U)<R_C$}.
    \item(Bounded \markbox{6147}{geodesic} \markbox{6148}{image)} \markbox{6149}{If} \markbox{m6150}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}, \markbox{6151}{then} \markbox{6152}{any} \markbox{6153}{component} \markbox{m6154}{$C \subset T_V - \calN_{R_C}(\delta^U_V)$} \markbox{6155}{satisfies} \markbox{m6156}{$\diam_{T_U}(\delta^V_U(C))<R_C$}.
  
\end{enumerate}

\end{lemma}

It \markbox{6157}{will} \markbox{6158}{be} \markbox{6159}{useful} \markbox{6160}{for} \markbox{6161}{us} \markbox{6162}{to} \markbox{6163}{abstract} \markbox{6164}{the} \markbox{6165}{properties} \markbox{6166}{obtained} \markbox{6167}{for} \markbox{6168}{the} \markbox{6169}{intervals} \markbox{m6170}{$T_U$} \markbox{6171}{in} \markbox{6172}{the} \markbox{6173}{last} \markbox{6174}{subsection.}  \markbox{6175}{We} \markbox{6176}{are} \markbox{6177}{doing} \markbox{6178}{this} \markbox{6179}{so} \markbox{6180}{that} \markbox{6181}{we} \markbox{6182}{can} \markbox{6183}{later} \markbox{6184}{plug} \markbox{6185}{in} \markbox{6186}{the} \markbox{6187}{intervals} \markbox{6188}{produced} \markbox{6189}{by} \markbox{6190}{the} \markbox{6191}{Stable} \markbox{6192}{Interval} \markbox{6193}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{6194}{below} \markbox{6195}{directly} \markbox{6196}{into} \markbox{6197}{this} setup.

\begin{definition}[Interval system]\label{defn:interval axioms}
