Given \markbox{m6198}{$R>0$}, \markbox{6199}{an} \markbox{m6200}{$R$}-\emph{interval system} \markbox{6201}{for} \markbox{m6202}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{6203}{and} \markbox{m6204}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$} \markbox{6205}{is} \markbox{6206}{the} \markbox{6207}{following} \markbox{6208}{set} \markbox{6209}{of} data:
\begin{enumerate}
\item For \markbox{6210}{each} \markbox{m6211}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{6212}{we} \markbox{6213}{have} \markbox{6214}{an} \markbox{6215}{interval} \markbox{m6216}{$T_U$} \markbox{6217}{and} \markbox{6218}{a} \markbox{m6219}{$(R,R)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{6220}{embedding} \markbox{m6221}{$\phi_U:T_U \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{6222}{so} \markbox{6223}{that} \markbox{m6224}{$d^{Haus}_U(\phi_U(T_U), \hull_U(a,b))<R$}.
\item For \markbox{6225}{each} \markbox{m6226}{$U \in\calU$}, \markbox{6227}{there} \markbox{6228}{exists} \markbox{6229}{a} \markbox{6230}{marked} \markbox{6231}{point} \markbox{m6232}{$a_U \in T_U$} \markbox{6233}{with} \markbox{m6234}{$d_{\calC(U)}(\phi_U(a_U),\pi_U(a))<R$}, \markbox{6235}{and} \markbox{6236}{similarly} \markbox{6237}{for} \markbox{m6238}{$b$}.
\item There \markbox{6239}{are} \markbox{m6240}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6241}{sets} \markbox{6242}{which} \markbox{6243}{satisfy} \markbox{6244}{the} \markbox{6245}{conclusions} \markbox{6246}{of} \markbox{6247}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}.


\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}


\begin{remark}
When \markbox{6248}{stabilizing} \markbox{6249}{the} \markbox{6250}{construction} \markbox{6251}{of} \markbox{6252}{the} \markbox{6253}{cubical} \markbox{6254}{models} \markbox{6255}{in} \markbox{6256}{Section} \ref{sec:stable cubes}, \markbox{6257}{we} \markbox{6258}{will} \markbox{6259}{want} \markbox{6260}{to} \markbox{6261}{use} \markbox{6262}{the} \markbox{6263}{stable} \markbox{6264}{intervals} \markbox{6265}{provided} \markbox{6266}{by} \markbox{6267}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{6268}{below.}  \markbox{6269}{For} \markbox{6270}{these,} \markbox{6271}{we} \markbox{6272}{will} \markbox{6273}{induce} \markbox{6274}{an} \markbox{6275}{interval} \markbox{6276}{system} \markbox{6277}{structure} \markbox{6278}{by} \markbox{6279}{a} \markbox{6280}{slightly} \markbox{6281}{more} \markbox{6282}{careful} \markbox{6283}{construction} \markbox{6284}{than} \markbox{6285}{just} \markbox{6286}{working} \markbox{6287}{directly} \markbox{6288}{with} \markbox{6289}{Gromov} \markbox{6290}{trees,} \markbox{6291}{e.g.} \markbox{6292}{item} \markbox{6293}{(2)} \markbox{6294}{in} \markbox{6295}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{6296}{is} \markbox{6297}{immediate} \markbox{6298}{in} \markbox{6299}{that} \markbox{6300}{setting.}  \markbox{6301}{But} \markbox{6302}{the} \markbox{6303}{upshot} \markbox{6304}{is} \markbox{6305}{the} \markbox{6306}{same:} \markbox{6307}{the} \markbox{6308}{rest} \markbox{6309}{of} \markbox{6310}{the} \markbox{6311}{material} \markbox{6312}{in} \markbox{6313}{this} \markbox{6314}{section} \markbox{6315}{also} \markbox{6316}{holds} \markbox{6317}{for} \markbox{6318}{that} setup.
\end{remark}

\subsection{Interval consistency}

The \markbox{6319}{goal} \markbox{6320}{of} \markbox{6321}{this} \markbox{6322}{subsection} \markbox{6323}{is} \markbox{6324}{to} \markbox{6325}{define} \markbox{6326}{a} \markbox{6327}{map} \markbox{m6328}{$\Psi:\hull_{\calX}(a,b)\to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$} \markbox{6329}{and} \markbox{6330}{show} \markbox{6331}{that} \markbox{6332}{its} \markbox{6333}{image} \markbox{6334}{satisfies} \markbox{6335}{the} \markbox{6336}{appropriate} \markbox{6337}{analogue} \markbox{6338}{of} \markbox{6339}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency} \markbox{6340}{in} \markbox{6341}{this} \markbox{6342}{setting.}  \markbox{6343}{Toward} \markbox{6344}{that} \markbox{6345}{end,} \markbox{6346}{for} \markbox{6347}{any} \markbox{m6348}{$\alpha>0$}, \markbox{6349}{we} \markbox{6350}{set} \markbox{m6351}{$\calZ_{\alpha} \subset \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$} \markbox{6352}{to} \markbox{6353}{be} \markbox{6354}{the} \markbox{6355}{set} \markbox{6356}{of} \markbox{m6357}{$\alpha$}-consistent tuples.

We \markbox{6358}{can} \markbox{6359}{now} \markbox{6360}{define} \markbox{6361}{our} \markbox{6362}{map} \markbox{m6363}{$\Psi:H \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$} \markbox{6364}{for} \markbox{m6365}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}.  \markbox{6366}{Let} \markbox{m6367}{$x \in H$} \markbox{6368}{and} \markbox{6369}{for} \markbox{6370}{each} \markbox{m6371}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{6372}{let} \markbox{m6373}{$x_U$} \markbox{6374}{denote} \markbox{6375}{a} \markbox{6376}{choice} \markbox{6377}{of} \markbox{6378}{a} \markbox{6379}{point} \markbox{6380}{in} \markbox{m6381}{$\psi_U(x) = \phi_{U}^{-1}(p_U(\pi_U(x))) \subset T_U$}, \markbox{6382}{where} \markbox{m6383}{$p_U:\calC(U)\to \phi_U(T_U)$} \markbox{6384}{is} \markbox{6385}{closest} \markbox{6386}{point} \markbox{6387}{projection.}  \markbox{6388}{For} \markbox{6389}{each} \markbox{m6390}{$x \in H$}, \markbox{6391}{this} \markbox{6392}{defines} \markbox{6393}{a} \markbox{6394}{tuple} \markbox{m6395}{$(\psi_U(x)) = (x_U) \in \prod_{U \in \calU}T_U$}.  \markbox{6396}{That} \markbox{6397}{is,} \markbox{6398}{the} \markbox{6399}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{6400}{maps} \markbox{m6401}{$\psi_U:H \to T_U$} \markbox{6402}{combine} \markbox{6403}{to} \markbox{6404}{a} \markbox{6405}{global} \markbox{6406}{map} \markbox{m6407}{$\Psi:H \to \prod_U T_U$}.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:interval consistency}
For \markbox{6408}{any} \markbox{m6409}{$R>0$}, \markbox{6410}{there} \markbox{6411}{exists} \markbox{m6412}{$\alpha_0 = \alpha_0(\mathfrak S,R)>0$} \markbox{6413}{so} \markbox{6414}{that} \markbox{6415}{if} \markbox{m6416}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{6417}{is} \markbox{6418}{an} \markbox{m6419}{$R$}-interval \markbox{6420}{system} \markbox{6421}{for} \markbox{m6422}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{6423}{and} \markbox{m6424}{$x \in \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}, \markbox{6425}{then} \markbox{m6426}{$\Psi(x) = (x_U)$} \markbox{6427}{is} \markbox{m6428}{$\alpha_0$}-consistent.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}

Let \markbox{m6429}{$x \in \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}.  \markbox{6430}{The} \markbox{6431}{corresponding} \markbox{6432}{tuple} \markbox{m6433}{$(\pi_U(x_U))$} \markbox{6434}{is} \markbox{m6435}{$O(\theta, \mathfrak S)$}-consistent \markbox{6436}{by} \markbox{6437}{Lemma} \ref{lem:base consistency}.  \markbox{6438}{Moreover,} \markbox{6439}{by} \markbox{6440}{definition} \markbox{6441}{of} \markbox{m6442}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{6443}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hier hull}), \markbox{6444}{we} \markbox{6445}{have} \markbox{m6446}{$d_U(\pi_U(x_U), H_U) < \theta$}, \markbox{6447}{where} \markbox{m6448}{$H_U = \hull_{\calC(U)}(a,b)$} \markbox{6449}{and} \markbox{m6450}{$\theta = \theta(\mathfrak S)>0$}.  \markbox{6451}{Hence} \markbox{m6452}{$d_U(\pi_U(x_U), \phi_U(T_U))<\theta'$} \markbox{6453}{for} \markbox{6454}{some} \markbox{m6455}{$\theta' = \theta'(\mathfrak S, \theta)>0$}.  \markbox{6456}{At} \markbox{6457}{this} \markbox{6458}{point,} \markbox{6459}{a} \markbox{6460}{straight-forward} \markbox{6461}{argument} \markbox{6462}{using} \markbox{6463}{the} \markbox{6464}{properties} \markbox{6465}{in} \markbox{6466}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{6467}{gives} \markbox{6468}{the} \markbox{6469}{required} \markbox{6470}{consistency} \markbox{6471}{constant} \markbox{m6472}{$\alpha_0 = \alpha_0(\mathfrak S, R)$}.  \markbox{6473}{We} \markbox{6474}{leave} \markbox{6475}{the} \markbox{6476}{details} \markbox{6477}{to} \markbox{6478}{the} reader.
\end{proof}



\subsection{Interval thickenings}\label{subsec:thickenings}

Our \markbox{6479}{next} \markbox{6480}{goal} \markbox{6481}{is} \markbox{6482}{to} \markbox{6483}{define} \markbox{6484}{a} \markbox{6485}{way} \markbox{6486}{of} \markbox{6487}{collapsing} \markbox{6488}{the} \markbox{6489}{relative} \markbox{6490}{projection} \markbox{6491}{data} \markbox{6492}{associated} \markbox{6493}{to} \markbox{6494}{intervals} \markbox{m6495}{$T_U$}, \markbox{6496}{i.e.} \markbox{6497}{the} \markbox{m6498}{$\delta^V_U$}, \markbox{6499}{in} \markbox{6500}{an} \markbox{6501}{interval} \markbox{6502}{system} \markbox{6503}{to} \markbox{6504}{remove} \markbox{6505}{coarseness} \markbox{6506}{from} \markbox{6507}{the} \markbox{6508}{setup.}  \markbox{6509}{The} \markbox{6510}{idea} \markbox{6511}{is} \markbox{6512}{that} \markbox{6513}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{6514}{roughly} \markbox{6515}{encodes} \markbox{6516}{the} \markbox{6517}{projection} \markbox{6518}{data} \markbox{6519}{up} \markbox{6520}{to} \markbox{6521}{a} \markbox{6522}{controlled} \markbox{6523}{error.}  \markbox{6524}{In} \markbox{6525}{slightly} \markbox{6526}{more} \markbox{6527}{detail,} \markbox{6528}{observe} \markbox{6529}{that} \markbox{6530}{each} \markbox{6531}{interval} \markbox{m6532}{$T_U$} \markbox{6533}{contains} \markbox{6534}{the} \markbox{6535}{relative} \markbox{6536}{projections} \markbox{m6537}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6538}{for} \markbox{m6539}{$V \nest U$}.  \markbox{6540}{We} \markbox{6541}{would} \markbox{6542}{like} \markbox{6543}{to} \markbox{6544}{collect} \markbox{6545}{close-by} \markbox{6546}{relative} \markbox{6547}{projections} \markbox{6548}{into} \markbox{6549}{single} \markbox{6550}{intervals} \markbox{6551}{called} \emph{cluster components}, \markbox{6552}{so} \markbox{6553}{that} \markbox{6554}{we} \markbox{6555}{can} \markbox{6556}{later} \markbox{6557}{collapse} \markbox{6558}{them.}  \markbox{6559}{One} \markbox{6560}{complication} \markbox{6561}{is} \markbox{6562}{that} \markbox{6563}{the} \markbox{m6564}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6565}{need} \markbox{6566}{not} \markbox{6567}{be} \markbox{6568}{subintervals} \markbox{6569}{of} \markbox{m6570}{$T_U$}, \markbox{6571}{so} \markbox{6572}{we} \markbox{6573}{need} \markbox{6574}{a} \markbox{6575}{couple} \markbox{6576}{of} \markbox{6577}{constants---one} \markbox{6578}{to} \markbox{6579}{determine} \markbox{6580}{what} \markbox{6581}{it} \markbox{6582}{means} \markbox{6583}{for} \markbox{6584}{relative} \markbox{6585}{projections} \markbox{6586}{to} \markbox{6587}{be} ``close'', \markbox{6588}{and} \markbox{6589}{the} \markbox{6590}{other} \markbox{6591}{to} \markbox{6592}{guarantee} \markbox{6593}{that} \markbox{6594}{cluster} \markbox{6595}{components} \markbox{6596}{which} \markbox{6597}{are} \markbox{6598}{not} \markbox{6599}{close} \markbox{6600}{satisfy} \markbox{6601}{a} \markbox{6602}{minimum} \markbox{6603}{distance} bound.



We \markbox{6604}{will} \markbox{6605}{use} \markbox{6606}{the} \markbox{6607}{following} \markbox{6608}{slightly} \markbox{6609}{more} \markbox{6610}{abstract} \markbox{6611}{setup,} \markbox{6612}{as} \markbox{6613}{it} \markbox{6614}{will} \markbox{6615}{be} \markbox{6616}{useful} \markbox{6617}{later} \markbox{6618}{during} \markbox{6619}{our} \markbox{6620}{stabilization} process:

 \begin{definition}[Thickenings]\label{defn:thickening}
Let \markbox{m6621}{$T$} \markbox{6622}{be} \markbox{6623}{an} \markbox{6624}{interval} \markbox{6625}{with} \markbox{6626}{a} \markbox{6627}{decomposition} \markbox{m6628}{$T = A \cup B$} \markbox{6629}{into} \markbox{6630}{collections} \markbox{6631}{of} \markbox{6632}{segments.}  \markbox{6633}{Given} \markbox{m6634}{$r_1,r_2>0$}, \markbox{6635}{the} \markbox{m6636}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-\emph{thickening} \markbox{6637}{of} \markbox{m6638}{$T$} \emph{along $B$} \markbox{6639}{defines} \markbox{6640}{a} \markbox{6641}{decomposition} \markbox{m6642}{$T = \bT_e \cup \bT_c$} \markbox{6643}{into} \emph{edge} \markbox{m6644}{$\bT_e$} \markbox{6645}{and} \emph{cluster} \markbox{m6646}{$\bT_c$} \markbox{6647}{components} \markbox{6648}{as} follows:
\begin{enumerate}
\item First, \markbox{6649}{take} \markbox{6650}{the} \markbox{m6651}{$r_1$}-neighborhoods \markbox{6652}{in} \markbox{m6653}{$T$} \markbox{6654}{of} \markbox{6655}{the} \markbox{6656}{components} \markbox{6657}{of} \markbox{m6658}{$B$}.  \markbox{6659}{Call} \markbox{6660}{the} \markbox{6661}{collection} \markbox{6662}{of} \markbox{6663}{these} \markbox{6664}{neighborhood} \markbox{m6665}{$\calB$}, \markbox{6666}{and} \markbox{6667}{their} \markbox{6668}{complement} \markbox{m6669}{$T - \calB = \calA$}.
\item Second, \markbox{6670}{connect} \markbox{6671}{any} \markbox{6672}{two} \markbox{6673}{subintervals} \markbox{6674}{in} \markbox{m6675}{$\calB$} \markbox{6676}{which} \markbox{6677}{come} \markbox{6678}{within} \markbox{m6679}{$r_2$} \markbox{6680}{of} \markbox{6681}{each} \markbox{6682}{other} \markbox{6683}{in} \markbox{m6684}{$T$} \markbox{6685}{by} \markbox{6686}{the} \markbox{6687}{geodesic} \markbox{6688}{between} \markbox{6689}{them.}  \markbox{6690}{Call} \markbox{6691}{the} \markbox{6692}{resulting} \markbox{6693}{collection} \markbox{6694}{of} \markbox{6695}{subintervals} \markbox{m6696}{$\bT_c$} \markbox{6697}{and} \markbox{6698}{set} \markbox{m6699}{$\bT_e = T- \bT_c$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}



In \markbox{6700}{our} \markbox{6701}{current} \markbox{6702}{context,} \markbox{6703}{we} \markbox{6704}{can} \markbox{6705}{take} \markbox{m6706}{$B$} \markbox{6707}{to} \markbox{6708}{be} \markbox{6709}{the} \markbox{6710}{collection} \markbox{6711}{of} \markbox{m6712}{$\delta^V_U \subset T_U$} \markbox{6713}{segments} \markbox{6714}{for} \markbox{m6715}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{6716}{along} \markbox{6717}{with} \markbox{6718}{the} \markbox{6719}{marked} \markbox{6720}{points} \markbox{m6721}{$a_U,b_U$} \markbox{6722}{on} \markbox{m6723}{$T_U$} \markbox{6724}{(Definition} \ref{defn:marked}).  \markbox{6725}{Thus} \markbox{6726}{a} \markbox{6727}{thickening} \markbox{6728}{of} \markbox{m6729}{$T_U$} \markbox{6730}{along} \markbox{6731}{this} \markbox{6732}{collection} \markbox{m6733}{$B$} \markbox{6734}{expands} \markbox{6735}{the} \markbox{m6736}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6737}{segments} \markbox{6738}{and} \markbox{m6739}{$a_U,b_U$} \markbox{6740}{and} \markbox{6741}{combines} \markbox{6742}{nearby} \markbox{6743}{expansions.}  \markbox{6744}{For} \markbox{6745}{each} \markbox{m6746}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{6747}{we} \markbox{6748}{denote} \markbox{6749}{the} \markbox{6750}{resulting} \markbox{6751}{decomposition} \markbox{6752}{of} \markbox{6753}{the} \markbox{6754}{thickened} \markbox{6755}{interval} \markbox{6756}{by} \markbox{m6757}{$T_U = \bT^e_{U} \cup \bT^c_{U}$}.  \markbox{6758}{When} \markbox{6759}{we} \markbox{6760}{perform} \markbox{6761}{an} \markbox{m6762}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{6763}{to} \markbox{6764}{each} \markbox{6765}{interval} \markbox{6766}{in} \markbox{6767}{an} \markbox{6768}{interval} \markbox{6769}{system,} \markbox{6770}{we} \markbox{6771}{refer} \markbox{6772}{to} \markbox{6773}{the} \markbox{6774}{resulting} \markbox{6775}{collection} \markbox{6776}{of} \markbox{6777}{thickened} \markbox{6778}{intervals} \markbox{6779}{as} \markbox{6780}{a} \markbox{m6781}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-\emph{thickening} \markbox{6782}{of} \markbox{6783}{the} \markbox{6784}{interval} system.

\begin{remark}
In \markbox{6785}{our} \markbox{6786}{context,} \markbox{6787}{we} \markbox{6788}{will} \markbox{6789}{be} \markbox{6790}{able} \markbox{6791}{to} \markbox{6792}{control} \markbox{6793}{the} \markbox{6794}{constants} \markbox{m6795}{$r_1,r_2>0$} \markbox{6796}{in} \markbox{6797}{terms} \markbox{6798}{of} \markbox{6799}{the} \markbox{6800}{ambient} \markbox{6801}{HHS,} \markbox{6802}{and,} \markbox{6803}{importantly,} \markbox{6804}{we} \markbox{6805}{will} \markbox{6806}{be} \markbox{6807}{able} \markbox{6808}{to} \markbox{6809}{choose} \markbox{6810}{our} \markbox{6811}{largeness} \markbox{6812}{constant} \markbox{m6813}{$K$} \markbox{6814}{to} \markbox{6815}{be} \markbox{6816}{independent} \markbox{6817}{of} them.
\end{remark}





\subsection{Collapsed intervals and $0$-consistency} \label{subsec:collapsing}

Let \markbox{m6818}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{6819}{be} \markbox{6820}{an} \markbox{m6821}{$R$}-interval \markbox{6822}{system} \markbox{6823}{for} \markbox{m6824}{$a,b \in \calX$}.  \markbox{6825}{Fix} \markbox{m6826}{$r_i = r_i(R, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{6827}{for} \markbox{m6828}{$i=1,2$} \markbox{6829}{to} \markbox{6830}{be} \markbox{6831}{determined} \markbox{6832}{soon.}  \markbox{6833}{For} \markbox{6834}{each} \markbox{m6835}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{6836}{let} \markbox{m6837}{$T_U = \bT^e_U \cup \bT^c_U$} \markbox{6838}{denote} \markbox{6839}{its} \markbox{m6840}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening, \markbox{6841}{as} \markbox{6842}{in} \markbox{6843}{Definition} \ref{defn:thickening}.

Let \markbox{m6844}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{6845}{denote} \markbox{6846}{the} \markbox{6847}{map} \markbox{6848}{which} \markbox{6849}{collapses} \markbox{6850}{each} \markbox{6851}{component} \markbox{6852}{of} \markbox{m6853}{$\bT^c_U$} \markbox{6854}{to} \markbox{6855}{a} \markbox{6856}{point,} \markbox{6857}{each} \markbox{6858}{of} \markbox{6859}{which} \markbox{6860}{we} \markbox{6861}{call} \markbox{6862}{a} \emph{collapsed point}.  \markbox{6863}{The} \markbox{6864}{resulting} \markbox{6865}{object} \markbox{m6866}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{6867}{is} \markbox{6868}{an} \markbox{6869}{interval.}  \markbox{6870}{Note} \markbox{6871}{that} \markbox{6872}{by} \markbox{6873}{construction} \markbox{m6874}{$a_U, b_U \in \bT^c_U$} \markbox{6875}{for} \markbox{6876}{each} \markbox{m6877}{$U \in \calU$}.  \markbox{6878}{Hence} \markbox{6879}{each} \markbox{6880}{of} \markbox{m6881}{$a_U,b_U$} \markbox{6882}{determines} \markbox{6883}{a} \emph{marked point} \markbox{m6884}{$\ha_U,\hb_U \in \hT_U$}, \markbox{6885}{and} \markbox{6886}{these} \markbox{6887}{marked} \markbox{6888}{points} \markbox{m6889}{$\ha_U,\hb_U$} \markbox{6890}{will} \markbox{6891}{be} \markbox{6892}{the} \markbox{6893}{endpoints} \markbox{6894}{of} \markbox{6895}{the} \markbox{6896}{(collapsed)} \markbox{6897}{interval} \markbox{m6898}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{6899}{Moreover,} \markbox{6900}{the} \markbox{6901}{decomposition} \markbox{m6902}{$T_U = \bT^e_U \cup \bT^c_U$} \markbox{6903}{descends} \markbox{6904}{to} \markbox{6905}{a} \markbox{6906}{decomposition} \markbox{m6907}{$\hT_U = \hT^e_U \cup \hT^c_U$}, \markbox{6908}{where} \markbox{6909}{the} \markbox{6910}{components} \markbox{6911}{of} \markbox{m6912}{$\hT^c_U$} \markbox{6913}{are} \markbox{6914}{the} \markbox{6915}{collapsed} \markbox{6916}{points} \markbox{6917}{corresponding} \markbox{6918}{to} \markbox{6919}{the} \markbox{6920}{components} \markbox{6921}{of} \markbox{m6922}{$\bT^c_U$}, \markbox{6923}{and} \markbox{6924}{the} \markbox{6925}{components} \markbox{6926}{of} \markbox{m6927}{$\hT^e_U$} \markbox{6928}{are} \markbox{6929}{isometric} \markbox{6930}{images} \markbox{6931}{of} \markbox{6932}{the} \markbox{6933}{components} \markbox{6934}{of} \markbox{m6935}{$\bT^e_U$}.

Combining \markbox{6936}{these} \markbox{m6937}{$q_U$} \markbox{6938}{maps} \markbox{6939}{with} \markbox{6940}{our} \markbox{6941}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{6942}{projections} \markbox{m6943}{$\psi_U:H \to T_U$}, \markbox{6944}{we} \markbox{6945}{get} \markbox{6946}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{6947}{maps} \markbox{m6948}{$\hpsi_U:H \to \hT_U$} \markbox{6949}{to} \markbox{6950}{the} \markbox{6951}{collapsed} \markbox{6952}{intervals,} \markbox{6953}{and} \markbox{6954}{hence} \markbox{6955}{combining} \markbox{6956}{these} \markbox{6957}{gives} \markbox{6958}{a} \markbox{6959}{global} \markbox{6960}{map} \markbox{m6961}{$\hPsi:H \to \prod_U \hT_U$}.

We \markbox{6962}{can} \markbox{6963}{define} \emph{collapsed relative projections} \markbox{m6964}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{6965}{in} \markbox{6966}{the} \markbox{6967}{obvious} \markbox{6968}{way,} \markbox{6969}{by} \markbox{6970}{composing} \markbox{6971}{with} \markbox{6972}{the} \markbox{6973}{quotient} \markbox{6974}{maps} \markbox{m6975}{$q_U$}.  \markbox{6976}{Similarly,} \markbox{6977}{consistency} \markbox{6978}{in} \markbox{6979}{this} \markbox{6980}{setting} \markbox{6981}{is} \markbox{6982}{the} \markbox{6983}{appropriate} \markbox{6984}{analogue} \markbox{6985}{of} \markbox{6986}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency}, \markbox{6987}{except} \markbox{6988}{now} \markbox{6989}{all} \markbox{6990}{coarseness} \markbox{6991}{has} \markbox{6992}{been} removed:

\begin{definition} \label{defn:Q defined}
A \markbox{6993}{tuple} \markbox{m6994}{$(\hx_U) \in \prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U$} \markbox{6995}{is} \markbox{m6996}{$0$}-\emph{consistent} \markbox{6997}{if} \markbox{6998}{the} \markbox{6999}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item For \markbox{7000}{any} \markbox{m7001}{$U \pitchfork V \in \calU$}, \markbox{7002}{either} \markbox{m7003}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$} \markbox{7004}{or} \markbox{m7005}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V$}.
\item For \markbox{7006}{any} \markbox{m7007}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}, \markbox{7008}{either} \markbox{m7009}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V$} \markbox{7010}{or} \markbox{m7011}{$\hx_U \in \hd^V_U(\hx_V) \subset \hT_U$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item We \markbox{7012}{let} \markbox{m7013}{$\calQ$} \markbox{7014}{denote} \markbox{7015}{set} \markbox{7016}{of} \markbox{m7017}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{7018}{tuples} \markbox{7019}{in} \markbox{m7020}{$\prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}



We \markbox{7021}{can} \markbox{7022}{prove} \markbox{7023}{that} \markbox{m7024}{$\hPsi$} \markbox{7025}{has} \markbox{7026}{image} \markbox{7027}{in} \markbox{m7028}{$\calQ$}:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:hPsi defined}
For \markbox{7029}{any} \markbox{m7030}{$R>0$},  \markbox{7031}{there} \markbox{7032}{exists} \markbox{m7033}{$R_1 = R_1(R,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7034}{so} \markbox{7035}{that} \markbox{7036}{for} \markbox{7037}{any} \markbox{m7038}{$r_1 > R_1$} \markbox{7039}{and} \markbox{m7040}{$r_2>0$}, \markbox{7041}{if} \markbox{m7042}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{7043}{are} \markbox{7044}{the} \markbox{7045}{collapsed} \markbox{7046}{intervals} \markbox{7047}{associated} \markbox{7048}{to} \markbox{7049}{an} \markbox{m7050}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{7051}{of} \markbox{7052}{an} \markbox{m7053}{$R$}-interval \markbox{7054}{system} \markbox{7055}{for} \markbox{m7056}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{7057}{and} \markbox{m7058}{$x \in \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}, \markbox{7059}{then} \markbox{m7060}{$\hPsi(x) = (\hx_U) \in \calQ$}.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
We \markbox{7061}{need} \markbox{7062}{to} \markbox{7063}{prove} \markbox{m7064}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{7065}{of} \markbox{m7066}{$\hPsi(x)$} \markbox{7067}{as} \markbox{7068}{in} \markbox{7069}{Definition} \ref{defn:Q defined}.

First \markbox{7070}{suppose} \markbox{7071}{that} \markbox{m7072}{$U \pitchfork V \in \calU$}.  \markbox{7073}{Since} \markbox{m7074}{$\Psi(x) = (x_V)$} \markbox{7075}{is} \markbox{m7076}{$\alpha_0$}-consistent \markbox{7077}{by} \markbox{7078}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval consistency} \markbox{7079}{where} \markbox{m7080}{$\alpha_0=\alpha_0(R,\theta,\mathfrak S)>0$}, \markbox{7081}{we} \markbox{7082}{have,} \markbox{7083}{without} \markbox{7084}{loss} \markbox{7085}{of} \markbox{7086}{generality,} \markbox{7087}{that} \markbox{m7088}{$d_{T_U}(x_U, \delta^V_U)< \alpha_0$}.  \markbox{7089}{Hence} \markbox{m7090}{$q_U(x_U) = \hd^V_U$} \markbox{7091}{as} \markbox{7092}{long} \markbox{7093}{as} \markbox{m7094}{$r_1 > \alpha_0$}.  

Next \markbox{7095}{suppose} \markbox{7096}{that} \markbox{m7097}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}.  \markbox{7098}{If} \markbox{m7099}{$d_{T_V}(x_V, \delta^U_V)< \alpha_0 < r_1$}, \markbox{7100}{then} \markbox{m7101}{$q_V(x_V) = \hd^U_V$}, \markbox{7102}{and} \markbox{7103}{we} \markbox{7104}{are} \markbox{7105}{done.}  \markbox{7106}{Otherwise,} \markbox{7107}{we} \markbox{7108}{have} \markbox{m7109}{$\diam_{T_U}(x_U \cup \delta^V_U(x_V))<\alpha_0$} \markbox{7110}{while} \markbox{7111}{also} \markbox{m7112}{$d_{T_V}(x_V, \delta^U_V)>\alpha_0$}.  \markbox{7113}{By} \markbox{7114}{taking} \markbox{m7115}{$\alpha_0 > R$}, \markbox{7116}{we} \markbox{7117}{have} \markbox{7118}{that} \markbox{m7119}{$\diam_{T_U}(\delta^V_U(x_V)\cup f_U)< R$} \markbox{7120}{for} \markbox{7121}{some} \markbox{m7122}{$f \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{7123}{by} \markbox{7124}{the} \markbox{7125}{BGI} \markbox{7126}{property} \markbox{7127}{in} \markbox{7128}{item} \markbox{7129}{(4)} \markbox{7130}{of} \markbox{7131}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}.  \markbox{7132}{In} \markbox{7133}{particular,} \markbox{7134}{setting} \markbox{m7135}{$r_1>\alpha_0 + R$}, \markbox{7136}{then} \markbox{7137}{both} \markbox{m7138}{$x_U$} \markbox{7139}{and} \markbox{m7140}{$\delta^V_U(x_V)$} \markbox{7141}{are} \markbox{7142}{within} \markbox{m7143}{$\alpha_0 + R< r_1$} \markbox{7144}{of} \markbox{m7145}{$f_U$}, \markbox{7146}{and} \markbox{7147}{hence} \markbox{m7148}{$q_U(x_U) = q_V(\delta^V_U(x_V))$}.  \markbox{7149}{Finally,} \markbox{7150}{observe} \markbox{7151}{that} \markbox{m7152}{$q^{-1}_V(q_V(x_V))$} \markbox{7153}{is} \markbox{7154}{contained} \markbox{7155}{in} \markbox{7156}{the} \markbox{7157}{component} \markbox{7158}{of} \markbox{m7159}{$T_V - \mathcal{N}_{R}(\delta^U_V)$} \markbox{7160}{containing} \markbox{m7161}{$x_V$}, \markbox{7162}{and} \markbox{7163}{hence} \markbox{m7164}{$q_V(\delta^V_U(x_V)) = \hd^V_U(q_V(x_V))$}.  \markbox{7165}{This} \markbox{7166}{completes} \markbox{7167}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\subsection{Controlling the collapsed intervals}

In \markbox{7168}{this} \markbox{7169}{subsection,} \markbox{7170}{we} \markbox{7171}{record} \markbox{7172}{the} \markbox{7173}{following} \markbox{7174}{technical} \markbox{7175}{lemma,} \markbox{7176}{which} \markbox{7177}{is} \markbox{7178}{in} \markbox{7179}{part} \markbox{7180}{a} \markbox{7181}{collapsed} \markbox{7182}{version} \markbox{7183}{of} \markbox{7184}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}, \markbox{7185}{but} \markbox{7186}{also} \markbox{7187}{contains} \markbox{7188}{the} \markbox{7189}{conclusion} \markbox{7190}{of} \markbox{7191}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}.  \markbox{7192}{The} \markbox{7193}{statement} \markbox{7194}{and} \markbox{7195}{its} \markbox{7196}{proof} \markbox{7197}{are} \markbox{7198}{basically} \cite[Lemma 7.13]{Dur_infcube}.

\begin{lemma}[Collapsed \markbox{7199}{interval} control]\label{lem:collapsed interval control}
Let \markbox{m7200}{$R>0$} \markbox{7201}{and} \markbox{m7202}{$r_1 > R_1$} \markbox{7203}{for} \markbox{m7204}{$R_1 = R_1(R,\theta, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7205}{as} \markbox{7206}{in} \markbox{7207}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}.  \markbox{7208}{There} \markbox{7209}{exists} \markbox{m7210}{$R_2 = R_2(R,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7211}{so} \markbox{7212}{that} \markbox{7213}{for} \markbox{7214}{any} \markbox{m7215}{$r_2>R_2$}, \markbox{7216}{the} \markbox{7217}{following} \markbox{7218}{hold} \markbox{7219}{for} \markbox{7220}{any} \markbox{m7221}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{7222}{of} \markbox{7223}{an} \markbox{m7224}{$R$}-interval \markbox{7225}{system} \markbox{7226}{for} \markbox{m7227}{$a,b \in \calX$}: 
\begin{enumerate}
    \item For \markbox{7228}{any} \markbox{m7229}{$x \in H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}, \markbox{7230}{the} \markbox{7231}{tuple} \markbox{m7232}{$\hPsi(x) \in \calQ$} \markbox{7233}{is} \markbox{m7234}{$0$}-consistent.
    
    \item If \markbox{m7235}{$U \pitchfork V \in \calU$}, \markbox{7236}{then} \markbox{7237}{both} \markbox{m7238}{$\hd^V_U \in \hT_U$} \markbox{7239}{and} \markbox{m7240}{$\hd^U_V \in \hT_V$} \markbox{7241}{are} \markbox{7242}{in} \markbox{m7243}{$\{\ha_U, \hb_U\}$}.
    
    \item If \markbox{m7244}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}, \markbox{7245}{then} \markbox{m7246}{$\hd^U_V$} \markbox{7247}{coincides} \markbox{7248}{with} \markbox{7249}{a} \markbox{7250}{collapsed} point.
    
    \item For \markbox{7251}{any} \markbox{m7252}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{7253}{and} \markbox{7254}{any} \markbox{m7255}{$x,y \in H$}, \markbox{7256}{we} \markbox{7257}{have} \markbox{m7258}{$d_U(x,y) \asymp d_{T_U}(x_u,y_U)\geq d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)$}, \markbox{7259}{with} \markbox{7260}{the} \markbox{7261}{constants} \markbox{7262}{in} \markbox{m7263}{$\asymp$} \markbox{7264}{depending} \markbox{7265}{only} \markbox{7266}{on} \markbox{m7267}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{7268}{and} \markbox{m7269}{$R$}.
  
    
    \item If \markbox{m7270}{$x,y \in H$} \markbox{7271}{and} \markbox{m7272}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{7273}{and} \markbox{m7274}{$\hpsi_U(x), \hpsi_U(y)$} \markbox{7275}{are} \markbox{7276}{distinct} \markbox{7277}{collapsed} \markbox{7278}{points,} \markbox{7279}{then} \markbox{m7280}{$d_U(x,y) > 50\ES$}.
    
    \item If \markbox{m7281}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{7282}{is} \markbox{m7283}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal, \markbox{7284}{then} \markbox{m7285}{$d_{\hT_U}(\ha_U,\hb_U) \succ K - 2r_1$}, \markbox{7286}{with} \markbox{7287}{the} \markbox{7288}{constants} \markbox{7289}{in} \markbox{m7290}{$\succ$} \markbox{7291}{depending} \markbox{7292}{only} \markbox{7293}{on} \markbox{m7294}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{7295}{and} \markbox{7296}{where} \markbox{m7297}{$K = K(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7298}{is} \markbox{7299}{chosen} \markbox{7300}{independent} \markbox{7301}{of} \markbox{7302}{the} setup.
    
    \item (Bounded \markbox{7303}{geodesic} \markbox{7304}{image)} \markbox{7305}{Suppose} \markbox{m7306}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{m7307}{$C \subset \hT_U - \hd^V_U$} \markbox{7308}{is} \markbox{7309}{a} \markbox{7310}{component,} \markbox{7311}{then} \markbox{m7312}{$\hd^U_V(C)$} \markbox{7313}{is} \markbox{7314}{a} \markbox{7315}{point.}  \markbox{7316}{In} \markbox{7317}{particular,} \markbox{7318}{if} \markbox{m7319}{$f \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{7320}{with} \markbox{m7321}{$\hf_U$} \markbox{7322}{contained} \markbox{7323}{in} \markbox{m7324}{$C$}, \markbox{7325}{then} \markbox{m7326}{$\hd^U_V(C) = \hf_V.$}

 \item If \markbox{m7327}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{7328}{then} \markbox{m7329}{$\{U \in \calU| \hx_U \notin \{\ha_U,\hb_U\}\}$} \markbox{7330}{is} \markbox{7331}{pairwise} \markbox{7332}{non-transverse,} \markbox{7333}{and} \markbox{7334}{hence} \markbox{7335}{has} \markbox{7336}{cardinality} \markbox{7337}{bounded} \markbox{7338}{in} \markbox{7339}{terms} \markbox{7340}{of} \markbox{m7341}{$\mathfrak S$}.
   
    
    \item If \markbox{m7342}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{7343}{then} \markbox{m7344}{$E(\hx) = \{U \in \calU| \hx_U \in \hT^e_U\}$} \markbox{7345}{is} \markbox{7346}{pairwise} orthogonal.
    
   
\end{enumerate}
\end{lemma}

\begin{remark}
Item \markbox{7347}{(5)} \markbox{7348}{is} \markbox{7349}{notably} \markbox{7350}{the} \markbox{7351}{first} \markbox{7352}{time} \markbox{7353}{that} \markbox{7354}{the} \markbox{7355}{constant} \markbox{m7356}{$r_2$} \markbox{7357}{from} \markbox{7358}{Definition} \ref{defn:thickening} \markbox{7359}{plays} \markbox{7360}{a} \markbox{7361}{substantial} \markbox{7362}{role.}  \markbox{7363}{This} \markbox{7364}{is} \markbox{7365}{important} \markbox{7366}{later} \markbox{7367}{in} \markbox{7368}{proving} \markbox{7369}{that} \markbox{7370}{the} \markbox{7371}{map} \markbox{m7372}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{7373}{between}  \markbox{m7374}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{7375}{set} \markbox{m7376}{$\calQ$} \markbox{7377}{and} \markbox{7378}{the} \markbox{7379}{hierarchical} \markbox{7380}{hull} \markbox{m7381}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{7382}{is} \markbox{7383}{a} \markbox{7384}{quasi-isometry.}  \markbox{7385}{Another} \markbox{7386}{notable} \markbox{7387}{statement} \markbox{7388}{is} \markbox{7389}{item} \markbox{7390}{(6),} \markbox{7391}{which} \markbox{7392}{is} \markbox{7393}{about} \markbox{m7394}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{7395}{domains,} \markbox{7396}{namely} \markbox{7397}{domains} \markbox{m7398}{$U$} \markbox{7399}{for} \markbox{7400}{which} \markbox{7401}{no} \markbox{m7402}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{7403}{has} \markbox{m7404}{$V \nest U$}.  \markbox{7405}{Here} \markbox{7406}{is} \markbox{7407}{where} \markbox{7408}{our} \markbox{7409}{largeness} \markbox{7410}{constant} \markbox{m7411}{$K$} \markbox{7412}{plays} \markbox{7413}{a} \markbox{7414}{crucial} \markbox{7415}{role.}  \markbox{7416}{In} \markbox{7417}{particular,} \markbox{7418}{since} \markbox{7419}{nothing} \markbox{7420}{nests} \markbox{7421}{into} \markbox{7422}{a} \markbox{m7423}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{7424}{domain} \markbox{m7425}{$U$}, \markbox{7426}{the} \markbox{7427}{map} \markbox{m7428}{$q_U: T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{7429}{only} \markbox{7430}{collapses} \markbox{7431}{the} \markbox{m7432}{$r_1$}-neighborhood \markbox{7433}{of} \markbox{7434}{each} \markbox{7435}{endpoint,} \markbox{7436}{and} \markbox{7437}{hence} \markbox{7438}{the} \markbox{7439}{diameter} \markbox{7440}{of} \markbox{m7441}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{7442}{is} \markbox{7443}{coarsely} \markbox{7444}{bounded} \markbox{7445}{below} \markbox{7446}{by} \markbox{m7447}{$K$}.  \markbox{7448}{This} \markbox{7449}{is} \markbox{7450}{also} \markbox{7451}{important} \markbox{7452}{for} \markbox{7453}{confirming} \markbox{7454}{that} \markbox{m7455}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{7456}{is} \markbox{7457}{a} \markbox{7458}{quasi-isometry;} \markbox{7459}{see} \markbox{7460}{Section} \ref{sec:hPsi qi} below.
\end{remark}

\begin{proof}
Item \markbox{7461}{(1)} \markbox{7462}{is}  \markbox{7463}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}.  \markbox{7464}{Item} \markbox{7465}{(2)follows} \markbox{7466}{from} \markbox{7467}{item} \markbox{7468}{(2)} \markbox{7469}{of} \markbox{7470}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{7471}{by} \markbox{7472}{choosing} \markbox{m7473}{$r_1>2R$}.  \markbox{7474}{Similarly,} \markbox{7475}{item} \markbox{7476}{(3)} \markbox{7477}{follows} \markbox{7478}{from} \markbox{7479}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{7480}{(namely,} \markbox{7481}{item} \markbox{7482}{(1)} \markbox{7483}{of} \markbox{7484}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}) \markbox{7485}{by} \markbox{7486}{choosing} \markbox{m7487}{$r_1 > 2R$}.  

Item \markbox{7488}{(4)} \markbox{7489}{follows} \markbox{7490}{directly} \markbox{7491}{from} \markbox{7492}{the} \markbox{7493}{construction} \markbox{7494}{and} \markbox{7495}{item} \markbox{7496}{(3)} \markbox{7497}{of} \markbox{7498}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}.

Item \markbox{7499}{(4)} \markbox{7500}{is} \markbox{7501}{an} \markbox{7502}{immediate} \markbox{7503}{consequence} \markbox{7504}{of} \markbox{7505}{the} \markbox{7506}{definition} \markbox{7507}{of} \markbox{7508}{the} \markbox{7509}{hull} \markbox{m7510}{$H$} \markbox{7511}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hier hull}) \markbox{7512}{and} \markbox{7513}{the} \markbox{7514}{construction} \markbox{7515}{in} \markbox{7516}{this} \markbox{7517}{subsection.}  \markbox{7518}{In} \markbox{7519}{particular,} \markbox{7520}{by} \markbox{7521}{assumption} \markbox{m7522}{$\phi_U:T_U \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{7523}{is} \markbox{7524}{an} \markbox{m7525}{$(R,R)$}-quasi-geodesic \markbox{7526}{between} \markbox{m7527}{$\pi_U(a), \pi_U(b)$}, \markbox{7528}{giving} \markbox{7529}{the} \markbox{7530}{coarse} \markbox{7531}{equality,} \markbox{7532}{while} \markbox{7533}{the} \markbox{7534}{inequality} \markbox{7535}{follows} \markbox{7536}{because} \markbox{m7537}{$q_U:T_U\to \hT_U$} \markbox{7538}{collapses} \markbox{7539}{subintervals} \markbox{7540}{and} \markbox{7541}{therefore} \markbox{7542}{is} \markbox{7543}{distance} non-increasing.


For \markbox{7544}{item} \markbox{7545}{(5),} \markbox{7546}{if} \markbox{m7547}{$\hpsi_U(x),\hpsi_U(y)$} \markbox{7548}{are} \markbox{7549}{in} \markbox{7550}{distinct} \markbox{7551}{clusters,} \markbox{7552}{then} \markbox{m7553}{$d_{T_U}(x,y) > r_2$}, \markbox{7554}{and} \markbox{7555}{hence} \markbox{m7556}{$d_U(x,y) \succ r_2$} \markbox{7557}{by} \markbox{7558}{item} \markbox{7559}{(4).}  \markbox{7560}{Hence} \markbox{7561}{choosing} \markbox{m7562}{$r_2$} \markbox{7563}{large} \markbox{7564}{enough} \markbox{7565}{gives} \markbox{7566}{the} \markbox{7567}{desired} \markbox{7568}{lower} bound.

For \markbox{7569}{item} \markbox{7570}{(6):} \markbox{7571}{When} \markbox{m7572}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{7573}{is} \markbox{m7574}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{7575}{with} \markbox{7576}{respect} \markbox{7577}{to} \markbox{m7578}{$\calU$}, \markbox{7579}{then} \markbox{m7580}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{7581}{only} \markbox{7582}{collapses} \markbox{7583}{the} \markbox{m7584}{$r_1$}-neighborhoods \markbox{7585}{of} \markbox{m7586}{$a_U,b_U$} \markbox{7587}{in} \markbox{m7588}{$T_U$}.  \markbox{7589}{Since} \markbox{m7590}{$d_U(a,b)>K$} \markbox{7591}{by} \markbox{7592}{assumption,} \markbox{7593}{it} \markbox{7594}{follows} \markbox{7595}{that} \markbox{m7596}{$d_{T_U}(a_U,b_U) \succ K$}, \markbox{7597}{while} \markbox{7598}{the} \markbox{7599}{map} \markbox{m7600}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{7601}{only} \markbox{7602}{collapses} \markbox{7603}{the} \markbox{m7604}{$r_1$}-neighborhoods \markbox{7605}{of} \markbox{m7606}{$a_U,b_U$}.  \markbox{7607}{Thus} \markbox{7608}{provided} \markbox{7609}{that} \markbox{m7610}{$K -2r_1 > r_2$} \markbox{7611}{(which} \markbox{7612}{we} \markbox{7613}{can} \markbox{7614}{arrange),} \markbox{7615}{the} \markbox{7616}{claim} follows.



For \markbox{7617}{item} \markbox{7618}{(7):} \markbox{7619}{By} \markbox{7620}{item} \markbox{7621}{(1),} \markbox{7622}{if} \markbox{m7623}{$\hf_U$} \markbox{7624}{is} \markbox{7625}{a} \markbox{7626}{marked} \markbox{7627}{point,} \markbox{7628}{then} \markbox{m7629}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{7630}{of} \markbox{m7631}{$(\hf_V) = \hPsi(f)$} \markbox{7632}{implies} \markbox{7633}{that} \markbox{m7634}{$\hd^U_V(\hf_U) = \hf_V$} \markbox{7635}{because} \markbox{m7636}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U(f_U),f_V)<\alpha_0 < r_1$}, \markbox{7637}{where} \markbox{7638}{we} \markbox{7639}{note} \markbox{7640}{that} \markbox{m7641}{$\alpha_0 = \alpha_0(R, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7642}{by} \markbox{7643}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval consistency}.  \markbox{7644}{On} \markbox{7645}{the} \markbox{7646}{other} \markbox{7647}{hand,} \markbox{7648}{since} \markbox{m7649}{$C \cap \hd^V_U = \emptyset$}, \markbox{7650}{we} \markbox{7651}{have} \markbox{m7652}{$d_{T_U}(q^{-1}_U(C), \delta^V_U)>R$}.  \markbox{7653}{Hence} \markbox{7654}{item} \markbox{7655}{(4)} \markbox{7656}{of} \markbox{7657}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{7658}{says} \markbox{7659}{that} \markbox{m7660}{$\diam_{T_V}(\delta^U_V(C))<R$}, \markbox{7661}{while} \markbox{7662}{also} \markbox{m7663}{$\delta^U_V(f_U) \subset \delta^V_U(C)$}.  \markbox{7664}{Hence} \markbox{m7665}{$d_{T_V}(\delta^U_V(C), f_V)<\alpha_0 + R<r_1$}, \markbox{7666}{where} \markbox{7667}{we} \markbox{7668}{guarantee} \markbox{7669}{the} \markbox{7670}{last} \markbox{7671}{inequality} \markbox{7672}{by} \markbox{7673}{increasing} \markbox{m7674}{$r_1$} \markbox{7675}{as} \markbox{7676}{necessary.}  \markbox{7677}{It} \markbox{7678}{follows} \markbox{7679}{then} \markbox{7680}{that} \markbox{m7681}{$\hd^U_V(C) = \hf_V$}, \markbox{7682}{as} claimed.



For \markbox{7683}{item} \markbox{7684}{(8):} \markbox{7685}{Suppose} \markbox{m7686}{$U, V$} \markbox{7687}{are} \markbox{7688}{transverse} \markbox{7689}{and} \markbox{m7690}{$\hx_U \notin  \{\ha_U, \hb_U\}$}.  \markbox{7691}{Since} \markbox{m7692}{$\hd^V_U \in \{\ha_U,\hb_U\}$} \markbox{7693}{by} \markbox{7694}{item} \markbox{7695}{(2)} \markbox{7696}{and} \markbox{7697}{hence} \markbox{m7698}{$\hx_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{7699}{it} \markbox{7700}{follows} \markbox{7701}{from} \markbox{m7702}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{7703}{of} \markbox{m7704}{$\hx$} \markbox{7705}{that} \markbox{m7706}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V$}.  \markbox{7707}{Thus} \markbox{m7708}{$\hx_V \in \{\ha_V,\hb_V\}$} \markbox{7709}{and} \markbox{7710}{so} \markbox{7711}{the} \markbox{7712}{set} \markbox{7713}{in} \markbox{7714}{the} \markbox{7715}{statement} \markbox{7716}{of} \markbox{7717}{item} \markbox{7718}{(8)} \markbox{7719}{is} \markbox{7720}{pairwise} \markbox{7721}{non-transverse,} \markbox{7722}{and} \markbox{7723}{hence} \markbox{7724}{has} \markbox{7725}{bounded} \markbox{7726}{complexity} \markbox{7727}{by} \markbox{7728}{item} \markbox{7729}{(2)} \markbox{7730}{in} \markbox{7731}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:basic HHS}.

Finally, \markbox{7732}{for} \markbox{7733}{item} \markbox{7734}{(9):} \markbox{7735}{Recall} \markbox{7736}{that} \markbox{m7737}{$\hT^e_U = \hT_U - \hT^c_U$}, \markbox{7738}{where} \markbox{m7739}{$\hT^c_U$} \markbox{7740}{are} \markbox{7741}{the} \markbox{7742}{collapsed} \markbox{7743}{points.}  \markbox{7744}{Hence} \markbox{m7745}{$E(\hx)$} \markbox{7746}{is} \markbox{7747}{the} \markbox{7748}{set} \markbox{7749}{of} \markbox{7750}{domains} \markbox{7751}{where} \markbox{m7752}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{7753}{is} \markbox{7754}{not} \markbox{7755}{a} \markbox{7756}{collapsed} \markbox{7757}{point.}  \markbox{7758}{Supposing} \markbox{7759}{that} \markbox{m7760}{$U,V$} \markbox{7761}{are} \markbox{7762}{neither} \markbox{7763}{orthogonal} \markbox{7764}{nor} \markbox{7765}{(by} \markbox{7766}{item} \markbox{7767}{(8))} \markbox{7768}{transverse.}  \markbox{7769}{When} \markbox{m7770}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{7771}{and} \markbox{m7772}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{7773}{we} \markbox{7774}{are} \markbox{7775}{done} \markbox{7776}{by} \markbox{7777}{items} \markbox{7778}{(1)} \markbox{7779}{and} \markbox{7780}{(3).}  \markbox{7781}{When} \markbox{m7782}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{7783}{and} \markbox{m7784}{$\hx_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{7785}{item} \markbox{7786}{(7)} \markbox{7787}{implies} \markbox{7788}{there} \markbox{7789}{is} \markbox{7790}{some} \markbox{m7791}{$f \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{7792}{so} \markbox{7793}{that} \markbox{m7794}{$\hd^U_V(\hx_U) = \hf_V$}, \markbox{7795}{while} \markbox{m7796}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{7797}{says} \markbox{7798}{that} \markbox{m7799}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V(\hx_U)$}, \markbox{7800}{giving} \markbox{m7801}{$\hx_V = \hf_V$}.  \markbox{7802}{Hence} \markbox{7803}{if} \markbox{m7804}{$U$} \markbox{7805}{and} \markbox{m7806}{$V$} \markbox{7807}{are} \markbox{7808}{not} \markbox{7809}{orthogonal,} \markbox{7810}{then} \markbox{7811}{one} \markbox{7812}{of} \markbox{m7813}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{7814}{or} \markbox{m7815}{$\hx_V$} \markbox{7816}{must} \markbox{7817}{be} \markbox{7818}{a} \markbox{7819}{collapsed} \markbox{7820}{point,} \markbox{7821}{proving} \markbox{7822}{this} \markbox{7823}{item.}  \markbox{7824}{This} \markbox{7825}{completes} \markbox{7826}{the} proof.



\end{proof}














\section{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$ is a quasi-isometry} \label{sec:hPsi qi}

In \markbox{7827}{this} \markbox{7828}{section,} \markbox{7829}{we} \markbox{7830}{explain} \markbox{7831}{why} \markbox{7832}{the} \markbox{7833}{map} \markbox{m7834}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{7835}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}) \markbox{7836}{between} \markbox{7837}{the} \markbox{7838}{hierarchical} \markbox{7839}{hull} \markbox{m7840}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{7841}{of} \markbox{7842}{a} \markbox{7843}{pair} \markbox{7844}{of} \markbox{7845}{points} \markbox{m7846}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{7847}{and} \markbox{7848}{the} \markbox{m7849}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{7850}{set} \markbox{7851}{associated} \markbox{7852}{to} \markbox{7853}{any} \markbox{7854}{sufficiently} \markbox{7855}{wide} \markbox{m7856}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{7857}{of} \markbox{7858}{an} \markbox{m7859}{$R$}-interval \markbox{7860}{system} \markbox{7861}{for} \markbox{m7862}{$a,b$} \markbox{7863}{is} \markbox{7864}{a} \markbox{7865}{quasi-isometry.}  \markbox{7866}{There} \markbox{7867}{are} \markbox{7868}{two} \markbox{7869}{main} \markbox{7870}{parts} \markbox{7871}{to} this:

\begin{enumerate}
\item Proving \markbox{7872}{that} \markbox{m7873}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{7874}{is} \markbox{7875}{a} \markbox{7876}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{7877}{embedding,} and
\item Proving \markbox{7878}{that} \markbox{m7879}{$\hPsi$} \markbox{7880}{is} \markbox{7881}{coarsely} \markbox{7882}{surjective.}  \markbox{7883}{This} \markbox{7884}{is} \markbox{7885}{accomplished} \markbox{7886}{by} \markbox{7887}{defining} \markbox{7888}{a} \markbox{7889}{coarse} \markbox{7890}{inverse} \markbox{m7891}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$}, \markbox{7892}{so} \markbox{7893}{that} \markbox{m7894}{$\hPsi \circ \hO$} \markbox{7895}{is} \markbox{7896}{coarsely} \markbox{7897}{the} \markbox{7898}{identity} \markbox{7899}{on} \markbox{m7900}{$\calQ$}.
\end{enumerate}

As \markbox{7901}{we} \markbox{7902}{shall} \markbox{7903}{see,} \markbox{7904}{these} \markbox{7905}{two} \markbox{7906}{results} \markbox{7907}{have} \markbox{7908}{fairly} \markbox{7909}{different} \markbox{7910}{flavors---(1)} \markbox{7911}{is} \markbox{7912}{essentially} \markbox{7913}{purely} \markbox{7914}{hierarchical,} \markbox{7915}{while} \markbox{7916}{(2)} \markbox{7917}{has} \markbox{7918}{distinctly} \markbox{7919}{cubical} \markbox{7920}{elements.}  \markbox{7921}{Item} \markbox{7922}{(1)} \markbox{7923}{essentially} \markbox{7924}{says} \markbox{7925}{that} \markbox{7926}{one} \markbox{7927}{can} \markbox{7928}{encode} \markbox{7929}{the} \markbox{7930}{distance} \markbox{7931}{formula} \markbox{7932}{in} \markbox{m7933}{$\calX$} \markbox{7934}{as} \markbox{7935}{the} \markbox{m7936}{$\ell^1$}-distance \markbox{7937}{in} \markbox{7938}{a} \markbox{7939}{product} \markbox{7940}{of} \markbox{7941}{intervals.}  \markbox{7942}{Its} \markbox{7943}{proof} \markbox{7944}{involves} \markbox{7945}{mostly} \markbox{7946}{distance} \markbox{7947}{formula-type} \markbox{7948}{arguments} \markbox{7949}{and} \markbox{7950}{we} \markbox{7951}{present} \markbox{7952}{it} \markbox{7953}{in} \markbox{7954}{full.}  \markbox{7955}{On} \markbox{7956}{the} \markbox{7957}{other} \markbox{7958}{hand,} \markbox{7959}{the} \markbox{7960}{proof} \markbox{7961}{of} \markbox{7962}{item} \markbox{7963}{(2),} \markbox{7964}{which} \markbox{7965}{is} \markbox{7966}{contained} \markbox{7967}{in} \cite[Sections 9--11]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{7968}{is} \markbox{7969}{rather} \markbox{7970}{involved} \markbox{7971}{and} \markbox{7972}{many} \markbox{7973}{of} \markbox{7974}{the} \markbox{7975}{details} \markbox{7976}{of} \markbox{7977}{the} \markbox{7978}{argument} \markbox{7979}{are} \markbox{7980}{not} \markbox{7981}{crucial} \markbox{7982}{to} \markbox{7983}{our} \markbox{7984}{expository} \markbox{7985}{purposes} \markbox{7986}{in} \markbox{7987}{this} \markbox{7988}{article.}  \markbox{7989}{Thus,} \markbox{7990}{in} \markbox{7991}{this} \markbox{7992}{section,} \markbox{7993}{we} \markbox{7994}{will} \markbox{7995}{mostly} \markbox{7996}{explain} \markbox{7997}{the} \markbox{7998}{basics} \markbox{7999}{of} \markbox{8000}{the} \markbox{8001}{construction,} \markbox{8002}{including} \markbox{8003}{the} \markbox{8004}{points} \markbox{8005}{where} \markbox{8006}{our} \markbox{8007}{simpler} \markbox{8008}{setting} \markbox{8009}{simplifies} \markbox{8010}{things} considerably.

The \markbox{8011}{one} \markbox{8012}{exception} \markbox{8013}{here} \markbox{8014}{is} \markbox{8015}{the} \markbox{8016}{Tree} \markbox{8017}{Trimming} \markbox{8018}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}, \markbox{8019}{which} \markbox{8020}{is} \markbox{8021}{a} \markbox{8022}{distance-formula} \markbox{8023}{like} \markbox{8024}{tool} \markbox{8025}{that} \markbox{8026}{we} \markbox{8027}{need} \markbox{8028}{both} \markbox{8029}{here} \markbox{8030}{and} \markbox{8031}{for} \markbox{8032}{our} \markbox{8033}{stability} \markbox{8034}{results} \markbox{8035}{in} \markbox{8036}{Section} \ref{sec:stable cubes}.  \markbox{8037}{We} \markbox{8038}{will} \markbox{8039}{discuss} \markbox{8040}{it} \markbox{8041}{in} \markbox{8042}{detail} \markbox{8043}{and} \markbox{8044}{present} \markbox{8045}{its} \markbox{8046}{proof} \markbox{8047}{in} \markbox{8048}{Appendix} \ref{app:TT}.

For \markbox{8049}{the} \markbox{8050}{rest} \markbox{8051}{of} \markbox{8052}{this} \markbox{8053}{section,} \markbox{8054}{fix} \markbox{m8055}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{8056}{and} \markbox{8057}{let} \markbox{m8058}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{8059}{to} \markbox{8060}{be} \markbox{8061}{their} \markbox{8062}{hierarchical} \markbox{8063}{hull.}  \markbox{8064}{Fix} \markbox{8065}{a} \markbox{8066}{largeness} \markbox{8067}{constant} \markbox{m8068}{$K$}, \markbox{8069}{which} \markbox{8070}{we} \markbox{8071}{will} \markbox{8072}{be} \markbox{8073}{able} \markbox{8074}{to} \markbox{8075}{control} \markbox{8076}{relative} \markbox{8077}{to} \markbox{8078}{all} \markbox{8079}{other} \markbox{8080}{involved} \markbox{8081}{constants,} \markbox{8082}{and} \markbox{8083}{set} \markbox{m8084}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$}.  \markbox{8085}{Finally,} \markbox{8086}{fix} \markbox{m8087}{$R>0$} \markbox{8088}{and} \markbox{8089}{an} \markbox{m8090}{$R$}-interval \markbox{8091}{system} \markbox{m8092}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{8093}{for} \markbox{m8094}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{8095}{Let} \markbox{m8096}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{8097}{denote} \markbox{8098}{the} \markbox{8099}{family} \markbox{8100}{of} \markbox{8101}{collapsed} \markbox{8102}{intervals} \markbox{8103}{corresponding} \markbox{8104}{to} \markbox{8105}{an} \markbox{m8106}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening, \markbox{8107}{where} \markbox{m8108}{$r_i = r_i(R,\theta,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8109}{are} \markbox{8110}{provided} \markbox{8111}{by} \markbox{8112}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined} \markbox{8113}{and} \markbox{8114}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.

\subsection{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$ is a quasi-isometric embedding}\label{subsec:Q qie}

The \markbox{8115}{content} \markbox{8116}{of} \markbox{8117}{this} \markbox{8118}{subsection} \markbox{8119}{is} \markbox{8120}{roughly} \markbox{8121}{contained} \markbox{8122}{in} \cite[Section 8]{Dur_infcube}.  

Before \markbox{8123}{we} \markbox{8124}{state} \markbox{8125}{the} \markbox{8126}{result,} \markbox{8127}{we} \markbox{8128}{set} \markbox{8129}{some} \markbox{8130}{additional} \markbox{8131}{notation:} \markbox{8132}{For} \markbox{8133}{numbers} \markbox{m8134}{$A,B$}, \markbox{8135}{the} \markbox{8136}{notation} \markbox{m8137}{$[A]_B$} \markbox{8138}{means} \markbox{m8139}{$0$} \markbox{8140}{when} \markbox{m8141}{$A<B$} \markbox{8142}{and} \markbox{m8143}{$A$} \markbox{8144}{when} \markbox{m8145}{$A\geq B$}.  \markbox{8146}{For} \markbox{m8147}{$x \in H$} \markbox{8148}{and} \markbox{m8149}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{8150}{we} \markbox{8151}{will} write
\begin{itemize}
\item \markbox{m8152}{$x = \pi_U(x) \in \calC(U)$};
\item \markbox{m8153}{$x_U = \psi_U(x) \in T_U$};
\item \markbox{m8154}{$\hx_U = \hpsi_U(x) \in \hT_U$}.
\end{itemize}

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:Q distance estimate}
There \markbox{8155}{exists} \markbox{m8156}{$K_1 = K_1(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8157}{so} \markbox{8158}{that} \markbox{8159}{for} \markbox{8160}{any} \markbox{m8161}{$K_2 \geq K_1$} \markbox{8162}{and} \markbox{8163}{any} \markbox{m8164}{$x, y \in H$}, \markbox{8165}{we} \markbox{8166}{have} that
$$d_{\calX}(a,b) \asymp \sum_{U \in \mathfrak S} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} \asymp \sum_{U \in \calU} d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)$$
where \markbox{8167}{the} \markbox{8168}{constants} \markbox{8169}{in} \markbox{m8170}{$\asymp$} \markbox{8171}{only} \markbox{8172}{depend} \markbox{8173}{on} \markbox{m8174}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{8175}{and} \markbox{8176}{the} \markbox{8177}{choice} \markbox{8178}{of} \markbox{m8179}{$K_2$}.
\end{theorem}

We \markbox{8180}{note} \markbox{8181}{that} \markbox{8182}{the} \markbox{8183}{left} \markbox{8184}{coarse} \markbox{8185}{equality} \markbox{8186}{of} \markbox{8187}{the} \markbox{8188}{above} \markbox{8189}{statement} \markbox{8190}{is} \markbox{8191}{simply} \markbox{8192}{the} \markbox{8193}{Distance} \markbox{8194}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}, \markbox{8195}{hence} \markbox{8196}{the} \markbox{8197}{content} \markbox{8198}{is} \markbox{8199}{the} \markbox{8200}{right} \markbox{8201}{coarse} \markbox{8202}{equality.}  \markbox{8203}{In} \markbox{8204}{fact,} \markbox{8205}{one} \markbox{8206}{can} \markbox{8207}{obtain} \markbox{8208}{the} \markbox{8209}{(more} \markbox{8210}{difficult)} \markbox{8211}{lower-bound} \markbox{8212}{in} \markbox{8213}{the} \markbox{8214}{distance} \markbox{8215}{formula} \markbox{8216}{by} \markbox{8217}{combining} \markbox{8218}{the} \markbox{8219}{above} \markbox{8220}{theorem} \markbox{8221}{with} \markbox{8222}{the} \markbox{8223}{construction} \markbox{8224}{of} \markbox{8225}{hierarchy} \markbox{8226}{paths} \markbox{8227}{via} \markbox{8228}{cubical} \markbox{8229}{models,} \markbox{8230}{as} \markbox{8231}{we} \markbox{8232}{do} \markbox{8233}{below} \markbox{8234}{in} \markbox{8235}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF lower bound}.

Before \markbox{8236}{beginning} \markbox{8237}{the} \markbox{8238}{discussion} \markbox{8239}{of} \markbox{8240}{the} \markbox{8241}{proof} \markbox{8242}{properly,} \markbox{8243}{we} \markbox{8244}{make} \markbox{8245}{a} \markbox{8246}{couple} \markbox{8247}{of} \markbox{8248}{simplifying} \markbox{8249}{observations,} \markbox{8250}{which} \markbox{8251}{are} \markbox{8252}{all} \markbox{8253}{basically} \markbox{8254}{distance} \markbox{8255}{formula-type} manipulations.

First, \markbox{8256}{note} \markbox{8257}{that} \markbox{8258}{if} \markbox{m8259}{$x,y \in H$} \markbox{8260}{and} \markbox{m8261}{$V \in \Rel_K(x,y)$} \markbox{8262}{but} \markbox{m8263}{$V \notin \calU$}, \markbox{8264}{then} \markbox{m8265}{$d_V(x,y) < K + \epsilon$} \markbox{8266}{for} \markbox{8267}{some} \markbox{m8268}{$\epsilon = \epsilon(\mathfrak S)>0$}.  \markbox{8269}{This} \markbox{8270}{is} \markbox{8271}{because} \markbox{m8272}{$\pi_V(x), \pi_V(y) \in \calN_{\theta}(\hull_V(a,b))$}.  \markbox{8273}{Hence} \markbox{8274}{by} \markbox{8275}{taking} \markbox{m8276}{$K_2 \geq K_1 > K + \epsilon$}, \markbox{8277}{we} \markbox{8278}{may} \markbox{8279}{increase} \markbox{8280}{the} \markbox{8281}{threshold} \markbox{8282}{to} \markbox{8283}{remove} \markbox{8284}{any} \markbox{8285}{extraneous} \markbox{8286}{domains.}  \markbox{8287}{That} is:
$$\sum_{U \in \mathfrak S} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} = \sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2}.$$

We \markbox{8288}{next} \markbox{8289}{observe} \markbox{8290}{that} \markbox{8291}{for} \markbox{8292}{any} \markbox{m8293}{$x,y \in H$}, \markbox{8294}{item} \markbox{8295}{(4)} \markbox{8296}{of} \markbox{8297}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{8298}{implies} \markbox{8299}{that} \markbox{m8300}{$d_U(x,y) \asymp d_{T_U}(x_U, y_U)$}, \markbox{8301}{with} \markbox{8302}{constants} \markbox{8303}{depending} \markbox{8304}{only} \markbox{8305}{on} \markbox{m8306}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{8307}{Thus} \markbox{8308}{we} \markbox{8309}{can} \markbox{8310}{use} \markbox{8311}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF replace} \markbox{8312}{to} \markbox{8313}{replace} \markbox{8314}{the} \markbox{8315}{terms} \markbox{m8316}{$d_U(x,y)$} \markbox{8317}{with} \markbox{m8318}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)$} \markbox{8319}{in} \markbox{8320}{the} \markbox{8321}{sum,} namely:

$$\sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} \asymp \sum_{U \in \calU} [d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)]_{K_2}.$$

The \markbox{8322}{two} \markbox{8323}{bounds} \markbox{8324}{in} \markbox{8325}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q distance estimate} \markbox{8326}{are} \markbox{8327}{proven} \markbox{8328}{separately.}  \markbox{8329}{The} \markbox{8330}{upper} \markbox{8331}{bound} \markbox{8332}{only} \markbox{8333}{requires} \markbox{8334}{the} \markbox{8335}{basic} \markbox{8336}{details} \markbox{8337}{from} \markbox{8338}{the} \markbox{8339}{construction} \markbox{8340}{of} \markbox{8341}{the} \markbox{m8342}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{8343}{and} \markbox{8344}{some} \markbox{8345}{distance} \markbox{8346}{formula} \markbox{8347}{tools.}  \markbox{8348}{We} \markbox{8349}{have} \markbox{8350}{included} \markbox{8351}{the} \markbox{8352}{full} \markbox{8353}{proof} \markbox{8354}{of} \markbox{8355}{the} \markbox{8356}{proposition} \markbox{8357}{for} \markbox{8358}{clarity} \markbox{8359}{but} \markbox{8360}{also} \markbox{8361}{because} \markbox{8362}{it} \markbox{8363}{is} \markbox{8364}{used} \markbox{8365}{in} \markbox{8366}{proving} \markbox{8367}{the} \markbox{8368}{existence} \markbox{8369}{of} \markbox{8370}{hierarchy} \markbox{8371}{paths} \markbox{8372}{and} \markbox{8373}{the} \markbox{8374}{upper} \markbox{8375}{bound} \markbox{8376}{of} \markbox{8377}{the} \markbox{8378}{distance} \markbox{8379}{formula;} \markbox{8380}{moreover,} \markbox{8381}{the} \markbox{8382}{argument} \markbox{8383}{is} \markbox{8384}{similar} \markbox{8385}{to} \markbox{8386}{the} \markbox{8387}{proof} \markbox{8388}{of} \markbox{8389}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF replace}, \markbox{8390}{which} \markbox{8391}{actually} \markbox{8392}{implies} \markbox{8393}{the} proposition.

\begin{proposition}[Upper bound]\label{prop:upper bound}
There \markbox{8394}{exists} \markbox{m8395}{$K_1= K_1(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8396}{so} \markbox{8397}{that} \markbox{8398}{for} \markbox{8399}{any} \markbox{m8400}{$K_2 >K_1$} \markbox{8401}{and} \markbox{8402}{any} \markbox{m8403}{$x, y \in H$} \markbox{8404}{we} have
\begin{equation}\label{eqn:upper}
    \sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} \succ \sum_{U \in \calU} d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)
\end{equation}
with \markbox{8405}{the} \markbox{8406}{constants} \markbox{8407}{in} \markbox{m8408}{$\succ$} \markbox{8409}{depending} \markbox{8410}{only} \markbox{8411}{on} \markbox{m8412}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{8413}{and} \markbox{m8414}{$K_2$}.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}

As \markbox{8415}{above,} \markbox{8416}{let} \markbox{m8417}{$K_1 \geq K + \epsilon$} \markbox{8418}{and} \markbox{8419}{set} \markbox{m8420}{$K_2 \geq K_1 + 100\ES$}.  \markbox{8421}{Let} \markbox{m8422}{$\calU_i = \Rel_{K_i}(x,y)$}, \markbox{8423}{so} \markbox{8424}{that} \markbox{m8425}{$\calU_2 \subset \calU_1 \subset \calU$}.  \markbox{8426}{If} \markbox{m8427}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{8428}{satisfies} \markbox{m8429}{$\hx_U = \hy_U$}, \markbox{8430}{then} \markbox{8431}{the} \markbox{8432}{corresponding} \markbox{8433}{term} \markbox{8434}{disappears} \markbox{8435}{on} \markbox{8436}{the} \markbox{8437}{right-hand} \markbox{8438}{side.}  \markbox{8439}{Hence} \markbox{8440}{it} \markbox{8441}{suffices} \markbox{8442}{to} \markbox{8443}{account} \markbox{8444}{for} \markbox{8445}{the} \markbox{8446}{domains} \markbox{8447}{in} \markbox{m8448}{$\calV = \{V \in \calU | d_V(x,y) < K_2 \textrm{ and } \hx_U \neq \hy_U\}$}, \markbox{8449}{which} \markbox{8450}{appear} \markbox{8451}{on} \markbox{8452}{the} \markbox{8453}{right-hand} \markbox{8454}{side} \markbox{8455}{(RHS)} \markbox{8456}{but} \markbox{8457}{not} \markbox{8458}{the} \markbox{8459}{left-hand} \markbox{8460}{side} \markbox{8461}{(LHS)} \markbox{8462}{of} \markbox{8463}{equation} \eqref{eqn:upper}.

For \markbox{8464}{this,} \markbox{8465}{item} \markbox{8466}{(9)} \markbox{8467}{of} \markbox{8468}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{8469}{says} \markbox{8470}{that} \markbox{m8471}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{8472}{is} \markbox{8473}{not} \markbox{8474}{contained} \markbox{8475}{in} \markbox{8476}{some} \markbox{8477}{cluster} \markbox{8478}{point} \markbox{8479}{of} \markbox{m8480}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{8481}{for} \markbox{8482}{only} \markbox{8483}{boundedly-many} \markbox{m8484}{$U$}, \markbox{8485}{and} \markbox{8486}{the} \markbox{8487}{same} \markbox{8488}{for} \markbox{m8489}{$\hy_U$}.  \markbox{8490}{(In} \markbox{8491}{fact,} \markbox{8492}{we} \markbox{8493}{can} \markbox{8494}{take} \markbox{m8495}{$\hx_U = \ha_U$} \markbox{8496}{and} \markbox{m8497}{$\hy_U = \hb_U$}, \markbox{8498}{be} \markbox{8499}{this} \markbox{8500}{will} \markbox{8501}{not} \markbox{8502}{simplify} \markbox{8503}{things.)} \markbox{8504}{This} \markbox{8505}{means} \markbox{8506}{that,} \markbox{8507}{up} \markbox{8508}{to} \markbox{8509}{ignoring} \markbox{8510}{a} \markbox{8511}{bounded} \markbox{8512}{collection} \markbox{8513}{of} \markbox{8514}{domains} \markbox{m8515}{$\calV' \subset \calV$}, \markbox{8516}{if} \markbox{m8517}{$V \in \calV - \calV'$} \markbox{8518}{then} \markbox{m8519}{$\hx_V$} \markbox{8520}{and} \markbox{m8521}{$\hy_V$} \markbox{8522}{are} \markbox{8523}{at} \markbox{8524}{distinct} \markbox{8525}{cluster} \markbox{8526}{points,} \markbox{8527}{and} \markbox{8528}{so} \markbox{m8529}{$d_V(x,y) > 50\ES$} \markbox{8530}{by} \markbox{8531}{item} \markbox{8532}{(5)} \markbox{8533}{of} \markbox{8534}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}, \markbox{8535}{i.e.,} \markbox{m8536}{$\calV-\calV' \subset \Rel_{50\ES}(x,y)$}, \markbox{8537}{while} \markbox{8538}{also} \markbox{m8539}{$d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V) \geq r_2 \geq 1$}.

One \markbox{8540}{finishes} \markbox{8541}{the} \markbox{8542}{proof} \markbox{8543}{with} \markbox{8544}{an} \markbox{8545}{application} \markbox{8546}{of} \markbox{8547}{Proposition} \ref{prop:bounding containers} \markbox{8548}{as} \markbox{8549}{follows.}  \markbox{8550}{Set} \markbox{m8551}{$\calU_i = \Rel_{K_i}(x,y)$} \markbox{8552}{and} \markbox{8553}{observe} \markbox{8554}{that} \markbox{m8555}{$\calV - \calV' \subset \calU_1 - \calU_2$}.  \markbox{8556}{Proposition} \ref{prop:bounding containers} \markbox{8557}{says} \markbox{8558}{that} \markbox{8559}{up} \markbox{8560}{to} \markbox{8561}{ignoring} \markbox{8562}{a} \markbox{8563}{subset} \markbox{m8564}{$\calV'' \subset \calV - \calV'$} \markbox{8565}{with} \markbox{m8566}{$\#\calV'' \leq P(K_2)$}, \markbox{8567}{for} \markbox{8568}{each} \markbox{m8569}{$V \in \calV_0 = \calV - (\calV' \cup \calV'')$} \markbox{8570}{there} \markbox{8571}{exists} \markbox{8572}{some} \markbox{8573}{domain} \markbox{m8574}{$W \in \calU_2$} \markbox{8575}{determining} \markbox{8576}{a} \markbox{8577}{term} \markbox{8578}{on} \markbox{8579}{the} \markbox{8580}{RHS} \markbox{8581}{with} \markbox{m8582}{$V \nest W$}.  \markbox{8583}{Moreover,} \markbox{8584}{it} \markbox{8585}{says} \markbox{8586}{that} \markbox{8587}{the} \markbox{8588}{set} \markbox{8589}{of} \markbox{8590}{domains} \markbox{m8591}{$\calW = \{V \in \calV| V\nest W\}$} \markbox{8592}{for} \markbox{8593}{which} \markbox{8594}{each} \markbox{8595}{such} \markbox{m8596}{$W$} \markbox{8597}{accounts} \markbox{8598}{in} \markbox{8599}{this} \markbox{8600}{way} \markbox{8601}{satisfies} \markbox{m8602}{$\#\calW \leq (1+A)\cdot d_W(x,y) + A$}, \markbox{8603}{for} \markbox{8604}{some} \markbox{m8605}{$A = A(K_2, \mathfrak S)>0$}.

Combining \markbox{8606}{these} \markbox{8607}{observations} \markbox{8608}{leads} \markbox{8609}{to} \markbox{8610}{the} computation
\begin{eqnarray*}
\sum_{U \in \calU_2} d_U(x,y) &=& \sum_{U \in \calU_2} d_U(x,y) + \sum_{V \in \calV - \calV'} d_V(x,y)+ \sum_{Z \in \calV'} d_Z(x,y)\\
&\leq& \sum_{U \in \calU_2} ((1+A)\cdot d_U(x,y)+A) + K_2 \cdot P(K_2)\\
&\leq& (1+2A)\cdot \sum_{U \in \calU_2} d_U(x,y) + K_2 \cdot P(K_2)
\end{eqnarray*}
where \markbox{8611}{the} \markbox{8612}{last} \markbox{8613}{inequality} \markbox{8614}{follows} \markbox{8615}{from} \markbox{8616}{the} \markbox{8617}{fact} \markbox{8618}{that} \markbox{m8619}{$d_U(x,y) > K_2$} \markbox{8620}{for} \markbox{8621}{each} \markbox{m8622}{$U \in \calU_2$}.  \markbox{8623}{This} \markbox{8624}{completes} \markbox{8625}{the} \markbox{8626}{proof.} 

\end{proof}


\begin{figure}[h]
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.8\textwidth]{figures/lower_bound_interval.pdf}
    \caption{Proof of Proposition \ref{prop:lower bound}: The subcluster $C'$ isolates the portion of $C$ which intersects $[x_U,y_U]$ but avoids the $(\alpha_0+R)$-neighborhoods of $x_U$ and $y_U$.  The (pink) net of $\delta$-sets from $\nest_{\calU}$-minimal domains $V \nest U$ with $\delta^V_U \subset C'$ coarsely encodes the length of $C'$, with the BGIA property guaranteeing that $\hx_V = \ha_V$ and $\hy_V = \hb_V$ and hence $d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V) \geq K - B^2 - 2r_1$ for each such $V$.}
    \label{fig:subcluster}
\end{figure}

\begin{proposition}[Lower bound]\label{prop:lower bound}
There \markbox{8627}{exists} \markbox{m8628}{$K_1= K_1(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8629}{so} \markbox{8630}{that} \markbox{8631}{for} \markbox{8632}{any} \markbox{m8633}{$K_2 >K_1$} \markbox{8634}{and} \markbox{8635}{any} \markbox{m8636}{$x, y \in H$} \markbox{8637}{we} have
\begin{equation}\label{eqn:lower}
    \sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} \prec \sum_{U \in \calU} d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)
\end{equation}
with \markbox{8638}{the} \markbox{8639}{constants} \markbox{8640}{in} \markbox{m8641}{$\prec$} \markbox{8642}{depending} \markbox{8643}{only} \markbox{8644}{on} \markbox{m8645}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{8646}{and} \markbox{m8647}{$K_2$}.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}

Observe \markbox{8648}{that} \markbox{8649}{since} \markbox{m8650}{$d_U(x,y) \prec d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)$} \markbox{8651}{for} \markbox{8652}{each} \markbox{m8653}{$U$}, \markbox{8654}{it} \markbox{8655}{suffices} \markbox{8656}{by} \markbox{8657}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF replace} \markbox{8658}{to} \markbox{8659}{show} \markbox{8660}{that} 
$$\sum_{U \in \calU} [d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)]_{K_2} \prec \sum_{U \in \calU} d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U).$$

For \markbox{8661}{this} \markbox{8662}{bound,} \markbox{8663}{there} \markbox{8664}{are} \markbox{8665}{possibly} \markbox{8666}{domains} \markbox{m8667}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{8668}{where} \markbox{m8669}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U) > K_2$} \markbox{8670}{but} \markbox{8671}{there} \markbox{8672}{is} \markbox{8673}{a} \markbox{8674}{discrepancy} \markbox{m8675}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U) > d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)$}.  \markbox{8676}{Let} \markbox{m8677}{$\calW$} \markbox{8678}{denote} \markbox{8679}{the} \markbox{8680}{collection} \markbox{8681}{of} \markbox{8682}{such} domains.

Since \markbox{m8683}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{8684}{is} \markbox{8685}{obtained} \markbox{8686}{from} \markbox{m8687}{$T_U$} \markbox{8688}{by} \markbox{8689}{collapsing} \markbox{8690}{clusters,} \markbox{8691}{we} \markbox{8692}{need} \markbox{8693}{to} \markbox{8694}{analyze} \markbox{8695}{the} \markbox{8696}{clusters} \markbox{8697}{which} \markbox{8698}{separate} \markbox{m8699}{$x_U$} \markbox{8700}{from} \markbox{m8701}{$y_U$}, \markbox{8702}{i.e.} \markbox{8703}{those} \markbox{8704}{clusters} \markbox{m8705}{$C_1, \dots, C_n$} \markbox{8706}{which} \markbox{8707}{intersect,} \markbox{8708}{in} \markbox{8709}{that} \markbox{8710}{order,} \markbox{8711}{the} \markbox{8712}{geodesic} \markbox{m8713}{$[x_U,y_U]$} \markbox{8714}{in} \markbox{m8715}{$T_U$}.  \markbox{8716}{The} \markbox{8717}{proof} \markbox{8718}{is} \markbox{8719}{mainly} \markbox{8720}{a} \markbox{8721}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA} \markbox{8722}{type} \markbox{8723}{argument} \markbox{8724}{along} \markbox{8725}{with} \markbox{8726}{an} \markbox{8727}{application} \markbox{8728}{of} \markbox{8729}{Proposition} \ref{prop:bounding containers} \markbox{8730}{and} \markbox{8731}{the} \markbox{8732}{Covering} \markbox{8733}{Lemma} \ref{lem:covering}.

Continuing \markbox{8734}{with} \markbox{8735}{the} \markbox{8736}{above} \markbox{8737}{notation,} \markbox{8738}{for} \markbox{8739}{each} \markbox{m8740}{$i$}, \markbox{8741}{let} \markbox{m8742}{$C'_i = C_i \cap [x_U,y_U]_{T_U} - \left(B_{\alpha_0 + R}(x_U) \cup B_{\alpha_0 + R}(y_U)\right)$}, \markbox{8743}{where} \markbox{m8744}{$\alpha_0 = \alpha(R, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8745}{is} \markbox{8746}{the} \markbox{8747}{interval} \markbox{8748}{consistency} \markbox{8749}{constant} \markbox{8750}{provided} \markbox{8751}{by} \markbox{8752}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval consistency}; \markbox{8753}{see} \markbox{8754}{Figure} \ref{fig:subcluster}.

Observe \markbox{8755}{that} \markbox{8756}{for} \markbox{8757}{each} \markbox{m8758}{$i$}, \markbox{8759}{if} \markbox{8760}{we} \markbox{8761}{set} \markbox{m8762}{$\calV_i = \{V \in \calU|V \nest U \text{ and } \delta^V_U \subset C_i\}$} \markbox{8763}{then} \markbox{m8764}{$\{\delta^V_U| V \in \calV_i\}$} \markbox{8765}{is} \markbox{m8766}{$(r_2 + 2r_1)$}-dense \markbox{8767}{in} \markbox{m8768}{$C_i$}.  \markbox{8769}{Hence} \markbox{8770}{we} \markbox{8771}{can} \markbox{8772}{find} \markbox{8773}{a} \markbox{8774}{subcollection} \markbox{m8775}{$\calV_i'$} \markbox{8776}{so} that
\begin{itemize}
    \item Each \markbox{m8777}{$V \in \calV_i'$} \markbox{8778}{is} \markbox{m8779}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal;
    \item For \markbox{8780}{each} \markbox{m8781}{$V \in \calV'$}, \markbox{8782}{we} \markbox{8783}{have} \markbox{m8784}{$\delta^V_U \subset C_i'$};
    \item \markbox{m8785}{$\{\delta^V_U| V \in \calV_i\}$} \markbox{8786}{is} \markbox{8787}{a} \markbox{m8788}{$(2r_2+4r_1, r_2)$}-net \markbox{8789}{on} \markbox{m8790}{$C_i'$} \markbox{8791}{(see} \markbox{8792}{Definition} \ref{defn:net} below).
\end{itemize}

Note \markbox{8793}{that} \markbox{8794}{the} \markbox{8795}{increase} \markbox{8796}{in} \markbox{8797}{the} \markbox{8798}{net} \markbox{8799}{constants} \markbox{8800}{in} \markbox{8801}{the} \markbox{8802}{third} \markbox{8803}{item} \markbox{8804}{is} \markbox{8805}{required} \markbox{8806}{to} \markbox{8807}{guarantee} \markbox{8808}{the} \markbox{8809}{second} \markbox{8810}{item.}  \markbox{8811}{In} \markbox{8812}{particular,} \markbox{8813}{we} \markbox{8814}{have} \markbox{m8815}{$\#\calV_i \succ \diam_{T_U}(C_i') \geq \diam_{T_U}(C_i \cap [x_U,y_U])- 2(\alpha_0+R)$}, \markbox{8816}{where} \markbox{m8817}{$\#\calV_i$} \markbox{8818}{denotes} \markbox{8819}{the} \markbox{8820}{cardinality} \markbox{8821}{of} \markbox{m8822}{$\calV_i$}.

Let \markbox{m8823}{$V \in \calV_i'$}.  \markbox{8824}{Then,} \markbox{8825}{by} \markbox{8826}{construction,} \markbox{m8827}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, x_U)> \alpha + R$} \markbox{8828}{and} \markbox{m8829}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, y_U)>\alpha_0 + R$}.  \markbox{8830}{Hence,} \markbox{8831}{up} \markbox{8832}{to} \markbox{8833}{switching} \markbox{8834}{the} \markbox{8835}{roles} \markbox{8836}{of} \markbox{m8837}{$a$} \markbox{8838}{and} \markbox{m8839}{$b$}, \markbox{8840}{the} \markbox{8841}{BGI} \markbox{8842}{property} \markbox{8843}{(5)} \markbox{8844}{of} \markbox{8845}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{8846}{says} \markbox{8847}{that} \markbox{m8848}{$d_{T_V}(\delta^U_V(a_V),\delta^U_V(x_V))<R$} \markbox{8849}{and} \markbox{m8850}{$d_{T_V}(\delta^U_V(b_V),\delta^U_V(y_V))<R$}. 

Lemma \ref{lem:interval consistency} \markbox{8851}{says} \markbox{8852}{that} \markbox{8853}{the} \markbox{8854}{tuples} \markbox{m8855}{$(a_U), (b_U), (x_U), (y_U)$} \markbox{8856}{are} \markbox{8857}{all} \markbox{m8858}{$\alpha_0$}-consistent.  \markbox{8859}{Thus} \markbox{8860}{since} \markbox{m8861}{$d_{T_U}(a_U, \delta^V_U)>R + \alpha_0$} \markbox{8862}{and} \markbox{8863}{similarly} \markbox{8864}{for} \markbox{m8865}{$b_U,x_U,y_U$}, \markbox{m8866}{$\alpha_0$}-consistency \markbox{8867}{forces} \markbox{8868}{that} \markbox{m8869}{$d_{T_V}(a_V, \delta^U_V(a_U)) < \alpha_0$}, \markbox{8870}{and} \markbox{8871}{similarly} \markbox{8872}{for} \markbox{m8873}{$b_V,x_V,y_V$}.  \markbox{8874}{As} \markbox{8875}{such,} \markbox{8876}{we} \markbox{8877}{get} \markbox{8878}{that} \markbox{m8879}{$d_{T_V}(x_V,a_V) < \alpha_0 + R$} \markbox{8880}{and} \markbox{m8881}{$d_{T_V}(y_V,b_V) < \alpha_0 + R$}, \markbox{8882}{and} \markbox{8883}{so} \markbox{8884}{that} \markbox{m8885}{$d_{T_V}(x_V,y_V) \geq d_{T_V}(a_V,b_V) - 2\alpha_0 - 2R$}, \markbox{8886}{from} \markbox{8887}{which} \markbox{8888}{we} \markbox{8889}{can} \markbox{8890}{conclude} \markbox{8891}{that} \markbox{m8892}{$\ha_V = \hx_V$} \markbox{8893}{and} \markbox{m8894}{$\hb_V = \hy_V$} \markbox{8895}{by} \markbox{8896}{requiring} \markbox{m8897}{$r_1 > \alpha_0 + R$}.




On \markbox{8898}{the} \markbox{8899}{other} \markbox{8900}{hand,} \markbox{8901}{since} \markbox{8902}{each} \markbox{m8903}{$V \in \calV_i'$} \markbox{8904}{is} \markbox{m8905}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{8906}{and} \markbox{m8907}{$d_V(a,b) > K$}, \markbox{8908}{item} \markbox{8909}{(4)} \markbox{8910}{of} \markbox{8911}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{8912}{says} \markbox{8913}{that} \markbox{m8914}{$d_{\hT_V}(\hat{a}_V,\hat{b}_V) \succ K$}.  \markbox{8915}{Hence} \markbox{8916}{we} \markbox{8917}{obtain} \markbox{8918}{that} \markbox{m8919}{$d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V)  = d_{\hT_V}(\ha_V,\hb_V) \succ K$}.

Thus \markbox{8920}{for} \markbox{8921}{each} \markbox{m8922}{$U \in \calW$}, \markbox{8923}{we} have
\begin{eqnarray*}
d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U) & = & d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) + \sum_{i=1}^n \diam_{T_U}(C_i \cap [x_U,y_U]_{T_U})\\
&\prec& d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) + \sum_{i=1}^n \#\calV_i'\\
&\prec& d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) + \sum_{i=1}^n \left(\sum_{V \in \calV_i'} d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V)\right).
\end{eqnarray*}

Finally, \markbox{8924}{the} \markbox{8925}{Covering} \markbox{8926}{Lemma} \ref{lem:covering} \markbox{8927}{says} \markbox{8928}{that} \markbox{8929}{any} \markbox{8930}{domain} \markbox{m8931}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{8932}{can} \markbox{8933}{nest} \markbox{8934}{into} \markbox{8935}{only} \markbox{8936}{boundedly-many} \markbox{8937}{domains} \markbox{8938}{in} \markbox{m8939}{$\calU$}, \markbox{8940}{with} \markbox{8941}{bounds} \markbox{8942}{determined} \markbox{8943}{by} \markbox{m8944}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{8945}{Hence,} \markbox{8946}{each} \markbox{m8947}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{8948}{domain} \markbox{m8949}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{8950}{must} \markbox{8951}{account} \markbox{8952}{for} \markbox{8953}{at} \markbox{8954}{most} \markbox{8955}{boundedly-many} \markbox{m8956}{$U \in \calW$} \markbox{8957}{in} \markbox{8958}{the} \markbox{8959}{above} \markbox{8960}{way.}  \markbox{8961}{Thus,} \markbox{8962}{using} \markbox{8963}{an} \markbox{8964}{argument} \markbox{8965}{similar} \markbox{8966}{to} \markbox{8967}{the} \markbox{8968}{end} \markbox{8969}{of} \markbox{8970}{the} \markbox{8971}{proof} \markbox{8972}{of} \markbox{8973}{Proposition} \ref{prop:upper bound}, \markbox{8974}{we} \markbox{8975}{can} \markbox{8976}{account} \markbox{8977}{for} \markbox{8978}{the} \markbox{8979}{distance} \markbox{8980}{lost} \markbox{8981}{by} \markbox{8982}{collapsing} \markbox{8983}{clusters} \markbox{8984}{in} \markbox{8985}{each} \markbox{8986}{domain} \markbox{8987}{in} \markbox{m8988}{$\calW$} \markbox{8989}{with} \markbox{8990}{these} \markbox{8991}{large} \markbox{m8992}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{8993}{domains} \markbox{8994}{by} \markbox{8995}{increasing} \markbox{8996}{the} \markbox{8997}{multiplicative} \markbox{8998}{constant} \markbox{8999}{for} \markbox{9000}{the} \markbox{9001}{estimate} \markbox{9002}{in} \markbox{9003}{equation} \eqref{eqn:upper} \markbox{9004}{by} \markbox{9005}{a} \markbox{9006}{bounded} \markbox{9007}{amount.}  \markbox{9008}{This} \markbox{9009}{completes} \markbox{9010}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

We \markbox{9011}{used} \markbox{9012}{the} \markbox{9013}{following} \markbox{9014}{definition} \markbox{9015}{in} \markbox{9016}{the} \markbox{9017}{above} proof:

\begin{definition}[Net]\label{defn:net}
Given \markbox{9018}{constants} \markbox{m9019}{$a,A\geq 0$}, \markbox{9020}{a} \markbox{m9021}{$(a,A)$}-\emph{net} \markbox{9022}{on} \markbox{9023}{a} \markbox{9024}{subspace} \markbox{m9025}{$Y \subset X$} \markbox{9026}{of} \markbox{9027}{a} \markbox{9028}{metric} \markbox{9029}{space} \markbox{9030}{is} \markbox{9031}{a} \markbox{9032}{collection} \markbox{m9033}{$Z \subset Y$} \markbox{9034}{of} \markbox{9035}{points} \markbox{9036}{so} that:
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m9037}{$Z$} \markbox{9038}{is} \markbox{m9039}{$a$}-coarsely \markbox{9040}{dense} \markbox{9041}{in} \markbox{m9042}{$Y$}, \markbox{9043}{i.e.} \markbox{9044}{for} \markbox{9045}{every} \markbox{m9046}{$y \in Y$} \markbox{9047}{there} \markbox{9048}{is} \markbox{9049}{some} \markbox{m9050}{$z \in Z$} \markbox{9051}{with} \markbox{m9052}{$d(z,y)<a$}, and
\item For \markbox{9053}{any} \markbox{m9054}{$z,z' \in Z$}, \markbox{9055}{we} \markbox{9056}{have} \markbox{m9057}{$d_X(z,z') \geq A$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

In \markbox{9058}{particular,} \markbox{9059}{an} \markbox{m9060}{$(a,A)$}-net \markbox{m9061}{$Z$} \markbox{9062}{on} \markbox{m9063}{$Y$} \markbox{9064}{satisfies} \markbox{m9065}{$\#Z \asymp \diam(Y)$} \markbox{9066}{with} \markbox{9067}{the} \markbox{9068}{constants} \markbox{9069}{depending} \markbox{9070}{only} \markbox{9071}{on} \markbox{m9072}{$a,A$}.








\subsection{The map $\hO:\calQ \to H$ and honing clusters}\label{subsec:hO defined}

With \markbox{9073}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q distance estimate} \markbox{9074}{in} \markbox{9075}{hand,} \markbox{9076}{in} \markbox{9077}{order} \markbox{9078}{to} \markbox{9079}{prove} \markbox{9080}{that} \markbox{m9081}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{9082}{is} \markbox{9083}{a} \markbox{9084}{quasi-isometry,} \markbox{9085}{we} \markbox{9086}{need} \markbox{9087}{to} \markbox{9088}{explain} \markbox{9089}{why} \markbox{m9090}{$\hPsi$} \markbox{9091}{is} \markbox{9092}{coarsely} \markbox{9093}{surjective.}  \markbox{9094}{The} \markbox{9095}{proof} \markbox{9096}{of} \markbox{9097}{this} \markbox{9098}{fact} \markbox{9099}{is} \markbox{9100}{quite} \markbox{9101}{involved} \markbox{9102}{and} \markbox{9103}{beyond} \markbox{9104}{the} \markbox{9105}{scope} \markbox{9106}{of} \markbox{9107}{an} \markbox{9108}{expository} \markbox{9109}{paper.}  \markbox{9110}{As} \markbox{9111}{such,} \markbox{9112}{we} \markbox{9113}{will} \markbox{9114}{mostly} \markbox{9115}{present} \markbox{9116}{key} \markbox{9117}{ideas} \markbox{9118}{and} \markbox{9119}{not} \markbox{9120}{a} \markbox{9121}{full} \markbox{9122}{detailed} \markbox{9123}{proof} \markbox{9124}{because} \markbox{9125}{the} \markbox{9126}{proof} \markbox{9127}{is} \markbox{9128}{not} \markbox{9129}{greatly} \markbox{9130}{simplified} \markbox{9131}{versus} \markbox{9132}{the} \markbox{9133}{most} \markbox{9134}{general} \markbox{9135}{version,} \markbox{9136}{see} \cite[Sections 9--11]{Dur_infcube}.

In \markbox{9137}{this} \markbox{9138}{subsection,} \markbox{9139}{we} \markbox{9140}{will} \markbox{9141}{construct} \markbox{9142}{a} \markbox{9143}{map} \markbox{m9144}{$\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}, \markbox{9145}{and} \markbox{9146}{sketch} \markbox{9147}{why} \markbox{9148}{its} \markbox{9149}{image} \markbox{9150}{is} \markbox{m9151}{$\beta$}-consistent \markbox{9152}{for} \markbox{9153}{some} \markbox{m9154}{$\beta = \beta(\mathfrak S, R, r_1,r_2)>0$}.   \markbox{9155}{Upgrading} \markbox{9156}{this} \markbox{9157}{to} \markbox{9158}{a} \markbox{9159}{map} \markbox{m9160}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{9161}{involves} \markbox{9162}{standard} \markbox{9163}{HHS} \markbox{9164}{techniques.}  \markbox{9165}{In} \markbox{9166}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tree trimming}, \markbox{9167}{we} \markbox{9168}{will} \markbox{9169}{prove} \markbox{9170}{our} \markbox{9171}{Tree} \markbox{9172}{Trimming} \markbox{9173}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}, \markbox{9174}{which} \markbox{9175}{is} \markbox{9176}{a} \markbox{9177}{useful} \markbox{9178}{distance} \markbox{9179}{formula-like} \markbox{9180}{tool} \markbox{9181}{that} \markbox{9182}{will} \markbox{9183}{allow} \markbox{9184}{us} \markbox{9185}{modify} \markbox{9186}{our} \markbox{9187}{collapsed} \markbox{9188}{interval} \markbox{9189}{setup} \markbox{9190}{while} \markbox{9191}{coarsely} \markbox{9192}{preserving} \markbox{9193}{the} \markbox{9194}{geometry} \markbox{9195}{of} \markbox{m9196}{$\calQ$}.  \markbox{9197}{This} \markbox{9198}{tool} \markbox{9199}{is} \markbox{9200}{a} \markbox{9201}{key} \markbox{9202}{ingredient} \markbox{9203}{in} \markbox{9204}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:upgrade to HHS}, \markbox{9205}{where} \markbox{9206}{we} \markbox{9207}{sketch} \markbox{9208}{why} \markbox{m9209}{$\hO$} \markbox{9210}{is} \markbox{9211}{a} \markbox{9212}{coarse} \markbox{9213}{inverse} \markbox{9214}{to} \markbox{m9215}{$\hPsi$}, \markbox{9216}{namely} \markbox{9217}{that} \markbox{m9218}{$d_{\calQ}(\hPsi \circ \hO(\hx), \hx)$} \markbox{9219}{is} \markbox{9220}{bounded} \markbox{9221}{independently} \markbox{9222}{of} \markbox{m9223}{$\hx \in \calQ$}.
