We \markbox{9224}{can} \markbox{9225}{now} \markbox{9226}{set} \markbox{9227}{about} \markbox{9228}{defining} \markbox{9229}{the} \markbox{9230}{map} \markbox{m9231}{$\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}, \markbox{9232}{which} \markbox{9233}{is} \markbox{9234}{defined} \markbox{9235}{coordinate-wise.}  \markbox{9236}{To} \markbox{9237}{put} \markbox{9238}{things} \markbox{9239}{more} \markbox{9240}{precisely,} \markbox{9241}{we} \markbox{9242}{want} \markbox{9243}{to} \markbox{9244}{define} \markbox{m9245}{$\Omega$} \markbox{9246}{so} that:

\begin{itemize}
    \item For \markbox{9247}{each} \markbox{m9248}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{9249}{the} \markbox{9250}{tuple} \markbox{m9251}{$\Omega(\hx)$} \markbox{9252}{is} \markbox{m9253}{$\omega$}-consistent \markbox{9254}{for} \markbox{9255}{some} \markbox{m9256}{$\omega = \omega(\mathfrak S)>0$}, and
    \item when \markbox{m9257}{$\hx  = (\hx_U)\in \calQ$} \markbox{9258}{and} \markbox{m9259}{$(x_U) = \Omega(\hx)$}, \markbox{9260}{then} \markbox{m9261}{$q_U(x_U) = \hx_U$} \markbox{9262}{for} \markbox{9263}{each} \markbox{m9264}{$U \in \calU$}.
\end{itemize}


Unsurprisingly, \markbox{9265}{the} \markbox{9266}{cluster} \markbox{9267}{subintervals,} \markbox{9268}{which} \markbox{9269}{are} \markbox{9270}{collapsed} \markbox{9271}{under} \markbox{9272}{each} \markbox{m9273}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$}, \markbox{9274}{play} \markbox{9275}{a} \markbox{9276}{key} \markbox{9277}{role.}  \markbox{9278}{In} \markbox{9279}{particular,} \markbox{9280}{these} \markbox{9281}{cluster} \markbox{9282}{subintervals} \markbox{9283}{can} \markbox{9284}{have} \markbox{9285}{arbitrarily} \markbox{9286}{large} \markbox{9287}{diameter,} \markbox{9288}{and} \markbox{9289}{so} \markbox{9290}{if} \markbox{9291}{a} \markbox{9292}{coordinate} \markbox{m9293}{$\hx_U\in \hT_U$} \markbox{9294}{lies} \markbox{9295}{in} \markbox{9296}{a} \markbox{9297}{cluster} \markbox{9298}{point} \markbox{9299}{of} \markbox{m9300}{$\hT_U$}, \markbox{9301}{then} \markbox{9302}{its} \markbox{9303}{preimage} \markbox{m9304}{$q_U^{-1}(\hx_U)$} \markbox{9305}{is} \markbox{9306}{that} \markbox{9307}{whole} \markbox{9308}{cluster.}  \markbox{9309}{Choosing} \markbox{9310}{a} \markbox{9311}{point} \markbox{9312}{within} \markbox{9313}{that} \markbox{9314}{cluster} \markbox{9315}{then} \markbox{9316}{requires} \markbox{9317}{utilizing} \markbox{9318}{the} \markbox{9319}{coordinates} \markbox{9320}{for} \markbox{m9321}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{9322}{with} \markbox{m9323}{$\hd^V_U = \hx_U$}.  \markbox{9324}{We} \markbox{9325}{think} \markbox{9326}{of} \markbox{9327}{this} \markbox{9328}{process} \markbox{9329}{as} \emph{honing} \markbox{9330}{the} cluster.


\smallskip


\textbf{\underline{Honing clusters}}: \markbox{9331}{Let} \markbox{m9332}{$\hx = (\hx_U) \in \calQ$}.  \markbox{9333}{When} \markbox{m9334}{$U\in \calU$} \markbox{9335}{has} \markbox{m9336}{$\hx_U \in \hT^e_U$}, \markbox{9337}{then} \markbox{9338}{the} \markbox{9339}{definition} \markbox{9340}{is} \markbox{9341}{simple:} \markbox{m9342}{$x_U = q_U^{-1}(\hx_U)$}, \markbox{9343}{which} \markbox{9344}{is} \markbox{9345}{a} \markbox{9346}{unique} \markbox{9347}{point.}  \markbox{9348}{For} \markbox{9349}{the} \markbox{9350}{other} \markbox{9351}{domains,} \markbox{9352}{we} \markbox{9353}{need} \markbox{9354}{some} \markbox{9355}{more} setup.

\begin{remark}
    \markbox{9356}{The} \markbox{9357}{reader} \markbox{9358}{should} \markbox{9359}{be} \markbox{9360}{warned} \markbox{9361}{here} \markbox{9362}{that} \markbox{9363}{one} \markbox{9364}{has} \markbox{9365}{to} \markbox{9366}{deal} \markbox{9367}{with} \markbox{9368}{the} \markbox{9369}{case} \markbox{9370}{where} \markbox{9371}{all} \markbox{9372}{coordinates} \markbox{m9373}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{9374}{are} \markbox{9375}{contained} \markbox{9376}{in} \markbox{9377}{a} \markbox{9378}{collapsed} \markbox{9379}{point.}  \markbox{9380}{When} \markbox{9381}{this} \markbox{9382}{happens,} \markbox{9383}{there} \markbox{9384}{is} \markbox{9385}{not} \markbox{9386}{an} \markbox{9387}{obvious} \markbox{9388}{choice} \markbox{9389}{of} \markbox{9390}{collection} \markbox{9391}{of} \markbox{9392}{minimal} \markbox{9393}{domains} \markbox{9394}{to} \markbox{9395}{work} \markbox{9396}{with,} \markbox{9397}{and} \markbox{9398}{in} \markbox{9399}{order} \markbox{9400}{to} \markbox{9401}{determine} \markbox{9402}{coordinates} \markbox{9403}{back} \markbox{9404}{in} \markbox{9405}{the} \markbox{9406}{intervals} \markbox{m9407}{$T_U$}, \markbox{9408}{one} \markbox{9409}{must} \markbox{9410}{use} \markbox{9411}{all} \markbox{9412}{of} \markbox{9413}{the} \markbox{9414}{hierarchical} \markbox{9415}{data} \markbox{9416}{at} \markbox{9417}{hand.} 
\end{remark}

Suppose \markbox{9418}{that} \markbox{m9419}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9420}{and} \markbox{m9421}{$\hx_U \notin \hT^e_U$}.  \markbox{9422}{Let} \markbox{m9423}{$C$} \markbox{9424}{denote} \markbox{9425}{the} \markbox{9426}{cluster} \markbox{9427}{in} \markbox{m9428}{$T_U$} \markbox{9429}{so} \markbox{9430}{that} \markbox{m9431}{$q_U(C) = \hx_U$}.  \markbox{9432}{The} \markbox{9433}{first} \markbox{9434}{step} \markbox{9435}{is} \markbox{9436}{to} \markbox{9437}{associate} \markbox{9438}{a} \markbox{9439}{marked} \markbox{9440}{point} \markbox{m9441}{$l_V \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{9442}{to} \markbox{9443}{each} \markbox{m9444}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{9445}{domain} \markbox{m9446}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{9447}{with} \markbox{m9448}{$\delta^V_U \subset C$}.  \markbox{9449}{We} \markbox{9450}{then} \markbox{9451}{use} \markbox{9452}{these} \markbox{m9453}{$l_V$} \markbox{9454}{to} \markbox{9455}{hone} \markbox{9456}{the} \markbox{9457}{clusters} \markbox{9458}{of} \markbox{9459}{the} \markbox{9460}{larger} \markbox{m9461}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9462}{in} \markbox{9463}{which} \markbox{9464}{such} \markbox{m9465}{$V$} \markbox{9466}{are} involved.

Suppose \markbox{9467}{then} \markbox{9468}{that} \markbox{m9469}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9470}{is} \markbox{m9471}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.  \markbox{9472}{Since} \markbox{m9473}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{9474}{has} \markbox{9475}{no} \markbox{9476}{internal} \markbox{9477}{cluster} \markbox{9478}{points,} \markbox{m9479}{$\hat{x}_U$} \markbox{9480}{is} \markbox{9481}{either} \markbox{9482}{a} \markbox{9483}{marked} \markbox{9484}{point---either} \markbox{m9485}{$\ha_U$} \markbox{9486}{or} \markbox{m9487}{$\hb_U$}---or \markbox{9488}{a} \markbox{9489}{point} \markbox{9490}{in} \markbox{m9491}{$\hT^e_U$}.  \markbox{9492}{If} \markbox{9493}{the} \markbox{9494}{former,} \markbox{9495}{let} \markbox{m9496}{$l_U$} \markbox{9497}{be} \markbox{9498}{the} \markbox{9499}{corresponding} \markbox{9500}{marked} \markbox{9501}{point---i.e.} \markbox{9502}{either} \markbox{m9503}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{9504}{If} \markbox{9505}{the} \markbox{9506}{latter,} \markbox{9507}{set} \markbox{m9508}{$l_U = \emptyset$}.  \markbox{9509}{We} \markbox{9510}{note} \markbox{9511}{that} \markbox{m9512}{$\ha_U \neq \hb_U$} \markbox{9513}{by} \markbox{9514}{construction} \markbox{9515}{when} \markbox{m9516}{$U$} \markbox{9517}{is} \markbox{m9518}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.

Now \markbox{9519}{suppose} \markbox{9520}{that} \markbox{m9521}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9522}{is} \markbox{9523}{not} \markbox{m9524}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.  \markbox{9525}{We} \markbox{9526}{have} \markbox{9527}{that} \markbox{9528}{either} \markbox{m9529}{$\hat{x}_U \in \hT^e_U$}, \markbox{9530}{in} \markbox{9531}{which} \markbox{9532}{case} \markbox{9533}{we} \markbox{9534}{set} \markbox{m9535}{$l_U = \emptyset$} \markbox{9536}{and} \markbox{m9537}{$x_U = q_U^{-1}(\hat{x}_U)$}.  \markbox{9538}{Otherwise,} \markbox{m9539}{$\hat{x}_U$} \markbox{9540}{is} \markbox{9541}{contained} \markbox{9542}{in} \markbox{9543}{a} \markbox{9544}{collapsed} \markbox{9545}{cluster} \markbox{m9546}{$q_U(C)$} \markbox{9547}{for} \markbox{9548}{the} \markbox{9549}{cluster} \markbox{m9550}{$C \subset T_U$}.  \markbox{9551}{Let} \markbox{m9552}{$\calB_{\min}(C)$} \markbox{9553}{denote} \markbox{9554}{the} \markbox{9555}{set} \markbox{9556}{of} \markbox{m9557}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{9558}{domains} \markbox{m9559}{$V\nest U$} \markbox{9560}{so} \markbox{9561}{that} \markbox{m9562}{$\delta^V_U \subset C$}.  \markbox{9563}{Observe} \markbox{9564}{that} \markbox{9565}{if} \markbox{m9566}{$\BM(C) = \emptyset$}, \markbox{9567}{then} \markbox{m9568}{$\diam_{T_U}(C)$} \markbox{9569}{is} \markbox{9570}{bounded} \markbox{9571}{in} \markbox{9572}{terms} \markbox{9573}{of} \markbox{m9574}{$r_1,r_2$} \markbox{9575}{and} \markbox{9576}{hence} \markbox{9577}{in} \markbox{9578}{terms} \markbox{9579}{of} \markbox{m9580}{$\mathfrak S$}.

We \markbox{9581}{now} \markbox{9582}{explain} \markbox{9583}{the} \markbox{9584}{honing} \markbox{9585}{process} \markbox{9586}{for} \markbox{9587}{domains} \markbox{9588}{in} \markbox{m9589}{$\BM(C)$}, \markbox{9590}{which} \markbox{9591}{will} \markbox{9592}{associate} \markbox{9593}{to} \markbox{m9594}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{9595}{a} \markbox{9596}{bounded} \markbox{9597}{diameter} \markbox{9598}{subset} \markbox{9599}{of} \markbox{9600}{the} \markbox{9601}{cluster} \markbox{m9602}{$C$} \markbox{9603}{in} \markbox{m9604}{$T_U$} \markbox{9605}{(Lemma} \ref{lem:bdd int total}).

Let \markbox{m9606}{$V \in \BM(C)$}.  \markbox{9607}{Then} \markbox{9608}{we} \markbox{9609}{set} 
$$C^V_U = \hull_C(C \cap (\calN_{r_2}(\delta^V_U) \cup l_V)),$$
which \markbox{9610}{is} \markbox{9611}{a} \markbox{9612}{subinterval} \markbox{9613}{of} \markbox{m9614}{$C$}, \markbox{9615}{see} \markbox{9616}{Figure} \ref{fig:C^V_U}.  \markbox{9617}{Finally,} \markbox{9618}{let} \markbox{m9619}{$B_U(\hx) = \bigcap_{V \in \BM(C)} C^V_U$} \markbox{9620}{be} \markbox{9621}{the} \markbox{9622}{total} \markbox{9623}{intersection} \markbox{9624}{of} \markbox{9625}{the} \markbox{m9626}{$C^V_U$}.

\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.8\textwidth]{figures/C_V_U_interval.pdf}
    \caption{The cluster $C$ (green) in $T_U$ is identified with $\hx_U$ in $\hT_U$.  Since $V \in \BM(C)$, its shadow $\delta^V_U$ (orange) avoids all branches of $T_U$.  The marked points and leaves $l_V$ (pink) chosen by $\hx_V$ determine the half-subtree $C^V_U$ (blue) of $C$ chosen by $V$.} 
    \label{fig:C^V_U}
\end{figure}



In \markbox{9627}{Lemma} \ref{lem:bdd int pair} \markbox{9628}{below,} \markbox{9629}{we} \markbox{9630}{prove} \markbox{9631}{that} \markbox{9632}{if} \markbox{m9633}{$V, W \in \BM(C)$}, \markbox{9634}{then} \markbox{m9635}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \neq \emptyset$}.  \markbox{9636}{Since} \markbox{9637}{each} \markbox{m9638}{$C^V_U$} \markbox{9639}{is} \markbox{9640}{a} \markbox{9641}{subinterval,} \markbox{9642}{it} \markbox{9643}{follows} \markbox{9644}{from} \markbox{9645}{the} \markbox{9646}{Helly} \markbox{9647}{property} \markbox{9648}{for} \markbox{9649}{trees} \markbox{9650}{that} \markbox{m9651}{$B_U(x)$} \markbox{9652}{is} \markbox{9653}{nonempty.}  \markbox{9654}{Finally,} \markbox{9655}{in} \markbox{9656}{Lemma} \ref{lem:bdd int total} \markbox{9657}{we} \markbox{9658}{prove} \markbox{9659}{that} \markbox{9660}{this} \markbox{9661}{intersection} \markbox{9662}{has} \markbox{9663}{diameter} \markbox{9664}{bounded} \markbox{9665}{in} \markbox{9666}{terms} \markbox{9667}{of} \markbox{m9668}{$\mathfrak S$}.

Thus \markbox{9669}{we} \markbox{9670}{can} \markbox{9671}{define} \markbox{9672}{a} \markbox{9673}{tuple} \markbox{m9674}{$\Omega(\hx) = (x_U)_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{9675}{as} follows:
\begin{itemize}
    \item For \markbox{m9676}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9677}{with} \markbox{m9678}{$U \in E(\hx)$}, \markbox{9679}{we} \markbox{9680}{set} \markbox{m9681}{$x_U = q_U^{-1}(\hx_U)$}.
    \item For \markbox{m9682}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9683}{with} \markbox{m9684}{$U \notin E(\hx)$} \markbox{9685}{and} \markbox{m9686}{$U \nest_{\calU}$}-minimal, \markbox{9687}{we} \markbox{9688}{let} \markbox{m9689}{$x_U$} \markbox{9690}{be} \markbox{9691}{any} \markbox{9692}{point} \markbox{9693}{in} \markbox{m9694}{$q_U^{-1}(\hx_U)$}.
    \item Otherwise, \markbox{9695}{we} \markbox{9696}{let} \markbox{m9697}{$x_U \in B_U(\hx)$}.
\end{itemize}

The \markbox{9698}{following} \markbox{9699}{is} \markbox{9700}{immediate} \markbox{9701}{from} \markbox{9702}{the} construction:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:B_U in cluster}
For \markbox{9703}{every} \markbox{m9704}{$\hx \in \calQ$} \markbox{9705}{and} \markbox{m9706}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{9707}{we} \markbox{9708}{have} \markbox{m9709}{$q_U(x_U) = \hx_U$}.
\end{lemma}


In \markbox{9710}{Proposition} \ref{prop:Q-consistent} \markbox{9711}{below,} \markbox{9712}{we} \markbox{9713}{prove} \markbox{9714}{that} \markbox{m9715}{$(x_U)$} \markbox{9716}{is} \markbox{9717}{a} \markbox{m9718}{$\omega$}-consistent \markbox{9719}{tuple} \markbox{9720}{for} \markbox{m9721}{$\omega = \omega(\mathfrak S)>0$}.

\begin{remark}[Cubical flavor]
The \markbox{9722}{process} \markbox{9723}{of} \markbox{9724}{cluster} \markbox{9725}{honing} \markbox{9726}{is} \markbox{9727}{one} \markbox{9728}{of} \markbox{9729}{the} \markbox{9730}{few} \markbox{9731}{places} \markbox{9732}{where} \markbox{9733}{one} \markbox{9734}{sees} \markbox{9735}{cubical-like} \markbox{9736}{features} \markbox{9737}{appearing} \markbox{9738}{in} \markbox{9739}{a} \markbox{9740}{non-explicitly} \markbox{9741}{cubical} \markbox{9742}{part} \markbox{9743}{of} \markbox{9744}{the} \markbox{9745}{construction.}  \markbox{9746}{In} \markbox{9747}{particular,} \markbox{9748}{it} \markbox{9749}{is} \markbox{9750}{crucial} \markbox{9751}{that} \markbox{9752}{the} \markbox{9753}{two} \markbox{9754}{endpoints} \markbox{m9755}{$\ha_V, \hb_V$} \markbox{9756}{for} \markbox{9757}{every} \markbox{m9758}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m9759}{$V$} \markbox{9760}{are} \markbox{9761}{distinct} \markbox{9762}{in} \markbox{m9763}{$\hT_V$}.  \markbox{9764}{Hence} \markbox{m9765}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{9766}{domains} \markbox{9767}{determine} \markbox{9768}{a} \markbox{9769}{choice} \markbox{9770}{of} \markbox{9771}{endpoint} \markbox{9772}{between} \markbox{m9773}{$a,b$}, \markbox{9774}{like} \markbox{9775}{a} \markbox{9776}{wall} \markbox{9777}{choosing} \markbox{9778}{a} half-space.

When \markbox{m9779}{$U$} \markbox{9780}{is} \markbox{9781}{not} \markbox{m9782}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{9783}{and} \markbox{m9784}{$\hd^V_U = \hx_U$}, \markbox{9785}{then} \markbox{9786}{the} \markbox{9787}{coordinate} \markbox{m9788}{$\hx_V$} \markbox{9789}{either} \markbox{9790}{chooses} \markbox{9791}{neither} \markbox{9792}{endpoint} \markbox{9793}{of} \markbox{m9794}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{9795}{(if} \markbox{m9796}{$\hx_V \in \hT^e_V$}), \markbox{9797}{or} \markbox{9798}{chooses} \markbox{9799}{one} \markbox{9800}{of} \markbox{m9801}{$\ha_V,\hb_V$}.  \markbox{9802}{This} \markbox{9803}{choice} \markbox{9804}{then} \markbox{9805}{determines} \markbox{9806}{a} \markbox{9807}{sort} \markbox{9808}{of} ``half-interval'' \markbox{m9809}{$C^V_U$} \markbox{9810}{of} \markbox{m9811}{$C$}, \markbox{9812}{where} \markbox{9813}{we} \markbox{9814}{can} \markbox{9815}{think} \markbox{9816}{of} \markbox{m9817}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{9818}{as} \markbox{9819}{functioning} \markbox{9820}{like} \markbox{9821}{a} \markbox{9822}{hyperplane} \markbox{9823}{here.}  \markbox{9824}{In} \markbox{9825}{Lemmas} \ref{lem:bdd int pair} \markbox{9826}{and} \ref{lem:bdd int total} \markbox{9827}{below,} \markbox{9828}{we} \markbox{9829}{see} \markbox{9830}{that} \markbox{9831}{the} \markbox{9832}{intersection} \markbox{9833}{over} \markbox{9834}{all} \markbox{9835}{such} ``half-intervals'' \markbox{m9836}{$B_U = \bigcap_{V \in \BM(C)} C^V_U$} \markbox{9837}{is} \markbox{9838}{nonempty} \markbox{9839}{and} \markbox{9840}{has} \markbox{9841}{bounded} \markbox{9842}{diameter,} \markbox{9843}{and} \markbox{9844}{this} \markbox{9845}{ultra-filter-like} \markbox{9846}{behavior} \markbox{9847}{is} \markbox{9848}{forced} \markbox{9849}{by} \markbox{9850}{consistency} \markbox{9851}{of} \markbox{9852}{the} \markbox{9853}{tuple} \markbox{m9854}{$\hx$}.
\end{remark}

\begin{remark}[A warning]
    \markbox{9855}{The} \markbox{9856}{reader} \markbox{9857}{should} \markbox{9858}{be} \markbox{9859}{warned} \markbox{9860}{that} \markbox{9861}{one} \markbox{9862}{has} \markbox{9863}{to} \markbox{9864}{deal} \markbox{9865}{with} \markbox{9866}{the} \markbox{9867}{case} \markbox{9868}{of} \markbox{m9869}{$\hx \in \calQ$} \markbox{9870}{where} \markbox{m9871}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{9872}{is} \markbox{9873}{a} \markbox{9874}{cluster} \markbox{9875}{or} \markbox{9876}{endpoint} \markbox{9877}{for} \markbox{9878}{every} \markbox{9879}{coordinate} \markbox{m9880}{$U$}.  \markbox{9881}{While,} \markbox{9882}{as} \markbox{9883}{in} \markbox{9884}{the} \markbox{9885}{previous} \markbox{9886}{remark,} \markbox{9887}{such} \markbox{9888}{points} \markbox{9889}{determine} \markbox{9890}{unambiguous} \markbox{9891}{coordinates} \markbox{9892}{in} \markbox{m9893}{$T_U$} \markbox{9894}{for} \markbox{9895}{all} \markbox{m9896}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{9897}{domains} \markbox{m9898}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{9899}{there} \markbox{9900}{is} \markbox{9901}{no} \markbox{9902}{way} \markbox{9903}{to} \markbox{9904}{leverage} \markbox{9905}{this} \markbox{9906}{data} \markbox{9907}{alone} \markbox{9908}{into} \markbox{9909}{choosing} \markbox{9910}{coordinates} \markbox{9911}{in} \markbox{m9912}{$T_V$} \markbox{9913}{for} \markbox{9914}{domains} \markbox{m9915}{$V$} \markbox{9916}{higher} \markbox{9917}{up} \markbox{9918}{the} \markbox{m9919}{$\nest$}-lattice.  \markbox{9920}{One} \markbox{9921}{must} \markbox{9922}{utilize} \markbox{9923}{the} \markbox{9924}{full} \markbox{9925}{set} \markbox{9926}{of} \markbox{9927}{relations} \markbox{9928}{between} \markbox{9929}{all} \markbox{9930}{of} \markbox{9931}{the} domains.
\end{remark}






\subsection{Bounding intersections}

In \markbox{9932}{this} \markbox{9933}{subsection,} \markbox{9934}{we} \markbox{9935}{prove} \markbox{9936}{the} \markbox{9937}{supporting} \markbox{9938}{statements} \markbox{9939}{we} \markbox{9940}{need} \markbox{9941}{to} \markbox{9942}{define} \markbox{9943}{the} \markbox{9944}{map} \markbox{m9945}{$\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}.  \markbox{9946}{Again} \markbox{9947}{fix} \markbox{m9948}{$\hx \in \calQ$}.

The \markbox{9949}{first} \markbox{9950}{says} \markbox{9951}{that} \markbox{9952}{the} \markbox{m9953}{$C^V_U$} \markbox{9954}{for} \markbox{m9955}{$V \in \BM(C)$} \markbox{9956}{have} \markbox{9957}{pairwise} \markbox{9958}{nonempty} intersection:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:bdd int pair}
If \markbox{m9959}{$V, W \in \BM(C)$}, \markbox{9960}{then} \markbox{m9961}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \neq \emptyset$}.  \markbox{9962}{Moreover,} \markbox{9963}{if} \markbox{m9964}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U)>r_2$}, \markbox{9965}{then} \markbox{9966}{at} \markbox{9967}{least} \markbox{9968}{one} \markbox{9969}{of} \markbox{m9970}{$\delta^V_U \subset C^W_U$} \markbox{9971}{or} \markbox{m9972}{$\delta^W_U \subset C^V_U$} holds.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}[Sketch \markbox{9973}{of} proof]

We \markbox{9974}{provide} \markbox{9975}{a} \markbox{9976}{sketch} \markbox{9977}{of} \markbox{9978}{the} \markbox{9979}{proof,} \markbox{9980}{see} \cite[Lemma 9.9]{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{9981}{We} \markbox{9982}{shall} \markbox{9983}{observe} \markbox{9984}{item} \markbox{9985}{(1)} \markbox{9986}{during} \markbox{9987}{the} \markbox{9988}{course} \markbox{9989}{of} \markbox{9990}{the} \markbox{9991}{proof} \markbox{9992}{of} \markbox{9993}{the} sketch.

By \markbox{9994}{definition} \markbox{9995}{of} \markbox{m9996}{$C^V_U = \hull_C((\calN_{r_2}(\delta^V_U) \cup l_V)\cap C)$}, \markbox{9997}{we} \markbox{9998}{may} \markbox{9999}{assume} \markbox{10000}{that} \markbox{m10001}{$\calN_{r_2}(\delta^V_U) \cap \calN_{r_2}(\delta^W_U) = \emptyset$}, \markbox{10002}{and} \markbox{10003}{hence} \markbox{10004}{that} \markbox{m10005}{$V \pitchfork W$} \markbox{10006}{by} \markbox{10007}{item} \markbox{10008}{(3)} \markbox{10009}{of} \markbox{10010}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}.  \markbox{10011}{The} \markbox{10012}{idea} \markbox{10013}{now} \markbox{10014}{is} \markbox{10015}{that} \markbox{m10016}{$\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U$} \markbox{10017}{must} \markbox{10018}{occur} \markbox{10019}{separately} \markbox{10020}{along} \markbox{10021}{the} \markbox{10022}{cluster} \markbox{m10023}{$C$}.  \markbox{10024}{Without} \markbox{10025}{loss} \markbox{10026}{of} \markbox{10027}{generality,} \markbox{10028}{we} \markbox{10029}{can} \markbox{10030}{assume} \markbox{10031}{that} \markbox{m10032}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{10033}{separates} \markbox{m10034}{$a_U$} \markbox{10035}{from} \markbox{m10036}{$\delta^W_U$}.  \markbox{10037}{One} \markbox{10038}{can} \markbox{10039}{then} \markbox{10040}{use} \markbox{10041}{the} \markbox{10042}{consistency} \markbox{10043}{of} \markbox{m10044}{$(\hx_U)$} \markbox{10045}{and} \markbox{10046}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{10047}{and} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{10048}{to} \markbox{10049}{show} \markbox{10050}{that} \markbox{10051}{at} \markbox{10052}{least} \markbox{10053}{one} \markbox{10054}{of} \markbox{m10055}{$l_V = b$} \markbox{10056}{or} \markbox{m10057}{$l_W = a$}, \markbox{10058}{which} \markbox{10059}{would} \markbox{10060}{force} \markbox{m10061}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \neq \emptyset$}, \markbox{10062}{as} \markbox{10063}{required;} \markbox{10064}{see} \markbox{10065}{Figure} \ref{fig:cluster_int}.

\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.8\textwidth]{figures/cluster_int_interval.pdf}
    \caption{The impossible situation in which $V\pitchfork W \in \BM(C)$ choose non-intersecting sides $C^V_U$ (pink) and $C^W_U$ (blue) of $C$ (green).  This forces inconsistency of $\hx_V$ and $\hx_W$.} 
    \label{fig:cluster_int}
\end{figure}
\end{proof}

As \markbox{10066}{discussed} \markbox{10067}{above,} \markbox{10068}{we} \markbox{10069}{can} \markbox{10070}{define} \markbox{m10071}{$B_U = \bigcap_{V \in \BM(C)}C^V_U$} \markbox{10072}{and} \markbox{10073}{it} \markbox{10074}{must} \markbox{10075}{be} \markbox{10076}{non-empty} \markbox{10077}{by} \markbox{10078}{the} \markbox{10079}{Helly} \markbox{10080}{property} \markbox{10081}{for} \markbox{10082}{trees} \markbox{10083}{as} \markbox{10084}{long} \markbox{10085}{as} \markbox{m10086}{$\BM(C) \neq \emptyset$}.

\begin{remark}\label{rem:Helly}
The \markbox{10087}{Helly} \markbox{10088}{property} \markbox{10089}{for} \markbox{10090}{trees} \markbox{10091}{says} \markbox{10092}{that} \markbox{10093}{if} \markbox{10094}{one} \markbox{10095}{has} \markbox{10096}{a} \markbox{10097}{pairwise-intersecting} \markbox{10098}{collection} \markbox{10099}{of} \markbox{10100}{subtrees} \markbox{10101}{then} \markbox{10102}{the} \markbox{10103}{collection} \markbox{10104}{has} \markbox{10105}{nonempty} \markbox{10106}{total} \markbox{10107}{intersection.}  \markbox{10108}{In} \markbox{10109}{the} \markbox{10110}{general} \markbox{10111}{version} \markbox{10112}{of} \markbox{10113}{our} \markbox{10114}{current} \markbox{10115}{construction} \markbox{10116}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{10117}{the} \markbox{10118}{trees} \markbox{10119}{and} \markbox{10120}{subtrees} \markbox{10121}{in} \markbox{10122}{question} \markbox{10123}{need} \markbox{10124}{not} \markbox{10125}{be} \markbox{10126}{finite} \markbox{10127}{diameter.}  \markbox{10128}{This} \markbox{10129}{is} \markbox{10130}{one} \markbox{10131}{place} \markbox{10132}{where} \markbox{10133}{the} \markbox{10134}{arguments} \markbox{10135}{in} \markbox{10136}{our} \markbox{10137}{current} \markbox{10138}{context} \markbox{10139}{are} \markbox{10140}{simpler} \markbox{10141}{than} \markbox{10142}{that} \markbox{10143}{considered} \markbox{10144}{in} \cite{Dur_infcube}.
\end{remark}

The \markbox{10145}{next} \markbox{10146}{lemma} \markbox{10147}{bounds} \markbox{10148}{the} \markbox{10149}{diameter} \markbox{10150}{of} \markbox{m10151}{$B_U$}:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:bdd int total}
There \markbox{10152}{exists} \markbox{m10153}{$B_1 = B_1(\mathfrak S,r_2)>0$} \markbox{10154}{such} \markbox{10155}{that} \markbox{10156}{for} \markbox{10157}{all} \markbox{m10158}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{10159}{we} \markbox{10160}{have} 
\markbox{m10161}{$\diam_{T_U}(B_U) < B_1$}.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}

If \markbox{m10162}{$B_U$} \markbox{10163}{is} \markbox{10164}{too} \markbox{10165}{wide} \markbox{10166}{(relative} \markbox{10167}{to} \markbox{m10168}{$r_2$}), \markbox{10169}{then} \markbox{10170}{we} \markbox{10171}{can} \markbox{10172}{find} \markbox{m10173}{$V, W \in \BM(C)$} \markbox{10174}{with} \markbox{m10175}{$\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U \subset B_U$} \markbox{10176}{and} \markbox{m10177}{$r'< d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U) < 2r'$} \markbox{10178}{for} \markbox{m10179}{$r' = r'(r_2)>0$}, \markbox{10180}{since} \markbox{10181}{the} \markbox{m10182}{$\delta$}-sets \markbox{10183}{for} \markbox{10184}{domains} \markbox{10185}{in} \markbox{m10186}{$\BM(C)$} \markbox{10187}{coarsely} \markbox{10188}{cover} \markbox{m10189}{$C$} \markbox{10190}{with} \markbox{10191}{coarseness} \markbox{10192}{depending} \markbox{10193}{only} \markbox{10194}{on} \markbox{m10195}{$r_2$}.  \markbox{10196}{By} \markbox{10197}{Lemma} \ref{lem:bdd int pair}, \markbox{10198}{we} \markbox{10199}{must} \markbox{10200}{have} \markbox{10201}{at} \markbox{10202}{least} \markbox{10203}{one} \markbox{10204}{of} \markbox{m10205}{$\delta^V_U \subset C^W_U$} \markbox{10206}{or} \markbox{m10207}{$\delta^W_U \subset C^V_U$}, \markbox{10208}{or} \markbox{10209}{possibly} \markbox{10210}{both.}  \markbox{10211}{In} \markbox{10212}{fact,} \markbox{10213}{both} \markbox{10214}{must} \markbox{10215}{hold,} \markbox{10216}{for} \markbox{10217}{if} \markbox{m10218}{$\delta^V_U \notin C^W_U$}, \markbox{10219}{then} \markbox{m10220}{$\delta^V_U \notin B_U$}, \markbox{10221}{which} \markbox{10222}{is} \markbox{10223}{impossible.}  \markbox{10224}{But} \markbox{10225}{then} \markbox{m10226}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \subset \hull_C(\calN_{r_2}(\delta^V_U) \cup \calN_{r_2}(\delta^W_U))$}, \markbox{10227}{which} \markbox{10228}{has} \markbox{10229}{diameter} \markbox{10230}{bounded} \markbox{10231}{by} \markbox{m10232}{$2r' + 2r_2$} \markbox{10233}{since} \markbox{m10234}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U) < 2r'$}.  \markbox{10235}{Since} \markbox{m10236}{$B_U \subset C^V_U \cap C^W_U$}, \markbox{10237}{this} \markbox{10238}{completes} \markbox{10239}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

We \markbox{10240}{are} \markbox{10241}{now} \markbox{10242}{in} \markbox{10243}{place} \markbox{10244}{to} \markbox{10245}{state} \markbox{10246}{the} \markbox{10247}{consistency} result:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:Q-consistent}
There \markbox{10248}{exist} \markbox{m10249}{$\alpha_{\omega}=\alpha_{\omega}(\mathfrak S,r_1,r_2,R)>0$} \markbox{10250}{and} \markbox{10251}{a} \markbox{10252}{map} \markbox{m10253}{$\Omega: \calQ \to \calY$} \markbox{10254}{so} \markbox{10255}{that} \markbox{10256}{for} \markbox{10257}{any} \markbox{m10258}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{10259}{the} \markbox{10260}{tuple} \markbox{m10261}{$\Omega(\hx)$} \markbox{10262}{is} \markbox{m10263}{$\alpha_{\omega}$}-consistent.  \markbox{10264}{Moreover,} \markbox{10265}{if} \markbox{m10266}{$\Omega(\hx) = (x_U)$}, \markbox{10267}{then} \markbox{m10268}{$q_U(x_U) = \hx_U$} \markbox{10269}{for} \markbox{10270}{each} \markbox{m10271}{$U \in \calU$}.
\end{proposition}

The \markbox{10272}{proof} \markbox{10273}{of} \markbox{10274}{this} \markbox{10275}{proposition} \markbox{10276}{is} \markbox{10277}{a} \markbox{10278}{somewhat} \markbox{10279}{elaborate} \markbox{10280}{exercise} \markbox{10281}{in} \markbox{10282}{the} \markbox{10283}{definition} \markbox{10284}{of} \markbox{m10285}{$\Omega$} \markbox{10286}{and} \markbox{10287}{the} \markbox{10288}{construction} \markbox{10289}{of} \markbox{10290}{the} \markbox{10291}{clusters,} \markbox{10292}{in} \markbox{10293}{which} \markbox{10294}{one} \markbox{10295}{utilizes} \markbox{10296}{many} \markbox{10297}{standard} \markbox{10298}{HHS-type} \markbox{10299}{arguments.}  \markbox{10300}{Unlike} \markbox{10301}{other} \markbox{10302}{proofs} \markbox{10303}{in} \markbox{10304}{this} \markbox{10305}{paper,} \markbox{10306}{the} \markbox{10307}{proof} \markbox{10308}{of} \markbox{10309}{this} \markbox{10310}{fact} \markbox{10311}{in} \markbox{10312}{our} \markbox{10313}{current} \markbox{10314}{setting} \markbox{10315}{is} \markbox{10316}{not} \markbox{10317}{substantially} \markbox{10318}{different} \markbox{10319}{from} \markbox{10320}{proof} \markbox{10321}{in} \markbox{10322}{the} \markbox{10323}{general} \markbox{10324}{case} \markbox{10325}{in} \cite[Subsection 9.5]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{10326}{beyond} \markbox{10327}{the} \markbox{10328}{need} \markbox{10329}{for} \markbox{10330}{working} \markbox{10331}{with} \markbox{m10332}{$\nest$}-minimal \emph{bipartite domains} \markbox{10333}{as} \markbox{10334}{defined} \markbox{10335}{in} \cite[Definition 9.2]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{10336}{instead} \markbox{10337}{of} \markbox{10338}{all} \markbox{m10339}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{10340}{domains.}  \markbox{10341}{Thus} \markbox{10342}{instead} \markbox{10343}{of} \markbox{10344}{repeating} \markbox{10345}{it} \markbox{10346}{here,} \markbox{10347}{we} \markbox{10348}{leave} \markbox{10349}{it} \markbox{10350}{to} \markbox{10351}{the} \markbox{10352}{interested} \markbox{10353}{reader} \markbox{10354}{to} \markbox{10355}{check} \markbox{10356}{the} details.

\subsection{Tree trimming}\label{subsec:tree trimming}

In \markbox{10357}{this} \markbox{10358}{subsection,} \markbox{10359}{we} \markbox{10360}{introduce} \markbox{10361}{a} \markbox{10362}{useful} \markbox{10363}{tool} \markbox{10364}{for} \markbox{10365}{modifying} \markbox{10366}{collapsed} \markbox{10367}{interval} \markbox{10368}{systems} \markbox{10369}{and} \markbox{10370}{their} \markbox{10371}{associated} \markbox{m10372}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{10373}{sets.}  \markbox{10374}{These} ``tree-trimming'' \markbox{10375}{techniques} \markbox{10376}{will} \markbox{10377}{allow} \markbox{10378}{us} \markbox{10379}{to} \markbox{10380}{perform} \markbox{10381}{controlled} \markbox{10382}{collapses} \markbox{10383}{of} \markbox{10384}{subintervals} \markbox{10385}{across} \markbox{10386}{the} \markbox{10387}{various} \markbox{10388}{collapsed} \markbox{10389}{intervals} \markbox{m10390}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{10391}{while} \markbox{10392}{coarsely} \markbox{10393}{preserving} \markbox{10394}{the} \markbox{10395}{associated} \markbox{m10396}{$\calQ$}-distance.  \markbox{10397}{We} \markbox{10398}{think} \markbox{10399}{of} \markbox{10400}{them} \markbox{10401}{as} \markbox{10402}{a} \markbox{10403}{more} \markbox{10404}{flexible} \markbox{10405}{version} \markbox{10406}{of} \markbox{10407}{the} \markbox{10408}{distance} \markbox{10409}{formula,} \markbox{10410}{as} \markbox{10411}{they} \markbox{10412}{allow} \markbox{10413}{us} \markbox{10414}{to} \markbox{10415}{modify} \markbox{10416}{distance} \markbox{10417}{terms} \markbox{10418}{instead} \markbox{10419}{of} \markbox{10420}{just} \markbox{10421}{throwing} \markbox{10422}{them} \markbox{10423}{out} \markbox{10424}{by} \markbox{10425}{increasing} \markbox{10426}{a} \markbox{10427}{threshold.}  \markbox{10428}{For} \markbox{10429}{our} \markbox{10430}{purposes,} \markbox{10431}{they} \markbox{10432}{will} \markbox{10433}{be} \markbox{10434}{used} \markbox{10435}{in} \markbox{10436}{two} \markbox{10437}{different} \markbox{10438}{ways:} \markbox{10439}{We} \markbox{10440}{will} \markbox{10441}{need} \markbox{10442}{them} \markbox{10443}{in} \markbox{10444}{the} \markbox{10445}{proof} \markbox{10446}{of} \markbox{10447}{coarse} \markbox{10448}{surjectivity} \markbox{10449}{of} \markbox{m10450}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$}, \markbox{10451}{and} \markbox{10452}{they} \markbox{10453}{will} \markbox{10454}{also} \markbox{10455}{be} \markbox{10456}{useful} \markbox{10457}{later} \markbox{10458}{in} \markbox{10459}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tt cube} \markbox{10460}{to} \markbox{10461}{modify} \markbox{10462}{the} \markbox{10463}{cubical} \markbox{10464}{structure} \markbox{10465}{on} \markbox{m10466}{$\calQ$}.

The \markbox{10467}{main} \markbox{10468}{idea} \markbox{10469}{is} \markbox{10470}{simple:} \markbox{10471}{Given} \markbox{10472}{a} \markbox{10473}{family} \markbox{10474}{of} \markbox{10475}{subintervals} \markbox{m10476}{$\calB$} \markbox{10477}{across} \markbox{10478}{of} \markbox{10479}{the} \markbox{10480}{family} \markbox{10481}{of} \markbox{10482}{intervals} \markbox{m10483}{$\hT_U$}, \markbox{10484}{we} \markbox{10485}{want} \markbox{10486}{to} \markbox{10487}{collapse} \markbox{10488}{these} \markbox{10489}{subintervals} \markbox{m10490}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U \to \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{10491}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{10492}{and} \markbox{10493}{then} \markbox{10494}{combine} \markbox{10495}{them} \markbox{10496}{into} \markbox{10497}{a} \markbox{10498}{global} \markbox{10499}{collapsing} \markbox{10500}{map} \markbox{m10501}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$}, \markbox{10502}{where} \markbox{m10503}{$\calQ'$} \markbox{10504}{is} \markbox{10505}{the} \markbox{m10506}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{10507}{set} \markbox{10508}{of} \markbox{m10509}{$\prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_{U,0}$}, \markbox{10510}{defined} \markbox{10511}{the} \markbox{10512}{same} \markbox{10513}{way} \markbox{10514}{as} \markbox{10515}{in} \markbox{10516}{Definition} \ref{defn:Q defined}.  \markbox{10517}{Formally,} \markbox{10518}{we} \markbox{10519}{use} \markbox{10520}{the} \markbox{10521}{following} definition:

\begin{definition}[Admissible \markbox{10522}{trimming} setup]\label{defn:trimming setup}
Given \markbox{m10523}{$B>0$}, \markbox{10524}{a} \markbox{m10525}{$B$}-\emph{admissible trimming setup} \markbox{10526}{is} \markbox{10527}{a} \markbox{10528}{collection} \markbox{10529}{of} \emph{trimming intervals} \markbox{m10530}{$\calB$} \markbox{10531}{in} \markbox{10532}{the} \markbox{10533}{various} \markbox{m10534}{$\hT_{U,e}$} \markbox{10535}{satisfying} \markbox{10536}{the} following:
\begin{itemize}
\item For \markbox{10537}{each} \markbox{10538}{component}  \markbox{m10539}{$E \in \pi_0(\hT_{U,e})$}, \markbox{10540}{there} \markbox{10541}{are} \markbox{10542}{at} \markbox{10543}{most} \markbox{m10544}{$B$}-many \markbox{10545}{components} \markbox{m10546}{$D \in \calB$} \markbox{10547}{with} \markbox{m10548}{$D \subset E$}.
\item For \markbox{10549}{each} \markbox{10550}{component} \markbox{m10551}{$D \in \calB$} \markbox{10552}{satisfies} \markbox{m10553}{$|D|<B$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

Given \markbox{10554}{a} \markbox{m10555}{$B$}-admissible \markbox{10556}{trimming} \markbox{10557}{setup} \markbox{m10558}{$\calB$} \markbox{10559}{on} \markbox{m10560}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in\calU}$}, \markbox{10561}{for} \markbox{10562}{each} \markbox{m10563}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{10564}{let} \markbox{m10565}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U \to \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{10566}{denote} \markbox{10567}{the} \markbox{10568}{map} \markbox{10569}{which} \markbox{10570}{collapses} \markbox{10571}{each} \markbox{10572}{trimming} \markbox{10573}{interval} \markbox{10574}{in} \markbox{m10575}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{10576}{to} \markbox{10577}{a} \markbox{10578}{point.}  \markbox{10579}{These} \markbox{10580}{allow} \markbox{10581}{us} \markbox{10582}{to} \markbox{10583}{induce} \markbox{10584}{projection} \markbox{10585}{data} \markbox{10586}{on} \markbox{10587}{the} \markbox{m10588}{$\hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{10589}{as} \markbox{10590}{follows:} \markbox{10591}{For} \markbox{m10592}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{10593}{and} \markbox{m10594}{$V \pitchfork U$}, \markbox{10595}{we} \markbox{10596}{set} \markbox{m10597}{$(\hd^V_U)_0 = \Delta_U(\hd^V_U)$}, \markbox{10598}{and} \markbox{10599}{if} \markbox{m10600}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{10601}{we} \markbox{10602}{set} \markbox{m10603}{$(\hd^V_U)_0 = \Delta_U \circ \hd^V_U \circ \Delta^{-1}_V$}.  \markbox{10604}{We} \markbox{10605}{let} \markbox{m10606}{$\Delta: \prod_{\calU} \hT_U \to \prod_{\calU} \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{10607}{denote} \markbox{10608}{the} \markbox{10609}{product} map.


\begin{theorem}[Tree Trimming]\label{thm:tree trimming}
There \markbox{10610}{exists} \markbox{m10611}{$B_{tt} = B_{tt}(\mathfrak S, K)>0$} \markbox{10612}{so} \markbox{10613}{that} \markbox{10614}{for} \markbox{10615}{any} \markbox{m10616}{$B < B_{tt}$}, \markbox{10617}{there} \markbox{10618}{exists} \markbox{m10619}{$L =L(\mathfrak S, B)>0$} \markbox{10620}{so} \markbox{10621}{that} \markbox{10622}{the} \markbox{10623}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item We \markbox{10624}{have} \markbox{m10625}{$\Delta(\calQ) \subset \calQ'$}.
\item There \markbox{10626}{is} \markbox{10627}{a} \markbox{10628}{map} \markbox{m10629}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{10630}{so} \markbox{10631}{that} \markbox{m10632}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ'}$}.  \markbox{10633}{In} \markbox{10634}{particular,} \markbox{m10635}{$\Delta(\calQ) = \calQ'$}.
\item The \markbox{10636}{map} \markbox{m10637}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{10638}{is} \markbox{10639}{an} \markbox{m10640}{$(L,L)$}-quasi-isometry.
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

While \markbox{10641}{the} \markbox{10642}{statement} \markbox{10643}{is} \markbox{10644}{quite} \markbox{10645}{believable} \markbox{10646}{in} \markbox{10647}{light} \markbox{10648}{of} \markbox{10649}{the} \markbox{10650}{Distance} \markbox{10651}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}, \markbox{10652}{the} \markbox{10653}{proof} \markbox{10654}{of} \markbox{10655}{this} \markbox{10656}{theorem} \markbox{10657}{is} \markbox{10658}{quite} \markbox{10659}{involved.}  \markbox{10660}{While} \markbox{10661}{these} \markbox{10662}{ideas} \markbox{10663}{were} \markbox{10664}{first} \markbox{10665}{developed} \markbox{10666}{in} \markbox{10667}{greater} \markbox{10668}{generality} \markbox{10669}{in} \cite[Section 10]{Dur_infcube}---where \markbox{10670}{it} \markbox{10671}{also} \markbox{10672}{works} \markbox{10673}{when} \markbox{10674}{the} \markbox{10675}{underlying} \markbox{10676}{data} \markbox{10677}{involves} \markbox{10678}{more} \markbox{10679}{than} \markbox{10680}{two} \markbox{10681}{points} \markbox{10682}{and} \markbox{10683}{also} \markbox{10684}{hierarchy} \markbox{10685}{rays---the} \markbox{10686}{proof} \markbox{10687}{these} \markbox{10688}{is} \markbox{10689}{only} \markbox{10690}{slightly} \markbox{10691}{more} \markbox{10692}{involved} \markbox{10693}{than} \markbox{10694}{that} \markbox{10695}{required} \markbox{10696}{in} \markbox{10697}{our} \markbox{10698}{setting.}  \markbox{10699}{Moreover,} \markbox{10700}{many} \markbox{10701}{of} \markbox{10702}{the} \markbox{10703}{technicalities} \markbox{10704}{from} \markbox{10705}{dealing} \markbox{10706}{with} \markbox{10707}{rays} \markbox{10708}{are} \markbox{10709}{dealt} \markbox{10710}{with} \markbox{10711}{in} \markbox{10712}{separate} \markbox{10713}{arguments,} \markbox{10714}{so} \markbox{10715}{the} \markbox{10716}{interested} \markbox{10717}{reader} \markbox{10718}{is} \markbox{10719}{encouraged} \markbox{10720}{to} \markbox{10721}{see} \markbox{10722}{a} \markbox{10723}{full} \markbox{10724}{proof} there.

Instead, \markbox{10725}{we} \markbox{10726}{will} \markbox{10727}{present} \markbox{10728}{a} \markbox{10729}{short} \markbox{10730}{sketch} \markbox{10731}{below,} \markbox{10732}{which} \markbox{10733}{will} \markbox{10734}{hopefully} \markbox{10735}{provide} \markbox{10736}{enough} \markbox{10737}{intuition} \markbox{10738}{to} \markbox{10739}{make} \markbox{10740}{the} \markbox{10741}{statement} \markbox{10742}{believable.}  \markbox{10743}{We} \markbox{10744}{have} \markbox{10745}{included} \markbox{10746}{a} \markbox{10747}{proof} \markbox{10748}{of} \markbox{10749}{the} \markbox{10750}{stated} \markbox{10751}{version} \markbox{10752}{of} \markbox{10753}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{10754}{in} \markbox{10755}{Appendix} \ref{app:TT}.



\begin{proof}[Sketch \markbox{10756}{of} proof]
The \markbox{10757}{fact} \markbox{10758}{that} \markbox{m10759}{$\Delta(\calQ) \subset \calQ'$}, \markbox{10760}{namely} \markbox{10761}{that} \markbox{m10762}{$\Delta$} \markbox{10763}{preserves} \markbox{m10764}{$0$}-consistency, \markbox{10765}{is} \markbox{10766}{immediate} \markbox{10767}{from} \markbox{10768}{the} \markbox{10769}{fact} \markbox{10770}{that} \markbox{10771}{the} \markbox{m10772}{$\Delta_U$} \markbox{10773}{just} \markbox{10774}{collapse} \markbox{10775}{subintervals,} \markbox{10776}{so} \markbox{10777}{coordinates} \markbox{10778}{which} \markbox{10779}{were} \markbox{10780}{collapsed} \markbox{10781}{projections} \markbox{10782}{remain} \markbox{10783}{collapsed} \markbox{10784}{projections,} \markbox{10785}{showing} \markbox{10786}{item} (1).

Item \markbox{10787}{(2)} \markbox{10788}{is} \markbox{10789}{the} \markbox{10790}{most} \markbox{10791}{involved} \markbox{10792}{part.}  \markbox{10793}{For} \markbox{10794}{each} \markbox{m10795}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{10796}{let} \markbox{m10797}{$C_U = \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}.  \markbox{10798}{The} \markbox{10799}{goal} \markbox{10800}{is} \markbox{10801}{to} \markbox{10802}{pick,} \markbox{10803}{for} \markbox{10804}{each} \markbox{m10805}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{10806}{a} \markbox{10807}{point} \markbox{m10808}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{10809}{and} \markbox{10810}{then} \markbox{10811}{prove} \markbox{m10812}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{10813}{of} \markbox{10814}{the} \markbox{10815}{tuple} \markbox{m10816}{$\hx = (\hx_U)$}.  \markbox{10817}{Note} \markbox{10818}{that} \markbox{m10819}{$\Delta(\hx) =\hy$} \markbox{10820}{for} \markbox{10821}{such} \markbox{10822}{a} \markbox{10823}{tuple,} \markbox{10824}{by} construction.

The \markbox{10825}{proof} \markbox{10826}{is} \markbox{10827}{similar} \markbox{10828}{in} \markbox{10829}{spirit} \markbox{10830}{to} \markbox{10831}{the} \markbox{10832}{cluster-honing} \markbox{10833}{procedure} \markbox{10834}{from} \markbox{10835}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:hO defined}.  \markbox{10836}{The} \markbox{10837}{main} \markbox{10838}{difference} \markbox{10839}{is} \markbox{10840}{that} \markbox{10841}{the} \markbox{10842}{collapsing} \markbox{10843}{subintervals} \markbox{10844}{are} \markbox{10845}{not} \markbox{10846}{automatically} \markbox{10847}{associated} \markbox{10848}{to} \markbox{10849}{a} \markbox{10850}{collection} \markbox{10851}{of} \markbox{10852}{domains,} \markbox{10853}{and} \markbox{10854}{this} \markbox{10855}{is} \markbox{10856}{where} \markbox{10857}{the} \markbox{10858}{work} \markbox{10859}{lies.}  \markbox{10860}{The} \markbox{10861}{argument} \markbox{10862}{is} \markbox{10863}{inductive} \markbox{10864}{on} \markbox{10865}{level} \markbox{10866}{in} \markbox{10867}{the} \markbox{m10868}{$\nest$}-lattice \markbox{10869}{and} \markbox{10870}{requires} \markbox{10871}{a} \markbox{10872}{careful} \markbox{10873}{analysis} \markbox{10874}{of} \markbox{10875}{the} \markbox{10876}{construction} \markbox{10877}{and} \markbox{10878}{number} \markbox{10879}{of} \markbox{10880}{hierarchal} techniques.

Finally, \markbox{10881}{for} \markbox{10882}{item} \markbox{10883}{(3),} \markbox{10884}{since} \markbox{m10885}{$\Delta|_{\calQ}$} \markbox{10886}{is} \markbox{10887}{surjective} \markbox{10888}{and} \markbox{10889}{distance} \markbox{10890}{non-increasing,} \markbox{10891}{it} \markbox{10892}{suffices} \markbox{10893}{to} \markbox{10894}{prove} \markbox{10895}{that} \markbox{m10896}{$d_{\calQ} \prec d_{\calQ'}$}, \markbox{10897}{and} \markbox{10898}{for} \markbox{10899}{this} \markbox{10900}{it} \markbox{10901}{suffices} \markbox{10902}{to} \markbox{10903}{bound} \markbox{10904}{the} \markbox{10905}{distances} \markbox{10906}{in} \markbox{10907}{each} \markbox{m10908}{$U \in \calU$}.

Given \markbox{m10909}{$\hx, \hy \in \calQ$} \markbox{10910}{with} \markbox{m10911}{$\hx' = \Delta(\hx)$} \markbox{10912}{and} \markbox{m10913}{$\hy' = \Delta(\hy)$}, \markbox{10914}{the} \markbox{10915}{concern} \markbox{10916}{is} \markbox{10917}{that} \markbox{10918}{somehow} \markbox{10919}{one} \markbox{10920}{will} \markbox{10921}{have} \markbox{10922}{arbitrarily} \markbox{10923}{shrunk} \markbox{10924}{distances} \markbox{10925}{during} \markbox{10926}{the} \markbox{10927}{trimming} \markbox{10928}{process.}  \markbox{10929}{However,} \markbox{10930}{each} \markbox{10931}{edge} \markbox{10932}{component} \markbox{10933}{of} \markbox{m10934}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{10935}{through} \markbox{10936}{which} \markbox{10937}{the} \markbox{10938}{geodesic} \markbox{m10939}{$[\hx_U,\hy_U]$} \markbox{10940}{passes} \markbox{10941}{can} \markbox{10942}{only} \markbox{10943}{contain} \markbox{10944}{boundedly-many} \markbox{10945}{subintervals} \markbox{10946}{collapsed.}  \markbox{10947}{However,} \markbox{10948}{all} \markbox{10949}{but} \markbox{10950}{at} \markbox{10951}{most} \markbox{10952}{two} \markbox{10953}{of} \markbox{10954}{such} \markbox{10955}{edge} \markbox{10956}{components} \markbox{10957}{have} \markbox{10958}{endpoints} \markbox{10959}{which} \markbox{10960}{are} \markbox{10961}{cluster} \markbox{10962}{points} \markbox{10963}{labeled} \markbox{10964}{by} \markbox{m10965}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{10966}{for} \markbox{m10967}{$V$} \markbox{m10968}{$\nest$}-minimal.  \markbox{10969}{Since} \markbox{10970}{for} \markbox{10971}{such} \markbox{m10972}{$V$}, \markbox{10973}{the} \markbox{10974}{map} \markbox{m10975}{$\Delta_V:\hT_V \to \hT'_V$} \markbox{10976}{collapses} \markbox{10977}{subintervals} \markbox{10978}{of} \markbox{10979}{total} \markbox{10980}{diameter} \markbox{10981}{at} \markbox{10982}{most} \markbox{m10983}{$B^2$}, \markbox{10984}{we} \markbox{10985}{can} \markbox{10986}{use} \markbox{10987}{these} \markbox{m10988}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{10989}{domains} \markbox{10990}{to} \markbox{10991}{account} \markbox{10992}{for} \markbox{10993}{all} \markbox{10994}{information} \markbox{10995}{lost} \markbox{10996}{up} \markbox{10997}{the} hierarchy.

Making \markbox{10998}{this} \markbox{10999}{precise} \markbox{11000}{takes} \markbox{11001}{care} \markbox{11002}{and} \markbox{11003}{utilizes} \markbox{11004}{Proposition} \ref{prop:bounding containers}.  \markbox{11005}{The} \markbox{11006}{interested} \markbox{11007}{reader} \markbox{11008}{can} \markbox{11009}{see} \cite[Section 10]{Dur_infcube}. 
\end{proof}

\subsection{Converting to simplicial intervals}

One \markbox{11010}{application} \markbox{11011}{of} \markbox{11012}{the} \markbox{11013}{Tree} \markbox{11014}{Trimming} \markbox{11015}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{11016}{is} \markbox{11017}{that} \markbox{11018}{we} \markbox{11019}{can} \markbox{11020}{replace} \markbox{11021}{the} \markbox{11022}{family} \markbox{11023}{of} \markbox{11024}{collapsed} \markbox{11025}{intervals} \markbox{m11026}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{11027}{with} \markbox{11028}{a} \markbox{11029}{family} \markbox{11030}{of} \markbox{11031}{simplicial} \markbox{11032}{intervals,} \markbox{11033}{where} \markbox{11034}{the} \markbox{11035}{cluster} \markbox{11036}{and} \markbox{11037}{marked} \markbox{11038}{points} \markbox{11039}{lie} \markbox{11040}{at} \markbox{11041}{vertices.}  \markbox{11042}{The} \markbox{11043}{idea} \markbox{11044}{here} \markbox{11045}{is} \markbox{11046}{that} \markbox{11047}{one} \markbox{11048}{can} \markbox{11049}{trim} \markbox{11050}{each} \markbox{11051}{edge} \markbox{11052}{component} \markbox{m11053}{$E \subset \hT^e_U$} \markbox{11054}{to} \markbox{11055}{have} \markbox{11056}{a} \markbox{11057}{nonnegative} \markbox{11058}{integer} \markbox{11059}{length} \markbox{11060}{simply} \markbox{11061}{by} \markbox{11062}{collapsing} \markbox{11063}{some} \markbox{11064}{small} \markbox{11065}{segment} \markbox{11066}{of} \markbox{m11067}{$E$} \markbox{11068}{of} \markbox{11069}{length} \markbox{11070}{less} \markbox{11071}{than} \markbox{m11072}{$1$}.  \markbox{11073}{The} \markbox{11074}{family} \markbox{11075}{of} \markbox{11076}{such} \markbox{11077}{segments} \markbox{11078}{is} \markbox{11079}{an} \markbox{m11080}{$1$}-admissible \markbox{11081}{trimming} \markbox{11082}{setup,} \markbox{11083}{and} \markbox{11084}{this} \markbox{11085}{provides} \markbox{11086}{us} \markbox{11087}{a} \markbox{11088}{family} \markbox{11089}{of} \markbox{11090}{intervals} \markbox{m11091}{$\{\hT'_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{11092}{where} \markbox{m11093}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U\to \hT'_U$} \markbox{11094}{collapses} \markbox{11095}{these} \markbox{11096}{small} \markbox{11097}{segments,} \markbox{11098}{and} \markbox{m11099}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{11100}{combines} \markbox{11101}{these} \markbox{11102}{to} \markbox{11103}{a} \markbox{11104}{map} \markbox{11105}{between} \markbox{11106}{their} \markbox{m11107}{$0$}-consistent sets.

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:simplicial version}
Suppose \markbox{11108}{that} \markbox{m11109}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{11110}{are} \markbox{11111}{the} \markbox{11112}{collapsed} \markbox{11113}{intervals} \markbox{11114}{associated} \markbox{11115}{to} \markbox{11116}{an} \markbox{m11117}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{11118}{of} \markbox{11119}{an} \markbox{m11120}{$R$}-interval \markbox{11121}{system} \markbox{11122}{for} \markbox{m11123}{$a,b \in \calX$}.  \markbox{11124}{There} \markbox{11125}{exists} \markbox{m11126}{$L_{simp} = L_{simp}(R, \calX)>0$} \markbox{11127}{so} \markbox{11128}{that} \markbox{m11129}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{11130}{is} \markbox{11131}{an} \markbox{m11132}{$(L_{simp},L_{simp})$}-quasi-isometry.

\begin{itemize}
\item In \markbox{11133}{particular,} \markbox{11134}{up} \markbox{11135}{to} \markbox{11136}{a} \markbox{11137}{uniform} \markbox{11138}{quasi-isometry} \markbox{11139}{of} \markbox{m11140}{$\calQ$}, \markbox{11141}{we} \markbox{11142}{can} \markbox{11143}{assume} \markbox{11144}{that} \markbox{11145}{the} \markbox{11146}{collapsed} \markbox{11147}{intervals} \markbox{m11148}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{11149}{are} \markbox{11150}{all} \markbox{11151}{simplicial} \markbox{11152}{intervals} \markbox{11153}{with} \markbox{11154}{cluster} \markbox{11155}{and} \markbox{11156}{marked} \markbox{11157}{points} \markbox{11158}{at} \markbox{11159}{vertices.} 
\end{itemize}
\end{corollary}

See \cite[Subsection 10.1]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{11160}{for} \markbox{11161}{more} \markbox{11162}{discussion.}  \markbox{11163}{We} \markbox{11164}{note} \markbox{11165}{that} \markbox{11166}{the} \markbox{11167}{above} \markbox{11168}{corollary} \markbox{11169}{will} \markbox{11170}{not} \markbox{11171}{be} \markbox{11172}{used} \markbox{11173}{in} \markbox{11174}{the} \markbox{11175}{proof} \markbox{11176}{of} \markbox{11177}{the} \markbox{11178}{Main} \markbox{11179}{Theorem} \ref{thmi:main}, \markbox{11180}{because} \markbox{11181}{we} \markbox{11182}{will} \markbox{11183}{carefully} \markbox{11184}{construct} \markbox{11185}{stable} \markbox{11186}{intervals} \markbox{11187}{to} \markbox{11188}{be} \markbox{11189}{simplicial.}  \markbox{11190}{However,} \markbox{11191}{it} \markbox{11192}{is} \markbox{11193}{necessary} \markbox{11194}{for} \markbox{11195}{taking} \markbox{11196}{general} \markbox{11197}{intervals} \markbox{11198}{in} \markbox{11199}{each} \markbox{11200}{hyperbolic} \markbox{11201}{spaces} \markbox{11202}{and} \markbox{11203}{performing} \markbox{11204}{the} \markbox{11205}{above} \markbox{11206}{constructions} \markbox{11207}{to} \markbox{11208}{form} \markbox{11209}{a} \markbox{11210}{hierarchical} \markbox{11211}{family} \markbox{11212}{of} \markbox{11213}{intervals} \markbox{11214}{(see} \markbox{11215}{Definition} \ref{defn:HFI}, \markbox{11216}{which} \markbox{11217}{is} \markbox{11218}{necessary} \markbox{11219}{for} \markbox{11220}{our} \markbox{11221}{proof} \markbox{11222}{of} \markbox{11223}{the} \markbox{11224}{distance} \markbox{11225}{formula} \markbox{11226}{below} \markbox{11227}{(Corollary} \ref{cor:DF lower bound}).


\subsection{From $\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$ to $\hO:\calQ \to H$} \label{subsec:upgrade to HHS}

We \markbox{11228}{return} \markbox{11229}{to} \markbox{11230}{our} \markbox{11231}{main} \markbox{11232}{task,} \markbox{11233}{namely} \markbox{11234}{defining} \markbox{11235}{a} \markbox{11236}{quasi-isometry} \markbox{m11237}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$}.  \markbox{11238}{So} \markbox{11239}{far,} \markbox{11240}{we} \markbox{11241}{have} \markbox{11242}{defined} \markbox{11243}{a} \markbox{11244}{map} \markbox{m11245}{$\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}, \markbox{11246}{which} \markbox{11247}{was} \markbox{11248}{the} \markbox{11249}{bulk} \markbox{11250}{of} \markbox{11251}{the} \markbox{11252}{work.}  \markbox{11253}{Our} \markbox{11254}{next} \markbox{11255}{step} \markbox{11256}{is} \markbox{11257}{to} \markbox{11258}{upgrade} \markbox{11259}{this} \markbox{11260}{to} \markbox{11261}{a} \markbox{11262}{map} \markbox{m11263}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$}.  \markbox{11264}{Since} \markbox{11265}{this} \markbox{11266}{part} \markbox{11267}{of} \markbox{11268}{the} \markbox{11269}{argument} \markbox{11270}{mostly} \markbox{11271}{uses} \markbox{11272}{standard} \markbox{11273}{HHS} \markbox{11274}{techniques,} \markbox{11275}{we} \markbox{11276}{will} \markbox{11277}{just} \markbox{11278}{outline} \markbox{11279}{it,} \markbox{11280}{with} \markbox{11281}{appropriate} \markbox{11282}{citations} \markbox{11283}{to} \cite{Dur_infcube}.

For \markbox{11284}{each} \markbox{m11285}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{11286}{we} \markbox{11287}{first} \markbox{11288}{take} \markbox{11289}{our} \markbox{11290}{tuple} \markbox{m11291}{$\Omega(\hx) = (x_U) \subset \prod_{\calU} T_U$} \markbox{11292}{and} \markbox{11293}{push} \markbox{11294}{it} \markbox{11295}{forward} \markbox{11296}{to} \markbox{11297}{a} \markbox{11298}{tuple} \markbox{m11299}{$(y_U) \in \prod_{\calU} \calC(U)$} \markbox{11300}{by} \markbox{m11301}{$\phi_U(x_U) = y_U$}, \markbox{11302}{where} \markbox{m11303}{$\phi_U:T_U \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{11304}{are} \markbox{11305}{the} \markbox{11306}{maps} \markbox{11307}{provided} \markbox{11308}{by} \markbox{11309}{the} \markbox{m11310}{$R$}-interval \markbox{11311}{system} \markbox{11312}{structure} \markbox{11313}{(Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}).  \markbox{11314}{These} \markbox{11315}{combine} \markbox{11316}{to} \markbox{11317}{define} \markbox{11318}{a} \markbox{11319}{map} \markbox{m11320}{$\Phi:\prod_{U \in \calU} T_U \to \prod_{U \in \calU} \calC(U)$}.  \markbox{11321}{By} \markbox{11322}{Proposition} \ref{prop:Q-consistent}, \markbox{11323}{there} \markbox{11324}{is} \markbox{11325}{some} \markbox{m11326}{$\alpha_{\omega} = \alpha_{\omega}(\mathfrak S, R,r_1,r_2)>0$} \markbox{11327}{so} \markbox{11328}{that} \markbox{11329}{the} \markbox{11330}{tuple} \markbox{m11331}{$\Omega(\hx) \in \prod_{U \in \calU}T_U$} \markbox{11332}{is} \markbox{m11333}{$\alpha_{\omega}$}-consistent.  \markbox{11334}{Using} \markbox{11335}{just} \markbox{11336}{the} \markbox{m11337}{$R$}-system \markbox{11338}{axioms} \markbox{11339}{and} \markbox{11340}{standard} \markbox{11341}{HHS} \markbox{11342}{techniques,} \cite[Proposition 6.17]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{11343}{implies} \markbox{11344}{that} \markbox{m11345}{$(y_U) \in \prod_{U \in \calU} \calC(U)$} \markbox{11346}{is} \markbox{11347}{consistent} \markbox{11348}{in} \markbox{11349}{the} \markbox{11350}{sense} \markbox{11351}{of} \markbox{11352}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency} \markbox{11353}{for} \markbox{11354}{some} \markbox{11355}{consistency} \markbox{11356}{constant} \markbox{11357}{depending} \markbox{11358}{only} \markbox{11359}{on} \markbox{m11360}{$\mathfrak S, \alpha_{\omega}$}. 

Since \markbox{m11361}{$d_V(a,b) < K$} \markbox{11362}{for} \markbox{11363}{all} \markbox{m11364}{$V \in \mathfrak S - \calU$}, \markbox{11365}{it} \markbox{11366}{follows} \markbox{11367}{that} \markbox{11368}{by} \markbox{11369}{choosing} \markbox{m11370}{$y_V \in \pi_V(a)$} \markbox{11371}{for} \markbox{11372}{all} \markbox{m11373}{$V \in \mathfrak S - \calU$}, \markbox{11374}{then} \markbox{11375}{the} \markbox{11376}{complete} \markbox{11377}{tuple} \markbox{m11378}{$(y_U) \in \prod_{U \in \mathfrak S} \calC(U)$} \markbox{11379}{is} \markbox{m11380}{$\beta$}-consistent \markbox{11381}{for} \markbox{m11382}{$\beta = \beta(\mathfrak S, R, K)>0$} \markbox{11383}{(as} \markbox{m11384}{$\alpha_{\omega}$} \markbox{11385}{only} \markbox{11386}{depended} \markbox{11387}{on} \markbox{m11388}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{11389}{and} \markbox{m11390}{$R$}).

Now \markbox{11391}{with} \markbox{11392}{a} \markbox{11393}{complete} \markbox{11394}{consistent} \markbox{11395}{tuple} \markbox{11396}{in} \markbox{11397}{hand,} \markbox{11398}{we} \markbox{11399}{can} \markbox{11400}{apply} \markbox{11401}{the} \markbox{11402}{Realization} \markbox{11403}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization} \markbox{11404}{to} \markbox{11405}{define} \markbox{11406}{a} \markbox{11407}{map} \markbox{m11408}{$\mathrm{Real}_{\beta}:\prod_{U \in \mathfrak S} \calC(U) \to \calX$} \markbox{11409}{which} \markbox{11410}{takes} \markbox{11411}{each} \markbox{m11412}{$\beta$}-consistent \markbox{11413}{tuple} \markbox{11414}{and} \markbox{11415}{produces} \markbox{11416}{a} \markbox{11417}{point} \markbox{m11418}{$x \in \calX$} \markbox{11419}{whose} \markbox{11420}{projections} \markbox{11421}{coarsely} \markbox{11422}{coincide} \markbox{11423}{with} \markbox{11424}{the} \markbox{11425}{tuple,} \markbox{11426}{with} \markbox{11427}{error} \markbox{11428}{depending} \markbox{11429}{on} \markbox{m11430}{$\beta, \mathfrak S$}.

Finally, \cite[Lemma 6.6]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{11431}{which} \markbox{11432}{depends} \markbox{11433}{on} \markbox{11434}{the} \markbox{11435}{more} \markbox{11436}{general} \markbox{11437}{fact} \cite[Proposition 6.3]{HHS_II}, \markbox{11438}{provides} \markbox{11439}{a} \markbox{m11440}{$(J,J)$}-coarse \markbox{11441}{retraction} \markbox{11442}{map} \markbox{m11443}{$\mathrm{ret}_H:\calX \to H$}, \markbox{11444}{where} \markbox{m11445}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{11446}{where} \markbox{m11447}{$J = J(\mathfrak S)>0$}.  \markbox{11448}{This} \markbox{11449}{map} \markbox{11450}{is} \markbox{11451}{just} \markbox{11452}{closest-point} \markbox{11453}{projection} \markbox{11454}{to} \markbox{m11455}{$\hull_U(a,b)$} \markbox{11456}{in} \markbox{11457}{each} \markbox{m11458}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{11459}{plus} \markbox{11460}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization}. 

Combining \markbox{11461}{these,} \markbox{11462}{we} \markbox{11463}{get} \markbox{11464}{a} \markbox{11465}{map} \markbox{m11466}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{11467}{given} \markbox{11468}{by} \markbox{m11469}{$\hO = \mathrm{ret}_H \circ \mathrm{Real}_{\beta} \circ \Phi \circ \Omega$}.  \markbox{11470}{Our} \markbox{11471}{main} \markbox{11472}{goal} \markbox{11473}{is} \markbox{11474}{to} \markbox{11475}{show} \markbox{11476}{that} \markbox{m11477}{$\hPsi \circ \hO:\calQ \to \calQ$} \markbox{11478}{is} \markbox{11479}{coarsely} \markbox{11480}{the} \markbox{11481}{identity,} \markbox{11482}{where} \markbox{m11483}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{11484}{is} \markbox{11485}{the} \markbox{11486}{map} \markbox{11487}{defined} \markbox{11488}{in} \markbox{11489}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}.

Before \markbox{11490}{analyzing} \markbox{11491}{this} \markbox{11492}{total} \markbox{11493}{composition,} \markbox{11494}{we} \markbox{11495}{want} \markbox{11496}{to} \markbox{11497}{look} \markbox{11498}{at} \markbox{11499}{an} \markbox{11500}{intermediate} \markbox{11501}{step.}  \markbox{11502}{For} \markbox{11503}{convenience,} \markbox{11504}{if} \markbox{m11505}{$\alpha>0$}, \markbox{11506}{we} \markbox{11507}{let} \markbox{m11508}{$\calZ_{\alpha}$} \markbox{11509}{denote} \markbox{11510}{the} \markbox{11511}{collection} \markbox{11512}{of} \markbox{m11513}{$\alpha$}-consistent \markbox{11514}{tuples} \markbox{11515}{in} \markbox{m11516}{$\prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}.  Define
$$\Phi_{\alpha}:\calZ_{\alpha} \to H$$ \markbox{11517}{by} \markbox{m11518}{$\mathrm{ret}_H \circ \mathrm{Real}_{\beta} \circ \Phi$}.

The \markbox{11519}{following} \markbox{11520}{proposition} \markbox{11521}{says} \markbox{11522}{that} \markbox{11523}{this} \markbox{11524}{map} \markbox{11525}{behaves} \markbox{11526}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{11527}{as} \markbox{11528}{one} \markbox{11529}{might} \markbox{11530}{expect} \markbox{11531}{upon} \markbox{11532}{composition} \markbox{11533}{with} \markbox{11534}{the} \markbox{11535}{coordinate} \markbox{11536}{maps} \markbox{m11537}{$\psi_U:\calX \to T_U$}, \markbox{11538}{which} \markbox{11539}{we} \markbox{11540}{recall} \markbox{11541}{are} \markbox{11542}{defined} \markbox{11543}{by} \markbox{m11544}{$\psi_U = \phi^{-1}_U\circ p_U \circ \pi_U$}, \markbox{11545}{where} \markbox{m11546}{$p_U:\calC(U) \to \phi_U(T_U)$} \markbox{11547}{is} \markbox{11548}{closest-point} \markbox{11549}{projection.}  

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:interval coordinate control}
There \markbox{11550}{exists} \markbox{m11551}{$D_1 = D_1(K, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{11552}{so} \markbox{11553}{that} \markbox{11554}{if} \markbox{m11555}{$x = (x_V) \in \calZ_{\alpha_{\omega}}$}, \markbox{11556}{then} \markbox{11557}{we} have
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m11558}{$d_{T_U}(x_U, \psi_U \circ \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}}(x))<D_1$} \markbox{11559}{for} \markbox{11560}{all} \markbox{m11561}{$U \in \calU$}, and
\item \markbox{m11562}{$\#\{U \in \calU| d_{T_U}(x_U, \psi_U \circ \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}}(x)) > 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R\} < D_1$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item In \markbox{11563}{particular,} \markbox{11564}{by} \markbox{11565}{choosing} \markbox{m11566}{$L>2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}, \markbox{11567}{we} get
$$\sum_{U \in \calU} [d_{T_U}(x_U, \psi_U \circ \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}}(x)]_L < D_1^2.$$
\end{itemize}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}[Sketch]
This \markbox{11568}{proposition} \markbox{11569}{is} \markbox{11570}{a} \markbox{11571}{special} \markbox{11572}{case} \markbox{11573}{of} \cite[Proposition 11.4]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{11574}{and} \markbox{11575}{the} \markbox{11576}{proof} \markbox{11577}{is} \markbox{11578}{almost} \markbox{11579}{entirely} \markbox{11580}{the} \markbox{11581}{same.}  \markbox{11582}{The} \markbox{11583}{proof} \markbox{11584}{of} \markbox{11585}{item} \markbox{11586}{(1)} \markbox{11587}{is} \markbox{11588}{a} \markbox{11589}{definition} \markbox{11590}{chase.}  \markbox{11591}{It} \markbox{11592}{is} \markbox{11593}{basically} \markbox{11594}{saying} \markbox{11595}{that} \markbox{11596}{consistency} \markbox{11597}{in} \markbox{11598}{the} \markbox{11599}{interval} \markbox{11600}{setting} \markbox{11601}{is} \markbox{11602}{roughly} \markbox{11603}{consistency} \markbox{11604}{in} \markbox{11605}{the} \markbox{11606}{hierarchical} \markbox{11607}{setting,} \markbox{11608}{and} \markbox{11609}{that} \markbox{11610}{flowing} \markbox{11611}{from} \markbox{11612}{the} \markbox{11613}{former} \markbox{11614}{to} \markbox{11615}{the} \markbox{11616}{latter} \markbox{11617}{and} \markbox{11618}{back} \markbox{11619}{only} \markbox{11620}{moves} \markbox{11621}{coordinates} \markbox{11622}{a} \markbox{11623}{bounded} amount.

On \markbox{11624}{the} \markbox{11625}{other} \markbox{11626}{hand,} \markbox{11627}{the} \markbox{11628}{proof} \markbox{11629}{of} \markbox{11630}{(2)---which} \markbox{11631}{says} \markbox{11632}{that} \markbox{11633}{only} \markbox{11634}{boundedly-many} \markbox{11635}{coordinates} \markbox{11636}{move} \markbox{11637}{more} \markbox{11638}{than} \markbox{11639}{a} \markbox{11640}{bounded} \markbox{11641}{amount---is} \markbox{11642}{more} \markbox{11643}{involved,} \markbox{11644}{but} \markbox{11645}{also} \markbox{11646}{fairly} \markbox{11647}{standard.}  \markbox{11648}{It} \markbox{11649}{uses} \markbox{11650}{a} \markbox{11651}{variation} \markbox{11652}{on} \markbox{11653}{the} \markbox{11654}{Passing-Up} \markbox{11655}{property} \markbox{11656}{from} \markbox{11657}{Lemma} \ref{lem:passing-up}, \markbox{11658}{and} \markbox{11659}{the} \markbox{11660}{BGI} \markbox{11661}{property} \markbox{11662}{from} \markbox{11663}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}.  \markbox{11664}{Set} \markbox{m11665}{$\psi_U \circ \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}}(x) = y = (y_U)$}.  \markbox{11666}{The} \markbox{11667}{idea} \markbox{11668}{here} \markbox{11669}{is} \markbox{11670}{that} \markbox{11671}{if} \markbox{11672}{there} \markbox{11673}{are} \markbox{11674}{too} \markbox{11675}{many} \markbox{11676}{coordinates} \markbox{11677}{where} \markbox{m11678}{$d_{T_U}(x_U, y_U) > 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}, \markbox{11679}{then} \markbox{11680}{we} \markbox{11681}{can} \markbox{11682}{force} \markbox{11683}{the} \markbox{11684}{existence} \markbox{11685}{of} \markbox{11686}{some} \markbox{11687}{coordinate} \markbox{m11688}{$T_W$} \markbox{11689}{where} \markbox{m11690}{$d_{T_W}(x_W,y_W)>D_1$}, \markbox{11691}{which} \markbox{11692}{is} \markbox{11693}{impossible} \markbox{11694}{by} (1).
\end{proof}

\subsection{The map $\hO:\calQ \to H$ and coarse surjectivity of $\hPsi$}

We \markbox{11695}{are} \markbox{11696}{ready} \markbox{11697}{to} \markbox{11698}{analyze} \markbox{11699}{the} \markbox{11700}{map} \markbox{m11701}{$\hO = \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}} \circ \Omega:\calQ \to H$}.    \markbox{11702}{Since} \markbox{m11703}{$\hPsi(H) \subset \calQ$} \markbox{11704}{by} \markbox{11705}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}, \markbox{11706}{we} \markbox{11707}{see} \markbox{11708}{that} \markbox{m11709}{$\hPsi \circ \hO:\calQ \to \calQ$}.  \markbox{11710}{We} \markbox{11711}{prove} \markbox{11712}{that} \markbox{11713}{this} \markbox{11714}{map} \markbox{11715}{is} \markbox{11716}{coarsely} \markbox{11717}{the} identity:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:coarse surjectivity}
There \markbox{11718}{exists} \markbox{m11719}{$M_0 = M_0(R, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{11720}{so} \markbox{11721}{that} \markbox{11722}{for} \markbox{11723}{any} \markbox{m11724}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{11725}{we} \markbox{11726}{have} \markbox{m11727}{$d_{\calQ}(\hx, \hPsi \circ \hO(\hx)) < M_0$}. 
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}[Sketch]
This \markbox{11728}{proposition} \markbox{11729}{is} \markbox{11730}{a} \markbox{11731}{special} \markbox{11732}{case} \markbox{11733}{of} \markbox{11734}{the} \markbox{11735}{proof} \markbox{11736}{contained} \markbox{11737}{in} \cite[Subsection 11.2]{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{11738}{Since} \markbox{11739}{the} \markbox{11740}{details} \markbox{11741}{of} \markbox{11742}{the} \markbox{11743}{proof} \markbox{11744}{are} \markbox{11745}{very} \markbox{11746}{similar} \markbox{11747}{to} \markbox{11748}{the} \markbox{11749}{original,} \markbox{11750}{we} \markbox{11751}{will} \markbox{11752}{again} \markbox{11753}{only} \markbox{11754}{provide} \markbox{11755}{a} sketch.

Fix \markbox{m11756}{$\hx \in \calQ$} \markbox{11757}{and} \markbox{11758}{let} \markbox{m11759}{$\hy \in \hPsi \circ \hO(\hx)$}. \markbox{11760}{We} \markbox{11761}{will} \markbox{11762}{argue} \markbox{11763}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{11764}{since} \markbox{11765}{that} \markbox{11766}{is} \markbox{11767}{how} \markbox{11768}{the} \markbox{m11769}{$\ell^1$} \markbox{11770}{distance} \markbox{11771}{on} \markbox{m11772}{$\calQ$} \markbox{11773}{is} \markbox{11774}{defined.}  \markbox{11775}{The} \markbox{11776}{difference} \markbox{11777}{from} \markbox{11778}{the} \markbox{11779}{usual} \markbox{11780}{HHS} \markbox{11781}{style} \markbox{11782}{argument} \markbox{11783}{here} \markbox{11784}{is} \markbox{11785}{that} \markbox{m11786}{$d_{\calQ}$} \markbox{11787}{is} \markbox{11788}{an} \markbox{m11789}{$\ell^1$} \markbox{11790}{sum} \markbox{11791}{not} \markbox{11792}{involving} \markbox{11793}{a} \markbox{11794}{threshold.}  \markbox{11795}{To} \markbox{11796}{get} \markbox{11797}{around} \markbox{11798}{that} \markbox{11799}{issue,} \markbox{11800}{we} \markbox{11801}{will} \markbox{11802}{make} \markbox{11803}{an} \markbox{11804}{argument} \markbox{11805}{using} \markbox{11806}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control} \markbox{11807}{and} \markbox{11808}{Tree} \markbox{11809}{Trimming} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{11810}{as} \markbox{11811}{follows.}  \markbox{11812}{We} \markbox{11813}{show} \markbox{11814}{that} \markbox{11815}{all} \markbox{11816}{coordinate} \markbox{11817}{distances} \markbox{m11818}{$d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U, \hy_U)$} \markbox{11819}{are} \markbox{11820}{bounded} \markbox{11821}{in} \markbox{11822}{terms} \markbox{11823}{of} \markbox{m11824}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{11825}{and} \markbox{m11826}{$K$}, \markbox{11827}{with} \markbox{11828}{all} \markbox{11829}{but} \markbox{11830}{boundedly-many} \markbox{11831}{(in} \markbox{11832}{terms} \markbox{11833}{of} \markbox{m11834}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{11835}{being} \markbox{11836}{bounded} \markbox{11837}{in} \markbox{11838}{terms} \markbox{11839}{of} \markbox{m11840}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{11841}{We} \markbox{11842}{can} \markbox{11843}{then} \markbox{11844}{collapse} \markbox{11845}{the} \markbox{11846}{subintervals} \markbox{11847}{between} \markbox{m11848}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{11849}{and} \markbox{m11850}{$\hy_U$} \markbox{11851}{in} \markbox{11852}{the} \markbox{11853}{latter} \markbox{11854}{domains} \markbox{11855}{while} \markbox{11856}{only} \markbox{11857}{incurring} \markbox{11858}{a} \markbox{11859}{bounded} \markbox{11860}{error} \markbox{11861}{globally,} \markbox{11862}{resulting} \markbox{11863}{in} \markbox{11864}{images} \markbox{11865}{for} \markbox{m11866}{$\hx,\hy$} \markbox{11867}{which} \markbox{11868}{are} \markbox{11869}{bounded} \markbox{11870}{distance} \markbox{11871}{in} \markbox{11872}{the} \markbox{11873}{quotient,} \markbox{11874}{showing} \markbox{11875}{that} \markbox{m11876}{$\hx,\hy$} \markbox{11877}{were} \markbox{11878}{bounded} \markbox{11879}{distance} \markbox{11880}{in} \markbox{m11881}{$\calQ$}.

Let \markbox{m11882}{$\Omega(\hx) = (x_U)$} \markbox{11883}{and} \markbox{m11884}{$\Psi \circ \hO(\hx) = (y_U)$}, \markbox{11885}{and} \markbox{11886}{observe} \markbox{11887}{that} \markbox{11888}{since} \markbox{m11889}{$q\circ \Omega(\hx) = \hx$}, \markbox{11890}{the} \markbox{11891}{tuples} \markbox{m11892}{$(x_U), (y_U)$} \markbox{11893}{are} \markbox{11894}{exactly} \markbox{11895}{the} \markbox{11896}{type} \markbox{11897}{in} \markbox{11898}{the} \markbox{11899}{statement} \markbox{11900}{of} \markbox{11901}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control}.  \markbox{11902}{Moreover,} \markbox{11903}{since} \markbox{m11904}{$q \circ \Omega(\hy) = \hy$} \markbox{11905}{by} \markbox{11906}{construction,} \markbox{11907}{while} \markbox{m11908}{$q$} \markbox{11909}{is} \markbox{m11910}{$1$}-Lipschitz \markbox{11911}{by} \markbox{11912}{item} \markbox{11913}{(4)} \markbox{11914}{of} \markbox{11915}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}, \markbox{11916}{it} \markbox{11917}{will} \markbox{11918}{suffice} \markbox{11919}{to} \markbox{11920}{control} \markbox{11921}{the} \markbox{11922}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{11923}{distances} \markbox{11924}{of} \markbox{11925}{the} \markbox{m11926}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)$} \markbox{11927}{in} \markbox{11928}{order} \markbox{11929}{to} \markbox{11930}{utilize} \markbox{11931}{the} \markbox{11932}{above} argument.

Let \markbox{m11933}{$\calV = \{U \in \calU| \hx_U \neq \hy_U\}$}.  \markbox{11934}{One} \markbox{11935}{proceeds} \markbox{11936}{inductively} \markbox{11937}{on} \markbox{11938}{the} \markbox{m11939}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-level.  \markbox{11940}{Let} \markbox{m11941}{$\calV_{min} \subset \calV$} \markbox{11942}{denote} \markbox{11943}{the} \markbox{m11944}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{11945}{domains} \markbox{11946}{in} \markbox{m11947}{$\calV$}.

By \markbox{11948}{item} \markbox{11949}{(8)} \markbox{11950}{of} \markbox{11951}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}, \markbox{11952}{for} \markbox{11953}{all} \markbox{11954}{but} \markbox{m11955}{$A$}-many \markbox{m11956}{$U \in \calV_{min}$} \markbox{11957}{with} \markbox{m11958}{$A = A(\mathfrak S)>0$}, \markbox{11959}{we} \markbox{11960}{have} \markbox{m11961}{$\hx_U,\hy_U \in \{\ha_U,\hb_U\}$}, \markbox{11962}{and} \markbox{11963}{hence} \markbox{11964}{for} \markbox{11965}{all} \markbox{11966}{but} \markbox{11967}{at} \markbox{11968}{most} \markbox{m11969}{$A$} \markbox{11970}{domains} \markbox{11971}{in} \markbox{m11972}{$\calV_{min}$}, \markbox{11973}{we} \markbox{11974}{have} \markbox{11975}{that} \markbox{m11976}{$\hx_U,\hy_U$} \markbox{11977}{are} \markbox{11978}{the} \markbox{11979}{(opposite)} \markbox{11980}{endpoints} \markbox{11981}{of} \markbox{m11982}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{11983}{By} \markbox{11984}{item} \markbox{11985}{(6)} \markbox{11986}{of} \markbox{11987}{that} \markbox{11988}{lemma,} \markbox{m11989}{$d_{T_U}(a_U,b_U) > d_{\hT_U}(\ha_U,\hb_U) \succ K$}, \markbox{11990}{while} \markbox{m11991}{$K$} \markbox{11992}{can} \markbox{11993}{be} \markbox{11994}{taken} \markbox{11995}{to} \markbox{11996}{be} \markbox{11997}{as} \markbox{11998}{much} \markbox{11999}{larger} \markbox{12000}{than} \markbox{m12001}{$2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$} \markbox{12002}{as} \markbox{12003}{we} \markbox{12004}{need,} \markbox{12005}{as} \markbox{m12006}{$\alpha_{\omega}$} \markbox{12007}{and} \markbox{m12008}{$R$} \markbox{12009}{depend} \markbox{12010}{only} \markbox{12011}{on} \markbox{m12012}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{12013}{Since} \markbox{12014}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control} \markbox{12015}{bounds} \markbox{12016}{the} \markbox{12017}{number} \markbox{12018}{of} \markbox{12019}{domains} \markbox{m12020}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{12021}{where} \markbox{m12022}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)> 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}, \markbox{12023}{we} \markbox{12024}{can} \markbox{12025}{conclude} \markbox{12026}{that} \markbox{m12027}{$\#\calV_{min} < D_1 + A$}.

Now \markbox{12028}{let} \markbox{m12029}{$\calV' \subset \calV - \calV_{min}$} \markbox{12030}{denote} \markbox{12031}{the} \markbox{12032}{set} \markbox{12033}{of} \markbox{12034}{non-minimal} \markbox{12035}{domains} \markbox{m12036}{$V$} \markbox{12037}{where} \markbox{m12038}{$\hx_V \neq \hy_V$} \markbox{12039}{and} \markbox{m12040}{$d_{T_V}(x_V,y_V) < 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}, \markbox{12041}{which} \markbox{12042}{we} \markbox{12043}{note} \markbox{12044}{only} \markbox{12045}{excludes} \markbox{12046}{boundedly-many} \markbox{12047}{domains} \markbox{12048}{by} \markbox{12049}{item} \markbox{12050}{(2)} \markbox{12051}{of} \markbox{12052}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control}.

Since \markbox{12053}{the} \markbox{12054}{maps} \markbox{m12055}{$q_V:T_V \to \hT_V$} \markbox{12056}{are} \markbox{m12057}{$1$}-Lipschitz \markbox{12058}{(item} \markbox{12059}{(4)} \markbox{12060}{of} \markbox{12061}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}), \markbox{12062}{we} \markbox{12063}{have} \markbox{m12064}{$d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V) < 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}.  \markbox{12065}{The} \markbox{12066}{idea} \markbox{12067}{now} \markbox{12068}{is} \markbox{12069}{to} \markbox{12070}{use} \markbox{12071}{the} \markbox{12072}{Tree} \markbox{12073}{Trimming} \markbox{12074}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{12075}{to} \markbox{12076}{collapse} \markbox{12077}{the} \markbox{12078}{geodesics} \markbox{m12079}{$[\hx_V,\hy_V]$} \markbox{12080}{between} \markbox{m12081}{$\hx_V,\hy_V$} \markbox{12082}{in} \markbox{m12083}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{12084}{to} \markbox{12085}{points.}  \markbox{12086}{Each} \markbox{12087}{interval} \markbox{m12088}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{12089}{contains} \markbox{12090}{at} \markbox{12091}{most} \markbox{12092}{one} \markbox{12093}{such} \markbox{12094}{geodesic,} \markbox{12095}{and} \markbox{12096}{each} \markbox{12097}{such} \markbox{12098}{geodesic} \markbox{12099}{has} \markbox{12100}{a} \markbox{12101}{length} \markbox{12102}{bounded} \markbox{12103}{independently} \markbox{12104}{of} \markbox{m12105}{$K$}.  \markbox{12106}{Hence} \markbox{12107}{the} \markbox{12108}{set} \markbox{12109}{of} \markbox{12110}{such} \markbox{12111}{intervals} \markbox{12112}{across} \markbox{12113}{both} \markbox{m12114}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{12115}{and} \markbox{12116}{non-minimal} \markbox{12117}{domains} \markbox{12118}{with} \markbox{12119}{this} \markbox{12120}{distance} \markbox{12121}{bound} \markbox{12122}{is} \markbox{12123}{an} \markbox{12124}{admissible} \markbox{12125}{trimming} \markbox{12126}{set} \markbox{12127}{in} \markbox{12128}{the} \markbox{12129}{sense} \markbox{12130}{required} \markbox{12131}{for} \markbox{12132}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}.

If \markbox{12133}{we} \markbox{12134}{take} \markbox{m12135}{$\hT'_V$} \markbox{12136}{to} \markbox{12137}{be} \markbox{12138}{the} \markbox{12139}{interval} \markbox{12140}{obtained} \markbox{12141}{from} \markbox{m12142}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{12143}{post-trimming} \markbox{12144}{and} \markbox{m12145}{$\calQ'$} \markbox{12146}{the} \markbox{12147}{corresponding} \markbox{m12148}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{12149}{set,} \markbox{12150}{then} \markbox{12151}{the} \markbox{12152}{images} \markbox{m12153}{$\hx', \hy'$} \markbox{12154}{of} \markbox{m12155}{$\hx,\hy$} \markbox{12156}{now} \markbox{12157}{satisfy} \markbox{m12158}{$\hx'_V = \hy'_V$} \markbox{12159}{for} \markbox{12160}{all} \markbox{12161}{but} \markbox{12162}{boundedly-many} \markbox{m12163}{$V$}, \markbox{12164}{and} \markbox{12165}{the} \markbox{12166}{remaining} \markbox{12167}{distances} \markbox{12168}{are} \markbox{12169}{all} \markbox{12170}{bounded} \markbox{12171}{by} \markbox{12172}{some} \markbox{12173}{function} \markbox{12174}{of} \markbox{m12175}{$D_1$} \markbox{12176}{by} \markbox{12177}{item} \markbox{12178}{(1)} \markbox{12179}{of} \markbox{12180}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control}.  \markbox{12181}{In} \markbox{12182}{particular,} \markbox{m12183}{$d_{\calQ'}(\hx,\hy)$} \markbox{12184}{is} \markbox{12185}{bounded.}  \markbox{12186}{But} \markbox{12187}{the} \markbox{12188}{map} \markbox{m12189}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{12190}{is} \markbox{12191}{a} \markbox{12192}{uniform} \markbox{12193}{quasi-isometry,} \markbox{12194}{so} \markbox{12195}{that} \markbox{12196}{means} \markbox{12197}{that} \markbox{m12198}{$d_{\calQ}(\hx,\hy)$} \markbox{12199}{is} \markbox{12200}{also} \markbox{12201}{bounded,} \markbox{12202}{which} \markbox{12203}{is} \markbox{12204}{what} \markbox{12205}{we} \markbox{12206}{wanted.}  \markbox{12207}{We} \markbox{12208}{leave} \markbox{12209}{checking} \markbox{12210}{the} \markbox{12211}{details} \markbox{12212}{to} \markbox{12213}{the} reader.
\end{proof}

\section{Building a cube complex from a hierarchical family of intervals}\label{sec:cubulation}

The \markbox{12214}{goal} \markbox{12215}{of} \markbox{12216}{this} \markbox{12217}{section} \markbox{12218}{is} \markbox{12219}{to} \markbox{12220}{explain} \markbox{12221}{how} \markbox{12222}{to} \markbox{12223}{take} \markbox{12224}{a} \markbox{12225}{special} \markbox{12226}{collection} \markbox{12227}{of} \markbox{12228}{intervals} \markbox{12229}{satisfying} \markbox{12230}{certain} \markbox{12231}{HHS-like} \markbox{12232}{properties,} \markbox{12233}{and} \markbox{12234}{to} \markbox{12235}{produce} \markbox{12236}{from} \markbox{12237}{them} \markbox{12238}{a} \markbox{12239}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12240}{cube} \markbox{12241}{complex.}  \markbox{12242}{The} \markbox{12243}{details} \markbox{12244}{of} \markbox{12245}{this} \markbox{12246}{construction} \markbox{12247}{motivate} \markbox{12248}{the} \markbox{12249}{stabilization} \markbox{12250}{techniques} \markbox{12251}{we} \markbox{12252}{develop} \markbox{12253}{later} \markbox{12254}{in} \markbox{12255}{this} article.


\subsection{Hierarchical families of intervals}
