In \markbox{12256}{this} \markbox{12257}{subsection,} \markbox{12258}{we} \markbox{12259}{axiomatize} \markbox{12260}{the} \markbox{12261}{properties} \markbox{12262}{we} \markbox{12263}{need} \markbox{12264}{from} \markbox{12265}{a} \markbox{12266}{family} \markbox{12267}{of} \markbox{12268}{intervals} \markbox{12269}{in} \markbox{12270}{order} \markbox{12271}{to} \markbox{12272}{build} \markbox{12273}{a} \markbox{12274}{cube} \markbox{12275}{complex.}  \markbox{12276}{The} \markbox{12277}{purpose} \markbox{12278}{of} \markbox{12279}{this} \markbox{12280}{axiomatization} \markbox{12281}{is} \markbox{12282}{to} \markbox{12283}{allow} \markbox{12284}{us} \markbox{12285}{to} \markbox{12286}{modify} \markbox{12287}{our} \markbox{12288}{construction} \markbox{12289}{in} \markbox{12290}{various} \markbox{12291}{ways} \markbox{12292}{while} \markbox{12293}{preserving} \markbox{12294}{the} \markbox{12295}{axioms,} \markbox{12296}{as} \markbox{12297}{any} \markbox{12298}{setup} \markbox{12299}{which} \markbox{12300}{satisfies} \markbox{12301}{the} \markbox{12302}{axioms} \markbox{12303}{produces} \markbox{12304}{a} \markbox{12305}{cube} \markbox{12306}{complex.}  \markbox{12307}{The} \markbox{12308}{properties} \markbox{12309}{themselves} \markbox{12310}{are} \markbox{12311}{motivated} \markbox{12312}{by} \markbox{12313}{the} \markbox{12314}{HHS} \markbox{12315}{axioms} \markbox{12316}{and} \markbox{12317}{the} \markbox{12318}{properties} \markbox{12319}{in} \markbox{12320}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.

\begin{definition}[Hierarchical \markbox{12321}{family} \markbox{12322}{of} intervals] \label{defn:HFI}
A \emph{hierarchical family of intervals (HFI)} \markbox{12323}{is} \markbox{12324}{the} \markbox{12325}{following} \markbox{12326}{collection} \markbox{12327}{of} \markbox{12328}{objects} \markbox{12329}{and} properties:

\begin{enumerate}
\item A \markbox{12330}{finite} \markbox{12331}{index} \markbox{12332}{set} \markbox{m12333}{$\calU$} \markbox{12334}{of} \emph{domains} \markbox{12335}{with} \emph{relations} \markbox{m12336}{$\nest, \pitchfork, \perp$} \markbox{12337}{so} that
\begin{itemize}
    \item \markbox{m12338}{$\nest$} \markbox{12339}{is} \markbox{12340}{anti-reflexive} \markbox{12341}{and} \markbox{12342}{anti-symmetric,} \markbox{12343}{and} \markbox{12344}{gives} \markbox{12345}{a} \markbox{12346}{partial} \markbox{12347}{order} \markbox{12348}{with} \markbox{12349}{a} \markbox{12350}{bound} \markbox{12351}{on} \markbox{12352}{the} \markbox{12353}{length} \markbox{12354}{of} chains;
    \item \markbox{m12355}{$\pitchfork$} \markbox{12356}{is} \markbox{12357}{symmetric} \markbox{12358}{and} anti-reflexive;
    \item There \markbox{12359}{is} \markbox{12360}{a} \markbox{12361}{unique} \markbox{m12362}{$\nest$}-maximal \markbox{12363}{element} \markbox{m12364}{$S$};
    \item Any \markbox{12365}{pair} \markbox{12366}{of} \markbox{12367}{domains} \markbox{m12368}{$U,V \in \calU$} \markbox{12369}{satisfies} \markbox{12370}{exactly} \markbox{12371}{one} \markbox{12372}{of} \markbox{12373}{the} \markbox{12374}{relations.} 
\end{itemize}
\item There \markbox{12375}{is} \markbox{12376}{a} \markbox{12377}{bound} \markbox{12378}{on} \markbox{12379}{the} \markbox{12380}{size} \markbox{12381}{of} \markbox{12382}{any} \markbox{12383}{pairwise} \markbox{m12384}{$\perp$}-comparable \markbox{12385}{subset} \markbox{12386}{of} \markbox{m12387}{$\calU$}. \label{item:finite dim}
\item To \markbox{12388}{each} \markbox{m12389}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{12390}{there} \markbox{12391}{is} \markbox{12392}{an} \markbox{12393}{associated} \markbox{12394}{finite} \markbox{12395}{simplicial} \markbox{12396}{interval} \markbox{m12397}{$\hT_U$}. \label{item:simplicial}
\item A \markbox{12398}{pair} \markbox{12399}{of} \markbox{12400}{labels} \markbox{m12401}{$F = \{x,y\}$} \markbox{12402}{which} \markbox{12403}{determined} \markbox{12404}{the} \markbox{12405}{endpoints,} \markbox{12406}{called} \emph{marked points} \markbox{m12407}{$\hx_U, \hy_U$}, \markbox{12408}{of} \markbox{12409}{the} \markbox{12410}{interval} \markbox{m12411}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{12412}{for} \markbox{12413}{each} \markbox{m12414}{$U \in \calU$}.
\item A \markbox{12415}{family} \markbox{12416}{of} \emph{relative projections} determining:
\begin{itemize}
    \item For \markbox{12417}{each} \markbox{m12418}{$U, V \in \calU$} \markbox{12419}{with} \markbox{m12420}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{12421}{or} \markbox{m12422}{$V \pitchfork U$}, \markbox{12423}{there} \markbox{12424}{is} \markbox{12425}{a} \markbox{12426}{vertex} \markbox{m12427}{$\hd^V_U \in \hT^{(0)}_U$} \markbox{12428}{called} \markbox{12429}{a} \emph{cluster point}.
 
\end{itemize}
    \item There \markbox{12430}{exist} \markbox{12431}{projection} \markbox{12432}{maps} \markbox{m12433}{$\hd^U_V: \hT_U \to \hT_V$} \markbox{12434}{when} \markbox{m12435}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{12436}{satisfying} \markbox{12437}{the} \markbox{12438}{following} properties:\label{item:BGI HFI}
    \begin{enumerate}
    	\item (Consistency) \markbox{12439}{For} \markbox{12440}{each} \markbox{m12441}{$f \in F$}, \markbox{12442}{we} \markbox{12443}{have} \markbox{m12444}{$\hd^U_V(\hf_U) = \hf_V$}.
        \item (BGI) \markbox{12445}{If} \markbox{m12446}{$C \subset \hT_U - \hd^V_U$} \markbox{12447}{is} \markbox{12448}{a} \markbox{12449}{component,} \markbox{12450}{then} \markbox{m12451}{$\hd^U_V(C)$} \markbox{12452}{coincides} \markbox{12453}{with} \markbox{m12454}{$\hf_V$} \markbox{12455}{for} \markbox{m12456}{$f \in F$} \markbox{12457}{with} \markbox{m12458}{$\hf_U \in C$}. 
    \end{enumerate}

\item If \markbox{m12459}{$U,V,W \in \calU$} \markbox{12460}{with} \markbox{m12461}{$V,W \nest U$}, \markbox{m12462}{$V \pitchfork W$}, \markbox{12463}{and} \markbox{m12464}{$\hd^V_U \neq \hd^W_U$}, \markbox{12465}{then} \markbox{m12466}{$\hd^U_V(\hd^W_U) = \hd^W_V \in \hT_V$}. \label{item:delta control HFI}
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}
In \cite[Definition 12.1]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{12467}{the} \markbox{12468}{definition} \markbox{12469}{of} \markbox{12470}{a} \emph{hierarchical family of trees} \markbox{12471}{allows} \markbox{12472}{for} \markbox{12473}{the} \markbox{12474}{trees} \markbox{12475}{to} \markbox{12476}{have} \markbox{12477}{more} \markbox{12478}{than} \markbox{m12479}{$2$} \markbox{12480}{leaves.}  \markbox{12481}{This} \markbox{12482}{is} \markbox{12483}{only} \markbox{12484}{needed} \markbox{12485}{for} \markbox{12486}{modeling} \markbox{12487}{tuples} \markbox{12488}{of} \markbox{m12489}{$3$} \markbox{12490}{or} \markbox{12491}{more} points.
\end{remark}

The \markbox{12492}{following} \markbox{12493}{is} \markbox{12494}{an} \markbox{12495}{immediate} \markbox{12496}{consequence} \markbox{12497}{of} \markbox{12498}{our} \markbox{12499}{work} \markbox{12500}{in} \markbox{12501}{Section} \ref{sec:interval systems}, \markbox{12502}{especially} \markbox{12503}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:HHS to HFI}
Let \markbox{m12504}{$R>0$}, \markbox{m12505}{$r_1 > R_1=R_1(R,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{12506}{as} \markbox{12507}{in} \markbox{12508}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined} \markbox{12509}{and} \markbox{m12510}{$r_2 > R_2=R_2(R,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{12511}{as} \markbox{12512}{in} \markbox{12513}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.  \markbox{12514}{For} \markbox{12515}{any} \markbox{m12516}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{12517}{of} \markbox{12518}{an} \markbox{m12519}{$R$}-interval \markbox{12520}{system} \markbox{12521}{for} \markbox{m12522}{$a,b \in \calX$}, \markbox{12523}{the} \markbox{12524}{associated} \markbox{12525}{family} \markbox{12526}{of} \markbox{12527}{collapsed} \markbox{12528}{intervals} \markbox{12529}{and} \markbox{12530}{their} \markbox{12531}{collapsed} \markbox{12532}{projections} \markbox{12533}{form} \markbox{12534}{a} \markbox{12535}{hierarchical} \markbox{12536}{family} \markbox{12537}{of} intervals.
\end{lemma}

As \markbox{12538}{above} \markbox{12539}{in} \markbox{12540}{Definition} \ref{defn:Q defined}, \markbox{12541}{we} \markbox{12542}{can} \markbox{12543}{define} \markbox{12544}{a} \markbox{m12545}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{12546}{subset} \markbox{12547}{of} \markbox{12548}{the} \markbox{12549}{product} \markbox{m12550}{$\prod_U \hT_U$}.  \markbox{12551}{Our} \markbox{12552}{next} \markbox{12553}{goal} \markbox{12554}{is} \markbox{12555}{the} \markbox{12556}{following} theorem:

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:Q CCC}
The \markbox{m12557}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{12558}{subset} \markbox{12559}{of} \markbox{12560}{an} \markbox{12561}{HFI} \markbox{12562}{is} \markbox{12563}{a} \markbox{12564}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12565}{cube} \markbox{12566}{complex.}  \markbox{12567}{Moreover,} \markbox{12568}{there} \markbox{12569}{is} \markbox{12570}{a} \markbox{12571}{bijective} \markbox{12572}{correspondence} \markbox{12573}{between} \markbox{12574}{its} \markbox{12575}{hyperplanes} \markbox{12576}{and} \markbox{12577}{the} \markbox{12578}{edges} \markbox{12579}{of} \markbox{12580}{the} \markbox{12581}{factors.} 
\end{theorem}
    

\subsection{Median graphs and dual cube complexes}

The \markbox{12582}{proof} \markbox{12583}{of} \markbox{12584}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC} \markbox{12585}{that} \markbox{12586}{we} \markbox{12587}{give} \markbox{12588}{here} \markbox{12589}{will} \markbox{12590}{use} \markbox{12591}{the} \markbox{12592}{notion} \markbox{12593}{of} \markbox{12594}{median} \markbox{12595}{spaces.}  \markbox{12596}{The} \markbox{12597}{connection} \markbox{12598}{between} \markbox{12599}{median} \markbox{12600}{graphs} \markbox{12601}{and} \markbox{12602}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12603}{cube} \markbox{12604}{complexes} \markbox{12605}{goes} \markbox{12606}{back} \markbox{12607}{to} Roller's \cite{Roller} \markbox{12608}{reframing} \markbox{12609}{of} Sageev's \markbox{12610}{construction} \cite{Sageev:cubulation}, \markbox{12611}{see} \markbox{12612}{also} \cite{CN05, Nica}.  \markbox{12613}{Notably,} \markbox{12614}{Chepoi} \cite[Theorem 6.1]{Che00} \markbox{12615}{showed} \markbox{12616}{that} \markbox{12617}{every} \markbox{12618}{median} \markbox{12619}{graph} \markbox{12620}{is} \markbox{12621}{the} \markbox{m12622}{$1$}-skeleton \markbox{12623}{of} \markbox{12624}{a} \markbox{12625}{unique} \markbox{12626}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12627}{cube} \markbox{12628}{complex.}  \markbox{12629}{Bowditch} \markbox{12630}{explains} \markbox{12631}{these} \markbox{12632}{connections} \markbox{12633}{in} \markbox{12634}{detail} \markbox{12635}{in} \cite[Section 11]{bowditch2022median}.

Let \markbox{m12636}{$X$} \markbox{12637}{be} \markbox{12638}{a} \markbox{12639}{space} \markbox{12640}{and} \markbox{m12641}{$\mm:X^3\to X$} \markbox{12642}{a} \markbox{12643}{ternary} \markbox{12644}{operator.}  \markbox{12645}{We} \markbox{12646}{call} \markbox{m12647}{$(X,\mm)$} \markbox{12648}{a} \emph{median algebra} \markbox{12649}{if} \markbox{12650}{for} \markbox{12651}{all} \markbox{m12652}{$a,b,c,d,e \in X$} \markbox{12653}{we} have
$$\mm(a,b,c) = \mm(b,a,c) = \mm(c,a,b), \hspace{.1in} \mm(a,a,b) = a, \hspace{.1in} \mm(a,b,\mm(c,d,e)) = \mm(\mm(a,b,c),\mm(a,b,d),e).$$


A \markbox{12654}{graph} \markbox{m12655}{$\Gamma$} \markbox{12656}{is} \emph{median} \markbox{12657}{if} \markbox{12658}{all} \markbox{12659}{choices} \markbox{12660}{of} \markbox{m12661}{$v_1,v_2,v_3 \in \Gamma^{(0)}$}, \markbox{12662}{there} \markbox{12663}{exists} \markbox{12664}{a} \markbox{12665}{unique} \markbox{12666}{point} \markbox{12667}{lying} \markbox{12668}{on} \markbox{12669}{some} \markbox{12670}{geodesic} \markbox{12671}{from} \markbox{m12672}{$v_i,v_j$} \markbox{12673}{for} \markbox{12674}{all} \markbox{m12675}{$i,j$}; \markbox{12676}{then} \markbox{m12677}{$\mm(v_1,v_2,v_3)$} \markbox{12678}{is} \markbox{12679}{that} \markbox{12680}{unique} point.

Given \markbox{m12681}{$a,b \in X$}, \markbox{12682}{the} \markbox{12683}{(median)} \emph{interval} \markbox{12684}{between} \markbox{m12685}{$a,b$} \markbox{12686}{is} \markbox{m12687}{$I(a,b) = \{x \in X| \hspace{.01in} \mm(a,x,b) = x\}$}.  \markbox{12688}{We} \markbox{12689}{say} \markbox{12690}{a} \markbox{12691}{median} \markbox{12692}{algebra} \markbox{m12693}{$(X, \mm)$} \markbox{12694}{is} \emph{discrete} \markbox{12695}{when} \markbox{m12696}{$I(a,b)$} \markbox{12697}{is} \markbox{12698}{finite} \markbox{12699}{for} \markbox{12700}{every} \markbox{m12701}{$a,b \in X$}.  \markbox{12702}{A} \emph{subalgebra} \markbox{12703}{is} \markbox{12704}{a} \markbox{12705}{subset} \markbox{m12706}{$S \subset X$} \markbox{12707}{which} \markbox{12708}{is} \markbox{12709}{closed} \markbox{12710}{under} \markbox{m12711}{$\mm$}.  \markbox{12712}{In} \markbox{12713}{particular,} \markbox{12714}{locally} \markbox{12715}{finite} \markbox{12716}{median} \markbox{12717}{graphs} \markbox{12718}{are} \markbox{12719}{discrete} \markbox{12720}{median} algebras.


Every \markbox{12721}{median} \markbox{12722}{algebra} \markbox{m12723}{$(X,\mm)$} \markbox{12724}{determines} \markbox{12725}{a} \markbox{12726}{graph} \markbox{12727}{called} \markbox{12728}{its} \emph{adjacency graph} \markbox{m12729}{$\Gamma(X)$} \markbox{12730}{as} \markbox{12731}{follows.}  \markbox{12732}{We} \markbox{12733}{say} \markbox{12734}{that} \markbox{m12735}{$a,b \in X$} \markbox{12736}{are} \emph{adjacent} \markbox{12737}{when} \markbox{m12738}{$I(a,b) = \emptyset$}.  \markbox{12739}{The} \markbox{12740}{vertices} \markbox{12741}{of} \markbox{m12742}{$\Gamma(X)$} \markbox{12743}{are} \markbox{12744}{the} \markbox{12745}{points} \markbox{12746}{of} \markbox{m12747}{$X$}, \markbox{12748}{with} \markbox{m12749}{$a,b \in X$} \markbox{12750}{connected} \markbox{12751}{by} \markbox{12752}{an} \markbox{12753}{edge} \markbox{12754}{in} \markbox{m12755}{$\Gamma(X)$} \markbox{12756}{exactly} \markbox{12757}{when} \markbox{m12758}{$a,b$} \markbox{12759}{are} \markbox{12760}{adjacent.}  \markbox{12761}{This} \markbox{12762}{graph} \markbox{12763}{is} \markbox{12764}{median} \markbox{12765}{exactly} \markbox{12766}{when} \markbox{m12767}{$(X,\mm)$} \markbox{12768}{is} \markbox{12769}{a} \markbox{12770}{discrete} \markbox{12771}{median} \markbox{12772}{algebra} \cite[Lemma 16.1.2]{bowditch2022median}.

Every \markbox{12773}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12774}{cube} \markbox{12775}{complex} \markbox{m12776}{$X$} \markbox{12777}{admits} \markbox{12778}{a} \markbox{12779}{canonical} \markbox{12780}{median} \markbox{12781}{structure} \markbox{12782}{as} \markbox{12783}{follows.}  \markbox{12784}{For} \markbox{12785}{any} \markbox{m12786}{$a,b \in X^{(0)}$}, \markbox{12787}{let} \markbox{m12788}{$J(a,b)$} \markbox{12789}{denote} \markbox{12790}{the} \markbox{12791}{set} \markbox{12792}{of} \markbox{m12793}{$\ell^1$}-geodesics \markbox{12794}{between} \markbox{m12795}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{12796}{Then} \markbox{12797}{given} \markbox{m12798}{$a,b,c \in X^{(0)}$}, \markbox{12799}{we} \markbox{12800}{have} \markbox{m12801}{$\mm(a,b,c) = J(a,b) \cap J(a,c) \cap J(b,c)$} \markbox{12802}{is} \markbox{12803}{a} \markbox{12804}{single} \markbox{12805}{point,} \markbox{12806}{and} \markbox{m12807}{$(X, \mm)$} \markbox{12808}{is} \markbox{12809}{a} \markbox{12810}{median} \markbox{12811}{structure} \markbox{12812}{with} \markbox{m12813}{$X^{(1)}$} \markbox{12814}{a} \markbox{12815}{median} \markbox{12816}{graph,} \markbox{12817}{with} \markbox{12818}{notably} \markbox{m12819}{$J(a,b) = I(a,b)$} \markbox{12820}{for} \markbox{12821}{all} \markbox{m12822}{$a, b \in X^{(0)}$}.  \markbox{12823}{Moreover,} \markbox{12824}{it} \markbox{12825}{is} \markbox{12826}{immediate} \markbox{12827}{that} \markbox{m12828}{$X^{(1)} = \Gamma(X^{(0)})$}, \markbox{12829}{since} \markbox{12830}{median} \markbox{12831}{adjacent} \markbox{12832}{vertices} \markbox{12833}{in} \markbox{m12834}{$X^{(0)}$} \markbox{12835}{are} \markbox{12836}{exactly} \markbox{12837}{those} \markbox{12838}{spanning} \markbox{12839}{an} \markbox{12840}{edge} \markbox{12841}{in} \markbox{m12842}{$X^{(1)}$}.

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{12843}{of} \markbox{12844}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC}]
   \markbox{12845}{First,} \markbox{12846}{observe} \markbox{12847}{that} \markbox{m12848}{$\calY = \prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U$} \markbox{12849}{is} \markbox{12850}{a} \markbox{12851}{product} \markbox{12852}{of} \markbox{12853}{simplicial} \markbox{12854}{trees} \markbox{12855}{and} \markbox{12856}{hence} \markbox{12857}{a} \markbox{12858}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12859}{cube} complex.
   
   \markbox{12860}{Next,} \markbox{12861}{observe} \markbox{12862}{that} \markbox{m12863}{$\calQ \subset \calY$} \markbox{12864}{is} \markbox{12865}{a} \markbox{12866}{cubical} \markbox{12867}{subcomplex} \markbox{12868}{as} \markbox{12869}{follows.}  \markbox{12870}{For} \markbox{12871}{any} \markbox{m12872}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{12873}{let} \markbox{m12874}{$C \subset \calY$} \markbox{12875}{be} \markbox{12876}{the} \markbox{12877}{minimal} \markbox{12878}{cube} \markbox{12879}{containing} \markbox{m12880}{$\hx$} \markbox{12881}{in} \markbox{12882}{its} \markbox{12883}{interior.}  \markbox{12884}{Presuming} \markbox{m12885}{$C$} \markbox{12886}{is} \markbox{12887}{not} \markbox{12888}{a} \markbox{12889}{vertex,} \markbox{12890}{minimality} \markbox{12891}{says} \markbox{12892}{that} \markbox{m12893}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{12894}{is} \markbox{12895}{in} \markbox{12896}{the} \markbox{12897}{interior} \markbox{12898}{of} \markbox{12899}{an} \markbox{12900}{edge} \markbox{12901}{in} \markbox{12902}{each} \markbox{12903}{of} \markbox{12904}{the} \markbox{12905}{defining} \markbox{12906}{coordinate} \markbox{12907}{intervals} \markbox{12908}{of} \markbox{m12909}{$C$}, \markbox{12910}{whose} \markbox{12911}{domain} \markbox{12912}{labels} \markbox{12913}{are} \markbox{12914}{pairwise} \markbox{12915}{orthogonal} \markbox{12916}{by} \markbox{12917}{item} \markbox{12918}{(9)} \markbox{12919}{of} \markbox{12920}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.  \markbox{12921}{This} \markbox{12922}{means} \markbox{12923}{that} \markbox{12924}{we} \markbox{12925}{can} \markbox{12926}{freely} \markbox{12927}{alter} \markbox{12928}{those} \markbox{12929}{coordinates} \markbox{12930}{of} \markbox{m12931}{$\hx$} \markbox{12932}{to} \markbox{12933}{be} \markbox{12934}{any} \markbox{12935}{choice} \markbox{12936}{of} \markbox{12937}{points} \markbox{12938}{in} \markbox{12939}{those} \markbox{12940}{edges,} \markbox{12941}{meaning} \markbox{m12942}{$C \subset \calQ$}.  \markbox{12943}{Hence} \markbox{m12944}{$\calQ$} \markbox{12945}{is} \markbox{12946}{a} \markbox{12947}{cubical} \markbox{12948}{subcomplex} \markbox{12949}{of} \markbox{m12950}{$\calY$}.

   \markbox{12951}{It} \markbox{12952}{is} \markbox{12953}{enough} \markbox{12954}{then} \markbox{12955}{to} \markbox{12956}{show} \markbox{12957}{that} \markbox{m12958}{$\calQ^{(0)} \subset \calY$} \markbox{12959}{is} \markbox{12960}{a} \markbox{12961}{discrete} \markbox{12962}{median} \markbox{12963}{subalgebra.}  \markbox{12964}{For} \markbox{12965}{once} \markbox{12966}{that} \markbox{12967}{is} \markbox{12968}{done,} \markbox{12969}{it} \markbox{12970}{will} \markbox{12971}{follow} \markbox{12972}{that} \markbox{m12973}{$\Gamma(\calQ)$} \markbox{12974}{is} \markbox{12975}{a} \markbox{12976}{median} \markbox{12977}{graph,} \markbox{12978}{but} \markbox{12979}{evidently} \markbox{m12980}{$\Gamma(\calQ) = \calQ^{(1)}$}, \markbox{12981}{as} \markbox{m12982}{$\calQ$} \markbox{12983}{is} \markbox{12984}{a} \markbox{12985}{cubical} \markbox{12986}{subcomplex} \markbox{12987}{of} \markbox{m12988}{$\calY$}.  \markbox{12989}{Since} \markbox{12990}{every} \markbox{12991}{median} \markbox{12992}{graph} \markbox{12993}{is} \markbox{12994}{the} \markbox{m12995}{$1$}-skeleton \markbox{12996}{of} \markbox{12997}{a} \markbox{12998}{unique} \markbox{12999}{CAT(0)} \markbox{13000}{cube} \markbox{13001}{complex} \cite[Theorem 6.1]{Che00}, \markbox{13002}{it} \markbox{13003}{follows} \markbox{13004}{that} \markbox{m13005}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13006}{must} \markbox{13007}{be} \markbox{13008}{that} \markbox{13009}{cube} \markbox{13010}{complex,} \markbox{13011}{completing} \markbox{13012}{the} proof.

   \markbox{13013}{The} \markbox{13014}{claim} \markbox{13015}{boils} \markbox{13016}{down} \markbox{13017}{to} \markbox{13018}{three} \markbox{13019}{exercises} \markbox{13020}{that} \markbox{13021}{we} \markbox{13022}{leave} \markbox{13023}{for} \markbox{13024}{the} reader:
   \begin{itemize}
       \item Any \markbox{13025}{(finite)} \markbox{13026}{product} \markbox{13027}{of} \markbox{13028}{median} \markbox{13029}{spaces} \markbox{13030}{admits} \markbox{13031}{the} \markbox{13032}{structure} \markbox{13033}{of} \markbox{13034}{a} \markbox{13035}{median} \markbox{13036}{space,} \markbox{13037}{where} \markbox{13038}{the} \markbox{13039}{median} \markbox{13040}{on} \markbox{13041}{the} \markbox{13042}{product} \markbox{13043}{is} \markbox{13044}{the} \markbox{13045}{tuple} \markbox{13046}{of} \markbox{13047}{medians} \markbox{13048}{in} \markbox{13049}{the} coordinates.
       \item For \markbox{13050}{any} \markbox{m13051}{$\ha,\hb,\hc \in \calQ^{(0)}$}, \markbox{13052}{we} \markbox{13053}{have} \markbox{m13054}{$\left(\mm_U(\ha_U,\hb_U,\hc_U)\right)_U \in \calQ$}.  \markbox{13055}{This} \markbox{13056}{can} \markbox{13057}{be} \markbox{13058}{proven} \markbox{13059}{using} \markbox{13060}{a} \markbox{13061}{basic} \markbox{13062}{consistency} \markbox{13063}{argument} \markbox{13064}{(see} \cite[Lemma 15.12]{Dur_infcube}).
       \item With \markbox{13065}{this} \markbox{13066}{median} \markbox{13067}{structure,} \markbox{m13068}{$a,b \in \calQ^{(0)}$} \markbox{13069}{are} \markbox{13070}{median} \markbox{13071}{adjacent} \markbox{13072}{exactly} \markbox{13073}{when} \markbox{13074}{they} \markbox{13075}{span} \markbox{13076}{an} \markbox{13077}{edge} \markbox{13078}{in} \markbox{m13079}{$\calQ^{(1)}$}.
   \end{itemize}

   \markbox{13080}{Finally,} \markbox{13081}{observe} \markbox{13082}{that} \markbox{13083}{the} \markbox{13084}{hyperplanes} \markbox{13085}{of} \markbox{m13086}{$\calY$} \markbox{13087}{are} \markbox{13088}{of} \markbox{13089}{the} \markbox{13090}{form} \markbox{m13091}{$\hh \times \prod_{V\neq U} \hT_V$} \markbox{13092}{for} \markbox{m13093}{$\hh$} \markbox{13094}{some} \markbox{13095}{hyperplane} \markbox{13096}{in} \markbox{m13097}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{13098}{Since} \markbox{m13099}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13100}{is} \markbox{13101}{a} \markbox{13102}{median} \markbox{13103}{subalgebra} \markbox{13104}{of} \markbox{m13105}{$\calY$}, \markbox{13106}{the} \markbox{13107}{hyperplanes} \markbox{13108}{of} \markbox{m13109}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13110}{are} \markbox{13111}{just} \markbox{13112}{hyperplanes} \markbox{13113}{of} \markbox{m13114}{$\calY$} \markbox{13115}{intersected} \markbox{13116}{with} \markbox{m13117}{$\calQ$}, \markbox{13118}{so} \markbox{13119}{the} \markbox{13120}{moreover} \markbox{13121}{statement} \markbox{13122}{follows.}  \markbox{13123}{This} \markbox{13124}{completes} \markbox{13125}{the} proof.
\end{proof}














\subsection{More tree trimming and hyperplane deletions}\label{subsec:tt cube}


In \markbox{13126}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tree trimming}, \markbox{13127}{we} \markbox{13128}{introduced} \markbox{13129}{our} \markbox{13130}{tree} \markbox{13131}{trimming} \markbox{13132}{techniques,} \markbox{13133}{which} \markbox{13134}{allowed} \markbox{13135}{us} \markbox{13136}{to} \markbox{13137}{take} \markbox{13138}{a} \markbox{13139}{family} \markbox{13140}{of} \markbox{13141}{collapsed} \markbox{13142}{intervals} \markbox{13143}{and} \markbox{13144}{collapse} \markbox{13145}{a} \markbox{13146}{further} \markbox{13147}{family} \markbox{13148}{of} \markbox{13149}{subintervals} \markbox{13150}{while} \markbox{13151}{maintaining} \markbox{13152}{control} \markbox{13153}{over} \markbox{13154}{their} \markbox{13155}{associated} \markbox{m13156}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{13157}{subsets.}  \markbox{13158}{In} \markbox{13159}{this} \markbox{13160}{subsection,} \markbox{13161}{we} \markbox{13162}{need} \markbox{13163}{a} \markbox{13164}{further} \markbox{13165}{refinement} \markbox{13166}{applied} \markbox{13167}{to} \markbox{13168}{HFIs} \markbox{13169}{and} \markbox{13170}{their} \markbox{13171}{associated} \markbox{13172}{cube} complexes.

To \markbox{13173}{set} \markbox{13174}{up} \markbox{13175}{the} \markbox{13176}{statement,} \markbox{13177}{let} \markbox{m13178}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13179}{be} \markbox{13180}{a} \markbox{13181}{hierarchical} \markbox{13182}{family} \markbox{13183}{of} \markbox{13184}{intervals,} \markbox{13185}{as} \markbox{13186}{in} \markbox{13187}{Definition} \ref{defn:HFI}.  \markbox{13188}{Fix} \markbox{13189}{a} \markbox{13190}{constant} \markbox{m13191}{$B>0$}, \markbox{13192}{which} \markbox{13193}{will} \markbox{13194}{control} \markbox{13195}{the} \markbox{13196}{size} \markbox{13197}{and} \markbox{13198}{number} \markbox{13199}{of} \markbox{13200}{subintervals} \markbox{13201}{we} \markbox{13202}{will} \markbox{13203}{collapse} \markbox{13204}{across} \markbox{13205}{all} \markbox{13206}{of} \markbox{13207}{the} \markbox{13208}{intervals.}  \markbox{13209}{In} \markbox{13210}{our} \markbox{13211}{applications,} \markbox{13212}{we} \markbox{13213}{will} \markbox{13214}{be} \markbox{13215}{able} \markbox{13216}{to} \markbox{13217}{control} \markbox{13218}{the} \markbox{13219}{size} \markbox{13220}{of} \markbox{m13221}{$B$}, \markbox{13222}{but} \markbox{13223}{notably} \markbox{13224}{not} \markbox{13225}{with} \markbox{13226}{respect} \markbox{13227}{to} \markbox{13228}{the} \markbox{13229}{largeness} \markbox{13230}{constant} \markbox{m13231}{$K$}, \markbox{13232}{unlike} \markbox{13233}{in} \markbox{13234}{the} \markbox{13235}{statement} \markbox{13236}{of} \markbox{13237}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}.

\begin{definition}[Admissible \markbox{13238}{simplicial} \markbox{13239}{trimming} setup]\label{defn:simplicial trimming setup}
Given \markbox{m13240}{$B>0$}, \markbox{13241}{a} \markbox{m13242}{$B$}-\emph{admissible simplicial trimming setup} \markbox{13243}{is} \markbox{13244}{a} \markbox{13245}{collection} \markbox{13246}{of} \emph{trimming intervals} \markbox{m13247}{$\calB$} \markbox{13248}{in} \markbox{13249}{the} \markbox{13250}{various} \markbox{m13251}{$\hT_{U,e}$} \markbox{13252}{satisfying} \markbox{13253}{the} following:
\begin{enumerate}
\item For \markbox{13254}{each} \markbox{m13255}{$D \in \calB$} \markbox{13256}{with} \markbox{m13257}{$D \subset E \in \pi_0(\hT_{U,e})$}, \markbox{13258}{we} \markbox{13259}{have} \label{item:trimming integer}
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m13260}{$D$} \markbox{13261}{is} \markbox{13262}{a} \markbox{13263}{subinterval} \markbox{13264}{of} \markbox{m13265}{$E$} \markbox{13266}{with} \markbox{13267}{endpoints} \markbox{13268}{at} \markbox{13269}{vertices,} and
\item the \markbox{13270}{length} \markbox{m13271}{$l(D)$} \markbox{13272}{of} \markbox{m13273}{$D$} \markbox{13274}{is} \markbox{13275}{a} \markbox{13276}{positive} \markbox{13277}{integer} \markbox{13278}{whose} \markbox{13279}{length} \markbox{13280}{is} \markbox{13281}{bounded} \markbox{13282}{above} \markbox{13283}{by} \markbox{m13284}{$B$}.
\end{enumerate}
\item The \markbox{13285}{number} \markbox{13286}{of} \markbox{13287}{subintervals} \markbox{13288}{in} \markbox{m13289}{$\calB$} \markbox{13290}{is} \markbox{13291}{bounded} \markbox{13292}{by} \markbox{m13293}{$B$}, \markbox{13294}{that} \markbox{13295}{is} \markbox{m13296}{$\#\calB < B$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}
We \markbox{13297}{note} \markbox{13298}{that} \markbox{13299}{the} \markbox{13300}{conditions} \markbox{13301}{in} \markbox{13302}{Definition} \ref{defn:simplicial trimming setup} \markbox{13303}{guarantee} \markbox{13304}{that} \markbox{13305}{each} \markbox{13306}{quotient} \markbox{13307}{interval} \markbox{m13308}{$\hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{13309}{is} \markbox{13310}{a} \markbox{13311}{simplicial} \markbox{13312}{interval} \markbox{13313}{of} \markbox{13314}{the} \markbox{13315}{usual} \markbox{13316}{type} \markbox{13317}{we} \markbox{13318}{consider.}  \markbox{13319}{The} \markbox{13320}{requirement} \markbox{13321}{that} \markbox{13322}{each} \markbox{13323}{segment} \markbox{m13324}{$D \in \calB$} \markbox{13325}{has} \markbox{13326}{endpoints} \markbox{13327}{at} \markbox{13328}{vertices} \markbox{13329}{guarantees} \markbox{13330}{that} \markbox{13331}{when} \markbox{13332}{we} \markbox{13333}{collapse} \markbox{13334}{such} \markbox{13335}{a} \markbox{13336}{segment,} \markbox{13337}{then} \markbox{13338}{it} \markbox{13339}{only} \markbox{13340}{affects} \markbox{13341}{the} \markbox{13342}{interval-hyperplanes} \markbox{13343}{it} \markbox{13344}{contains,} \markbox{13345}{preserving} \markbox{13346}{those} \markbox{13347}{in} \markbox{13348}{its} complement.
\end{remark}

We \markbox{13349}{use} \markbox{13350}{the} \markbox{13351}{same} \markbox{13352}{associated} \markbox{13353}{notation} \markbox{13354}{as} \markbox{13355}{in} \markbox{13356}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tree trimming}.  \markbox{13357}{Furthermore,} \markbox{13358}{we} \markbox{13359}{note} \markbox{13360}{that} \markbox{13361}{if} \markbox{m13362}{$\hT^e_U \subset \calB$}, \markbox{13363}{then} \markbox{m13364}{$\diam (\hT_U) < B^2$} \markbox{13365}{and} \markbox{m13366}{$\hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{13367}{is} \markbox{13368}{a} \markbox{13369}{point.}  \markbox{13370}{Let} \markbox{m13371}{$\calU_0 \subset \calU$} \markbox{13372}{denote} \markbox{13373}{the} \markbox{13374}{subset} \markbox{13375}{of} \markbox{13376}{domains} \markbox{13377}{for} \markbox{13378}{which} \markbox{m13379}{$\hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{13380}{is} \markbox{13381}{not} \markbox{13382}{a} \markbox{13383}{point.}  \markbox{13384}{By} \markbox{13385}{ignoring} \markbox{13386}{the} \markbox{13387}{domains} \markbox{13388}{in} \markbox{m13389}{$\calU - \calU_0$}, \markbox{13390}{we} \markbox{13391}{can} \markbox{13392}{consider} \markbox{13393}{the} \markbox{13394}{set} \markbox{13395}{of} \markbox{13396}{collapsed} \markbox{13397}{intervals} \markbox{m13398}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$}, \markbox{13399}{where} \markbox{13400}{we} \markbox{13401}{remove} \markbox{13402}{any} \markbox{13403}{labels} \markbox{m13404}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{13405}{from} \markbox{m13406}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{13407}{from} \markbox{13408}{any} \markbox{13409}{domain} \markbox{m13410}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{13411}{with} \markbox{m13412}{$V \in \calU - \calU_0$}.

The \markbox{13413}{following} \markbox{13414}{theorem} \markbox{13415}{expands} \markbox{13416}{on} \markbox{13417}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{13418}{in} \markbox{13419}{the} \markbox{13420}{HFI} setting:

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:simplicial tree trimming}
Let \markbox{m13421}{$B>0$} \markbox{13422}{and} \markbox{m13423}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13424}{be} \markbox{13425}{an} \markbox{13426}{HFI.}  \markbox{13427}{For} \markbox{13428}{any} \markbox{m13429}{$B$}-admissible \markbox{13430}{simplicial} \markbox{13431}{trimming} \markbox{13432}{setup} \markbox{m13433}{$\calB$}, \markbox{13434}{the} \markbox{13435}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item The \markbox{13436}{collections} \markbox{m13437}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13438}{and} \markbox{m13439}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{13440}{are} \markbox{13441}{HFIs.}  \markbox{13442}{We} \markbox{13443}{let} \markbox{m13444}{$\calQ', \calQ_0$} \markbox{13445}{denote} \markbox{13446}{their} \markbox{13447}{corresponding} \markbox{m13448}{$0$}-consistent subsets.
\item We \markbox{13449}{have} \markbox{m13450}{$\Delta(\calQ) = \calQ'$}, \markbox{13451}{where} \markbox{m13452}{$\Delta:\prod_U \hT_U \to \prod_U \hT'_U$} \markbox{13453}{is} \markbox{13454}{the} \markbox{13455}{global} \markbox{13456}{collapsing} map.
\item There \markbox{13457}{exists} \markbox{13458}{a} \markbox{13459}{map} \markbox{m13460}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{13461}{with} \markbox{m13462}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ'}$}.
\item The \markbox{13463}{map} \markbox{m13464}{$\Delta|_{\calQ}: \calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{13465}{is} \markbox{13466}{a} \markbox{m13467}{$(1, B^2)$}-quasi-isometry.
\item At \markbox{13468}{the} \markbox{13469}{level} \markbox{13470}{of} \markbox{13471}{cube} \markbox{13472}{complexes,} \markbox{13473}{the} \markbox{13474}{map} \markbox{m13475}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{13476}{is} \markbox{13477}{a} \markbox{13478}{hyperplane} \markbox{13479}{deletion} \markbox{13480}{map} \markbox{13481}{deleting} \markbox{13482}{at} \markbox{13483}{most} \markbox{m13484}{$B^2$}-many hyperplanes.
\end{enumerate}

\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
Item \markbox{13485}{(1)} \markbox{13486}{is} \markbox{13487}{straightforward,} \markbox{13488}{since} \markbox{13489}{we} \markbox{13490}{are} \markbox{13491}{just} \markbox{13492}{collapsing} \markbox{13493}{simplicial} \markbox{13494}{subintervals.}  \markbox{13495}{Items} \markbox{13496}{(2)--(3)} \markbox{13497}{follow} \markbox{13498}{from} \markbox{13499}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}, \markbox{13500}{where} \markbox{13501}{in} \markbox{13502}{the} \markbox{13503}{argument} \markbox{13504}{we} \markbox{13505}{just} \markbox{13506}{replace} \markbox{13507}{the} \markbox{13508}{HFI} \markbox{13509}{axioms} \markbox{13510}{(Definition} \ref{defn:HFI}) \markbox{13511}{with} \markbox{13512}{the} \markbox{13513}{appropriate} \markbox{13514}{properties} \markbox{13515}{from} \markbox{13516}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.  \markbox{13517}{The} \markbox{13518}{fact} \markbox{13519}{that} \markbox{m13520}{$\Delta$} \markbox{13521}{deletes} \markbox{13522}{at} \markbox{13523}{most} \markbox{m13524}{$B^2$}-many \markbox{13525}{hyperplanes} \markbox{13526}{from} \markbox{m13527}{$\prod_U \hT_U$}, \markbox{13528}{so} \markbox{13529}{item} \markbox{13530}{(5)} \markbox{13531}{follows} \markbox{13532}{from} \markbox{13533}{the} ``moreover'' \markbox{13534}{part} \markbox{13535}{of} \markbox{13536}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC}.  \markbox{13537}{Finally,} \markbox{13538}{item} \markbox{13539}{(4)} \markbox{13540}{follows} \markbox{13541}{immediately} \markbox{13542}{from} \markbox{13543}{item} \markbox{13544}{(5).}  \markbox{13545}{This} \markbox{13546}{completes} \markbox{13547}{the} proof.


\end{proof}







\subsection{Hierarchy paths and the distance formula}\label{subsec:HP and DF}

With \markbox{13548}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC} \markbox{13549}{in} \markbox{13550}{hand,} \markbox{13551}{we} \markbox{13552}{can} \markbox{13553}{make} \markbox{13554}{some} \markbox{13555}{observations} \markbox{13556}{about} \markbox{13557}{the} \markbox{13558}{cubical} \markbox{13559}{structure} \markbox{13560}{of} \markbox{m13561}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13562}{and} \markbox{13563}{how} \markbox{13564}{it} \markbox{13565}{relates} \markbox{13566}{to} \markbox{13567}{its} \markbox{13568}{hierarchical} \markbox{13569}{nature.}  \markbox{13570}{In} \markbox{13571}{particular,} \markbox{13572}{we} \markbox{13573}{get} \markbox{13574}{a} \markbox{13575}{proof} \markbox{13576}{of} \markbox{13577}{the} \markbox{13578}{(more} \markbox{13579}{difficult)} \markbox{13580}{lower} \markbox{13581}{bound} \markbox{13582}{of} \markbox{13583}{the} \markbox{13584}{Distance} \markbox{13585}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF} \markbox{13586}{and} \markbox{13587}{the} \markbox{13588}{existence} \markbox{13589}{of} \markbox{13590}{hierarchy} paths.

The \markbox{13591}{following} \markbox{13592}{lemma} \markbox{13593}{is} \cite[Lemma 14.7]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{13594}{and} \markbox{13595}{we} \markbox{13596}{have} \markbox{13597}{included} \markbox{13598}{its} \markbox{13599}{proof} \markbox{13600}{here} \markbox{13601}{for} completeness.


\begin{lemma}\label{lem:NR hp in Q}
Let \markbox{m13602}{$\hx,\hy \in \calQ$}.  \markbox{13603}{Let} \markbox{m13604}{$\gamma$} \markbox{13605}{be} \markbox{13606}{any} \markbox{13607}{combinatorial} \markbox{13608}{geodesic} \markbox{13609}{in} \markbox{m13610}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13611}{from} \markbox{m13612}{$\hx$} \markbox{13613}{to} \markbox{m13614}{$\hy$}.  \markbox{13615}{Then} \markbox{13616}{for} \markbox{13617}{all} \markbox{m13618}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{13619}{the} \markbox{13620}{projection} \markbox{m13621}{$\hpi_U(\gamma) \subset \hT_U$} \markbox{13622}{is} \markbox{13623}{an} \markbox{13624}{unparameterized} \markbox{13625}{geodesic} \markbox{13626}{between} \markbox{m13627}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{13628}{and} \markbox{m13629}{$\hy_U$}.
\end{lemma} 

\begin{proof}
Since \markbox{13630}{combinatorial} \markbox{13631}{geodesics} \markbox{13632}{do} \markbox{13633}{not} \markbox{13634}{cross} \markbox{13635}{a} \markbox{13636}{hyperplane} \markbox{13637}{twice} \markbox{13638}{and} \markbox{13639}{the} \markbox{13640}{restriction} \markbox{13641}{quotient} \markbox{m13642}{$\hpi_U:\calQ \to \hT_U$} \markbox{13643}{is} \markbox{m13644}{$1$}-Lipschitz, \markbox{13645}{it} \markbox{13646}{follows} \markbox{13647}{that} \markbox{m13648}{$\hpi_U(\gamma)$} \markbox{13649}{does} \markbox{13650}{not} \markbox{13651}{backtrack} \markbox{13652}{either.}  \markbox{13653}{This} \markbox{13654}{completes} \markbox{13655}{the} proof.





\end{proof}

This \markbox{13656}{lemma} \markbox{13657}{plays} \markbox{13658}{two} \markbox{13659}{roles:} it's \markbox{13660}{useful} \markbox{13661}{for} \markbox{13662}{proving} \markbox{13663}{that} \markbox{13664}{an} \markbox{13665}{isomorphism} \markbox{13666}{of} \markbox{13667}{HFIs} \markbox{13668}{induces} \markbox{13669}{an} \markbox{13670}{isomorphism} \markbox{13671}{of} \markbox{13672}{their} \markbox{13673}{cubical} \markbox{13674}{duals} \markbox{13675}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:HFI isomorphism}), \markbox{13676}{and,} \markbox{13677}{in} \markbox{13678}{the} \markbox{13679}{next} \markbox{13680}{proposition,} \markbox{13681}{we} \markbox{13682}{use} \markbox{13683}{it} \markbox{13684}{directly} \markbox{13685}{to} \markbox{13686}{show} \markbox{13687}{that} \markbox{13688}{combinatorial} \markbox{13689}{geodesics} \markbox{13690}{in} \markbox{13691}{a} \markbox{13692}{cubical} \markbox{13693}{model} \markbox{13694}{get} \markbox{13695}{sent} \markbox{13696}{to} \markbox{13697}{hierarchy} \markbox{13698}{paths} \markbox{13699}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hp}) \markbox{13700}{in} \markbox{13701}{the} \markbox{13702}{ambient} \markbox{13703}{HHS.}  \markbox{13704}{That} \markbox{13705}{is} \markbox{13706}{the} \markbox{13707}{content} \markbox{13708}{of} \markbox{13709}{the} \markbox{13710}{next} \markbox{13711}{proposition,} \markbox{13712}{which} \markbox{13713}{is} \markbox{13714}{simplified} \markbox{13715}{version} \markbox{13716}{of} \cite[Proposition 14.8]{Dur_infcube}:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:cubical hp}
Let \markbox{m13717}{$a,b \in \calX$}, \markbox{m13718}{$K \geq K_0$} \markbox{13719}{where} \markbox{m13720}{$K_0 = K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{13721}{is} \markbox{13722}{from} \markbox{13723}{Theorem} \ref{thm:DF}, \markbox{m13724}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$}, \markbox{13725}{and} \markbox{13726}{let} \markbox{m13727}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}.  \markbox{13728}{Let} \markbox{m13729}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13730}{be} \markbox{13731}{any} \markbox{m13732}{$R$}-interval \markbox{13733}{system} \markbox{13734}{for} \markbox{m13735}{$a,b$} \markbox{13736}{and} \markbox{m13737}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13738}{the} \markbox{13739}{HFI} \markbox{13740}{associated} \markbox{13741}{to} \markbox{13742}{any} \markbox{m13743}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{13744}{for} \markbox{m13745}{$r_1 \geq R_1, r_2 \geq R_2$}  \markbox{13746}{with} \markbox{m13747}{$r_1$} \markbox{13748}{a} \markbox{13749}{positive} \markbox{13750}{integer.}  \markbox{13751}{Let} \markbox{m13752}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13753}{be} \markbox{13754}{the} \markbox{13755}{corresponding} \markbox{m13756}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{13757}{set} \markbox{13758}{and} \markbox{m13759}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{13760}{the} \markbox{13761}{quasi-isometry} \markbox{13762}{constructed} \markbox{13763}{in} \markbox{13764}{Section} \ref{sec:hPsi qi}.
\begin{itemize}
\item If \markbox{m13765}{$\ha, \hb$} \markbox{13766}{are} \markbox{13767}{the} \markbox{13768}{points} \markbox{m13769}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13770}{corresponding} \markbox{13771}{to} \markbox{m13772}{$a, b$} \markbox{13773}{and} \markbox{m13774}{$\gamma$} \markbox{13775}{is} \markbox{13776}{a} \markbox{13777}{combinatorial} \markbox{13778}{geodesic} \markbox{13779}{between} \markbox{13780}{them,} \markbox{13781}{then} \markbox{m13782}{$\hO(\gamma) \subset H$} \markbox{13783}{is} \markbox{13784}{an} \markbox{m13785}{$(L_{hp},L_{hp})$}-hierarchy \markbox{13786}{path} \markbox{13787}{between} \markbox{m13788}{$a,b$} \markbox{13789}{for} \markbox{m13790}{$L_{hp} = L_{hp}(R,r_1,r_2,K, \mathfrak S)>0$}.
\end{itemize} 
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
The \markbox{13791}{following} \markbox{13792}{is} \markbox{13793}{a} \markbox{13794}{fairly} \markbox{13795}{complete} \markbox{13796}{sketch} \markbox{13797}{of} \markbox{13798}{the} \markbox{13799}{proof,} \markbox{13800}{which} \markbox{13801}{is} \markbox{13802}{simpler} \markbox{13803}{than} \markbox{13804}{the} \markbox{13805}{more} \markbox{13806}{general} \markbox{13807}{version} \markbox{13808}{from} \cite[Proposition 14.8]{Dur_infcube}.

Since \markbox{13809}{the} \markbox{13810}{map} \markbox{m13811}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{13812}{is} \markbox{13813}{effectively} \markbox{13814}{defined} \markbox{13815}{coordinate-wise,} \markbox{13816}{its} \markbox{13817}{enough} \markbox{13818}{to} \markbox{13819}{consider} \markbox{13820}{the} \markbox{13821}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{13822}{maps} \markbox{m13823}{$B_U:\hT_U \to T_U$} \markbox{13824}{as} \markbox{13825}{described} \markbox{13826}{in} \markbox{13827}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:hO defined}, \markbox{13828}{as} \markbox{13829}{the} \markbox{13830}{map} \markbox{m13831}{$\phi_U:T_U\to \calC(U)$} \markbox{13832}{is} \markbox{13833}{an} \markbox{m13834}{$(R,R)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{13835}{embedding} \markbox{13836}{by} \markbox{13837}{assumption.}  \markbox{13838}{For} \markbox{13839}{this,} \markbox{13840}{we} \markbox{13841}{can} \markbox{13842}{let} \markbox{m13843}{$\gamma_U$} \markbox{13844}{denote} \markbox{13845}{the} \markbox{13846}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{13847}{projection} \markbox{13848}{of} \markbox{m13849}{$\gamma$} \markbox{13850}{to} \markbox{13851}{each} \markbox{m13852}{$\hT_U$}, \markbox{13853}{and} \markbox{13854}{we} \markbox{13855}{want} \markbox{13856}{to} \markbox{13857}{show} \markbox{13858}{that} \markbox{m13859}{$B_U(\gamma_U)$} \markbox{13860}{is} \markbox{13861}{an} \markbox{13862}{unparameterized} \markbox{13863}{quasi-geodesic} \markbox{13864}{in} \markbox{m13865}{$T_U$}.

By \markbox{13866}{construction,} \markbox{m13867}{$B_U(\gamma_U) \subset [a_U,b_U] = T_U$}, \markbox{13868}{so} \markbox{13869}{it} \markbox{13870}{suffices} \markbox{13871}{to} \markbox{13872}{show} \markbox{13873}{that} \markbox{13874}{this} \markbox{13875}{path} \markbox{13876}{never} \markbox{13877}{backtracks} \markbox{13878}{an} \markbox{13879}{unbounded} \markbox{13880}{amount.}  \markbox{13881}{Proceeding} \markbox{13882}{by} \markbox{13883}{induction} \markbox{13884}{in} \markbox{13885}{the} \markbox{m13886}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-level \markbox{13887}{in} \markbox{m13888}{$\calU$}, \markbox{13889}{if} \markbox{m13890}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{13891}{is} \markbox{m13892}{$\nest$}-minimal, \markbox{13893}{then} \markbox{13894}{the} \markbox{13895}{amount} \markbox{13896}{of} \markbox{13897}{collapsing} \markbox{13898}{in} \markbox{m13899}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{13900}{is} \markbox{13901}{bounded} \markbox{13902}{by} \markbox{m13903}{$2r_1$}, \markbox{13904}{and} \markbox{13905}{we} \markbox{13906}{are} \markbox{13907}{done} \markbox{13908}{by} \markbox{13909}{Lemma} \ref{lem:NR hp in Q}.  \markbox{13910}{For} \markbox{13911}{non-minimal} \markbox{13912}{domains} \markbox{m13913}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{13914}{note} \markbox{13915}{that} \markbox{13916}{by} \markbox{13917}{Lemma} \ref{lem:NR hp in Q}, \markbox{13918}{backtracking} \markbox{13919}{in} \markbox{m13920}{$T_U$} \markbox{13921}{is} \markbox{13922}{only} \markbox{13923}{possible} \markbox{13924}{if} \markbox{m13925}{$\gamma_U(t), \gamma_U(s)$} \markbox{13926}{are} \markbox{13927}{at} \markbox{13928}{the} \markbox{13929}{same} \markbox{13930}{collapsed} \markbox{13931}{point} \markbox{13932}{corresponding} \markbox{13933}{to} \markbox{13934}{some} \markbox{13935}{cluster} \markbox{m13936}{$C$}.  \markbox{13937}{If} \markbox{13938}{there} \markbox{13939}{are} \markbox{13940}{times} \markbox{m13941}{$s < t$} \markbox{13942}{so} \markbox{13943}{that} \markbox{m13944}{$d_{T_U}(B_U(\gamma(s), b_U) - d_{T_U}(B_U(\gamma(s)),b_U) \gg 100r_2 + 100r_1$}, \markbox{13945}{then} \markbox{13946}{there} \markbox{13947}{is} \markbox{13948}{some} \markbox{m13949}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{13950}{domain} \markbox{m13951}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{13952}{with} \markbox{m13953}{$\hd^V_U = q_U(C)$} \markbox{13954}{for} \markbox{13955}{which} \markbox{m13956}{$B_U(\gamma_U(t))$} \markbox{13957}{is} \markbox{13958}{on} \markbox{13959}{the} \markbox{13960}{side} \markbox{13961}{of} \markbox{m13962}{$a_U$} \markbox{13963}{while} \markbox{m13964}{$B_U(\gamma_U(s))$} \markbox{13965}{is} \markbox{13966}{on} \markbox{13967}{the} \markbox{13968}{side} \markbox{13969}{of} \markbox{m13970}{$b_U$}, \markbox{13971}{with} \markbox{13972}{both} \markbox{m13973}{$(50r_2 + 50r_1)$}-away \markbox{13974}{from} \markbox{m13975}{$\delta^V_U$}.  \markbox{13976}{But} \markbox{13977}{then} \markbox{13978}{consistency} \markbox{13979}{and} \markbox{13980}{the} \markbox{13981}{BGI} \markbox{13982}{properties} \markbox{13983}{from} \markbox{13984}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{13985}{implies} \markbox{13986}{that} \markbox{m13987}{$B_V(\gamma_V(t)), a_V$} \markbox{13988}{and} \markbox{m13989}{$B_V(\gamma_V(s)),b_V$} \markbox{13990}{are} \markbox{m13991}{$R$}-close, \markbox{13992}{and} \markbox{13993}{so} \markbox{m13994}{$\gamma_V(t) = \ha_V$} \markbox{13995}{and} \markbox{m13996}{$\gamma_V(s) = \hb_V$}, \markbox{13997}{which} \markbox{13998}{contradicts} \markbox{13999}{the} \markbox{14000}{base} \markbox{14001}{case} \markbox{14002}{of} \markbox{14003}{this} \markbox{14004}{induction.}  \markbox{14005}{This} \markbox{14006}{completes} \markbox{14007}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}
     \markbox{14008}{Since} \markbox{14009}{the} \markbox{14010}{map} \markbox{m14011}{$\hO: \calQ \to \calX$} \markbox{14012}{is} \markbox{14013}{uniformly} \markbox{14014}{quasi-median} \cite[Section 15]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{14015}{one} \markbox{14016}{could} \markbox{14017}{alternatively} \markbox{14018}{use} \markbox{14019}{the} \markbox{14020}{fact} \markbox{14021}{that} \markbox{14022}{median} \markbox{14023}{paths} \markbox{14024}{in} \markbox{14025}{HHSes} \markbox{14026}{are} \markbox{14027}{hierarchy} \markbox{14028}{paths} \cite[Lemma 1.37]{HHS_quasi}.
\end{remark}

As \markbox{14029}{a} \markbox{14030}{consequence} \markbox{14031}{of} \markbox{14032}{Propositions} \ref{prop:cubical hp} \markbox{14033}{and} \ref{prop:lower bound}, \markbox{14034}{we} \markbox{14035}{obtain} \markbox{14036}{the} \markbox{14037}{lower} \markbox{14038}{bound} \markbox{14039}{of} \markbox{14040}{the} \markbox{14041}{Distance} \markbox{14042}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}:

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:DF lower bound}
There \markbox{14043}{exists} \markbox{m14044}{$K_0 = K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{14045}{such} \markbox{14046}{that} \markbox{14047}{for} \markbox{14048}{all} \markbox{m14049}{$K>K_0$} \markbox{14050}{and} \markbox{14051}{any} \markbox{m14052}{$x, y \in \calX$}, \markbox{14053}{we} have
$$\sum_{U \in \mathfrak S} \left[d_U(x,y)\right]_K \prec d_{\calX}(x,y).$$
\end{corollary}

\subsection{Isomorphisms of HFIs and their associated cube complexes}

In \markbox{14054}{this} \markbox{14055}{final} \markbox{14056}{subsection,} \markbox{14057}{we} \markbox{14058}{will} \markbox{14059}{discuss} \markbox{14060}{when} \markbox{14061}{two} \markbox{14062}{HFIs} \markbox{14063}{to} \markbox{14064}{determine} \markbox{14065}{isomorphic} \markbox{14066}{cube} \markbox{14067}{complexes.}  \markbox{14068}{This} \markbox{14069}{statement,} \markbox{14070}{while} \markbox{14071}{unsurprising,} \markbox{14072}{motivates} \markbox{14073}{what} \markbox{14074}{happens} \markbox{14075}{in} \markbox{14076}{the} \markbox{14077}{subsequent} \markbox{14078}{sections,} \markbox{14079}{hence} \markbox{14080}{its} \markbox{14081}{placement} here.

Let \markbox{m14082}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{14083}{and} \markbox{m14084}{$\{\hT'_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{14085}{be} \markbox{14086}{two} \markbox{14087}{HFIs} \markbox{14088}{over} \markbox{14089}{a} \markbox{14090}{common} \markbox{14091}{index} \markbox{14092}{set} \markbox{m14093}{$\calU$} \markbox{14094}{and} \markbox{14095}{common} \markbox{14096}{relations,} \markbox{14097}{i.e.} \markbox{m14098}{$U,V \in \calU$} \markbox{14099}{have} \markbox{14100}{the} \markbox{14101}{same} \markbox{14102}{relation} \markbox{14103}{in} \markbox{14104}{both} \markbox{14105}{HFIs.}  \markbox{14106}{Any} \markbox{14107}{family} \markbox{14108}{of} \markbox{14109}{maps} \markbox{m14110}{$i_U:\hT_U \to \hT'_U$} \markbox{14111}{induces} \markbox{14112}{a} \markbox{14113}{global} \markbox{14114}{map} \markbox{m14115}{$I:\prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U \to \prod_{U \in \calU} \hT'_U$}, \markbox{14116}{where} \markbox{m14117}{$I((\hx_U)) = (i_U(\hx_U))$}.

The \markbox{14118}{following} \markbox{14119}{proposition,} \markbox{14120}{which} \markbox{14121}{is} \markbox{14122}{an} \markbox{14123}{interval} \markbox{14124}{version} \markbox{14125}{of} \cite[Proposition 14.12]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{14126}{gives} \markbox{14127}{sufficient} \markbox{14128}{conditions} \markbox{14129}{for} \markbox{14130}{the} \markbox{14131}{induced} \markbox{14132}{map} \markbox{14133}{to} \markbox{14134}{be} \markbox{14135}{an} \markbox{14136}{isometry} \markbox{m14137}{$I:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{14138}{which} \markbox{14139}{induces} \markbox{14140}{a} \markbox{14141}{cubical} \markbox{14142}{isomorphism} \markbox{14143}{between} \markbox{14144}{their} \markbox{14145}{dual} \markbox{14146}{cube} complexes.

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:HFI isomorphism}
Let \markbox{m14147}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{14148}{and} \markbox{m14149}{$\{\hT'_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{14150}{be} \markbox{14151}{two} \markbox{14152}{HFIs} \markbox{14153}{over} \markbox{14154}{a} \markbox{14155}{common} \markbox{14156}{index} \markbox{14157}{set} \markbox{m14158}{$\calU$} \markbox{14159}{with} \markbox{14160}{marked} \markbox{14161}{points} \markbox{m14162}{$F = \{a,b\}$}, \markbox{14163}{and} \markbox{14164}{let} \markbox{m14165}{$\calQ, \calQ'$} \markbox{14166}{be} \markbox{14167}{their} \markbox{14168}{corresponding} \markbox{m14169}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{14170}{sets.}  \markbox{14171}{Suppose} \markbox{14172}{that} \markbox{14173}{for} \markbox{14174}{each} \markbox{m14175}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{14176}{there} \markbox{14177}{is} \markbox{14178}{a} \markbox{14179}{simplicial} \markbox{14180}{isometry} \markbox{m14181}{$i_U:\hT_U \to \hT'_U$} \markbox{14182}{which} \markbox{14183}{also} satisfies:
\begin{enumerate}
	\item We \markbox{14184}{have} \markbox{m14185}{$i_U(\ha_U) = \ha'_U \in \hT'_U$} \markbox{14186}{and} \markbox{m14187}{$i_U(\hb_U) = \hb'_U \in \hT'_U$}.
	\item For \markbox{14188}{all} \markbox{m14189}{$V  \in \calU$} \markbox{14190}{with} \markbox{m14191}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{14192}{or} \markbox{m14193}{$V \pitchfork U$}, \markbox{14194}{we} \markbox{14195}{have} \markbox{m14196}{$i_U(\hd^V_U) = \left(\hd^V_U\right)'$}.
	\item For \markbox{14197}{all} \markbox{m14198}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{14199}{with} \markbox{m14200}{$U \nest V$} \markbox{14201}{and} \markbox{m14202}{$\hx_V \in \hT_V$}, \markbox{14203}{we} \markbox{14204}{have} \markbox{m14205}{$\left(\hd^V_U\right)'(i_V(\hx_V)) = i_U(\hd^V_U(\hx_V))$}.
\end{enumerate}
Then \markbox{14206}{the} \markbox{14207}{corresponding} \markbox{14208}{map} \markbox{14209}{induces} \markbox{14210}{a} \markbox{14211}{cubical} \markbox{14212}{isomorphism} \markbox{m14213}{$I:\calQ \to \calQ'$}.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}[Sketch \markbox{14214}{of} proof]


The \markbox{14215}{proof} \markbox{14216}{of} \markbox{14217}{this} \markbox{14218}{version} \markbox{14219}{below} \markbox{14220}{is} \markbox{14221}{the} \markbox{14222}{same} \markbox{14223}{as} \markbox{14224}{the} \markbox{14225}{original,} \markbox{14226}{which} \markbox{14227}{is,} \markbox{14228}{in} \markbox{14229}{turn,} \markbox{14230}{an} \markbox{14231}{exercise} \markbox{14232}{in} \markbox{14233}{the} \markbox{14234}{construction} \markbox{14235}{from} \markbox{14236}{this} \markbox{14237}{section} \markbox{14238}{plus} \markbox{14239}{Lemma} \ref{lem:NR hp in Q}.  \markbox{14240}{The} \markbox{14241}{main} \markbox{14242}{idea} \markbox{14243}{is} \markbox{14244}{that} \markbox{14245}{items} \markbox{14246}{in} \markbox{14247}{the} \markbox{14248}{statement} \markbox{14249}{guarantee} \markbox{14250}{that} \markbox{14251}{the} \markbox{14252}{global} \markbox{14253}{map} \markbox{m14254}{$I$} \markbox{14255}{induced} \markbox{14256}{from} \markbox{14257}{the} \markbox{14258}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{14259}{isometries} \markbox{14260}{preserves} \markbox{m14261}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{14262}{and} \markbox{14263}{distances,} \markbox{14264}{i.e.} \markbox{14265}{we} \markbox{14266}{have} \markbox{m14267}{$I:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{14268}{is} \markbox{14269}{an} \markbox{14270}{isometric} \markbox{14271}{embedding,} \markbox{14272}{with} \markbox{14273}{surjectivity} \markbox{14274}{following} \markbox{14275}{from} \markbox{14276}{a} \markbox{14277}{consistency} \markbox{14278}{argument.}  \markbox{14279}{Since} \markbox{14280}{the} \markbox{14281}{interval-wise} \markbox{14282}{maps} \markbox{14283}{respect} \markbox{14284}{the} \markbox{14285}{simplicial} \markbox{14286}{structure,} \markbox{14287}{we} \markbox{14288}{have} \markbox{14289}{that} \markbox{m14290}{$I$} \markbox{14291}{is} \markbox{14292}{also} \markbox{14293}{a} \markbox{14294}{cubical} \markbox{14295}{isomorphism} \markbox{14296}{via} \markbox{14297}{Lemma} \ref{lem:halfspaces_bijection}.  \markbox{14298}{We} \markbox{14299}{leave} \markbox{14300}{the} \markbox{14301}{details} \markbox{14302}{to} \markbox{14303}{the} reader.



\end{proof}
















\section{Controlling domains} \label{sec:controlling domains}

In \markbox{14304}{this} \markbox{14305}{section,} \markbox{14306}{we} \markbox{14307}{turn} \markbox{14308}{toward} \markbox{14309}{the} \markbox{14310}{proof} \markbox{14311}{of} \markbox{14312}{our} \markbox{14313}{main} \markbox{14314}{technical} \markbox{14315}{result,} \markbox{14316}{namely} \markbox{14317}{the} \markbox{14318}{Stable} \markbox{14319}{Cubical} \markbox{14320}{Interval} \markbox{14321}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}, \markbox{14322}{which} \markbox{14323}{is} \markbox{14324}{a} \markbox{14325}{stabilized} \markbox{14326}{version} \markbox{14327}{of} \markbox{14328}{the} \markbox{14329}{cubical} \markbox{14330}{model} \markbox{14331}{construction} \markbox{14332}{for} \markbox{14333}{a} \markbox{14334}{pair} \markbox{14335}{of} \markbox{14336}{points} \markbox{m14337}{$a,b$} \markbox{14338}{in} \markbox{14339}{any} \markbox{14340}{HHS} \markbox{m14341}{$\calX$}.  \markbox{14342}{The} \markbox{14343}{goal} \markbox{14344}{is} \markbox{14345}{to} \markbox{14346}{show} \markbox{14347}{that} \markbox{14348}{if} \markbox{14349}{we} \markbox{14350}{perturb} \markbox{m14351}{$a,b$} \markbox{14352}{a} \markbox{14353}{small} \markbox{14354}{amount} \markbox{14355}{to} \markbox{14356}{a} \markbox{14357}{pair} \markbox{14358}{of} \markbox{14359}{points} \markbox{m14360}{$a',b'$} \markbox{14361}{with} \markbox{m14362}{$d_{\calX}(a,a') \leq 1$} \markbox{14363}{and} \markbox{m14364}{$d_{\calX}(b,b') \leq 1$}, \markbox{14365}{then} \markbox{14366}{we} \markbox{14367}{can} \markbox{14368}{produce} \markbox{14369}{cubical} \markbox{14370}{models} \markbox{m14371}{$\calQ$} \markbox{14372}{for} \markbox{m14373}{$a,b$} \markbox{14374}{and} \markbox{m14375}{$\calQ'$} \markbox{14376}{for} \markbox{m14377}{$a',b'$} \markbox{14378}{which} \markbox{14379}{are} \markbox{14380}{isomorphic} \markbox{14381}{up} \markbox{14382}{to} \markbox{14383}{deleting} \markbox{14384}{boundedly-many} \markbox{14385}{hyperplanes.}  \markbox{14386}{Doing} \markbox{14387}{so} \markbox{14388}{requires} \markbox{14389}{carefully} \markbox{14390}{controlling} \markbox{14391}{the} \markbox{14392}{main} \markbox{14393}{inputs} \markbox{14394}{into} \markbox{14395}{the} \markbox{14396}{cubulation} \markbox{14397}{machine---namely} \markbox{14398}{the} \markbox{14399}{families} \markbox{14400}{of} \markbox{14401}{intervals} \markbox{14402}{we} \markbox{14403}{construct} \markbox{14404}{from} \markbox{14405}{the} \markbox{14406}{projections} \markbox{14407}{of} \markbox{14408}{the} points.

The \markbox{14409}{first} \markbox{14410}{step} \markbox{14411}{in} \markbox{14412}{the} \markbox{14413}{process} \markbox{14414}{involves} \markbox{14415}{explaining} \markbox{14416}{how} \markbox{14417}{to} \markbox{14418}{gain} \markbox{14419}{control} \markbox{14420}{over} \markbox{14421}{the} \markbox{14422}{set} \markbox{14423}{of} \markbox{14424}{relevant} \markbox{14425}{domains} \markbox{14426}{(Definition} \ref{defn:relevant}) \markbox{14427}{for} \markbox{14428}{a} \markbox{14429}{pair} \markbox{14430}{of} \markbox{14431}{points} \markbox{m14432}{$F = \{a,b\} \subset \calX$} \markbox{14433}{and} \markbox{14434}{its} \markbox{14435}{perturbation} \markbox{m14436}{$F' = \{a',b'\}$}  \markbox{14437}{as} \markbox{14438}{above.}  \markbox{14439}{In} \markbox{14440}{the} \markbox{14441}{next} \markbox{14442}{sections,} \markbox{14443}{we} \markbox{14444}{explain} \markbox{14445}{how} \markbox{14446}{to} \markbox{14447}{take} \markbox{14448}{this} \markbox{14449}{projection} \markbox{14450}{data} \markbox{14451}{to} \markbox{14452}{build} \markbox{14453}{a} \markbox{14454}{family} \markbox{14455}{of} \markbox{14456}{stable} \markbox{14457}{intervals} \markbox{14458}{that} \markbox{14459}{we} \markbox{14460}{can} \markbox{14461}{plug} \markbox{14462}{into} \markbox{14463}{the} \markbox{14464}{cubulation} machine.

The \markbox{14465}{main} \markbox{14466}{bit} \markbox{14467}{of} \markbox{14468}{work} \markbox{14469}{for} \markbox{14470}{this} \markbox{14471}{first} \markbox{14472}{part} \markbox{14473}{has} \markbox{14474}{already} \markbox{14475}{been} \markbox{14476}{done} \markbox{14477}{for} \markbox{14478}{us} \markbox{14479}{by} \markbox{14480}{Bestvina--Bromberg--Fujiwara} \cite{BBF} \markbox{14481}{and} \markbox{14482}{Bestvina--Bromberg--Fujiwara--Sisto} \cite{BBFS}.  \markbox{14483}{The} \markbox{14484}{work} \markbox{14485}{we} \markbox{14486}{did} \markbox{14487}{with} \markbox{14488}{Minsky} \markbox{14489}{and} \markbox{14490}{Sisto} \markbox{14491}{in} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{14492}{mostly} \markbox{14493}{adapts} \markbox{14494}{their} \markbox{14495}{setup} \markbox{14496}{to} \markbox{14497}{the} \markbox{14498}{HHS} \markbox{14499}{setting,} \markbox{14500}{and} \markbox{14501}{makes} \markbox{14502}{some} \markbox{14503}{straight-forward} \markbox{14504}{but} \markbox{14505}{important} observations.

In \cite[Subsections \markbox{14506}{2.3} \markbox{14507}{and} 2.4]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{14508}{we} \markbox{14509}{were} \markbox{14510}{dealing} \markbox{14511}{with} \markbox{14512}{the} \markbox{14513}{situation} \markbox{14514}{where} \markbox{m14515}{$F,F'$} \markbox{14516}{were} \markbox{14517}{finite} \markbox{14518}{sets} \markbox{14519}{of} \markbox{14520}{points} \markbox{14521}{with} \markbox{14522}{cardinality} \markbox{14523}{possibly} \markbox{14524}{larger} \markbox{14525}{than} \markbox{m14526}{$2$}.  \markbox{14527}{Nonetheless,} \markbox{14528}{all} \markbox{14529}{of} \markbox{14530}{the} \markbox{14531}{arguments} \markbox{14532}{there} \markbox{14533}{reduce} \markbox{14534}{to} \markbox{14535}{considering} \markbox{14536}{pairs} \markbox{14537}{of} \markbox{14538}{points,} \markbox{14539}{and} \markbox{14540}{so} \markbox{14541}{the} \markbox{14542}{proofs} \markbox{14543}{for} \markbox{14544}{our} \markbox{14545}{current} \markbox{14546}{setting} \markbox{14547}{are} \markbox{14548}{essentially} \markbox{14549}{the} \markbox{14550}{same.}  \markbox{14551}{As} \markbox{14552}{such,} \markbox{14553}{we} \markbox{14554}{will} \markbox{14555}{mainly} \markbox{14556}{explain} \markbox{14557}{the} \markbox{14558}{setup} \markbox{14559}{and} \markbox{14560}{key} \markbox{14561}{statements,} \markbox{14562}{only} \markbox{14563}{giving} \markbox{14564}{minimal} \markbox{14565}{sketches} \markbox{14566}{of} proofs.

\subsection{Colorability}

The \markbox{14567}{hierarchical} \markbox{14568}{setting} \markbox{14569}{in} \markbox{14570}{which} \cite{BBFS} \markbox{14571}{works} \markbox{14572}{is} \markbox{14573}{for} \markbox{14574}{the} \markbox{14575}{following} \markbox{14576}{class,} \markbox{14577}{which} \markbox{14578}{was} \markbox{14579}{first} \markbox{14580}{defined} \markbox{14581}{in} \cite[Definition 2.8]{DMS_bary} \markbox{14582}{and} \markbox{14583}{later} \markbox{14584}{used} \markbox{14585}{in} \cite{HP_proj,Petyt_quasicube}:

\begin{definition}[Colorable HHS]\label{defn:colorable}
We \markbox{14586}{say} \markbox{14587}{that} \markbox{14588}{an} HHS
\markbox{m14589}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{14590}{is} \emph{colorable} \markbox{14591}{if} \markbox{14592}{there} \markbox{14593}{exists} \markbox{14594}{a} \markbox{14595}{decomposition} of
\markbox{m14596}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{14597}{into} \markbox{14598}{finitely} \markbox{14599}{many} \markbox{14600}{families} \markbox{m14601}{$\mathfrak S_i$}, \markbox{14602}{so} \markbox{14603}{that} \markbox{14604}{each} \markbox{m14605}{$\mathfrak S_i$} is
pairwise-\markbox{m14606}{$\pitchfork$}.

\begin{itemize}
\item We \markbox{14607}{refer} \markbox{14608}{to} \markbox{14609}{the} \markbox{m14610}{$\mathfrak S_i$} \markbox{14611}{as} \emph{BBF families}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}
The \markbox{14612}{notion} \markbox{14613}{of} \markbox{14614}{colorability} \markbox{14615}{was} \markbox{14616}{inspired} \markbox{14617}{by} \markbox{14618}{work} \markbox{14619}{of} \markbox{14620}{Bestvina-Bromberg-Fujiwara} \cite{BBF}, \markbox{14621}{who} \markbox{14622}{proved} \markbox{14623}{that} \markbox{14624}{the} \markbox{14625}{curve} \markbox{14626}{graph} \markbox{14627}{is} \markbox{14628}{finitely-colorable.}  \markbox{14629}{As} \markbox{14630}{a} \markbox{14631}{consequence} \markbox{14632}{of} \markbox{14633}{this,} \markbox{14634}{the} \markbox{14635}{set} \markbox{14636}{of} \markbox{14637}{subsurfaces} \markbox{14638}{of} \markbox{14639}{a} \markbox{14640}{given} \markbox{14641}{finite-type} \markbox{14642}{surface} \markbox{m14643}{$S$} \markbox{14644}{can} \markbox{14645}{be} \markbox{14646}{decomposed} \markbox{14647}{into} \markbox{14648}{finitely-many} \markbox{14649}{families} \markbox{14650}{of} \markbox{14651}{pairwise-interlocking} \markbox{14652}{subsurfaces,} \markbox{14653}{which} \markbox{14654}{the} \markbox{14655}{above} \markbox{14656}{definition} \markbox{14657}{directly} \markbox{14658}{generalizes.}  \markbox{14659}{See} \cite[Subsection 2.3]{DMS_bary} \markbox{14660}{for} \markbox{14661}{a} \markbox{14662}{detailed} \markbox{14663}{discussion} \markbox{14664}{of} \markbox{14665}{this} connection.
\end{remark}

\subsection{Stable projections}

Our \markbox{14666}{next} \markbox{14667}{goal} \markbox{14668}{is} \markbox{14669}{to} \markbox{14670}{state} \markbox{14671}{a} \markbox{14672}{theorem} \markbox{14673}{which} \markbox{14674}{equips} \markbox{14675}{any} \markbox{14676}{colorable} \markbox{14677}{HHS} \markbox{14678}{with} \markbox{14679}{a} \markbox{14680}{set} \markbox{14681}{of} \markbox{14682}{projections} \markbox{14683}{which} \markbox{14684}{satisfy} \markbox{14685}{certain} \markbox{14686}{key} \markbox{14687}{stability} \markbox{14688}{properties.}  \markbox{14689}{We} \markbox{14690}{need} \markbox{14691}{some} \markbox{14692}{definitions} first.

Given \markbox{14693}{a} \markbox{14694}{pair} \markbox{14695}{of} \markbox{14696}{points} \markbox{m14697}{$F = \{x,y\} \subset \calX$} \markbox{14698}{and} \markbox{m14699}{$K>0$}, \markbox{14700}{we} \markbox{14701}{let} \markbox{m14702}{$\calU(F) = \Rel_K(F)$}.  \markbox{14703}{If} \markbox{m14704}{$V \in \calU(F)$}, \markbox{14705}{then} \markbox{14706}{we} \markbox{14707}{let} \markbox{m14708}{$\calU^V(F) = \{W \in \calU(F) | W \sqsubsetneq V\}$}.

The \markbox{14709}{following} \markbox{14710}{definition} \cite[Definition 2.13]{DMS_bary} \markbox{14711}{describes} \markbox{14712}{the} \markbox{14713}{domains} \markbox{14714}{we} \markbox{14715}{want} \markbox{14716}{to} \markbox{14717}{control} \markbox{14718}{when} \markbox{14719}{perturbing} \markbox{m14720}{$F$}:

\begin{definition}[Involved domains]\label{defn:involved}
Let \markbox{m14721}{$F = \{x,y\}, F' = \{x', y'\} \subset \calX$} \markbox{14722}{be} \markbox{14723}{so} \markbox{14724}{that} \markbox{m14725}{$d_{\calX}(x,x') \leq 1 $} \markbox{14726}{and} \markbox{m14727}{$d_{\calX}(y,y') \leq 1$}.  \markbox{14728}{For} \markbox{m14729}{$K>0$}, \markbox{14730}{we} \markbox{14731}{say} \markbox{14732}{that} \markbox{m14733}{$V \in \calU(F) \cup \calU(F')$} \markbox{14734}{is} \emph{involved in the transition} \markbox{14735}{between} \markbox{m14736}{$F$} \markbox{14737}{and} \markbox{m14738}{$F'$} \markbox{14739}{if} \markbox{14740}{one} \markbox{14741}{of} \markbox{14742}{the} \markbox{14743}{following} holds:

\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m14744}{$\pi_V(F) \neq \pi_V(F')$}.
\item \markbox{m14745}{$\calU^V(F) \neq \calU^V(F')$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

The \markbox{14746}{following,} \markbox{14747}{which} \markbox{14748}{combines} \markbox{14749}{the} \markbox{14750}{statements} \markbox{14751}{of} \cite[Theorem \markbox{14752}{2.9} \markbox{14753}{and} \markbox{14754}{Proposition} 2.14]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{14755}{states} \markbox{14756}{that,} \markbox{14757}{for} \markbox{14758}{any} \markbox{14759}{colorable} \markbox{14760}{HHS} \markbox{m14761}{$\calX$}, \markbox{14762}{we} \markbox{14763}{can} \markbox{14764}{replace} \markbox{14765}{its} \markbox{14766}{given} \markbox{14767}{projections} \markbox{14768}{with} \markbox{14769}{coarsely} \markbox{14770}{equivalent} \markbox{14771}{projections} \markbox{14772}{with} \markbox{14773}{which} \markbox{14774}{we} \markbox{14775}{can} \markbox{14776}{control} \markbox{14777}{involved} \markbox{14778}{domains} \markbox{14779}{up} \markbox{14780}{to} \markbox{14781}{a} \markbox{14782}{bounded} error:

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:controlling domains}
Let \markbox{m14783}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{14784}{be} \markbox{14785}{a} \markbox{14786}{colorable} \markbox{14787}{HHS} \markbox{14788}{with} \markbox{14789}{standard} \markbox{14790}{projections} \markbox{m14791}{$\hat{\pi}_{-}, \hat{\rho}^{-}_{-}$}.  \markbox{14792}{Then} \markbox{14793}{there} \markbox{14794}{exists} \markbox{m14795}{$\theta>0$} \markbox{14796}{and} \markbox{14797}{new} \markbox{14798}{projections} \markbox{m14799}{$\pi_{-}, \rho^{-}_{-}$} \markbox{14800}{with} \markbox{14801}{the} \markbox{14802}{same} \markbox{14803}{domains} \markbox{14804}{and} \markbox{14805}{ranges,} \markbox{14806}{respectively,} \markbox{14807}{such} \markbox{14808}{that} \markbox{14809}{the} \markbox{14810}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item The \markbox{14811}{new} \markbox{14812}{projections} \markbox{m14813}{$\pi_{-}, \rho^{-}_{-}$} \markbox{14814}{coarsely} \markbox{14815}{coincide} \markbox{14816}{with} \markbox{14817}{the} \markbox{14818}{old} \markbox{14819}{ones} \markbox{m14820}{$\hat{\pi}_{-}, \hat{\rho}^{-}_{-}$}.  \markbox{14821}{More} precisely:
\begin{enumerate}
\item If \markbox{m14822}{$X,Y$} \markbox{14823}{lie} \markbox{14824}{in} \markbox{14825}{different} \markbox{m14826}{$\mathfrak S_j$} \markbox{14827}{and} \markbox{m14828}{$\hat{\rho}^X_Y$} \markbox{14829}{is} \markbox{14830}{defined,} \markbox{14831}{then} \markbox{m14832}{$\rho^X_Y = \hat{\rho}^X_Y$}.
\item If \markbox{m14833}{$X,Y \in \mathfrak S_j$}, \markbox{14834}{then} \markbox{m14835}{$d^{Haus}_{Y}(\rho^X_Y, \hat{\rho}^X_Y)<\theta.$}
\item If \markbox{m14836}{$x \in \calX$} \markbox{14837}{and} \markbox{m14838}{$Y \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{14839}{then} \markbox{m14840}{$d^{Haus}_Y(\pi_Y(x),\hat{\pi}_Y(x))<\theta$}.
\end{enumerate}
\item There \markbox{14841}{exists} \markbox{m14842}{$K_0 = K_0(\calX)>0$} \markbox{14843}{and} \markbox{m14844}{$N_0(\calX)>0$} \markbox{14845}{so} \markbox{14846}{that} \markbox{14847}{if} \markbox{m14848}{$K>K_0$}, \markbox{14849}{then} \markbox{14850}{the} \markbox{14851}{following} \markbox{14852}{holds.}  \markbox{14853}{Let} \markbox{m14854}{$x,y,x',y' \in \calX$} \markbox{14855}{with} \markbox{m14856}{$d_{\calX}(x,x') \leq 1 $} \markbox{14857}{and} \markbox{m14858}{$d_{\calX}(y,y') \leq 1$}, \markbox{14859}{and} \markbox{14860}{let} \markbox{m14861}{$\calU = \Rel_K(\{x,y\})$} \markbox{14862}{and} \markbox{m14863}{$\calU' = \Rel_K(\{x',y'\})$} \markbox{14864}{be} \markbox{14865}{the} \markbox{14866}{relevant} \markbox{14867}{sets} \markbox{14868}{for} \markbox{14869}{the} \markbox{14870}{new} \markbox{14871}{projections} \markbox{m14872}{$\pi_-$}.  Then:
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m14873}{$\#(\calU \triangle \calU') < N_0$}, \markbox{14874}{and} \markbox{14875}{if} \markbox{m14876}{$V \in \calU \triangle \calU'$}, \markbox{14877}{then} \markbox{m14878}{$d_V(x,y) \prec K$} \markbox{14879}{and} \markbox{m14880}{$d_V(x',y') \prec K$}. \label{item:bounded symdiff}
\item  There \markbox{14881}{are} \markbox{14882}{at} \markbox{14883}{most} \markbox{m14884}{$N_0$} \markbox{14885}{domains} \markbox{m14886}{$V \in \calU(F) \cup \calU(F')$} \markbox{14887}{involved} \markbox{14888}{in} \markbox{14889}{the} \markbox{14890}{transition} \markbox{14891}{between} \markbox{m14892}{$F$} \markbox{14893}{and} \markbox{m14894}{$F'$}. \label{item:bounded involved}
\end{enumerate}
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}[Sketch \markbox{14895}{of} proof]
The \markbox{14896}{existence} \markbox{14897}{of} \markbox{14898}{new} \markbox{14899}{projections} \markbox{14900}{satisfying} \markbox{14901}{the} \markbox{14902}{conditions} \markbox{14903}{of} \markbox{14904}{item} \markbox{14905}{(1)} \markbox{14906}{is} \markbox{14907}{essentially} \markbox{14908}{an} \markbox{14909}{immediate} \markbox{14910}{consequence} \markbox{14911}{of} \markbox{14912}{the} \markbox{14913}{construction} \markbox{14914}{in} \cite[Theorem 4.1]{BBFS}.  \markbox{14915}{Item} \markbox{14916}{(2),} \markbox{14917}{which} \markbox{14918}{regards} \markbox{14919}{stability} \markbox{14920}{of} \markbox{14921}{the} \markbox{14922}{relevant} \markbox{14923}{sets} \markbox{m14924}{$\calU, \calU'$}, \markbox{14925}{requires} \markbox{14926}{a} \markbox{14927}{bit} \markbox{14928}{more} \markbox{14929}{work,} \markbox{14930}{but} \markbox{14931}{the} \markbox{14932}{key} \markbox{14933}{ideas} \markbox{14934}{are} \markbox{14935}{as} follows:

Using \cite[Proposition 2.8]{HHS_II} \markbox{14936}{(which} \markbox{14937}{generalizes} \cite{CLM12, BKMM:qirigid, BBF}), \markbox{14938}{there} \markbox{14939}{is} \markbox{14940}{a} \markbox{14941}{partial} \markbox{14942}{order} \markbox{m14943}{$\prec$} \markbox{14944}{on} \markbox{m14945}{$\Rel(x,y)$}, \markbox{14946}{which} \markbox{14947}{becomes} \markbox{14948}{a} \markbox{14949}{total} \markbox{14950}{order} \markbox{14951}{on} \markbox{m14952}{$\Rel^i(x,y) = \Rel_K(x,y) \cap \mathfrak S_i$} \markbox{14953}{for} \markbox{14954}{each} \markbox{m14955}{$i$}.  \markbox{14956}{In} \markbox{14957}{particular,} \markbox{14958}{we} \markbox{14959}{can} \markbox{14960}{think} \markbox{14961}{of} \markbox{14962}{each} \markbox{m14963}{$\Rel^i(x,y)$} \markbox{14964}{as} \markbox{14965}{an} \markbox{14966}{interval} \markbox{m14967}{$X_1 \prec \cdots \prec X_n$}.  \markbox{14968}{One} \markbox{14969}{of} \markbox{14970}{the} \markbox{14971}{additional} \markbox{14972}{properties} \markbox{14973}{that} \markbox{14974}{the} \markbox{14975}{new} \markbox{14976}{projections} \markbox{m14977}{$\pi_{-}, \rho^{-}_{-}$} \markbox{14978}{satisfy} \markbox{14979}{(see} \cite[Theorem 2.9]{DMS_bary}) \markbox{14980}{is} \markbox{14981}{that} \markbox{14982}{if} \markbox{m14983}{$X \prec Y$} \markbox{14984}{along} \markbox{14985}{both} \markbox{m14986}{$\Rel(x,y)$} \markbox{14987}{and} \markbox{m14988}{$\Rel(x',y')$}, \markbox{14989}{then} \markbox{m14990}{$\pi_Y(x) = \pi_Y(x') = \rho^X_Y$} \markbox{14991}{and} \markbox{m14992}{$\pi_X(y) = \pi_X(y') = \rho^Y_X$}.  \markbox{14993}{Using} \markbox{14994}{this,} \markbox{14995}{one} \markbox{14996}{can} \markbox{14997}{show} \markbox{14998}{that} \markbox{m14999}{$\Rel(x,y)$} \markbox{15000}{and} \markbox{m15001}{$\Rel(x',y')$} \markbox{15002}{can} \markbox{15003}{only} \markbox{15004}{differ} \markbox{15005}{at} \markbox{15006}{their} \markbox{15007}{first} \markbox{15008}{or} \markbox{15009}{last} \markbox{15010}{elements} \markbox{15011}{in} \markbox{15012}{the} \markbox{15013}{order} \markbox{m15014}{$\prec$}.  \markbox{15015}{Hence} \markbox{m15016}{$\#\left(\Rel^i(x,y) \triangle \Rel^i(x',y')\right) \leq 4$}; \markbox{15017}{see} \cite[Lemma \markbox{15018}{2.11} \markbox{15019}{and} \markbox{15020}{Proposition} 2.12]{DMS_bary}.  \markbox{15021}{Since} \markbox{15022}{there} \markbox{15023}{are} \markbox{15024}{only} \markbox{15025}{boundedly-many} \markbox{15026}{BBF} \markbox{15027}{families} \markbox{m15028}{$\mathfrak S_i$}, \markbox{15029}{item} \eqref{item:bounded symdiff} \markbox{15030}{follows} easily.

A \markbox{15031}{similar} \markbox{15032}{argument} \markbox{15033}{can} \markbox{15034}{now} \markbox{15035}{be} \markbox{15036}{used} \markbox{15037}{to} \markbox{15038}{control} \markbox{15039}{the} \markbox{15040}{number} \markbox{15041}{of} \markbox{15042}{involved} \markbox{15043}{domains} \markbox{15044}{of} \markbox{15045}{type} \markbox{15046}{(1)} \markbox{15047}{of} \markbox{15048}{Definition} \ref{defn:involved}, \markbox{15049}{see} \markbox{15050}{the} \markbox{15051}{proof} \markbox{15052}{of} \cite[Proposition 2.14]{DMS_bary}.  \markbox{15053}{For} \markbox{15054}{involved} \markbox{15055}{domains} \markbox{15056}{of} \markbox{15057}{type} \markbox{15058}{(2),} \markbox{15059}{this} \markbox{15060}{is} \markbox{15061}{an} \markbox{15062}{immediate} \markbox{15063}{consequence} \markbox{15064}{of} \markbox{15065}{item} \eqref{item:bounded symdiff} \markbox{15066}{and} \markbox{15067}{the} \markbox{15068}{Covering} \markbox{15069}{Lemma} \ref{lem:covering}, \markbox{15070}{which} \markbox{15071}{bounds} \markbox{15072}{the} \markbox{15073}{number} \markbox{15074}{of} \markbox{15075}{domains} \markbox{m15076}{$W \in \calU$} \markbox{15077}{into} \markbox{15078}{which} \markbox{15079}{a} \markbox{15080}{given} \markbox{m15081}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{15082}{can} nest.
\end{proof}





\section{Stable Intervals}\label{sec:stable intervals}

With \markbox{15083}{the} \markbox{15084}{new} \markbox{15085}{HHS} \markbox{15086}{projections} \markbox{15087}{provided} \markbox{15088}{by} \markbox{15089}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains}, \markbox{15090}{we} \markbox{15091}{now} \markbox{15092}{turn} \markbox{15093}{toward} \markbox{15094}{converting} \markbox{15095}{stabilized} \markbox{15096}{projection} \markbox{15097}{data} \markbox{15098}{into} \markbox{15099}{stable} \markbox{15100}{families} \markbox{15101}{of} \markbox{15102}{intervals,} \markbox{15103}{in} \markbox{15104}{partivuvlar} \markbox{15105}{stabilizing} \markbox{15106}{the} \markbox{15107}{input} \markbox{15108}{into} \markbox{15109}{the} \markbox{15110}{cubical} \markbox{15111}{model} \markbox{15112}{construction} \markbox{15113}{from} \markbox{15114}{Section} \ref{sec:interval systems}.


Our \markbox{15115}{ultimate} \markbox{15116}{goal} \markbox{15117}{is} \markbox{15118}{to} \markbox{15119}{produce} \markbox{15120}{cubical} \markbox{15121}{models} \markbox{15122}{for} \markbox{15123}{pairs} \markbox{15124}{of} \markbox{15125}{nearby} \markbox{15126}{points} \markbox{15127}{that} \markbox{15128}{differ} \markbox{15129}{by} \markbox{15130}{a} \markbox{15131}{controlled} \markbox{15132}{number} \markbox{15133}{of} \markbox{15134}{hyperplane} \markbox{15135}{deletions} \markbox{15136}{(Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}). \markbox{15137}{Since} \markbox{15138}{the} \markbox{15139}{hyperplanes} \markbox{15140}{in} \markbox{15141}{the} \markbox{15142}{cubical} \markbox{15143}{models} \markbox{15144}{come} \markbox{15145}{from} \markbox{15146}{edges} \markbox{15147}{of} \markbox{15148}{the} \markbox{15149}{simplicial} \markbox{15150}{intervals} \markbox{15151}{in} \markbox{15152}{our} \markbox{15153}{HFIs} \markbox{15154}{(Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC}), \markbox{15155}{it} \markbox{15156}{will} \markbox{15157}{suffice} \markbox{15158}{to} \markbox{15159}{build} \markbox{15160}{HFIs} \markbox{15161}{where} \markbox{15162}{the} \markbox{15163}{intervals} \markbox{15164}{only} \markbox{15165}{differ} \markbox{15166}{by} \markbox{15167}{boundedly-many} \markbox{15168}{bounded-size} \markbox{15169}{collections} \markbox{15170}{of} \markbox{15171}{edges.}  \markbox{15172}{That} \markbox{15173}{is} \markbox{15174}{the} \markbox{15175}{content} \markbox{15176}{of} \markbox{15177}{the} \markbox{15178}{Stable} \markbox{15179}{Intervals} \markbox{15180}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}. 



We \markbox{15181}{first} \markbox{15182}{explain} \markbox{15183}{the} \markbox{15184}{build-up} \markbox{15185}{to} \markbox{15186}{this} \markbox{15187}{theorem} \markbox{15188}{and} \markbox{15189}{defer} \markbox{15190}{the} \markbox{15191}{explicit} \markbox{15192}{statement.}  \markbox{15193}{We} \markbox{15194}{will} \markbox{15195}{work} \markbox{15196}{in} \markbox{15197}{the} \markbox{15198}{setting} \markbox{15199}{of} \markbox{15200}{a} \markbox{15201}{hyperbolic} \markbox{15202}{space} \markbox{15203}{with} \markbox{15204}{a} \markbox{15205}{hierarchical-like} \markbox{15206}{configuration.}  \markbox{15207}{The} \markbox{15208}{construction} \markbox{15209}{is} \markbox{15210}{a} \markbox{15211}{somewhat} \markbox{15212}{long} \markbox{15213}{and} \markbox{15214}{delicate} \markbox{15215}{exercise} \markbox{15216}{in} \markbox{15217}{hyperbolic} \markbox{15218}{geometry} \markbox{15219}{and} \markbox{15220}{we} \markbox{15221}{will} \markbox{15222}{mainly} \markbox{15223}{provide} \markbox{15224}{a} \markbox{15225}{detailed} sketch.

\subsection{Basic setup and assumptions}\label{subsec:stable setup}
