For \markbox{15226}{the} \markbox{15227}{rest} \markbox{15228}{of} \markbox{15229}{this} \markbox{15230}{section,} \markbox{15231}{let} \markbox{15232}{us} \markbox{15233}{assume} \markbox{15234}{that} \markbox{m15235}{$\calZ$} \markbox{15236}{is} \markbox{15237}{a} \markbox{m15238}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{15239}{geodesic} \markbox{15240}{space.}  \markbox{15241}{The} \markbox{15242}{first} \markbox{15243}{bit} \markbox{15244}{of} \markbox{15245}{notation} \markbox{15246}{we} \markbox{15247}{want} \markbox{15248}{to} \markbox{15249}{set} \markbox{15250}{is} \markbox{15251}{a} \markbox{15252}{choice} \markbox{15253}{of} \markbox{15254}{geodesic} \markbox{15255}{between} \markbox{15256}{any} \markbox{15257}{pair} \markbox{15258}{of} \markbox{15259}{points.}  \markbox{15260}{That} \markbox{15261}{is,} \markbox{15262}{for} \markbox{15263}{any} \markbox{m15264}{$x,y \in \calZ$}, \markbox{15265}{we} \markbox{15266}{fix} \markbox{15267}{(once} \markbox{15268}{and} \markbox{15269}{for} \markbox{15270}{all)} \markbox{15271}{a} \markbox{15272}{geodesic} \markbox{m15273}{$\lambda(x,y)$}.  \markbox{15274}{More} \markbox{15275}{generally,} \markbox{15276}{if} \markbox{m15277}{$C,C' \subset \calZ$} \markbox{15278}{are} \markbox{15279}{finite} \markbox{15280}{subsets,} \markbox{15281}{then} \markbox{15282}{we} \markbox{15283}{let} \markbox{m15284}{$\lambda(C,C')$} \markbox{15285}{denote} \markbox{15286}{a} \markbox{15287}{choice} \markbox{15288}{of} \markbox{15289}{geodesic} \markbox{15290}{between} \markbox{15291}{them} \markbox{15292}{whose} \markbox{15293}{length} \markbox{15294}{satisfies} \markbox{m15295}{$|\lambda(C,C')| = d_{\calZ}(C,C')$}, \markbox{15296}{and} \markbox{15297}{we} \markbox{15298}{require} \markbox{15299}{symmetry,} \markbox{15300}{namely} \markbox{m15301}{$\lambda(C,C') = \lambda(C',C)$}.

It \markbox{15302}{will} \markbox{15303}{also} \markbox{15304}{be} \markbox{15305}{necessary} \markbox{15306}{to} \markbox{15307}{perform} \markbox{15308}{a} \markbox{15309}{slight} \markbox{15310}{modification} \markbox{15311}{on} \markbox{15312}{the} \markbox{15313}{geodesic} \markbox{15314}{function} \markbox{m15315}{$\lambda$}, \markbox{15316}{so} \markbox{15317}{that} \markbox{15318}{its} \markbox{15319}{resulting} \markbox{15320}{length} \markbox{15321}{is} \markbox{15322}{an} \markbox{15323}{integer.}  \markbox{15324}{To} \markbox{15325}{fix} \markbox{15326}{this,} \markbox{15327}{we} \markbox{15328}{let} \markbox{m15329}{$\lambda_0(C,C')$} \markbox{15330}{denote} \markbox{15331}{the} \markbox{15332}{restriction} \markbox{15333}{of} \markbox{m15334}{$\lambda(C,C'):[0, d_{\calZ}(C,C')]\to \calZ$} \markbox{15335}{to} \markbox{15336}{the} \markbox{15337}{interval} \markbox{m15338}{$[0, \lfloor{d_{\calZ}(C,C')}\rfloor]$}.  \markbox{15339}{The} \markbox{15340}{effect} \markbox{15341}{of} \markbox{15342}{this} \markbox{15343}{is} \markbox{15344}{to} \markbox{15345}{trim} \markbox{m15346}{$\lambda(A,B)$} \markbox{15347}{so} \markbox{15348}{that} \markbox{15349}{it} \markbox{15350}{has} \markbox{15351}{positive} \markbox{15352}{integer} \markbox{15353}{length} \markbox{15354}{and} \markbox{15355}{their} \markbox{15356}{lengths} \markbox{15357}{satisfy} \markbox{m15358}{$l(\lambda(C,C')) -l(\lambda_0(C,C')) < 1$}.  \markbox{15359}{While} \markbox{15360}{not} \markbox{15361}{necessary,} \markbox{15362}{one} \markbox{15363}{could} \markbox{15364}{make} \markbox{15365}{this} \markbox{15366}{symmetric} \markbox{15367}{by} \markbox{15368}{trimming} \markbox{15369}{both} \markbox{15370}{the} \markbox{15371}{sides} \markbox{15372}{by} \markbox{15373}{half} \markbox{15374}{of} \markbox{m15375}{$l(\lambda(C,C')) -l(\lambda_0(C,C'))$}.  \markbox{15376}{In} \markbox{15377}{the} \markbox{15378}{course} \markbox{15379}{of} \markbox{15380}{the} \markbox{15381}{arguments,} \markbox{15382}{however,} \markbox{15383}{one} \markbox{15384}{can} \markbox{15385}{usually} \markbox{15386}{work} \markbox{15387}{with} \markbox{m15388}{$\lambda$} \markbox{15389}{instead} \markbox{15390}{of} \markbox{m15391}{$\lambda_0$}.

Now, \markbox{15392}{for} \markbox{15393}{the} \markbox{15394}{rest} \markbox{15395}{of} \markbox{15396}{this} \markbox{15397}{section,} \markbox{15398}{we} \markbox{15399}{fix} \markbox{15400}{a} \markbox{15401}{pair} \markbox{15402}{of} \markbox{15403}{points} \markbox{m15404}{$\{a,b\} \subset \calZ$}.  \markbox{15405}{Furthermore,} \markbox{15406}{let} \markbox{m15407}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{15408}{be} \markbox{15409}{a} \markbox{15410}{finite} \markbox{15411}{(but} \markbox{15412}{possibly} \markbox{15413}{arbitrarily} \markbox{15414}{large)} \markbox{15415}{set} \markbox{15416}{of} \markbox{15417}{points} \markbox{15418}{of} \markbox{m15419}{$\calZ$} \markbox{15420}{and} \markbox{15421}{let} \markbox{m15422}{$\epsilon>0$} \markbox{15423}{so} \markbox{15424}{that} \markbox{m15425}{$d_{\calZ}(\lambda(a,b), y) < \epsilon/2$} \markbox{15426}{for} \markbox{15427}{all} \markbox{m15428}{$y \in \calY$}.  \markbox{15429}{We} \markbox{15430}{call} \markbox{15431}{such} \markbox{15432}{an} \markbox{15433}{arrangement} \markbox{m15434}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{15435}{an} \markbox{m15436}{$\epsilon$}-\emph{setup} \markbox{15437}{in} \markbox{m15438}{$\calZ$}.

In \markbox{15439}{the} \markbox{15440}{hierarchical} \markbox{15441}{setting,} \markbox{m15442}{$\calZ$} \markbox{15443}{will} \markbox{15444}{be} \markbox{15445}{one} \markbox{15446}{of} \markbox{15447}{the} \markbox{15448}{hyperbolic} \markbox{15449}{spaces} \markbox{m15450}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{15451}{for} \markbox{m15452}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{15453}{and} \markbox{15454}{the} \markbox{15455}{points} \markbox{m15456}{$\calY$} \markbox{15457}{will} \markbox{15458}{be} \markbox{15459}{the} \markbox{15460}{points} \markbox{15461}{in} \markbox{m15462}{$\rho^V_U$} \markbox{15463}{for} \markbox{m15464}{$V \nest U \in \calU$}.  \markbox{15465}{The} \markbox{15466}{proximity} \markbox{15467}{condition} \markbox{15468}{of} \markbox{15469}{the} \markbox{15470}{points} \markbox{15471}{in} \markbox{m15472}{$\calY$} \markbox{15473}{to} \markbox{m15474}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{15475}{comes} \markbox{15476}{from} \markbox{15477}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA}.

\begin{notation}[\markbox{m15478}{$O(\epsilon)$}-notation]
In \markbox{15479}{this} \markbox{15480}{section,} \markbox{15481}{we} \markbox{15482}{will} \markbox{15483}{often} \markbox{15484}{want} \markbox{15485}{to} \markbox{15486}{get} \markbox{15487}{controlled} \markbox{15488}{bounds} \markbox{15489}{over} \markbox{15490}{various} \markbox{15491}{distance} \markbox{15492}{quantities,} \markbox{15493}{where} \markbox{15494}{the} \markbox{15495}{bounds} \markbox{15496}{will} \markbox{15497}{depend} \markbox{15498}{on} \markbox{15499}{our} \markbox{15500}{choice} \markbox{15501}{of} \markbox{m15502}{$\epsilon$} \markbox{15503}{and} \markbox{15504}{the} \markbox{15505}{hyperbolicity} \markbox{15506}{constant} \markbox{m15507}{$\delta$} \markbox{15508}{for} \markbox{m15509}{$\calZ$}.  \markbox{15510}{When} \markbox{15511}{a} \markbox{15512}{number} \markbox{m15513}{$A$} \markbox{15514}{is} \markbox{15515}{bounded} \markbox{15516}{above} \markbox{15517}{as} \markbox{15518}{a} \markbox{15519}{function} \markbox{15520}{of} \markbox{m15521}{$\epsilon, \delta$}, \markbox{15522}{we} \markbox{15523}{will} \markbox{15524}{simply} \markbox{15525}{write} 
$$A < O(\epsilon),$$
since \markbox{m15526}{$\delta$} \markbox{15527}{is} \markbox{15528}{given} \markbox{15529}{to} \markbox{15530}{us,} \markbox{15531}{while} \markbox{15532}{we} \markbox{15533}{need} \markbox{15534}{some} \markbox{15535}{flexibility} \markbox{15536}{to} \markbox{15537}{choose} \markbox{m15538}{$\epsilon$}.
\end{notation}

The \markbox{15539}{following} \markbox{15540}{lemma,} \markbox{15541}{which} \markbox{15542}{is} \markbox{15543}{essentially} \markbox{15544}{a} \markbox{15545}{consequence} \markbox{15546}{of} \markbox{15547}{the} \markbox{15548}{Morse} \markbox{15549}{Lemma} \markbox{15550}{for} \markbox{15551}{hyperbolic} \markbox{15552}{spaces,} \markbox{15553}{gives} \markbox{15554}{us} \markbox{15555}{control} \markbox{15556}{over} \markbox{15557}{how} \markbox{15558}{far} \markbox{m15559}{$\lambda(C,C')$} \markbox{15560}{can} \markbox{15561}{get} \markbox{15562}{from} \markbox{m15563}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{15564}{when} \markbox{m15565}{$C, C' \subset \calY$}, \markbox{15566}{and} \markbox{15567}{are} \markbox{15568}{thus} \markbox{m15569}{$\epsilon$}-close \markbox{15570}{to} \markbox{m15571}{$\lambda(a,b)$}:

\begin{lemma}[Fellow-traveling, \markbox{m15572}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic]\label{lem:Morse close}
Let \markbox{m15573}{$\calZ$} \markbox{15574}{be} \markbox{m15575}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{15576}{and} \markbox{15577}{geodesic,} \markbox{15578}{and} \markbox{m15579}{$\gamma$} \markbox{15580}{a} \markbox{15581}{geodesic} \markbox{15582}{between} \markbox{m15583}{$a,b \in \calZ$}.  \markbox{15584}{For} \markbox{15585}{every} \markbox{m15586}{$\epsilon>0$} \markbox{15587}{there} \markbox{15588}{exists} \markbox{m15589}{$\epsilon'=O(\epsilon)>0$} \markbox{15590}{so} \markbox{15591}{that} \markbox{15592}{the} \markbox{15593}{following} holds:

\begin{itemize}
\item Suppose \markbox{m15594}{$\gamma'$} \markbox{15595}{is} \markbox{15596}{a} \markbox{15597}{geodesic} \markbox{15598}{connecting} \markbox{15599}{points} \markbox{m15600}{$x,y \in \calN_{\epsilon}(\gamma)$}, \markbox{15601}{and} \markbox{15602}{that} \markbox{m15603}{$x',y'$} \markbox{15604}{are} \markbox{15605}{closest} \markbox{15606}{points} \markbox{15607}{to} \markbox{m15608}{$x,y$} \markbox{15609}{on} \markbox{m15610}{$\gamma$}, \markbox{15611}{respectively.}  \markbox{15612}{Then} \markbox{15613}{any} \markbox{15614}{geodesic} \markbox{m15615}{$[x,y]$} \markbox{15616}{satisfies} \markbox{m15617}{$d_{\calZ}^{Haus}([x,y], [x',y']) < \epsilon'$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{lemma}

As \markbox{15618}{a} \markbox{15619}{consequence,} \markbox{15620}{if} \markbox{m15621}{$C, C' \subset \calY$} \markbox{15622}{are} \markbox{15623}{finite} \markbox{15624}{subsets,} \markbox{15625}{then} \markbox{m15626}{$\lambda(C,C') \subset \calN_{\epsilon'}(\lambda(a,b))$}.  \markbox{15627}{Finally,} \markbox{15628}{it} \markbox{15629}{will} \markbox{15630}{be} \markbox{15631}{convenient} \markbox{15632}{for} \markbox{15633}{us} \markbox{15634}{to} \markbox{15635}{assume} \markbox{15636}{that} \markbox{m15637}{$\epsilon' > \epsilon$}.



  
\subsection{Clusters and the cluster graph} \label{subsec:clusters}

Our \markbox{15638}{first} \markbox{15639}{goal} \markbox{15640}{is} \markbox{15641}{to} \markbox{15642}{group} \markbox{15643}{the} \markbox{15644}{points} \markbox{15645}{of} \markbox{m15646}{$\calY$} \markbox{15647}{into} \emph{clusters} \markbox{15648}{of} \markbox{15649}{nearby} \markbox{15650}{sets.}  \markbox{15651}{To} \markbox{15652}{that} \markbox{15653}{end,} \markbox{15654}{let} \markbox{m15655}{$E = E(\epsilon)> \epsilon$} \markbox{15656}{be} \markbox{15657}{sufficiently} \markbox{15658}{large,} \markbox{15659}{to} \markbox{15660}{be} \markbox{15661}{determined} below.

Let \markbox{m15662}{$\calC_E$} \markbox{15663}{denote} \markbox{15664}{the} \markbox{15665}{graph} \markbox{15666}{whose} \markbox{15667}{vertices} \markbox{15668}{are} \markbox{15669}{points} \markbox{15670}{of} \markbox{m15671}{$\calY \cup \{a,b\}$}, \markbox{15672}{with} \markbox{15673}{two} \markbox{15674}{points} \markbox{m15675}{$x,y \in \calY \cup \{a,b\}$} \markbox{15676}{connected} \markbox{15677}{by} \markbox{15678}{an} \markbox{15679}{edge} \markbox{15680}{exactly} \markbox{15681}{when} \markbox{m15682}{$d_{\calZ}(x,y) < E$}.  \markbox{15683}{The} \markbox{15684}{connected} \markbox{15685}{components} \markbox{15686}{of} \markbox{m15687}{$\calC_E$} \markbox{15688}{are} \markbox{15689}{called} \markbox{m15690}{$E$}-\emph{clusters}, \markbox{15691}{or} \markbox{15692}{simply} \emph{clusters} \markbox{15693}{when} \markbox{m15694}{$E$} \markbox{15695}{is} fixed.

For \markbox{15696}{any} \markbox{m15697}{$E$}-cluster \markbox{m15698}{$C$}, \markbox{15699}{let} \markbox{m15700}{$s(C) = \hull_{\lambda(a,b)}(p_{\lambda(a,b)}(C))$} \markbox{15701}{denote} \markbox{15702}{the} \markbox{15703}{hull} \markbox{15704}{(in} \markbox{m15705}{$\lambda(a,b)$}) \markbox{15706}{of} \markbox{15707}{the} \markbox{15708}{closest} \markbox{15709}{point} \markbox{15710}{projection} \markbox{15711}{of} \markbox{m15712}{$C$} \markbox{15713}{to} \markbox{m15714}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{15715}{The} \markbox{15716}{set} \markbox{m15717}{$s(C)$} \markbox{15718}{is} \markbox{15719}{called} \markbox{15720}{the} \emph{shadow} \markbox{15721}{of} \markbox{m15722}{$C$} \markbox{15723}{on} \markbox{m15724}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.

The \markbox{15725}{following} \markbox{15726}{lemma} \markbox{15727}{controls} \markbox{15728}{how} \markbox{15729}{shadows} \markbox{15730}{of} \markbox{15731}{clusters} \markbox{15732}{are} \markbox{15733}{arranged} \markbox{15734}{along} \markbox{m15735}{$\lambda(a,b)$}. \markbox{15736}{Its} \markbox{15737}{proof} \markbox{15738}{is} \markbox{15739}{straightforward} \markbox{15740}{(see} \cite[Lemma 3.6]{DMS_bary}), \markbox{15741}{so} \markbox{15742}{we} \markbox{15743}{leave} \markbox{15744}{it} \markbox{15745}{to} \markbox{15746}{the} \markbox{15747}{reader} \markbox{15748}{to} \markbox{15749}{check} (:

\begin{lemma} \label{lem:cluster arrangement}
If \markbox{m15750}{$E > 5\epsilon$} \markbox{15751}{and} \markbox{m15752}{$C \neq C'$} \markbox{15753}{are} \markbox{15754}{distinct} \markbox{m15755}{$E$}-clusters, \markbox{15756}{then} \markbox{m15757}{$s(C) \cap s(C') = \emptyset$}.
\end{lemma}




In \markbox{15758}{what} \markbox{15759}{follows,} \markbox{15760}{we} \markbox{15761}{will} \markbox{15762}{need} \markbox{15763}{to} \markbox{15764}{adjust} \markbox{15765}{the} \markbox{15766}{cluster} \markbox{15767}{constant} \markbox{m15768}{$E$} \markbox{15769}{a} \markbox{15770}{number} \markbox{15771}{of} \markbox{15772}{times,} \markbox{15773}{but} \markbox{15774}{we} \markbox{15775}{will} \markbox{15776}{usually} \markbox{15777}{omit} \markbox{15778}{the} \markbox{15779}{constant} \markbox{15780}{and} \markbox{15781}{refer} \markbox{15782}{to} \markbox{15783}{them} \markbox{15784}{simply} \markbox{15785}{as} clusters.

We \markbox{15786}{now} \markbox{15787}{can} \markbox{15788}{define} \markbox{15789}{our} \markbox{15790}{notion} \markbox{15791}{of} \markbox{15792}{cluster} \markbox{15793}{separation} \markbox{15794}{using} \markbox{15795}{Lemma} \ref{lem:Morse close}.  \markbox{15796}{The} \markbox{15797}{idea} \markbox{15798}{here} \markbox{15799}{is} \markbox{15800}{that} \markbox{15801}{clusters} \markbox{15802}{are} \markbox{m15803}{$\epsilon$}-close \markbox{15804}{to} \markbox{m15805}{$\lambda(a,b)$}, \markbox{15806}{and} \markbox{15807}{hence} \markbox{15808}{geodesics} \markbox{15809}{connecting} \markbox{15810}{them} \markbox{15811}{stay} \markbox{m15812}{$\epsilon'$}-close \markbox{15813}{to} \markbox{m15814}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{15815}{by} \markbox{15816}{Lemma} \ref{lem:Morse close}.

\begin{definition}
Let \markbox{m15817}{$C_1, C_2, C_3$} \markbox{15818}{be} \markbox{15819}{clusters.}  \markbox{15820}{Given} \markbox{m15821}{$\epsilon'>0$}, \markbox{15822}{we} \markbox{15823}{say} \markbox{m15824}{$C_2$} \markbox{m15825}{$\epsilon'$}-\emph{separates} \markbox{m15826}{$C_1$} \markbox{15827}{from} \markbox{m15828}{$C_3$} \markbox{15829}{if} \markbox{15830}{there} \markbox{15831}{exists} \markbox{15832}{a} \markbox{15833}{minimal} \markbox{15834}{length} \markbox{15835}{geodesic} \markbox{15836}{connecting} \markbox{m15837}{$C_1$} \markbox{15838}{to} \markbox{m15839}{$C_3$} \markbox{15840}{which} \markbox{15841}{passes} \markbox{15842}{within} \markbox{m15843}{$2\epsilon'$} \markbox{15844}{of} \markbox{m15845}{$C_2$}.

\begin{itemize}
\item Given \markbox{m15846}{$E>0$}, \markbox{15847}{the} \emph{$E$-cluster separation graph} \markbox{15848}{for} \markbox{m15849}{$(a,b; \calY)$}, \markbox{15850}{denoted} \markbox{m15851}{$\calG_E = \calG_{E,\epsilon'}(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{15852}{is} \markbox{15853}{defined} \markbox{15854}{as} \markbox{15855}{follows:} \markbox{15856}{The} \markbox{15857}{vertices} \markbox{15858}{of} \markbox{m15859}{$\calG_E$} \markbox{15860}{are} \markbox{15861}{clusters,} \markbox{15862}{and} \markbox{15863}{two} \markbox{15864}{vertices} \markbox{15865}{are} \markbox{15866}{connected} \markbox{15867}{by} \markbox{15868}{an} \markbox{15869}{edge} \markbox{15870}{if} \markbox{15871}{and} \markbox{15872}{only} \markbox{15873}{if} \markbox{15874}{they} \markbox{15875}{are} \markbox{15876}{not} \markbox{m15877}{$2\epsilon'$}-separated \markbox{15878}{by} \markbox{15879}{another} cluster.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}


The \markbox{15880}{following} \markbox{15881}{is} \markbox{15882}{essentially} \markbox{15883}{a} \markbox{15884}{consequence} \markbox{15885}{of} \markbox{15886}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster arrangement}.  \markbox{15887}{It} \markbox{15888}{states} \markbox{15889}{that} \markbox{15890}{the} \markbox{15891}{cluster} \markbox{15892}{graph} \markbox{15893}{is} \markbox{15894}{an} \markbox{15895}{interval} \markbox{15896}{with} \markbox{15897}{the} \markbox{15898}{order} \markbox{15899}{of} \markbox{15900}{vertices} \markbox{15901}{corresponding} \markbox{15902}{to} \markbox{15903}{the} \markbox{15904}{order} \markbox{15905}{of} \markbox{15906}{the} \markbox{15907}{cluster} \markbox{15908}{shadows} \markbox{15909}{along} \markbox{m15910}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{15911}{We} \markbox{15912}{omit} \markbox{15913}{its} \markbox{15914}{proof,} \markbox{15915}{which} \markbox{15916}{uses} \markbox{15917}{only} \markbox{15918}{hyperbolic} \markbox{15919}{geometry} \markbox{15920}{and} \markbox{15921}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster arrangement}.


\begin{proposition}\label{prop:cluster sep graph}
Let \markbox{m15922}{$\calZ$} \markbox{15923}{be} \markbox{m15924}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic, \markbox{m15925}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{15926}{a} \markbox{15927}{geodesic} \markbox{15928}{connecting} \markbox{m15929}{$a,b \in \calZ$}, \markbox{15930}{and} \markbox{m15931}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{15932}{finite} \markbox{15933}{with} \markbox{m15934}{$\calY \subset \calN_{\epsilon}(\lambda(a,b))$}.  \markbox{15935}{Also} \markbox{15936}{let} \markbox{m15937}{$\epsilon' = \epsilon'(\epsilon, \delta)>0$} \markbox{15938}{as} \markbox{15939}{in} \markbox{15940}{Lemma} \ref{lem:Morse close}, \markbox{15941}{with} \markbox{15942}{also} \markbox{m15943}{$\epsilon' > \epsilon$}.

There \markbox{15944}{exists} \markbox{m15945}{$E = E(\epsilon, \delta)>0$} \markbox{15946}{so} \markbox{15947}{that} \markbox{15948}{the} \markbox{m15949}{$E$}-cluster \markbox{15950}{separation} \markbox{15951}{graph} \markbox{m15952}{$\calG_{E,\epsilon'}(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{15953}{is} \markbox{15954}{an} \markbox{15955}{interval} \markbox{15956}{whose} \markbox{15957}{order} \markbox{15958}{coincides} \markbox{15959}{with} \markbox{15960}{the} \markbox{15961}{order} \markbox{15962}{of} \markbox{15963}{cluster} \markbox{15964}{shadows} \markbox{15965}{along} \markbox{m15966}{$\lambda(a,b)$}, \markbox{15967}{with} \markbox{15968}{the} \markbox{15969}{endpoint} \markbox{15970}{clusters} \markbox{15971}{containing} \markbox{m15972}{$a,b$}, \markbox{15973}{respectively.} 
\end{proposition}



\subsection{Stable intervals defined}

We \markbox{15974}{are} \markbox{15975}{now} \markbox{15976}{ready} \markbox{15977}{to} \markbox{15978}{describe} \markbox{15979}{the} \markbox{15980}{stable} intervals.

By \markbox{15981}{Proposition} \ref{prop:cluster sep graph}, \markbox{15982}{the} \markbox{15983}{cluster} \markbox{15984}{separation} \markbox{15985}{graph} \markbox{15986}{is} \markbox{15987}{an} \markbox{15988}{interval.}  \markbox{15989}{Our} \markbox{15990}{stable} \markbox{15991}{intervals} \markbox{15992}{admit} \markbox{15993}{a} \markbox{15994}{decomposition} \markbox{15995}{into} \markbox{15996}{two} \markbox{15997}{families} \markbox{15998}{of} \markbox{15999}{intervals,} \markbox{16000}{namely} \markbox{16001}{of} \emph{edge} \markbox{16002}{components} \markbox{16003}{and} \emph{cluster} \markbox{16004}{components.}  \markbox{16005}{An} \markbox{16006}{edge} \markbox{16007}{component} \markbox{16008}{connects} \markbox{16009}{adjacent} \markbox{16010}{clusters} \markbox{16011}{at} \markbox{16012}{their} \markbox{16013}{nearest} \markbox{16014}{points,} \markbox{16015}{while} \markbox{16016}{a} \markbox{16017}{cluster} \markbox{16018}{component} \markbox{16019}{connects} \markbox{16020}{the} \markbox{16021}{endpoints} \markbox{16022}{of}  \markbox{16023}{whatever} \markbox{16024}{edge} \markbox{16025}{components} \markbox{16026}{are} \markbox{16027}{connected} \markbox{16028}{to} \markbox{16029}{a} \markbox{16030}{given} cluster.

\begin{definition}[Stable interval]\label{defn:stable interval}
Let \markbox{m16031}{$\calZ$} \markbox{16032}{be} \markbox{m16033}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic, \markbox{m16034}{$a,b \in \calZ$} \markbox{16035}{with} \markbox{m16036}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{16037}{a} \markbox{16038}{geodesic} \markbox{16039}{connecting} \markbox{16040}{them,} \markbox{16041}{and} \markbox{m16042}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{16043}{finite} \markbox{16044}{with} \markbox{m16045}{$\calY \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b))$}.  \markbox{16046}{The} \emph{stable interval} \markbox{16047}{for} \markbox{16048}{this} \markbox{16049}{setup} \markbox{16050}{is} \markbox{16051}{the} \markbox{16052}{union} \markbox{16053}{of} \markbox{16054}{the} \markbox{16055}{following} \markbox{16056}{two} \markbox{16057}{families} \markbox{16058}{of} \markbox{16059}{geodesic} segments:

\begin{enumerate}
\item (Edge \markbox{16060}{components)} \markbox{16061}{For} \markbox{16062}{each} \markbox{16063}{adjacent} \markbox{16064}{pair} \markbox{16065}{of} \markbox{m16066}{$C, C'$} \markbox{16067}{of} \markbox{16068}{clusters} \markbox{16069}{in} \markbox{m16070}{$\calG = \calG_{E,\epsilon'}(a,b;\calY)$}, \markbox{16071}{the} \emph{edge component} \markbox{16072}{between} \markbox{16073}{them} \markbox{16074}{is} \markbox{m16075}{$\lambda_0(C,C')$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item The \markbox{16076}{edge} \markbox{16077}{components} \markbox{16078}{comprise} \markbox{16079}{the} \emph{edge forest}, \markbox{16080}{which} \markbox{16081}{we} \markbox{16082}{denote} \markbox{16083}{by} \markbox{m16084}{$T_e$}.
\end{itemize}
\item (Cluster \markbox{16085}{components)} \markbox{16086}{For} \markbox{16087}{each} \markbox{16088}{cluster} \markbox{m16089}{$C$}, \markbox{16090}{we} \markbox{16091}{let} \markbox{m16092}{$C_1,C_2$} \markbox{16093}{be} \markbox{16094}{the} \markbox{16095}{clusters} \markbox{16096}{adjacent} \markbox{16097}{to} \markbox{m16098}{$C$} \markbox{16099}{in} \markbox{m16100}{$\calG$}.  \markbox{16101}{Let} \markbox{m16102}{$r(C) = C \cap (\lambda(C_1,C) \cup \lambda(C,C_2) \cup \{a,b\})$}, \markbox{16103}{where} \markbox{m16104}{$\lambda(C_i,C) = \emptyset$} \markbox{16105}{if} \markbox{m16106}{$C$} \markbox{16107}{is} \markbox{16108}{an} \markbox{16109}{endpoint} \markbox{16110}{cluster,} \markbox{16111}{for} \markbox{16112}{the} \markbox{16113}{appropriate} \markbox{m16114}{$i \in \{1,2\}$}.  \markbox{16115}{The} \markbox{16116}{cluster} \markbox{m16117}{$C$} \markbox{16118}{then} \markbox{16119}{determines} \markbox{16120}{the} \emph{cluster component} \markbox{m16121}{$\mu(C) = \lambda(r(C))$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item The \markbox{16122}{cluster} \markbox{16123}{components} \markbox{16124}{comprise} \markbox{16125}{the} \emph{cluster forest}, \markbox{16126}{which} \markbox{16127}{we} \markbox{16128}{denote} \markbox{16129}{by} \markbox{m16130}{$T_c$}.
\end{itemize} 
\end{enumerate}

\begin{itemize}
\item The \emph{stable interval} \markbox{16131}{is}  \markbox{m16132}{$T(a,b; \calY) = T_e \sqcup T_c$}, \markbox{16133}{by} \markbox{16134}{which} \markbox{16135}{we} \markbox{16136}{mean} \markbox{16137}{the} \markbox{16138}{abstract} \markbox{16139}{union} \markbox{16140}{of} \markbox{16141}{these} \markbox{16142}{two} \markbox{16143}{forests,} \markbox{16144}{where} \markbox{16145}{we} \markbox{16146}{attach} \markbox{m16147}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{16148}{to} \markbox{16149}{the} \markbox{16150}{corresponding} \markbox{16151}{endpoints} \markbox{16152}{of} \markbox{m16153}{$\mu(C_1), \mu(C_2)$} \markbox{16154}{for} \markbox{16155}{adjacent} \markbox{m16156}{$C_1, C_2$} \markbox{16157}{as} \markbox{16158}{determined} \markbox{16159}{by} \markbox{m16160}{$\calG$}.
\item We \markbox{16161}{let} \markbox{m16162}{$\phi:T(a,b;\calY) \to \calZ$} \markbox{16163}{denote} \markbox{16164}{the} \markbox{16165}{map} \markbox{16166}{induced} \markbox{16167}{from} \markbox{16168}{the} \markbox{16169}{fact} \markbox{16170}{that} \markbox{16171}{its} \markbox{16172}{pieces} \markbox{16173}{are} \markbox{16174}{geodesics} \markbox{16175}{in} \markbox{m16176}{$\calZ$}. 
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}




\begin{remark}
    \markbox{16177}{We} \markbox{16178}{note} \markbox{16179}{that} \markbox{16180}{stable} \markbox{16181}{intervals} \markbox{16182}{are} \markbox{16183}{abstractly} \markbox{16184}{intervals,} \markbox{16185}{but} \markbox{16186}{not} \markbox{16187}{necessarily} \markbox{16188}{as} \markbox{16189}{subsets} \markbox{16190}{of} \markbox{m16191}{$\calZ$}.  \markbox{16192}{In} \markbox{16193}{particular,} \markbox{16194}{the} \markbox{16195}{points} \markbox{m16196}{$a,b$} \markbox{16197}{need} \markbox{16198}{not} \markbox{16199}{be} \markbox{16200}{the} ``endpoints'' \markbox{16201}{of} \markbox{16202}{the} \markbox{16203}{stable} \markbox{16204}{interval} \markbox{m16205}{$T$}, \markbox{16206}{either} \markbox{16207}{abstractly} \markbox{16208}{or} \markbox{16209}{in} \markbox{m16210}{$\calZ$}.  \markbox{16211}{However,} \markbox{16212}{their} \markbox{16213}{images} \markbox{16214}{in} \markbox{16215}{the} \markbox{16216}{collapsed} \markbox{16217}{stable} \markbox{16218}{interval} \markbox{16219}{will} \markbox{16220}{be} \markbox{16221}{the} \markbox{16222}{endpoints,} \markbox{16223}{see} \markbox{16224}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:collapsed stable intervals}.
\end{remark}


The \markbox{16225}{following} \markbox{16226}{lemma} \markbox{16227}{is} \markbox{16228}{the} \markbox{16229}{key} \markbox{16230}{to} \markbox{16231}{controlling} \markbox{16232}{the} \markbox{16233}{structure} \markbox{16234}{of} \markbox{m16235}{$T(a,b;\calY)$}.  \markbox{16236}{We} \markbox{16237}{omit} \markbox{16238}{its} \markbox{16239}{proof} \markbox{16240}{since} \markbox{16241}{it} \markbox{16242}{again} \markbox{16243}{uses} \markbox{16244}{only} \markbox{16245}{hyperbolic} \markbox{16246}{geometry,} \markbox{16247}{though} \markbox{16248}{see} \markbox{16249}{Figure} \ref{fig:cluster close} \markbox{16250}{for} \markbox{16251}{a} schematic:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:cluster close}
Let \markbox{m16252}{$C_1, C_2$} \markbox{16253}{be} \markbox{16254}{distinct} \markbox{16255}{clusters} \markbox{16256}{along} \markbox{m16257}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{16258}{Suppose} \markbox{16259}{that} \markbox{m16260}{$p_1 \in C_1$} \markbox{16261}{and} \markbox{m16262}{$p_2 \in C_2$} \markbox{16263}{are} \markbox{16264}{closest} \markbox{16265}{points,} \markbox{16266}{while} \markbox{m16267}{$x_1 \in s(C_1)$} \markbox{16268}{and} \markbox{m16269}{$x_2 \in s(C_2)$} \markbox{16270}{are} \markbox{16271}{closest} \markbox{16272}{points.}  \markbox{16273}{Then} \markbox{m16274}{$d_{\calZ}(x_i, p_i) \leq 7\epsilon$} \markbox{16275}{for} \markbox{m16276}{$i=1,2$}.

As \markbox{16277}{a} \markbox{16278}{consequence,} \markbox{16279}{the} \markbox{16280}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item For \markbox{16281}{distinct} \markbox{16282}{clusters} \markbox{m16283}{$C_1,C_2$}, \markbox{16284}{we} \markbox{16285}{have} \markbox{m16286}{$|d(C_1,C_2) - d(s(C_1),s(C_2))| < 14\epsilon.$}
\item For \markbox{16287}{any} \markbox{m16288}{$p \in T_e$}, \markbox{16289}{we} \markbox{16290}{have} \markbox{16291}{that} \markbox{m16292}{$d_{\calZ}(p, \calY \cup \{a,b\}) \leq d_{\calZ}(p, \partial T_e) + O(\epsilon).$}
\item For \markbox{16293}{any} \markbox{16294}{components} \markbox{m16295}{$V,W$} \markbox{16296}{of} \markbox{m16297}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$}, \markbox{16298}{we} \markbox{16299}{have} \markbox{m16300}{$\diam_{\calZ}(s(V)\cap s(W)) < O(\epsilon)$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{lemma}



\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.75\textwidth]{figures/cluster_close}
    \caption{Proof of Lemma \ref{lem:cluster close}: Clusters can have multiple pairs of closest points.  In this example, the red and pink points on $C_1$ are equidistant from their matching point on $C_2$, while the red and pink cluster points in $C_1$ are both within $7\epsilon$ of the endpoint of the shadow $s(C_1)$ nearest $s(C_2)$, and the same for the roles of $C_1,C_2$ switched.  In subsequent arguments, this will allow us to conclude that connecting points between clusters are close even after we alter the clusters.}
    \label{fig:cluster close}
\end{figure}




\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=1\textwidth]{figures/pathologies.pdf}
    \caption{This figure, which is essentially \cite[Figure 11]{DMS_bary}, is an example of two phenomena.  First, the edge components of a stable interval can have bounded overlap in the space $\calZ$.  This can lead to a bounded multiplicative error in the quasi-isometric embedding $\phi:T(a,b;\calY) \to \calZ$; see item (3) of Proposition \ref{prop:stable interval structure}.  In the figure, the multiplicative constant is at least $\frac{102}{100}$.  Second, the image of $T(a,b;\calY)$ in $\calZ$ need not itself be an interval, as the clusters can form leaves on the image.}
    \label{fig:pathologies}
\end{figure}


With \markbox{16301}{the} \markbox{16302}{above} \markbox{16303}{lemma} \markbox{16304}{in} \markbox{16305}{hand,} \markbox{16306}{we} \markbox{16307}{can} \markbox{16308}{prove} \markbox{16309}{the} \markbox{16310}{following} \markbox{16311}{structural} \markbox{16312}{proposition:}                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
 
 \begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable interval structure}
 
There \markbox{16313}{exists} \markbox{m16314}{$L_0 = L_0(\delta, \epsilon)>0$} \markbox{16315}{so} \markbox{16316}{that} \markbox{16317}{the} \markbox{16318}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m16319}{$T(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{16320}{is} \markbox{16321}{an} \markbox{16322}{interval} \markbox{16323}{with} \markbox{16324}{endpoints} \markbox{16325}{contained} \markbox{16326}{in} \markbox{m16327}{$\calY \cup \{a,b\}$} \markbox{16328}{whose} \markbox{16329}{images} \markbox{16330}{in} \markbox{m16331}{$\calZ$} \markbox{16332}{are} \markbox{m16333}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{16334}{of} \markbox{m16335}{$a,b \in \calZ$}.
\item For \markbox{16336}{every} \markbox{16337}{cluster} \markbox{m16338}{$C$},we \markbox{16339}{have} \markbox{16340}{that} \markbox{m16341}{$d_{\calZ}^{Haus}(\mu(C), C) < L_0$} \markbox{16342}{and} \markbox{m16343}{$\phi(T_C) \subset \calN_{L_0}(\calY \cup \{a,b\})$}. 
\item The \markbox{16344}{map} \markbox{m16345}{$\phi:T(a,b;\calY) \to \calZ$} \markbox{16346}{is} \markbox{16347}{an} \markbox{m16348}{$(L_0,L_0)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{16349}{embedding} \markbox{16350}{with} \markbox{16351}{image} \markbox{m16352}{$L_0$}-Hausdorff \markbox{16353}{close} \markbox{16354}{to} \markbox{m16355}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.
\item Each \markbox{16356}{edge} \markbox{16357}{component} \markbox{16358}{of} \markbox{m16359}{$T$} \markbox{16360}{has} \markbox{16361}{positive} \markbox{16362}{integer} length.
\end{enumerate}
 \end{proposition}
 
 \begin{proof}
 
 \markbox{16363}{For} \markbox{16364}{(1),} \markbox{16365}{observe} \markbox{16366}{that} \markbox{m16367}{$T(a,b;\calZ)$} \markbox{16368}{is} \markbox{16369}{an} \markbox{16370}{interval} \markbox{16371}{by} \markbox{16372}{construction} \markbox{16373}{and} \markbox{16374}{Proposition} \ref{prop:cluster sep graph}, \markbox{16375}{and} \markbox{16376}{the} \markbox{16377}{end} \markbox{16378}{clusters} \markbox{16379}{contain} \markbox{m16380}{$a,b$}, \markbox{16381}{respectively,} \markbox{16382}{also} \markbox{16383}{by} \markbox{16384}{that} \markbox{16385}{proposition.}  \markbox{16386}{Since} \markbox{16387}{each} \markbox{16388}{cluster} \markbox{m16389}{$C \subset \calN_{E}(\lambda(a,b))$}, \markbox{16390}{if} \markbox{m16391}{$a \in C$}, \markbox{16392}{then} \markbox{16393}{the} \markbox{16394}{outer-most} \markbox{16395}{endpoint} \markbox{16396}{of} \markbox{m16397}{$\mu(C)$} \markbox{16398}{must} \markbox{16399}{be} \markbox{16400}{within} \markbox{m16401}{$E$} \markbox{16402}{of} \markbox{m16403}{$a$}, \markbox{16404}{as} required.
 
 \markbox{16405}{For} \markbox{16406}{(2),} \markbox{16407}{observe} \markbox{16408}{that} \markbox{16409}{each} \markbox{16410}{cluster} \markbox{m16411}{$C$} \markbox{16412}{is} \markbox{16413}{within} \markbox{16414}{Hausdorff} \markbox{16415}{distance} \markbox{m16416}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{16417}{of} \markbox{m16418}{$s(C)$}, \markbox{16419}{while} \markbox{16420}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{16421}{implies} \markbox{16422}{that} \markbox{m16423}{$\mu(C)$} \markbox{16424}{is} \markbox{16425}{within} \markbox{16426}{Hausdorff} \markbox{16427}{distance} \markbox{m16428}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{16429}{of} \markbox{m16430}{$s(C)$}.  \markbox{16431}{The} \markbox{16432}{conclusion} follows.
 
 \markbox{16433}{Item} \markbox{16434}{(3)} \markbox{16435}{is} \markbox{16436}{essentially} \markbox{16437}{a} \markbox{16438}{consequence} \markbox{16439}{of} \markbox{16440}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{16441}{and} \markbox{16442}{the} \markbox{16443}{construction} \markbox{16444}{as} \markbox{16445}{follows.}  \markbox{16446}{By} \markbox{16447}{Lemma} \ref{lem:Morse close}, \markbox{16448}{the} \markbox{16449}{image} \markbox{16450}{under} \markbox{16451}{the} \markbox{16452}{map} \markbox{m16453}{$\phi:T \to \calZ$} \markbox{16454}{of} \markbox{16455}{each} \markbox{16456}{component} \markbox{16457}{of} \markbox{m16458}{$T_e$} \markbox{16459}{and} \markbox{m16460}{$T_c$} \markbox{16461}{is} \markbox{16462}{within} \markbox{m16463}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{16464}{of} \markbox{16465}{its} \markbox{16466}{shadow} \markbox{16467}{on} \markbox{m16468}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{16469}{In} \markbox{16470}{other} \markbox{16471}{words,} \markbox{16472}{for} \markbox{16473}{any} \markbox{16474}{component} \markbox{m16475}{$V$} \markbox{16476}{of} \markbox{m16477}{$T_e$} \markbox{16478}{or} \markbox{m16479}{$T_c$}, \markbox{16480}{the} \markbox{16481}{shadow} \markbox{16482}{map} \markbox{16483}{induces} \markbox{16484}{a} \markbox{m16485}{$(1,O(\epsilon))$}-quasi-isometry \markbox{m16486}{$s:\phi(V) \to s(\phi(V))$}.  \markbox{16487}{On} \markbox{16488}{the} \markbox{16489}{other} \markbox{16490}{hand,} \markbox{16491}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{16492}{says} \markbox{16493}{every} \markbox{16494}{pair} \markbox{16495}{of} \markbox{16496}{components} \markbox{16497}{of} \markbox{m16498}{$T$} \markbox{16499}{have} \markbox{16500}{shadows} \markbox{16501}{on} \markbox{m16502}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{16503}{with} \markbox{m16504}{$O(\epsilon)$}-bounded \markbox{16505}{overlap.}  \markbox{16506}{It} \markbox{16507}{follows} \markbox{16508}{that} \markbox{m16509}{$\phi:T \to \calZ$} \markbox{16510}{is} \markbox{16511}{an} \markbox{m16512}{$(O(\epsilon), O(\epsilon))$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{16513}{embedding,} \markbox{16514}{as} required.
 
 \markbox{16515}{Finally,} \markbox{16516}{item} \markbox{16517}{(4)} \markbox{16518}{follows} \markbox{16519}{because} \markbox{16520}{we} \markbox{16521}{have} \markbox{16522}{used} \markbox{16523}{the} \markbox{16524}{function} \markbox{m16525}{$\lambda_0$} \markbox{16526}{as} \markbox{16527}{our} \markbox{16528}{connectors} \markbox{16529}{in} \markbox{16530}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable interval}, \markbox{16531}{which} \markbox{16532}{performs} \markbox{16533}{a} \markbox{16534}{small} \markbox{16535}{surgery} \markbox{16536}{at} \markbox{16537}{one} \markbox{16538}{of} \markbox{16539}{the} \markbox{16540}{ends} \markbox{16541}{of} \markbox{m16542}{$\lambda$} \markbox{16543}{so} \markbox{16544}{that} \markbox{16545}{the} \markbox{16546}{result} \markbox{16547}{has} \markbox{16548}{integer} \markbox{16549}{length.}  \markbox{16550}{This} \markbox{16551}{completes} \markbox{16552}{the} proof.
\end{proof}


\subsection{Stable decompositions}\label{subsec:stable decomp}

Having \markbox{16553}{defined} \markbox{16554}{stable} \markbox{16555}{intervals} \markbox{16556}{above,} \markbox{16557}{we} \markbox{16558}{are} \markbox{16559}{almost} \markbox{16560}{ready} \markbox{16561}{to} \markbox{16562}{state} \markbox{16563}{the} \markbox{16564}{Stable} \markbox{16565}{Intervals} \markbox{16566}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.  \markbox{16567}{The} \markbox{16568}{motivation} \markbox{16569}{for} \markbox{16570}{the} \markbox{16571}{definitions} \markbox{16572}{in} \markbox{16573}{this} \markbox{16574}{section} \markbox{16575}{comes} \markbox{16576}{from} \markbox{16577}{our} \markbox{16578}{desire} \markbox{16579}{to} \markbox{16580}{plug} \markbox{16581}{things} \markbox{16582}{into} \markbox{16583}{our} \markbox{16584}{cubical} \markbox{16585}{model} \markbox{16586}{machinery.}  \markbox{16587}{We} \markbox{16588}{describe} \markbox{16589}{how} \markbox{16590}{this} \markbox{16591}{works} \markbox{16592}{in} \markbox{16593}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:perturbed to stable} \markbox{16594}{below,} \markbox{16595}{and} \markbox{16596}{we} \markbox{16597}{point} \markbox{16598}{the} \markbox{16599}{reader} \markbox{16600}{to} \markbox{16601}{it} \markbox{16602}{for} \markbox{16603}{motivation} \markbox{16604}{for} \markbox{16605}{what} follows.

A \markbox{16606}{stable} \markbox{16607}{decomposition} \markbox{16608}{involves} \markbox{16609}{decomposing} \markbox{16610}{a} \markbox{16611}{pair} \markbox{16612}{of} \markbox{16613}{stable} \markbox{16614}{intervals} \markbox{16615}{for} \markbox{16616}{a} \markbox{16617}{pair} \markbox{16618}{of} \markbox{16619}{admissible} \markbox{16620}{setups} \markbox{16621}{into} \markbox{16622}{subintervals,} \markbox{16623}{with} \markbox{16624}{some} \markbox{16625}{maps} \markbox{16626}{which} \markbox{16627}{identify} \markbox{16628}{and} \markbox{16629}{organize} \markbox{16630}{the} \markbox{16631}{various} \markbox{16632}{pieces.}  \markbox{16633}{The} \markbox{16634}{purpose} \markbox{16635}{of} \markbox{16636}{the} \markbox{16637}{next} \markbox{16638}{definition} \markbox{16639}{is} \markbox{16640}{to} \markbox{16641}{give} \markbox{16642}{shorthand} \markbox{16643}{for} \markbox{16644}{requiring} \markbox{16645}{that} \markbox{16646}{the} \markbox{16647}{various} \markbox{16648}{maps} \markbox{16649}{involved} \markbox{16650}{respect} \markbox{16651}{how} \markbox{16652}{the} \markbox{16653}{various} \markbox{16654}{pieces} \markbox{16655}{are} \markbox{16656}{oriented} \markbox{16657}{towards} \markbox{16658}{the} \markbox{16659}{endpoints} \markbox{16660}{of} \markbox{16661}{the} \markbox{16662}{ambient} intervals.

\begin{definition}[Order-preserving maps]\label{defn:order preserving}
Let \markbox{m16663}{$T_1, T_2$} \markbox{16664}{be} \markbox{16665}{two} \markbox{16666}{intervals} \markbox{16667}{with} \markbox{16668}{the} \markbox{16669}{endpoints} \markbox{16670}{of} \markbox{m16671}{$T_i$} \markbox{16672}{labeled} \markbox{16673}{by} \markbox{m16674}{$a_i,b_i$}.  \markbox{16675}{Suppose} \markbox{16676}{that} \markbox{m16677}{$T_i = T_{i,1} \sqcup T_{i,2}$} \markbox{16678}{are} \markbox{16679}{subdivisions} \markbox{16680}{of} \markbox{m16681}{$T_i$} \markbox{16682}{into} \markbox{16683}{finite} \markbox{16684}{collections} \markbox{16685}{of} \markbox{16686}{subintervals} \markbox{16687}{with} \markbox{m16688}{$\# T_{1,1} = \#T_{2,1}$} \markbox{16689}{(and} \markbox{16690}{hence} \markbox{m16691}{$\#T_{1,2} = \#T_{2,2}$}).

\begin{itemize}
\item We \markbox{16692}{say} \markbox{16693}{an} \markbox{16694}{isometry} \markbox{m16695}{$i_{E,E'}:E \to E'$} \markbox{16696}{between} \markbox{16697}{components} \markbox{m16698}{$E \subset T_{1,1}$} \markbox{16699}{and} \markbox{m16700}{$E' \subset T_{2,1}$} \markbox{16701}{is} \emph{order preserving} \markbox{16702}{if} \markbox{m16703}{$i_{E,E'}$} \markbox{16704}{sends} \markbox{16705}{the} \markbox{16706}{endpoint} \markbox{16707}{of} \markbox{m16708}{$E$} \markbox{16709}{closest} \markbox{16710}{to} \markbox{m16711}{$a_1$} \markbox{16712}{to} \markbox{16713}{the} \markbox{16714}{endpoint} \markbox{16715}{of} \markbox{m16716}{$E'$} \markbox{16717}{closest} \markbox{16718}{to} \markbox{m16719}{$a_2$}.
\item We \markbox{16720}{say} \markbox{16721}{a} \markbox{16722}{bijection} \markbox{m16723}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_{1,1}) \to \pi_0(T_{2,1})$} \markbox{16724}{is} \emph{order-preserving} \markbox{16725}{if} \markbox{16726}{it} \markbox{16727}{coincides} \markbox{16728}{with} \markbox{16729}{the} \markbox{16730}{bijection} \markbox{16731}{obtained} \markbox{16732}{by} \markbox{16733}{recording} \markbox{16734}{the} \markbox{16735}{orders} \markbox{16736}{of} \markbox{16737}{appearance} \markbox{16738}{of} \markbox{16739}{the} \markbox{16740}{components} \markbox{16741}{of} \markbox{m16742}{$T_{i,1}$} \markbox{16743}{along} \markbox{m16744}{$T_i$} \markbox{16745}{from} \markbox{m16746}{$a_i$} \markbox{16747}{to} \markbox{m16748}{$b_i$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}\label{rem:order preserving}
Using \markbox{16749}{the} \markbox{16750}{above} \markbox{16751}{notation,} \markbox{16752}{note} \markbox{16753}{that} \markbox{16754}{an} \markbox{16755}{order-preserving} \markbox{16756}{bijection} \markbox{m16757}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_{1,1}) \to \pi_0(T_{2,1})$} \markbox{16758}{automatically} \markbox{16759}{induces} \markbox{16760}{an} \markbox{16761}{order-preserving} \markbox{16762}{bijection} \markbox{m16763}{$\beta:\pi_0(T_{1,2}) \to \pi_0(T_{2,2})$}.  \markbox{16764}{Moreover,} \markbox{16765}{in} \markbox{16766}{this} \markbox{16767}{paper,} \markbox{16768}{we} \markbox{16769}{will} \markbox{16770}{only} \markbox{16771}{be} \markbox{16772}{working} \markbox{16773}{with} \markbox{16774}{intervals} \markbox{16775}{between} \markbox{16776}{a} \markbox{16777}{pair} \markbox{16778}{of} \markbox{16779}{points,} \markbox{16780}{which} \markbox{16781}{are} \markbox{16782}{usually} \markbox{16783}{denoted} \markbox{16784}{by} \markbox{16785}{(some} \markbox{16786}{form} \markbox{16787}{of)} \markbox{m16788}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{16789}{We} \markbox{16790}{will} \markbox{16791}{always} \markbox{16792}{take} \markbox{16793}{order-preserving} \markbox{16794}{to} \markbox{16795}{mean} \markbox{16796}{as} \markbox{16797}{one} \markbox{16798}{moves} \markbox{16799}{from} \markbox{16800}{the} \markbox{m16801}{$a$}-side \markbox{16802}{to} \markbox{16803}{the} \markbox{m16804}{$b$}-side \markbox{16805}{of} \markbox{16806}{the} \markbox{16807}{given} intervals.
\end{remark}

We \markbox{16808}{also} \markbox{16809}{set} \markbox{16810}{one} \markbox{16811}{last} \markbox{16812}{bit} \markbox{16813}{of} \markbox{16814}{notation:} \markbox{16815}{Given} \markbox{16816}{a} \markbox{16817}{stable} \markbox{16818}{tree} \markbox{m16819}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$} \markbox{16820}{for} \markbox{16821}{an} \markbox{m16822}{$\epsilon$}-setup \markbox{m16823}{$(\calY; \{a,b\})$}, \markbox{16824}{if} \markbox{m16825}{$y \in \calY \cup \{a,b\}$}, \markbox{16826}{we} \markbox{16827}{let} \markbox{m16828}{$C_y$} \markbox{16829}{denote} \markbox{16830}{the} \markbox{16831}{cluster} \markbox{16832}{containing} \markbox{m16833}{$y$}, \markbox{16834}{and} \markbox{m16835}{$\mu(C_y)$} \markbox{16836}{the} \markbox{16837}{corresponding} \markbox{16838}{component} \markbox{16839}{of} \markbox{m16840}{$T^c$}.

The \markbox{16841}{following} \markbox{16842}{definition} \markbox{16843}{contains} \markbox{16844}{the} \markbox{16845}{stability} \markbox{16846}{properties} \markbox{16847}{we} want:

\begin{definition}[Stable decomposition] \label{defn:stable decomp}
Let \markbox{m16848}{$\calZ$} \markbox{16849}{be} \markbox{m16850}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{16851}{and} \markbox{16852}{geodesic.}  
\begin{enumerate}
\item Given \markbox{m16853}{$N>0$}, \markbox{16854}{two} \markbox{m16855}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{m16856}{$(a,b; \calY)$} \markbox{16857}{and} \markbox{m16858}{$(a',b'; \calY')$} \markbox{16859}{are} \markbox{m16860}{$(N,\epsilon)$}-\emph{admissible} if
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m16861}{$d_{\calZ}(a,a'), d_{\calZ}(b,b') \leq \epsilon$},
\item \markbox{m16862}{$\calY, \calY' \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b)) \cap \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a',b'))$},
\item \markbox{m16863}{$|\calY \triangle \calY'| < N$}.
\end{enumerate}
\item Given \markbox{16864}{an} \markbox{m16865}{$\epsilon$}-setup \markbox{m16866}{$(a,b;\calY)$}, \markbox{16867}{an} \emph{edge decomposition} \markbox{16868}{of} \markbox{16869}{its} \markbox{16870}{stable} \markbox{16871}{interval} \markbox{m16872}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$} \markbox{16873}{is} \markbox{16874}{a} \markbox{16875}{collection} \markbox{16876}{of} \markbox{16877}{subintervals} \markbox{m16878}{$T_s \subset T_e$}.
\item Given \markbox{m16879}{$L>0$}, \markbox{m16880}{$\calY_0 \subset \calY \cap \calY'$}, \markbox{16881}{and} \markbox{16882}{two} \markbox{m16883}{$(N,\epsilon)$}-admissible \markbox{16884}{setups} \markbox{m16885}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{16886}{and} \markbox{m16887}{$(a',b'; \calY')$}, \markbox{16888}{we} \markbox{16889}{say} \markbox{16890}{that} \markbox{16891}{two} \markbox{16892}{edge} \markbox{16893}{decompositions} \markbox{m16894}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{16895}{and} \markbox{m16896}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$} \markbox{16897}{are} \markbox{m16898}{$\calY_0$}-\emph{stably} \markbox{m16899}{$L$}-\emph{compatible} if
\begin{enumerate}
\item Each \markbox{16900}{component} \markbox{16901}{of} \markbox{m16902}{$T_s$} \markbox{16903}{and} \markbox{m16904}{$T'_s$} \markbox{16905}{has} \markbox{16906}{positive} \markbox{16907}{integer} \markbox{16908}{length} \markbox{16909}{with} \markbox{16910}{endpoints} \markbox{16911}{at} \markbox{16912}{vertices} \markbox{16913}{of} \markbox{m16914}{$T_e$} \markbox{16915}{and} \markbox{m16916}{$T'_e$}, \markbox{16917}{respectively.} \label{item:integer length}
\item There \markbox{16918}{is} \markbox{16919}{an} \markbox{16920}{order-preserving} \markbox{16921}{bijection} \markbox{m16922}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_s) \to \pi_0(T'_s)$} \markbox{16923}{between} \markbox{16924}{the} \markbox{16925}{sets} \markbox{16926}{of} \markbox{16927}{stable} \markbox{16928}{components.} \label{item:stable bijection}
\item For \markbox{16929}{each} \emph{stable pair} \markbox{m16930}{$(E, E')$} \markbox{16931}{identified} \markbox{16932}{by} \markbox{m16933}{$\alpha$}, \markbox{16934}{there} \markbox{16935}{exists} \markbox{16936}{an} \markbox{16937}{order-preserving} \markbox{16938}{isometry} \markbox{m16939}{$i_{E,E'}:E \to E'$}. \label{item:stable pairs}
\item For \markbox{16940}{all} \markbox{16941}{but} \markbox{16942}{at} \markbox{16943}{most} \markbox{m16944}{$L$} \markbox{16945}{pairs} \markbox{16946}{of} \markbox{16947}{stable} \markbox{16948}{components} \markbox{m16949}{$(E,E')$}, \markbox{16950}{we} \markbox{16951}{have} \markbox{m16952}{$\phi(E) = \phi(E')$} \markbox{16953}{are} \markbox{16954}{identical} \markbox{16955}{with} \markbox{m16956}{$\phi(x) = \phi'(i_{E,E'}(x))$} \markbox{16957}{for} \markbox{16958}{all} \markbox{m16959}{$x \in E$}. \label{item:identical pairs}
\item For \markbox{16960}{the} \markbox{16961}{(at} \markbox{16962}{most)} \markbox{m16963}{$L$}-many \markbox{16964}{remaining} \markbox{16965}{stable} \markbox{16966}{pairs} \markbox{m16967}{$(E,E')$}, \markbox{16968}{we} \markbox{16969}{have} \markbox{m16970}{$d_{\calZ}(\phi(x), \phi'(i_{E,E'}(x)))< L$} \markbox{16971}{for} \markbox{16972}{all} \markbox{m16973}{$x \in E$}. \label{item:close pairs}
\item The \markbox{16974}{complements} \markbox{m16975}{$T_{e} - T_s$} \markbox{16976}{and} \markbox{m16977}{$T'_{e} - T'_s$} \markbox{16978}{consist} \markbox{16979}{of} \markbox{16980}{at} \markbox{16981}{most} \markbox{m16982}{$L$}-many \emph{unstable components} \markbox{16983}{of} \markbox{16984}{diameter} \markbox{16985}{at} \markbox{16986}{most} \markbox{m16987}{$L$}.\label{item:unstable components}
\item The \markbox{16988}{induced} \markbox{16989}{order-preserving} \markbox{16990}{bijection} \markbox{m16991}{$\beta:\pi_0(T-T_s) \to \pi_0(T' - T'_s)$} \markbox{16992}{satisfies:} \label{item:adjacency}
\begin{enumerate}
\item (Endpoints) \markbox{16993}{Let} \markbox{m16994}{$D_a$} \markbox{16995}{denote} \markbox{16996}{the} \markbox{16997}{component} \markbox{16998}{of} \markbox{m16999}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17000}{containing} \markbox{m17001}{$\mu(C_a)$}, \markbox{17002}{and} \markbox{17003}{define} \markbox{m17004}{$D_b,D_{a'},D_{b'}$} \markbox{17005}{similarly.}  \markbox{17006}{Then} \markbox{m17007}{$\beta(D_a) = D_{a'}$} \markbox{17008}{and} \markbox{m17009}{$\beta(D_b) = D_{b'}$}. \label{item:endpoint condition}
\item (Identifying \markbox{17010}{clusters)} \markbox{17011}{For} \markbox{17012}{any} \markbox{m17013}{$y \in \calY_0$}, \markbox{17014}{let} \markbox{m17015}{$D_y, D'_y$} \markbox{17016}{denote} \markbox{17017}{the} \markbox{17018}{components} \markbox{17019}{of} \markbox{m17020}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17021}{and} \markbox{m17022}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{17023}{containing} \markbox{m17024}{$\mu(C_y), \mu(C'_y)$}, \markbox{17025}{respectively.}  \markbox{17026}{Then} \markbox{m17027}{$\beta(D_y) = D'_y$}. \label{item:cluster identify}
\end{enumerate}
\end{enumerate}
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}%% remark 8.13
The \markbox{17028}{above} \markbox{17029}{definition} \markbox{17030}{is} \markbox{17031}{a} \markbox{17032}{refinement} \markbox{17033}{of} \markbox{17034}{the} \markbox{17035}{properties} \markbox{17036}{contained} \markbox{17037}{in} \cite[Stable \markbox{17038}{Tree} \markbox{17039}{Theorem} 3.2]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{17040}{where} \markbox{17041}{we} \markbox{17042}{have} \markbox{17043}{set} \markbox{17044}{up} \markbox{17045}{these} \markbox{17046}{stable} \markbox{17047}{decompositions} \markbox{17048}{to} \markbox{17049}{plug} \markbox{17050}{nicely} \markbox{17051}{into} \markbox{17052}{the} \markbox{17053}{cubical} \markbox{17054}{model} \markbox{17055}{machinery} \markbox{17056}{described} \markbox{17057}{earlier} \markbox{17058}{in} \markbox{17059}{the} \markbox{17060}{paper.} \markbox{17061}{How} \markbox{17062}{this} \markbox{17063}{process} \markbox{17064}{works} \markbox{17065}{is} \markbox{17066}{described} \markbox{17067}{below} \markbox{17068}{in} \markbox{17069}{more} \markbox{17070}{detail} \markbox{17071}{in} Subsection~\ref{subsec:perturbed to stable}, \markbox{17072}{but} \markbox{17073}{for} \markbox{17074}{now} \markbox{17075}{we} \markbox{17076}{motivate} \markbox{17077}{some} \markbox{17078}{parts} \markbox{17079}{of} \markbox{17080}{the} \markbox{17081}{definition.}  \markbox{17082}{Roughly} \markbox{17083}{speaking,} \markbox{17084}{the} \markbox{17085}{points} \markbox{m17086}{$\calY$} \markbox{17087}{and} \markbox{m17088}{$\calY'$} \markbox{17089}{stand} \markbox{17090}{in} \markbox{17091}{for} \markbox{17092}{the} \markbox{17093}{relative} \markbox{17094}{projection} \markbox{17095}{data} \markbox{17096}{on} \markbox{17097}{each} \markbox{17098}{interval,} \markbox{17099}{with} \markbox{17100}{each} \markbox{17101}{component} \markbox{17102}{of} \markbox{m17103}{$T - T_s$} \markbox{17104}{and} \markbox{m17105}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{17106}{being} \markbox{17107}{labeled} \markbox{17108}{by} \markbox{17109}{some} \markbox{17110}{such} \markbox{17111}{point.}  \markbox{17112}{Eventually,} \markbox{17113}{we} \markbox{17114}{will} \markbox{17115}{collapse} \markbox{17116}{each} \markbox{17117}{of} \markbox{17118}{the} \markbox{17119}{components} \markbox{17120}{of} \markbox{m17121}{$T - T_s$} \markbox{17122}{and} \markbox{m17123}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{17124}{to} \markbox{17125}{points.}  \markbox{17126}{Item} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{17127}{says} \markbox{17128}{that} \markbox{17129}{the} \markbox{17130}{common} \markbox{17131}{labels} \markbox{m17132}{$\calY \cap \calY'$} \markbox{17133}{are} \markbox{17134}{identified,} \markbox{17135}{as} \markbox{17136}{well} \markbox{17137}{as} \markbox{17138}{the} \markbox{17139}{endpoint} \markbox{17140}{pairs} \markbox{m17141}{$a,a'$} \markbox{17142}{and} \markbox{m17143}{$b,b'$}.  \markbox{17144}{The} \markbox{17145}{rest} \markbox{17146}{of} \markbox{17147}{the} \markbox{17148}{statement} \markbox{17149}{now} \markbox{17150}{says} \markbox{17151}{that} \markbox{17152}{the} \markbox{17153}{components} \markbox{17154}{of} \markbox{m17155}{$T_s$} \markbox{17156}{and} \markbox{m17157}{$T'_s$} \markbox{17158}{are} \markbox{17159}{in} \markbox{17160}{bijection} \markbox{17161}{with} \markbox{17162}{each} \markbox{17163}{other,} \markbox{17164}{where} \markbox{17165}{identified} \markbox{17166}{components} \markbox{17167}{are} \markbox{17168}{isometric,} \markbox{17169}{and} \markbox{17170}{the} \markbox{17171}{order-preserving} \markbox{17172}{properties} \markbox{17173}{explain} \markbox{17174}{how} \markbox{17175}{to} \markbox{17176}{glue} \markbox{17177}{these} \markbox{17178}{components} \markbox{17179}{to} \markbox{17180}{obtain} \markbox{17181}{an} \markbox{17182}{isometry} \markbox{17183}{between} \markbox{17184}{collapsed} \markbox{17185}{intervals.}  \markbox{17186}{Finally,} \markbox{17187}{the} \markbox{17188}{proximity} \markbox{17189}{properties} \markbox{17190}{in} \markbox{17191}{items} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{17192}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{17193}{are} \markbox{17194}{necessary} \markbox{17195}{for} \markbox{17196}{controlling} \markbox{17197}{the} \markbox{17198}{maps} \markbox{17199}{back} \markbox{17200}{into} \markbox{17201}{the} \markbox{17202}{ambient} \markbox{17203}{HHS;} \markbox{17204}{see} \markbox{17205}{the} \markbox{17206}{proof} \markbox{17207}{of} \markbox{17208}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}.  \markbox{17209}{A} \markbox{17210}{more} \markbox{17211}{general} \markbox{17212}{version} \markbox{17213}{can} \markbox{17214}{be} \markbox{17215}{found} \markbox{17216}{in} \cite[Definition 10.18]{DMS_FJ}. 
\end{remark}

\subsection{The stable interval theorem}

With \markbox{17217}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{17218}{in} \markbox{17219}{hand,} \markbox{17220}{we} \markbox{17221}{can} \markbox{17222}{now} \markbox{17223}{state} \markbox{17224}{the} \markbox{17225}{main} \markbox{17226}{result} \markbox{17227}{of} \markbox{17228}{this} \markbox{17229}{section,} \markbox{17230}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{17231}{below.}  \markbox{17232}{It} \markbox{17233}{says} \markbox{17234}{that} \markbox{17235}{the} \markbox{17236}{stable} \markbox{17237}{intervals} \markbox{17238}{for} \markbox{17239}{a} \markbox{17240}{pair} \markbox{17241}{of} \markbox{17242}{admissible} \markbox{m17243}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{17244}{admit} \markbox{17245}{compatible} \markbox{17246}{stable} \markbox{17247}{decompositions---that} \markbox{17248}{is,} \markbox{17249}{decompositions} \markbox{17250}{into} \markbox{17251}{subintervals} \markbox{17252}{which} \markbox{17253}{are} \markbox{17254}{in} \markbox{17255}{bijective} \markbox{17256}{correspondence} \markbox{17257}{with} \markbox{17258}{idenitified} \markbox{17259}{pairs} \markbox{17260}{uniformly} \markbox{17261}{close,} \markbox{17262}{up} \markbox{17263}{to} \markbox{17264}{ignored} \markbox{17265}{a} \markbox{17266}{bounded} \markbox{17267}{collection} \markbox{17268}{of} \markbox{17269}{bounded-length} \markbox{17270}{subintervals.}  \markbox{17271}{We} \markbox{17272}{first} \markbox{17273}{state} \markbox{17274}{this} \markbox{17275}{technical} \markbox{17276}{result,} \markbox{17277}{and} \markbox{17278}{then} \markbox{17279}{prove} \markbox{17280}{a} \markbox{17281}{corollary} \markbox{17282}{which} \markbox{17283}{gives} \markbox{17284}{the} \markbox{17285}{main} \markbox{17286}{upshot} \markbox{17287}{for} \markbox{17288}{our} \markbox{17289}{purposes} \markbox{17290}{of} \markbox{17291}{building} \markbox{17292}{stable} \markbox{17293}{cubical} \markbox{17294}{models.}  

For \markbox{17295}{a} \markbox{17296}{bit} \markbox{17297}{of} \markbox{17298}{setup,} \markbox{17299}{recall} \markbox{17300}{the} \markbox{17301}{notion} \markbox{17302}{of} \markbox{17303}{a} \markbox{17304}{thickening} \markbox{17305}{of} \markbox{17306}{an} \markbox{17307}{interval} \markbox{17308}{from} \markbox{17309}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:thickenings}.  \markbox{17310}{This} \markbox{17311}{was} \markbox{17312}{a} \markbox{17313}{way} \markbox{17314}{of} \markbox{17315}{taking} \markbox{17316}{an} \markbox{17317}{interval} \markbox{17318}{with} \markbox{17319}{a} \markbox{17320}{decomposition} \markbox{m17321}{$T = A \cup B$} \markbox{17322}{into} \markbox{17323}{collections} \markbox{17324}{of} \markbox{17325}{segments,} \markbox{17326}{and} \markbox{17327}{expanding} \markbox{17328}{and} \markbox{17329}{combining} \markbox{17330}{one} \markbox{17331}{collection} \markbox{17332}{of} \markbox{17333}{the} \markbox{17334}{segments.}  \markbox{17335}{Our} \markbox{17336}{stable} \markbox{17337}{intervals} \markbox{17338}{come} \markbox{17339}{with} \markbox{17340}{such} \markbox{17341}{a} \markbox{17342}{decomposition} \markbox{m17343}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$}, \markbox{17344}{and} \markbox{17345}{we} \markbox{17346}{will} \markbox{17347}{always} \markbox{17348}{mean} \markbox{17349}{a} \markbox{17350}{thickening} \markbox{17351}{of} \markbox{17352}{a} \markbox{17353}{stable} \markbox{17354}{interval} \markbox{m17355}{$T$} \markbox{17356}{to} \markbox{17357}{be} \markbox{17358}{a} \markbox{17359}{thickening} \markbox{17360}{of} \markbox{m17361}{$T$} \markbox{17362}{along} \markbox{17363}{the} \markbox{17364}{components} \markbox{17365}{of} \markbox{17366}{the} \markbox{17367}{cluster} \markbox{17368}{forest} \markbox{m17369}{$T_c$}.  \markbox{17370}{Finally,} \markbox{17371}{we} \markbox{17372}{denote} \markbox{17373}{the} \markbox{17374}{components} \markbox{17375}{of} \markbox{17376}{the} \markbox{17377}{resulting} \markbox{17378}{thickening} \markbox{17379}{by} \markbox{m17380}{$T = \bT_{e} \cup \bT_c$}, \markbox{17381}{and} \markbox{17382}{we} \markbox{17383}{note} \markbox{17384}{that} \markbox{m17385}{$\bT_e \subset T_e$} \markbox{17386}{and} \markbox{m17387}{$T_c \subset \bT_c$}. 

\begin{theorem}[Stable intervals]\label{thm:stable intervals}
Let \markbox{m17388}{$\calZ$} \markbox{17389}{be} \markbox{m17390}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{17391}{and} \markbox{17392}{geodesic.}  \markbox{17393}{For} \markbox{17394}{any} \markbox{m17395}{$\epsilon, N>0$} \markbox{17396}{and} \markbox{17397}{positive} \markbox{17398}{integers} \markbox{m17399}{$r_1,r_2>0$}, \markbox{17400}{there} \markbox{17401}{exist} \markbox{m17402}{$L_1 = L_1(\delta, \epsilon, N)>0$} \markbox{17403}{and} \markbox{m17404}{$L_2 = L_2(\delta, \epsilon, N,r_1,r_2)>0$} \markbox{17405}{so} \markbox{17406}{that} \markbox{17407}{the} \markbox{17408}{following} \markbox{17409}{holds.}  \markbox{17410}{Suppose} \markbox{m17411}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{17412}{and} \markbox{m17413}{$(a',b';\calY')$} \markbox{17414}{are} \markbox{m17415}{$(N,\epsilon)$}-admissible \markbox{m17416}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{17417}{and} \markbox{17418}{let} \markbox{m17419}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$} \markbox{17420}{and} \markbox{m17421}{$T' = T'_e \cup T'_c$} \markbox{17422}{denote} \markbox{17423}{their} \markbox{17424}{stable} \markbox{17425}{intervals.}  Then
\begin{enumerate}
\item There \markbox{17426}{exist} \markbox{m17427}{$(\calY \cap \calY')$}-stable \markbox{m17428}{$L_1$}-compatible \markbox{17429}{decompositions} \markbox{m17430}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{17431}{and} \markbox{m17432}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$}, and
\item There \markbox{17433}{exist} \markbox{m17434}{$(\calY \cap \calY')$}-stable \markbox{m17435}{$L_2$}-compatible \markbox{17436}{edge} \markbox{17437}{decompositions} \markbox{m17438}{$\bT_{s} \subset \bT_{e}$} \markbox{17439}{and} \markbox{m17440}{$\bT'_{s} \subset \bT'_{e}$} \markbox{17441}{of} \markbox{17442}{the} \markbox{m17443}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{17444}{of} \markbox{m17445}{$T, T'$} \markbox{17446}{along} \markbox{m17447}{$T_c,T'_c$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item Moreover, \markbox{17448}{we} \markbox{17449}{have} \markbox{m17450}{$\bT_s \subset T_s$} \markbox{17451}{and} \markbox{m17452}{$\bT_s \subset T'_s$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{enumerate}

\end{theorem}

\begin{remark}
In \markbox{17453}{the} \markbox{17454}{HHS} \markbox{17455}{setting,} \markbox{17456}{we} \markbox{17457}{will} \markbox{17458}{be} \markbox{17459}{able} \markbox{17460}{to} \markbox{17461}{control} \markbox{17462}{each} \markbox{17463}{of} \markbox{17464}{the} \markbox{17465}{constants} \markbox{m17466}{$\delta, \epsilon, N, r_1,r_2$} \markbox{17467}{in} \markbox{17468}{terms} \markbox{17469}{of} \markbox{17470}{the} \markbox{17471}{ambient} \markbox{17472}{HHS} \markbox{17473}{structure.}  \markbox{17474}{We} \markbox{17475}{have} \markbox{17476}{written} \markbox{17477}{the} \markbox{17478}{statement} \markbox{17479}{with} \markbox{17480}{two} \markbox{17481}{conclusions} \markbox{17482}{because} \markbox{17483}{the} \markbox{17484}{first} \markbox{17485}{conclusion} \markbox{17486}{is} \markbox{17487}{a} \markbox{17488}{mild} \markbox{17489}{reformulation} \markbox{17490}{of} \markbox{17491}{the} \markbox{17492}{original} \markbox{17493}{theorem} \cite[Theorem 3.2]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{17494}{while} \markbox{17495}{the} \markbox{17496}{second} \markbox{17497}{is} \markbox{17498}{what} \markbox{17499}{we} \markbox{17500}{actually} \markbox{17501}{need} \markbox{17502}{for} \markbox{17503}{the} \markbox{17504}{cubulation} \markbox{17505}{machine} \markbox{17506}{discussed} \markbox{17507}{in} \markbox{17508}{this} \markbox{17509}{paper.}  \markbox{17510}{Notably,} \markbox{17511}{the} \markbox{17512}{second} \markbox{17513}{statement} \markbox{17514}{will} \markbox{17515}{be} \markbox{17516}{an} \markbox{17517}{easy} \markbox{17518}{consequence} \markbox{17519}{of} \markbox{17520}{the} first.
\end{remark}

Before \markbox{17521}{we} \markbox{17522}{move} \markbox{17523}{onto} \markbox{17524}{the} \markbox{17525}{proof,} \markbox{17526}{we} \markbox{17527}{observe} \markbox{17528}{the} \markbox{17529}{following} \markbox{17530}{corollary,} \markbox{17531}{whose} \markbox{17532}{statement} \markbox{17533}{and} \markbox{17534}{proof} \markbox{17535}{motivate} \markbox{17536}{the} \markbox{17537}{statement} \markbox{17538}{of} \markbox{17539}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.  \markbox{17540}{In} \markbox{17541}{particular,} \markbox{17542}{this} \markbox{17543}{corollary} \markbox{17544}{will} \markbox{17545}{allow} \markbox{17546}{us} \markbox{17547}{to} \markbox{17548}{verify} \markbox{17549}{the} \markbox{17550}{interval-wise} \markbox{17551}{condition} \markbox{17552}{in} \markbox{17553}{Proposition} \ref{prop:HFI isomorphism} \markbox{17554}{and} \markbox{17555}{give} \markbox{17556}{us} \markbox{17557}{the} \markbox{17558}{cubical} \markbox{17559}{isomorphism} \markbox{17560}{we} \markbox{17561}{need} \markbox{17562}{for} \markbox{17563}{the} \markbox{17564}{Stable} \markbox{17565}{Cubulations} \markbox{17566}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}; \markbox{17567}{see} \markbox{17568}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:perturbed to stable}.

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:interval isometry}
Let \markbox{m17569}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{17570}{and} \markbox{m17571}{$(a',b'; \calY')$} \markbox{17572}{be} \markbox{m17573}{$(N,\epsilon)$}-admissible \markbox{m17574}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{17575}{with} \markbox{m17576}{$(\calY \cap \calY')$}-stable \markbox{m17577}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{17578}{decompositions} \markbox{m17579}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{17580}{and} \markbox{m17581}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$}.   \markbox{17582}{Let} \markbox{m17583}{$\Delta:T \to \hT$} \markbox{17584}{and} \markbox{m17585}{$\Delta':T' \to \hT'$} \markbox{17586}{denote} \markbox{17587}{the} \markbox{17588}{quotients} \markbox{17589}{obtained} \markbox{17590}{by} \markbox{17591}{collapsing} \markbox{17592}{each} \markbox{17593}{component} \markbox{17594}{of} \markbox{m17595}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17596}{and} \markbox{m17597}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{17598}{to} \markbox{17599}{a} \markbox{17600}{point.}  \markbox{17601}{The} \markbox{17602}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m17603}{$\hT$} \markbox{17604}{and} \markbox{m17605}{$\hT'$} \markbox{17606}{are} \markbox{17607}{simplicial} \markbox{17608}{intervals} \markbox{17609}{where} \markbox{17610}{each} \markbox{17611}{collapsed} \markbox{17612}{component} \markbox{17613}{of} \markbox{m17614}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17615}{and} \markbox{m17616}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{17617}{is} \markbox{17618}{a} \markbox{17619}{vertex,} and
\item There \markbox{17620}{exists} \markbox{17621}{an} \markbox{17622}{isometry} \markbox{m17623}{$\Phi:\hT \to \hT'$} \markbox{17624}{which} \markbox{17625}{is} \markbox{17626}{induced} \markbox{17627}{from} \markbox{17628}{the} \markbox{17629}{bijections} \markbox{m17630}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_s) \to \pi_0(T'_s)$} \markbox{17631}{and} \markbox{m17632}{$\beta:\pi_0(T-T_s) \to \pi_0(T'-T'_s)$}, \markbox{17633}{and} \markbox{17634}{the} \markbox{17635}{isometries} \markbox{17636}{of} \markbox{17637}{pairs} \markbox{17638}{of} \markbox{17639}{stable} \markbox{17640}{components} \markbox{m17641}{$i_{E,\alpha(E)}:E \to \alpha(E)$} \markbox{17642}{for} \markbox{m17643}{$E \subset T_s$}.   \markbox{17644}{Moreover,} \markbox{17645}{we} have
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m17646}{$\Phi(\Delta(a)) = \Delta'(a')$} \markbox{17647}{and} \markbox{m17648}{$\Phi(\Delta(b)) = \Delta'(b')$},
\item If \markbox{m17649}{$y \in \calY \cap \calY'$} \markbox{17650}{and} \markbox{m17651}{$D_y \in \pi_0(T - T_s)$} \markbox{17652}{and} \markbox{m17653}{$D'_y \in \pi_0(T - T_s)$} \markbox{17654}{contain} \markbox{m17655}{$\mu(C_y)$} \markbox{17656}{and} \markbox{m17657}{$\mu(C'_y)$}, \markbox{17658}{respectively,} \markbox{17659}{then} \markbox{m17660}{$\Phi(\Delta(D_y)) = \Delta'(D'_y)$}. 
\end{enumerate}
\end{enumerate}
\end{corollary}


\begin{proof}
First, \markbox{17661}{observe} \markbox{17662}{that} \markbox{m17663}{$\hT$} \markbox{17664}{and} \markbox{m17665}{$\hT'$} \markbox{17666}{are} \markbox{17667}{intervals} \markbox{17668}{because} \markbox{m17669}{$T,T'$} \markbox{17670}{are} \markbox{17671}{and} \markbox{17672}{each} \markbox{17673}{component} \markbox{17674}{of} \markbox{m17675}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17676}{and} \markbox{m17677}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{17678}{is} \markbox{17679}{a} \markbox{17680}{subinterval.}  \markbox{17681}{They} \markbox{17682}{are} \markbox{17683}{simplicial} \markbox{17684}{intervals} \markbox{17685}{with} \markbox{17686}{the} \markbox{17687}{given} \markbox{17688}{description} \markbox{17689}{because} \markbox{17690}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{17691}{(specifically} \markbox{17692}{item} \markbox{17693}{(4a)} \markbox{17694}{of} \markbox{17695}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}) \markbox{17696}{provides} \markbox{17697}{that} \markbox{17698}{each} \markbox{17699}{component} \markbox{17700}{of} \markbox{m17701}{$T_s,T'_s$} \markbox{17702}{has} \markbox{17703}{positive} \markbox{17704}{integer} \markbox{17705}{length,} \markbox{17706}{and} \markbox{17707}{so} \markbox{17708}{the} \markbox{17709}{distance} \markbox{17710}{between} \markbox{17711}{the} \markbox{17712}{points} \markbox{17713}{corresponding} \markbox{17714}{to} \markbox{17715}{pairs} \markbox{17716}{of} \markbox{17717}{collapsed} \markbox{17718}{components} \markbox{17719}{of} \markbox{m17720}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17721}{and} \markbox{m17722}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{17723}{is} \markbox{17724}{a} \markbox{17725}{positive} integer.

For \markbox{17726}{the} \markbox{17727}{second} \markbox{17728}{conclusion,} \markbox{17729}{we} \markbox{17730}{can} \markbox{17731}{define} \markbox{m17732}{$\Phi:\hT\to \hT'$} \markbox{17733}{as} \markbox{17734}{follows:} \markbox{17735}{For} \markbox{17736}{each} \markbox{17737}{vertex} \markbox{m17738}{$v \in \hT$} \markbox{17739}{corresponding} \markbox{17740}{to} \markbox{17741}{a} \markbox{17742}{component} \markbox{m17743}{$C \in \pi_0(T-T_s)$}, \markbox{17744}{we} \markbox{17745}{define} \markbox{m17746}{$\Phi(v) = v'$}, \markbox{17747}{where} \markbox{m17748}{$v'$} \markbox{17749}{is} \markbox{17750}{the} \markbox{17751}{vertex} \markbox{17752}{of} \markbox{m17753}{$\hT'$} \markbox{17754}{corresponding} \markbox{17755}{to} \markbox{m17756}{$\beta(C) \in \pi_0(T'-T'_s)$}.  \markbox{17757}{If} \markbox{17758}{now} \markbox{m17759}{$x \in \hT$} \markbox{17760}{is} \markbox{17761}{not} \markbox{17762}{such} \markbox{17763}{a} \markbox{17764}{vertex,} \markbox{17765}{then} \markbox{m17766}{$x \in \Delta(E)$} \markbox{17767}{for} \markbox{17768}{some} \markbox{17769}{component} \markbox{m17770}{$E \in \pi_0(T_s)$}.  \markbox{17771}{So} \markbox{17772}{we} \markbox{17773}{define} \markbox{m17774}{$\Phi(x) = \Delta'(i_{E, \alpha(E)}(x))$}.  \markbox{17775}{The} \markbox{17776}{fact} \markbox{17777}{that} \markbox{17778}{these} \markbox{17779}{piece-wise} \markbox{17780}{maps} \markbox{17781}{glue} \markbox{17782}{coherently} \markbox{17783}{is} \markbox{17784}{a} \markbox{17785}{direct} \markbox{17786}{consequence} \markbox{17787}{of} \markbox{17788}{the} \markbox{17789}{fact} \markbox{17790}{that} \markbox{m17791}{$\alpha$} \markbox{17792}{is} \markbox{17793}{order-preserving.}  \markbox{17794}{The} \markbox{17795}{subitems} \markbox{17796}{of} \markbox{17797}{(2)} \markbox{17798}{are} \markbox{17799}{direct} \markbox{17800}{consequences} \markbox{17801}{of} \markbox{17802}{item} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{17803}{of} \markbox{17804}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.  \markbox{17805}{This} \markbox{17806}{completes} \markbox{17807}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}
Notably, \markbox{17808}{the} \markbox{17809}{above} \markbox{17810}{corollary} \markbox{17811}{holds} \markbox{17812}{whenever} \markbox{17813}{we} \markbox{17814}{have} \markbox{17815}{a} \markbox{17816}{stable} \markbox{17817}{decomposition,} \markbox{17818}{so} \markbox{17819}{in} \markbox{17820}{particular} \markbox{17821}{when} \markbox{17822}{this} \markbox{17823}{is} \markbox{17824}{a} \markbox{17825}{stable} \markbox{17826}{decomposition} \markbox{17827}{arising} \markbox{17828}{from} \markbox{17829}{the} \markbox{17830}{thickened} \markbox{17831}{versions} \markbox{17832}{of} \markbox{17833}{our} \markbox{17834}{stable} intervals.
\end{remark}

\subsection{Detailed sketch of the proof} \label{subsec:detailed sketch}

In \markbox{17835}{lieu} \markbox{17836}{of} \markbox{17837}{a} \markbox{17838}{full} \markbox{17839}{proof} \markbox{17840}{(see} \markbox{17841}{Appendix} \ref{app:SI}), \markbox{17842}{we} \markbox{17843}{provide} \markbox{17844}{a} \markbox{17845}{detailed} \markbox{17846}{sketch} \markbox{17847}{of} \markbox{17848}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{17849}{with} \markbox{17850}{figures} \markbox{17851}{illustrating} \markbox{17852}{the} \markbox{17853}{key} \markbox{17854}{technical} \markbox{17855}{arguments,} \markbox{17856}{which} \markbox{17857}{are} \markbox{17858}{easier} \markbox{17859}{to} \markbox{17860}{understand} \markbox{17861}{at} \markbox{17862}{a} \markbox{17863}{fairly} \markbox{17864}{close} \markbox{17865}{level} \markbox{17866}{than} \markbox{17867}{to} \markbox{17868}{write} \markbox{17869}{down} \markbox{17870}{carefully.}  \markbox{17871}{Our} \markbox{17872}{proof} \markbox{17873}{strategy} \markbox{17874}{here} \markbox{17875}{follows} \markbox{17876}{more} \markbox{17877}{closely} \markbox{17878}{the} \markbox{17879}{proof} \markbox{17880}{of} \cite[Theorem 10.23]{DMS_FJ} \markbox{17881}{than} \markbox{17882}{the} \markbox{17883}{original} \cite[Theorem 3.1]{DMS_bary}.

The \markbox{17884}{goal} \markbox{17885}{is} \markbox{17886}{to} \markbox{17887}{show} \markbox{17888}{that} \markbox{17889}{the} \markbox{17890}{stable} \markbox{17891}{intervals} \markbox{17892}{(Definition} \ref{defn:stable interval}) \markbox{17893}{for} \markbox{17894}{pairs} \markbox{17895}{of} \markbox{17896}{admissible} \markbox{m17897}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{17898}{admit} \markbox{17899}{stable} \markbox{17900}{decompositions} \markbox{17901}{in} \markbox{17902}{the} \markbox{17903}{sense} \markbox{17904}{of} \markbox{17905}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.  \markbox{17906}{Roughly,} \markbox{17907}{these} \markbox{17908}{are} \markbox{17909}{decompositions} \markbox{17910}{of} \markbox{17911}{the} \markbox{17912}{intervals} \markbox{17913}{into} \markbox{17914}{collections} \markbox{17915}{of} \markbox{17916}{subintervals,} \markbox{17917}{which} \markbox{17918}{are} \markbox{17919}{either} \markbox{17920}{identical} \markbox{17921}{(as} \markbox{17922}{in} \markbox{17923}{item} \markbox{17924}{(d)),} \markbox{17925}{or} \markbox{17926}{the} \markbox{17927}{same} \markbox{17928}{length} \markbox{17929}{and} \markbox{17930}{uniformly} \markbox{17931}{close} \markbox{17932}{(as} \markbox{17933}{in} \markbox{17934}{item} \markbox{17935}{(e)),} \markbox{17936}{or} \markbox{17937}{are} \markbox{17938}{one} \markbox{17939}{of} \markbox{17940}{boundedly-many} \markbox{17941}{unstable} \markbox{17942}{components} \markbox{17943}{we} \markbox{17944}{can} \markbox{17945}{ignore} \markbox{17946}{(as} \markbox{17947}{in} \markbox{17948}{item} \markbox{17949}{(f)).}  \markbox{17950}{We} \markbox{17951}{need} \markbox{17952}{to} \markbox{17953}{show} \markbox{17954}{how} \markbox{17955}{to} \markbox{17956}{constraints} \markbox{17957}{on} \markbox{17958}{the} \markbox{17959}{input} \markbox{17960}{data} \markbox{17961}{assumed} \markbox{17962}{in} \markbox{17963}{item} \markbox{17964}{(1)} \markbox{17965}{translates} \markbox{17966}{into} \markbox{17967}{control} \markbox{17968}{over} \markbox{17969}{the} \markbox{17970}{components} \markbox{17971}{of} \markbox{17972}{the} \markbox{17973}{stable} intervals.

To \markbox{17974}{begin} \markbox{17975}{the} \markbox{17976}{sketch,} \markbox{17977}{first} \markbox{17978}{observe} \markbox{17979}{that} \markbox{17980}{the} \markbox{17981}{two} \markbox{17982}{main} \markbox{17983}{assumptions} \markbox{17984}{of} \markbox{17985}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{17986}{on} \markbox{17987}{the} \markbox{17988}{setups} \markbox{m17989}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{17990}{and} \markbox{m17991}{$(a',b';\calY')$} \markbox{17992}{are} that
\begin{itemize}
\item The \markbox{17993}{sets} \markbox{17994}{of} \markbox{17995}{cluster} \markbox{17996}{points} \markbox{m17997}{$\calY, \calY'$} \markbox{17998}{are} \markbox{17999}{close} \markbox{18000}{to} \markbox{18001}{both} \markbox{m18002}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{18003}{and} \markbox{m18004}{$\lambda(a',b')$} \markbox{18005}{and} \markbox{18006}{have} \markbox{18007}{bounded} \markbox{18008}{symmetric} \markbox{18009}{difference,} \markbox{18010}{and} 
\item The \markbox{18011}{endpoints} \markbox{18012}{pairs} \markbox{m18013}{$(a,b)$} \markbox{18014}{and} \markbox{m18015}{$(a',b')$} \markbox{18016}{are} \markbox{18017}{within} \markbox{m18018}{$\epsilon$} \markbox{18019}{of} \markbox{18020}{each} other.
\end{itemize}

This \markbox{18021}{suggests} \markbox{18022}{the} \markbox{18023}{following} \markbox{18024}{iterated} \markbox{18025}{proof} \markbox{18026}{strategy:} 
\begin{enumerate}
\item First, \markbox{18027}{show} \markbox{18028}{that} \markbox{18029}{we} \markbox{18030}{can} \markbox{18031}{build} \markbox{18032}{a} \markbox{18033}{stable} \markbox{18034}{decomposition} \markbox{18035}{when} \markbox{18036}{we} \markbox{18037}{add} \markbox{18038}{a} \markbox{18039}{single} \markbox{18040}{nearby} \markbox{18041}{cluster} \markbox{18042}{point,} \markbox{18043}{while} \markbox{18044}{keeping} \markbox{18045}{the} \markbox{18046}{endpoints} \markbox{18047}{the} same.
\item Next, \markbox{18048}{show} \markbox{18049}{that} \markbox{18050}{we} \markbox{18051}{can} \markbox{18052}{iteratively} \markbox{18053}{combine} \markbox{18054}{stable} \markbox{18055}{decompositions} \markbox{18056}{to} \markbox{18057}{obtain} \markbox{18058}{a} \markbox{18059}{stable} decomposition.
\item Finally, \markbox{18060}{show} \markbox{18061}{that} \markbox{18062}{we} \markbox{18063}{can} \markbox{18064}{build} \markbox{18065}{a} \markbox{18066}{stable} \markbox{18067}{decomposition} \markbox{18068}{when} \markbox{18069}{we} \markbox{18070}{only} \markbox{18071}{wiggle} \markbox{18072}{a} \markbox{18073}{single} \markbox{18074}{endpoint} \markbox{18075}{and} \markbox{18076}{keep} \markbox{18077}{everything} \markbox{18078}{else} \markbox{18079}{(including} \markbox{18080}{the} \markbox{18081}{cluster} \markbox{18082}{sets)} \markbox{18083}{the} same.

\end{enumerate}

Steps \markbox{18084}{(1)} \markbox{18085}{and} \markbox{18086}{(3)} \markbox{18087}{can} \markbox{18088}{be} \markbox{18089}{thought} \markbox{18090}{of} \markbox{18091}{as} \emph{moves}, \markbox{18092}{where} \markbox{18093}{we} \markbox{18094}{only} \markbox{18095}{change} \markbox{18096}{one} \markbox{18097}{piece} \markbox{18098}{of} \markbox{18099}{data} \markbox{18100}{at} \markbox{18101}{a} \markbox{18102}{time,} \markbox{18103}{and} \markbox{18104}{we} \markbox{18105}{will} \markbox{18106}{see} \markbox{18107}{that} \markbox{18108}{type} \markbox{18109}{(3)} \markbox{18110}{moves} \markbox{18111}{are} \markbox{18112}{basically} \markbox{18113}{type} \markbox{18114}{(1)} \markbox{18115}{moves.}  \markbox{18116}{For} \markbox{18117}{step} \markbox{18118}{(2),} \markbox{18119}{we} \markbox{18120}{will} \markbox{18121}{want} \markbox{18122}{to} \markbox{18123}{iteratively} \markbox{18124}{perform} \markbox{18125}{type} \markbox{18126}{(1)} \markbox{18127}{moves} \markbox{18128}{by} \markbox{18129}{adding} \markbox{18130}{the} \markbox{18131}{extra} \markbox{18132}{cluster} \markbox{18133}{points} \markbox{18134}{of} \markbox{m18135}{$\calY' - \calY$} \markbox{18136}{to} \markbox{18137}{the} \markbox{18138}{setup} \markbox{m18139}{$(a,b;\calY)$}, \markbox{18140}{thereby} \markbox{18141}{shifting} \markbox{18142}{from} \markbox{m18143}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{18144}{to} \markbox{m18145}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \calY')$}.  \markbox{18146}{Then} \markbox{18147}{we} \markbox{18148}{make} \markbox{18149}{two} \markbox{18150}{type} \markbox{18151}{(3)} \markbox{18152}{moves} \markbox{18153}{to} \markbox{18154}{shift} \markbox{m18155}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \calY') \to (a',b;\calY \cup \calY') \to (a',b';\calY \cup \calY')$}.  \markbox{18156}{Finally,} \markbox{18157}{we} \markbox{18158}{make} \markbox{18159}{another} \markbox{18160}{sequence} \markbox{18161}{of} \markbox{18162}{iterated} \markbox{18163}{type} \markbox{18164}{(1)} \markbox{18165}{moves} \markbox{18166}{to} \markbox{18167}{shift} \markbox{18168}{from} \markbox{m18169}{$(a',b';\calY \cup \calY')$} \markbox{18170}{down} \markbox{18171}{to} \markbox{m18172}{$(a',b';\calY')$}.  \markbox{18173}{Since} \markbox{18174}{this} \markbox{18175}{total} \markbox{18176}{sequence} \markbox{18177}{of} \markbox{18178}{moves} \markbox{18179}{is} \markbox{18180}{bounded} \markbox{18181}{by} \markbox{m18182}{$N+2$}, \markbox{18183}{we} \markbox{18184}{will} \markbox{18185}{be} done.
