For \markbox{18186}{step} \markbox{18187}{(1),} \markbox{18188}{there} \markbox{18189}{are} \markbox{18190}{two} \markbox{18191}{main} \markbox{18192}{cases---the} \emph{split cluster} \markbox{18193}{case,} \markbox{18194}{where} \markbox{18195}{we} \markbox{18196}{add} \markbox{18197}{a} \markbox{18198}{point} \markbox{m18199}{$z$} \markbox{18200}{to} \markbox{m18201}{$\calY$} \markbox{18202}{far} \markbox{18203}{from} \markbox{18204}{all} \markbox{m18205}{$\calY$}-clusters; \markbox{18206}{and} \markbox{18207}{the} \emph{affected cluster} \markbox{18208}{case,} \markbox{18209}{where} \markbox{m18210}{$z$} \markbox{18211}{is} \markbox{18212}{close} \markbox{18213}{to} \markbox{18214}{some} \markbox{18215}{existing} \markbox{m18216}{$\calY$}-cluster.  \markbox{18217}{See} \markbox{18218}{Figures} \ref{fig:split cluster} \markbox{18219}{and} \ref{fig:affected cluster}, \markbox{18220}{respectively,} \markbox{18221}{for} \markbox{18222}{relevant} \markbox{18223}{schematics.}  \markbox{18224}{The} \markbox{18225}{philosophy} \markbox{18226}{here} \markbox{18227}{is} \markbox{18228}{simple:} \markbox{18229}{adding} \markbox{18230}{a} \markbox{18231}{cluster} \markbox{18232}{point} \markbox{18233}{only} \markbox{18234}{affects} \markbox{18235}{things} \markbox{18236}{locally,} \markbox{18237}{thus} \markbox{18238}{one} \markbox{18239}{only} \markbox{18240}{needs} \markbox{18241}{to} \markbox{18242}{make} \markbox{18243}{bounded} \markbox{18244}{local} modifications.


Step \markbox{18245}{(2)} \markbox{18246}{of} \markbox{18247}{the} \markbox{18248}{proof} \markbox{18249}{now} \markbox{18250}{involves} \markbox{18251}{iteratively} \markbox{18252}{applying} \markbox{18253}{step} \markbox{18254}{(1),} \markbox{18255}{and} \markbox{18256}{thus} \markbox{18257}{one} \markbox{18258}{must} \markbox{18259}{show} \markbox{18260}{that} \markbox{18261}{one} \markbox{18262}{can} \markbox{18263}{coherently} \markbox{18264}{combine} \markbox{18265}{two} \markbox{18266}{pairs} \markbox{18267}{of} \markbox{18268}{stable} \markbox{18269}{decompositions} \markbox{18270}{across} \markbox{18271}{a} \markbox{18272}{common} \markbox{18273}{setup.}  \markbox{18274}{Figure} \ref{fig:iterated stable decomp} \markbox{18275}{shows} \markbox{18276}{a} \markbox{18277}{schematic} \markbox{18278}{for} \markbox{18279}{the} \markbox{18280}{argument,} \markbox{18281}{in} \markbox{18282}{which} \markbox{18283}{one} \markbox{18284}{has} \markbox{18285}{three} \markbox{18286}{stable} \markbox{18287}{trees} \markbox{m18288}{$T_1,T_2,T_3$} \markbox{18289}{with} \markbox{18290}{associated} \markbox{18291}{stable} \markbox{18292}{decompositions,} \markbox{18293}{so} \markbox{18294}{that} \markbox{18295}{those} \markbox{18296}{for} \markbox{m18297}{$T_1,T_2$} \markbox{18298}{and} \markbox{m18299}{$T_2,T_3$} \markbox{18300}{are} \markbox{18301}{compatible.}  \markbox{18302}{The} \markbox{18303}{idea} \markbox{18304}{is} \markbox{18305}{to} \markbox{18306}{intersect} \markbox{18307}{the} \markbox{18308}{two} \markbox{18309}{decompositions} \markbox{18310}{on} \markbox{m18311}{$T_2$} \markbox{18312}{and} \markbox{18313}{pull} \markbox{18314}{them} \markbox{18315}{back} \markbox{18316}{to} \markbox{m18317}{$T_1,T_3$}.

The \markbox{18318}{associated} \markbox{18319}{stability} \markbox{18320}{constants} \markbox{18321}{increase} \markbox{18322}{a} \markbox{18323}{controlled} \markbox{18324}{amount} \markbox{18325}{with} \markbox{18326}{each} \markbox{18327}{iteration,} \markbox{18328}{but} \markbox{18329}{we} \markbox{18330}{are} \markbox{18331}{assuming} \markbox{18332}{that} \markbox{18333}{we} \markbox{18334}{only} \markbox{18335}{need} \markbox{18336}{to} \markbox{18337}{perform} \markbox{18338}{boundedly-many} \markbox{18339}{such} \markbox{18340}{iterations} \markbox{18341}{in} \markbox{18342}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.


\smallskip

Finally, \markbox{18343}{step} \markbox{18344}{(3)} \markbox{18345}{is} \markbox{18346}{an} \markbox{18347}{application} \markbox{18348}{of} \markbox{18349}{steps} \markbox{18350}{(1)} \markbox{18351}{and} \markbox{18352}{(2).}  \markbox{18353}{To} \markbox{18354}{get} \markbox{18355}{the} \markbox{18356}{idea,} \markbox{18357}{we} \markbox{18358}{can} \markbox{18359}{consider} \markbox{18360}{the} \markbox{18361}{following} \markbox{18362}{restricted} \markbox{18363}{setup,} \markbox{18364}{which} \markbox{18365}{we} \markbox{18366}{highlight} \markbox{18367}{to} \markbox{18368}{focus} \markbox{18369}{on} \markbox{18370}{what} \markbox{18371}{happens} \markbox{18372}{when} \markbox{18373}{we} \markbox{18374}{perturb} \markbox{18375}{an} \markbox{18376}{endpoint.}  \markbox{18377}{Let} \markbox{m18378}{$a,b,a' \in \calZ$} \markbox{18379}{and} \markbox{m18380}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{18381}{be} \markbox{18382}{finite} \markbox{18383}{with} \markbox{m18384}{$\calY \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b)) \cap \calN_{\epsilon/2}(a',b)$}.  \markbox{18385}{The} \markbox{18386}{following} \markbox{18387}{collection} \markbox{18388}{of} \markbox{18389}{setups,} \markbox{18390}{each} \markbox{18391}{of} \markbox{18392}{which} \markbox{18393}{differs} \markbox{18394}{by} \markbox{18395}{adding} \markbox{18396}{or} \markbox{18397}{deleting} \markbox{18398}{one} \markbox{18399}{cluster} \markbox{18400}{point,} \markbox{18401}{or} \markbox{18402}{by} \markbox{18403}{switching} \markbox{18404}{the} \markbox{18405}{role} \markbox{18406}{that} \markbox{m18407}{$a,a'$} \markbox{18408}{or} \markbox{m18409}{$b,b'$} \markbox{18410}{play} \markbox{18411}{between} \markbox{18412}{cluster} \markbox{18413}{or} endpoint:
\vspace{-.09in}
\begin{multicols}{3}
\begin{enumerate}
\item $(a,b;\calY)$,
\item $(a,b;\calY \cup \{a\})$,
\item $(a,b;\calY \cup \{a, a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY \cup \{a,a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY \cup \{a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY)$.
\end{enumerate}
\end{multicols}

Hence \markbox{18414}{we} \markbox{18415}{can} \markbox{18416}{use} \markbox{18417}{steps} \markbox{18418}{(1),(2),} \markbox{18419}{(3)} \markbox{18420}{plus} \markbox{18421}{iteration} \markbox{18422}{to} \markbox{18423}{change} \markbox{18424}{the} \markbox{18425}{roles} \markbox{18426}{of} \markbox{18427}{endpoints} \markbox{18428}{once} \markbox{18429}{we} \markbox{18430}{have} \markbox{18431}{added} \markbox{18432}{all} \markbox{18433}{of} \markbox{18434}{the} \markbox{18435}{necessary} \markbox{18436}{cluster} \markbox{18437}{points.}  \markbox{18438}{See} \markbox{18439}{Appendix} \ref{app:SI} \markbox{18440}{for} \markbox{18441}{the} \markbox{18442}{full} argument.


\begin{figure}[b]
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=1\textwidth]{figures/split_cluster}
    \caption{Step (1) of the proof of Theorem \ref{thm:stable intervals}, split cluster case:  In the first figure, the two edge components of the two stable intervals are shown.  The point $z$ forms an individual cluster and therefore must be inserted as a vertex in the graph $\calG$, between clusters $C_1, C_2$.  Every cluster to the left of $C_1$ is unchanged, as are all of the connecting segments (in pink), and same for those to the right of $C_2$.  The second figure shows the stable decomposition of the stable intervals.  Here, we need to include the shadow of the cluster $z$ on $\lambda(C_1,C_2)$ as an unstable component.  This cuts $\lambda(C_1,C_2)$ into two segments, which are paired with $\lambda(C_1,z)$ and $\lambda(z,C_2)$, though these need to be slightly truncated so guarantee they have the same lengths; the unstable segments accomplishing this are red.  The third figure shows the stable decomposition for their $(r_1,r_2)$-thickenings, which are subsets of the edge components $T_e \subset T$ and $T'_e \subset T$, are indicated in brown.  Note that this can result in collapsing an entire edge component if its diameter is less than $r_2-2r_1$.  These brown segments refine the stable decompositions $T_s \subset T_e$ and $T'_s \subset T'_e$.}    \label{fig:split cluster}
\end{figure}

\newpage
\begin{figure}[!htb]
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=1\textwidth]{figures/affect_cluster}
    \caption{Step (1) of the proof of Theorem \ref{thm:stable intervals}, affected cluster case.  Two phenomena are shown.  In the top figure, there are three affected clusters, $P,Q,R$, for $(a,b;\calY)$ which combine with $z$ into a new cluster $C'$ for $(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$.  By definition, $P,Q,R$ must be $O(\epsilon)$ apart, and actually are adjacent in $\calG$.  The clusters $C_1,C_2$ appear in both setups, and the subgraph of $\calG$ to the left of $C_1$ coincides with the same subgraph for $\calG'$, and similarly for $C_2$.  So the corresponding (pink) components form (stable) components of $T_s \subset T_e$ and $T'_s \subset T'_e$.  The components of $T_e$ connecting $P,Q,R$ are declared unstable and, in this example, the components $\lambda(C_1,P)$ and $\lambda(R,C_2)$ of $T_e$ coincide with the components $\lambda(C_1,C')$ and $\lambda(C',C_2)$ of $T'_e$, and hence are stable.  The second figure shows the stable decomposition for the $(r_1,r_2)$-thickenings, which are just the thickenings of the components of $T_s = T'_s$, and hence are also exactly the same.  In the second example, the same discussion applies to the outside parts.  For the middle of the graph, $z$ combines with the cluster $A$, which results in pairs of segments $\lambda(C_1,A)$ and $\lambda(C_1, C')$, and $\lambda(A,C_2)$ and $\lambda(C',C_2)$, which have $O(\epsilon)$-close endpoints and are thus $O(\epsilon)$-Hausdorff close, with the same length up to error $O(\epsilon)$.  Small surgeries provide the required stable components for the stable intervals $T, T'$, shown in the third figure.  The fourth figure shows the stable decomposition for the $(R,r)$-thickenings of this example.}
    \label{fig:affected cluster}
\end{figure}

\begin{figure}[t]
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=1\textwidth]{figures/iterated_stabledecomp}
    \caption{The proof of Theorem \ref{thm:stable intervals}, iterating stable decompositions: The idea for the iteration argument is to intersect the stable decompositions $T^1_{s,2} \cap T^3_{s,2} \subset T_2$ for $T_1,T_3$, respectively, and then use the isometries which identify the stable pairs for $T_1, T_2$ to give a refined stable decomposition for $(T_1,T_2)$, which can be combined with a refinement for $(T_2,T_3)$ via simple composition.  In the schematic (which is \emph{not} happening in $\calZ$), we have lined up the stable intervals $T_1,T_2,T_3$ to indicate how to refine the pairwise stable decompositions for $(T_1,T_2)$ and $(T_2,T_3)$ for one for $(T_1,T_3)$.  The orange segments correspond to cluster components of the intervals, while the blue and green segments correspond to the unstable components for the pairs $(T_1,T_2)$ and $(T_2,T_3)$, respectively.  The complement of the orange, blue, and green segments on $T_2$ form the refined stable decomposition on $T_2$, and the purple squares indicate how these segments induce refined stable decompositions on $T_1$ and $T_3$.}
    \label{fig:iterated stable decomp}
\end{figure}


\newpage
\section{Stable cubical models} \label{sec:stable cubes}

In \markbox{18443}{this} \markbox{18444}{section,} \markbox{18445}{we} \markbox{18446}{explain} \markbox{18447}{how} \markbox{18448}{to} \markbox{18449}{combine} \markbox{18450}{the} \markbox{18451}{cubulation} \markbox{18452}{machinery} \markbox{18453}{described} \markbox{18454}{in} \markbox{18455}{Sections} \ref{sec:interval systems}--\ref{sec:cubulation} \markbox{18456}{with} \markbox{18457}{the} \markbox{18458}{Controlling} \markbox{18459}{Domains} \markbox{18460}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains} \markbox{18461}{established} \markbox{18462}{in} \markbox{18463}{Section} \ref{sec:controlling domains} \markbox{18464}{and} \markbox{18465}{the} \markbox{18466}{Stable} \markbox{18467}{Interval} \markbox{18468}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{18469}{from} \markbox{18470}{Section} \ref{sec:stable intervals}.  \markbox{18471}{Over} \markbox{18472}{the} \markbox{18473}{first} \markbox{18474}{two} \markbox{18475}{subsections,} \markbox{18476}{we} \markbox{18477}{prove} \markbox{18478}{that} \markbox{18479}{our} \markbox{18480}{stable} \markbox{18481}{intervals} \markbox{18482}{can} \markbox{18483}{be} \markbox{18484}{plugged} \markbox{18485}{into} \markbox{18486}{our} \markbox{18487}{interval} \markbox{18488}{system} \markbox{18489}{machinery} \markbox{18490}{to} \markbox{18491}{produce} \markbox{18492}{an} \markbox{18493}{HFI} \markbox{18494}{for} \markbox{18495}{any} \markbox{18496}{pair} \markbox{18497}{of} \markbox{18498}{points} \markbox{m18499}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{18500}{in} \markbox{18501}{an} HHS.

The \markbox{18502}{heart} \markbox{18503}{of} \markbox{18504}{the} \markbox{18505}{section} \markbox{18506}{is} \markbox{18507}{then} \markbox{18508}{explaining} \markbox{18509}{how} \markbox{18510}{to} \markbox{18511}{relate} \markbox{18512}{two} \markbox{18513}{such} \markbox{18514}{HFIs} \markbox{18515}{for} \markbox{18516}{a} \markbox{18517}{pair} \markbox{18518}{of} \markbox{18519}{points} \markbox{m18520}{$a,b$} \markbox{18521}{and} \markbox{18522}{a} \markbox{18523}{perturbed} \markbox{18524}{pair} \markbox{m18525}{$a',b'$}.  \markbox{18526}{We} \markbox{18527}{explain} \markbox{18528}{this} \markbox{18529}{below} \markbox{18530}{in} \markbox{18531}{detail} \markbox{18532}{in} \markbox{18533}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:perturbed to stable}.




\subsection{Stable intervals form an interval system}

Our \markbox{18534}{first} \markbox{18535}{goal} \markbox{18536}{is} \markbox{18537}{to} \markbox{18538}{explain} \markbox{18539}{how} \markbox{18540}{to} \markbox{18541}{take} \markbox{18542}{the} \markbox{18543}{family} \markbox{18544}{of} \markbox{18545}{stable} \markbox{18546}{intervals} \markbox{18547}{associated} \markbox{18548}{to} \markbox{18549}{a} \markbox{18550}{pair} \markbox{18551}{of} \markbox{18552}{points} \markbox{m18553}{$a, b\in \calX$} \markbox{18554}{and} \markbox{18555}{produce} \markbox{18556}{a} \markbox{18557}{hierarchical} \markbox{18558}{family} \markbox{18559}{of} intervals.


First, \markbox{18560}{we} \markbox{18561}{need} \markbox{18562}{to} \markbox{18563}{induce} \markbox{18564}{a} \markbox{18565}{collection} \markbox{18566}{of} \markbox{18567}{relative} \markbox{18568}{projections} \markbox{18569}{on} \markbox{18570}{the} \markbox{18571}{stable} \markbox{18572}{intervals} \markbox{18573}{which} \markbox{18574}{turn} \markbox{18575}{them} \markbox{18576}{into} \markbox{18577}{an} \markbox{m18578}{$R$}-interval \markbox{18579}{system} \markbox{18580}{(Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}) \markbox{18581}{for} \markbox{18582}{a} \markbox{18583}{uniform} \markbox{m18584}{$R = R(\mathfrak S)>0$}.

Let \markbox{m18585}{$U \in \calU$}.  \markbox{18586}{Recall} \markbox{18587}{that} \markbox{18588}{the} \markbox{18589}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA} \markbox{18590}{says} \markbox{18591}{that} \markbox{18592}{if} \markbox{m18593}{$d_V(a,b)$} \markbox{18594}{is} \markbox{18595}{sufficiently} \markbox{18596}{large} \markbox{18597}{for} \markbox{m18598}{$V \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{18599}{then} \markbox{m18600}{$\rho^V_U \subset \calN_{\ES}(\lambda(a,b))$} \markbox{18601}{when} \markbox{m18602}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{18603}{and,} \markbox{18604}{even} \markbox{18605}{better,} \markbox{m18606}{$\rho^V_U \subset \calN_{\ES}(a \cup b)$} \markbox{18607}{when} \markbox{m18608}{$V \pitchfork U$}.  \markbox{18609}{If} \markbox{18610}{we} \markbox{18611}{set} \markbox{m18612}{$\calY_U= \{\rho^V_U|V \nest U \in \calU\}$}, \markbox{18613}{then} \markbox{m18614}{$(\pi_U(a), \pi_U(b); \calY_U)$} \markbox{18615}{is} \markbox{18616}{an} \markbox{m18617}{$\epsilon$}-setup \markbox{18618}{in} \markbox{m18619}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{18620}{for} \markbox{m18621}{$\epsilon = 2\ES$} \markbox{18622}{in} \markbox{18623}{the} \markbox{18624}{sense} \markbox{18625}{of} \markbox{18626}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:stable setup}.  \markbox{18627}{In} \markbox{18628}{particular,} \markbox{18629}{our} \markbox{18630}{stable} \markbox{18631}{interval} \markbox{18632}{construction} \markbox{18633}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure}) applies.

For \markbox{18634}{each} \markbox{m18635}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{18636}{let} \markbox{m18637}{$T_U = T_{U,e} \cup T_{U,c}$} \markbox{18638}{denote} \markbox{18639}{the} \markbox{18640}{stable} \markbox{18641}{interval} \markbox{18642}{for} \markbox{18643}{the} \markbox{18644}{setup} \markbox{m18645}{$(a,b;\calY_U)$} \markbox{18646}{in} \markbox{m18647}{$\calC(U)$}.  \markbox{18648}{Recall} \markbox{18649}{that} \markbox{18650}{each} \markbox{18651}{component} \markbox{18652}{of} \markbox{m18653}{$T_{U,c}$} \markbox{18654}{coincides} \markbox{18655}{with} \markbox{m18656}{$\mu(C)$} \markbox{18657}{for} \markbox{18658}{some} \markbox{18659}{cluster} \markbox{m18660}{$C$} \markbox{18661}{of} \markbox{18662}{points} \markbox{18663}{in} \markbox{m18664}{$\calY_U \cup \{a,b\}$} \markbox{18665}{(Subsection} \ref{subsec:clusters}).  \markbox{18666}{Importantly,} \markbox{18667}{item} \markbox{18668}{(2)} \markbox{18669}{of} \markbox{18670}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure} \markbox{18671}{says} \markbox{18672}{that} \markbox{m18673}{$\phi_U(\mu(C))$} \markbox{18674}{is} \markbox{m18675}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{18676}{(and} \markbox{18677}{hence} \markbox{m18678}{$O(\mathfrak S)$}) \markbox{18679}{Hausdorff} \markbox{18680}{close} \markbox{18681}{to} \markbox{m18682}{$C$} \markbox{18683}{itself.}  \markbox{18684}{This} \markbox{18685}{property} \markbox{18686}{is} \markbox{18687}{what} \markbox{18688}{makes} \markbox{18689}{the} \markbox{18690}{following} \markbox{18691}{definition} work:

\begin{definition}[Stable \markbox{18692}{interval} projections]\label{defn:stable interval projections}
For \markbox{18693}{each} \markbox{m18694}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{18695}{we} \markbox{18696}{define} \markbox{18697}{the} \markbox{18698}{following} \emph{stable interval projections}:
\begin{itemize}
\item For \markbox{18699}{each} \markbox{m18700}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{18701}{with} \markbox{m18702}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{18703}{let} \markbox{m18704}{$C$} \markbox{18705}{be} \markbox{18706}{the} \markbox{18707}{cluster} \markbox{18708}{containing} \markbox{m18709}{$\rho^V_U$}.  \markbox{18710}{Define} 
$$\delta^V_U = \phi_U^{-1}(\hull_{\mu(C)}(p_{\phi_U(\mu(C))}(\rho^V_U))) \subset \mu(C),$$where \markbox{m18711}{$p_U:\calC(U) \to \phi_U(\mu(C))$} \markbox{18712}{is} \markbox{18713}{the} \markbox{18714}{closest} \markbox{18715}{point} \markbox{18716}{projection} \markbox{18717}{to} \markbox{18718}{the} \markbox{18719}{geodesic} \markbox{18720}{segment} \markbox{m18721}{$\phi_U(\mu(C)) = \mu(C)$}.
\item For \markbox{18722}{each} \markbox{m18723}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{18724}{with} \markbox{m18725}{$V \pitchfork U$}, \markbox{18726}{let} \markbox{m18727}{$f \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{18728}{denote} \markbox{18729}{the} \markbox{18730}{point} \markbox{18731}{(provided} \markbox{18732}{by} \markbox{18733}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency}) \markbox{18734}{for} \markbox{18735}{which} \markbox{m18736}{$d_U(\pi_U(f), \rho^V_U)<\epsilon$}, \markbox{18737}{and} \markbox{18738}{let} \markbox{m18739}{$C$} \markbox{18740}{denote} \markbox{18741}{the} \markbox{18742}{cluster} \markbox{18743}{containing} \markbox{m18744}{$f$}.  \markbox{18745}{Again} \markbox{18746}{we} \markbox{18747}{define} \markbox{m18748}{$\delta^V_U = \phi_U^{-1}(\hull_{\mu(C)}(p_{\phi_U(\mu(C)}(\rho^V_U))) \subset \mu(C)$}.
\item If \markbox{m18749}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{18750}{then} \markbox{18751}{we} \markbox{18752}{define} \markbox{18753}{the} \emph{interval projection map} \markbox{m18754}{$\delta^V_U:T_V \to T_U$} \markbox{18755}{by} \markbox{m18756}{$\delta^V_U = \phi^{-1}_U \circ p_{T_U} \circ \rho^V_U \circ \phi_V.$}
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

The \markbox{18757}{next} \markbox{18758}{lemma} \markbox{18759}{says} \markbox{18760}{that} \markbox{18761}{these} \markbox{18762}{projections} \markbox{18763}{turn} \markbox{18764}{the} \markbox{18765}{family} \markbox{18766}{of} \markbox{18767}{stable} \markbox{18768}{intervals} \markbox{18769}{into} \markbox{18770}{an} \markbox{18771}{interval} \markbox{18772}{system.}  \markbox{18773}{The} \markbox{18774}{proof,} \markbox{18775}{which} \markbox{18776}{we} \markbox{18777}{leave} \markbox{18778}{to} \markbox{18779}{the} \markbox{18780}{reader,} \markbox{18781}{involves} \markbox{18782}{verifying} \markbox{18783}{the} \markbox{18784}{conditions} \markbox{18785}{of} \markbox{18786}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{18787}{(and} \markbox{18788}{hence} \markbox{18789}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}, \markbox{18790}{and} \markbox{18791}{one} \markbox{18792}{does} \markbox{18793}{this} \markbox{18794}{via} \markbox{18795}{Lemma} \ref{lem:rho control} \markbox{18796}{and} \markbox{18797}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure}.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:stable interval system}
There \markbox{18798}{exists} \markbox{m18799}{$R_s = R_s(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{18800}{so} \markbox{18801}{that} \markbox{18802}{the} \markbox{18803}{stable} \markbox{18804}{intervals} \markbox{m18805}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{18806}{endowed} \markbox{18807}{with} \markbox{18808}{the} \markbox{18809}{stable} \markbox{18810}{interval} \markbox{18811}{projections} \markbox{18812}{forms} \markbox{18813}{an} \markbox{m18814}{$R_s$}-interval \markbox{18815}{system} \markbox{18816}{for} \markbox{m18817}{$a,b$}.
\end{lemma}



\subsection{Thickenings of stable intervals, their collapses, and HFIs}\label{subsec:collapsed stable intervals}

In \markbox{18818}{this} \markbox{18819}{subsection,} \markbox{18820}{we} \markbox{18821}{explain} \markbox{18822}{why} \markbox{18823}{collapsed} \markbox{18824}{thickened} \markbox{18825}{interval} \markbox{18826}{systems} \markbox{18827}{of} \markbox{18828}{stable} \markbox{18829}{intevals} \markbox{18830}{form} HFIs.

To \markbox{18831}{begin,} \markbox{18832}{in} \markbox{18833}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:thickenings}, \markbox{18834}{we} \markbox{18835}{took} \markbox{18836}{an} \markbox{18837}{interval} \markbox{18838}{system} \markbox{m18839}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{18840}{along} \markbox{18841}{with} \markbox{18842}{its} \markbox{18843}{relative} \markbox{18844}{projection} \markbox{18845}{data} \markbox{m18846}{$\delta^V_U$}, \markbox{18847}{and} \markbox{18848}{then} \markbox{18849}{thickened} \markbox{18850}{the} \markbox{18851}{intervals} \markbox{18852}{along} \markbox{18853}{the} \markbox{18854}{components} \markbox{m18855}{$B$} \markbox{18856}{of} \markbox{18857}{a} \markbox{18858}{decomposition} \markbox{m18859}{$T_U = A \cup B$}, \markbox{18860}{where} \markbox{m18861}{$B$} \markbox{18862}{consists} \markbox{18863}{of} \markbox{18864}{these} \markbox{m18865}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{18866}{along} \markbox{18867}{with} \markbox{18868}{the} \markbox{18869}{marked} \markbox{18870}{points} \markbox{m18871}{$a_U,b_U$}.  \markbox{18872}{Then} \markbox{18873}{in} \markbox{18874}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:collapsing}, \markbox{18875}{we} \markbox{18876}{collapsed} \markbox{18877}{along} \markbox{18878}{this} \markbox{18879}{thickening} \markbox{18880}{which} \markbox{18881}{induced} \markbox{18882}{collapsed} \markbox{18883}{relative} \markbox{18884}{projections} \markbox{18885}{on} \markbox{18886}{the} \markbox{18887}{collapsed} \markbox{18888}{intervals.}  \markbox{18889}{On} \markbox{18890}{the} \markbox{18891}{other} \markbox{18892}{hand,} \markbox{18893}{the} \markbox{18894}{thickenings} \markbox{18895}{of} \markbox{18896}{stable} \markbox{18897}{intervals} \markbox{18898}{we} \markbox{18899}{considered} \markbox{18900}{in} \markbox{18901}{the} \markbox{18902}{Stable} \markbox{18903}{Intervals} \markbox{18904}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{18905}{were} \markbox{18906}{thickenings} \markbox{18907}{along} \markbox{18908}{the} \markbox{18909}{cluster} components.

The \markbox{18910}{following} \markbox{18911}{lemma,} \markbox{18912}{whose} \markbox{18913}{proof} \markbox{18914}{we} \markbox{18915}{leave} \markbox{18916}{to} \markbox{18917}{the} \markbox{18918}{reader,} \markbox{18919}{says} \markbox{18920}{that} \markbox{18921}{these} \markbox{18922}{thickenings} \markbox{18923}{coincide,} \markbox{18924}{and} \markbox{18925}{hence} \markbox{18926}{that} \markbox{18927}{the} \markbox{18928}{corresponding} \markbox{18929}{collapsed} \markbox{18930}{trees} \markbox{18931}{are} identical:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:same thickenings}
For \markbox{18932}{any} \markbox{m18933}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{18934}{let} \markbox{m18935}{$T_U = A \cup B$} \markbox{18936}{be} \markbox{18937}{the} \markbox{18938}{decomposition} \markbox{18939}{where} \markbox{m18940}{$B$} \markbox{18941}{is} \markbox{18942}{the} \markbox{18943}{union} \markbox{18944}{of} \markbox{18945}{all} \markbox{m18946}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{18947}{for} \markbox{m18948}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{18949}{along} \markbox{18950}{with} \markbox{m18951}{$a_U,b_U$}.  \markbox{18952}{Let} \markbox{m18953}{$T_U = T_{U,e} \cup T_{U,c}$} \markbox{18954}{denote} \markbox{18955}{the} \markbox{18956}{decomposition} \markbox{18957}{provided} \markbox{18958}{by} \markbox{18959}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure}.  \markbox{18960}{There} \markbox{18961}{exists} \markbox{m18962}{$R_3 = R_3(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{18963}{so} \markbox{18964}{that} \markbox{18965}{for} \markbox{18966}{any} \markbox{m18967}{$r_1>R_3$} \markbox{18968}{and} \markbox{m18969}{$r_2>0$}, \markbox{18970}{the} \markbox{m18971}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{18972}{of} \markbox{m18973}{$T_U$} \markbox{18974}{along} \markbox{m18975}{$B$} \markbox{18976}{and} \markbox{18977}{along} \markbox{m18978}{$T_{U,c}$} \markbox{18979}{are} identical.
\end{lemma}




The \markbox{18980}{upshot} \markbox{18981}{of} \markbox{18982}{Lemmas} \ref{lem:stable interval system} \markbox{18983}{and} \ref{lem:same thickenings} \markbox{18984}{is} \markbox{18985}{that} \markbox{18986}{we} \markbox{18987}{can} \markbox{18988}{plug} \markbox{18989}{our} \markbox{18990}{stable} \markbox{18991}{intervals} \markbox{18992}{directly} \markbox{18993}{into} \markbox{18994}{our} \markbox{18995}{interval} \markbox{18996}{system} \markbox{18997}{machinery.}  \markbox{18998}{The} \markbox{18999}{next} \markbox{19000}{step} \markbox{19001}{is} \markbox{19002}{to} \markbox{19003}{explain} \markbox{19004}{how} \markbox{19005}{to} \markbox{19006}{produce} \markbox{19007}{an} \markbox{19008}{HFI} \markbox{19009}{(Definition} \ref{defn:HFI}) \markbox{19010}{from} \markbox{19011}{this} \markbox{19012}{system} \markbox{19013}{using} \markbox{19014}{the} \markbox{19015}{thickenings} \markbox{19016}{and} \markbox{19017}{collapsing} \markbox{19018}{procedures} \markbox{19019}{discussed} \markbox{19020}{in} \markbox{19021}{Subsections} \ref{subsec:thickenings} \markbox{19022}{and} \ref{subsec:collapsing}.

Continuing \markbox{19023}{with} \markbox{19024}{our} \markbox{19025}{notation,} \markbox{19026}{Lemma} \ref{lem:stable interval system} \markbox{19027}{says} \markbox{19028}{that} \markbox{19029}{the} \markbox{19030}{stable} \markbox{19031}{intervals} \markbox{m19032}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19033}{endowed} \markbox{19034}{with} \markbox{19035}{the} \markbox{19036}{interval} \markbox{19037}{projections} \markbox{19038}{via} \markbox{19039}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable interval projections} \markbox{19040}{form} \markbox{19041}{an} \markbox{m19042}{$R_s$}-interval \markbox{19043}{system} \markbox{19044}{for} \markbox{m19045}{$a,b\in \calX$}, \markbox{19046}{where} \markbox{m19047}{$R_s = R_s(\mathfrak S)>0$}.  \markbox{19048}{Since} \markbox{m19049}{$R_s= R_s(\mathfrak S)>0$}, \markbox{19050}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined} \markbox{19051}{and} \markbox{19052}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{19053}{provide} \markbox{19054}{constants} \markbox{m19055}{$R_1 = R_1(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19056}{and} \markbox{m19057}{$R_2(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19058}{so} \markbox{19059}{that} \markbox{19060}{for} \markbox{19061}{any} \markbox{m19062}{$r_1\geq R_1$} \markbox{19063}{and} \markbox{m19064}{$r_2 \geq R_2$}, \markbox{19065}{the} \markbox{19066}{conclusions} \markbox{19067}{of} \markbox{19068}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{19069}{hold} \markbox{19070}{for} \markbox{19071}{the} \markbox{19072}{family} \markbox{19073}{of} \markbox{19074}{collapsed} \markbox{19075}{intervals} \markbox{m19076}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19077}{obtained} \markbox{19078}{from} \markbox{19079}{the} \markbox{m19080}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{19081}{of} \markbox{19082}{the} \markbox{19083}{system} \markbox{m19084}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$}.  \markbox{19085}{We} \markbox{19086}{also} \markbox{19087}{want} \markbox{19088}{to} \markbox{19089}{assume} \markbox{19090}{that} \markbox{m19091}{$r_1>R_3 = R_3(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19092}{so} \markbox{19093}{that} \markbox{19094}{Lemma} \ref{lem:same thickenings} holds.

The \markbox{19095}{next} \markbox{19096}{proposition} \markbox{19097}{states} \markbox{19098}{that} \markbox{19099}{as} \markbox{19100}{long} \markbox{19101}{as} \markbox{m19102}{$r_1$} \markbox{19103}{is} \markbox{19104}{a} \markbox{19105}{positive} \markbox{19106}{integer,} \markbox{19107}{the} \markbox{19108}{collapsed} \markbox{19109}{intervals} \markbox{m19110}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{19111}{are} \markbox{19112}{all} \markbox{19113}{simplicial} \markbox{19114}{intervals,} \markbox{19115}{where} \markbox{19116}{the} \markbox{19117}{collapsed} \markbox{19118}{points} \markbox{19119}{lie} \markbox{19120}{at} \markbox{19121}{vertices.}  \markbox{19122}{The} \markbox{19123}{proof} \markbox{19124}{is} \markbox{19125}{a} \markbox{19126}{straightforward} \markbox{19127}{application} \markbox{19128}{of} \markbox{19129}{the} \markbox{19130}{ideas} \markbox{19131}{in} \markbox{19132}{the} \markbox{19133}{preceding} \markbox{19134}{sections,} \markbox{19135}{so} \markbox{19136}{we} \markbox{19137}{leave} \markbox{19138}{it} \markbox{19139}{to} \markbox{19140}{the} reader.

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable HFI}
As \markbox{19141}{long} \markbox{19142}{as} \markbox{m19143}{$r_1\geq \max\{R_1,R_3\}$} \markbox{19144}{is} \markbox{19145}{a} \markbox{19146}{positive} \markbox{19147}{integer} \markbox{19148}{and} \markbox{m19149}{$r_2\geq R_2$}, \markbox{19150}{the} \markbox{19151}{family} \markbox{19152}{of} \markbox{19153}{collapsed} \markbox{19154}{stable} \markbox{19155}{intervals} \markbox{m19156}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19157}{associated} \markbox{19158}{to} \markbox{19159}{an} \markbox{m19160}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{19161}{of} \markbox{m19162}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19163}{along} \markbox{m19164}{$T_{U,c}$} \markbox{19165}{and} \markbox{19166}{endowed} \markbox{19167}{with} \markbox{19168}{their} \markbox{19169}{collapsed} \markbox{19170}{projections} \markbox{19171}{forms} \markbox{19172}{a} \markbox{19173}{hierarchical} \markbox{19174}{family} \markbox{19175}{of} intervals.
\end{proposition} 



We \markbox{19176}{note} \markbox{19177}{the} \markbox{19178}{following} \markbox{19179}{immediate} \markbox{19180}{corollary} \markbox{19181}{of} \markbox{19182}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable HFI} \markbox{19183}{and} \markbox{19184}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC}:

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:stable HFI cube}
Let \markbox{m19185}{$a,b \in \calX$}, \markbox{m19186}{$K > K_0$} \markbox{19187}{for} \markbox{m19188}{$K_0$} \markbox{19189}{as} \markbox{19190}{in} \markbox{19191}{Theorem} \ref{thm:DF} \markbox{19192}{and} \markbox{m19193}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$}.  \markbox{19194}{Let} \markbox{m19195}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19196}{be} \markbox{19197}{the} \markbox{19198}{associated} \markbox{19199}{family} \markbox{19200}{of} \markbox{19201}{stable} \markbox{19202}{intervals.}  \markbox{19203}{Then} \markbox{19204}{the} \markbox{19205}{hierarchical} \markbox{19206}{hull} \markbox{m19207}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{19208}{is} \markbox{19209}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{19210}{to} \markbox{19211}{the} \markbox{19212}{dual} \markbox{19213}{cube} \markbox{19214}{complex} \markbox{19215}{of} \markbox{19216}{the} \markbox{19217}{associated} \markbox{19218}{HFI,} \markbox{19219}{with} \markbox{19220}{constants} \markbox{19221}{depending} \markbox{19222}{only} \markbox{19223}{on} \markbox{m19224}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{19225}{and} \markbox{m19226}{$K$}.
\end{corollary}





\subsection{From a perturbed pair to a family of stable decompositions} \label{subsec:perturbed to stable}

In \markbox{19227}{this} \markbox{19228}{subsection,} \markbox{19229}{we} \markbox{19230}{explain} \markbox{19231}{how} \markbox{19232}{the} \markbox{19233}{basic} \markbox{19234}{setup} \markbox{19235}{of} \markbox{19236}{this} \markbox{19237}{paper} \markbox{19238}{can} \markbox{19239}{be} \markbox{19240}{plugged} \markbox{19241}{into} \markbox{19242}{the} \markbox{19243}{machinery} \markbox{19244}{we} \markbox{19245}{have} \markbox{19246}{built} \markbox{19247}{so} far.

For \markbox{19248}{the} \markbox{19249}{rest} \markbox{19250}{of} \markbox{19251}{this} \markbox{19252}{section,} \markbox{19253}{assume} \markbox{19254}{that} \markbox{19255}{we} \markbox{19256}{have} \markbox{19257}{a} \markbox{19258}{colorable} \markbox{19259}{HHS} \markbox{m19260}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{19261}{endowed} \markbox{19262}{with} \markbox{19263}{the} \markbox{19264}{stable} \markbox{19265}{projections} \markbox{19266}{from} \markbox{19267}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains}.  \markbox{19268}{Let} \markbox{m19269}{$K > K_0=K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19270}{be} \markbox{19271}{as} \markbox{19272}{in} \markbox{19273}{item} \markbox{19274}{(2)} \markbox{19275}{of} \markbox{19276}{that} \markbox{19277}{theorem.}  



Also \markbox{19278}{for} \markbox{19279}{the} \markbox{19280}{rest} \markbox{19281}{of} \markbox{19282}{this} \markbox{19283}{section,} \markbox{19284}{fix} \markbox{m19285}{$a,b,a',b' \in \calX$} \markbox{19286}{so} \markbox{19287}{that} \markbox{m19288}{$d_{\calX}(a,a'), d_{\calX}(b,b') \leq 1$}.  \markbox{19289}{We} \markbox{19290}{refer} \markbox{19291}{to} \markbox{19292}{the} \markbox{19293}{points} \markbox{m19294}{$a',b'$} \markbox{19295}{as} \markbox{19296}{a} \emph{perturbed pair} \markbox{19297}{from} \markbox{m19298}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{19299}{Let} \markbox{m19300}{$\calU = \Rel_{K}(a,b)$} \markbox{19301}{and} \markbox{m19302}{$\calU' = \Rel_{K}(a',b')$}.  \markbox{19303}{Let} \markbox{m19304}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19305}{and} \markbox{m19306}{$\{T'_U\}_{U \in \calU'}$} \markbox{19307}{denote} \markbox{19308}{the} \markbox{19309}{families} \markbox{19310}{of} \markbox{19311}{stable} \markbox{19312}{intervals} \markbox{19313}{produced} \markbox{19314}{as} \markbox{19315}{above.} 

The \markbox{19316}{first} \markbox{19317}{thing} \markbox{19318}{to} \markbox{19319}{observe} \markbox{19320}{is} \markbox{19321}{that} \markbox{19322}{item} \markbox{19323}{(2)(a)} \markbox{19324}{of} \markbox{19325}{Controlling} \markbox{19326}{Domains} \markbox{19327}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains} \markbox{19328}{provides} \markbox{19329}{that} 
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m19330}{$|\calU \triangle \calU'|<N_0 = N_0(\mathfrak S)$}, and
\item Each \markbox{19331}{domain} \markbox{m19332}{$V \in \calU \triangle \calU'$} \markbox{19333}{satisfies} \markbox{m19334}{$d_V(a,b) \leq K'$} \markbox{19335}{and} \markbox{m19336}{$d_V(a',b') \leq K'$}, \markbox{19337}{where} \markbox{m19338}{$|K-K'|$} \markbox{19339}{is} \markbox{19340}{bounded} \markbox{19341}{in} \markbox{19342}{terms} \markbox{19343}{of} \markbox{m19344}{$\mathfrak S$}.
\end{enumerate}

Item \markbox{19345}{(2)} \markbox{19346}{plus} \markbox{19347}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{19348}{says} \markbox{19349}{that} \markbox{19350}{each} \markbox{19351}{of} \markbox{19352}{the} \markbox{19353}{associated} \markbox{19354}{collapsed} \markbox{19355}{intervals} \markbox{m19356}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{19357}{or} \markbox{m19358}{$\hT'_V$} \markbox{19359}{for} \markbox{m19360}{$V\in \calU \triangle \calU'$} \markbox{19361}{has} \markbox{19362}{bounded} \markbox{19363}{diameter.}  \markbox{19364}{For} \markbox{19365}{the} \markbox{19366}{rest} \markbox{19367}{of} \markbox{19368}{the} \markbox{19369}{domains,} \markbox{19370}{namely} \markbox{19371}{the} \markbox{19372}{domains} \markbox{m19373}{$U \in \calU_0 = \calU \cap \calU'$}, \markbox{19374}{we} \markbox{19375}{want} \markbox{19376}{to} \markbox{19377}{obtain} \markbox{19378}{compatible} \markbox{19379}{stable} \markbox{19380}{decompositions} \markbox{19381}{between} \markbox{19382}{the} \markbox{19383}{intervals} \markbox{m19384}{$T_U$} \markbox{19385}{and} \markbox{m19386}{$T'_U$}, \markbox{19387}{which} \markbox{19388}{we} \markbox{19389}{do} \markbox{19390}{as} follows.

First, \markbox{19391}{observe} \markbox{19392}{that} \markbox{19393}{if} \markbox{m19394}{$V \nest U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{19395}{then} \markbox{m19396}{$d_V(a,b)\geq K>\ES$} \markbox{19397}{and} \markbox{m19398}{$d_V(a',b') \geq K> \ES$}, \markbox{19399}{so} \markbox{19400}{the} \markbox{19401}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA} \markbox{19402}{implies} \markbox{19403}{that} \markbox{m19404}{$\rho^V_U \subset \calN_{\ES}(\lambda_U(a,b)) \cap \calN_{\ES}(\lambda_U(a',b'))$}, \markbox{19405}{where} \markbox{m19406}{$\lambda_U$} \markbox{19407}{is} \markbox{19408}{the} \markbox{19409}{function} \markbox{19410}{which} \markbox{19411}{assigns} \markbox{19412}{a} \markbox{19413}{geodesic} \markbox{19414}{in} \markbox{m19415}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{19416}{to} \markbox{19417}{any} \markbox{19418}{pair} \markbox{19419}{of} \markbox{19420}{points} \markbox{19421}{from} \markbox{19422}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:stable setup}.  \markbox{19423}{Hence} \markbox{19424}{taking} \markbox{m19425}{$\epsilon = 2\ES$} \markbox{19426}{in} \markbox{19427}{our} \markbox{19428}{stable} \markbox{19429}{tree} \markbox{19430}{setup} \markbox{19431}{suffices} \markbox{19432}{to} \markbox{19433}{make} \markbox{m19434}{$(\pi_U(a),\pi_U(b);\calY_U)$} \markbox{19435}{and} \markbox{m19436}{$(\pi_U(a'),\pi_U(b');\calY'_U)$} \markbox{19437}{into} \markbox{m19438}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{19439}{in} \markbox{m19440}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{19441}{(item} \markbox{19442}{(1)} \markbox{19443}{of} \markbox{19444}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}).

Moreover, \markbox{19445}{for} \markbox{19446}{each} \markbox{m19447}{$U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{19448}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains} \markbox{19449}{provides} \markbox{19450}{that} 
\begin{itemize}
\item[(a)] \markbox{19451}{The} \markbox{m19452}{$\rho$}-sets \markbox{19453}{for} \markbox{19454}{the} \markbox{19455}{domains} \markbox{19456}{in} \markbox{m19457}{$\calU$} \markbox{19458}{and} \markbox{m19459}{$\calU'$} \markbox{19460}{which} \markbox{19461}{nest} \markbox{19462}{into} \markbox{m19463}{$U$}---namely \markbox{m19464}{$\calY_U$} \markbox{19465}{and} \markbox{m19466}{$\calY'_U$} \markbox{19467}{respectively---satisfy} \markbox{m19468}{$|\calY_U \triangle \calY'_U| < N_0 = N_0(\mathfrak S)$}, and
\item[(b)] \markbox{19469}{If} \markbox{m19470}{$\calU^*_0 \subset \calU_0$} \markbox{19471}{is} \markbox{19472}{the} \markbox{19473}{set} \markbox{19474}{of} \markbox{19475}{domains} \markbox{m19476}{$U \in \calU_0$} \markbox{19477}{for} \markbox{19478}{which} \markbox{m19479}{$\calY_U \neq \calY'_U$} \markbox{19480}{or} \markbox{m19481}{$\pi_U(a) \neq \pi_U(a')$} \markbox{19482}{or} \markbox{m19483}{$\pi_U(b) \neq \pi_U(b')$}, \markbox{19484}{then} \markbox{m19485}{$\#\calU^*_0 < N_0$}.
\end{itemize}

Hence, \markbox{19486}{by} \markbox{19487}{item} \markbox{19488}{(a),} \markbox{19489}{these} \markbox{m19490}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{19491}{are} \markbox{m19492}{$(N_0, \epsilon)$}-admissible \markbox{19493}{in} \markbox{19494}{the} \markbox{19495}{sense} \markbox{19496}{of} \markbox{19497}{item} \markbox{19498}{(2)} \markbox{19499}{of} \markbox{19500}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{19501}{for} \markbox{19502}{all} \markbox{19503}{domains} \markbox{19504}{in} \markbox{m19505}{$\calU_0$}, \markbox{19506}{while} \markbox{19507}{item} \markbox{19508}{(b)} \markbox{19509}{says} \markbox{19510}{that} \markbox{19511}{for} \markbox{19512}{domains} \markbox{19513}{in} \markbox{m19514}{$\calU_0 - \calU^*_0$}, \markbox{19515}{these} \markbox{m19516}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{19517}{exactly} \markbox{19518}{coincide.}  \markbox{19519}{Thus} \markbox{19520}{item} \markbox{19521}{(2)} \markbox{19522}{of} \markbox{19523}{the} \markbox{19524}{Stable} \markbox{19525}{Intervals} \markbox{19526}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{19527}{implies} \markbox{19528}{that} \markbox{19529}{the} \markbox{m19530}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{19531}{of} \markbox{19532}{their} \markbox{19533}{stable} \markbox{19534}{intervals} \markbox{m19535}{$T_U, T'_U$} \markbox{19536}{admit} \markbox{m19537}{$L_s$}-compatible \markbox{19538}{stable} \markbox{19539}{decompositions,} \markbox{19540}{where} \markbox{m19541}{$L_s=L_s(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19542}{by} \markbox{19543}{choosing} \markbox{m19544}{$r_1 = \max\{R_1,R_3\}$} \markbox{19545}{and} \markbox{m19546}{$r_2 = R_2$}, \markbox{19547}{since} \markbox{19548}{the} \markbox{19549}{constants} \markbox{m19550}{$R_i = R_i(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19551}{depend} \markbox{19552}{only} \markbox{19553}{on} \markbox{m19554}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{19555}{In} \markbox{19556}{particular,} \markbox{19557}{we} have:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable interval decomp}
For \markbox{19558}{each} \markbox{m19559}{$U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{19560}{the} \markbox{m19561}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{19562}{of} \markbox{19563}{the} \markbox{19564}{stable} \markbox{19565}{intervals} \markbox{m19566}{$T_U = T_{U,e} \cup T_{U,c}$} \markbox{19567}{and} \markbox{m19568}{$T'_U = T'_{U,e} \cup T'_{U,c}$} \markbox{19569}{along} \markbox{m19570}{$T_{U,c}, T'_{U,c}$} \markbox{19571}{respectively} \markbox{19572}{admit} \markbox{m19573}{$L_s$}-compatible \markbox{19574}{stable} \markbox{19575}{decompositions,} \markbox{19576}{where} \markbox{m19577}{$L_s = L_s(\mathfrak S)>0$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item Moreover, \markbox{19578}{if} \markbox{m19579}{$U \in \calU_0 - \calU^*_0$}, \markbox{19580}{then} \markbox{m19581}{$T_U = T'_U$} \markbox{19582}{and} \markbox{19583}{these} \markbox{19584}{thickenings} \markbox{19585}{coincide} exactly.
\end{itemize}
\end{proposition}

For \markbox{19586}{each} \markbox{m19587}{$U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{19588}{let} \markbox{m19589}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U \to \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{19590}{and} \markbox{m19591}{$\Delta'_U:\hT'_U \to \hT'_{U,0}$} \markbox{19592}{denote} \markbox{19593}{the} \markbox{19594}{maps} \markbox{19595}{which} \markbox{19596}{collapse} \markbox{19597}{the} \markbox{19598}{unstable} \markbox{19599}{components} \markbox{19600}{these} \markbox{19601}{decompositions} \markbox{19602}{to} \markbox{19603}{points;} \markbox{19604}{we} \markbox{19605}{note} \markbox{19606}{that} \markbox{19607}{these} \markbox{19608}{maps} \markbox{19609}{are} \markbox{19610}{the} \markbox{19611}{identity} \markbox{19612}{when} \markbox{m19613}{$U \in \calU_0- \calU^*_0$}.  \markbox{19614}{By} \markbox{19615}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{19616}{of} \markbox{19617}{a} \markbox{19618}{stable} \markbox{19619}{decomposition,} \markbox{19620}{the} \markbox{19621}{subintervals} \markbox{19622}{of} \markbox{19623}{the} \markbox{m19624}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{19625}{and} \markbox{m19626}{$\hT'_U$} \markbox{19627}{being} \markbox{19628}{collapsed} \markbox{19629}{for} \markbox{m19630}{$U \in \calU_0$} \markbox{19631}{along} \markbox{19632}{with} \markbox{19633}{the} \markbox{19634}{whole} \markbox{19635}{intervals} \markbox{m19636}{$\hT_V, \hT'_V$} \markbox{19637}{(whichever} \markbox{19638}{is} \markbox{19639}{defined)} \markbox{19640}{for} \markbox{m19641}{$V \in \calU \triangle \calU'$} \markbox{19642}{collectively} \markbox{19643}{form} \markbox{m19644}{$(L_s^2+2K'N_0)$}-admissible \markbox{19645}{simplicial} \markbox{19646}{trimming} \markbox{19647}{setups} \markbox{19648}{for} \markbox{m19649}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19650}{and} \markbox{m19651}{$\{\hT'_U\}_{U \in \calU'}$}, \markbox{19652}{in} \markbox{19653}{the} \markbox{19654}{sense} \markbox{19655}{of} \markbox{19656}{Definition} \ref{defn:simplicial trimming setup}.  \markbox{19657}{This} \markbox{19658}{is} \markbox{19659}{because} \markbox{19660}{the} \markbox{19661}{set} \markbox{m19662}{$(\calU \cup \calU') - \calU_0$} \markbox{19663}{has} \markbox{19664}{at} \markbox{19665}{most} \markbox{m19666}{$N_0$}-many \markbox{19667}{domains} \markbox{19668}{by} \markbox{19669}{(1)} \markbox{19670}{above,} \markbox{19671}{each} \markbox{19672}{of} \markbox{19673}{which} \markbox{19674}{has} \markbox{19675}{diameter} \markbox{19676}{bounded} \markbox{19677}{by} \markbox{m19678}{$K'$}, \markbox{19679}{while} \markbox{19680}{the} \markbox{19681}{unstable} \markbox{19682}{pieces} \markbox{19683}{for} \markbox{19684}{the} \markbox{19685}{domains} \markbox{19686}{in} \markbox{m19687}{$\calU_0$} \markbox{19688}{consist} \markbox{19689}{of} \markbox{19690}{at} \markbox{19691}{most} \markbox{m19692}{$L_2$}-many \markbox{19693}{pieces} \markbox{19694}{of} \markbox{19695}{diameter} \markbox{19696}{at} \markbox{19697}{most} \markbox{m19698}{$L_2$}.

Set \markbox{m19699}{$L_2^2 + 2K'N_0 = S_0$}, \markbox{19700}{which} \markbox{19701}{we} \markbox{19702}{note} \markbox{19703}{depends} \markbox{19704}{only} \markbox{19705}{on} \markbox{m19706}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{19707}{and} \markbox{19708}{our} \markbox{19709}{choice} \markbox{19710}{of} \markbox{m19711}{$K$}.  \markbox{19712}{We} \markbox{19713}{now} \markbox{19714}{obtain} \markbox{19715}{the} \markbox{19716}{following} \markbox{19717}{from} \markbox{19718}{Theorem} \ref{thm:simplicial tree trimming} \markbox{19719}{and} \markbox{19720}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval decomp}:

\begin{proposition} \label{prop:stable collapse}
The \markbox{19721}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item The \markbox{19722}{collections} \markbox{m19723}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{19724}{and} \markbox{m19725}{$\{\hT'_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{19726}{are} \markbox{19727}{HFIs.}  \markbox{19728}{Let} \markbox{m19729}{$\calQ_0, \calQ'_0$} \markbox{19730}{denote} \markbox{19731}{their} \markbox{19732}{corresponding} \markbox{m19733}{$0$}-consistent subsets.
\item The \markbox{19734}{combined} \markbox{19735}{maps} \markbox{m19736}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ_0$} \markbox{19737}{and} \markbox{m19738}{$\Delta':\calQ' \to \calQ'_0$} \markbox{19739}{satisfy} \markbox{m19740}{$\Delta(\calQ) = \calQ_0$} \markbox{19741}{and} \markbox{m19742}{$\Delta'(\calQ') = \calQ'_0$} \markbox{19743}{and} \markbox{19744}{are} \markbox{19745}{both} \markbox{m19746}{$(1, S_0^2)$}-quasi-isometries.
\item There \markbox{19747}{exists} \markbox{19748}{maps} \markbox{m19749}{$\Xi:\calQ_0 \to \calQ$} \markbox{19750}{and} \markbox{m19751}{$\Xi':\calQ'_0 \to \calQ'$} \markbox{19752}{with} \markbox{m19753}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ_0}$} \markbox{19754}{and} \markbox{m19755}{$\Delta' \circ \Xi' = id_{\calQ'_0}$}.
\item At \markbox{19756}{the} \markbox{19757}{level} \markbox{19758}{of} \markbox{19759}{cube} \markbox{19760}{complexes,} \markbox{19761}{the} \markbox{19762}{maps} \markbox{m19763}{$\Delta\calQ \to \calQ_0$} \markbox{19764}{and} \markbox{m19765}{$\Delta':\calQ' \to \calQ'_0$} \markbox{19766}{delete} \markbox{19767}{at} \markbox{19768}{most} \markbox{m19769}{$S_0^2$}-many hyperplanes.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

Using \markbox{19770}{this} \markbox{19771}{proposition,} \markbox{19772}{we} \markbox{19773}{can} \markbox{19774}{define} \markbox{19775}{maps} \markbox{m19776}{$\hO_0:\calQ_0 \to \calX$} \markbox{19777}{and} \markbox{m19778}{$\hO'_0:\calQ'_0 \to \calX$} \markbox{19779}{by} \markbox{m19780}{$\hO_0 = \hO \circ \Xi$} \markbox{19781}{and} \markbox{m19782}{$\hO'_0 = \hO' \circ \Xi'$}, \markbox{19783}{where} \markbox{m19784}{$\hO:\calQ \to \calX$} \markbox{19785}{and} \markbox{m19786}{$\hO':\calQ \to \calX$} \markbox{19787}{are} \markbox{19788}{the} \markbox{19789}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{19790}{embeddings} \markbox{19791}{defined} \markbox{19792}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:upgrade to HHS}.

For \markbox{19793}{the} \markbox{19794}{final} \markbox{19795}{piece} \markbox{19796}{of} \markbox{19797}{setup,} \markbox{19798}{we} \markbox{19799}{want} \markbox{19800}{to} \markbox{19801}{observe} \markbox{19802}{that} \markbox{19803}{these} \markbox{19804}{HFIs} \markbox{m19805}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{19806}{and} \markbox{m19807}{$\{\hT'_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{19808}{admit} \markbox{19809}{an} \markbox{19810}{isomorphism} \markbox{19811}{in} \markbox{19812}{the} \markbox{19813}{sense} \markbox{19814}{of} \markbox{19815}{Proposition} \ref{prop:HFI isomorphism}.  \markbox{19816}{For} \markbox{19817}{this,} \markbox{19818}{we} \markbox{19819}{require} \markbox{19820}{the} \markbox{19821}{following} \markbox{19822}{lemma,} \markbox{19823}{whose} \markbox{19824}{proof} \markbox{19825}{is} \markbox{19826}{a} \markbox{19827}{straightforward} \markbox{19828}{application} \markbox{19829}{of} \markbox{19830}{the} \markbox{19831}{definitions} \markbox{19832}{and} \markbox{19833}{Corollary} \ref{cor:interval isometry}.  

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:interval isometries}
For \markbox{19834}{each} \markbox{m19835}{$U \in \calU^*_0$}, \markbox{19836}{the} \markbox{19837}{isometry} \markbox{m19838}{$i_U:\hT_{U,0} \to \hT'_{U,0}$} \markbox{19839}{provided} \markbox{19840}{by} \markbox{19841}{Corollary} \ref{cor:interval isometry} \markbox{19842}{satisfies} \markbox{19843}{the} \markbox{19844}{conditions} \markbox{19845}{of} \markbox{19846}{Proposition} \ref{prop:HFI isomorphism}.
\begin{itemize}
\item Thus \markbox{19847}{these} \markbox{19848}{component-wise} \markbox{19849}{isometries} \markbox{19850}{combine} \markbox{19851}{to} \markbox{19852}{give} \markbox{19853}{an} \markbox{19854}{isometry} \markbox{m19855}{$I_0:\calQ_0 \to \calQ'_0$}. 
\end{itemize}


\end{lemma}




\subsection{Statement of the stable cubulations theorem}

We \markbox{19856}{are} \markbox{19857}{now} \markbox{19858}{ready} \markbox{19859}{to} \markbox{19860}{state} \markbox{19861}{the} \markbox{19862}{stable} \markbox{19863}{cubical} \markbox{19864}{intervals} theorem:

\begin{theorem}[Stable \markbox{19865}{cubical} intervals]\label{thm:stable cubes}
Continuing \markbox{19866}{with} \markbox{19867}{our} \markbox{19868}{standing} \markbox{19869}{notation,} \markbox{19870}{there} \markbox{19871}{exists} \markbox{m19872}{$\Sigma = \Sigma(\mathfrak S, K)>0$} \markbox{19873}{so} \markbox{19874}{that} \markbox{19875}{the} \markbox{19876}{following} \markbox{19877}{diagram} \markbox{19878}{commutes} \markbox{19879}{up} \markbox{19880}{to} \markbox{19881}{error} \markbox{m19882}{$\Sigma$}:
\begin{equation}\label{Phi diagram}
  \begin{tikzcd}
   \calQ \arrow[ddrr,"\hO", bend left=40] \arrow[dr,"\Delta_0 \hspace{.075in}" left] &  \\
    &\calQ_{0} \arrow[dr,"\hO_0 \hspace{.2in}" below]\arrow[dd, "I_0"] \\
    & & \calX\\
    & \calQ'_{0} \arrow[ur,"\hO'_0"] \\
    \calQ'\arrow[uurr,"\hspace{.2in} \vspace{.1in} \hO'" below, bend right=40] \arrow[ur,"\Delta'_0"] & \\
  \end{tikzcd}
  \end{equation}

\begin{itemize}
\item In \markbox{19883}{the} \markbox{19884}{above,} \markbox{m19885}{$I_0:\calQ_0 \to \calQ'_0$} \markbox{19886}{is} \markbox{19887}{the} \markbox{19888}{isomorphism} \markbox{19889}{from} \markbox{19890}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval isometries}.
\item In \markbox{19891}{particular,} \markbox{19892}{any} \markbox{19893}{colorable} \markbox{19894}{hierarchically} \markbox{19895}{hyperbolic} \markbox{19896}{space} \markbox{19897}{is} \markbox{m19898}{$\Sigma$}-stably \markbox{19899}{weakly} \markbox{19900}{locally} \markbox{19901}{quasi-cubical} \markbox{19902}{(Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes}). 
\end{itemize}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}

It \markbox{19903}{remains} \markbox{19904}{to} \markbox{19905}{prove} \markbox{19906}{that} \markbox{19907}{the} \markbox{19908}{upper,} \markbox{19909}{lower,} \markbox{19910}{and} \markbox{19911}{middle} \markbox{19912}{triangles} \markbox{19913}{coarsely} \markbox{19914}{commute.}  \markbox{19915}{The} \markbox{19916}{proof} \markbox{19917}{for} \markbox{19918}{the} \markbox{19919}{upper} \markbox{19920}{(and} \markbox{19921}{hence} \markbox{19922}{the} \markbox{19923}{lower)} \markbox{19924}{is} \markbox{19925}{essentially} \markbox{19926}{automatic} \markbox{19927}{by} \markbox{19928}{construction.}  \markbox{19929}{In} \markbox{19930}{particular,} \markbox{19931}{by} \markbox{19932}{item} \markbox{19933}{(2)} \markbox{19934}{of} \markbox{19935}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable collapse}, \markbox{19936}{the} \markbox{19937}{map} \markbox{m19938}{$\Delta_0:\calQ \to \calQ_0$} \markbox{19939}{is} \markbox{19940}{a} \markbox{m19941}{$(1,S^2_0)$}-quasi-isometry \markbox{19942}{for} \markbox{m19943}{$S_0 = S_0(\mathfrak S, K)>0$}.  \markbox{19944}{On} \markbox{19945}{the} \markbox{19946}{other} \markbox{19947}{hand,} \markbox{19948}{item} \markbox{19949}{(3)} \markbox{19950}{of} \markbox{19951}{that} \markbox{19952}{proposition} \markbox{19953}{implies} \markbox{19954}{that} \markbox{m19955}{$\Delta_0 \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ_0}$} \markbox{19956}{while} \markbox{m19957}{$\hO_0:\calQ_0 \to \calX$} \markbox{19958}{is} \markbox{19959}{defined} \markbox{19960}{by} \markbox{m19961}{$\hO_0 = \hO \circ \Xi$}.  \markbox{19962}{Hence} \markbox{19963}{the} \markbox{19964}{top} \markbox{19965}{triangle} \markbox{19966}{commutes} \markbox{19967}{up} \markbox{19968}{to} \markbox{19969}{error} \markbox{m19970}{$S_0$}, \markbox{19971}{and} \markbox{19972}{the} \markbox{19973}{same} \markbox{19974}{holds} \markbox{19975}{for} \markbox{19976}{the} \markbox{19977}{bottom} triangle.

For \markbox{19978}{the} \markbox{19979}{middle} \markbox{19980}{triangle,} \markbox{19981}{we} \markbox{19982}{want} \markbox{19983}{to} \markbox{19984}{show} \markbox{19985}{that} \markbox{m19986}{$d_{\calX}(\hO_0(\hx), \hO'_0 \circ I_0(\hx))$} \markbox{19987}{is} \markbox{19988}{bounded} \markbox{19989}{in} \markbox{19990}{terms} \markbox{19991}{of} \markbox{m19992}{$\mathfrak S, K$} \markbox{19993}{for} \markbox{19994}{any} \markbox{m19995}{$\hx \in \calQ_0$}.  \markbox{19996}{However,} \markbox{19997}{we} \markbox{19998}{note} \markbox{19999}{that} \markbox{20000}{the} \markbox{20001}{maps} \markbox{m20002}{$\hO_0:\calQ_0 \to H$} \markbox{20003}{and} \markbox{m20004}{$\Delta_0 \circ \hPsi:H \to \calQ_0$} \markbox{20005}{are} \markbox{20006}{quasi-inverses} \markbox{20007}{(with} \markbox{20008}{errors} \markbox{20009}{depending} \markbox{20010}{on} \markbox{m20011}{$\mathfrak S, K$}), \markbox{20012}{and} \markbox{20013}{similarly} \markbox{20014}{for} \markbox{m20015}{$\hO'_0:\calQ'_0 \to H'$} \markbox{20016}{and} \markbox{m20017}{$\Delta_0 \circ \hPsi:H' \to \calQ'_0$}.  \markbox{20018}{Here,} \markbox{m20019}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{20020}{and} \markbox{m20021}{$H' = \hull_{\calX}(a',b')$}.  \markbox{20022}{But} \markbox{20023}{since} \markbox{m20024}{$d_{\calX}(a,a')\leq 1$} \markbox{20025}{and} \markbox{m20026}{$d_{\calX}(b,b')\leq 1$}, \markbox{20027}{it} \markbox{20028}{follows} \markbox{20029}{from} \markbox{20030}{the} \markbox{20031}{Distance} \markbox{20032}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF} \markbox{20033}{and} \markbox{20034}{Definition} \ref{defn:hier hull} \markbox{20035}{that} \markbox{m20036}{$d^{Haus}_{\calX}(H,H')$} \markbox{20037}{is} \markbox{20038}{bounded} \markbox{20039}{in} \markbox{20040}{terms} \markbox{20041}{of} \markbox{m20042}{$\mathfrak S$}.

Hence \markbox{20043}{it} \markbox{20044}{suffices} \markbox{20045}{to} \markbox{20046}{show} \markbox{20047}{that} \markbox{20048}{for} \markbox{m20049}{$x \in H \cap H'$} \markbox{20050}{(so} \markbox{20051}{that} \markbox{m20052}{$\hPsi(x)$} \markbox{20053}{and} \markbox{m20054}{$\hPsi'(x)$} \markbox{20055}{are} \markbox{20056}{both} \markbox{20057}{defined),} \markbox{20058}{we} have
$$d_{\calQ'_0}(\Delta'_0 \circ \hPsi'(x), I_0 \circ \Delta_0 \circ \hPsi(x))< \Sigma,$$
for \markbox{m20059}{$\Sigma = \Sigma(\mathfrak S, K)$}.  \markbox{20060}{Set} \markbox{m20061}{$\Delta'_0 \circ \hPsi'(x) = \hx'_0 = (\hx'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20062}{and} \markbox{m20063}{$I_0 \circ \Delta_0 \circ \hPsi(x) = \hy'_0= (\hy'_{U,0})$}, \markbox{20064}{where} \markbox{20065}{we} \markbox{20066}{note} \markbox{20067}{that} \markbox{20068}{both} \markbox{m20069}{$\hx'_0,\hy'_0 \in \calQ'_0$}.  

We \markbox{20070}{argue} \markbox{20071}{component-wise} \markbox{20072}{that} \markbox{m20073}{$d_{\calQ'_0}(\hx'_0,\hy'_0)$} \markbox{20074}{is} \markbox{20075}{bounded.}  \markbox{20076}{Recall} \markbox{20077}{that} \markbox{20078}{the} \markbox{20079}{map} \markbox{m20080}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{20081}{is} \markbox{20082}{defined} \markbox{20083}{component-wise} \markbox{20084}{(over} \markbox{20085}{the} \markbox{20086}{set} \markbox{m20087}{$\calU$}) \markbox{20088}{by} \markbox{m20089}{$\hpsi_U = q_U \circ \phi_U^{-1} \circ p_U \circ \pi_U$}, \markbox{20090}{where} \markbox{m20091}{$\pi_U:\calX \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{20092}{is} \markbox{20093}{the} \markbox{20094}{HHS} \markbox{20095}{projection,} \markbox{m20096}{$p_U:\calC(U) \to \phi_U(T_U)$} \markbox{20097}{is} \markbox{20098}{closest} \markbox{20099}{point} \markbox{20100}{projection,} \markbox{m20101}{$\phi_U:T_U \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{20102}{is} \markbox{20103}{the} \markbox{m20104}{$(L_0,L_0)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{20105}{embedding} \markbox{20106}{provided} \markbox{20107}{by} \markbox{20108}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure} \markbox{20109}{(here} \markbox{m20110}{$L_0=L_0(\mathfrak S)$}), \markbox{20111}{and} \markbox{m20112}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{20113}{is} \markbox{20114}{the} \markbox{20115}{map} \markbox{20116}{which} \markbox{20117}{collapses} \markbox{20118}{a} \markbox{20119}{uniform} \markbox{20120}{thickening} \markbox{20121}{of} \markbox{m20122}{$T_U$} \markbox{20123}{along} \markbox{20124}{the} \markbox{20125}{cluster} \markbox{20126}{components,} \markbox{20127}{with} \markbox{20128}{constants} \markbox{20129}{depending} \markbox{20130}{only} \markbox{20131}{on} \markbox{m20132}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{20133}{The} \markbox{20134}{map} \markbox{m20135}{$\hPsi':H' \to \calQ'$} \markbox{20136}{is} \markbox{20137}{defined} similarly.

First, \markbox{20138}{we} \markbox{20139}{can} \markbox{20140}{reduce} \markbox{20141}{to} \markbox{20142}{involved} \markbox{20143}{domains} \markbox{20144}{in} \markbox{m20145}{$\calU_0 = \calU \cap \calU'$}.  \markbox{20146}{If} \markbox{m20147}{$U \in \calU \triangle \calU'$}, \markbox{20148}{then} \markbox{m20149}{$a,b$} \markbox{20150}{and} \markbox{m20151}{$a',b'$} \markbox{20152}{have} \markbox{20153}{bounded} \markbox{20154}{diameter} \markbox{20155}{projections} \markbox{20156}{to} \markbox{m20157}{$U$} \markbox{20158}{in} \markbox{20159}{terms} \markbox{20160}{of} \markbox{m20161}{$K$} \markbox{20162}{and} \markbox{m20163}{$\mathfrak S$}, \markbox{20164}{while} \markbox{20165}{also} \markbox{20166}{each} \markbox{20167}{such} \markbox{20168}{domain} \markbox{20169}{is} \markbox{20170}{involved} \markbox{20171}{in} \markbox{20172}{the} \markbox{20173}{sense} \markbox{20174}{of} \markbox{20175}{Definition} \ref{defn:involved} \markbox{20176}{and} \markbox{20177}{hence} \markbox{20178}{there} \markbox{20179}{are} \markbox{20180}{only} \markbox{20181}{boundedly-many} \markbox{20182}{by} \markbox{20183}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains}. \markbox{20184}{Next} \markbox{20185}{observe} \markbox{20186}{that} \markbox{20187}{if} \markbox{m20188}{$U \in \calU_0$} \markbox{20189}{is} \markbox{20190}{not} \markbox{20191}{involved,} \markbox{20192}{then} \markbox{20193}{the} \markbox{20194}{stable} \markbox{20195}{trees} \markbox{m20196}{$T_U, T'_U$} \markbox{20197}{for} \markbox{20198}{the} \markbox{20199}{two} \markbox{20200}{setups} \markbox{20201}{are} \markbox{20202}{exactly} \markbox{20203}{the} \markbox{20204}{same,} \markbox{20205}{and} \markbox{20206}{hence} \markbox{20207}{have} \markbox{20208}{identical} \markbox{20209}{thickenings,} \markbox{20210}{and} \markbox{20211}{thus} \markbox{20212}{the} \markbox{20213}{stable} \markbox{20214}{decompositions} \markbox{20215}{the} \markbox{20216}{pair} \markbox{20217}{are} \markbox{20218}{the} \markbox{20219}{(identical)} \markbox{20220}{collection} \markbox{20221}{of} \markbox{20222}{edge} \markbox{20223}{components} \markbox{20224}{for} \markbox{20225}{each,} \markbox{20226}{and} \markbox{20227}{their} \markbox{20228}{corresponding} \markbox{20229}{collapsed} \markbox{20230}{trees} \markbox{m20231}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{20232}{and} \markbox{m20233}{$\hT'_U$} \markbox{20234}{are} \markbox{20235}{identical.}  \markbox{20236}{Hence,} \markbox{20237}{for} \markbox{20238}{uninvolved} \markbox{m20239}{$U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{20240}{we} \markbox{20241}{have} \markbox{m20242}{$\hx'_{U,0} = \hy'_{U,0}$}.

Let \markbox{m20243}{$U \in \calU_0$} \markbox{20244}{be} \markbox{20245}{involved.}  \markbox{20246}{Since} \markbox{20247}{there} \markbox{20248}{are} \markbox{20249}{boundedly-many} \markbox{20250}{(in} \markbox{m20251}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20252}{such} \markbox{20253}{domains} \markbox{20254}{by} \markbox{20255}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains}, \markbox{20256}{it} \markbox{20257}{suffices} \markbox{20258}{to} \markbox{20259}{bound} \markbox{20260}{the} \markbox{20261}{diameter} \markbox{m20262}{$d_{\hT'_{U,0}}(\hx'_{U,0}, \hy'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20263}{in} \markbox{20264}{terms} \markbox{20265}{of} \markbox{m20266}{$\mathfrak S$}.

  \markbox{20267}{The} \markbox{20268}{distance} \markbox{m20269}{$d_{\hT'_{U,0}}(\hx'_{U,0}, \hy'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20270}{is} \markbox{20271}{measured} \markbox{20272}{in} \markbox{20273}{the} \markbox{20274}{edge} \markbox{20275}{components} \markbox{20276}{of} \markbox{m20277}{$\hT'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20278}{which} \markbox{20279}{separate} \markbox{20280}{them,} \markbox{20281}{and} \markbox{20282}{these} \markbox{20283}{edge} \markbox{20284}{components} \markbox{20285}{are} \markbox{20286}{stable} \markbox{20287}{components} \markbox{20288}{of} \markbox{m20289}{$T'_U$}.  \markbox{20290}{This} \markbox{20291}{means} \markbox{20292}{that} \markbox{20293}{if} \markbox{20294}{the} \markbox{20295}{distance} \markbox{m20296}{$d_{\hT'_{U,0}}(\hx'_{U,0}, \hy'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20297}{is} \markbox{20298}{very} \markbox{20299}{large,} \markbox{20300}{then} \markbox{20301}{there} \markbox{20302}{must} \markbox{20303}{be} \markbox{20304}{either} 
\begin{enumerate}
\item some \markbox{20305}{long} \markbox{20306}{stable} \markbox{20307}{component} \markbox{m20308}{$E' \subset T'_{U,s}$} \markbox{20309}{so} \markbox{20310}{that} \markbox{20311}{some} \markbox{20312}{long} \markbox{20313}{segment} \markbox{20314}{of} \markbox{m20315}{$\Delta'_U(q'_U(E'))$} \markbox{20316}{separates} \markbox{m20317}{$\hx'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20318}{from} \markbox{m20319}{$\hy'_{U,0}$}, or
\item if \markbox{20320}{no} \markbox{20321}{such} \markbox{20322}{long} \markbox{20323}{component} \markbox{20324}{exists,} \markbox{20325}{there} \markbox{20326}{must} \markbox{20327}{be} \markbox{20328}{some} \markbox{20329}{large} \markbox{20330}{number} \markbox{20331}{of} \markbox{20332}{such} \markbox{20333}{stable} \markbox{20334}{components} \markbox{20335}{separating} them.
\end{enumerate}

In \markbox{20336}{case} \markbox{20337}{(1),} \markbox{20338}{let} \markbox{m20339}{$E \subset T_{U,s}$} \markbox{20340}{be} \markbox{20341}{the} \markbox{20342}{stable} \markbox{20343}{component} \markbox{20344}{paired} \markbox{20345}{with} \markbox{m20346}{$E' \subset T'_{U,s}$}.  \markbox{20347}{Note} \markbox{20348}{that} \markbox{m20349}{$\phi_U(E) \cup \phi'_U(E')$} \markbox{20350}{is} \markbox{20351}{uniformly} \markbox{20352}{quasi-convex} \markbox{20353}{(in} \markbox{m20354}{$\mathfrak S$}), \markbox{20355}{and} \markbox{20356}{hence} \markbox{m20357}{$\pi_U(x)$} \markbox{20358}{has} \markbox{20359}{a} \markbox{20360}{uniformly} \markbox{20361}{bounded} \markbox{20362}{projection} \markbox{20363}{to} \markbox{20364}{it.}  \markbox{20365}{However} \markbox{20366}{the} \markbox{20367}{fact} \markbox{20368}{that} \markbox{20369}{a} \markbox{20370}{long} \markbox{20371}{segment} \markbox{20372}{of} \markbox{m20373}{$\Delta'_U(q_U(E')) \subset \hT'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20374}{separates} \markbox{m20375}{$\hx'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20376}{from} \markbox{m20377}{$\hy'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20378}{means} \markbox{20379}{that} \markbox{20380}{some} \markbox{20381}{large} \markbox{20382}{diameter} \markbox{20383}{portion} \markbox{20384}{of} \markbox{m20385}{$\phi_U(E) \cup \phi'_U(E')$} \markbox{20386}{coarsely} \markbox{20387}{(in} \markbox{m20388}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20389}{separates} \markbox{m20390}{$p_U(\pi_U(x))$} \markbox{20391}{from} \markbox{m20392}{$p'_U(\pi_U(x))$}, \markbox{20393}{which} \markbox{20394}{is} impossible.

In \markbox{20395}{case} \markbox{20396}{(2),} \markbox{20397}{we} \markbox{20398}{can} \markbox{20399}{assume} \markbox{20400}{that} \markbox{20401}{no} \markbox{20402}{such} \markbox{20403}{long} \markbox{20404}{stable} \markbox{20405}{component} \markbox{20406}{exists,} \markbox{20407}{so} \markbox{20408}{that} \markbox{20409}{the} \markbox{20410}{distance} \markbox{m20411}{$d_{\hT'_{U,0}}(\hx'_{U,0}, \hy'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20412}{corresponds} \markbox{20413}{to} \markbox{20414}{some} \markbox{20415}{sequence} \markbox{m20416}{$E'_1, \dots, E'_n \subset T'_{U,s}$} \markbox{20417}{of} \markbox{20418}{short} \markbox{20419}{stable} \markbox{20420}{components} \markbox{20421}{of} \markbox{20422}{length} \markbox{20423}{bounded} \markbox{20424}{in} \markbox{20425}{terms} \markbox{20426}{of} \markbox{m20427}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{20428}{Let} \markbox{m20429}{$E_i \subset T_{U,s}$} \markbox{20430}{denote} \markbox{20431}{the} \markbox{20432}{stable} \markbox{20433}{component} \markbox{20434}{paired} \markbox{20435}{with} \markbox{m20436}{$E'_i$}.  \markbox{20437}{By} \markbox{20438}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure} \markbox{20439}{and} \markbox{20440}{the} \markbox{20441}{fact} \markbox{20442}{that} \markbox{m20443}{$d_{\calX}(a,a') \leq 1$} \markbox{20444}{and} \markbox{m20445}{$d_{\calX}(b,b')\leq 1$}, \markbox{20446}{we} \markbox{20447}{have} \markbox{20448}{that} \markbox{m20449}{$\phi_U(T_U)$} \markbox{20450}{and} \markbox{m20451}{$\phi'_U(T'_U)$} \markbox{20452}{are} \markbox{20453}{within} \markbox{20454}{bounded} \markbox{20455}{(in} \markbox{m20456}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20457}{Hausdorff} \markbox{20458}{distance} \markbox{20459}{in} \markbox{m20460}{$\calC(U)$}.  \markbox{20461}{Since} \markbox{20462}{each} \markbox{20463}{of} \markbox{20464}{the} \markbox{m20465}{$E'_i$} \markbox{20466}{are} \markbox{20467}{uniformly} \markbox{20468}{close} \markbox{20469}{(in} \markbox{m20470}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20471}{to} \markbox{m20472}{$E_i$} \markbox{20473}{and} \markbox{20474}{the} \markbox{20475}{bijection} \markbox{m20476}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_{U,s}) \to \pi_0(T'_{U,s})$} \markbox{20477}{is} \markbox{20478}{order-preserving,} \markbox{20479}{it} \markbox{20480}{follows} \markbox{20481}{that} \markbox{20482}{the} \markbox{20483}{hulls} \markbox{m20484}{$\hull_{\phi_U(T_U)}(E_1, E_n)$} \markbox{20485}{and} \markbox{m20486}{$\hull_{\phi'_U(T'_U)}(E'_1,E'_n)$} \markbox{20487}{are} \markbox{20488}{within} \markbox{20489}{uniform} \markbox{20490}{(in} \markbox{m20491}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20492}{Hausdorff} \markbox{20493}{distance} \markbox{20494}{of} \markbox{20495}{each} \markbox{20496}{other,} \markbox{20497}{and} \markbox{20498}{hence} \markbox{20499}{their} \markbox{20500}{union} \markbox{20501}{is} \markbox{20502}{uniformly} \markbox{20503}{quasi-convex} \markbox{20504}{(in} \markbox{m20505}{$\mathfrak S$}).  \markbox{20506}{Thus,} \markbox{20507}{if} \markbox{m20508}{$\Delta'_U(q'_U(E'_1)), \dots, \Delta'_U(q'_U(E'_n))$} \markbox{20509}{separate} \markbox{m20510}{$\hx'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20511}{from} \markbox{m20512}{$\hy'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20513}{in} \markbox{m20514}{$\hT'_{U,0}$}, \markbox{20515}{then} \markbox{20516}{the} \markbox{20517}{union} \markbox{20518}{of} \markbox{20519}{these} \markbox{20520}{hulls} \markbox{20521}{coarsely} \markbox{20522}{(in} \markbox{m20523}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20524}{separates} \markbox{m20525}{$p_U(\pi_U(x))$} \markbox{20526}{from} \markbox{m20527}{$p'_U(\pi_U(x))$}.

Since \markbox{20528}{each} \markbox{20529}{of} \markbox{20530}{the} \markbox{20531}{segments} \markbox{m20532}{$E'_i$} \markbox{20533}{is} \markbox{20534}{bounded} \markbox{20535}{length,} \markbox{20536}{the} \markbox{20537}{union} \markbox{20538}{of} \markbox{20539}{these} \markbox{20540}{hulls} \markbox{20541}{is} \markbox{20542}{long} \markbox{20543}{if} \markbox{20544}{the} \markbox{20545}{number} \markbox{20546}{of} \markbox{20547}{segments} \markbox{m20548}{$n$} \markbox{20549}{is} \markbox{20550}{very} \markbox{20551}{large.}  \markbox{20552}{Moreover,} \markbox{20553}{each} \markbox{20554}{pair} \markbox{20555}{of} \markbox{20556}{segments} \markbox{m20557}{$E'_i, E'_{i+1}$} \markbox{20558}{is} \markbox{20559}{separated} \markbox{20560}{by} \markbox{20561}{some} \markbox{20562}{complementary} \markbox{20563}{component} \markbox{m20564}{$C_i \subset T'_U - T'_{U,s}$}.  \markbox{20565}{By} \markbox{20566}{construction,} \markbox{20567}{all} \markbox{20568}{but} \markbox{20569}{boundedly-many} \markbox{20570}{(in} \markbox{m20571}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20572}{of} \markbox{20573}{these} \markbox{20574}{components} \markbox{20575}{corresponds} \markbox{20576}{to} \markbox{20577}{some} \markbox{20578}{cluster} \markbox{20579}{component} \markbox{20580}{of} \markbox{m20581}{$T'_U$}.  \markbox{20582}{Since} \markbox{20583}{there} \markbox{20584}{are} \markbox{20585}{only} \markbox{20586}{boundedly-many} \markbox{20587}{(in} \markbox{m20588}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20589}{involved} \markbox{20590}{domains,} \markbox{20591}{by} \markbox{20592}{choosing} \markbox{m20593}{$n$} \markbox{20594}{to} \markbox{20595}{be} \markbox{20596}{sufficiently} \markbox{20597}{large,} \markbox{20598}{there} \markbox{20599}{exists} \markbox{20600}{some} \markbox{m20601}{$C_j$} \markbox{20602}{which} \markbox{20603}{contains} \markbox{20604}{a} \markbox{m20605}{$\nest_{\calU_0}$}-minimal \markbox{20606}{domain} \markbox{m20607}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{20608}{which} \markbox{20609}{is} \markbox{20610}{both} \markbox{m20611}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{20612}{and} \markbox{m20613}{$\nest_{\calU'}$}-minimal.  \markbox{20614}{But} \markbox{20615}{this} \markbox{20616}{is} \markbox{20617}{impossible,} \markbox{20618}{for} \markbox{20619}{the} \markbox{20620}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA} \markbox{20621}{would} \markbox{20622}{imply} \markbox{20623}{that} \markbox{m20624}{$d_V(\rho^U_V(p_U(\pi_U(x)), \rho^U_V(p'_U(\pi_U(x)))) \succ K$}, \markbox{20625}{and} \markbox{20626}{this} \markbox{20627}{cannot} \markbox{20628}{happen} \markbox{20629}{as} \markbox{20630}{we} \markbox{20631}{can} \markbox{20632}{also} \markbox{20633}{arrange} \markbox{m20634}{$\pi_U(x)$} \markbox{20635}{to} \markbox{20636}{be} \markbox{20637}{as} \markbox{20638}{far} \markbox{20639}{from} \markbox{m20640}{$\rho^V_U$} \markbox{20641}{as} \markbox{20642}{necessary.}  \markbox{20643}{Hence} \markbox{20644}{no} \markbox{20645}{such} \markbox{20646}{long} \markbox{20647}{sequence} \markbox{m20648}{$E'_1, \dots E'_n$} \markbox{20649}{can} \markbox{20650}{exist,} \markbox{20651}{completing} \markbox{20652}{the} proof.



\end{proof}



\appendix
\section{Proof of the Tree Trimming Theorem \ref{thm:tree trimming}}\label{app:TT}

Below \markbox{20653}{is} \markbox{20654}{a} \markbox{20655}{re-statement} \markbox{20656}{of} \markbox{20657}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}.  \markbox{20658}{See} \markbox{20659}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tree trimming} \markbox{20660}{for} \markbox{20661}{the} \markbox{20662}{contextual} \markbox{20663}{definitions} \markbox{20664}{and} notation.

\begin{theorem}[Tree Trimming]
There \markbox{20665}{exists} \markbox{m20666}{$B_{tt} = B_{tt}(\mathfrak S, K)>0$} \markbox{20667}{so} \markbox{20668}{that} \markbox{20669}{for} \markbox{20670}{any} \markbox{m20671}{$B < B_{tt}$}, \markbox{20672}{there} \markbox{20673}{exists} \markbox{m20674}{$L =L(\mathfrak S, B)>0$} \markbox{20675}{so} \markbox{20676}{that} \markbox{20677}{the} \markbox{20678}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item We \markbox{20679}{have} \markbox{m20680}{$\Delta(\calQ) \subset \calQ'$}.
\item There \markbox{20681}{is} \markbox{20682}{a} \markbox{20683}{map} \markbox{m20684}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{20685}{so} \markbox{20686}{that} \markbox{m20687}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ'}$}.  \markbox{20688}{In} \markbox{20689}{particular,} \markbox{m20690}{$\Delta(\calQ) = \calQ'$}.
\item The \markbox{20691}{map} \markbox{m20692}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{20693}{is} \markbox{20694}{an} \markbox{m20695}{$(L,L)$}-quasi-isometry.
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
The \markbox{20696}{fact} \markbox{20697}{that} \markbox{m20698}{$\Delta(\calQ) \subset \calQ'$}, \markbox{20699}{namely} \markbox{20700}{that} \markbox{m20701}{$\Delta$} \markbox{20702}{preserves} \markbox{m20703}{$0$}-consistency, \markbox{20704}{is} \markbox{20705}{immediate} \markbox{20706}{from} \markbox{20707}{the} \markbox{20708}{fact} \markbox{20709}{that} \markbox{20710}{the} \markbox{m20711}{$\Delta_U$} \markbox{20712}{just} \markbox{20713}{collapse} \markbox{20714}{subintervals,} \markbox{20715}{so} \markbox{20716}{coordinates} \markbox{20717}{which} \markbox{20718}{were} \markbox{20719}{collapsed} \markbox{20720}{projections} \markbox{20721}{remain} \markbox{20722}{collapsed} \markbox{20723}{projections,} \markbox{20724}{showing} \markbox{20725}{item} \markbox{20726}{(1).}  \markbox{20727}{Items} \markbox{20728}{(2)} \markbox{20729}{and} \markbox{20730}{(3)} \markbox{20731}{require} \markbox{20732}{more} \markbox{20733}{work} \markbox{20734}{and} \markbox{20735}{we} \markbox{20736}{provide} \markbox{20737}{a} \markbox{20738}{detailed} \markbox{20739}{sketch} \markbox{20740}{of} both.
\medskip

\textbf{\underline{Item (2): Surjectivity of $\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$}}: \markbox{20741}{Let} \markbox{m20742}{$\hy \in \calQ'$}.  \markbox{20743}{We} \markbox{20744}{will} \markbox{20745}{construct} \markbox{20746}{a} \markbox{20747}{point} \markbox{m20748}{$\hx \in \calQ$} \markbox{20749}{with} \markbox{m20750}{$\Delta(\hx) = \hy$} \markbox{20751}{by} \markbox{20752}{a} \markbox{20753}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{20754}{argument,} \markbox{20755}{thereby} \markbox{20756}{defining} \markbox{20757}{a} \markbox{20758}{map} \markbox{m20759}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{20760}{with} \markbox{m20761}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ'}$}.

For \markbox{20762}{each} \markbox{m20763}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{20764}{let} \markbox{m20765}{$C_U = \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}.  \markbox{20766}{Our} \markbox{20767}{goal} \markbox{20768}{is} \markbox{20769}{to} \markbox{20770}{pick,} \markbox{20771}{for} \markbox{20772}{each} \markbox{m20773}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{20774}{a} \markbox{20775}{point} \markbox{m20776}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{20777}{and} \markbox{20778}{then} \markbox{20779}{prove} \markbox{m20780}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{20781}{of} \markbox{20782}{the} \markbox{20783}{tuple} \markbox{m20784}{$\hx = (\hx_U)$}.  \markbox{20785}{Note} \markbox{20786}{that} \markbox{m20787}{$\Delta(\hx) =\hy$} \markbox{20788}{for} \markbox{20789}{such} \markbox{20790}{a} \markbox{20791}{tuple,} \markbox{20792}{by} \markbox{20793}{construction.}  \markbox{20794}{The} \markbox{20795}{proof} \markbox{20796}{is} \markbox{20797}{by} \markbox{20798}{induction} \markbox{20799}{on} \markbox{20800}{the} \markbox{20801}{nesting} \markbox{20802}{level} \markbox{20803}{in} \markbox{m20804}{$\calU$}, \markbox{20805}{and} \markbox{20806}{is} \markbox{20807}{similar} \markbox{20808}{to} \markbox{20809}{the} \markbox{20810}{construction} \markbox{20811}{of} \markbox{20812}{the} \markbox{20813}{map} \markbox{m20814}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{20815}{as} \markbox{20816}{in} \markbox{20817}{Proposition} \ref{prop:coarse surjectivity}.  \markbox{20818}{The} \markbox{20819}{main} \markbox{20820}{difference} \markbox{20821}{is} \markbox{20822}{that} \markbox{20823}{the} \markbox{20824}{collapsing} \markbox{20825}{subintervals} \markbox{20826}{are} \markbox{20827}{not} \markbox{20828}{automatically} \markbox{20829}{associated} \markbox{20830}{to} \markbox{20831}{a} \markbox{20832}{collection} \markbox{20833}{of} \markbox{20834}{domains,} \markbox{20835}{and} \markbox{20836}{this} \markbox{20837}{is} \markbox{20838}{where} \markbox{20839}{the} \markbox{20840}{work} \markbox{20841}{lies.}  \markbox{20842}{The} \markbox{20843}{proof} \markbox{20844}{is} \markbox{20845}{basically} \markbox{20846}{the} \markbox{20847}{proof} \markbox{20848}{of} \markbox{20849}{the} \markbox{20850}{analogous} \markbox{20851}{fact} \markbox{20852}{in} \cite[Theorem 10.2]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{20853}{except} \markbox{20854}{that} \markbox{20855}{our} \markbox{20856}{setup} \markbox{20857}{is} \markbox{20858}{much} \markbox{20859}{simpler.}  \markbox{20860}{What} \markbox{20861}{follows} \markbox{20862}{is} \markbox{20863}{a} \markbox{20864}{very} \markbox{20865}{detailed} \markbox{20866}{sketch,} \markbox{20867}{which} \markbox{20868}{leaves} \markbox{20869}{some} \markbox{20870}{small} \markbox{20871}{bits} \markbox{20872}{to} \markbox{20873}{the} reader.

For \markbox{20874}{the} \markbox{20875}{base} \markbox{20876}{case,} \markbox{20877}{let} \markbox{m20878}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{20879}{be} \markbox{m20880}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.   \markbox{20881}{If} \markbox{m20882}{$\hy_U \in \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{20883}{is} \markbox{20884}{not} \markbox{20885}{contained} \markbox{20886}{in} \markbox{m20887}{$\Delta_U(B)$} \markbox{20888}{for} \markbox{20889}{some} \markbox{m20890}{$B \in \calB$}, \markbox{20891}{then} \markbox{m20892}{$C_U\subset \hT_U$} \markbox{20893}{is} \markbox{20894}{a} \markbox{20895}{point} \markbox{20896}{and} \markbox{20897}{we} \markbox{20898}{set} \markbox{m20899}{$\hx_U = C_U$}.  \markbox{20900}{If} \markbox{m20901}{$\hy_U \in \Delta_U(B)$} \markbox{20902}{for} \markbox{20903}{some} \markbox{m20904}{$B \in \calB$} \markbox{20905}{and} \markbox{m20906}{$B \subset \hT_U$} \markbox{20907}{does} \markbox{20908}{not} \markbox{20909}{contain} \markbox{20910}{an} \markbox{20911}{endpoint,} \markbox{20912}{then} \markbox{20913}{let} \markbox{m20914}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{20915}{be} \markbox{20916}{any} \markbox{20917}{point.}  \markbox{20918}{If} \markbox{20919}{instead} \markbox{m20920}{$C_U$} \markbox{20921}{does} \markbox{20922}{contain} \markbox{20923}{an} \markbox{20924}{endpoint,} \markbox{20925}{then} \markbox{20926}{it} \markbox{20927}{is} \markbox{20928}{possible} \markbox{20929}{that} \markbox{20930}{it} \markbox{20931}{contains} \markbox{20932}{both} \markbox{20933}{endpoints,} \markbox{20934}{and} \markbox{20935}{we} \markbox{20936}{need} \markbox{20937}{to} \markbox{20938}{choose} one.

The \markbox{20939}{following} \markbox{20940}{claim,} \markbox{20941}{which} \markbox{20942}{is} \markbox{20943}{exactly} \cite[Claim 10.3]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{20944}{does} \markbox{20945}{not} \markbox{20946}{require} \markbox{m20947}{$U$} \markbox{20948}{to} \markbox{20949}{be} \markbox{m20950}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal:

\begin{claim} \label{claim:choose one}
If \markbox{m20951}{$W, Z \in \{V \in \calU| V\pitchfork U, \hspace{.1in} \text{and} \hspace{.1in} \hy_V \neq (\hd^U_V)_0\}$}, \markbox{20952}{then} \markbox{m20953}{$\hd^W_U = \hd^Z_U$}.
\end{claim}
