With \markbox{20954}{Claim} \ref{claim:choose one} \markbox{20955}{in} \markbox{20956}{hand,} \markbox{20957}{we} \markbox{20958}{can} \markbox{20959}{define} \markbox{m20960}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{20961}{for} \markbox{m20962}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m20963}{$U$} \markbox{20964}{as} follows:

\begin{itemize}
\item If \markbox{m20965}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork} = \{V \in \calU| V \pitchfork U \hspace{.1in} \mathrm{ and } \hspace{.1in} \hy_W \neq (\hd^V_U)_0\} \neq \emptyset$}, \markbox{20966}{then} \markbox{20967}{we} \markbox{20968}{set} \markbox{m20969}{$\hx_U = \hd^W_U$} \markbox{20970}{for} \markbox{20971}{any} \markbox{20972}{(and} \markbox{20973}{hence} \markbox{20974}{all,} \markbox{20975}{by} \markbox{20976}{the} \markbox{20977}{claim)} \markbox{m20978}{$W \in \calW_U^{\pitchfork}$}.
\item If \markbox{m20979}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork} = \emptyset$}, \markbox{20980}{then} \markbox{20981}{we} \markbox{20982}{let} \markbox{m20983}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{20984}{be} \markbox{20985}{any} \markbox{20986}{marked} \markbox{20987}{point} \markbox{20988}{in} \markbox{m20989}{$C_U$}.
\end{itemize}

At \markbox{20990}{this} \markbox{20991}{point,} \markbox{20992}{we} \markbox{20993}{also} \markbox{20994}{want} \markbox{20995}{to} \markbox{20996}{set} \markbox{m20997}{$l_U$} \markbox{20998}{to} \markbox{20999}{be} \markbox{21000}{equal} \markbox{21001}{to} \markbox{21002}{the} \markbox{21003}{endpoint} \markbox{m21004}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21005}{when} \markbox{m21006}{$U$} \markbox{21007}{is} \markbox{m21008}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal, \markbox{21009}{where} \markbox{m21010}{$l_U = \emptyset$} \markbox{21011}{when} \markbox{m21012}{$C_U$} \markbox{21013}{does} \markbox{21014}{not} \markbox{21015}{contain} \markbox{21016}{an} \markbox{21017}{endpoint} \markbox{21018}{of} \markbox{m21019}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{21020}{These} \markbox{21021}{labels} \markbox{21022}{will} \markbox{21023}{play} \markbox{21024}{a} \markbox{21025}{similar} \markbox{21026}{role} \markbox{21027}{as} \markbox{21028}{in} \markbox{21029}{the} \markbox{21030}{cluster} \markbox{21031}{honing} \markbox{21032}{process} \markbox{21033}{in} \markbox{21034}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:hO defined}.

For \markbox{21035}{the} \markbox{21036}{inductive} \markbox{21037}{step,} \markbox{21038}{suppose} \markbox{21039}{that} \markbox{m21040}{$U$} \markbox{21041}{is} \markbox{21042}{not} \markbox{m21043}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{21044}{and} \markbox{21045}{that} \markbox{21046}{we} \markbox{21047}{have} \markbox{21048}{defined} \markbox{m21049}{$\hx_V$} \markbox{21050}{for} \markbox{21051}{all} \markbox{m21052}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{21053}{and,} \markbox{21054}{in} \markbox{21055}{particular,} \markbox{21056}{for} \markbox{21057}{all} \markbox{m21058}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m21059}{$V \in \calU$}.  \markbox{21060}{As} \markbox{21061}{before,} \markbox{21062}{if} \markbox{m21063}{$C_U$} \markbox{21064}{does} \markbox{21065}{not} \markbox{21066}{contain} \markbox{21067}{a} \markbox{21068}{marked} \markbox{21069}{or} \markbox{21070}{a} \markbox{21071}{projection} \markbox{m21072}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21073}{for} \markbox{21074}{some} \markbox{m21075}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{21076}{then} \markbox{21077}{we} \markbox{21078}{let} \markbox{m21079}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{21080}{be} \markbox{21081}{any} \markbox{21082}{point.}  \markbox{21083}{If} \markbox{m21084}{$C_U$} \markbox{21085}{happens} \markbox{21086}{to} \markbox{21087}{contain} \markbox{21088}{one} \markbox{21089}{of} \markbox{21090}{the} \markbox{21091}{endpoints} \markbox{21092}{but} \markbox{21093}{no} \markbox{m21094}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21095}{for} \markbox{m21096}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{21097}{then} \markbox{m21098}{$C_U$} \markbox{21099}{contains} \markbox{21100}{only} \markbox{21101}{that} \markbox{21102}{one} \markbox{21103}{endpoint} \markbox{21104}{(since} \markbox{m21105}{$U$} \markbox{21106}{is} \markbox{21107}{not} \markbox{m21108}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal), \markbox{21109}{and} \markbox{21110}{we} \markbox{21111}{let} \markbox{m21112}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{21113}{be} \markbox{21114}{any} point

Otherwise, \markbox{21115}{we} \markbox{21116}{set} \markbox{m21117}{$C=C_U$} \markbox{21118}{and} \markbox{21119}{let} \markbox{m21120}{$\calV_U$} \markbox{21121}{denote} \markbox{21122}{the} \markbox{21123}{set} \markbox{21124}{of} \markbox{m21125}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{21126}{domains} \markbox{m21127}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{21128}{so} \markbox{21129}{that} \markbox{m21130}{$\hd^V_U \in C$} \markbox{21131}{(or} \markbox{21132}{equivalently,} \markbox{m21133}{$(\hd^V_U)_0 = \hy_U$}).  \markbox{21134}{For} \markbox{21135}{each} \markbox{m21136}{$V \in \calV_U$}, \markbox{21137}{set} \markbox{m21138}{$C^V_U = \hull_C(\hd^V_U \cup \pi_C(\hx_V))$}, \markbox{21139}{namely} \markbox{21140}{the} \markbox{21141}{convex} \markbox{21142}{hull} \markbox{21143}{in} \markbox{m21144}{$C$} \markbox{21145}{of} \markbox{m21146}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21147}{and} \markbox{21148}{the} \markbox{21149}{projections} \markbox{21150}{of} \markbox{21151}{the} \markbox{21152}{marked} \markbox{21153}{point} \markbox{21154}{labeled} \markbox{21155}{by} \markbox{m21156}{$l_V$} \markbox{21157}{down} \markbox{21158}{to} \markbox{21159}{the} \markbox{21160}{convex} \markbox{21161}{subset} \markbox{m21162}{$C$}.  \markbox{21163}{The} \markbox{21164}{following} \markbox{21165}{claim,} \markbox{21166}{which} \markbox{21167}{is} \markbox{21168}{exactly} \cite[Claim 10.4]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{21169}{helps} \markbox{21170}{us} \markbox{21171}{choose} \markbox{21172}{a} \markbox{21173}{point} \markbox{21174}{in} \markbox{21175}{such} \markbox{21176}{a} \markbox{m21177}{$C_U$}:

\begin{claim}\label{claim:cluster overlap}
For \markbox{21178}{every} \markbox{m21179}{$V, W \in \calV_U$}, \markbox{21180}{we} \markbox{21181}{have} \markbox{m21182}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \neq \emptyset$}.  \markbox{21183}{Moreover,} \markbox{21184}{at} \markbox{21185}{least} \markbox{21186}{one} \markbox{21187}{of} \markbox{m21188}{$\hd^V_U \in C^W_U$} \markbox{21189}{or} \markbox{m21190}{$\hd^W_U \in C^V_U$} holds.


\end{claim}

\begin{proof}
We \markbox{21191}{may} \markbox{21192}{assume} \markbox{21193}{that} \markbox{m21194}{$\hd^V_U \neq \hd^W_U$}, \markbox{21195}{and} \markbox{21196}{hence} \markbox{21197}{that} \markbox{m21198}{$V \pitchfork W$}.  \markbox{21199}{If} \markbox{m21200}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U = \emptyset$}, \markbox{21201}{then} \markbox{m21202}{$\hd^V_U \notin C^W_U$} \markbox{21203}{and} \markbox{m21204}{$\hd^W_U \notin C^V_U$}, \markbox{21205}{and} \markbox{21206}{it} \markbox{21207}{follows} \markbox{21208}{that} \markbox{m21209}{$l_V \neq l_W$}.  \markbox{21210}{The} \markbox{21211}{BGI} \markbox{21212}{property} \markbox{21213}{in} \markbox{21214}{(7)} \markbox{21215}{of} \markbox{21216}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{21217}{plus} \markbox{21218}{item} \markbox{21219}{(4)} \markbox{21220}{of} \markbox{21221}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{21222}{imply} \markbox{21223}{that}  \markbox{m21224}{$\hd^W_V \notin \Delta^{-1}_V(\hy_V)$} \markbox{21225}{and} \markbox{m21226}{$\hd^V_W \notin \Delta^{-1}_W(\hy_W)$}, \markbox{21227}{and} \markbox{21228}{hence} \markbox{m21229}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^W_V)_0$} \markbox{21230}{and} \markbox{m21231}{$\hy_W \neq (\hd^V_W)_0$}, \markbox{21232}{which} \markbox{21233}{is} \markbox{21234}{a} \markbox{21235}{contradiction} \markbox{21236}{of} \markbox{m21237}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21238}{of} \markbox{m21239}{$\hy$}.  \markbox{21240}{This} \markbox{21241}{proves} \markbox{21242}{the} claim.
\end{proof}

Hence \markbox{21243}{the} \markbox{21244}{Helly} \markbox{21245}{property} \markbox{21246}{for} \markbox{21247}{trees} \markbox{21248}{implies} \markbox{21249}{that} \markbox{m21250}{$\bigcap_{V \in \calV_U} C^V_U \subset \hT_U$} \markbox{21251}{is} \markbox{21252}{nonempty.}  \markbox{21253}{This} \markbox{21254}{intersection,} \markbox{21255}{nonetheless,} \markbox{21256}{may} \markbox{21257}{contain} \markbox{21258}{many} \markbox{m21259}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21260}{for} \markbox{m21261}{$V \in \calV_U$}.  \markbox{21262}{The} \markbox{21263}{following} \markbox{21264}{claim,} \markbox{21265}{which} \markbox{21266}{is} \markbox{21267}{exactly} \cite[Claim 10.6]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{21268}{helps} \markbox{21269}{us} \markbox{21270}{make} \markbox{21271}{a} \markbox{21272}{consistent} choice:

\begin{claim}\label{claim:choose two}
Suppose \markbox{m21273}{$V, W \in \calW_U^{\nest}$}, \markbox{21274}{then} \markbox{m21275}{$\hd^V_U = \hd^W_U$}.
\end{claim}

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{21276}{of} \markbox{21277}{Claim} \ref{claim:choose two}]
For \markbox{21278}{a} \markbox{21279}{contradiction,} \markbox{21280}{suppose} \markbox{21281}{that} \markbox{m21282}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{21283}{so} \markbox{21284}{that} \markbox{m21285}{$V \pitchfork W$}.  \markbox{21286}{Then} \markbox{21287}{again} \markbox{21288}{the} \markbox{21289}{BGI} \markbox{21290}{property} \markbox{21291}{in} \markbox{21292}{item} \markbox{21293}{(7)} \markbox{21294}{of} \markbox{21295}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{21296}{implies} \markbox{21297}{that} \markbox{m21298}{$\hd^V_W = \hd^U_W(\hd^V_U)$} \markbox{21299}{and} \markbox{m21300}{$\hd^W_V = \hd^U_V(\hd^W_U)$}.  \markbox{21301}{But} \markbox{21302}{then} \markbox{m21303}{$\hy_W \neq (\hd^V_W)_0 = (\hd^U_W)_0((\hd^V_U)_0)$} \markbox{21304}{and} \markbox{m21305}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^W_V)_0 = (\hd^U_V)_0((\hd^W_U)_0)$}, \markbox{21306}{which} \markbox{21307}{contradicts} \markbox{m21308}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21309}{of} \markbox{m21310}{$\hy$}, \markbox{21311}{completing} \markbox{21312}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

Finally, \markbox{21313}{this} \markbox{21314}{last} \markbox{21315}{claim} \markbox{21316}{helps} \markbox{21317}{us} \markbox{21318}{make} \markbox{21319}{a} \markbox{21320}{consistent} \markbox{21321}{choice} \markbox{21322}{between} \markbox{m21323}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21324}{sets} \markbox{21325}{and} \markbox{21326}{marked} \markbox{21327}{points} \markbox{21328}{when} \markbox{m21329}{$C_U$} \markbox{21330}{contains} both:

\begin{claim}\label{claim:good choice}
The \markbox{21331}{following} holds:
\begin{enumerate}
\item If \markbox{21332}{there} \markbox{21333}{exists} \markbox{m21334}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21335}{so} \markbox{21336}{that} \markbox{m21337}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^U_V)'$}, \markbox{21338}{then} \markbox{21339}{for} \markbox{21340}{all} \markbox{m21341}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21342}{with} \markbox{m21343}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{21344}{we} \markbox{21345}{have} \markbox{m21346}{$\hx_W = \hd^V_W$}.
\item If \markbox{21347}{there} \markbox{21348}{exists} \markbox{m21349}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21350}{with} \markbox{m21351}{$\hy_W \neq (\hd^U_W)'(\hy_U)$}, \markbox{21352}{then} \markbox{21353}{for} \markbox{21354}{all} \markbox{m21355}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21356}{with} \markbox{m21357}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{21358}{we} \markbox{21359}{have} \markbox{m21360}{$\hy_V = (\hd^U_V)'$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item In \markbox{21361}{particular,} \markbox{21362}{if} \markbox{m21363}{$V \in \calW_U^{\pitchfork}$} \markbox{21364}{and} \markbox{m21365}{$W \in \calW_U^{\nest}$}, \markbox{21366}{then} \markbox{m21367}{$\hd^V_U = \hd^W_U$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{claim}

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{21368}{of} \markbox{21369}{Claim} \ref{claim:good choice}]
Suppose \markbox{m21370}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21371}{as} \markbox{21372}{in} \markbox{21373}{item} \markbox{21374}{(1)} \markbox{21375}{of} \markbox{21376}{the} \markbox{21377}{claim,} \markbox{21378}{and} \markbox{21379}{let} \markbox{m21380}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21381}{with} \markbox{m21382}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}.  \markbox{21383}{Then} \markbox{m21384}{$W \pitchfork V$}, \markbox{21385}{and} \markbox{21386}{since} \markbox{m21387}{$W \nest U$}, \markbox{21388}{we} \markbox{21389}{have} \markbox{m21390}{$(\hd^W_V)_0 = (\hd^U_V)_0 \neq \hy_V$}, \markbox{21391}{and} \markbox{21392}{hence} \markbox{m21393}{$\hx_W = \hd^V_W$}, \markbox{21394}{by} \markbox{21395}{definition} \markbox{21396}{of} \markbox{m21397}{$\hx_W$}.

Now \markbox{21398}{suppose} \markbox{m21399}{$W \in \calV_U$}, \markbox{21400}{as} \markbox{21401}{in} \markbox{21402}{item} \markbox{21403}{(2),} \markbox{21404}{and} \markbox{21405}{that} \markbox{m21406}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21407}{with} \markbox{m21408}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}. \markbox{21409}{Then} \markbox{m21410}{$W \pitchfork V$}.  \markbox{21411}{By} \markbox{m21412}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21413}{of} \markbox{m21414}{$\hy$}, \markbox{21415}{we} \markbox{21416}{have} \markbox{21417}{that} \markbox{m21418}{$\hy_U = (\hd^W_U)_0$}.  \markbox{21419}{But} \markbox{21420}{since} \markbox{m21421}{$\hd^V_U \neq \hd^W_U$}, \markbox{21422}{we} \markbox{21423}{have} \markbox{m21424}{$(\hd^V_U)_0 \neq (\hd^W_U)_0$}, \markbox{21425}{and} \markbox{21426}{so} \markbox{m21427}{$\hy_V = (\hd^U_V)_0 = (\hd^W_V)_0$} \markbox{21428}{since} \markbox{m21429}{$W \nest U$}.  \markbox{21430}{This} \markbox{21431}{completes} \markbox{21432}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

We \markbox{21433}{are} \markbox{21434}{finally} \markbox{21435}{ready} \markbox{21436}{to} \markbox{21437}{define} \markbox{21438}{our} \markbox{21439}{tuple} \markbox{m21440}{$\hx$}, \markbox{21441}{which} \markbox{21442}{we} \markbox{21443}{do} \markbox{21444}{domain-wise} \markbox{21445}{for} \markbox{21446}{each} \markbox{m21447}{$U \in \calU$}:

\begin{enumerate}
\item If \markbox{m21448}{$\hy_U$} \markbox{21449}{is} \markbox{21450}{not} \markbox{21451}{a} \markbox{21452}{marked} \markbox{21453}{or} \markbox{21454}{cluster} \markbox{21455}{point} \markbox{21456}{of} \markbox{m21457}{$\hT_{U,0}$}, \markbox{21458}{then} \markbox{21459}{we} \markbox{21460}{let} \markbox{m21461}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{21462}{be} \markbox{21463}{any} \markbox{21464}{point} \markbox{21465}{in} \markbox{m21466}{$\Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}.
\item For \markbox{21467}{any} \markbox{m21468}{$U$} \markbox{21469}{of} \markbox{21470}{type} \markbox{21471}{(1):} \markbox{21472}{If} \markbox{m21473}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21474}{or} \markbox{m21475}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{21476}{we} \markbox{21477}{set} \markbox{m21478}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V$}, \markbox{21479}{and} \markbox{21480}{if} \markbox{m21481}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{21482}{we} \markbox{21483}{set} \markbox{m21484}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V(\hx_U)$}.
\item If \markbox{m21485}{$U$} \markbox{21486}{is} \markbox{m21487}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{21488}{and} \markbox{m21489}{$\hy_U$} \markbox{21490}{is} \markbox{21491}{a} \markbox{21492}{marked} \markbox{21493}{point} \markbox{21494}{of} \markbox{m21495}{$\hT_{U,0}$}, \markbox{21496}{then} \markbox{21497}{there} \markbox{21498}{are} \markbox{21499}{three} \markbox{21500}{subcases:} \label{item:minimal choice}
\begin{enumerate}
\item The \markbox{21501}{set} \markbox{m21502}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork} = \{W \in \calU| W \pitchfork U \hspace{.1in}  \textrm{and } \hspace{.1in} (\hd^U_W)' \neq \hy_W\}$} \markbox{21503}{is} \markbox{21504}{nonempty,} \markbox{21505}{and} \markbox{21506}{we} \markbox{21507}{set} \markbox{m21508}{$\hx_U = \hd^W_U$} \markbox{21509}{for} \markbox{21510}{any} \markbox{21511}{(and} \markbox{21512}{hence} \markbox{21513}{all} \markbox{21514}{by} \markbox{21515}{Claim} \ref{claim:choose one}) \markbox{m21516}{$W \in \calW_U^{\pitchfork}$};
\item \markbox{m21517}{$\calW_U^{\nest} = \{V \nest U| (\hd^U_V)'(\hy_U) \neq \hy_V \hspace{.1in} \textrm{and} \hspace{.1in} (\hd^U_W)'(\hy_U) \neq \hy_W\}$} \markbox{21518}{is} \markbox{21519}{nonempty,} \markbox{21520}{and} \markbox{21521}{we} \markbox{21522}{set} \markbox{m21523}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$} \markbox{21524}{for} \markbox{21525}{any} \markbox{21526}{(and} \markbox{21527}{hence} \markbox{21528}{all} \markbox{21529}{by} \markbox{21530}{Claim} \ref{claim:choose two}) \markbox{m21531}{$V \in \calW_U^{\nest}$}; \markbox{21532}{or} 
\item \markbox{m21533}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork}$} \markbox{21534}{and} \markbox{m21535}{$\calW_U^{\nest}$} \markbox{21536}{are} \markbox{21537}{both} \markbox{21538}{empty,} \markbox{21539}{and} \markbox{21540}{we} \markbox{21541}{set} \markbox{m21542}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21543}{to} \markbox{21544}{be} \markbox{21545}{any} \markbox{21546}{point} \markbox{21547}{of} \markbox{m21548}{$\hT^e_U$} \markbox{21549}{contained} \markbox{21550}{in} \markbox{m21551}{$C_U$}, \markbox{21552}{in} \markbox{21553}{particular} \markbox{21554}{a} \markbox{21555}{point} \markbox{21556}{which} \markbox{21557}{is} \markbox{21558}{not} \markbox{21559}{a} \markbox{21560}{cluster} \markbox{21561}{or} \markbox{21562}{marked} \markbox{21563}{point.} 
\end{enumerate}
\item Proceeding \markbox{21564}{inductively,} \markbox{21565}{if} \markbox{m21566}{$U$} \markbox{21567}{is} \markbox{21568}{not} \markbox{21569}{in} \markbox{21570}{cases} \markbox{21571}{(1)--(3)} \markbox{21572}{above,} \markbox{21573}{then} \markbox{m21574}{$\bigcap_{V \in \calV_U} C^V_U \neq \emptyset$} \markbox{21575}{and} \markbox{21576}{has} \markbox{21577}{finite} \markbox{21578}{diameter.}  \markbox{21579}{There} \markbox{21580}{are} \markbox{21581}{three} \markbox{21582}{subcases:} \label{item:general choice}
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m21583}{$\hx_U = \hd^W_U$} \markbox{21584}{for} \markbox{21585}{any} \markbox{m21586}{$W \in \calW_U^{\pitchfork}$} \markbox{21587}{if} \markbox{m21588}{$ \calW_U^{\pitchfork} \neq \emptyset$}, \label{item:choose transverse}
\item \markbox{m21589}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$} \markbox{21590}{for} \markbox{21591}{any} \markbox{m21592}{$V \in \calW_U^{\nest}$} \markbox{21593}{when} \markbox{m21594}{$\calW_U^{\nest} \neq \emptyset$}, \markbox{21595}{or} \label{item:choose nested}
\item Otherwise, \markbox{21596}{both} \markbox{m21597}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork}$} \markbox{21598}{and} \markbox{m21599}{$\calW_U^{\nest}$} \markbox{21600}{are} \markbox{21601}{empty,} \markbox{21602}{and} \markbox{21603}{we} \markbox{21604}{set} \markbox{m21605}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21606}{to} \markbox{21607}{be} \markbox{21608}{any} \markbox{21609}{point} \markbox{21610}{in} \markbox{m21611}{$\hT^e_U \cap C_U$}.
\end{enumerate}

\end{enumerate}

Finally, \markbox{21612}{we} \markbox{21613}{prove} \markbox{21614}{that} \markbox{m21615}{$\hx = (\hx_U)$} \markbox{21616}{is} \markbox{m21617}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{21618}{by} \markbox{21619}{a} \markbox{21620}{case-wise} \markbox{21621}{analysis,} \markbox{21622}{similar} \markbox{21623}{to} \markbox{21624}{the} \markbox{21625}{proof} \markbox{21626}{of} \markbox{21627}{Proposition} \ref{prop:Q-consistent}.  \markbox{21628}{Showing} \markbox{21629}{this} \markbox{21630}{will} \markbox{21631}{complete} \markbox{21632}{the} \markbox{21633}{proof} \markbox{21634}{of} \markbox{21635}{surjectivity} \markbox{21636}{of} \markbox{m21637}{$\Delta: \calQ \to \calQ'$}.  \markbox{21638}{The} \markbox{21639}{proof} \markbox{21640}{closely} \markbox{21641}{follows} \markbox{21642}{the} \markbox{21643}{analogous} \markbox{21644}{part} \markbox{21645}{of} \markbox{21646}{the} \markbox{21647}{proof} \markbox{21648}{from} \cite[Theorem 10.2]{Dur_infcube}.

\vspace{.1in}

\underline{$U \pitchfork V$:} \markbox{21649}{We} \markbox{21650}{may} \markbox{21651}{assume} \markbox{21652}{that} \markbox{m21653}{$\hx_V \neq \hd^U_V$}, \markbox{21654}{for} \markbox{21655}{we} \markbox{21656}{are} \markbox{21657}{done} \markbox{21658}{otherwise.}  \markbox{21659}{Then} \markbox{m21660}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^U_V)_0$}, \markbox{21661}{and} \markbox{21662}{so} \markbox{m21663}{$\hy_U = (\hd^V_U)_0$} \markbox{21664}{by} \markbox{m21665}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21666}{of} \markbox{m21667}{$\hy$}.  \markbox{21668}{It} \markbox{21669}{follows} \markbox{21670}{that} \markbox{m21671}{$\hd^V_U \in C_U = \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}, \markbox{21672}{and} \markbox{21673}{necessarily} \markbox{m21674}{$\hd^V_U  \in \{\ha_V, \hb_V\}$}, \markbox{21675}{so} \markbox{21676}{we} \markbox{21677}{may} \markbox{21678}{assume} \markbox{21679}{without} \markbox{21680}{loss} \markbox{21681}{of} \markbox{21682}{generality} \markbox{21683}{that} \markbox{m21684}{$\hd^V_U = \ha_V$}.  \markbox{21685}{If} \markbox{m21686}{$U$} \markbox{21687}{is} \markbox{m21688}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal, \markbox{21689}{then} \markbox{21690}{our} \markbox{21691}{choice} \markbox{21692}{of} \markbox{m21693}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21694}{in} \eqref{item:minimal choice} \markbox{21695}{says} \markbox{21696}{that} \markbox{m21697}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{21698}{as} required.

Now \markbox{21699}{suppose} \markbox{21700}{that} \markbox{m21701}{$U$} \markbox{21702}{is} \markbox{21703}{not} \markbox{m21704}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.  \markbox{21705}{Set} \markbox{m21706}{$\calV_U$} \markbox{21707}{to} \markbox{21708}{be} \markbox{21709}{the} \markbox{21710}{set} \markbox{21711}{of} \markbox{m21712}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m21713}{$W \nest U$} \markbox{21714}{with} \markbox{m21715}{$\hd^W_U \in C_U$}.  \markbox{21716}{Let} \markbox{m21717}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21718}{be} \markbox{21719}{so} \markbox{21720}{that} \markbox{m21721}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}.  \markbox{21722}{Then} \markbox{m21723}{$W \pitchfork V$} \markbox{21724}{and} \markbox{m21725}{$(\hd^W_V)_0 = (\hd^U_V)_0 \neq \hy_V$}, \markbox{21726}{and} \markbox{21727}{so} \markbox{m21728}{$\hx_W = \hd^V_W = \ha_W$}, \markbox{21729}{with} \markbox{21730}{the} \markbox{21731}{first} \markbox{21732}{equality} \markbox{21733}{following} \markbox{21734}{from} \markbox{21735}{our} \markbox{21736}{choice} \markbox{21737}{in} \eqref{item:minimal choice} \markbox{21738}{and} \markbox{21739}{the} \markbox{21740}{last} \markbox{21741}{equality} \markbox{21742}{by} \markbox{m21743}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21744}{of} \markbox{m21745}{$a$}.  \markbox{21746}{But} \markbox{21747}{this} \markbox{21748}{says} \markbox{21749}{that} \markbox{m21750}{$a = l_W$}, \markbox{21751}{and} \markbox{21752}{hence} \markbox{m21753}{$\ha_U \in C^W_U$} \markbox{21754}{for} \markbox{21755}{all} \markbox{m21756}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21757}{(including} \markbox{21758}{those} \markbox{21759}{for} \markbox{21760}{which} \markbox{m21761}{$\hd^W_U = \hd^V_U = \ha_U$}).

It \markbox{21762}{follows} \markbox{21763}{then} \markbox{21764}{that} \markbox{m21765}{$\ha_U \in \bigcap_{W \in \calV_U}C^W_U$} \markbox{21766}{and} \markbox{21767}{so} \markbox{m21768}{$\hx_U = \ha_U$} \markbox{21769}{by} \markbox{21770}{definition} \markbox{21771}{of} \markbox{m21772}{$\hx$} \markbox{21773}{in} \markbox{21774}{item} \eqref{item:choose transverse} above.

\vspace{.1in}

\underline{$V \nest U$:} \markbox{21775}{We} \markbox{21776}{may} \markbox{21777}{assume} \markbox{21778}{that} \markbox{m21779}{$\hx_V \neq \hd^U_V(\hx_U)$}, \markbox{21780}{for} \markbox{21781}{we} \markbox{21782}{are} \markbox{21783}{done} \markbox{21784}{otherwise.}  \markbox{21785}{Then} \markbox{m21786}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^U_V)_0(\hy_U)$}, \markbox{21787}{and} \markbox{m21788}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21789}{of} \markbox{m21790}{$\hy$} \markbox{21791}{implies} \markbox{21792}{that} \markbox{m21793}{$\hy_U = (\hd^V_U)'$}, \markbox{21794}{and} \markbox{21795}{thus} \markbox{m21796}{$\hd^V_U \in C_U = \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}.  \markbox{21797}{We} \markbox{21798}{claim} \markbox{21799}{that} \markbox{21800}{for} \markbox{21801}{all} \markbox{m21802}{$W \in \calV_U$}, \markbox{21803}{we} \markbox{21804}{have} \markbox{m21805}{$\hd^V_U \in C^W_U$}.

To \markbox{21806}{see} \markbox{21807}{this,} \markbox{21808}{is} \markbox{21809}{suffices} \markbox{21810}{to} \markbox{21811}{consider} \markbox{m21812}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21813}{with} \markbox{m21814}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}.  \markbox{21815}{Then} \markbox{m21816}{$W \pitchfork V$}.  \markbox{21817}{But} \markbox{m21818}{$\hx_V \neq \hd^U_V(\hx_U)$}, \markbox{21819}{so} \markbox{21820}{if} \markbox{21821}{also} \markbox{m21822}{$\hd^V_U \notin C^W_U$}, \markbox{21823}{then} \markbox{m21824}{$\hx_V \neq \hd^U_V(\hd^W_U) = \hd^W_V$}, \markbox{21825}{while} \markbox{21826}{also} \markbox{m21827}{$\hx_W \neq \hd^U_W(\hd^V_U) = \hd^V_W$}, \markbox{21828}{which} \markbox{21829}{both} \markbox{21830}{use} \markbox{21831}{the} \markbox{21832}{BGI} \markbox{21833}{property} \markbox{21834}{in} \markbox{21835}{item} \markbox{21836}{(7)} \markbox{21837}{of} \markbox{21838}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.  \markbox{21839}{But} \markbox{21840}{then} \markbox{m21841}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^W_V)_0$} \markbox{21842}{and} \markbox{m21843}{$\hy_W \neq (\hd^V_W)_0$}, \markbox{21844}{which} \markbox{21845}{contradicts} \markbox{m21846}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21847}{of} \markbox{m21848}{$\hy$}.

Hence \markbox{m21849}{$\hd^V_U \in C^W_U$} \markbox{21850}{for} \markbox{21851}{all} \markbox{m21852}{$W \in \calV_U$}.  \markbox{21853}{It} \markbox{21854}{follows} \markbox{21855}{that} \markbox{m21856}{$\hd^V_U \in \bigcap_{W \in \calV_U} C^W_U$}, \markbox{21857}{and} \markbox{21858}{then} \eqref{item:choose nested} \markbox{21859}{says} \markbox{21860}{that} \markbox{m21861}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$}.



\vspace{.1in}

Hence \markbox{m21862}{$(\hx)$} \markbox{21863}{is} \markbox{m21864}{$0$}-consistent.  \markbox{21865}{Since} \markbox{m21866}{$\Delta(\hx) = \hy$} \markbox{21867}{because} \markbox{m21868}{$\hx_U \in \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$} \markbox{21869}{for} \markbox{21870}{all} \markbox{m21871}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{21872}{we} \markbox{21873}{are} \markbox{21874}{done} \markbox{21875}{with} \markbox{21876}{the} \markbox{21877}{proof} \markbox{21878}{of} \markbox{21879}{surjectivity} \markbox{21880}{of} \markbox{m21881}{$\Delta: \calQ \to \calQ'$}, \markbox{21882}{and} \markbox{21883}{this} \markbox{21884}{also} \markbox{21885}{defines} \markbox{21886}{the} \markbox{21887}{map} \markbox{m21888}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{21889}{by} \markbox{m21890}{$\Xi(\hy) = \hx$}, \markbox{21891}{as} \markbox{21892}{defined} \markbox{21893}{above.}  \markbox{21894}{This} \markbox{21895}{completes} \markbox{21896}{the} \markbox{21897}{proof} \markbox{21898}{of} \markbox{21899}{item} (2).

\medskip

\textbf{\underline{Item (3): $\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$ is a quasi-isometry:}} \markbox{21900}{The} \markbox{21901}{proof} \markbox{21902}{of} \markbox{21903}{this} \markbox{21904}{part} \markbox{21905}{proceeds} \markbox{21906}{similarly} \markbox{21907}{to} \markbox{21908}{its} \markbox{21909}{analogue} \markbox{21910}{in} \cite[Theorem 10.2]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{21911}{though} \markbox{21912}{with} \markbox{21913}{some} \markbox{21914}{modest} \markbox{21915}{simplifications} \markbox{21916}{(see} \markbox{21917}{especially} \cite[Subsection 9.1]{Dur_infcube}).

Since \markbox{m21918}{$\Delta|_{\calQ}$} \markbox{21919}{is} \markbox{21920}{surjective} \markbox{21921}{and} \markbox{21922}{distance} \markbox{21923}{non-increasing,} \markbox{21924}{it} \markbox{21925}{suffices} \markbox{21926}{to} \markbox{21927}{prove} \markbox{21928}{that} \markbox{m21929}{$d_{\calQ} \prec d_{\calQ'}$}, \markbox{21930}{and} \markbox{21931}{for} \markbox{21932}{this} \markbox{21933}{it} \markbox{21934}{suffices} \markbox{21935}{to} \markbox{21936}{bound} \markbox{21937}{the} \markbox{21938}{distances} \markbox{21939}{in} \markbox{21940}{each} \markbox{m21941}{$U \in \calU$}.

Let \markbox{m21942}{$\hx, \hy \in \calQ$} \markbox{21943}{with} \markbox{m21944}{$\hx' = \Delta(\hx)$} \markbox{21945}{and} \markbox{m21946}{$\hy' = \Delta(\hy)$}.  \markbox{21947}{We} \markbox{21948}{may} \markbox{21949}{assume} \markbox{21950}{that} \markbox{m21951}{$\hx_U \neq \hy_U$} \markbox{21952}{for} \markbox{21953}{any} \markbox{m21954}{$U\in \calU$} \markbox{21955}{that} \markbox{21956}{we} \markbox{21957}{will} \markbox{21958}{consider.}  \markbox{21959}{We} \markbox{21960}{begin} \markbox{21961}{by} \markbox{21962}{making} \markbox{21963}{a} \markbox{21964}{useful} reduction.

Observe \markbox{21965}{that} \markbox{21966}{item} \markbox{21967}{(9)} \markbox{21968}{of} \markbox{21969}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{21970}{implies} \markbox{21971}{that} \markbox{21972}{there} \markbox{21973}{are} \markbox{21974}{at} \markbox{21975}{most} \markbox{21976}{boundedly-many} \markbox{21977}{domains} \markbox{m21978}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{21979}{for} \markbox{21980}{which} \markbox{m21981}{$\hx_U,\hy_U$} \markbox{21982}{are} \markbox{21983}{in} \markbox{21984}{the} \markbox{21985}{same} \markbox{21986}{component} \markbox{21987}{of} \markbox{m21988}{$\hT^e_U$}, \markbox{21989}{where} \markbox{21990}{the} \markbox{21991}{bound} \markbox{21992}{is} \markbox{21993}{controlled} \markbox{21994}{by} \markbox{m21995}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{21996}{For} \markbox{21997}{such} \markbox{m21998}{$U$}, \markbox{21999}{we} \markbox{22000}{have} \markbox{m22001}{$d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U, \hy_U) \leq d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U, \hy'_U) + B^2$} \markbox{22002}{because} \markbox{22003}{at} \markbox{22004}{most} \markbox{m22005}{$B$}-many \markbox{22006}{subtrees} \markbox{22007}{of} \markbox{22008}{diameter} \markbox{m22009}{$B$} \markbox{22010}{have} \markbox{22011}{been} \markbox{22012}{deleted} \markbox{22013}{from} \markbox{22014}{that} \markbox{22015}{edge.}  \markbox{22016}{Hence} \markbox{22017}{we} \markbox{22018}{may} \markbox{22019}{deal} \markbox{22020}{with} \markbox{22021}{these} \markbox{22022}{boundedly-many} \markbox{22023}{domains} \markbox{22024}{with} \markbox{22025}{an} \markbox{22026}{additive} \markbox{22027}{constant} \markbox{22028}{in} \markbox{22029}{the} \markbox{22030}{distance} \markbox{22031}{estimate} \markbox{22032}{comparing} \markbox{m22033}{$d_{\calQ}(\hx,\hy)$} \markbox{22034}{and} \markbox{m22035}{$d_{\calQ'}(\hx',\hy')$}. \markbox{22036}{Hereafter,} \markbox{22037}{we} \markbox{22038}{assume} \markbox{22039}{that} \markbox{22040}{at} \markbox{22041}{least} \markbox{22042}{one} \markbox{22043}{of} \markbox{m22044}{$\hx_U, \hy_U$} \markbox{22045}{coincides} \markbox{22046}{with} \markbox{22047}{a} \markbox{22048}{cluster,} \markbox{22049}{or} \markbox{22050}{they} \markbox{22051}{are} \markbox{22052}{separated} \markbox{22053}{by} \markbox{22054}{at} \markbox{22055}{least} \markbox{22056}{one} cluster.



\smallskip

There \markbox{22057}{are} \markbox{22058}{two} \markbox{22059}{cases,} \markbox{22060}{(1)} \markbox{m22061}{$U$} \markbox{22062}{is} \markbox{m22063}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{22064}{and} \markbox{22065}{(2)} otherwise.

\smallskip

\underline{Case (1)}: \markbox{22066}{Then} \markbox{m22067}{$\hT^e_U$} \markbox{22068}{has} \markbox{22069}{one} \markbox{22070}{component.}  \markbox{22071}{So} \markbox{22072}{there} \markbox{22073}{are} \markbox{22074}{at} \markbox{22075}{most} \markbox{m22076}{$B$}-many \markbox{22077}{subtrees} \markbox{22078}{of} \markbox{22079}{diameter} \markbox{22080}{at} \markbox{22081}{most} \markbox{m22082}{$B$} \markbox{22083}{in} \markbox{m22084}{$\hT^e_U$} \markbox{22085}{being} \markbox{22086}{collapsed.}  \markbox{22087}{By} \markbox{22088}{item} \markbox{22089}{(9)} \markbox{22090}{of} \markbox{22091}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{22092}{there} \markbox{22093}{are} \markbox{22094}{at} \markbox{22095}{most} \markbox{22096}{boundedly-many} \markbox{22097}{(in} \markbox{m22098}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{22099}{such} \markbox{m22100}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m22101}{$U$} \markbox{22102}{for} \markbox{22103}{which} \markbox{22104}{one} \markbox{22105}{of} \markbox{m22106}{$\hx_U, \hy_U$} \markbox{22107}{is} \markbox{22108}{not} \markbox{22109}{a} \markbox{22110}{cluster} \markbox{22111}{point.}  \markbox{22112}{We} \markbox{22113}{may} \markbox{22114}{deal} \markbox{22115}{with} \markbox{22116}{such} \markbox{m22117}{$U$} \markbox{22118}{by} \markbox{22119}{increasing} \markbox{22120}{the} \markbox{22121}{additive} \markbox{22122}{constant} \markbox{22123}{in} \markbox{22124}{the} \markbox{22125}{distance} estimate.

The \markbox{22126}{general} \markbox{22127}{case} \markbox{22128}{is} \markbox{22129}{where} \markbox{m22130}{$\hx_U, \hy_U$} \markbox{22131}{are} \markbox{22132}{the} \markbox{22133}{distinct} \markbox{22134}{endpoint} \markbox{22135}{clusters} \markbox{22136}{of} \markbox{22137}{the} \markbox{22138}{interval} \markbox{m22139}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{22140}{In} \markbox{22141}{this} \markbox{22142}{case,} 
$$d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U,\hy'_U)  \geq d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) - B^2 \geq K - B^2 - 2r_1,$$ \markbox{22143}{by} \markbox{22144}{item} \markbox{22145}{(6)} \markbox{22146}{of} \markbox{22147}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.   \markbox{22148}{Hence} \markbox{22149}{by} \markbox{22150}{choosing} \markbox{m22151}{$K = K(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{22152}{sufficiently} \markbox{22153}{large} \markbox{22154}{and} \markbox{22155}{requiring} \markbox{22156}{that} \markbox{m22157}{$B^2_{tt}-2r_1<K$}, \markbox{22158}{we} \markbox{22159}{can} \markbox{22160}{guarantee} \markbox{22161}{that} \markbox{m22162}{$d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U,\hy'_U) >1$} \markbox{22163}{allowing} \markbox{22164}{the} estimate
$$d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) \leq d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U,\hy'_U) + B^2 \leq (1+B^2)d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U,\hy'_U).$$
Thus \markbox{22165}{we} \markbox{22166}{can} \markbox{22167}{account} \markbox{22168}{for} \markbox{22169}{these} \markbox{22170}{domains} \markbox{22171}{via} \markbox{22172}{a} \markbox{22173}{bounded} \markbox{22174}{multiplicative} error.


\smallskip
\underline{Case (2)}:  \markbox{22175}{Suppose} \markbox{22176}{that} \markbox{m22177}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{22178}{is} \markbox{22179}{not} \markbox{m22180}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.  \markbox{22181}{Since} \markbox{m22182}{$\hx_U \neq \hy_U$}, \markbox{22183}{there} \markbox{22184}{is} \markbox{22185}{some} \markbox{22186}{collection} \markbox{22187}{of} \markbox{22188}{edge} \markbox{22189}{components} \markbox{m22190}{$E_1, \dots, E_k\subset \hT^e_U$} \markbox{22191}{separating} \markbox{m22192}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{22193}{from} \markbox{m22194}{$\hy_U$}, \markbox{22195}{i.e.} \markbox{22196}{intersecting} \markbox{m22197}{$[\hx_U, \hy_U]_{\hT_U}$}.  \markbox{22198}{By} \markbox{22199}{assumption,} \markbox{22200}{each} \markbox{22201}{such} \markbox{22202}{component} \markbox{22203}{contains} \markbox{22204}{at} \markbox{22205}{most} \markbox{m22206}{$B$}-many \markbox{22207}{subintervals} \markbox{22208}{in} \markbox{m22209}{$\calB$} \markbox{22210}{of} \markbox{22211}{diameter} \markbox{22212}{at} \markbox{22213}{most} \markbox{m22214}{$B$} \markbox{22215}{which} \markbox{22216}{are} \markbox{22217}{collapsed} \markbox{22218}{by} \markbox{m22219}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U \to \hT'_U$}.  \markbox{22220}{Moreover,} \markbox{22221}{adjacent} \markbox{22222}{intervals} \markbox{m22223}{$E_i, E_{i+1}$} \markbox{22224}{are} \markbox{22225}{attached} \markbox{22226}{at} \markbox{22227}{some} \markbox{22228}{collapsed} \markbox{22229}{cluster} \markbox{m22230}{$C_i$}.  \markbox{22231}{For} \markbox{22232}{each} \markbox{22233}{such} \markbox{22234}{collapsed} \markbox{22235}{cluster} \markbox{m22236}{$C_i$}, \markbox{22237}{choose} \markbox{22238}{a} \markbox{m22239}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{22240}{domain} \markbox{m22241}{$V_i \nest U$} \markbox{22242}{with} \markbox{m22243}{$\hd^{V_i}_U \in C_i$}.  \markbox{22244}{Observe} that
\begin{eqnarray*}
d_{\hT_U}(C_i,C_{i+1}) &\leq& d_{\hT'_U}(\Delta_U(C_i), \Delta_U(C_{i+1})) + B^2\\
&\leq& d_{\hT'_U}(\Delta_U(C_i), \Delta_U(C_{i+1})) + B^2d_{\hT'_{V_i}}(\hx'_{V_i}, \hy'_{V_i}).
\end{eqnarray*}

Hence \markbox{22245}{we} \markbox{22246}{can} \markbox{22247}{account} \markbox{22248}{for} \markbox{22249}{the} \markbox{22250}{lost} \markbox{22251}{distance} \markbox{22252}{along} \markbox{m22253}{$[\hx_U, \hy_U]$} \markbox{22254}{between} \markbox{22255}{each} \markbox{22256}{pair} \markbox{22257}{of} \markbox{22258}{successive} \markbox{22259}{collapsed} \markbox{22260}{cluster} \markbox{22261}{points} \markbox{m22262}{$C_i, C_{i+1}$} \markbox{22263}{(i.e.,} \markbox{22264}{the} \markbox{22265}{distance} \markbox{22266}{lost} \markbox{22267}{in} \markbox{22268}{the} \markbox{22269}{edge} \markbox{m22270}{$E_i$}) \markbox{22271}{by} \markbox{22272}{distances} \markbox{22273}{in} \markbox{22274}{the} \markbox{m22275}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{22276}{domains} \markbox{m22277}{$V_i$}.  \markbox{22278}{Similarly,} \markbox{22279}{we} \markbox{22280}{can} \markbox{22281}{use} \markbox{m22282}{$V_1, V_k$} \markbox{22283}{to} \markbox{22284}{account} \markbox{22285}{for} \markbox{22286}{any} \markbox{22287}{lost} \markbox{22288}{distance} \markbox{22289}{between} \markbox{m22290}{$\hx_U, C_1$} \markbox{22291}{and} \markbox{m22292}{$C_n, \hy_U$}, \markbox{22293}{respectively.}  \markbox{22294}{Since} \markbox{22295}{each} \markbox{22296}{domain} \markbox{22297}{in} \markbox{m22298}{$\calU$} \markbox{22299}{nests} \markbox{22300}{into} \markbox{22301}{at} \markbox{22302}{most} \markbox{22303}{boundedly-many} \markbox{22304}{domains} \markbox{22305}{in} \markbox{m22306}{$\calU$} \markbox{22307}{by} \markbox{22308}{the} \markbox{22309}{Covering} \markbox{22310}{Lemma} \ref{lem:covering}, \markbox{22311}{the} \markbox{22312}{proof} \markbox{22313}{of} \markbox{22314}{case} \markbox{22315}{(2)} \markbox{22316}{is} \markbox{22317}{complete.}  \markbox{22318}{This} \markbox{22319}{completes} \markbox{22320}{the} \markbox{22321}{proof} \markbox{22322}{of} \markbox{22323}{the} theorem.
\end{proof}




\section{Proof of the Stable Intervals Theorem \ref{thm:stable intervals}} \label{app:SI}

We \markbox{22324}{will} \markbox{22325}{give} \markbox{22326}{a} \markbox{22327}{fairly} \markbox{22328}{complete} \markbox{22329}{accounting} \markbox{22330}{of} \markbox{22331}{the} \markbox{22332}{two} \markbox{22333}{main} \markbox{22334}{arguments} \markbox{22335}{involved} \markbox{22336}{in} \markbox{22337}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.  \markbox{22338}{See} \markbox{22339}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:detailed sketch} \markbox{22340}{for} \markbox{22341}{a} \markbox{22342}{detailed} \markbox{22343}{sketch} \markbox{22344}{and} \markbox{22345}{outline.}  \markbox{22346}{The} \markbox{22347}{two} \markbox{22348}{key} \markbox{22349}{arguments} \markbox{22350}{involve} \markbox{22351}{showing} \markbox{22352}{that} \markbox{22353}{we} \markbox{22354}{can} \markbox{22355}{stably} \markbox{22356}{add} \markbox{22357}{one} \markbox{22358}{cluster} \markbox{22359}{point} \markbox{22360}{and} \markbox{22361}{then} \markbox{22362}{that} \markbox{22363}{we} \markbox{22364}{can} \markbox{22365}{iterate} \markbox{22366}{this} process.

\subsection{Adding a cluster point}

In \markbox{22367}{this} \markbox{22368}{subsection,} \markbox{22369}{we} \markbox{22370}{explain} \markbox{22371}{how} \markbox{22372}{to} \markbox{22373}{build} \markbox{22374}{a} \markbox{22375}{stable} \markbox{22376}{decomposition} \markbox{22377}{when} \markbox{22378}{adding} \markbox{22379}{a} \markbox{22380}{cluster} \markbox{22381}{point} \markbox{22382}{to} \markbox{22383}{the} \markbox{22384}{setup.}  \markbox{22385}{This} \markbox{22386}{is} \markbox{22387}{the} \markbox{22388}{main} \markbox{22389}{bit} \markbox{22390}{of} \markbox{22391}{work} \markbox{22392}{for} \markbox{22393}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.

\begin{proposition} \label{prop:add cluster}
Let \markbox{m22394}{$\calZ$} \markbox{22395}{be} \markbox{22396}{a} \markbox{22397}{geodesic} \markbox{m22398}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{22399}{space,} \markbox{m22400}{$\epsilon>0$}, \markbox{22401}{and} \markbox{m22402}{$r_1,r_2>0$} \markbox{22403}{be} \markbox{22404}{positive} \markbox{22405}{integers.}  \markbox{22406}{Let} \markbox{m22407}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22408}{be} \markbox{22409}{an} \markbox{m22410}{$\epsilon$}-setup \markbox{22411}{and} \markbox{22412}{further} \markbox{22413}{fix} \markbox{22414}{a} \markbox{22415}{point} \markbox{m22416}{$z \in \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b))$}.  Then
\begin{enumerate}
\item \markbox{m22417}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$} \markbox{22418}{is} \markbox{22419}{an} \markbox{m22420}{$\epsilon$}-setup;
\item The \markbox{22421}{two} \markbox{22422}{setups} \markbox{m22423}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22424}{and} \markbox{m22425}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$} \markbox{22426}{are} \markbox{m22427}{$(1,\epsilon)$}-admissible;
\item There \markbox{22428}{exists} \markbox{m22429}{$L_1=L_1(\delta, \epsilon)>0$} \markbox{22430}{so} \markbox{22431}{that} \markbox{22432}{the} \markbox{22433}{stable} \markbox{22434}{intervals} \markbox{m22435}{$T$} \markbox{22436}{and} \markbox{m22437}{$T'$} \markbox{22438}{for} \markbox{22439}{the} \markbox{22440}{setups} \markbox{m22441}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22442}{and} \markbox{m22443}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$} \markbox{22444}{admit} \markbox{m22445}{$\calY$}-stable \markbox{m22446}{$L_1$}-compatible decompositions;
\item There \markbox{22447}{exists} \markbox{m22448}{$L_2 = L_2(\delta, \epsilon, r_1,r_2)>0$} \markbox{22449}{so} \markbox{22450}{that} \markbox{22451}{the} \markbox{m22452}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{22453}{of} \markbox{m22454}{$T,T'$} \markbox{22455}{admit} \markbox{m22456}{$\calY$}-stable \markbox{m22457}{$L_2$}-compatible decompositions.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Since \markbox{22458}{the} \markbox{22459}{points} \markbox{m22460}{$a,b$} \markbox{22461}{have} \markbox{22462}{not} \markbox{22463}{changed,} \markbox{22464}{the} \markbox{22465}{first} \markbox{22466}{two} \markbox{22467}{conclusions} \markbox{22468}{are} \markbox{22469}{automatic} \markbox{22470}{from} \markbox{22471}{the} assumptions.

Choosing \markbox{m22472}{$E \gg \epsilon$}, \markbox{22473}{Proposition} \ref{prop:cluster sep graph} \markbox{22474}{implies} \markbox{22475}{that} \markbox{22476}{both} \markbox{m22477}{$\calG = \calG_E(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22478}{and} \markbox{m22479}{$\calG' = \calG_E(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$} \markbox{22480}{are} \markbox{22481}{intervals.}  \markbox{22482}{There} \markbox{22483}{are} \markbox{22484}{two} \markbox{22485}{main} \markbox{22486}{cases:} \markbox{22487}{(a)} \markbox{m22488}{$d(z,C)>E$} \markbox{22489}{for} \markbox{22490}{all} \markbox{22491}{clusters} \markbox{m22492}{$C$}, \markbox{22493}{or} \markbox{22494}{(b)} otherwise.

We \markbox{22495}{will} \markbox{22496}{deal} \markbox{22497}{with} \markbox{22498}{these} \markbox{22499}{cases} \markbox{22500}{separately,} \markbox{22501}{though} \markbox{22502}{the} \markbox{22503}{arguments} \markbox{22504}{are} \markbox{22505}{similar.}  \markbox{22506}{Moreover,} \markbox{22507}{for} \markbox{22508}{each} \markbox{22509}{case,} \markbox{22510}{we} \markbox{22511}{will} \markbox{22512}{want} \markbox{22513}{to} \markbox{22514}{deal} \markbox{22515}{both} \markbox{22516}{with} \markbox{22517}{the} \markbox{22518}{original} \markbox{22519}{decompositions} \markbox{22520}{of} \markbox{22521}{the} \markbox{22522}{stable} \markbox{22523}{tree} \markbox{m22524}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$}, \markbox{22525}{as} \markbox{22526}{well} \markbox{22527}{as} \markbox{22528}{its} \markbox{m22529}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{m22530}{$T = \bT_{e} \cup \bT_{c}$}.  \markbox{22531}{The} \markbox{22532}{compatible} \markbox{22533}{decompositions} \markbox{22534}{for} \markbox{22535}{the} \markbox{22536}{latter} \markbox{22537}{will} \markbox{22538}{be} \markbox{22539}{refined} \markbox{22540}{for} \markbox{22541}{the} \markbox{22542}{decomposition} \markbox{22543}{for} \markbox{22544}{the} \markbox{22545}{former,} \markbox{22546}{with} \markbox{22547}{possibly} \markbox{22548}{a} \markbox{22549}{slight} \markbox{22550}{increase} \markbox{22551}{in} \markbox{22552}{the} \markbox{22553}{error} \markbox{22554}{depending} \markbox{22555}{on} \markbox{m22556}{$r_1,r_2$}.

\medskip

\underline{\textbf{Case (a), $z$ forms a split cluster}}: \markbox{22557}{In} \markbox{22558}{this} \markbox{22559}{case,} \markbox{m22560}{$z$} \markbox{22561}{forms} \markbox{22562}{its} \markbox{22563}{own} \markbox{22564}{cluster} \markbox{22565}{and,} \markbox{22566}{in} \markbox{22567}{particular,} \markbox{22568}{does} \markbox{22569}{not} \markbox{22570}{affect} \markbox{22571}{membership} \markbox{22572}{of} \markbox{22573}{any} \markbox{22574}{other} \markbox{22575}{cluster.}  \markbox{22576}{Moreover,} \markbox{22577}{it} \markbox{22578}{cannot} \markbox{22579}{be} \markbox{22580}{an} \markbox{22581}{endpoint} \markbox{22582}{cluster} \markbox{22583}{of} \markbox{m22584}{$\calG'$}, \markbox{22585}{as} \markbox{22586}{those} \markbox{22587}{necessarily} \markbox{22588}{contain} \markbox{m22589}{$a$} \markbox{22590}{and} \markbox{m22591}{$b$}.  \markbox{22592}{Hence} \markbox{22593}{there} \markbox{22594}{exist} \markbox{22595}{two} \markbox{22596}{clusters} \markbox{m22597}{$C_1,C_2$} \markbox{22598}{which} \markbox{22599}{are} \markbox{22600}{adjacent} \markbox{22601}{in} \markbox{m22602}{$\calG$} \markbox{22603}{but} \markbox{22604}{are} \markbox{22605}{separated} \markbox{22606}{by} \markbox{m22607}{$z$} \markbox{22608}{in} \markbox{m22609}{$\calG'$}, \markbox{22610}{say} \markbox{22611}{with} \markbox{m22612}{$C_1$} \markbox{22613}{on} \markbox{22614}{the} \markbox{22615}{side} \markbox{22616}{of} \markbox{m22617}{$a$} \markbox{22618}{and} \markbox{m22619}{$C_2$} \markbox{22620}{on} \markbox{22621}{the} \markbox{22622}{side} \markbox{22623}{of} \markbox{m22624}{$b$}.  \markbox{22625}{In} \markbox{22626}{this} \markbox{22627}{sense,} \markbox{22628}{we} \markbox{22629}{think} \markbox{22630}{of} \markbox{m22631}{$z$} \markbox{22632}{as} \markbox{22633}{splitting} \markbox{22634}{the} \markbox{22635}{clusters} \markbox{m22636}{$C_1,C_2$}.

Lemma \ref{lem:cluster arrangement} \markbox{22637}{implies} \markbox{22638}{that} \markbox{m22639}{$z$} \markbox{22640}{separates} \markbox{22641}{two} \markbox{22642}{clusters} \markbox{m22643}{$C,C'$} \markbox{22644}{for} \markbox{m22645}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22646}{if} \markbox{22647}{and} \markbox{22648}{only} \markbox{22649}{if} \markbox{m22650}{$s(z)$} \markbox{22651}{separates} \markbox{m22652}{$s(C), s(C')$} \markbox{22653}{along} \markbox{m22654}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{22655}{It} \markbox{22656}{follows} \markbox{22657}{then} \markbox{22658}{that} \markbox{22659}{the} \markbox{22660}{subgraph} \markbox{22661}{of} \markbox{m22662}{$\calG$} \markbox{22663}{connecting} \markbox{22664}{the} \markbox{22665}{cluster} \markbox{22666}{containing} \markbox{m22667}{$a$} \markbox{22668}{to} \markbox{m22669}{$C_1$} \markbox{22670}{is} \markbox{22671}{identical} \markbox{22672}{to} \markbox{22673}{the} \markbox{22674}{subgraph} \markbox{22675}{of} \markbox{m22676}{$\calG_E(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$}, \markbox{22677}{and} \markbox{22678}{similarly} \markbox{22679}{for} \markbox{22680}{the} \markbox{22681}{subgraphs} \markbox{22682}{connecting} \markbox{m22683}{$C_2$} \markbox{22684}{to} \markbox{22685}{the} \markbox{22686}{cluster} \markbox{22687}{containing} \markbox{m22688}{$b$}.  \markbox{22689}{This} \markbox{22690}{says} \markbox{22691}{that} \markbox{22692}{for} \markbox{22693}{any} \markbox{22694}{pair} \markbox{m22695}{$C,C'$} \markbox{22696}{on} \markbox{22697}{the} \markbox{m22698}{$a$}-side \markbox{22699}{of} \markbox{m22700}{$z$} \markbox{22701}{in} \markbox{m22702}{$\calG'$}, \markbox{m22703}{$\lambda_0(C,C')$} \markbox{22704}{is} \markbox{22705}{an} \markbox{22706}{edge} \markbox{22707}{component} \markbox{22708}{of} \markbox{22709}{both} \markbox{m22710}{$T$} \markbox{22711}{and} \markbox{m22712}{$T'$}, \markbox{22713}{and} \markbox{22714}{similarly} \markbox{22715}{for} \markbox{22716}{such} \markbox{22717}{pairs}  \markbox{22718}{on} \markbox{22719}{the} \markbox{m22720}{$b$}-side \markbox{22721}{of} \markbox{m22722}{$z$}.  \markbox{22723}{Thus} \markbox{22724}{we} \markbox{22725}{can} \markbox{22726}{include} \markbox{22727}{each} \markbox{22728}{such} \markbox{22729}{component} \markbox{22730}{of} \markbox{m22731}{$E \subset T_e$} \markbox{22732}{and} \markbox{m22733}{$E \subset T'_e$} \markbox{22734}{in} \markbox{22735}{the} \markbox{22736}{respective} \markbox{22737}{stable} \markbox{22738}{decomposition} \markbox{m22739}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{22740}{and} \markbox{m22741}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$}, \markbox{22742}{where} \markbox{22743}{the} \markbox{22744}{identity} \markbox{22745}{map} \markbox{22746}{is} \markbox{22747}{the} \markbox{22748}{map} \markbox{22749}{described} \markbox{22750}{in} \markbox{22751}{parts} \eqref{item:stable pairs} \markbox{22752}{and} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{22753}{of} \markbox{22754}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.  \markbox{22755}{By} \markbox{22756}{construction,} \markbox{22757}{each} \markbox{22758}{of} \markbox{22759}{these} \markbox{22760}{pieces} \markbox{22761}{has} \markbox{22762}{positive} \markbox{22763}{integer} \markbox{22764}{length,} \markbox{22765}{thus} \markbox{22766}{verifying} \markbox{22767}{property} \eqref{item:integer length}.

To \markbox{22768}{construct} \markbox{22769}{the} \markbox{22770}{rest} \markbox{22771}{of} \markbox{22772}{the} \markbox{22773}{stable} \markbox{22774}{decompositions,} \markbox{22775}{namely} \markbox{22776}{stable} \markbox{22777}{pieces} \markbox{22778}{of} \markbox{22779}{type} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{22780}{in} \markbox{22781}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}, \markbox{22782}{we} \markbox{22783}{need} \markbox{22784}{to} \markbox{22785}{compare} \markbox{22786}{the} \markbox{22787}{component} \markbox{m22788}{$\lambda_0(C_1, C_2) \subset T_e$} \markbox{22789}{to} \markbox{22790}{the} \markbox{22791}{two} \markbox{22792}{components} \markbox{m22793}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z) \cup \lambda_0(z, C_2) \subset T'_e$}.  \markbox{22794}{First,} \markbox{22795}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{22796}{says} \markbox{22797}{that} \markbox{22798}{the} \markbox{22799}{endpoints} \markbox{22800}{of} \markbox{m22801}{$\lambda(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{22802}{and} \markbox{m22803}{$\lambda(C_1,z)$} \markbox{22804}{on} \markbox{m22805}{$C_1$} \markbox{22806}{are} \markbox{m22807}{$14\epsilon$}-close, \markbox{22808}{and} \markbox{22809}{hence} \markbox{22810}{the} \markbox{22811}{endpoints} \markbox{22812}{of} \markbox{m22813}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{22814}{and} \markbox{m22815}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z)$} \markbox{22816}{are} \markbox{22817}{within} \markbox{m22818}{$14\epsilon+2$}, \markbox{22819}{and} \markbox{22820}{similarly} \markbox{22821}{for} \markbox{m22822}{$C_2$}.  \markbox{22823}{It} \markbox{22824}{follows} \markbox{22825}{from} \markbox{m22826}{$\delta$}-hyperbolicity \markbox{22827}{of} \markbox{m22828}{$\calZ$} \markbox{22829}{that} \markbox{m22830}{$\lambda_0(C_1, C_2)$} \markbox{22831}{and} \markbox{m22832}{$ \lambda_0(C_1,z) \cup \lambda_0(z, C_2)$} \markbox{22833}{are} \markbox{m22834}{$O(\epsilon)$}-Hausdorff \markbox{22835}{close.}  \markbox{22836}{Now,} \markbox{22837}{unless} \markbox{m22838}{$C_1,C_2$} \markbox{22839}{are} \markbox{m22840}{$O(\epsilon)$}-close \markbox{22841}{in} \markbox{m22842}{$\calZ$}---in \markbox{22843}{which} \markbox{22844}{case} \markbox{22845}{we} \markbox{22846}{can} \markbox{22847}{declare} \markbox{22848}{all} \markbox{22849}{three} \markbox{22850}{of} \markbox{22851}{these} \markbox{22852}{geodesics} \markbox{22853}{to} \markbox{22854}{be} \markbox{22855}{unstable---then} \markbox{22856}{the} \markbox{22857}{shadow} \markbox{m22858}{$s_T(z)$} \markbox{22859}{of} \markbox{m22860}{$z$} \markbox{22861}{on} \markbox{m22862}{$T$} \markbox{22863}{will} \markbox{22864}{be} \markbox{22865}{properly} \markbox{22866}{contained} \markbox{22867}{in} \markbox{m22868}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{22869}{and} \markbox{22870}{have} \markbox{m22871}{$O(\epsilon)$}-bounded \markbox{22872}{diameter.}    \markbox{22873}{Hence} \markbox{22874}{we} \markbox{22875}{can} \markbox{22876}{decompose} \markbox{22877}{these} \markbox{22878}{geodesics} \markbox{22879}{into} \markbox{m22880}{$O(\epsilon)$}-close \markbox{22881}{stable} \markbox{22882}{pieces} \markbox{22883}{and} \markbox{22884}{unstable} \markbox{22885}{pieces} \markbox{22886}{labeled} \markbox{22887}{by} \markbox{m22888}{$z$}, \markbox{22889}{as} \markbox{22890}{described} \markbox{22891}{in} \markbox{22892}{property} \eqref{item:unstable components}, \markbox{22893}{while} \markbox{22894}{satisfying} \markbox{22895}{the} \markbox{22896}{length} \markbox{22897}{requirement} \markbox{22898}{of} \eqref{item:integer length} \markbox{22899}{and} \markbox{22900}{proximity} \markbox{22901}{requirements} \markbox{22902}{of} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{22903}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs}; \markbox{22904}{see} \markbox{22905}{Figure} \ref{fig:split cluster} \markbox{22906}{for} \markbox{22907}{a} \markbox{22908}{heuristic} \markbox{22909}{picture.}  \markbox{22910}{For} \markbox{22911}{the} \markbox{22912}{bijection} \markbox{m22913}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_s) \to \pi_0(T'_s)$}, \markbox{22914}{since} \markbox{m22915}{$T_s,T'_s$} \markbox{22916}{have} \markbox{22917}{the} \markbox{22918}{same} \markbox{22919}{number} \markbox{22920}{of} \markbox{22921}{components,} \markbox{22922}{we} \markbox{22923}{can} \markbox{22924}{take} \markbox{22925}{let} \markbox{m22926}{$\alpha$} \markbox{22927}{denote} \markbox{22928}{the} \markbox{22929}{natural} \markbox{22930}{order-preserving} \markbox{22931}{bijection,} \markbox{22932}{i.e.} \markbox{22933}{the} \markbox{22934}{one} \markbox{22935}{obtained} \markbox{22936}{by} \markbox{22937}{moving} \markbox{22938}{along} \markbox{22939}{the} \markbox{22940}{geodesics} \markbox{m22941}{$[a,b]_{T}$} \markbox{22942}{and} \markbox{m22943}{$[a,b]_{T'}$}.  \markbox{22944}{By} \markbox{22945}{construction,} \markbox{22946}{this} \markbox{22947}{bijection} \markbox{22948}{identifies} \markbox{22949}{the} \markbox{22950}{components} \markbox{22951}{we} \markbox{22952}{want} \markbox{22953}{so} \markbox{22954}{that} \markbox{22955}{the} \markbox{22956}{related} \markbox{22957}{conditions} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{22958}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{22959}{are} satisfied.

Finally, \markbox{22960}{we} \markbox{22961}{need} \markbox{22962}{to} \markbox{22963}{confirm} \markbox{22964}{the} \markbox{22965}{properties} \markbox{22966}{in} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{22967}{for} \markbox{22968}{the} \markbox{22969}{order-preserving} \markbox{22970}{bijection} \markbox{m22971}{$\beta:\pi_0(T - T_s) \to \pi_0 (T'-T'_s)$} \markbox{22972}{induced} \markbox{22973}{by} \markbox{m22974}{$\alpha$}.  \markbox{22975}{Since} \markbox{m22976}{$\beta$} \markbox{22977}{is} \markbox{22978}{order-preserving} \markbox{22979}{(with} \markbox{22980}{the} \markbox{22981}{order} \markbox{22982}{being} ``from \markbox{m22983}{$a$} \markbox{22984}{to} \markbox{m22985}{$b$}'', \markbox{22986}{as} \markbox{22987}{in} \markbox{22988}{Definition} \ref{defn:order preserving}), \eqref{item:endpoint condition}, \markbox{22989}{i.e.} \markbox{22990}{that} \markbox{22991}{the} \markbox{22992}{components} \markbox{22993}{of} \markbox{m22994}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{22995}{and} \markbox{m22996}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{22997}{associated} \markbox{22998}{to} \markbox{m22999}{$a$} \markbox{23000}{and} \markbox{m23001}{$b$} \markbox{23002}{are} \markbox{23003}{identified,} \markbox{23004}{is} \markbox{23005}{automatically} \markbox{23006}{satisfied.}  \markbox{23007}{For} \eqref{item:cluster identify}, \markbox{23008}{note} \markbox{23009}{that} \markbox{m23010}{$\calY \cap (\calY \cup \{z\}) = \calY$}, \markbox{23011}{and,} \markbox{23012}{by} \markbox{23013}{construction} \markbox{23014}{again,} \markbox{23015}{if} \markbox{m23016}{$y \in \calY$}, \markbox{23017}{then} \markbox{m23018}{$\beta$} \markbox{23019}{identifies} \markbox{23020}{the} \markbox{23021}{component} \markbox{m23022}{$D_y$} \markbox{23023}{of} \markbox{m23024}{$T- T_s$} \markbox{23025}{corresponding} \markbox{23026}{to} \markbox{m23027}{$y$} \markbox{23028}{with} \markbox{m23029}{$D'_y$}, \markbox{23030}{the} \markbox{23031}{component} \markbox{23032}{of} \markbox{m23033}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{23034}{corresponding} \markbox{23035}{to} \markbox{m23036}{$y$}.  \markbox{23037}{In} \markbox{23038}{this} \markbox{23039}{case,} \markbox{23040}{this} \markbox{23041}{is} \markbox{23042}{because} \markbox{23043}{all} \markbox{23044}{such} \markbox{23045}{components} \markbox{23046}{are} \markbox{23047}{exactly} \markbox{23048}{the} \markbox{23049}{same.}   \markbox{23050}{This} \markbox{23051}{proves} \markbox{23052}{part} \markbox{23053}{(1)} \markbox{23054}{of} \markbox{23055}{the} statement.

For \markbox{23056}{part} \markbox{23057}{(2)} \markbox{23058}{of} \markbox{23059}{the} \markbox{23060}{statement,} \markbox{23061}{we} \markbox{23062}{want} \markbox{23063}{to} \markbox{23064}{consider} \markbox{23065}{how} \markbox{23066}{the} \markbox{m23067}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{23068}{of} \markbox{m23069}{$T,T'$} \markbox{23070}{along} \markbox{m23071}{$T_c,T'_c$} \markbox{23072}{respectively} \markbox{23073}{affect} \markbox{23074}{the} \markbox{23075}{decompositions} \markbox{m23076}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{23077}{and} \markbox{m23078}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$}.  \markbox{23079}{First,} \markbox{23080}{observe} \markbox{23081}{that} \markbox{m23082}{$\bT_e \subset T_e$} \markbox{23083}{and} \markbox{m23084}{$\bT'_e \subset T'_e$} \markbox{23085}{by} \markbox{23086}{definition.}  \markbox{23087}{In} \markbox{23088}{particular,} \markbox{23089}{consider} \markbox{23090}{a} \markbox{23091}{component} \markbox{m23092}{$D \subset T_e$}, \markbox{23093}{where} \markbox{m23094}{$D = \lambda_0(C,C')$} \markbox{23095}{for} \markbox{23096}{adjacent} \markbox{23097}{clusters} \markbox{m23098}{$C,C'$}.  \markbox{23099}{Then} \markbox{23100}{the} \markbox{m23101}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{23102}{of} \markbox{m23103}{$D$} \markbox{23104}{either} \markbox{23105}{truncates} \markbox{m23106}{$D$} \markbox{23107}{to} \markbox{m23108}{$D_{thick} = D - (\mu_{r_1}(C) \cup \mu_{r_1}(C'))$}, \markbox{23109}{or} \markbox{23110}{possibly} \markbox{23111}{removes} \markbox{m23112}{$D$} \markbox{23113}{entirely} \markbox{23114}{from} \markbox{m23115}{$\bT_e$} \markbox{23116}{if} \markbox{m23117}{$d_T(\mu(C), \mu(C'))<r_2-2r_1$}.  \markbox{23118}{A} \markbox{23119}{similar} \markbox{23120}{statement} \markbox{23121}{holds} \markbox{23122}{for} \markbox{23123}{components} \markbox{23124}{of} \markbox{m23125}{$T'_e$}.

By \markbox{23126}{the} \markbox{23127}{above,} \markbox{23128}{most} \markbox{23129}{components} \markbox{23130}{of} \markbox{m23131}{$T_s$} \markbox{23132}{and} \markbox{m23133}{$T'_s$} \markbox{23134}{are} \markbox{23135}{identical} \markbox{23136}{components} \markbox{23137}{of} \markbox{m23138}{$T_e, T'_e$}, \markbox{23139}{and} \markbox{23140}{hence} \markbox{23141}{their} \markbox{23142}{thickenings} \markbox{23143}{are} \markbox{23144}{exactly} \markbox{23145}{the} \markbox{23146}{same} \markbox{23147}{by} \markbox{23148}{the} \markbox{23149}{above.}  \markbox{23150}{For} \markbox{23151}{the} \markbox{23152}{remaining} \markbox{23153}{components,} \markbox{23154}{namely} \markbox{m23155}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z), \lambda_0(z,C_2)$} \markbox{23156}{of} \markbox{m23157}{$T'_e$} \markbox{23158}{and} \markbox{m23159}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{23160}{of} \markbox{m23161}{$T_e$}, \markbox{23162}{each} \markbox{23163}{is} \markbox{23164}{either} \markbox{23165}{truncated} \markbox{23166}{or} \markbox{23167}{removed} \markbox{23168}{as} \markbox{23169}{above.}  \markbox{23170}{The} \markbox{23171}{remaining} \markbox{23172}{two} \markbox{23173}{components} \markbox{23174}{of} \markbox{23175}{the} \markbox{23176}{stable} \markbox{23177}{decomposition} \markbox{m23178}{$T_s$} \markbox{23179}{correspond} \markbox{23180}{to} \markbox{m23181}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z)$} \markbox{23182}{and} \markbox{m23183}{$\lambda_0(z,C_2)$}, \markbox{23184}{and} \markbox{23185}{so} \markbox{23186}{one} \markbox{23187}{can} \markbox{23188}{construct} \markbox{23189}{the} \markbox{23190}{corresponding} \markbox{23191}{components} \markbox{23192}{of} \markbox{m23193}{$\bT_s$} \markbox{23194}{by} \markbox{23195}{applying} \markbox{23196}{the} \markbox{23197}{same} \markbox{23198}{procedure} \markbox{23199}{to} \markbox{23200}{the} \markbox{m23201}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{23202}{of} \markbox{m23203}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z)$} \markbox{23204}{and} \markbox{m23205}{$\lambda_0(z,C_2)$}.  \markbox{23206}{Note} \markbox{23207}{that} \markbox{23208}{this} \markbox{23209}{can} \markbox{23210}{inflate} \markbox{23211}{the} \markbox{23212}{proximity} \markbox{23213}{constants,} \markbox{23214}{but} \markbox{23215}{only} \markbox{23216}{in} \markbox{23217}{terms} \markbox{23218}{of} \markbox{m23219}{$r_1,r_2$}.  \markbox{23220}{The} \markbox{23221}{rest} \markbox{23222}{of} \markbox{23223}{the} \markbox{23224}{proof} \markbox{23225}{goes} \markbox{23226}{through} \markbox{23227}{unchanged;} \markbox{23228}{see} \markbox{23229}{Figure} \ref{fig:split cluster}.




\medskip

\underline{\textbf{Case (b), $z$ affects other clusters}}: \markbox{23230}{Suppose} \markbox{23231}{now} \markbox{23232}{instead} \markbox{23233}{that} \markbox{23234}{there} \markbox{23235}{exists} \markbox{23236}{some} \markbox{23237}{cluster} \markbox{m23238}{$C$} \markbox{23239}{for} \markbox{m23240}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{23241}{so} \markbox{23242}{that} \markbox{m23243}{$d(z,C)<E$}; \markbox{23244}{we} \markbox{23245}{say} \markbox{m23246}{$C$} \markbox{23247}{is} \markbox{23248}{an}  \emph{affected cluster}.

\begin{claim}\label{claim:bounded affect}
If \markbox{m23249}{$3E - 56\epsilon > 2E$}, \markbox{23250}{then} \markbox{23251}{there} \markbox{23252}{are} \markbox{23253}{at} \markbox{23254}{most} \markbox{23255}{three} \markbox{23256}{affected} \markbox{23257}{clusters,} \markbox{23258}{and} \markbox{23259}{they} \markbox{23260}{are} \markbox{23261}{adjacent} \markbox{23262}{in} \markbox{m23263}{$\calG$}.
\end{claim}

\begin{proof}
Suppose \markbox{23264}{that} \markbox{m23265}{$C_1,\dots, C_4$} \markbox{23266}{are} \markbox{23267}{four} \markbox{23268}{clusters} \markbox{23269}{appearing} \markbox{23270}{in} \markbox{23271}{that} \markbox{23272}{order} \markbox{23273}{along} \markbox{m23274}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{23275}{By} \markbox{23276}{item} \markbox{23277}{(1)} \markbox{23278}{of} \markbox{23279}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close}, \markbox{23280}{since} \markbox{m23281}{$d(C_i, C_{i+1})\geq E$}, \markbox{23282}{we} \markbox{23283}{have} \markbox{m23284}{$d(s(C_i), s(C_{i+1}))> E - 14\epsilon$}, \markbox{23285}{for} \markbox{m23286}{$i = 1,2,3$}.

Since \markbox{23287}{the} \markbox{23288}{shadows} \markbox{23289}{are} \markbox{23290}{disjoint} \markbox{23291}{segments} \markbox{23292}{of} \markbox{23293}{the} \markbox{23294}{geodesic} \markbox{m23295}{$\lambda(a,b)$}, \markbox{23296}{we} \markbox{23297}{have} that
$$d(s(C_1), s(C_4)) \geq d(s(C_1), s(C_2)) + d(s(C_2), s(C_3))+d(s(C_3), s(C_4)) \geq 3E -42\epsilon.$$
Hence \markbox{23298}{if} \markbox{m23299}{$3E-56\epsilon \geq 2E$}, \markbox{23300}{then} \markbox{23301}{item} \markbox{23302}{(1)} \markbox{23303}{of} \markbox{23304}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{23305}{says} \markbox{23306}{that} 
$$d(C_1,C_4) \geq d(s(C_1),s(C_4)) - 14\epsilon \geq 3E-56\epsilon > 2E.$$

This \markbox{23307}{is} \markbox{23308}{impossible} \markbox{23309}{if} \markbox{m23310}{$z$} \markbox{23311}{is} \markbox{m23312}{$E$}-close \markbox{23313}{to} \markbox{23314}{both} \markbox{m23315}{$C_1,C_4$}.  \markbox{23316}{Hence} \markbox{23317}{there} \markbox{23318}{are} \markbox{23319}{at} \markbox{23320}{most} \markbox{23321}{three} \markbox{23322}{affected} \markbox{23323}{clusters} \markbox{23324}{and} \markbox{23325}{they} \markbox{23326}{are} \markbox{23327}{adjacent} \markbox{23328}{vertices} \markbox{23329}{in} \markbox{m23330}{$\calG$}.
\end{proof}



Let \markbox{m23331}{$C'$} \markbox{23332}{denote} \markbox{23333}{the} \markbox{23334}{cluster} \markbox{23335}{formed} \markbox{23336}{by} \markbox{m23337}{$z$} \markbox{23338}{and} \markbox{23339}{the} \markbox{23340}{affected} \markbox{23341}{clusters} \markbox{23342}{from} \markbox{m23343}{$(a,b;\calY)$}.  \markbox{23344}{Note} \markbox{23345}{that} \markbox{23346}{the} \markbox{23347}{membership} \markbox{23348}{of} \markbox{23349}{all} \markbox{23350}{other} \markbox{m23351}{$(a,b;\calY)$}-clusters \markbox{23352}{are} \markbox{23353}{unchanged} \markbox{23354}{by} \markbox{23355}{the} \markbox{23356}{addition} \markbox{23357}{of} \markbox{m23358}{$z$}.  \markbox{23359}{Let} \markbox{m23360}{$C_1$} \markbox{23361}{and} \markbox{m23362}{$C_2$} \markbox{23363}{be} \markbox{23364}{the} \markbox{23365}{clusters} \markbox{23366}{adjacent} \markbox{23367}{to} \markbox{23368}{the} \markbox{23369}{affected} \markbox{23370}{clusters} \markbox{23371}{in} \markbox{m23372}{$\calG$} \markbox{23373}{on} \markbox{23374}{the} \markbox{23375}{side} \markbox{23376}{of} \markbox{m23377}{$a$} \markbox{23378}{and} \markbox{m23379}{$b$}, \markbox{23380}{respectively.}  \markbox{23381}{As} \markbox{23382}{in} \markbox{23383}{the} \markbox{23384}{split} \markbox{23385}{cluster} \markbox{23386}{case} \markbox{23387}{above,} \markbox{23388}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster arrangement} \markbox{23389}{implies} \markbox{23390}{that} \markbox{m23391}{$C_1$} \markbox{23392}{separates} \markbox{23393}{all} \markbox{23394}{clusters} \markbox{23395}{on} \markbox{23396}{the} \markbox{m23397}{$a$}-side \markbox{23398}{of} \markbox{m23399}{$\calG$} \markbox{23400}{from} \markbox{m23401}{$C'$}, \markbox{23402}{and} \markbox{23403}{similarly} \markbox{23404}{for} \markbox{m23405}{$C_2$} \markbox{23406}{and} \markbox{23407}{clusters} \markbox{23408}{on} \markbox{23409}{the} \markbox{m23410}{$b$}-side.  \markbox{23411}{Hence} \markbox{23412}{the} \markbox{23413}{subgraph} \markbox{23414}{of} \markbox{m23415}{$\calG$} \markbox{23416}{connecting} \markbox{23417}{the} \markbox{23418}{cluster} \markbox{23419}{containing} \markbox{m23420}{$a$} \markbox{23421}{to} \markbox{m23422}{$C_1$} \markbox{23423}{is} \markbox{23424}{the} \markbox{23425}{subgraph} \markbox{23426}{of} \markbox{m23427}{$\calG'$} \markbox{23428}{connecting} \markbox{23429}{the} \markbox{23430}{(same)} \markbox{23431}{cluster} \markbox{23432}{containing} \markbox{m23433}{$a$} \markbox{23434}{to} \markbox{m23435}{$C_1$}, \markbox{23436}{and} \markbox{23437}{similarly} \markbox{23438}{for} \markbox{23439}{the} \markbox{m23440}{$b$}-side \markbox{23441}{of} \markbox{m23442}{$\calG$} \markbox{23443}{and} \markbox{m23444}{$\calG'$}.  \markbox{23445}{As} \markbox{23446}{such,} \markbox{23447}{all} \markbox{23448}{of} \markbox{23449}{the} \markbox{23450}{corresponding} \markbox{23451}{components} \markbox{23452}{of} \markbox{m23453}{$T_e$} \markbox{23454}{and} \markbox{m23455}{$T'_e$} \markbox{23456}{are} \markbox{23457}{exactly} \markbox{23458}{the} \markbox{23459}{same,} \markbox{23460}{and} \markbox{23461}{have} \markbox{23462}{positive} \markbox{23463}{integer} \markbox{23464}{length} \markbox{23465}{by} \markbox{23466}{construction,} \markbox{23467}{verifying} \markbox{23468}{properties} \eqref{item:integer length}, \eqref{item:stable pairs}, \markbox{23469}{and} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{23470}{of} \markbox{23471}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{23472}{for} \markbox{23473}{these} components.

The \markbox{23474}{forests} \markbox{m23475}{$T_e$} \markbox{23476}{and} \markbox{m23477}{$T'_e$} \markbox{23478}{have} \markbox{23479}{some} \markbox{23480}{remaining} \markbox{23481}{components} \markbox{23482}{which} \markbox{23483}{we} \markbox{23484}{need} \markbox{23485}{to} \markbox{23486}{decompose.}  \markbox{23487}{In} \markbox{m23488}{$T_e$}, \markbox{23489}{there} \markbox{23490}{are} \markbox{23491}{the} \markbox{23492}{at-most} \markbox{m23493}{$2$} \markbox{23494}{components} \markbox{23495}{of} \markbox{m23496}{$T_e$} \markbox{23497}{which} \markbox{23498}{connect} \markbox{23499}{the} \markbox{23500}{affected} \markbox{23501}{clusters.}  \markbox{23502}{By} \markbox{23503}{assumption,} \markbox{23504}{these} \markbox{23505}{segments} \markbox{23506}{are} \markbox{23507}{at} \markbox{23508}{most} \markbox{m23509}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{23510}{long,} \markbox{23511}{so} \markbox{23512}{we} \markbox{23513}{can} \markbox{23514}{declare} \markbox{23515}{them} \markbox{23516}{to} \markbox{23517}{be} \markbox{23518}{unstable} components.

We \markbox{23519}{now} \markbox{23520}{explain} \markbox{23521}{how} \markbox{23522}{to} \markbox{23523}{handle} \markbox{23524}{the} \markbox{23525}{two} \markbox{23526}{remaining} \markbox{23527}{components.}  \markbox{23528}{Let} \markbox{m23529}{$A$} \markbox{23530}{be} \markbox{23531}{the} \markbox{23532}{affected} \markbox{23533}{cluster} \markbox{23534}{adjacent} \markbox{23535}{to} \markbox{m23536}{$C_1$} \markbox{23537}{in} \markbox{m23538}{$\calG$}.  \markbox{23539}{It} \markbox{23540}{is} \markbox{23541}{enough} \markbox{23542}{to} \markbox{23543}{show} \markbox{23544}{that} \markbox{23545}{the} \markbox{23546}{geodesic} \markbox{23547}{segments} \markbox{m23548}{$\lambda(C_1,A)$} \markbox{23549}{and} \markbox{m23550}{$\lambda(C_1,C')$} \markbox{23551}{are} \markbox{m23552}{$O(\epsilon)$}-Hausdorff \markbox{23553}{close,} \markbox{23554}{since} \markbox{23555}{then} \markbox{23556}{the} \markbox{23557}{lengths} \markbox{23558}{of} \markbox{m23559}{$\lambda_0(C_1,A)$} \markbox{23560}{and} \markbox{m23561}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C')$} \markbox{23562}{are} \markbox{23563}{the} \markbox{23564}{same} \markbox{23565}{up} \markbox{23566}{to} \markbox{23567}{error} \markbox{m23568}{$O(\epsilon)$}, \markbox{23569}{and} \markbox{23570}{we} \markbox{23571}{can} \markbox{23572}{declare} \markbox{23573}{a} \markbox{23574}{small} \markbox{23575}{end} \markbox{23576}{segment} \markbox{23577}{of} \markbox{23578}{each} \markbox{23579}{unstable,} \markbox{23580}{so} \markbox{23581}{that} \markbox{23582}{their} \markbox{23583}{(stable)} \markbox{23584}{complements} \markbox{23585}{have} \markbox{23586}{the} \markbox{23587}{same} \markbox{23588}{(positive} \markbox{23589}{integer)} \markbox{23590}{length} \markbox{23591}{and} \markbox{23592}{are} \markbox{m23593}{$O(\epsilon)$}-close.  \markbox{23594}{But} \markbox{23595}{this} \markbox{23596}{endpoint} \markbox{23597}{proximity} \markbox{23598}{statement} \markbox{23599}{is} \markbox{23600}{again} \markbox{23601}{a} \markbox{23602}{consequence} \markbox{23603}{of} \markbox{23604}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close}, \markbox{23605}{since} \markbox{23606}{the} \markbox{23607}{endpoints} \markbox{23608}{of} \markbox{m23609}{$\lambda(C_1,A)$} \markbox{23610}{and} \markbox{m23611}{$\lambda(C_1,C')$} \markbox{23612}{are} \markbox{23613}{within} \markbox{m23614}{$7\epsilon$} \markbox{23615}{of} \markbox{23616}{the} \markbox{23617}{endpoint} \markbox{23618}{of} \markbox{m23619}{$s(C_1)$} \markbox{23620}{on} \markbox{m23621}{$\lambda(a,b)$}, \markbox{23622}{while} \markbox{m23623}{$s(C')$} \markbox{23624}{contains} \markbox{m23625}{$s(A)$} \markbox{23626}{and} \markbox{23627}{its} \markbox{23628}{endpoint} \markbox{23629}{is} \markbox{23630}{at} \markbox{23631}{most} \markbox{m23632}{$(E+\epsilon)$}-away.  \markbox{23633}{Finally,} \markbox{23634}{the} \markbox{23635}{bijection} \markbox{m23636}{$\beta:\pi_0(T-T_s) \to \pi_0(T'-T'_s)$} \markbox{23637}{required} \markbox{23638}{for} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{23639}{is} \markbox{23640}{defined} \markbox{23641}{similar} \markbox{23642}{to} \markbox{23643}{the} \markbox{23644}{split} \markbox{23645}{cluster} \markbox{23646}{case} \markbox{23647}{(a),} \markbox{23648}{with} \markbox{23649}{the} \markbox{23650}{proof} \markbox{23651}{of} \markbox{23652}{condition} \eqref{item:endpoint condition} \markbox{23653}{being} \markbox{23654}{basically} \markbox{23655}{the} \markbox{23656}{same.}  \markbox{23657}{For} \markbox{23658}{condition} \eqref{item:cluster identify}, \markbox{23659}{observe} \markbox{23660}{again} \markbox{23661}{the} \markbox{m23662}{$\calY \cap (\calY \cup \{z\}) = \calY$}.  \markbox{23663}{Assuming} \markbox{23664}{that} \markbox{m23665}{$y \in \calY$} \markbox{23666}{is} \markbox{23667}{contained} \markbox{23668}{in} \markbox{23669}{an} \markbox{23670}{affected} \markbox{23671}{cluster} \markbox{23672}{in} \markbox{23673}{the} \markbox{m23674}{$(\calY; \{a,b\})$} \markbox{23675}{setup---since} \markbox{23676}{otherwise,} \markbox{23677}{it} \markbox{23678}{is} \markbox{23679}{contained} \markbox{23680}{in} \markbox{23681}{an} \markbox{23682}{identical} \markbox{23683}{cluster} \markbox{23684}{in} \markbox{23685}{the} \markbox{m23686}{$(\calY \cup \{z\};\{a,b\})$} \markbox{23687}{setup---then} \markbox{23688}{it} \markbox{23689}{corresponds} \markbox{23690}{to} \markbox{23691}{the} \markbox{23692}{single} \markbox{23693}{component} \markbox{23694}{which} \markbox{23695}{gets} \markbox{23696}{identified} \markbox{23697}{with} \markbox{23698}{the} \markbox{23699}{component} \markbox{23700}{of} \markbox{m23701}{$T'- T'_s$} \markbox{23702}{corresponding} \markbox{23703}{to} \markbox{23704}{the} \markbox{23705}{single} \markbox{23706}{cluster} \markbox{23707}{containing} \markbox{23708}{both} \markbox{m23709}{$y$} \markbox{23710}{and} \markbox{m23711}{$z$}.  \markbox{23712}{This} \markbox{23713}{completes} \markbox{23714}{the} \markbox{23715}{proof} \markbox{23716}{of} \markbox{23717}{(1)} \markbox{23718}{in} \markbox{23719}{the} \markbox{23720}{affected} \markbox{23721}{cluster} \markbox{23722}{case.}  \markbox{23723}{See} \markbox{23724}{Figure} \ref{fig:affected cluster} \markbox{23725}{for} \markbox{23726}{a} \markbox{23727}{heuristic} picture.

The \markbox{23728}{argument} \markbox{23729}{for} \markbox{23730}{(2)} \markbox{23731}{in} \markbox{23732}{the} \markbox{23733}{affected} \markbox{23734}{cluster} \markbox{23735}{case} \markbox{23736}{is} \markbox{23737}{essentially} \markbox{23738}{identical} \markbox{23739}{to} \markbox{23740}{the} \markbox{23741}{split} \markbox{23742}{cluster} \markbox{23743}{version:} \markbox{23744}{All} \markbox{23745}{but} \markbox{23746}{a} \markbox{23747}{few} \markbox{23748}{components} \markbox{23749}{of} \markbox{m23750}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{23751}{and} \markbox{m23752}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$} \markbox{23753}{are} \markbox{23754}{identical} \markbox{23755}{and} \markbox{23756}{thus} \markbox{23757}{have} \markbox{23758}{identical} \markbox{m23759}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings.  \markbox{23760}{And} \markbox{23761}{the} \markbox{23762}{remaining} \markbox{23763}{components} \markbox{23764}{of} \markbox{m23765}{$T_s, T'_s$} \markbox{23766}{are} \markbox{23767}{constructed} \markbox{23768}{by} \markbox{23769}{pairing} \markbox{23770}{the} \markbox{23771}{corresponding} \markbox{23772}{components} \markbox{23773}{of} \markbox{m23774}{$T_e, T'_e$} \markbox{23775}{adjacent} \markbox{23776}{to} \markbox{23777}{or} \markbox{23778}{connecting} \markbox{23779}{the} \markbox{23780}{affected} \markbox{23781}{clusters,} \markbox{23782}{and} \markbox{23783}{then} \markbox{23784}{either} \markbox{23785}{declaring} \markbox{23786}{them} \markbox{23787}{unstable} \markbox{23788}{or} \markbox{23789}{modifying} \markbox{23790}{them} \markbox{23791}{pairwise} \markbox{23792}{to} \markbox{23793}{achieve} \markbox{23794}{the} \markbox{23795}{length} \markbox{23796}{bound.}  \markbox{23797}{As} \markbox{23798}{above,} \markbox{23799}{this} \markbox{23800}{can} \markbox{23801}{be} \markbox{23802}{accomplished} \markbox{23803}{post-thickening;} \markbox{23804}{see} \markbox{23805}{Figure} \ref{fig:affected cluster}.  \markbox{23806}{This} \markbox{23807}{completes} \markbox{23808}{the} \markbox{23809}{proof} \markbox{23810}{of} \markbox{23811}{the} theorem.

\end{proof}

\subsection{Iterating stable decompositions}


Next \markbox{23812}{we} \markbox{23813}{move} \markbox{23814}{to} \markbox{23815}{proving} \markbox{23816}{our} \markbox{23817}{iteration} \markbox{23818}{statement} \markbox{23819}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:stable iteration}).  \markbox{23820}{The} \markbox{23821}{main} \markbox{23822}{work} \markbox{23823}{is} \markbox{23824}{the} \markbox{23825}{base} \markbox{23826}{case} \markbox{23827}{of} \markbox{23828}{combining} \markbox{23829}{two} \markbox{23830}{pairs} \markbox{23831}{of} \markbox{23832}{stable} \markbox{23833}{decompositions} \markbox{23834}{across} \markbox{23835}{a} \markbox{23836}{common} setup.

For \markbox{23837}{this,} \markbox{23838}{suppose} \markbox{23839}{we} \markbox{23840}{have} \markbox{23841}{three} \markbox{23842}{setups} \markbox{m23843}{$(a_i,b_i;\calY_i)$} \markbox{23844}{for} \markbox{m23845}{$i=1,2,3$}, \markbox{23846}{satisfying} \markbox{23847}{that} \markbox{m23848}{$\calY_i \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a_j,b_k))$} \markbox{23849}{for} \markbox{23850}{all} \markbox{m23851}{$i,j,k$}, \markbox{23852}{and} \markbox{23853}{that} \markbox{m23854}{$\calY_0 \subset \calY_i$} \markbox{23855}{for} \markbox{23856}{each} \markbox{m23857}{$i$}.  \markbox{23858}{Suppose} \markbox{23859}{that} \markbox{23860}{the} \markbox{23861}{stable} \markbox{23862}{intervals} \markbox{23863}{associated} \markbox{23864}{to} \markbox{m23865}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1)$} \markbox{23866}{and} \markbox{m23867}{$(a_2,b_2;\calY_2)$} \markbox{23868}{admits} \markbox{m23869}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m23870}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{23871}{decompositions,} \markbox{23872}{and} \markbox{23873}{the} \markbox{23874}{same} \markbox{23875}{for} \markbox{m23876}{$(a_2,b_2;\calY_2)$} \markbox{23877}{and} \markbox{m23878}{$(a_3,b_3;\calY_3)$}.  \markbox{23879}{Our} \markbox{23880}{goal} \markbox{23881}{is} \markbox{23882}{to} \markbox{23883}{induce} \markbox{23884}{new} \markbox{23885}{stable} \markbox{23886}{decompositions} \markbox{23887}{on} \markbox{m23888}{$T_1,T_2$} \markbox{23889}{and} \markbox{m23890}{$T_2,T_3$} \markbox{23891}{which} \markbox{23892}{encode} \markbox{23893}{the} \markbox{23894}{stable} \markbox{23895}{decompositions} \markbox{23896}{from} \markbox{m23897}{$T_2,T_3$} \markbox{23898}{and} \markbox{m23899}{$T_1,T_2$}, \markbox{23900}{respectively.}  \markbox{23901}{The} \markbox{23902}{following} \markbox{23903}{describes} \markbox{23904}{the} \markbox{23905}{properties} \markbox{23906}{we} \markbox{23907}{want} \markbox{23908}{for} \markbox{23909}{these} \markbox{23910}{induced} decompositions:

\begin{definition}[Refined \markbox{23911}{stable} decompositions]\label{defn:refined decomp}
Let \markbox{m23912}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{23913}{and} \markbox{m23914}{$(a',b';\calY')$} \markbox{23915}{denote} \markbox{23916}{two} \markbox{23917}{admissible} \markbox{m23918}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{23919}{and} \markbox{23920}{let} \markbox{m23921}{$\calY_0 = \calY \cap \calY'$}.  \markbox{23922}{Suppose} \markbox{23923}{we} \markbox{23924}{have} \markbox{23925}{two} \markbox{23926}{compatible} \markbox{m23927}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{23928}{decompositions} \markbox{m23929}{$T_s \subset T$} \markbox{23930}{and} \markbox{m23931}{$T'_s \subset T'$}.  \markbox{23932}{We} \markbox{23933}{say} \markbox{23934}{another} \markbox{23935}{pair} \markbox{23936}{of} \markbox{23937}{stable} \markbox{23938}{decompositions} \markbox{m23939}{$T_{s,0} \subset T$} \markbox{23940}{and} \markbox{m23941}{$T'_{s,0} \subset T'$} \emph{refine} \markbox{m23942}{$T_s \subset T$} \markbox{23943}{and} \markbox{m23944}{$T'_s \subset T'$} \markbox{23945}{if} \markbox{23946}{the} \markbox{23947}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item We \markbox{23948}{have} \markbox{m23949}{$T_{s,0} \subset T_s$} \markbox{23950}{and} \markbox{m23951}{$T'_{s,0} \subset T'_s$}, and
