\item Let \markbox{m23952}{$\beta:\pi_0(T - T_s) \to \pi_0(T'-T'_s)$} \markbox{23953}{and} \markbox{m23954}{$\beta_0:\pi_0(T-T_{s,0}) \to \pi_0(T' - T'_{s,0})$} \markbox{23955}{denote} \markbox{23956}{the} \markbox{23957}{associated} \markbox{23958}{order-preserving} \markbox{23959}{bijections.}  \markbox{23960}{Suppose} \markbox{m23961}{$C_1 \in \pi_0(T - T_s)$}  \markbox{23962}{and} \markbox{23963}{let} \markbox{m23964}{$C_{1,0} \in \pi_0(T-T_{s,0})$} \markbox{23965}{denote} \markbox{23966}{the} \markbox{23967}{component} \markbox{23968}{containing} \markbox{m23969}{$C_1$} \markbox{23970}{(which} \markbox{23971}{exists} \markbox{23972}{because} \markbox{m23973}{$T_{s,0} \subset T_s$}).  \markbox{23974}{Then} \markbox{m23975}{$\beta(C_1) \subset \beta_0(C_{1,0})$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}\label{rem:purpose of refined}
Condition \markbox{23976}{(2)} \markbox{23977}{in} \markbox{23978}{particular} \markbox{23979}{is} \markbox{23980}{used} \markbox{23981}{to} \markbox{23982}{verify} \markbox{23983}{the} \markbox{23984}{properties} \markbox{23985}{in} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{23986}{of} \markbox{23987}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{23988}{during} \markbox{23989}{our} \markbox{23990}{iteration} \markbox{23991}{procedure.}  \markbox{23992}{For} \markbox{23993}{item} \eqref{item:endpoint condition}, \markbox{23994}{since} \markbox{m23995}{$\beta$} \markbox{23996}{identifies} \markbox{23997}{the} \markbox{23998}{component} \markbox{23999}{of} \markbox{m24000}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{24001}{containing} \markbox{24002}{the} \markbox{24003}{cluster} \markbox{24004}{component} \markbox{24005}{associated} \markbox{24006}{to} \markbox{m24007}{$a$} \markbox{24008}{to} \markbox{24009}{the} \markbox{24010}{component} \markbox{24011}{of} \markbox{m24012}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{24013}{containing} \markbox{24014}{the} \markbox{24015}{cluster} \markbox{24016}{component} \markbox{24017}{associated} \markbox{24018}{to} \markbox{m24019}{$a'$}, \markbox{24020}{the} \markbox{24021}{refinement} \markbox{24022}{condition} \markbox{24023}{(2)} \markbox{24024}{forces} \markbox{24025}{the} \markbox{24026}{same} \markbox{24027}{to} \markbox{24028}{hold} \markbox{24029}{for} \markbox{m24030}{$\beta_0$}.  \markbox{24031}{A} \markbox{24032}{similar} \markbox{24033}{observation} \markbox{24034}{works} \markbox{24035}{to} \markbox{24036}{verify} \markbox{24037}{item} \eqref{item:cluster identify}.
\end{remark}

Following \markbox{24038}{our} \markbox{24039}{notation} \markbox{24040}{from} \markbox{24041}{before} \markbox{24042}{the} \markbox{24043}{above} \markbox{24044}{definition,} \markbox{24045}{let} \markbox{m24046}{$\phi_i:T_i \to \calZ$} \markbox{24047}{denote} \markbox{24048}{the} \markbox{24049}{maps} \markbox{24050}{into} \markbox{m24051}{$\calZ$}.  \markbox{24052}{Moreover,} \markbox{24053}{assume} \markbox{24054}{that} \markbox{24055}{we} have
\begin{itemize}
\item a \markbox{m24056}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{24057}{decomposition} \markbox{m24058}{$T^1_{s,2} \subset T_{e,2}$} \markbox{24059}{which} \markbox{24060}{is} \markbox{m24061}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{24062}{with} \markbox{m24063}{$T^2_{s,1} \subset T_{e,1} $} \markbox{24064}{for} \markbox{24065}{the} \markbox{24066}{setups} \markbox{m24067}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1)$} \markbox{24068}{and} \markbox{m24069}{$(a_2,b_2;\calY_2)$}, and
\item a \markbox{m24070}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{24071}{decomposition} \markbox{m24072}{$T^3_{s,2} \subset T_{e,2}$} \markbox{24073}{which} \markbox{24074}{is} \markbox{m24075}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{24076}{with} \markbox{m24077}{$T^2_{s,3} \subset T_{e,3}$} \markbox{24078}{for} \markbox{24079}{the} \markbox{24080}{setups} \markbox{m24081}{$(a_2,b_2;\calY_2)$} \markbox{24082}{and} \markbox{m24083}{$(a_3,b_3;\calY_3)$}.
\end{itemize}

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable iteration, pair}
There \markbox{24084}{exists} \markbox{m24085}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m24086}{$4L^2$}-compatible \markbox{24087}{decompositions} \markbox{m24088}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1} \subset T_{e,1}$} \markbox{24089}{and} \markbox{m24090}{$T^{2,1}_{s,3} \subset T_{e,3}$} \markbox{24091}{which} \markbox{24092}{refine} \markbox{m24093}{$T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24094}{and} \markbox{m24095}{$T^2_{s,3}$}. 
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Note \markbox{24096}{that} \markbox{24097}{the} \markbox{24098}{stable} \markbox{24099}{decompositions} \markbox{m24100}{$T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24101}{and} \markbox{m24102}{$T^3_{s,2}$} \markbox{24103}{both} \markbox{24104}{live} \markbox{24105}{on} \markbox{m24106}{$T_2$}.  \markbox{24107}{Set} \markbox{m24108}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2} = T^1_{s,2} \cap T^3_{s,2}$}.  \markbox{24109}{Observe} \markbox{24110}{that} \markbox{m24111}{$T_{e,2} - T^{1,3}_{s,2} = (T_{e,2} - T^1_{s,2}) \cup (T_{e,2} - T^3_{s,2})$} \markbox{24112}{has} \markbox{24113}{at} \markbox{24114}{most} \markbox{m24115}{$2L$}-many \markbox{24116}{components} \markbox{24117}{each} \markbox{24118}{of} \markbox{24119}{diameter} \markbox{24120}{at} \markbox{24121}{most} \markbox{m24122}{$4L^2$}; \markbox{24123}{note} \markbox{24124}{that} \markbox{24125}{the} \markbox{24126}{larger} \markbox{24127}{diameter} \markbox{24128}{bound} \markbox{24129}{accounts} \markbox{24130}{for} \markbox{24131}{unstable} \markbox{24132}{components} \markbox{24133}{to} \markbox{24134}{combine,} \markbox{24135}{but} \markbox{24136}{there} \markbox{24137}{are} \markbox{24138}{at} \markbox{24139}{most} \markbox{m24140}{$2L$}-many \markbox{24141}{of} \markbox{24142}{them.}  \markbox{24143}{Moreover,} \markbox{24144}{by} \markbox{24145}{item} \eqref{item:simplicial} \markbox{24146}{of} \markbox{24147}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}, \markbox{24148}{the} \markbox{24149}{endpoints} \markbox{24150}{of} \markbox{24151}{each} \markbox{24152}{component} \markbox{24153}{of} \markbox{m24154}{$T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24155}{and} \markbox{m24156}{$T^3_{s,2}$} \markbox{24157}{are} \markbox{24158}{at} \markbox{24159}{vertices} \markbox{24160}{of} \markbox{24161}{the} \markbox{24162}{components} \markbox{24163}{of} \markbox{m24164}{$T_{e,2}$} \markbox{24165}{which} \markbox{24166}{contain} \markbox{24167}{them,} \markbox{24168}{and} \markbox{24169}{hence} \markbox{24170}{this} \markbox{24171}{property} \markbox{24172}{holds} \markbox{24173}{for} \markbox{24174}{each} \markbox{24175}{component} \markbox{24176}{of} \markbox{m24177}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}$}

We \markbox{24178}{first} \markbox{24179}{produce} \markbox{24180}{refined} \markbox{24181}{decompositions} \markbox{24182}{of} \markbox{m24183}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1} \subset T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24184}{and} \markbox{m24185}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2} \subset T^1_{s,2}$}, \markbox{24186}{and} \markbox{24187}{the} \markbox{24188}{same} \markbox{24189}{argument} \markbox{24190}{produces} \markbox{24191}{the} \markbox{24192}{refined} \markbox{24193}{decompositions} \markbox{m24194}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}  \subset T^3_{s,2}$} \markbox{24195}{and} \markbox{m24196}{$T^{2,1}_{s,3} \subset T^2_{s,3}$}.  \markbox{24197}{We} \markbox{24198}{will} \markbox{24199}{then} \markbox{24200}{see} \markbox{24201}{the} \markbox{24202}{properties} \markbox{24203}{of} \markbox{24204}{Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp} \markbox{24205}{allow} \markbox{24206}{us} \markbox{24207}{to} \markbox{24208}{combine} \markbox{24209}{these,} \markbox{24210}{using} \markbox{m24211}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}$} \markbox{24212}{as} \markbox{24213}{a} \markbox{24214}{bridge} \markbox{24215}{to} \markbox{24216}{connect} them.

We \markbox{24217}{can} \markbox{24218}{induce} \markbox{24219}{a} \markbox{24220}{decomposition} \markbox{m24221}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24222}{on} \markbox{m24223}{$T_1$} \markbox{24224}{by} \markbox{24225}{taking} \markbox{24226}{the} \markbox{24227}{collection} \markbox{24228}{of} \markbox{24229}{all} \markbox{m24230}{$i^{-1}_{E,E'}(E' \cap T^{1,3}_{s,2})$} \markbox{24231}{over} \markbox{24232}{all} \markbox{24233}{stable} \markbox{24234}{pairs} \markbox{m24235}{$(E,E')$} \markbox{24236}{of} \markbox{m24237}{$T_1,T_2$} \markbox{24238}{as} \markbox{24239}{identified} \markbox{24240}{by} \markbox{24241}{the} \markbox{24242}{bijection} \markbox{m24243}{$\alpha_{1,2}:\pi_0(T_{s,1}) \to \pi_0(T_{s,2})$}.  \markbox{24244}{Observe} \markbox{24245}{that} \markbox{24246}{any} \markbox{24247}{component} \markbox{m24248}{$V \subset T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24249}{is} \markbox{24250}{contained} \markbox{24251}{in} \markbox{24252}{some} \markbox{24253}{component} \markbox{m24254}{$V \subset E \subset T_{s,1} \subset T_{e,1}$}, \markbox{24255}{and} \markbox{24256}{the} \markbox{24257}{map} \markbox{m24258}{$i_{E,E'}|_V:V \to i_{E,E'}(V)$} \markbox{24259}{is} \markbox{24260}{an} \markbox{24261}{isometry,} \markbox{24262}{where} \markbox{m24263}{$E' = \alpha_{1,2}(E)$}, \markbox{24264}{and} \markbox{24265}{vice} \markbox{24266}{versa.}  \markbox{24267}{Thus} \markbox{24268}{the} \markbox{24269}{components} \markbox{24270}{of} \markbox{m24271}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24272}{are} \markbox{24273}{in} \markbox{24274}{bijective} \markbox{24275}{correspondence} \markbox{24276}{with} \markbox{24277}{the} \markbox{24278}{components} \markbox{24279}{of} \markbox{m24280}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}$}, \markbox{24281}{with} \markbox{24282}{identified} \markbox{24283}{components} \markbox{24284}{being} \markbox{24285}{isometric.}  \markbox{24286}{Moreover,}  \markbox{24287}{the} \markbox{24288}{natural} \markbox{24289}{order-preserving} \markbox{24290}{bijection} \markbox{m24291}{$\alpha^3_{1,2}:\pi_0(T^{2,3}_{s,1}) \to \pi_0(T^{1,3}_{s,2})$} \markbox{24292}{(as} \markbox{24293}{in} \markbox{24294}{Definition} \ref{defn:order preserving}) \markbox{24295}{coincides} \markbox{24296}{with} \markbox{24297}{the} \markbox{24298}{bijective} \markbox{24299}{correspondence} \markbox{24300}{induced} \markbox{24301}{from} \markbox{m24302}{$\alpha_{1,2}$} \markbox{24303}{and} \markbox{24304}{the} \markbox{24305}{various} \markbox{24306}{order-preserving} \markbox{24307}{isometries} \markbox{m24308}{$i_{E,E'}$}.  \markbox{24309}{We} \markbox{24310}{also} \markbox{24311}{note} \markbox{24312}{that} \markbox{24313}{the} \markbox{24314}{various} \markbox{24315}{restrictions} \markbox{m24316}{$i_{E,E'}|V$} \markbox{24317}{are} \markbox{24318}{order-preserving} \markbox{24319}{since} \markbox{m24320}{$i_{E,E'}$} \markbox{24321}{is.}  \markbox{24322}{Next} \markbox{24323}{observe} \markbox{24324}{that} \markbox{24325}{the} \markbox{24326}{images} \markbox{m24327}{$\phi_1(V)$} \markbox{24328}{and} \markbox{m24329}{$\phi_2(i_{E,E'}(V))$} \markbox{24330}{are} \markbox{24331}{either} \markbox{24332}{exactly} \markbox{24333}{the} \markbox{24334}{same} \markbox{24335}{or} \markbox{24336}{are} \markbox{m24337}{$L$}-Hausdorff \markbox{24338}{close} \markbox{24339}{in} \markbox{m24340}{$\calZ$} \markbox{24341}{as} \markbox{24342}{items} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{24343}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{24344}{of} \markbox{24345}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.  \markbox{24346}{Thus} \markbox{24347}{the} \markbox{24348}{decompositions} \markbox{m24349}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1} \subset T_1$} \markbox{24350}{and} \markbox{m24351}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2} \subset T_2$} \markbox{24352}{satisfy} \markbox{24353}{all} \markbox{24354}{the} \markbox{24355}{properties} \markbox{24356}{of} \markbox{24357}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{24358}{except} \markbox{24359}{possibly} \eqref{item:adjacency}.  \markbox{24360}{We} \markbox{24361}{also} \markbox{24362}{want} \markbox{24363}{to} \markbox{24364}{show} \markbox{24365}{that} \markbox{24366}{they} \markbox{24367}{give} \markbox{24368}{a} \markbox{24369}{refinement} \markbox{24370}{as} \markbox{24371}{in} \markbox{24372}{Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp}.

To \markbox{24373}{prove} \eqref{item:adjacency}, \markbox{24374}{it} \markbox{24375}{will} \markbox{24376}{suffice} \markbox{24377}{to} \markbox{24378}{show} \markbox{24379}{the} \markbox{24380}{refinement} \markbox{24381}{property} \markbox{24382}{(Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp}), \markbox{24383}{as} \markbox{24384}{explained} \markbox{24385}{in} \markbox{24386}{Remark} \ref{rem:purpose of refined}.  \markbox{24387}{Property} \markbox{24388}{(1),} \markbox{24389}{namely} \markbox{24390}{that} \markbox{m24391}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1} \subset T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24392}{and} \markbox{m24393}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2} \subset T^1_{s,2}$}, \markbox{24394}{of} \markbox{24395}{Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp} \markbox{24396}{holds} \markbox{24397}{by} \markbox{24398}{construction.}  \markbox{24399}{For} \markbox{24400}{property} \markbox{24401}{(2),} \markbox{24402}{we} \markbox{24403}{argument} \markbox{24404}{one} \markbox{24405}{component} \markbox{24406}{at} \markbox{24407}{a} \markbox{24408}{time.}  \markbox{24409}{In} \markbox{24410}{particular,} \markbox{24411}{let} \markbox{m24412}{$\beta^3_{1,2}:\pi_0(T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}) \to \pi_0(T_2 - T^{1,3}_{s,2})$} \markbox{24413}{be} \markbox{24414}{the} \markbox{24415}{natural} \markbox{24416}{order-preserving} \markbox{24417}{bijections} \markbox{24418}{(which} \markbox{24419}{exists} \markbox{24420}{via} \markbox{24421}{Remark} \ref{rem:order preserving} \markbox{24422}{because} \markbox{m24423}{$\alpha^3_{1,2}$} does).

First, \markbox{24424}{since} \markbox{24425}{the} \markbox{24426}{(unstable)} \markbox{24427}{components} \markbox{24428}{of} \markbox{m24429}{$T_1 - T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24430}{only} \markbox{24431}{get} \markbox{24432}{expanded} \markbox{24433}{when} \markbox{24434}{passing} \markbox{24435}{to} \markbox{m24436}{$T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$}, \markbox{24437}{it} \markbox{24438}{follows} \markbox{24439}{that} \markbox{24440}{the} \markbox{24441}{first} \markbox{24442}{component} \markbox{m24443}{$C_0 \subset T_1 - T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24444}{one} \markbox{24445}{encounters} \markbox{24446}{when} \markbox{24447}{moving} \markbox{24448}{from} \markbox{m24449}{$a_1$} \markbox{24450}{to} \markbox{m24451}{$b_1$} \markbox{24452}{along} \markbox{24453}{the} \markbox{24454}{geodesic} \markbox{m24455}{$[a_1,b_1]_{T_1}$} \markbox{24456}{is} \markbox{24457}{contained} \markbox{24458}{in} \markbox{24459}{the} \markbox{24460}{first} \markbox{24461}{such} \markbox{24462}{component} \markbox{24463}{of} \markbox{m24464}{$C_{0,3} \subset T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$}, \markbox{24465}{and} \markbox{24466}{similarly} \markbox{24467}{for} \markbox{24468}{the} \markbox{24469}{setup} \markbox{24470}{on} \markbox{m24471}{$T_2$}.  \markbox{24472}{Hence} \markbox{24473}{these} \markbox{24474}{expanded} \markbox{24475}{clusters} \markbox{24476}{are} \markbox{24477}{identified} \markbox{24478}{by} \markbox{m24479}{$\beta^3_{1,2}$}, \markbox{24480}{which} \markbox{24481}{we} \markbox{24482}{note} \markbox{24483}{also} \markbox{24484}{confirms} \markbox{24485}{item} \eqref{item:endpoint condition} \markbox{24486}{of} \markbox{24487}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.

We \markbox{24488}{now} \markbox{24489}{proceed} \markbox{24490}{inductively} \markbox{24491}{along} \markbox{m24492}{$T_1$} \markbox{24493}{and} \markbox{m24494}{$T_2$}.  \markbox{24495}{Let} \markbox{m24496}{$C_1, C'_1$} \markbox{24497}{denote} \markbox{24498}{the} \markbox{24499}{second} \markbox{24500}{pairs} \markbox{24501}{of} \markbox{24502}{components} \markbox{24503}{of} \markbox{m24504}{$T_1 - T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24505}{and} \markbox{m24506}{$T_2 - T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24507}{encountered} \markbox{24508}{after} \markbox{m24509}{$C_0, C'_0$}.  \markbox{24510}{Let} \markbox{m24511}{$E, E'$} \markbox{24512}{denote} \markbox{24513}{the} \markbox{24514}{respective} \markbox{24515}{components} \markbox{24516}{of} \markbox{m24517}{$T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24518}{and} \markbox{m24519}{$T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24520}{connecting} \markbox{m24521}{$C_0,C'_0$} \markbox{24522}{to} \markbox{m24523}{$C_1,C'_1$}.  \markbox{24524}{The} \markbox{24525}{components} \markbox{24526}{of} \markbox{m24527}{$(T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}) \cap E$} \markbox{24528}{and} \markbox{m24529}{$(T_2 - T^{1,3}_{s,2}) \cap E'$} \markbox{24530}{are} \markbox{24531}{identified} \markbox{24532}{by} \markbox{24533}{the} \markbox{24534}{order-preserving} \markbox{24535}{isometry} \markbox{m24536}{$i_{E,E'}$} \markbox{24537}{in} \markbox{24538}{an} \markbox{24539}{order-preserving} \markbox{24540}{way.}  \markbox{24541}{In} \markbox{24542}{particular,} \markbox{24543}{the} \markbox{24544}{two} \markbox{24545}{sets} \markbox{24546}{of} \markbox{24547}{components} \markbox{24548}{are} \markbox{24549}{in} \markbox{24550}{bijective} \markbox{24551}{correspondence.}  \markbox{24552}{As} \markbox{24553}{a} \markbox{24554}{consequence,} \markbox{24555}{if} \markbox{m24556}{$C^3_1 \subset T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24557}{is}  \markbox{24558}{the} \markbox{24559}{component} \markbox{24560}{containing} \markbox{m24561}{$C_1$}, \markbox{24562}{then} \markbox{m24563}{$C'_1 \subset \beta^{3}_{1,2}(C^3_1)$}, \markbox{24564}{as} \markbox{24565}{required.}  \markbox{24566}{One} \markbox{24567}{can} \markbox{24568}{repeat} \markbox{24569}{this} \markbox{24570}{procedure} \markbox{24571}{on} \markbox{24572}{subsequent} \markbox{24573}{components} \markbox{24574}{of} \markbox{m24575}{$T_1 - T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24576}{and} \markbox{24577}{their} \markbox{24578}{paired} \markbox{24579}{components} \markbox{24580}{of} \markbox{m24581}{$T_2 - T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24582}{to} \markbox{24583}{see} \markbox{24584}{that} \markbox{m24585}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24586}{and} \markbox{m24587}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}$} \markbox{24588}{refine} \markbox{m24589}{$T^{2}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24590}{and} \markbox{m24591}{$T^1_{s,2}$}, respectively.

\medskip

\textbf{\underline{Combining the decompositions}}: \markbox{24592}{We} \markbox{24593}{now} \markbox{24594}{want} \markbox{24595}{to} \markbox{24596}{see} \markbox{24597}{that} \markbox{m24598}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24599}{and} \markbox{m24600}{$T^{2,1}_{s,3}$} \markbox{24601}{are} \markbox{m24602}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m24603}{$4L^2$}-compatible \markbox{24604}{decompositions} \markbox{24605}{for} \markbox{m24606}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1)$} \markbox{24607}{and} \markbox{m24608}{$(a_3,b_3;\calY_3)$}.  \markbox{24609}{For} \markbox{24610}{this,} \markbox{24611}{define} \markbox{m24612}{$\alpha_{1,3}:\pi_0(T^{2,3}_{s,1}) \to \pi_0(T^{2,1}_{s,3})$} \markbox{24613}{to} \markbox{24614}{be} \markbox{m24615}{$\alpha_{1,3} = \alpha^{1}_{2,3} \circ \alpha^3_{1,2}$}, \markbox{24616}{and} \markbox{24617}{similarly} \markbox{24618}{set} \markbox{m24619}{$\beta_{1,3} = \beta^1_{2,3} \circ \beta^3_{1,2}$}.  \markbox{24620}{These} \markbox{24621}{compositions} \markbox{24622}{are} \markbox{24623}{order-preserving} \markbox{24624}{bijections} \markbox{24625}{because} \markbox{24626}{their} \markbox{24627}{constituent} \markbox{24628}{maps} \markbox{24629}{are,} \markbox{24630}{and} \markbox{24631}{moreover} \markbox{24632}{we} \markbox{24633}{can} \markbox{24634}{similarly} \markbox{24635}{induce} \markbox{24636}{order-preserving} \markbox{24637}{isometries} \markbox{24638}{on} \markbox{24639}{the} \markbox{24640}{components} \markbox{24641}{of} \markbox{m24642}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24643}{and} \markbox{m24644}{$T^{2,1}_{s,3}$} \markbox{24645}{identified} \markbox{24646}{by} \markbox{m24647}{$\alpha_{1,3}$}, \markbox{24648}{which} \markbox{24649}{satisfy} \markbox{24650}{the} \markbox{24651}{proximity} \markbox{24652}{conditions} \markbox{24653}{of} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{24654}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{24655}{of} \markbox{24656}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{24657}{with} \markbox{24658}{a} \markbox{24659}{constant} \markbox{24660}{of} \markbox{m24661}{$2L$}.  \markbox{24662}{In} \markbox{24663}{particular,} \markbox{24664}{it} \markbox{24665}{remains} \markbox{24666}{to} \markbox{24667}{show} \markbox{24668}{the} \markbox{24669}{properties} \markbox{24670}{in} \eqref{item:adjacency}.

For \markbox{24671}{this,} \markbox{24672}{we} \markbox{24673}{use} \markbox{24674}{the} \markbox{24675}{refinement} \markbox{24676}{property} \markbox{24677}{(2)} \markbox{24678}{of} \markbox{24679}{Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp}.  \markbox{24680}{This} \markbox{24681}{is} \markbox{24682}{basically} \markbox{24683}{automatic.}  \markbox{24684}{For} \markbox{24685}{(1),} \markbox{24686}{the} \markbox{24687}{refinement} \markbox{24688}{property} \markbox{24689}{implies} \markbox{24690}{that} \markbox{m24691}{$\beta^3_{1,2}$} \markbox{24692}{identifies} \markbox{24693}{the} \markbox{24694}{component} \markbox{24695}{of} \markbox{m24696}{$T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24697}{associated} \markbox{24698}{to} \markbox{m24699}{$a_1$} \markbox{24700}{to} \markbox{24701}{the} \markbox{24702}{component} \markbox{24703}{of} \markbox{m24704}{$T_2 - T^{1,3}_{s,2}$} \markbox{24705}{associated} \markbox{24706}{to} \markbox{m24707}{$a_2$}, \markbox{24708}{and} \markbox{24709}{similarly} \markbox{24710}{for} \markbox{m24711}{$\beta^1_{2,3}$}.  \markbox{24712}{Hence} \markbox{m24713}{$\beta_{1,3}$} \markbox{24714}{identifies} \markbox{24715}{the} \markbox{24716}{components} \markbox{24717}{associated} \markbox{24718}{to} \markbox{m24719}{$a_1, a_3$} \markbox{24720}{and} \markbox{m24721}{$b_1,b_3$}.  \markbox{24722}{Similarly,} \markbox{24723}{if} \markbox{m24724}{$y \in \calY_0 \subset \calY_1 \cap \calY_2 \cap \calY_3$}, \markbox{24725}{then} \markbox{24726}{the} \markbox{24727}{refinement} \markbox{24728}{property} \markbox{24729}{implies} \markbox{24730}{that} \markbox{m24731}{$\beta^3_{1,2}$} \markbox{24732}{identifies} \markbox{24733}{the} \markbox{24734}{component} \markbox{24735}{of} \markbox{m24736}{$T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24737}{associated} \markbox{24738}{to} \markbox{m24739}{$y$} \markbox{24740}{to} \markbox{24741}{the} \markbox{24742}{component} \markbox{24743}{of} \markbox{m24744}{$T_2 - T^{1,3}_{s,2}$} \markbox{24745}{associated} \markbox{24746}{to} \markbox{m24747}{$y$}, \markbox{24748}{and} \markbox{24749}{similarly} \markbox{24750}{for} \markbox{m24751}{$\beta^1_{2,3}$}.  \markbox{24752}{Hence} \markbox{m24753}{$\beta_{1,3}$} \markbox{24754}{associates} \markbox{24755}{components} \markbox{24756}{associated} \markbox{24757}{to} \markbox{m24758}{$y$} \markbox{24759}{in} \markbox{24760}{both} \markbox{24761}{of} \markbox{m24762}{$T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24763}{and} \markbox{m24764}{$T_3 - T^{2,1}_{s,3}$}.  \markbox{24765}{This} \markbox{24766}{completes} \markbox{24767}{the} \markbox{24768}{proof} \markbox{24769}{of} \markbox{24770}{the} proposition.



\end{proof}

The \markbox{24771}{following} \markbox{24772}{proposition} \markbox{24773}{is} \markbox{24774}{now} \markbox{24775}{a} \markbox{24776}{simple} \markbox{24777}{iterative} \markbox{24778}{application} \markbox{24779}{of} \markbox{24780}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable iteration, pair}:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable iteration}
For \markbox{24781}{every} \markbox{m24782}{$n\geq 2$}, \markbox{24783}{there} \markbox{24784}{exists} \markbox{m24785}{$L_n = L_n(L,n)>0$} \markbox{24786}{so} \markbox{24787}{that} \markbox{24788}{the} \markbox{24789}{following} \markbox{24790}{holds.}  \markbox{24791}{Suppose} \markbox{m24792}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1), \dots, (a_n,b_n;\calY_n)$} \markbox{24793}{is} \markbox{24794}{a} \markbox{24795}{sequence} \markbox{24796}{of} \markbox{24797}{pairwise} \markbox{24798}{admissible} \markbox{m24799}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{24800}{and} \markbox{24801}{suppose} \markbox{24802}{that} \markbox{m24803}{$\calY_0 \subset \bigcap_i \calY_i$}.  \markbox{24804}{If} \markbox{24805}{each} \markbox{24806}{pair} \markbox{24807}{of} \markbox{24808}{consecutive} \markbox{24809}{setups} \markbox{24810}{admits} \markbox{m24811}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m24812}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{24813}{stable} \markbox{24814}{decompositions,} \markbox{24815}{then} \markbox{m24816}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1)$} \markbox{24817}{and} \markbox{m24818}{$(a_n,b_n;\calY_n)$} \markbox{24819}{admit} \markbox{m24820}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m24821}{$L_n$}-compatible \markbox{24822}{stable} \markbox{24823}{decompositions.} 
\end{proposition}


\subsubsection{Completing the proof} \markbox{24824}{To} \markbox{24825}{prove} \markbox{24826}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}, \markbox{24827}{we} \markbox{24828}{have} \markbox{24829}{two} \markbox{24830}{remaining} tasks:
\begin{enumerate}
\item We \markbox{24831}{need} \markbox{24832}{to} \markbox{24833}{explain} \markbox{24834}{how} \markbox{24835}{to} \markbox{24836}{build} \markbox{24837}{a} \markbox{24838}{stable} \markbox{24839}{decomposition} \markbox{24840}{when} \markbox{24841}{perturbing} \markbox{24842}{an} \markbox{24843}{endpoint} \markbox{24844}{but} \markbox{24845}{keeping} \markbox{24846}{the} \markbox{24847}{rest} \markbox{24848}{of} \markbox{24849}{the} \markbox{24850}{setup} \markbox{24851}{the} \markbox{24852}{same,} and
\item Show \markbox{24853}{how} \markbox{24854}{to} \markbox{24855}{stick} \markbox{24856}{this} \markbox{24857}{into} \markbox{24858}{an} \markbox{24859}{iterative} setup.
\end{enumerate}

\textbf{\underline{Perturbing an endpoint}:} \markbox{24860}{This} \markbox{24861}{is} \markbox{24862}{an} \markbox{24863}{iterated} \markbox{24864}{application} \markbox{24865}{of}  \markbox{24866}{Proposition} \ref{prop:add cluster}.

Consider \markbox{24867}{the} \markbox{24868}{following} \markbox{24869}{restricted} \markbox{24870}{setup,} \markbox{24871}{which} \markbox{24872}{we} \markbox{24873}{highlight} \markbox{24874}{to} \markbox{24875}{focus} \markbox{24876}{on} \markbox{24877}{what} \markbox{24878}{happens} \markbox{24879}{when} \markbox{24880}{we} \markbox{24881}{perturb} \markbox{24882}{an} \markbox{24883}{endpoint.}  \markbox{24884}{Let} \markbox{m24885}{$a,b,a' \in \calZ$} \markbox{24886}{and} \markbox{m24887}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{24888}{be} \markbox{24889}{finite} \markbox{24890}{with} \markbox{m24891}{$\calY \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b)) \cap \calN_{\epsilon/2}(a',b)$}.  \markbox{24892}{Consider} \markbox{24893}{the} \markbox{24894}{following} \markbox{24895}{collection} \markbox{24896}{of} \markbox{24897}{setups,} \markbox{24898}{each} \markbox{24899}{of} \markbox{24900}{which} \markbox{24901}{differs} \markbox{24902}{by} \markbox{24903}{adding} \markbox{24904}{or} \markbox{24905}{deleting} \markbox{24906}{one} \markbox{24907}{cluster} \markbox{24908}{point,} \markbox{24909}{or} \markbox{24910}{by} \markbox{24911}{switching} \markbox{24912}{the} \markbox{24913}{role} \markbox{24914}{that} \markbox{m24915}{$a,a'$} \markbox{24916}{or} \markbox{m24917}{$b,b'$} \markbox{24918}{play} \markbox{24919}{between} \markbox{24920}{cluster} \markbox{24921}{or} endpoint:
\vspace{-.09in}
\begin{multicols}{3}
\begin{enumerate}
\item $(a,b;\calY)$,
\item $(a,b;\calY \cup \{a\})$,
\item $(a,b;\calY \cup \{a, a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY \cup \{a,a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY \cup \{a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY)$.
\end{enumerate}
\end{multicols}

First \markbox{24922}{observe} \markbox{24923}{that} \markbox{m24924}{$\calY$} \markbox{24925}{is} \markbox{24926}{contained} \markbox{24927}{in} \markbox{24928}{each} \markbox{24929}{of} \markbox{24930}{the} \markbox{24931}{above} \markbox{24932}{sets} \markbox{24933}{of} \markbox{24934}{cluster} \markbox{24935}{points,} \markbox{24936}{so} \markbox{24937}{we} \markbox{24938}{want} \markbox{24939}{to} \markbox{24940}{see} \markbox{24941}{how} \markbox{24942}{to} \markbox{24943}{build} \markbox{m24944}{$\calY$}-stable \markbox{24945}{decompositions} \markbox{24946}{for} \markbox{24947}{each,} \markbox{24948}{which} \markbox{24949}{implies} \markbox{24950}{the} \markbox{24951}{existence} \markbox{24952}{of} \markbox{m24953}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{24954}{decompositions} \markbox{24955}{for} \markbox{24956}{any} \markbox{m24957}{$\calY_0 \subset \calY$}.  \markbox{24958}{Next,} \markbox{24959}{observe} \markbox{24960}{that} \markbox{24961}{in} \markbox{24962}{the} \markbox{24963}{construction} \markbox{24964}{of} \markbox{24965}{the} \markbox{24966}{stable} \markbox{24967}{interval} \markbox{m24968}{$T(a,b;\calY)$}, \markbox{24969}{the} \markbox{24970}{roles} \markbox{24971}{of} \markbox{24972}{points} \markbox{24973}{of} \markbox{24974}{the} \markbox{24975}{endpoints} \markbox{m24976}{$a,b$} \markbox{24977}{and} \markbox{24978}{the} \markbox{24979}{cluster} \markbox{24980}{points} \markbox{m24981}{$\calY$} \markbox{24982}{are} \markbox{24983}{equivalent} \markbox{24984}{in} \markbox{24985}{cluster} \markbox{24986}{formation} \markbox{24987}{process.}  \markbox{24988}{The} \markbox{24989}{only} \markbox{24990}{special} \markbox{24991}{role} \markbox{24992}{that} \markbox{24993}{endpoints} \markbox{24994}{play} \markbox{24995}{in} \markbox{24996}{the} \markbox{24997}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable interval} \markbox{24998}{of} \markbox{m24999}{$T(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{25000}{is} \markbox{25001}{in} \markbox{25002}{the} \markbox{25003}{segments} \markbox{25004}{defined} \emph{within} \markbox{25005}{clusters,} \markbox{25006}{namely} \markbox{25007}{the} \markbox{m25008}{$\mu(C)$} \markbox{25009}{components.}  \markbox{25010}{In} \markbox{25011}{particular,} \markbox{25012}{the} \markbox{25013}{edge} \markbox{25014}{components} \markbox{25015}{(i.e.,} \markbox{25016}{the} \markbox{25017}{components} \markbox{25018}{of} \markbox{m25019}{$T_e$}) \markbox{25020}{treat} \markbox{25021}{endpoints} \markbox{25022}{and} \markbox{25023}{cluster} \markbox{25024}{points} \markbox{25025}{equivalently.}  \markbox{25026}{As} \markbox{25027}{the} \markbox{25028}{desired} \markbox{25029}{stable} \markbox{25030}{decompositions} \markbox{25031}{from} \markbox{25032}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{25033}{are} \markbox{25034}{subsets} \markbox{25035}{of} \markbox{25036}{the} \markbox{25037}{edge} \markbox{25038}{components,} \markbox{25039}{we} \markbox{25040}{are} \markbox{25041}{free} \markbox{25042}{to} \markbox{25043}{treat} \markbox{25044}{the} \markbox{25045}{points} \markbox{m25046}{$a,a',b,b'$} \markbox{25047}{as} \markbox{25048}{cluster} \markbox{25049}{points} \markbox{25050}{in} \markbox{25051}{applying} \markbox{25052}{Proposition} \ref{prop:add cluster} \markbox{25053}{to} \markbox{25054}{obtain} \markbox{25055}{stable} \markbox{25056}{decompositions} \markbox{25057}{for} \markbox{25058}{each} \markbox{25059}{of} \markbox{25060}{the} \markbox{25061}{steps} \markbox{m25062}{$(1) \to (2) \to (3)$} \markbox{25063}{and} \markbox{m25064}{$(4) \to (5) \to (6)$}.  \markbox{25065}{The} \markbox{25066}{only} \markbox{25067}{exception} \markbox{25068}{is} \markbox{25069}{the} \markbox{25070}{step} \markbox{m25071}{$(3) \to (4)$}, \markbox{25072}{where} \markbox{25073}{we} \markbox{25074}{are} \markbox{25075}{switching} \markbox{25076}{the} \markbox{25077}{roles} \markbox{25078}{of} \markbox{m25079}{$a$} \markbox{25080}{and} \markbox{m25081}{$a'$}.  \markbox{25082}{Here} \markbox{25083}{Proposition} \ref{prop:add cluster} \markbox{25084}{does} \markbox{25085}{not} \markbox{25086}{directly} \markbox{25087}{apply,} \markbox{25088}{but,} \markbox{25089}{by} \markbox{25090}{the} \markbox{25091}{above} \markbox{25092}{discussion,} \markbox{25093}{these} \markbox{25094}{two} \markbox{25095}{setups} \markbox{25096}{have} \markbox{25097}{the} \markbox{25098}{exact} \markbox{25099}{same} \markbox{25100}{clusters} \markbox{25101}{and} \markbox{25102}{thus} \markbox{25103}{the} \markbox{25104}{exact} \markbox{25105}{same} \markbox{25106}{edge} \markbox{25107}{components.}  \markbox{25108}{Hence} \markbox{25109}{we} \markbox{25110}{get} \markbox{25111}{the} \markbox{25112}{desired} \markbox{25113}{bijections} \markbox{25114}{(with} \markbox{25115}{their} \markbox{25116}{proximity} \markbox{25117}{constraints)} \markbox{25118}{by} \markbox{25119}{identifying} \markbox{25120}{the} \markbox{25121}{edge} \markbox{25122}{components} \markbox{25123}{as} \markbox{25124}{stable} \markbox{25125}{components---which,} \markbox{25126}{again,} \markbox{25127}{are} \markbox{25128}{all} \markbox{25129}{exactly} \markbox{25130}{the} \markbox{25131}{same---and} \markbox{25132}{taking} \markbox{25133}{the} \markbox{25134}{bijection} \markbox{25135}{between} \markbox{25136}{the} \markbox{25137}{complementary} \markbox{25138}{components} \markbox{25139}{to} \markbox{25140}{be} \markbox{25141}{the} \markbox{25142}{obvious} map.

In \markbox{25143}{other} \markbox{25144}{words,} \markbox{25145}{provided} \markbox{25146}{an} \markbox{25147}{explanation} \markbox{25148}{for} \markbox{25149}{how} \markbox{25150}{to} \markbox{25151}{iteratively} \markbox{25152}{combine} \markbox{25153}{a} \markbox{25154}{sequence} \markbox{25155}{of} \markbox{25156}{stable} \markbox{25157}{decompositions,} \markbox{25158}{we} \markbox{25159}{can} \markbox{25160}{apply} \markbox{25161}{this} \markbox{25162}{process} \markbox{25163}{to} \markbox{25164}{move} \markbox{25165}{from} \markbox{25166}{setup} \markbox{25167}{(1)} \markbox{25168}{above} \markbox{25169}{to} \markbox{25170}{setup} (6).

\medskip

\textbf{\underline{Putting it all together}}: \markbox{25171}{In} \markbox{25172}{the} \markbox{25173}{more} \markbox{25174}{general} \markbox{25175}{setting} \markbox{25176}{of} \markbox{25177}{the} \markbox{25178}{theorem,} \markbox{25179}{the} \markbox{25180}{above} \markbox{25181}{sequence} \markbox{25182}{only} \markbox{25183}{appears} \markbox{25184}{in} \markbox{25185}{the} \markbox{25186}{middle} \markbox{25187}{of} \markbox{25188}{a} \markbox{25189}{longer} \markbox{25190}{sequence} \markbox{25191}{we} \markbox{25192}{need} \markbox{25193}{to} \markbox{25194}{consider.}  \markbox{25195}{In} \markbox{25196}{particular,} \markbox{25197}{let} \markbox{m25198}{$\calY' - \calY = \{x_1, \dots, x_n\}$} \markbox{25199}{and} \markbox{m25200}{$\calY - \calY' = \{z_1, \dots, z_m\}$}, \markbox{25201}{where} \markbox{m25202}{$n,m < N$} \markbox{25203}{by} \markbox{25204}{assumption.}  \markbox{25205}{Set} \markbox{m25206}{$\calY_i = \calY \cup \{x_1, \dots, x_i\}$} \markbox{25207}{and} \markbox{m25208}{$\calY'_i = \calY' \cup \{z_1, \dots, z_i\}$}, \markbox{25209}{and} \markbox{25210}{let} \markbox{m25211}{$\calY_0 = \calY \cap \calY'$} \markbox{25212}{and} \markbox{m25213}{$\calY_{all} = \calY \cup \calY'$}.  \markbox{25214}{Then,} \markbox{25215}{by} \markbox{25216}{the} \markbox{25217}{assumptions} \markbox{25218}{in} \markbox{25219}{our} \markbox{25220}{setup,} \markbox{25221}{we} \markbox{25222}{have} \markbox{25223}{two} \markbox{25224}{sequences} \markbox{25225}{of} \markbox{25226}{pairwise} \markbox{25227}{admissible} \markbox{m25228}{$\epsilon$}-setups
$$(a,b;\calY) \to (a,b;\calY_1) \to \cdots \to (a,b;\calY_{all}) \to (a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a'\}) \to (a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a',b'\})$$
and
$$(a',b';\calY') \to \cdots \to (a',b'; \calY_n) \to (a',b';\calY_{all}) \to (a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a\}) \to (a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a,b\}),$$
which \markbox{25229}{we} \markbox{25230}{note} \markbox{25231}{are} \markbox{25232}{connected} \markbox{25233}{in} \markbox{25234}{the} \markbox{25235}{middle} \markbox{25236}{by} \markbox{25237}{the} \markbox{25238}{above} \markbox{25239}{discussion,} \markbox{25240}{where} \markbox{25241}{we} \markbox{25242}{need} \markbox{25243}{to} \markbox{25244}{switch} \markbox{25245}{the} \markbox{25246}{roles} \markbox{25247}{of} \markbox{25248}{both} \markbox{m25249}{$a,a'$} \markbox{25250}{and} \markbox{m25251}{$b,b'$}.  \markbox{25252}{In} \markbox{25253}{particular,} \markbox{25254}{the} \markbox{25255}{stable} \markbox{25256}{trees} \markbox{25257}{for} \markbox{25258}{the} \markbox{25259}{setups} \markbox{m25260}{$(a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a',b'\})$} \markbox{25261}{and} \markbox{m25262}{$(a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a,b\})$} \markbox{25263}{have} \markbox{25264}{identical} \markbox{25265}{edge} components.

By \markbox{25266}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable iteration}, \markbox{25267}{we} \markbox{25268}{get} \markbox{m25269}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m25270}{$L_{n+2}$}-compatible \markbox{25271}{stable} \markbox{25272}{decompositions} \markbox{25273}{for} \markbox{m25274}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{25275}{and} \markbox{m25276}{$(a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a',b'\})$}, \markbox{25277}{and} \markbox{m25278}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m25279}{$L_{m+2}$}-compatible \markbox{25280}{stable} \markbox{25281}{decompositions} \markbox{25282}{for} \markbox{m25283}{$(a',b';\calY)$} \markbox{25284}{and} \markbox{m25285}{$(a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a,b\})$}.  \markbox{25286}{Since} \markbox{m25287}{$(a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a',b'\})$} \markbox{25288}{and} \markbox{m25289}{$(a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a,b\})$} \markbox{25290}{determine} \markbox{25291}{identical} \markbox{25292}{edge} \markbox{25293}{components,} \markbox{25294}{we} \markbox{25295}{can} \markbox{25296}{use} \markbox{25297}{an} \markbox{25298}{identical} \markbox{25299}{argument} \markbox{25300}{to} \markbox{25301}{the} \markbox{25302}{proof} \markbox{25303}{of} \markbox{25304}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable iteration, pair} \markbox{25305}{to} \markbox{25306}{induce} \markbox{25307}{refined} \markbox{m25308}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m25309}{$(L_n \cdot L_m)$}-compatible \markbox{25310}{stable} \markbox{25311}{decompositions} \markbox{25312}{for} \markbox{m25313}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{25314}{and} \markbox{m25315}{$(a',b';\calY)$}.  \markbox{25316}{We} \markbox{25317}{leave} \markbox{25318}{the} \markbox{25319}{details} \markbox{25320}{to} \markbox{25321}{the} \markbox{25322}{reader.}  \markbox{25323}{This} \markbox{25324}{completes} \markbox{25325}{the} \markbox{25326}{proof.} \qed
